nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayamudīrayet ।। namaskṛtvāprameyāya viṣṇave kūrmarūpiṇe । purāṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaduktaṃ viśvayoninā ।।
satrānte sūtamanaghaṃ naimiṣīyā maharṣayaḥ । purāṇasaṃhitāṃ puṇyāṃ papracchū romaharṣaṇam ।। tvayā sūta mahābuddhe bhagavān brahmavittamaḥ । itihāsapurāṇārthaṃ vyāsaḥ samyagupāsitaḥ ।।
tasya te sarvaromāṇi vacasā hṛṣitāni yat । dvaipāyanasya bhagavāṃstato vai romaharṣaṇaḥ ।। bhavantameva bhagavān vyājahāra svayaṃ prabhuḥ । munīnāṃ saṃhitāṃ vaktuṃ vyāsaḥ paurāṇikīṃ purā ।।
tvaṃ hi svāyaṃbhuve yajñe sutyāhe vitate hariḥ । saṃbhūtaḥ saṃhitāṃ vaktuṃ svāṃśena puruṣottamaḥ ।। tasmād bhavantaṃ pṛcchāmaḥ purāṇaṃ kaurmamuttamam । vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ purāṇārthaviśārada ।।
munīnāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ । praṇamya manasā prāha guruṃ satyavatīsutam ।। namaskṛtvā jagadyoniṃ kūrmarūpadharaṃ harim । vakṣye paurāṇikīṃ divyāṃ kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśinīm ।।
yāṃ śrutvā pāpakarmāpi gaccheta paramāṃ gatim । na nāstike kathāṃ puṇyāmimāṃ brūyāt kadācana ।। śraddadhānāya śāntāya dhārmikāya dvijātaye । imāṃ kathāmanubrūyāt sākṣānnārāyaṇeritām ।।
sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvantarāṇi ca । vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam ।। brāhmaṃ purāṇaṃ prathamaṃ pādmaṃ vaiṣṇavameva ca । śaivaṃ bhāgavataṃ caiva bhaviṣyaṃ nāradīyakam ।।
mārkaṇḍeyamathāgneyaṃ brahmavaivartameva ca । laiṅgaṃ tathā ca vārāhaṃ skāndaṃ vāmanameva ca ।। kaurmaṃ mātsyaṃ gāruḍaṃ ca vāyavīyamanantaram । aṣṭādaśaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ brahmaṇḍamiti saṃjñitam ।।
anyānyuparāṇāni munibhiḥ kathitāni tu । aṣṭādaśapurāṇāni śrutvā saṃkṣepato dvijāḥ ।। ādyaṃ sanatkumāroktaṃ nārasihamataḥ param । tṛtīyaṃ skāndamuddiṣṭaṃ kumāreṇa tu bhāṣitam ।।
caturthaṃ śivadharmākhyaṃ sākṣānnandīśabhāṣitam । durvāsasoktamāścaryaṃ nāradoktamataḥ param ।। kāpilaṃ mānavaṃ caiva tathaivośanaseritam । brahmāṇḍaṃ vāruṇaṃ cātha kālikāhvayameva ca ।।
māheśvaraṃ tathā sāmbaṃ sauraṃ sarvārthasaṃcayam । parāśaroktamaparaṃ mārīcaṃ bhārgavāhvayam ।। idaṃ tu pañcadaśamaṃ purāṇaṃ kaurmamuttamam । caturdhā saṃsthitaṃ puṇyaṃ saṃhitānāṃ prabhedataḥ ।।
brāhmī bhagavatī saurī vaiṣṇavī ca prakīrtitāḥ । catastraḥ saṃhitāḥ puṇyā dharmakāmārthamokṣadāḥ ।। iyaṃ tu saṃhitā brāhmī caturvedaistu sammitā । bhavanti ṣaṭsahastrāṇi ślokānāmatra saṃkhyayā ।।
yatra dharmārthakāmānāṃ mokṣasya ca munīśvarāḥ । māhātmyamakhilaṃ brahma jñāyate parameśvaraḥ ।। sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvantarāṇi ca । vaṃśānucaritaṃ divyāḥ puṇyāḥ prāsaṅgikīḥ kathāḥ ।।
brāhmaṇādyairiyaṃ dhāryā dhārmikaiḥ śāntamānasaiḥ । tāmahaṃ vartayiṣyāmi vyāsena kathitāṃ purā ।। purāmṛtārthaṃ daiteyadānavaiḥ saha devatāḥ । manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā mamanthuḥ kṣīrasāgaram ।।
mathyamāne tadā tasmin kūrmarūpī janārdanaḥ । babhāra mandaraṃ devo devānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। devāśca tuṣṭuvurdevaṃ nāradādyā maharṣayaḥ । kūrmarūpadharaṃ dṛṣṭvā sākṣiṇaṃ viṣṇumavyayam ।।
tadantare abhavad devī śrīrnārāyaṇavallabhā । jagrāha bhagavān viṣṇustāmeva puruṣottamaḥ ।। tejasā viṣṇumavyaktaṃ nāradādyā maharṣayaḥ । mohitāḥ saha śakreṇa śriyo vacanamabruvan ।।
bhagavan devadeveśa nārāyaṇa jaganmaya । kaiṣā devī viśālākṣī yathāvad brūhi pṛcchatām ।। śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ viṣṇurdānavamardanaḥ । provāca devīṃ saṃprekṣya nāradādīnakalmaṣān ।।
iyaṃ sā paramā śaktirmanmayī brahmarūpiṇī । māyā mama priyānantā yayedaṃ mohitaṃ jagat ।। anayaiva jagatsarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam । mohayāmi dvijaśreṣṭhā grasāmi visṛjāmi ca ।।
utpattiṃ pralayaṃ caiva bhūtanāmāgatiṃ gatim । vijñāyānvīkṣya cātmānaṃ taranti vipulāmimām ।। asyāstvaṃśānadhiṣṭhāya śaktimanto abhavan dvijāḥ । brahmeśānādayo devāḥ sarvaśaktiriyaṃ mama ।।
saiṣā sarvajagatsūtiḥ prakṛtistriguṇātmikā । prāgeva mattaḥ saṃjātā śrīkalpe padmavāsinī ।। caturbhujā śaṅkhacakrapadmahastā śubhānvitā । koṭisūryapratīkāśā mohinī sarvadehinām ।।
nālaṃ devā na pitaro mānavā vasavo api ca । māyāmetāṃ samuttartuṃ ye cānye bhuvi dehinaḥ ।। ityukto vāsudevena munayo viṣṇumabruvan । brūhi tvaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa yadi kālatraye api ca ।
ko vā tarati tāṃ māyāṃ durjayāṃ devanirmitām ।। athovāca hṛṣīkeśo munīn munigaṇārcitaḥ । asti dvijātipravara indradyumna iti śrutaḥ ।। pūrvajanmani rājāsāvadhṛṣyaḥ śaṅkarādibhiḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā māṃ kūrmasaṃsthānaṃ śrutvā paurāṇikīṃ svayam । saṃhitāṃ manmukhād divyāṃ puraskṛtya munīśvarān ।। brahmāṇaṃ ca mahādevaṃ devāṃścānyān svaśaktibhiḥ । macchaktau saṃsthitān buddhvā māmeva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।
saṃbhāṣito mayā cātha viprayoniṃ gamiṣyasi । indradyumna iti khyāto jātiṃ smarasi paurvikīm ।। sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ devānāmapyagocaram । vaktavyaṃ yad guhyatamaṃ dāsye jñānaṃ tavānagha ।
labdhvā tanmāmakaṃ jñānaṃ māmevānte pravekṣyasi ।। aṃśāntareṇa bhūmyāṃ tvaṃ tatra tiṣṭha sunirdṛtaḥ । vaivasvate antare atite kāryārthaṃ māṃ pravekṣyasi ।। māṃ praṇamya purīṃ gatvā pālayāmāsa medinīm ।
kāladharmaṃ gataḥ kālācchvetadvīpe mayā saha ।। bhuktvā tān vaiṣṇavān bhogān yogināmapyagocarān । madājñayā muniśreṣṭhā jajñe viprakule punaḥ ।। jñātvā māṃ vāsudevākhyaṃ yatra dve nihite akṣare ।
vidyāvidye gūḍharūpe yattad brahma paraṃ viduḥ ।। sor'cayāmāsa bhūtānāmāśrayaṃ parameśvaram । vratopavāsaniyamairhemairbrāhmaṇatarpaṇaiḥ ।। tadāśīstannamaskārastanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ ।
ārādhayan mahādevaṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam ।। tasyaivaṃ vartamānasya kadācit paramā kalā । svarūpaṃ darśayāmāsa divyaṃ viṣṇusamudbhavam ।। dṛṣṭvā praṇamya śirasā viṣṇorbhagavataḥ priyām ।
saṃstūya vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ kṛtāñjalirabhāṣata ।। kā tvaṃ deviviśālākṣi viṣṇucihnaṅkite śubhe । yāthātathyena vai bhāvaṃ tavedānīṃ bravīhi me ।। tasya tad vākyamākarṇya suprasannā sumaṅgalā ।
hasantī saṃsmaran viṣṇuṃ priyaṃ brāhmaṇamabravīt ।। na māṃ paśyanti munayo devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ । nārāyaṇātmikā caikā māyāhaṃ tanmayā parā ।। na me nārāyaṇād bhedo vidyate hi vicārataḥ ।
tanmayāhaṃ paraṃ brahma sa viṣṇuḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। yer'cayantīha bhūtānāmāśrayaṃ parameśvaram । jñānena karmayogena na teṣāṃ prabhavāmyaham ।। tasmādanādinidhanaṃ karmayogaparāyaṇaḥ ।
jñānenārādhayānantaṃ tato mokṣamavāpsyasi ।। ityuktaḥ sa muniśreṣṭha indradyumno mahāmatiḥ । praṇamya śirasā devīṃ prāñjaliḥ punarabravīt ।। kathaṃ sa bhagavānīśaḥ śāśvato niṣkalo acyutaḥ ।
jñātuṃ hi śakyate devi brūhi me parameśvari ।। ekamuktātha vipreṇa devī kamalavāsinī । sākṣānnārāyaṇo jñānaṃ dāsyatītyāha taṃ munim ।। ubhābhyāmatha hastābhyāṃ saṃspṛśya praṇataṃ munim ।
smṛtvā parātparaṃ viṣṇuṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। so api nārāyaṇaṃ draṣṭuṃ parameṇa samādhinā । ārādhayaddhṛṣīkeśaṃ praṇatārtiprabhañjanam ।। tato bahutithe kāle gate nārāyaṇaḥ svayam ।
prādurāsīnmahāyogī pītavāsā jaganmayaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā devaṃ samāyāntaṃ viṣṇumātmānamavyayam । jānubhyāmavaniṃ gatvā tuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam ।। yajñeśācyuta govinda mādhavānanta keśava ।
kuṣṇa viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśa tubhyaṃ viśvātmane namaḥ ।। namo astu te purāṇāya haraye viśvamūrtaye । sargasthitivināśānāṃ hetave anantaśakye ।। nirguṇāya namastubhyaṃ niṣkalāyāmalātmane ।
puruṣāya namastubhyaṃ viśvarūpāya te namaḥ ।। namaste vāsudevāya viṣṇave viśvayonaye । ādimadhyāntahīnāya jñānagamyāya te namaḥ ।। namaste nirvikārāya niṣprapañcāya te namaḥ ।
bhedābhedavihīnāya namo astvānandarūpiṇe ।। namastārāya śāntāya namo apratihatātmane । anantamūrtaye tubhyamamūrtāya namo namaḥ ।। namaste paramārthāya māyātītāya te namaḥ ।
namaste parameśāya brahmaṇe paramātmane ।। namo astu te susūkṣmāya mahādevāya te namaḥ । namaḥ śivāya śuddhāya namaste parameṣṭhine ।। tvayaiva sṛṣṭamakhilaṃ tvameva paramā gatiḥ ।
tvaṃ pitā sarvabhūtānāṃ tvaṃ mātā puruṣottama ।। tvamakṣaraṃ paraṃ dhāma cinmātraṃ vyoma niṣkalam । sarvasyādhāramavyaktamanantaṃ tamasaḥ param ।। prapaśyanti parātmānaṃ jñānadīpena kevalam ।
prapadye bhavato rūpaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। evaṃ stuvantaṃ bhagavān bhūtātmā bhūtabhāvanaḥ । ubhābhyāmatha hastābhyāṃ pasparśa prahasanniva ।। spṛṣṭamātro bhagavatā viṣṇunā munipuṅgavaḥ ।
yathāvat paramaṃ tattvaṃ jñātavāṃstatprasādataḥ ।। tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasā praṇipatya janārdanam । provāconnidrapadmākṣaṃ pītavāsasamacyutam ।। tvatprasādādasaṃdigdhamutpannaṃ puruṣottama ।
jñānaṃ brahmaikaviṣayaṃ paramānandasiddhidam ।। namo bhagavate tubhyaṃ vāsudevāya vedhase । kiṃ kariṣyāmi yogeśa tanme vada jaganmaya ।। śrutvā nārāyaṇo vākyamindradyumnasya mādhavaḥ ।
uvāca sasmitaṃ vākyamaśeṣajagato hitam ।। varṇāśramācāravatāṃ puṃsāṃ devo maheśvaraḥ । jñānena bhaktiyogena pūjanīyo na cānyathā ।। vijñāya tatparaṃ tattvaṃ vibhūtiṃ kāryakāraṇam ।
pravṛtiṃ cāpi me jñātvā mokṣārthośvaramarcayet ।। sarvasaṅgān parityajya jñātvā māyāmayaṃ jagat । advaitaṃ bhāvayātmānaṃ drakṣyase parameśvaram ।। trividhā bhāvanā brahman procyamānā nibodha me ।
ekā madviṣayā tatra dvitīyā vyaktasaṃśrayā । anyā ca bhāvanā brāhmī vijñeyā sā guṇātigā ।। āsāmanyatamāṃ cātha bhāvanāṃ bhāvayed budhaḥ । aśaktaḥ saṃśrayedādyāmityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ ।।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ । samārādhaya viśveśaṃ tato mokṣamavāpsyasi ।। kiṃ tat parataraṃ tattvaṃ kā vibhūtirjanārdana । kiṃ kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ kastvaṃ pravṛttiścāpi kā tava ।।
parātparataraṃ tattvaṃ paraṃ brahmaikamavyayam । nityānandaṃ svayañjyotirakṣaraṃ tamasaḥ param ।। aiśvaryaṃ tasya yannityaṃ vibhūtiriti gīyate । kāryaṃ jagadathāvyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ śuddhamakṣaram ।।
ahaṃ hi sarvabhūtānāmantaryāmīśvaraḥ paraḥ । sargasthityantakartṛtvaṃ pravṛttirmama gīyate ।। etad vijñāya bhāvena yathāvadakhilaṃ dvija । tatastvaṃ karmayogena śāśvataṃ samyagarcaya ।।
ke te varṇāśramācārā yaiḥ samārādhyate paraḥ । jñānaṃ ca kīdṛśaṃ divyaṃ bhāvanātrayasaṃsthitam ।। kathaṃ sṛṣṭamidaṃ pūrvaṃ kathaṃ saṃhriyate punaḥ । kiyatyaḥ sṛṣṭayo loke vaṃśā manvantarāṇi ca ।
kāni teṣāṃ pramāṇāni pāvanāni vratāni ca ।। tīrthānyarkādisaṃsthānaṃ pṛthivyāyāmavistare । kati dvīpāḥ samudrāśca parvatāśca nadīnadāḥ । brūhi me puṇḍarīkākṣa yathāvadadhunākhilam ।।
evamukto atha tenāhaṃ bhaktānugrahakāmyayā । yathāvadakhilaṃ sarvamavocaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। vyākhyāyāśeṣamevedaṃ yatpṛṣṭo ahaṃ dvijena tu । anugṛhya ca taṃ vipraṃ tatraivāntarhito abhavam ।।
so api tena vidhānena maduktena dvijottamaḥ । ārādhayāmāsa paraṃ bhāvapūtaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। tyaktvā putrādiṣu snehaṃ nirdvandvo niṣparigrahaḥ । saṃnyasya sarvakarmāṇi paraṃ vairāgyamāśritaḥ ।।
ātmanyātmānamanvīkṣya svātmanyevākhilaṃ jagat । saṃprāpya bhāvanāmantyāṃ brāhmīmakṣarapūrvikām ।। avāpa paramaṃ yogaṃ yenaikaṃ paripaśyati । yaṃ vinidrā jitaśvāsāḥ kāṅkṣante mokṣakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।।
tataḥ kadācid yogīndro brahmāṇaṃ draṣṭumavyayam । jagāmādityanirdeśānmānasottaraparvatam । ākāśenaiva viprendro yogaiśvaryaprabhāvataḥ ।। vimānaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ prādhurbhūtamanuttamam ।
anvagacchan devagaṇā gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ । dṛṣṭvānye pathi yogīndraṃ siddhā brahmarṣayo yayuḥ ।। tataḥ sa gatvā tu giriṃ viveśa suravanditam । sthānaṃ tadyogibhirjuṣṭaṃ yatrāste paramaḥ pumān ।।
saṃprāpya paramaṃ sthānaṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham । viveśa cāntarbhavanaṃ devānāṃ ca durāsadam ।। vicintayāmāsa paraṃ śaraṇyaṃ sarvadehinām । anādinidhanaṃ devaṃ devadevaṃ pitāmaham ।।
tataḥ prādurabhūt tasmin prakāśaḥ paramātmanaḥ । tanmadhye puruṣaṃ pūrvamapaśyat paramaṃ padam ।। mahāntaṃ tejaso rāśimagamyaṃ brahmavidviṣām । caturmukhamudārāṅgamarcibhirupaśobhitam ।।
so api yoginamanvīkṣya praṇamantamupasthitam । pratyudgamya svayaṃ devo viśvātmā pariṣasvaje ।। pariṣvaktasya devena dvijendrasyātha dehataḥ । nirgatya mahatī jyotsnā viveśādityamaṇḍalam ।
ṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃjñaṃ tat pavitramamalaṃ padam ।। hiraṇyagarbho bhagavān yatrāste havyakavyabhuk । dvāraṃ tad yogināmādyaṃ vedānteṣu pratiṣṭhitam । brahmatejomayaṃ śrīmanniṣṭhā caiva manīṣiṇām ।।
dṛṣṭamātro bhagavatāta brahmaṇārcirmayo muniḥ । apaśyadaiśvaraṃ tejaḥ śāntaṃ sarvatragaṃ śivam ।। svātmānamakṣaraṃ vyomatad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam । ānandamacalaṃ brahma sthānaṃ tatpārameśvaram ।।
sarvabhūtātmabhūtaḥ sa paramaiśvaryamāsthitaḥ । prāptavānātmano dhāma yattanmokṣākhyamavyayam ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena varṇāśramavidhau sthitaḥ । samāśrityāntimaṃ bhāvaṃ māyāṃ lakṣmīṃ tared budhaḥ ।।
vyāhṛtā hariṇā tvevaṃ nārādādyā maharṣayaḥ । śakreṇa sahitāḥ sarve papracchurgaruḍadhvajam ।। devadeva hṛṣīkeśa nātha nārāyaṇāmala । tad vadāśeṣamasmākaṃ yaduktaṃ bhavatā purā ।।
indradyumnāya viprayā jñānaṃ dharmādigocaram । śuśrūṣuścāpyayaṃ śakraḥ sakhā tava jaganmaya ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ kūrmarūpī janārdanaḥ । rasātalagato devo nāradādyairmaharṣibhiḥ ।।
pṛṣṭaḥ provāca sakalaṃ purāṇaṃ kaurmamuttamam । sannidhau devarājasya tad vakṣye bhavatāmaham ।। dhanyaṃ yaśasyāmāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ mokṣapradaṃ nṛṇām । purāṇaśravaṇaṃ viprāḥ kathanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
śrutvā cādhyāyamevaikaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate । upākhyānamathaikaṃ vā brahmaloke mahīyate ।। idaṃ purāṇaṃ paramaṃ kaurmaṃ kūrmasvarūpiṇā । uktaṃ devādhidevena śraddhātavyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ ।।
śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve yatpṛṣṭo ahaṃ jagaddhitam । vakṣyamāṇaṃ mayā sarvamindradyumnāya bhāṣitam ।। bhūtairbhavyairbhaviṣyadbhiścaritairupabṛṃhitam । purāṇaṃ puṇyadaṃ nṛṇāṃ mokṣadharmānukīrtanam ।।
ahaṃ nārāyaṇo devaḥ pūrvamāsaṃ na me param । upāsya vipulāṃ nidrāṃ bhogiśayyāṃ samāśritaḥ ।। cintayāmi punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ niśānte pratibudhya tu । tato me sahasotpannaḥ prasādo munipuṅgavā ।।
caturmukhastato jāto brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । tadantare abhavat krodhaḥ kasmāccit kāraṇāt tadā ।। ātmano muniśārdūlāstatra devo maheśvaraḥ । rudraḥ krodhātmajo jajñe śūlapāṇistrilocanaḥ ।
tejasā sūryasaṃkāśastrailokyaṃ saṃharanniva ।। tataḥ śrīrabhavad devi kamalāyatalocanā । surūpā saumyavadanā mohinī sarvadehinām ।। śucismitā suprasannā maṅgalā mahimāspadā ।
divyakāntisamāyuktā divyamālyopaśobhitā ।। nārāyaṇī mahāmāyā mūlaprakṛtiravyayā । svadhāmnā pūrayantīdaṃ matpārśvaṃ samupāviśat ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭavā bhagavān brahmā māmuvāca jagatpatiḥ ।
mohāyāśeṣabhūtānāṃ niyojaya surūpiṇīm । yeneyaṃ vipulā sṛṣṭirvardhate mama mādhava ।। tathokto ahaṃ śriyaṃ devīmabruvaṃ prahasanniva । devīdamakhilaṃ viśvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।
mohayitvā mamādeśāt saṃsāre vinipātaya ।। jñānayogaratān dāntān brahmiṣṭhān brahmavādinaḥ । akrodhanān satyaparān dūrataḥ parivarjaya ।। dhyāyino nirmamān śāntān dhārmikān vedapāragān ।
jāpinastāpasān viprān dūrataḥ parivarjaya ।। vedavedāntavijñānasaṃchinnāśeṣasaṃśayān । mahāyajñaparān viprān dūrataḥ parivarjaya ।। ye yajanti japairhemairdevadevaṃ maheśvaram ।
svādhyāyenejyayā dūrāt tān prayatnena varjaya ।। bhaktiyogasamāyuktānīśvarārpitamānasān । prāṇāyāmādiṣu ratān dūrāt pariharāmalān ।। praṇavāsaktamanaso rudrajapyaparāyaṇān ।
atharvaśiraso adhyetṛn dharmajñān parivarjaya ।। bahunātra kimuktena svadharmaparipālakān । īśvarārādhanaratān manniyogānna mohaya ।। evaṃ mayā mahāmāyā preritā harivallabhā ।
yathādeśaṃ cakārāsau tasmāllakṣmīṃ samarcayet ।। śriyaṃ dadāti vipulāṃ puṣṭiṃ medhāṃ yaśo balam । arcitā bhagavatpatnī tasmāllakṣmīṃ samarcayet ।। tato asṛjat sa bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
carācarāṇi bhūtāni yathāpūrvaṃ mamājñayā ।। parīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum । dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so asṛjad yogavidyayā ।। navaite brahmaṇaḥ putrā brahmāṇo brāhmaṇottamāḥ ।
brahmavādina evaite marīcyādyāstu sādhakāḥ ।। sasarja brāhmaṇān vaktrāt kṣatriyāṃśca bhujād vibhuḥ । vaiśyānūrudvayād devaḥ pādārchūdrān pitāmahaḥ ।। yajñaniṣpattaye brahmā śūdravarjaṃ sasarja ha ।
guptaye sarvavedānāṃ tebhyo yajño hi nirbabhau ।। ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni tathaivātharvaṇāni ca । brahmaṇaḥ sahajaṃ rūpaṃ nityaiṣā śaktiravyayā ।। anādinidhanā divyā vāgutsṛṣṭā svayaṃbhuvā ।
ādau vedamayī bhūtā yataḥ sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ ।। ato anyānitu śāstrāṇipṛthivyāṃyānikānicit । na teṣu ramate dhīraḥ pāṣaṇḍī tena jāyate ।। vedārthavittamaiḥ kāryaṃ yatsmṛtaṃ munibhiḥ purā ।
sa jñeyaḥ paramo dharmo nānyaśāstreṣu saṃsthitaḥ ।। yā vedabāhyāḥ smṛtayo yāśca kāśca kudṛṣṭayaḥ । sarvāstā niṣphalāḥ pretyatamoniṣṭhāhitāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। pūrvakalpe prajā jātāḥ sarvabādāvivarjitāḥ ।
śuddhāntaḥ karaṇāḥ sarvāḥ svadharmaniratāḥ sadā ।। tataḥ kālavaśāt tāsāṃ rāgadveṣādiko abhavat । adharmo muniśārdūlāḥ svadharmapratibandhakaḥ ।। tataḥ sā sahajā siddhistāsāṃ nātīva jāyate ।
rajomātrātmikāstāsāṃ siddhayo anyāstadābhavan ।। tāsu kṣīṇāsvaśeṣāsu kālayogena tāḥ punaḥ । vārtopāyaṃ punaścakrurhastasiddhiṃ ca karmajām । tatastāsāṃ vibhurbrahmā karmājīvamakalpayat ।।
svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ pūrvaṃ dharmān provāca dharmadṛk । sākṣāt prajāpatermūrtirnisṛṣṭā brahmaṇā dvijāḥ । bhṛgvādayastadvadanācchrutvā dharmānathocire ।। yajanaṃ yājanaṃ dānaṃ brāhmaṇasya pratigraham ।
adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ ṣaṭ karmāṇi dvijottamāḥ ।। dānamadhyayanaṃ yajño dharmaḥ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ । daṇḍo yuddhaṃ kṣatriyasya kṛṣirvaiśyasya śasyate ।। śuśrūṣaiva dvijātīnāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ dharmasādhanam ।
kārukarma tathājīvaḥ pākayajño api dharmataḥ ।। tataḥ sthiteṣu varṇeṣu sthāpayāmāsa cāśramān । gṛhasthaṃ ca vanasthaṃ ca bhikṣukaṃ brahmacāriṇam ।। agnayo atithiśuśrūṣā yajño dānaṃ surārcanam ।
gṛhasthasya samāsena dharmo ayaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। homo mūlaphalāśitvaṃ svādhyāyastapa eva ca । saṃvibhāgo yathānyāyaṃ dharmo ayaṃ vanavāsinām ।। bhaikṣāśanaṃ ca maunitvaṃ tapo dhyānaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
samyagjñānaṃ ca vairāgyaṃ dharmo ayaṃ bhikṣuke mataḥ ।। bhikṣācaryā ca śuśrūṣā guroḥ svādhyāya eva ca । sandhyākarmāgnikāryaṃ ca dharmo ayaṃ brahmacāriṇām ।। brahmacārivanasthānāṃ bhikṣukāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।
sādhāraṇaṃ brahmacaryaṃ provāca kamalodbhavaḥ ।। ṛtukālābhigāmitvaṃ svadāreṣu na cānyataḥ । parvavarjaṃ gṛhasthasya brahmacaryamudāhṛtam ।। āgarbhasaṃbhavādādyāt kāryaṃ tenāpramādataḥ ।
akurvāṇastu viprendrā bhrūṇahā tu prajāyate ।। vedābhyāso anvahaṃ śaktyā śrāddhaṃ cātithipūjanam । gṛhasthasya paro dharmo devatābhyarcanaṃ tathā ।। vaivāhmamagnimindhīta sāyaṃ prātaryathāvidhi ।
deśāntaragato vātha mṛtapatnīka eva vā ।। trayāṇāmāśramāṇāṃ tu gṛhastho yonirucyate । anye tamupajīvanti tasmācchreyān gṛhāśramī ।। aikāśramyaṃ gṛhasthasya trayāṇāṃ śrutidarśanāt ।
tasmād gārhasthyamevaikaṃ vijñeyaṃ dharmasādhanam ।। parityajedarthakāmau yau syātāṃ dharmavarjitau । sarvalokaviruddhaṃ ca dharmamapyācarenna tu ।। dharmāt saṃjāyate hyartho dharmāt kāmo abhijāyate ।
dharma evāpavargāya tasmād dharmaṃ samāśrayet ।। dharmaścārthaśca kāmaśca trivargastriguṇo mataḥ । sattvaṃ rajastamaśceti tasmāddharmaṃ samāśrayet ।। ūrdhvaṃ gacchanti sattvasthā madhye tiṣṭhanti rājasāḥ ।
jaghanyaguṇavṛttisthā adho gacchanti tāmasāḥ ।। yasmin dharmasamāyuktāvarthakāmau vyavasthitau । iha loke sukhī bhūtvā pretyānantyāya kalpate ।। dharmāt saṃjāyate mokṣo hyarthāt kāmo abhijāyate ।
evaṃ sādhanasādhyatvaṃ cāturvidhye pradarśitam ।। ya evaṃ veda dharmārthakāmamokṣasya mānavaḥ । māhātmyaṃ cānutiṣṭheta sa cānantyāya kalpate ।। tasmādarthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca tyaktvā dharmaṃ samāśrayet ।
dharmāt saṃjāyate sarvamityāhurbrahmavādinaḥ ।। dharmeṇa dhāryate sarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam । anādinidhanā śaktiḥ saiṣā brāhmī dvijottamāḥ ।। karmaṇā prāpyate dharmo jñānena ca na saṃśayaḥ ।
tasmājjñānena sahitaṃ karmayogaṃ samācaret ।। pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca dvividhaṃ karma vaidikam । jñānapūrvaṃ nivṛttaṃ syāt pravṛttaṃ yadato anyathā ।। nivṛttaṃ sevamānastu yāti tat paramaṃ padam ।
tasmānnivṛttaṃ saṃsevyamanyathā saṃsaret punaḥ ।। kṣamā damo dayā dānamalobhastyāga eva ca । ārjavaṃ cānasūyā ca tīrthānusaraṇaṃ tathā ।। satyaṃ santoṣa āstikyaṃ śraddhā cendriyanigrahaḥ ।
devatābhyarcanaṃ pūjā brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। āhiṃsā priyavāditvamapaiśunyamakalkatā । sāmāsikamimaṃ dharmaṃ cāturvarṇye abravīnmanuḥ ।। prājāpatyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ kriyāvatām ।
sthānamaindraṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ saṃgrāmeṣvapalāyinām ।। vaiśyānāṃ mārutaṃ sthānaṃ svadharmamanuvartatām । gāndharvaṃ śūdrajātīnāṃ paricāreṇa vartatām ।। aṣṭāśītisahastrāṇāmṛṣīṇāmūrdhvaretasām ।
smṛtaṃ teṣāṃ tu yatsthānaṃ tadeva guruvāsinām ।। saptarṣoṇāṃ tu yatsthānaṃ smṛtaṃ tad vai vanaukasām । prājāpatyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ sthānamuktaṃ svayaṃbhuvā ।। yatīnāṃ yatacittānāṃ nyāsināmūrdhvaretasām ।
hairaṇyagarbhaṃ tat sthānaṃ yasmānnāvartate punaḥ ।। yogināmamṛtaṃ sthānaṃ vyomākhyaṃ paramākṣaram । ānandamaiśvaraṃ dhāma sā kāṣṭhā sā parāgatiḥ ।। bhagavan devatārighna hiraṇyākṣaniṣūdana ।
catvāro hyāśramāḥ proktā yogināmeka ucyate ।। sarvakarmāṇi saṃnyasya samādhimacalaṃ śritaḥ । ya āste niścalo yogī sa saṃnyāsī na pañcamaḥ ।। sarveṣāmāśramāṇāṃ tu dvaividhyaṃ śrutadarśitam ।
brahmacāryupakurvāṇo naiṣṭhiko brahmatatparaḥ ।। yo adhītyavidhivadvedān gṛhasthāśramamāvrajet । upakurvāṇako jñeyo naiṣṭhiko maraṇāntikaḥ ।। udāsīnaḥ sādhakaśca gṛhastho dvividho bhavet ।
kuṭumbabharaṇe yattaḥ sādhako asau gṛhī bhavet ।। ṛṇānitrīṇyapākṛtyatyaktvā bhāryādhanādikam । ekākī yastu vicaredudāsīnaḥ sa maukṣikaḥ ।। tapastapyati yo araṇye yajed devān juhoti ca ।
svādhyāye caiva nirato vanasthastāpaso mataḥ ।। tapasā karṣito atyarthaṃ yastu dhyānaparo bhavet । sāṃnyāsikaḥ sa vijñeyo vānaprasthāśrame sthitaḥ ।। yogābhyāsarato nityamārurukṣurjitendriyaḥ ।
jñānāya vartate bhikṣuḥ procyate pārameṣṭhikaḥ ।। yastvātmaratireva syānnityatṛpto mahāmuniḥ । samyag darśanasaṃpannaḥ sa yogī bhikṣurucyate ।। jñānasaṃnyāsinaḥ kecid vedasaṃnyāsino apare ।
karmasanyāsinaḥ kecit trividhāḥ parāmeṣṭhikāḥ ।। yogī ca trividho jñeyo bhautikaḥ sāṃkhya eva ca । tṛtīyotyāśramī proktī yogamuttamamāsthitaḥ ।। prathamā bhāvanā pūrve sāṃkhye tvakṣarabhāvanā ।
tṛtīye cāntimā proktā bhāvanā pārameśvarī ।। tasmādetad vijānīdhvamāśramāṇāṃ catuṣṭayam । sarveṣu vedaśāstreṣu pañcamo nopapadyate ।। evaṃ varṇāśramān sṛṣṭvā devadevo nirañjanaḥ ।
dakṣādīn prāha viśvātmā sṛjadhvaṃ vividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। brahmaṇo vacanāt putrā dakṣādyā munisattamāḥ । asṛjanta prajāḥ sarvā devamānuṣapūrvikāḥ ।। ityeṣa bhagavān brahmā straṣṭvatve sa vyavasthitaḥ ।
ahaṃ vai pālayāmīdaṃ saṃhariṣyati śūlabhṛt ।। tistrastu mūrtayaḥ proktā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ । rajaḥ sattvatamoyogāt parasya paramātmanaḥ ।। anoyanyamanuraktāste hyanyonyamupajīvinaḥ ।
anyonyaṃ praṇatāścaiva līlayā parameśvarāḥ ।। brāhmī māheśvarī caiva tathaivākṣarabhāvanā । tistrastu bhāvanā rudre vartante satataṃ dvijāḥ ।। pravartate mayyajastramādyā cākṣarabhāvanā ।
dvitīyā brahmaṇaḥ proktā devasyākṣarabhāvanā ।। ahaṃ caiva mahādevo na bhinnau paramārthataḥ । vibhajyasvecchayātmānaṃ so anyaryāmīśvaraḥ sthitaḥ ।। trailokyamakhilaṃ straṣṭuṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।
puruṣaḥ parato avyaktād brahmatvaṃ samupāgamat ।। tasmād brahmā mahādevo viṣṇurviśveśvaraḥ paraḥ । ekasyaiva smṛtāstistrastanūḥ kāryavaśāt prabhoḥ ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena vandyāḥ pūjyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।
yadīcchedacirāt sthānaṃ yattanmokṣākhyamavyayam ।। varṇāśramaprayuktena dharmeṇa prītisaṃyutaḥ । pūjayed bhāvayuktena yāvajjīvaṃ pratijñayā ।। caturṇāmāśramāṇāṃ tu prokto ayaṃ vidhivaddvijāḥ ।
āśramo vaiṣṇavo brāhmo harāśrama iti trayaḥ ।। talliṅgadhārī satataṃ tadbhaktajanavatsalaḥ । dhyāyedathārcayedetān brahmavidyāparāyaṇaḥ ।। sarveṣāmeva bhaktānāṃ śaṃbhorliṅgamanuttamam ।
sitena bhasmanā kāryaṃ lalāṭe tu tripuṇḍrakam ।। yastu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ prapannaḥ paramaṃ padam । dhārayet sarvadā śūlaṃ lalāṭe gandhavāribhiḥ ।। prapannā ye jagadbījaṃ brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam ।
teṣāṃ lalāṭe tilakaṃ dhāraṇīyaṃ tu sarvadā ।। yo asāvanādirbhūtādiḥ kālātmāsau dhṛto bhavet । uparyadho bhāvayogāt tripuṇḍrasya tu dhāraṇāt ।। yattat pradhānaṃ triguṇaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam ।
dhṛtaṃ triśūladharaṇād bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ।। brahmatejomayaṃ śuklaṃ yadetan maṇḍalaṃ raveḥ । bhavatyeva dhṛtaṃ sthānamaiśvaraṃ tilake kṛte ।। tasmāt kāryaṃ triśūlāṅkaṃ tathā ca tilakaṃ śubham ।
triyāyuṣaṃ ca bhaktānāṃ trayāṇāṃ vidhipūrvakam ।। yajeta juhuyādagnau japed dadyājjitendriyaḥ । śānto dānto jitakrodho varṇāśramavidhānavit ।। evaṃ paricared devān yāvajjīvaṃ samāhitaḥ ।
teṣāṃ saṃsthānamacalaṃ so acirādadhigacchati ।। varṇā bhagavatoddiṣṭāścatvāro apyāśramāstathā । idānīṃ kramamasmākamāśramāṇāṃ vada prabho ।। brahmacārī gṛhasthaśca vānaprastho yatistathā ।
krameṇaivāśramāḥ proktāḥ kāraṇādanyathā bhavet ।। utpannajñānavijñāno vairāgyaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ । pravrajed brahmacaryāt tu yadicchet paramāṃ gatim ।। dārānāhṛtya vidhivadanyathā vividhairmakhaiḥ ।
yajedutpādayet putrān virakto yadi saṃnyaset ।। aniṣṭvā vidhivad yajñairanutpādya tathātmajam । nagārhasthyaṃ gṛhītyaktvā saṃnyased buddhimān dvijaḥ ।। atha vairāgyavegena sthātuṃ notsahate gṛhe ।
tatraiva saṃnyased vidvānaniṣṭvāpi dvijottamaḥ ।। anyathā vividhairyajñairiṣṭvā vanamathākṣayet । tapastaptvā tapoyogād viraktaḥ saṃnyased yadi ।। vānaprasthāśramaṃ gatvā na gṛhaṃ praviśet punaḥ ।
na saṃnyāsī vanaṃ cātha brahmācaryaṃ na sādhakaḥ ।। prājāpatyāṃ nirūpyeṣṭimāgneyīmathavā dvijaḥ । pravrajeta gṛhī vidvān vanād vā śruticodanāt ।। prakartumasamartho api juhotiyajatikriyāḥ ।
andhaḥ paṅgurdaridro vā viraktaḥ saṃnyased dvijaḥ ।। sarveṣāmeva vairāgyaṃ saṃnyāsāya vidhīyate । patatyevāvirakto yaḥ saṃnyāsaṃ kartumicchati ।। ekasminnathavā samyag vartetāmaraṇaṃ dvijaḥ ।
śraddhāvanāśrame yuktaḥ so amṛtatvāya kalpate ।। nyāyāgatadhanaḥ śānto brahmavidyāparāyaṇaḥ । svadharmapālako nityaṃ so amṛtatvāya kalpate ।। brahmaṇyādhāya kramāṇi niḥsaṅgaḥ kāmavarjitaḥ ।
prasannenaiva manasā kurvāṇo yāti tatpadam ।। brahmaṇā dīyate deyaṃ brahmaṇe saṃpradīyate । brahmaiva dīyate ceti brahmārpaṇamidaṃ param ।। nāhaṃ kartā sarvametad brahmaiva kurute tathā ।
etad brahmārpaṇaṃ proktamṛṣibhiḥ tattvadarśibhiḥ ।। prīṇātu bhagavānīśaḥ karmaṇānena śāśvataḥ । karoti satataṃ buddhyā brahmārpaṇamidaṃ param ।। yadvā phalānāṃ saṃnyāsaṃ prakuryāt parameśvare ।
karmaṇāmetadapyāhuḥ brahmārpaṇamanuttamam ।। kāryamityeva yatkarma niyataṃ saṅgavarjitam । kriyate viduṣā karma tadbhavedapi mokṣadam ।। anyathā yadi karmāṇi kuryānnityamapi dvijaḥ ।
akṛtvā phalasaṃnyāsaṃ badhyate tatphalena tu ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena tyaktvā karmāśritaṃ phalam । avidvānapi kurvota karmāpnotyacirāt padam ।। karmaṇā kṣīyate pāpamaihikaṃ paurvikaṃ tathā ।
manaḥ prasādamanveti brahma vijñāyate tataḥ ।। karmaṇā sahitājjñānāt samyag yogo abijāyate । jñānaṃ ca karmasahitaṃ jāyate doṣavarjitam ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena tatra tatrāśrame rataḥ ।
karmāṇīśvaratuṣṭyarthaṃ kuryānnaiṣkarmyamāpnuyāt ।। saṃprāpya paramaṃ jñānaṃ naiṣkarmyaṃ tatprasādataḥ । ekākī nirmamaḥ śānto jīvanneva vimucyate ।। vīkṣate paramātmānaṃ paraṃ brahma maheśvaram ।
nityānandaṃ nirābhāsaṃ tasminneva layaṃ vrajet ।। tasmāt seveta satataṃ karmayogaṃ prasannadhīḥ । tṛptaye parameśasya tat padaṃ yāti śāśvatam ।। etad vaḥ sathitaṃ sarvaṃ cāturāśramyamuttamam ।
na hyetat samatikramya siddhiṃ vindati mānavaḥ ।। śrutvā'śramavidhiṃ kṛtsanamṛṣayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ । namaskṛtya hṛṣīkeśaṃ punarvacanamabruvan ।। bhāṣitaṃ bhavatā sarvaṃ cāturāśramyamuttamam ।
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmo yathā saṃbhavate jagat ।। kutaḥ sarvamidaṃ jātaṃ kasmiṃśca layameṣyati । niyantā kaśca sarveṣāṃ vadasva puruṣottama ।। śrutvā nārāyaṇo vākyamṛṣīṇāṃ kūrmarūpadhṛk ।
prāha gambhīrayā vācā bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyayau ।। maheśvaraḥ paro avyaktaścaturvyūhaḥ sanātanaḥ । anantaścāprameyaśca niyantā viśvatomukhaḥ ।। avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattannityaṃ sadasadātmakam ।
pradhānaṃ prakṛtiśceti yadāhustattvacintakāḥ ।। gandhavarṇarasairhenaṃ śabdasparśavivarjitam । ajaraṃ dhruvamakṣayyaṃ nityaṃ svātmanyavasthitam ।। jagadyonirmahābhūtaṃ paraṃ brahma sanātanam ।
vigrahaḥ sarvabhūtānāmātmanādhiṣṭhitaṃ mahat ।। anādyantamajaṃ sūkṣmaṃ triguṇaṃ prabhavāpyayam । asāṃpratamavijñeyaṃ brahmāgre samavartata ।। guṇasāmye tadā tasmin puruṣe cātmani sthite ।
prākṛtaḥ pralayo jñeyo yāvad viśvasamudbhavaḥ ।। brāhmī rātririyaṃ proktā ahaḥ sṛṣṭirudāhṛtā । aharna vidyate tasya na rātrirhyupacārataḥ ।। niśānte pratibuddho asau jagadādiranādimān ।
sarvabhūtamayo avyakto hyantaryāmīśvaraḥ paraḥ ।। prakṛtiṃ puruṣaṃ caiva praviśyāśu maheśvaraḥ । kṣobhayāmāsa yogena pareṇa parameśvaraḥ ।। yathā mado narastrīṇāṃ yathā vā mādhavo anilaḥ ।
anupraviṣṭaḥ kṣobhāya tathāsau yogamūrtimān ।। sa eva kṣobhako viprāḥ kṣobhyaśca parameśvaraḥ । sa saṃkocavikāsābhyāṃ pradhānatve api ca sthitaḥ ।। pradhānāt kṣobhyamāṇācca tathā puṃsaḥ purātanāt ।
prādurāsīnmahad bījaṃ pradhānapuruṣātmakam ।। mahānātmā matirbrahmā prabuddhiḥ khyātirīśvaraḥ । prajñādhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ saṃvidetasmāditi tat smṛtam ।। vaikārikastaijasaśca bhūtādiścaiva tāmasaḥ ।
trividho ayamahaṅkāro mahataḥ saṃbabhūva ha ।। ahaṅkāro abimānaśca kartā mantā ca sa smṛtaḥ । ātmā ca pudgalo jīvo yataḥ sarvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ ।। pañcabhūtānyahaṅkārāt tanmātrāṇi ca jajñire ।
indriyāṇi tathā devāḥ sarvaṃ tasyātmajaṃ jagat ।। manastvavyaktajaṃ proktaṃ vikāraḥ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ । yenāsau jāyate kartā bhūtādīṃścānupaśyati ।। vaikārikādahaṅkārāt sargo vaikāriko abhavat ।
taijasānīndriyāṇi syurdevā vaikārikā daśa ।। ekādaśaṃ manastatra svaguṇenobhayātmakam । bhūtatanmātrasargo ayaṃ bhūtāderabhavan prajāḥ ।। bhūtādistu vikurvāṇaḥ śabdamātraṃ sasarja ha ।
ākāśaṃ śuṣiraṃ tasmādutpannaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam ।। ākāśastu vikurvāṇaḥ sparśamātraṃ sasarja ha । vāyurutpadyate tasmāt tasya sparśo guṇo mataḥ ।। vāyuścāpi vikurvāṇo rūpamātraṃ sasarja ha ।
jyotirutpadyate vāyostadrūpaguṇamucyate ।। jyotiścāpi vikurvāṇaṃ rasamātraṃ sasarja ha । saṃbhavanti tato ambhāṃsi rasādhārāṇi tāni tu ।। āpaścāpi vikurvantyo gandhamātraṃ sasarjire ।
saṃghāto jāyate tasmāt tasya gandho guṇo mataḥ ।। ākāśaṃ śabdamātraṃ yat sparśamātraṃ samāvṛṇot । dviguṇastu tato vāyuḥ śabdasparśātmako abhavat ।। rūpaṃ tathaivāviśataḥ śabdasparśau guṇāvubhau ।
triguṇaḥ syāt tato vahniḥ sa śabdasparśarūpavān ।। śabda sparśaśca rūpaṃ ca rasamātraṃ samāviśan । tasmāccaturguṇā āpo vijñeyāstu rasātmikāḥ ।। śabdaḥ sparśaśca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaṃ samāviśan ।
tasamāt pañcaguṇā bhūmiḥ sthūlā bhūteṣu śabdyate ।। śāntā ghorāśca mūḍhāśca viśeṣāstena te smṛtāḥ । parasparānupraveśād dhārayanti parasparam ।। ete sapta mahātmāno hyanyonyasya samāśrayāt ।
nāśaknuvan prajāḥ straṣṭumasamāgamya kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। puruṣādhiṣṭhitātvācca avyaktānugraheṇa ca । mahādādayo viśeṣāntā hmaṇḍamutpādayanti te ।। ekakālasamutpannaṃ jalabudbudavacca tat ।
viśeṣebhyo aṇḍamabhavad bṛhat tadudakeśayam ।। tasmin kāryasya karaṇaṃ saṃsiddhiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ । prākṛte aṇḍe vivṛttaḥ sa kṣetrajño brahmasaṃjñitaḥ ।। sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣa ucyate ।
ādikartā sa bhūtānāṃ brahmāgre samavartata ।। yamāhuḥ puruṣaṃ haṃsaṃ pradhānāt parataḥ sthitam । hiraṇyagarbhaṃ kapilaṃ chandomūrti sanātanam ।। merurulbamabhūt tasya jarāyuścāpi parvatāḥ ।
garbhodakaṃ samudrāśca tasyāsan paramātmanaḥ ।। tasminnaṇḍe abhavad viśvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam । candrādityau sanakṣatrau sagrahau saha vāyunā ।। adbhirdaśaguṇābhiśca bāhyato aṇḍaṃ samāvṛtam ।
āpo daśaguṇenaiva tejasā bāhyato vṛtāḥ ।। tejo daśaguṇenaiva bāhyato vāyunāvṛtam । ākāśenāvṛto vāyuḥ khaṃ tu bhūtādināvṛtam ।। bhūtādirmahatā tadvadavyaktenāvṛto mahān ।
ete lokā mahātmanaḥ sarvatattvābhimāninaḥ ।। vasanti tatra puruṣāstadātmāno vyavasthitāḥ । īśvarā yogadharmāṇo ye cānye tattvacintakāḥ ।। sarvajñāḥ śāntarajaso nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ ।
etairāvaraṇairaṇḍaṃ saptabhiḥ prākṛtairvṛtam ।। etāvacchakyate vaktuṃ māyaiṣā gahanā dvijāḥ । etat prādhānikaṃ kāryaṃ yanmayā bījamīritam । prajāpateḥ parā mūrtiritīyaṃ vaidikī śrutiḥ ।।
brahmāṇḍametat sakalaṃ saptalokatalānvitam । dvitīyaṃ tasya devasya śarīraṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। hiraṇyagarbho bhagavān brahmā vai kanakāṇḍajaḥ । tṛtīyaṃ bhagavadrūpaṃ prāhurvedārthavedinaḥ ।।
rajoguṇamayaṃ cānyad rūpaṃ tasyaiva dhīmataḥ । caturmukhaḥ sa bhagavān jagatsṛṣṭau pravartate ।। sṛṣṭaṃ ca pāti sakalaṃ viśvātmā viśvatomukhaḥ । sattvaṃ guṇamupāśritya viṣṇurviśveśvaraḥ svayam ।।
antakāle svayaṃ devaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ । tamoguṇaṃ samāśritya rudraḥ saṃharate jagat ।। eko api sanmahādevastridhāsau samavasthitaḥ । sargarakṣālayaguṇairnirguṇo api nirañjanaḥ ।
ekadhā sa dvidhā caiva tridhā ca bahudhā punaḥ ।। yogeśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikaroti ca । nānākṛtikriyārūpanāmavanti svalīlayā ।। hitāya caiva bhaktānāṃ sa eva grasate punaḥ ।
tridhā vibhajya cātmānaṃ traikālye saṃpravartate । sṛjate grasate caiva vīkṣate ca viśeṣataḥ ।। yasmāt sṛṣṭvānugṛhṇāti grasate ca punaḥ prajāḥ । guṇātmakatvāt traikālye tasmādekaḥ sa ucyate ।।
agre hiraṇyagarbhaḥ sa prādurbhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ । āditvādādidevo asau ajātatvādajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pātiyasmāt prajāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpatiriti smṛtaḥ । deveṣu ca mahādevo māhadeva iti smṛtaḥ ।।
bṛhattvācca smṛto brahmā paratvāt parameśvaraḥ । vaśitvādapyavaśyatvādīśvaraḥ paribhāṣitaḥ ।। ṛṣiḥ sarvatragatvena hariḥ sarvaharo yataḥ । anutpādācca pūrvatvāt svayaṃbhūriti sa smṛtaḥ ।।
narāṇāmayano yasmāt tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ । haraḥ saṃsāraharaṇād vibhutvād viṣṇurucyate ।। bhagavān sarvavijñānādavanādomiti smṛtaḥ । sarvajñaḥ sarvavijñānāt sarvaḥ sarvamayo yataḥ ।।
śivaḥ sa nirmalo yasmād vibhuḥ sarvagato yataḥ । tāraṇāt sarvaduḥ khānāṃ tārakaḥ parigīyate ।। bahunātra kimuktena sarvaṃ brahmamayaṃ jagat । anekabhedabhinnastu krīḍate parameśvaraḥ ।।
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃkṣepāt kathito mayā । abuddhipūrvako viprā brāhmīṃ sṛṣṭiṃ nibodhata ।। svayaṃbhuvo vivṛttasya kālasaṃkhyā dvijottamāḥ । na śakyate samākhyātuṃ bahuvarṣairapi svayam ।।
kālasaṃkhyā samāsena parārdhadvayakalpitā । sa eva syāt paraḥ kālaḥ tadante pratisṛjyate ।। nijena tasya mānena āyurvarṣaśataṃ smṛtam । tat parākhyaṃ tadardhaṃ ca parārdhamabhidīyate ।।
kāṣṭhā pañcadaśa khyātā nimeṣā dvijasattamāḥ । kāṣṭhāstriṃśat kalā triṃśat kalā mauhūrtikī gatiḥ ।। tāvatsaṃkhyairahorātraṃ muhūrtairmānuṣaṃ smṛtam । ahorātrāṇi tāvanti māsaḥ pakṣadvayātmakaḥ ।।
taiḥ ṣaḍbhirayanaṃ varṣaṃ dve ayane dakṣiṇottare । ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ rātrirdevānāmuttaraṃ dinam ।। divyairvarṣasahastraistu kṛtatretādisaṃjñitam । caturyugaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ tadvibhāgaṃ nibodhata ।।
catvāryāhuḥ sahastrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tatkṛtaṃ yugam । tasya tāvacchatī sandhyā sandhyāṃśaśca kṛtasya tu ।। triśatī dviśatī sandhyā tathā caikaśatī kramāt । aṃśakaṃ ṣaṭśataṃ tasmāt kṛsandhyāṃśakaṃ vinā ।।
tridvyekasāhastramato vinā sandhyāṃśakena tu । tretādvāparatiṣyāṇāṃ kālajñāne prakīrtitam ।। etad dvādaśasāhastraṃ sādhikaṃ parikalpitam । tadekasaptatiguṇaṃ manorantaramucyate ।।
brahmaṇo divase viprā manavaḥ syuścaturdaśa । svāyaṃbhuvādayaḥ sarve tataḥ sāvarṇikādayaḥ ।। tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā saparvatā । pūrṇaṃ yugasahastraṃ vai paripālyā nareśvaraiḥ ।।
manvantareṇa caikena sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi vai । vyākhyātāni na saṃdehaḥ kalpaṃ kalpena caiva hi ।। brāhmamekamahaḥ kalpastāvatī rātririṣyate । caturyugasahastraṃ tu kalpamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।।
trīṇi kalpaśatāni syuḥ tathā ṣaṣṭirdvijottamāḥ । brahmaṇaḥ kathitaṃ varṣaṃ parākhyaṃ tacchataṃ viduḥ ।। tasyānte sarvatattvānāṃ svahetau prakṛtau layaḥ । tenāyaṃ procyate sadbhiḥ prākṛtaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ ।।
brahmanārāyaṇeśānāṃ trayāṇāṃ prakṛtau layaḥ । procyate kālayogena punareva ca saṃbhavaḥ ।। evaṃ brahmā ca bhūtāni vāsudevo api śaṅkaraḥ । kālenaiva tu sṛjyante sa eva grasate punaḥ ।।
anādireṣa bhagavān kālo ananto ajaro amaraḥ । sarvagatvāt svatantratvāt sarvātmāsau maheśvaraḥ ।। brahmāṇo bahavo rudrā hyanye nārāyaṇādayaḥ । eko hi bhagavānīśaḥ kālaḥ kaviriti śruti ।।
ekamatra vyatītaṃ tu parārdhaṃ brahmaṇo dvijāḥ । sāṃprataṃ vartate tadvat tasya kalpo ayamaṣṭamaḥ ।। yo atītaḥ saptamaḥ kalpaḥ pādma ityucyate budhaiḥ । vārāho vartate kalpaḥ tasya vakṣyāmi vistaram ।।
āsīdekārṇavaṃ ghoramavibhāgaṃ tamomayam । śāntavātādikaṃ sarvaṃ na prajñāyata kiñcana ।। ekārṇave tadā tasmin naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame । tadā samabhavad brahmā sahastrākṣaḥ sahastrapāt ।।
sahastraśīrṣā puruṣo rukmavarṇastvatīndriyaḥ । brahmā nārāyaṇākhyastu suṣvāpa salile tadā ।। imaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati । brahmasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam ।।
āpo nārā iti proktā nāmnā pūrvamiti śrutiḥ । ayanaṃ tasya tā yasmāt tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tulyaṃ yugasahastrasya naiśaṃ kālamupāsya saḥ । śarvaryante prakurute brahmatvaṃ sargakāraṇāt ।।
tatastu salile tasmin vijñāyāntargatāṃ mahīm । anumānāt taduddhāraṃ kartukāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। jalakrīḍāsu ruciraṃ vārāhaṃ rupamāsthitaḥ । adhṛṣyaṃ manasāpyanyairvāṅmayaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam ।।
pṛthivyuddharaṇārthāya praviśya ca rasātalam । daṃṣṭrayābhyujjahāraināmātmādhāro dharādharaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā daṃṣṭrāgravinyastāṃ pṛthivīṃ prathitapauruṣam । astuvañjanalokasthāḥ siddhā brahmarṣayo harim ।।
namaste devadevāya brahmaṇe parameṣṭhine । puruṣāya purāṇāya śāśvatāya jayāya ca ।। namaḥ svayaṃbhuve tubhyaṃ straṣṭre sarvārthavedine । namo hiraṇyagarbhāya vedhase paramātmane ।।
namaste vāsudevāya viṣṇave viśvayonaye । nārāyaṇāya devāya devānāṃ hitakāriṇe ।। namo astu te caturvaktre śārṅgacakrāsidhāriṇe । sarvabhūtātmabhūtāya kūṭasthāya namo namaḥ ।।
namo vedarahasyāya namaste vedayonaye । namo buddhāya śuddhāya namaste jñānarūpiṇe ।। namo astvānandarūpāya sākṣiṇe jagatāṃ namaḥ । anantāyāprameyāya kāryāya karaṇāya ca ।।
namaste pañcabūtāya pañcabhūtātmane namaḥ । namo mūlaprakṛtaye māyārūpāya te namaḥ ।। namo astu te varāhāya namaste matsyarūpiṇe । namo yogādhigamyāya namaḥ sakarṣaṇāya te ।।
namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ tridhāmne divyatejase । namaḥ siddhāya pūjyāya guṇatrayavibhāvine ।। tamo astvādityavarṇāya namaste padmayonaye । namo amūrtāya mūrtāya mādhavāya namo namaḥ ।।
tvayaiva sṛṣṭamakhilaṃ tvayyeva layameṣyati । pālayaitajjagat sarvaṃ trātā tvaṃ śaraṇaṃ gati ।। itthaṃ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sanakādyairabhiṣṭutaḥ । prasādamakarot teṣāṃ varāhavapurīśvaraḥ ।।
tataḥ saṃsthānamānīya pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ । mumoca rūpaṃ manasā dhārayitvā prijāpatiḥ ।। tasyopari jalaughasya mahatī nauriva sthitā । vitatatvācca dehasya na mahī yāti saṃplavam ।।
pṛthivīṃ tu samīkṛtya pṛthivyāṃ so acinod girīn । prāksargadagdhānakhilāṃstataḥ sarge adadhanmanaḥ ।। sṛṣṭiṃ cintayatastasya kalpādiṣu yathā purā । abuddhipūrvakaḥ sargaḥ prādurbhūtastamomayaḥ ।।
tamo moho mahāmohastāmistraścāndhasaṃjñitaḥ । avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ ।। pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyataḥ so abhimāninaḥ । saṃvṛtastamasā caiva bījakambhuvanāvṛtaḥ ।।
varhirantaścāprakāśaḥ stabdho niḥ saṃjña eva ca । mukyā nagā iti proktā mukhyasargastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvāsādhakaṃ sargamamanyadaparaṃ prabhuḥ । tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargastiryakstroto abhyavartata ।।
yasmāt tiryak pravṛttaḥ sa tiryakstrotastataḥ smṛtaḥ । paśvādayaste vikhyātā utpathagrāhiṇo dvijāḥ ।। tamapyasādhakaṃ jñātvā sargamanyaṃ sasarja ha । ūrdhvastrota iti prokto devasargastu sāttvikaḥ ।।
te sukhapratibahulā bahirantaśca nāvṛtāḥ । prakāśā bahirantaśca svabhāvād devasaṃjñitāḥ ।। tato abidhāyāyatastasya satyābhidhyāyinastadā । prādurāsīt tadāvyaktādarvākstrotastu sādhakaḥ ।।
te ca prakāśabahulāstamodriktā rajodhikāḥ । duḥ khotkaṭāḥ sattvayutā manuṣyāḥ parikīrtitā ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā cāparaṃ sargamamanyad bhagavānajaḥ । tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ sargo bhūtādiko abhavat ।।
te aparigrāhiṇaḥ sarve saṃvibhāgaratāḥ punaḥ । khādanāścāpyaśīlāśca bhūtādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ । ityete pañca kathitāḥ sargā vai dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।। prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇastu saḥ ।
tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargo hi sa smṛtaḥ ।। vaikārikastṛtīyastu sarga aindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ । ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūto abuddhipūrvakaḥ ।। mukhyasargaścaturthastu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
tiryakstrotastu yaḥ proktastiryagyonyaḥ sa pañcamaḥ ।। tathordhvastrotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ । tator'vākstrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ ।। aṣṭamo bhautikaḥ sargo bhūtādīnāṃ prakīrtitaḥ ।
navamaścaiva kaumāraḥ prākṛtā vaikṛtāstvime ।। prākṛtāstu trayaḥ pūrve sargāste abuddhipūrvakāḥ । buddhipūrvaṃ pravartante mukhyādyā munipuṅgavāḥ ।। agre sasarja vai brahmā mānasānātmanaḥ samān ।
sanakaṃ sanātanaṃ caiva tathaiva ca sanandanam । ṛbhuṃ sanātkumāraṃ ca pūrvameva prajāpatiḥ ।। pañcaite yogino viprāḥ paraṃ vairāgyamāsthitāḥ । īśvarāsaktamanaso na sṛṣṭau dadhire matim ।।
teṣvevaṃ nirapekṣeṣu lokasṛṣṭau prajāpatiḥ । mumoha māyayā sadyo māyinaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। taṃ bodhayāmāsa sutaṃ jaganmāyo mahāmuniḥ । nārāyaṇo mahāyogī yogicittānurañjanaḥ ।।
bodhitastena viśvātmā tatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ । sa tapyamāno bhagavān na kiñcit pratipadyata ।। tato dīrgheṇa kālena dukhāt krodho vyajāyata । krodhāviṣṭasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatannaśru bindavaḥ ।।
bhrukuṭīkuṭilāt tasya lalāṭāt parameśvaraḥ । samutpanno mahādevaḥ śaraṇyo nīlalohitaḥ ।। sa eva bhagavānīśastejorāśiḥ sanātanaḥ । yaṃ prapaśyanti vidvāṃsaḥ svātmasthaṃ parameśvaram ।।
oṅkāraṃ samanusmṛtya praṇamya ca kṛtāñjaliḥ । tāma bhagavān brahmā sṛjemā vividhāḥ prajāḥ ।। niśamya bhagavān vākyaṃ śaṅkaro dharmavāhanaḥ । svātmanā sadśān rudrān sasarja manasā śivaḥ ।
kapardino nirātaṅkāṃstrinetrān nīlalohitān ।। taṃ prāha bhagavān brahmā janmamṛtyuyutāḥ prajāḥ । sṛjeti so abravīdīśo nāhaṃ mṛtyujarānvitāḥ । prajāḥ strakṣye jagannātha sṛja tvamaśubhāḥ prajāḥ ।।
nivārya ca tadā rudraṃ sasarja kamalodbhavaḥ । sthānābhimāninaḥ sarvān gadatastān nibodhata ।। apo agnirantarikṣaṃ ca dyaurvāyuḥ pṛthivī tathā । nadyaḥ samudrāḥ śailāśca vṛkṣā vīrudha eva ca ।।
lavāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kalāścaiva muhūrtā divasāḥ kṣapāḥ । ardhamāsāśca māsāśca ayanābdayugādayaḥ ।। sthānābimāninaḥ sṛṣṭvā sādhakānasṛjat punaḥ । marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ।
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca dharmaṃ saṃkalpameva ca ।। prāṇād brahmāsṛjad dakṣaṃ cakṣuṣaśca marīcinam । śiraso aṅgirasaṃ devo hṛdayād bhṛgumeva ca ।। śrotrābhyāmatrināmānaṃ dharmaṃ ca vyavasāyataḥ ।
saṃkalpaṃ caiva saṃkalpāt sarvalokapitāmahaḥ ।। pulastyaṃ ca tathodānād vyanācca pulahaṃ munim । apānāt kratumavyagraṃ samānācca vasiṣṭhakam ।। ityete brahmaṇā sṛṣṭāḥ sādhakā gṛhamedhinaḥ ।
āsthāya mānavaṃ rūpaṃ dharmastaiḥ saṃpravartitaḥ ।। tato devāsurapitṛn manuṣyāṃśca catuṣṭayam । sisṛkṣurambhāṃsyetāni svamātmānamayūyujat ।। yuktātmanastamomātrā udriktābhūt prajāpateḥ ।
tato asya jaghanāt pūrvamasurā jajñire sutāḥ ।। utsasarjāsurān sṛṣṭvā tāṃ tanuṃ puruṣottamaḥ । sā cotsṛṣṭā tanustena sadyo rātrirajāyata । sā tamobahulā yasmāt prajāstasyāṃsvapantyataḥ ।।
sattvamātratmikāṃ devastanumanyāmagṛhṇata । tato asya mukhato devā dīvyataḥ saṃprajajñire ।। tyaktā sāpi tanustena sattvaprāyamabhūd dinam । tasmādaho dharmayuktā devatāḥ samupāsate ।।
sattvamātrātmikāmeva tato anyāṃ jagṛhe tanum । pitṛvanmanyamānasya pitaraḥ saṃprajajñire ।। utsasarja pitṛn sṛṣṭvā tatastāmapi viśvasṛk । sāpaviddhā tanustena sadyaḥ sandhyā vyajāyata ।।
tasmādahardevatānāṃ rātriḥ syād devavidviṣām । tayormadhye pitṝṇāṃ tu mūrtiḥ sandhyā garīyasī ।। tasmād devāsurāḥ sarve manavo mānavāstathā । upāsate tadā yuktā rātryahnormadhyamāṃ tanum ।।
rajomātrātmikāṃ brahmā tanumanyāmagṛhṇata । tato asya jajñire putrā manuṣyā rajasāvṛtāḥ ।। tāmapyāśu sa tatyāja tanuṃ sadyaḥ prajāpatiḥ । jyotstrā sā cābhavadviprāḥ prāksandhyā yābidhīyate ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān brahmā saṃprāpya dvijapuṅgavāḥ । mūrti tamorajaḥ prāyāṃ punarevābhyayūyujat ।। andhakāre kṣudhāviṣṭā rākṣasāstasya jajñire । putrāstamorajaḥ prāyā balinaste niśācarāḥ ।।
sarpā yakṣāstathā būtā gandharvāḥ saṃprajajñire । rajastamobhyāmāviṣṭāṃstato anyānasṛjat prabhuḥ ।। vayāṃsi vayasaḥ sṛṣṭvā avayo vakṣaso asṛjat । mukhato ajān sasarjānyān udarādgāścanirmame ।।
padbhyāñcāśvān samātaṅgān rāsabhān gavayān mṛgān । uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva nyaṅkūnanyāṃśva jātayaḥ । aupadhyaḥ phalamūlinyo romabhyastasya jajñire ।। gāyatraṃ ca ṛcaṃ caiva trivṛtsāma rathantaram ।
agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamānmukhāt ।। yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ chandaḥ stomaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tathā । bṛhatsāma tathokthaṃ ca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmukhāt ।। sāmāni jāgataṃ chandastomaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā ।
vairūpamatirātraṃ ca paścimādasṛjanmukhāt ।। ekaviśamatharvāṇamāptoryāmāṇameva ca । anuṣṭubhaṃ savairājamuttarādasṛjanmukhāt ।। uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastasya jajñire ।
brahmaṇo hi prajāsargaṃ sṛjatastu prajāpateḥ ।। sṛṣṭvā catuṣṭayaṃ sargaṃ devarṣipitṛmānuṣam । tato asṛjacca bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। yakṣān piśācān gandharvāṃstathaivāpsarasaḥ śubhāḥ ।
narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥ puśumṛgoragān । avyayaṃ ca vyayaṃ caiva dvayaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। teṣāṃ ye yāni karmāṇi prāksṛṣṭau pratipedire । tānyeva te prapadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
hiṃstrāhiṃstre mṛdukrūre dharmādharmāvṛtānṛte । tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāt tat tasya rocate ।। mahābhūteṣu nānātvamindriyārtheṣu mūrtiṣu । viniyogaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ dhātaiva vidadhāt svayam ।।
nāmarūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ kṛtyānāṃ ca prapañcanam । vedaśabdebhya evādau nirmame sa maheśvaraḥ ।। ārṣāṇi caiva nāmāni yāśca vedeṣu dṛṣṭayaḥ । śarvaryante prasūtānāṃ tānyevaibhyo dadātyajaḥ ।।
yathartāvṛtuliṅgāni nānārūpāṇi paryaye । dṛśyante tāni tānyeva tathā bhāvā yugādiṣu ।। evaṃ bhūtāni sṛṣṭāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca । yadā cāsya prajāḥ sṛṣṭā na vyavardhanta dhīmataḥ ।।
tamomātrāvṛto brahmā tadāśocata duḥ khitaḥ । tataḥ sa vidadhe buddhimarthaniścayagāminīm ।। athātmani samadrākṣīt tamomātrāṃ niyāmikām । rajaḥ sattvaṃ ca saṃvṛtya vartamānāṃ svadharmataḥ ।।
tamastad vyanudat paścāt rajaḥ sattvena saṃyutaḥ । tat tamaḥ pratinunnaṃ vai mithunaṃ samajāyata ।। adharmācaraṇo viprā hiṃsā cāśubhalakṣaṇā । svāṃ tanuṃ sa tato brahmā tāmapohata bhāsvarām ।।
dvidhākarot punardehamardhena puruṣo abhavat । ardhena nārī puruṣo virājamasṛjat prabhuḥ ।। nārīṃ ca śatarūpākhyāṃ yoginīṃ sasṛje śubhām । sā divaṃ pṛthivīṃ caiva mahamnā vyāpya saṃsthitā ।।
yogaiśvaryabalopetā jñānavijñānasaṃyutā । yo abhavat puruṣāt putro virāḍavyaktajanmanaḥ ।। svāyaṃbhuvo manurdevaḥ so abhavat puruṣo muniḥ । sā devī śatarūpākhyā tapaḥ kṛtvā suduścaram ।।
bhartāraṃ brahmaṇaḥ putraṃ manumevānupadyata । tasmācca śatarūpā sā putradvayamasūyata ।। priyavratottānapādau kanyādvayamanuttamam । tayoḥ prasūtiṃ dakṣāya manuḥ kanyāṃ dadau punaḥ ।।
prajāpatirathākūtiṃ mānaso jagṛhe ruciḥ । ākūtyāṃ mithunaṃ jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham । yajñaśca dakṣiṇā caiva yābhyāṃ saṃvardhitaṃ jagat ।। yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ tu putrā dvādaśa jajñire ।
yāmā iti samākyatā devāḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare ।। prasūtyāṃ ca tathā dakṣaścatastro viṃśatiṃ tathā । sasarja kanyā nāmāni tāsāṃ samyam nibodhata ।। śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtistuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirmedhā kriyā tathā ।
buddhirlajjāvapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtistrayodaśī ।। patnyarthaṃ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ śubhāḥ । tābhyaḥ śiṣṭā yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ ।। khyātiḥ satyatha saṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā ।
saṃtatiścānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā ।। bhṛgurbhavo marīciśca tathā caivāṅgirā muniḥ । pulastyaḥ pulahaścaiva kratuḥ paramadharmavit ।। atrirvasiṣṭho vahniśca pitaraśca yathākramam ।
khyātyādyā jagṛhuḥ kanyā munayo munisattamāḥ ।। śraddhāyā ātmajaḥ kāmo darpo lakṣmīsutaḥ smṛtaḥ । dhṛtyāstu niyamaḥ putrastuṣṭyāḥ saṃtoṣa ucyate ।। puṣṭyā lābhaḥ sutaścāpi medhāputraḥ śrutastathā ।
kriyāyāścābhavat putro daṇḍaḥ samaya eva ca ।। buddhyā bodhaḥ sutastadvadapramādo vyajāyata । lajjāyā vinayaḥ putro vapuṣo vyavasāyakaḥ ।। kṣemaḥ śāntisutaścāpi sukhaṃ siddhirajāyata ।
yaśaḥ kīrtisutastadvadityete dharmasūnavaḥ ।। kāmasya harṣaḥ putro abhūd devānando vyajāyata । ityeṣa vai sukhodarkaḥ sargo dharmasya kīrtitaḥ ।। jajñe hiṃsā tvadharmād vai nikṛtiṃ cānṛtaṃ sutam ।
nikṛtyanṛtayorjajñe bhayaṃ naraka eva ca ।। māyā ca vedanā caiva mithunaṃ tvidametayoḥ । bhayājjajñe atha vai māyā mṛtyuṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam ।। vedanā ca sutaṃ cāpi duḥ khaṃ jajñe atha rauravāt ।
mṛtyorvyādhijarāśokatṛṣṇākrodhāśca jajñire ।। duḥ khottarāḥ smṛtā hyete sarve cādharmalakṣaṇāḥ । naiṣāṃ bhāryāsti putro vā sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ ।। ityeṣa tāmasaḥ sargo jajñe dharmaniyāmakaḥ ।
saṃkṣepeṇa mayā proktā visṛṣṭirmunipuṅgavā ।। etacchrutvā tu vacanaṃ nāradādyā maharṣayaḥ । praṇamya varadaṃ viṣṇuṃ papracchuḥ saṃśayānvitā ।। kathito bhavatā sargo mukhyādīnāṃ janārdana ।
idānīṃ saṃśayaṃ cemamasmākaṃ chettumarhasi ।। kathaṃ sa bhagavānīśaḥ pūrvajo api pinākadhṛk । putratvamagacchaṃbhurbrahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। kathaṃ ca bhagavāñjajñe brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
aṇḍajo jagatāmīśastanno vaktumihārhasi ।। śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve śaṅkarasyāmitaujasaḥ । putratvaṃ brahmaṇastasya padmayonitvameva ca ।। atītakalpāvasāne tamobhūtaṃ jagat trayam ।
āsīdekārṇavaṃ sarvaṃ na devādyā na carṣayaḥ ।। tatra nārāyaṇo devo nirjane nirupaplave । āśritya śeṣaśayanaṃ suṣvāpa puruṣottamaḥ ।। sahastraśīrṣā bhūtvā sa sahastrākṣaḥ sahastrapāt ।
sahastrabāhuḥ sarvajñaścintyamāno manīṣibhiḥ ।। pītavāsā viśālākṣo nīlajimūtasannibhaḥ । mahāvibhūtiryogātmā yogināṃ hṛdayālayaḥ ।। kadācit tasya suptasya līlārthaṃ divyamadbhutam ।
trailokyasāraṃ vimalaṃ nābhyāṃ paṅkajamudvabhau ।। śatayojanavistīrṇaṃ taruṇādityasannibham । divyagandhamayaṃ puṇyaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam ।। tasyaivaṃ suciraṃ kālaṃ vartamānasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।
hiraṇyagarbho bhagavāṃstaṃ deśamupacakrame ।। sa taṃ kareṇa viśvātmā samutthāpya sanātanam । provāca madhuraṃ vākyaṃ māyayā tasya mohitaḥ ।। asminnekārṇave ghore nirjane tamasāvṛte ।
ekākī ko bhavāñchete brūhi me puruṣarṣabha ।। tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vihasya garuḍadhvajaḥ । uvāca devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ meghagambhīraniḥ svanaḥ ।। bho bho nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ lokānāṃ prabhavāpyayam ।
mahāyogeśvaraṃ māṃ tvaṃ jānīhi puruṣottamam ।। mayi paśya jagat kṛtsnaṃ tvāṃ ca lokapitāmaham । saparvatamahādvīpaṃ samudraiḥ saptabhirvṛtam ।। evamābhāṣya viścātmā provāca puruṣaṃ hariḥ ।
jānannapi mahāyogī ko bhavāniti vedhasam ।। tataḥ prahasya bhagavān brahmā vedanidhiḥ prabhuḥ । pratyuvācāmbujābhākṣaṃ sasmitaṃ ślakṣṇayā girā ।। ahaṃ dhātā vidhātā ca svayaṃbhūḥ prapitāmahaḥ ।
mayyeva saṃsthitaṃ viśvaṃ brahmāhaṃ viśvatomukhaḥ ।। śrutvā vācaṃ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ satyaparākramaḥ । anujñāpyātha yogena praviṣṭo brahmaṇastanum ।। tralokyametat sakalaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।
udare tasya devasya dṛṣṭvā vismayamāgataḥ ।। tadāsya vaktrānniṣkramya pannagendraniketanaḥ । ajātaśatrurbhagavān pitāmahamathābravīt ।। bhavānapyevamevādya śāśvataṃ hi mamoharam ।
praviśya lokān paśyaitān vicitrān puruṣarṣabha ।। tataḥ prahlādanīṃ vāṇī śrutvā tasyābhinandya ca । śrīpaterudaraṃ bhūyaḥ praviveśa kuśadhvajaḥ ।। tāneva lokān garbhasthānapaśyat satyavikramaḥ ।
paryaṭitvā tu devasya dadṛśe antaṃ na vai hareḥ ।। tato dvārāṇi sarvāṇi pihitāni mahātmanā । janārdanena brahmāsau nābhyāṃ dvāramavindata ।। tatra yogabalenāsau praviśya kanakāṇḍajaḥ ।
ujjahārātmano rūpaṃ puṣkarāccaturānanaḥ ।। virarājāravindasthaḥ padmagarbhasamadyutiḥ । brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavān jagadyoniḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। samanyamāno viśveśamātmānaṃ paramaṃ padam ।
provāca puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ meghagambhīrayā girā ।। kiṃ kṛtaṃ bhavatedānīmātmano jayakāṅkṣayā । eko ahaṃ prabalo nānyo māṃ vai ko abibhaviṣyati ।। śrutvā nārāyaṇo vākyaṃ brahmaṇo lokatantriṇaḥ ।
sāntvapūrvamidaṃ vākyaṃ babhāṣe madhuraṃ hariḥ ।। bhavān dhātā vidhātā ca svayaṃbhūḥ prapitāmahaḥ । na mātsaryābhiyogena dvārāṇi pihitāni me ।। kintu līlārthamevaitanna tvāṃ bādhitumicchayā ।
ko hi bādhitumanvicched devadevaṃ pitāmaham ।। na te anyathāvagantavyaṃ mānyo me sarvathā bhavān । sarvamanvaya kalyāṇaṃ yanmayāpahṛtaṃ tava ।। asmācca kāraṇād brahman putro bhavatu me bhavān ।
padmayoniriti khyāto matpriyārthaṃ jaganmaya ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān devo varaṃ dattvā kirīṭine । praharṣamatulaṃ gatvā punarviṣṇumabhāṣata ।। bhavān sarvātmako anantaḥ sarveṣāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।
sarvabhūtāntarātmā vai paraṃ bahma sanātanam ।। ahaṃ vai sarvalokānāmātmā lokamaheśvaraḥ । manmayaṃ sarvamevedaṃ brahmāhaṃ puruṣaḥ paraḥ ।। nāvābhyāṃ vidyate hyanyo lokānāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।
ekā mūrtirdvidhā bhinnā nārāyaṇapitāmahau ।। tenaivamukto brahmāṇaṃ vāsudevo abravīdidam । iyaṃ pratijñā bhavato vināśāya bhaviṣyati ।। kiṃ na paśyasi yogeśaṃ brahmādhipatimavyayam ।
pradhānapuruṣeśānaṃ vedāhaṃ parameśvaram ।। yaṃ na paśyanti yogīndrāḥ sāṃkhyā api maheśvaram । anādinidhanaṃ brahma tameva śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। tataḥ kruddho ambujābhākṣaṃ brahmā provāca keśavam ।
bhavān na nūnamātmānaṃ vetti tat paramakṣaram ।। brahmāṇaṃ jagatāmekamātmānaṃ paramaṃ padam । nāvābhyāṃ vidyate hyanyo lokānāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। saṃtyajya nidrāṃ vipulāṃ svamātmānaṃ vilokaya ।
tasya tat krodhajaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā viṣṇurabhāṣata ।। mā maivaṃ vada kalyāṇa parivādaṃ mahātmanaḥ । na me astyaviditaṃ brahman nānyathāhaṃ vadāmite ।। kintu mohayati brahman bhavantaṃ pārameśvarī ।
māyāśeṣaviśeṣāṇāṃ heturātmasamudbhāvā ।। etāvaduktvā bhagavān viṣṇustūṣṇīṃ babhūva ha । jñātvā tat paramaṃ tattvaṃ svamātmānaṃ maheśvaram ।। kuto apyaparimeyātmā bhūtānāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।
prasādaṃ brahmaṇe kartuṃ prādurāsīt tato haraḥ ।। lalāṭanayano ananto jaṭāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitaḥ । triśūlapāṇirbhagavāṃstejasāṃ paramo nidhiḥ ।। divyāṃ viśālāṃ grathitāṃ grahaiḥ sārkendutārakaiḥ ।
mālāmatyadbhutākārāṃ dhārayan pādalambinīm ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā devamīśānaṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । mohito māyayātyarthaṃ pītavāsasamabvīt ।। ka eṣa puruṣo anantaḥ śūlapāṇistrilocanaḥ ।
tejorāśirameyātmā samāyāti janārdana ।। tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā viṣṇurdānavamardanaḥ । apaśyadīśvaraṃ devaṃ jvalantaṃ vimale ambhasi ।। jñātvā tatparamaṃ bhāvamaiśvaraṃ brahmabhāvanam ।
provācotthāya bhagavān devadevaṃ pitāmaham ।। ayaṃ devo mahādevaḥ svayañjyotiḥ sanātanaḥ । anādinidhano acintyo lokānāmīśvaro mahān ।। śaṅkaraḥ śaṃbhurīśānaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ ।
bhūtānāmadhipo yogī maheśo vimalaḥ śivaḥ ।। eṣa dhātā vidhātā ca pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ । yaṃ prapaśyanti yatayo brahmabhāvena bhāvitāḥ ।। sṛjatyeṣa jagat kṛtsnaṃ pāti saṃharate tathā ।
kālo bhūtvā mahādevaḥ kevalo niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ ।। brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe pūrvaṃ bhavantaṃ yaḥ sanātanaḥ । vedāṃśca pradadau tubhyaṃ so ayamāyāti śaṅkaraḥ ।। asyaiva cāparāṃ mūrti viśvayoniṃ sanātanīm ।
vāsudevābhidhānāṃ māmavehi prapitāmaha ।। kiṃ na paśyasi yogeśaṃ brahmādhipatimavyayam । divyaṃ bhavatu te cakṣuryena drakṣyasi tatparam ।। labdhvā śaivaṃ tadā cakṣurviṣṇorlokapitāmahaḥ ।
bubudhe parameśānaṃ purataḥ samavasthitam ।। sa labdhvā paramaṃ jñānamaiśvaraṃ prapitāmahaḥ । prapede śaraṇaṃ devaṃ tameva pitaraṃ śivam ।। oṅkāraṃ samanusmṛtya saṃstabhyātmānamātmanā ।
atharvaśirasā devaṃ tuṣṭāva ca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। saṃstutastena bhagavān brahmaṇā parameśvaraḥ । avāpa paramāṃ prītiṃ vyājahāra smayanniva ।। matsamastvaṃ na saṃdeho madbhaktaśca yato bhavān ।
mayaivotpāditaḥ pūrvaṃ lokasṛṣṭyarthamavyayam ।। tvamātmā hyādipuruṣo mama dehasamudbhavaḥ । varaṃ varaya viśvātman varado ahaṃ tavānagha ।। sa devadevavacanaṃ niśamya kamalodbhavaḥ ।
nirīkṣya viṣṇuṃ puruṣaṃ praṇamyāha vṛṣadhvajam ।। bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa mahādevāmbikāpate । tvāmeva putramicchāmi tvayā vā sadṛśaṃ satam ।। mohito asmi mahādeva māyayā sūkṣmayā tvayā ।
na jāne paramaṃ bhāvaṃ yāthātathyena te śiva ।। tvameva deva bhaktānāṃ bhrātā mātā pitā suhṛt । prasīda tava pādābjaṃ namāmi śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। sa tasya vacanaṃ śrutvā jagannātho vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।
vyājahāra tadā putraṃ samālokya janārdanam ।। yadarthitaṃ bhagavatā tat kariṣyāmi putraka । vijñānamaiśvaraṃ divyamutpatsyati tavānagha ।। tvameva sarvabhūtānāmādikartā niyojitaḥ ।
tathā kuruṣva deveśa mayā lokapitāmaha ।। eṣa nārāyaṇo ananto mamaiva paramā tanuḥ । bhaviṣyati taveśāno yogakṣemavaho hariḥ ।। evaṃ vyāhṛtya hastābhyāṃ prītātmā parameśvaraḥ ।
saṃspṛśya devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ hariṃ vacanamabravīt ।। tṛṣṭo asmi sarvathāhante bhaktyā tava jaganmaya । varaṃ vṛṇīṣvaṃ nahyāvāṃ vibhinnau paramārthataḥ ।। śrutvātha devavacanaṃ viṣṇurviśvajaganmayaḥ ।
prāha prasannayā vācā samālokya caturmukham ।। eṣa eva varaḥ śloghyo yadahaṃ parameśvaram । paśyāmi paramātmānaṃ bhaktirbhavatu me tvayi ।। tathetyuktvā mahādevaḥ punarviṣṇumabhāṣata ।
bhavān sarvasya kāryasya kartāha'madhidaivatam ।। manmayaṃ tvanmayaṃ caiva sarvametanna saṃśayaḥ । bhavān somastvahaṃ sūryo bhavān rātrirahaṃ dinam ।। bhavān prakṛtiravyaktamahaṃ puruṣa eva ca ।
bhavān jñānamahaṃ jñātā bhavān māyāhamīśvaraḥ ।। bhavān vidyātmikā śaktiḥ śaktimānahamīśvaraḥ । yo ahaṃ suniṣkalo devaḥ so api nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ।। ekībhāvena paśyanti yogino brahmavādinaḥ ।
tvāmanāśritya viśvātman na yogī māmupaiṣyati । pālayaitajjagat kṛtsnaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। svamāyayā mohitabhūtabhedaḥ । dhāmaikamavyaktamanantaśaktiḥ ।।
gate maheśvare deve svādhivāsaṃ pitāmahaḥ । tadeva sumahat padmaṃ bheje nābhisamutthitam ।। atha dīrgheṇa kālena tatrāpratimapauruṣau । mahāsurau samāyātau bhrātarau madhukaiṭabhau ।।
krodhena mahatāviṣṭau mahāparvatavigrahau । karṇāntarasamudbhūtau devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।। tāvāgatau samīkṣyāha nārāyaṇamajo vibhuḥ । trailokyakaṇṭakāvetāvasurau hantumarhasi ।।
tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ । ājñāpayāmāsa tayorvadhārthaṃ puruṣāvubhau ।। tadājñayā mahadyuddhaṃ tayostābhyāmabhūd dvijāḥ । vyanayat kaiṭabhaṃ viṣṇurjiṣṇuśca vyanayanmadhum ।।
tataḥ padmāsanāsīnaṃ jagannāthaṃ pitāmaham । babhāṣe madhuraṃ vākyaṃ snehāviṣṭamanā hariḥ ।। asmānmayocyamānastvaṃ padmādavatara prabho । nāhaṃ bhavantaṃ śaknomi voḍhuṃ tejāmayaṃ gurum ।।
tato avatīrya viśvātmā dehamāviśya cakriṇaḥ । avāca vaiṣṇavīṃ nidrāmekībhūyātha viṣṇunā ।। sahastraśīrṣanayanaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ । brahmā nārāyaṇākhyo asau suṣvāpa salile tadā ।।
so anubhūya ciraṃ kālamānandaṃ paramātmanaḥ । anādyanantamadvaitaṃ svātmānaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam ।। tataḥ prabhāte yogātmā bhūtvā devaścaturmukhaḥ । sasarja sṛṣṭiṃ tadrūpāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ bhāvamāśritaḥ ।।
purastādasṛjad devaḥ sanandaṃ sanakaṃ tathā । ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca purvajaṃ taṃ sanātanam ।। te dvandvamohanirmuktāḥ paraṃ vairāgyamāsthitāḥ । viditvā paramaṃ bhāvaṃ na sṛṣṭau dadhire matim ।।
teṣvevaṃ nirapekṣeṣu lokasṛṣṭau pitāmahaḥ । babhūva naṣṭacetā vai māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। tataḥ purāṇapuruṣo jaganmūrtirjanārdanaḥ । vyājahārātmanaḥ putraṃ mohanāśāya padmajam ।।
kaccinna vismṛto devaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ sanātanaḥ । yaduktavānātmano asau putratve tava śaṅkaraḥ ।। avāpya saṃjñāṃ govindāt padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ । prajāḥ straṣṭumanāstepe tapaḥ paramaduścaram ।।
tasyaivaṃ tapyamānasya na kiñcit samavartata । tato dīrgheṇa kālena duḥ khāt krodho abhyajāyata ।। krodhāviṣṭasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatannaśrubindavaḥ । tatastebhyo aśrubindubhyo bhūtāḥ pretāstathābhavan ।।
sarvāṃstānaśrujān dṛṣṭvā brahmātmānamanindana । jahau prāṇāṃśca bhagavān krodhāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। tadā prāṇamayo rudraḥ prādurasīt prabhīrmukhāt । sahastrādityasaṃkāśo yugāntadahanopamaḥ ।।
ruroda susvaraṃ ghoraṃ devadevaḥ svayaṃ śivaḥ । rodamānaṃ tato brahmā mā rodīrityabhāṣata । rodanād rudra ityevaṃ loke khyātiṃ gamiṣyasi ।। anyāni sapta nāmāni patnīḥ putrāṃścaśāśvatān ।
sthānāni caiṣāmaṣṭānāṃ dadau lokapitāmahaḥ ।। bhavaḥ śarvastatheśānaḥ paśūnāṃ patireva ca । bhīmaścogro mahādevastāni nāmāni sapta vai ।। sūryo jalaṃ mahī vahnirvāyurākāśameva ca ।
dīkṣito brāhmaṇaścandra ityetā aṣṭamūrtayaḥ ।। sthāneṣveteṣu ye rudraṃ dhyāyanti praṇamanti ca । teṣāmaṣṭatanurdevo dadāti paramaṃ padam ।। suvarcalā tathaivomā vikeśī ca tathā śivā ।
svāhā diśaśca dīkṣā ca rohiṇī ceti patnayaḥ ।। śanaiścarastathā śukro lohitāṅgo manojavaḥ । skandaḥ sargo atha santāno budhaścaiṣāṃ sutāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। evaṃprakāro bhagavān devadevo maheśvaraḥ ।
prajādharmaṃ ca kāma ca tyaktvā vairāgyamāśritaḥ ।। ātmanyādhya cātmānamaiśvaraṃ bhāvamāsthitaḥ । pītvā tadakṣaraṃ brahma śāśvataṃ paramāmṛtam ।। prajāḥ sṛjeti cādiṣṭo brahmaṇā nīlalohitaḥ ।
svātmanā sadṛśān rudrān sasarja manasā śivaḥ ।। kapardino nirātaṅkān nīlakaṇṭhān pinākinaḥ । triśūlahastānṛṣṭighnān mahānandāṃstrilocanān ।। jarāmaraṇanirmuktān mahāvṛṣabhavāhanān ।
vītarāgāṃśca sarvajñān koṭikoṭiśatān prabhuḥ ।। tān dṛṣṭvā vividhān rudrāna nirmalān nīlalohitān । jarāmaraṇanirmuktān vyājaharā haraṃ guruḥ ।। mā strākṣīrīdṛśīrdeva prajā mṛtyuvivarjitāḥ ।
anyāḥ sṛjasva bhūteśa janmamṛtyusamanvitāḥ ।। tatastamāha bhagavān kaparde kāmaśāsanaḥ । nāsti me tādṛśaḥ sargaḥ sṛja tvamaśubhāḥ prajāḥ ।। tataḥ prabhṛti devo asau na prasūte aśubhāḥ prajāḥ ।
svātmajaireva tai rudrairnivṛttātmā hyatiṣṭhata । sthāṇutvaṃ tena tasyāsīd devadevasya śūlinaḥ ।। jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ । straṣṭṛtvamātmasaṃbodho hyadhiṣṭhātṛtvameva ca ।।
avyayāni daśaitāni nityaṃ tiṣṭhanti śaṅkare । sa eva śaṅkaraḥ sākṣāt pinākī parameśvaraḥ ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān brahmā vīkṣya devaṃ trilocanam । sahaiva mānasaiḥ putraiḥ prītivisphārilocanaḥ ।।
jñātvā parataraṃ bhāvamaiśvaraṃ jñānacakṣuṣā । tuṣṭāva jagatāmekaṃ kṛtvā śirasi cāñjalim ।। namaste astu mahādeva namaste parameśvara । namaḥ śivāya devāya namaste brahmarūpiṇe ।।
namo astu te maheśāya namaḥ śāntāya hetave । pradhānapuruṣeśāya yogādhipataye namaḥ ।। namaḥ kālāya rudrāya mahāgrāsāya śūline । namaḥ pinākahastāya trinetrāya namo namaḥ ।।
namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ brahmaṇo janakāya te । brahmavidyādhipataye brahmavidyāpradāyine ।। namo vedarahasyāya kālakālāya te namaḥ । vedāntasārasārāya namo vedātmamūrtaye ।।
namo buddhāya śuddhāya yogināṃ gurave namaḥ । prahīṇaśokairvividhairbhūtaiḥ varivṛtāya te ।। namo brahmaṇyadevāya brahmādhipataye namaḥ । triyambakāya devāya namaste parameṣṭhine ।।
namo digvāsase tubhyaṃ namo muṇḍāyā daṇḍine । anādimalahīnāya jñānagamyāya te namaḥ ।। namastārāya tīrthāya namo yogardhihetave । namo dharmādhigamyāya yogagamyāya te namaḥ ।।
namaste niṣprapañcāya nirābhāsāya te namaḥ । brahmaṇe viśvarūpāya namaste paramātmane ।। tvayaiva sṛṣṭamakhilaṃ tvayyeva sakalaṃ sthitam । tvayā saṃhriyate viśvaṃ pradhānādyaṃ jaganmaya ।।
tvamīśvaro mahādevaḥ paraṃ brahma maheśvaraḥ । parameṣṭhī śivaḥ śāntaḥ puruṣo niṣkalo haraḥ ।। tvamakṣaraṃ paraṃ jyotistvaṃ kālaḥ parameśvaraḥ । tvameva puruṣo anantaḥ pradhānaṃ prakṛtistathā ।।
bhūmirāpo analo vāyurvyomāhaṅkāra eva ca । yasya rūpaṃ namasyāmi bhavantaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam ।। yasya dyaurabhavanmūrdhā pādau pṛthvī diśo bhujāḥ । ākāśamudaraṃ tasmai virāje praṇamāmyaham ।।
saṃtāpayati yo viśvaṃ svabhābhirbhāsayan diśaḥ । brahmatejomayaṃ nityaṃ tasmai sūryātmane namaḥ ।। havyaṃ vahati yo nityaṃ raudrī tejomayo tanuḥ । kavyaṃ pitṛgaṇānāṃ ca tasmai vahnyātmane namaḥ ।।
āpyāyati yo nityaṃ svadhāmnā sakalaṃ jagat । pīyate devatāsaṅghaistasmai somātmane namaḥ ।। vibhartyaśeṣabhūtāni yo antaścarati sarvadā । śaktirmāheścarī tubhyaṃ tasmai vāyvātmane namaḥ ।।
sṛjatyaśeṣamevedaṃ yaḥ svakarmānurūpataḥ । svātmanyavasthitastasmai caturvaktrātmane namaḥ ।। yaḥ śeṣaśayane śete viśvamāvṛtya māyayā । svātmānubhūtiyogena tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ ।।
vibharti śirasā nityaṃ dvisaptabhuvanātmakam । brahmāṇḍaṃ yo akhilādhārastasmai śeṣātmane namaḥ ।। yaḥ parānte parānandaṃ pītvā divyaikasākṣikam । nṛtyatyanantamahimā tasmai rudrātmane namaḥ ।।
yo antarā sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantā tiṣṭhatīśvaraḥ । taṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ devaṃ namasye bhavatastanum ।। yaṃ vinindrā jitaśvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ samadarśinaḥ । jyotiḥ paśyanti yuñjānāstasmai yogātmane namaḥ ।।
yayā saṃtarate māyāṃ yogī saṃkṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ । apārataraparyantāṃ tasmai vidyātmane namaḥ ।। yasya bhāsā vibhātīdamadvayaṃ tamasaḥ param । prapadye tat paraṃ tattvaṃ tadrūpaṃ parameśvaram ।।
nityānandaṃ nirādhāraṃ niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ śivam । prapadye paramātmānaṃ bhavantaṃ parameśvaram ।। evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ brahmā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ । prāñjaliḥ praṇatastasthau gṛṇan brahma sanātanam ।।
tatastasmai mahādevo divyaṃ yogamanuttamam । aiśvaryaṃ brahmasadbhāvaṃ vairāgyaṃ ca dadau haraḥ ।। karābhyāṃ suśubhābhyāṃ ca saṃspṛśya praṇatārtihā । vyājaharā svayaṃ devaḥ so anugṛhya pitāmaham ।।
yattvayābhyarthitaṃ brahman putratve bhavato mama । kṛtaṃ mayā tat sakalaṃ sṛjasva vividhaṃ jagat ।। tridhā bhinno asmyahaṃ brahman brahmaviṣṇuharākhyayā । sargarakṣālayaguṇairniṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।
sa tvaṃ mamāgrajaḥ putraḥ sṛṣṭihetorvinirmitaḥ । mamaiva dakṣiṇādaṅgād vāmāṅgāt puruṣottamaḥ ।। tasya devādidevasya śaṃbhorhṛdayadeśataḥ । saṃbabhūvātha rudro asāvahaṃ tasyāparā tanuḥ ।।
brahmaviṣṇuśivā brahman sargasthityantahetavaḥ । vibhajyātmānameko api svecchayā śaṅkaraḥ sthitaḥ ।। tathānyāni ca rūpāṇi mama māyākṛtāni tu । nirūpaḥ kevalaḥ svaccho mahādevaḥ svabhāvataḥ ।।
ebhyaḥ parataro devastrimūrtiḥ paramā tanuḥ । māheśvarī trinayanā yogināṃ śāntidā sadā ।। tasyā eva parāṃ mūrti māmavehi pitāmaha । śāśvataiśvaryavijñānatejoyogasamanvitām ।।
so ahaṃ grasāmi sakalamadhiṣṭhāya tamoguṇam । kālo bhūtvā na tamasā māmanyo abhibhaviṣyati ।। yadā yadā hi māṃ nityaṃ vicintayasi padmaja । tadā tadā me sānnidhyaṃ bhaviṣyati tavānagha ।।
etāvaduktvā brahmāṇaṃ so abhivandya guruṃ haraḥ । sahaiva mānasaiḥ putraiḥ kṣaṇādantaradhīyata ।। so api yogaṃ samāsthāya sasarja vividhaṃ jagat । nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavān yathāpūrvaṃ prijāpatiḥ ।।
marīcibhṛgvaṅgirasaṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum । dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca so asṛjad yogavidyayā ।। nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ । sarve te brahmaṇā tulyāḥ sādhakā brahmavādinaḥ ।।
saṃkalpaṃ caiva dharmaṃ ca yugadharmāṃśca śāśvatān । sthānābhimāninaḥ sarvān yathā te kathitaṃ purā ।। evaṃ sṛṣṭvā parīcyādīn devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ । sahaiva mānasaiḥ putraistatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ ।।
tasyaivaṃ tapato vaktrād rudraḥ kālāgnisannibhaḥ । triśūlapāṇirīśānaḥ pradurāsīt trilocanaḥ ।। ardhanārīnaravapuḥ duṣprekṣyo atibhayaṅkaraḥ । vibhajātmānamityuktvā brahmā cāntardadhe bhayāt ।।
tathokto asau dvidhā strītvaṃ puruṣatvamathākarot । bibheda puruṣatvaṃ ca daśadhā caikadhā punaḥ ।। ekādaśaite kathitā rudrāstribhuvaneśvarāḥ । kapālośādayo viprā devakārye niyojitāḥ ।।
saumyāsaumyaistathā śāntāśāntaiḥ strītvaṃ ca sa prabhuḥ । bibheda bahudhā devaḥ svarūpairasitaiḥ sitaiḥ ।। tā vai vibhūtayo viprā viśrutāḥ śaktayo bhuvi । lakṣmyādayo yābhirīśā viśvaṃvyāpnoti śāṅkarī ।।
vibhajya purarīśānī svātmānaṃ śaṅkarād vibhoḥ । mahādevaniyogena pitāmahamupasthitā ।। tāmāha bhagavān brahmā dakṣasya duhitā bhava । sāpi tasya niyogena prādurāsīt prajāpateḥ ।।
niyogād brahmaṇo devīṃ dadau rudrāya tāṃ satīm । dakṣād rudro api jagrāha svakīyāmeva śūlabhṛt ।। prajāpatiṃ vinindyaiṣā kālena parameśvarī । menāyāmabhavat putrī tadā himavataḥ satī ।।
sa cāpi parvatavaro dadau rudrāya pārvatīm । hitāya sarvadevānāṃ trilokasyātmano api ca ।। saiṣā māheśvarī devī śaṅkarārdhaśarīriṇī । śivā satī haimavatī surāsuranamaskṛtā ।।
tasyāḥ prabhāvamatulaṃ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ । vindanti munayo vetti śaṅkaro vā svayaṃ hariḥ ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ viprāḥ putratvaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ । brahmaṇaḥ padmayonitvaṃ śaṅkarasyāmitaujasaḥ ।।
ityākarṇyātha munayaḥ kūrmarūpeṇa bhāṣitam । viṣṇunā punarevainaṃ praṇatā harim ।। kaiṣā bhagavatī devī śaṅkarārdhaśarīriṇī । śivā satī haimavatī yathāvad brūhi pṛcchatām ।।
teṣāṃ tad vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ puruṣottamaḥ । pratyuvāca mahāyogī dhyātvā svaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। purā pitāmahenoktaṃ merupṛṣṭhe suśobhanam । rahasyametad vijñānaṃ gopanīyaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
sāṃkhyānāṃ paramaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ brahmavijñānamuttamam । saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ jantūnāmekamocanam ।। yā sā māheśvarī śaktirjñānarūpātilālasā । vyomasaṃjñā parā kāṣṭhā seyaṃ haimavatī matā ।।
śivā sarvagatānāntā guṇātītā suniṣkalā । ekānekavibhāgasthā jñānarūpātilālasā ।। ananyā niṣkale tattve saṃsthitā tasya tejasā । svābhāvikī ca tanmūlā prabhā bhānorivāmalā ।।
ekā māheśvarī śaktiranekopādhiyogataḥ । parāvareṇa rūpeṇa krīḍate tasya sannidhau ।। seyaṃ karoti sakalaṃ tasyāḥ kāryamidaṃ jagat । na kāryaṃ nāpi karaṇamīśvarasyeti sūrayaḥ ।।
catastraḥ śaktayo devyāḥ svarūpatvena saṃsthitāḥ । adhiṣṭhānavaśāt tasyāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। śāntirvidyā pratiṣṭhā ca nivṛttiścetitāḥ smṛtaḥ । caturvyūhastato devaḥ procyate parameśvaraḥ ।।
anayā parayā devaḥ svātmānandaṃ samaśnute । caturṣvapi ca vedeṣu caturmūrtirmaheśvaraḥ ।। asyāstvanādisaṃsiddhamaiśvaryamatulaṃ mahat । tatsambandhādanantāyā rudreṇa paramātmanā ।।
saiṣā sarveśvarī devī sarvabhūtapravartikā । procyate bhagavān kālo hariḥ prāṇo maheśvaraḥ ।। tatra sarvamidaṃ protamotaṃ caivākhilaṃ jagat । sa kālo agnirharo rudro gīyate vedavādibhiḥ ।।
kālaḥ sṛjati bhūtāni kālaḥ saṃharate prajāḥ । sarve kālasya vaśagā na kālaḥ kasyacid vaśe ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣastattvaṃ mahānātmā tvahaṅkṛtiḥ । kālenānyāni tattvāni samāviṣṭāni yoginā ।।
tasya sarvajagatsūtiḥ śaktirmāyeti viśrutā । tayedaṃ bhrāmayedīśo māyāvī puruṣottamaḥ ।। saiṣā māyātmikā śaktiḥ sarvākārā sanātanī । vaiśvarūpyaṃ maheśasya sarvadā saṃprakāśayet ।।
anyāśca śaktayo mukhyāstasya devasya nirmitāḥ । jñānaśaktiḥ kriyāśaktiḥ prāṇaśaktiriti trayam ।। sarvāsāmeva śaktīnāṃ śaktimanto vinirmitāḥ । māyayaivātha viprendrāḥ sā cānādiranantayā ।।
sarvaśaktyātmikā māyā durnivārā duratyayā । māyāvī sarvaśaktīśaḥ kālaḥ kālakāraḥ prabhuḥ ।। karoti kālaḥ sakalaṃ saṃharet kāla eva hi । kālaḥ sthāpayate viśvaṃ kālādhīnamidaṃ jagat ।।
labdhvā devādhidevasya sannidhiṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ । anantasyākhileśasya śaṃbhoḥ kālātmanaḥ prabhoḥ ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣo māyā māyā caivaṃ prapadyate । ekā sarvagatānantā kevalā niṣkalā śivā ।।
ekā śaktiḥ śivaiko api śaktimānucyate śivaḥ । śaktayaḥ śaktimanto anye sarvaśaktisamudbhavāḥ ।। śaktiśaktimatorbhedaṃ vadanti paramārthataḥ । abhedaṃ cānupaśyanti yoginastattvacintakāḥ ।।
śaktayo girajā devī śaktimanto atha śaṅkaraḥ । viśeṣaḥ kathyate cāyaṃ purāṇe brahmavādibhiḥ ।। bhogyā viśveśvarī devī maheśvarapativratā । procyate bhagavān bhoktā kaparde nīlalohitaḥ ।।
mantā viśveśvaro devaḥ śaṅkaro manmathāntakaḥ । procyate matirīśānī mantavyā ca vicārataḥ ।। ityetadakhilaṃ viprāḥ śaktiśaktimadudbhavam । procyate sarvavedeṣu munibhistattvadarśibhiḥ ।।
etat pradarśitaṃ divyaṃ devyā māhātmyamuttamam । sarvavedāntavedeṣu niścitaṃ brahmavādibhiḥ ।। ekaṃ sarvagataṃ sūkṣmaṃ kūṭasthamacalaṃ dhruvam । yoginastat prapaśyanti mahādevyāḥ paraṃ padam ।।
ānandamakṣaraṃ brahma kevalaṃ niṣkalaṃ param । yoginastat prapaśyanti mahādevyāḥ paraṃ padam ।। parātparataraṃ tattvaṃ śāśvataṃ śivamacyutam । anantaprakṛtau līnaṃ devyāstat paramaṃ padam ।।
śubhaṃ nirañjanaṃ śuddhaṃ nirguṇaṃ dvaitavarjitam । ātmopalabdhiviṣayaṃ devyāstat paramaṃ padam ।। saiṣā dhātrī vidhātrī ca paramānandamicchatām । saṃsāratāpānakhilān nihantīśvarasaṃśrayā ।।
tasmād vimuktimanvicchan pārvatīṃ parameśvarīm । āśrayet sarvabhāvānāmātmabhūtāṃ śivātmikām ।। labdhvā ca putrīṃ śarvāṇīṃ tapastaptvā suduścaram । sabhāryaḥ śaraṃ yātaḥ pārvatīṃ parameśvarīm ।।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā jāyamānāṃ ca svecchayaiva varānanām । menā himavataḥ patnī prāhedaṃ parvateśvaram ।। paśya bālāmimāṃ rājan rājīvasadṛśānanām । hitāya sarvabhūtānāṃ jātā ca tapasāvayoḥ ।।
so api dṛṣṭvā tataḥ putrīṃ taruṇādityasannibhām । kapardinīṃ caturvaktrāṃ trinetrāmatilālasām ।। aṣṭahastāṃ viśālākṣīṃ candrāvayavabhūṣaṇām । nirguṇāṃ saguṇāṃ sākṣāt sadasadvyaktivarjitām ।।
praṇamya śirasā bhūmau tejasā cātivihvalaḥ । bhītaḥ kṛtāñjalistasyāḥ provāca parameśvarīm ।। kā tvaṃ devi viśālākṣi śaśāṅkāvayavāṅkite । na jāne tvāmahaṃ vatse yathāvad brūhi pṛcchate ।।
girīndravacanaṃ śrutvā tataḥ sā parameśvarī । vyājahāra mahāśailaṃ yogināmabhayapradā ।। māṃ viddha paramāṃ śaktiṃ parameśvarasamāśrayām । ananyāmavyayāmekāṃ yāṃ paśyanti mumukṣavaḥ ।।
ahaṃ vai sarvabhāvānātmā sarvāntarā śivā । śāśvataiśvaryavijñānamūrtiḥ sarvapravartikā ।। anantānantamahimā saṃsārārṇavatāriṇī । divyaṃ dadāmi te cakṣuḥ paśya me rūpamaiśvaram ।।
etāvaduktvā vijñānaṃ dattvā himavate svayam । svaṃ rūpaṃ darśayāmāsa divyaṃ tat pārameśvaram ।। koṭisūryapritīkāśaṃ tejobimbaṃ nirākulam । jvālāmālāsahastrāḍhyaṃ kālānalaśatopamam ।।
daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ durdharṣa jaṭāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitam । triśūlavarahastaṃ ca ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam ।। praśāntaṃ saumyavadanamanantāścaryasaṃyutam । candrāvayavalakṣmāṇaṃ candrakoṭisamaprabham ।।
kirīṭinaṃ gadāhastaṃ nūpurairupaśobhitam । divyamālyāmbaradharaṃ divyagandhānulepanam ।। śaṅkhacakradharaṃ kāmyaṃ trinetraṃ kṛttivāsasam । aṇḍasthaṃ cāṇḍabāhyasthaṃ bāhyamābhyantaraṃ param ।।
sarvaśaktimayaṃ śubhraṃ sarvākāraṃ sanātanam । brahmondropendrayogīndrairvandyamānapadāmbujam ।। sarvataḥ pāṇipādāntaṃ sarvato akṣiśiromukham । sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhantaṃ dadarśa parameśvaram ।।
dṛṣṭvā tadīdṛśaṃ rūpaṃ devyā māheśvaraṃ param । bhayena ca samāviṣṭaḥ sa rājā hṛṣṭamānasaḥ ।। ātmanyādhāya cātmānamoṅkāraṃ samanusmaran । nāmnāmaṣṭasahastreṇa tuṣṭāva parameśvarīm ।।
śivomā paramā śaktiranantā niṣkalāmalā । śāntā māheśvarī nityā śāśvatī paramākṣarā ।। acintyā kevalānantyā śivātmā paramātmikā । anādiravyayā śuddhā devātmā sarvagācalā ।।
ekānekavibhāgasthā māyātītā sunirmalā । mahāmāheśvarī satyā mahādevī nirañjanā ।। kāṣṭhā sarvāntarasthā ca cicchaktiratilālasā । nandā sarvātmikā vidyā jyotīrūpāmṛtākṣarā ।।
śāntiḥ pratiṣṭhā sarveṣāṃ nivṛttiramṛtapradā । vyomamūrtirvyomalayā vyomādhārācyutāmarā ।। anādinidhanāmoghā kāraṇātmā kalākalā । kratuḥ prathamajā nābhiramṛtasyātmasaṃśrayā ।।
prāṇeśvarapriyā mātā mahāmahiṣaghātinī । prāṇeśvarī prāṇarūpā pradhānapuruṣeśvarī ।। sarvaśaktikalākārā jyotsnā dyormahimāspadā । sarvakāryaniyantrī ca sarvabhūteśvareśvarī ।।
anādiravyaktaguhā mahānandā sanātanī । ākāśayoniryogasthā mahāyogeśvareśvarī ।। mahāmāyā suduṣpūrā mūlaprakṛtirīśvarī । saṃsārayoniḥ sakalā sarvaśaktisamudbhavā ।।
saṃsārapārā durvārā durnirokṣyā durāsadā । prāṇaśaktiḥ praṇavidyā yoginī paramā kalā ।। mahāvibhūtirdurdharṣā mūlaprakṛtisaṃbhavā । anādyanantavibhavā parārthā puruṣāraṇiḥ ।।
sargasthityantakaraṇī sudurvācyā duratyayā । śabdayoniḥ śabdamayī nādākhyā nādavigrahā ।। pradhānapuruṣātītā pradhānapuruṣātmikā । purāṇī cinmayī puṃsāmādiḥ puruṣarūpiṇī ।।
bhūtāntarātmā kūṭasthā mahāpuruṣasaṃjñitā । janmamṛtyujarātītā sarvaśaktisamanvitā ।। vyāpinī cānavacchinnā pradhānānupraveśinī । kṣetrajñaśaktiravyaktalakṣaṇā malavarjitā ।।
anādimāyasaṃbhinnā tritattvā prakṛtirguhā । mahāmāyāsamutpannā tāmasī pauruṣī dhruvā ।। vyaktāvyaktātmikākṛṣṇā raktāśuklā prasūtikā । akāryā kāryajananī nityaṃ prasavadharmiṇī ।।
sargapralayanirmuktā sṛṣṭisthityantadharmiṇī । brahmagarbhā caturviśā padmanābhācyutātmikā ।। vaidyutī śāśvatī yonirjaganmāteśvarapriyā । sarvādhārā mahārūpā sarvaiśvaryasamanvitā ।।
viśvarūpā mahāgarbhā viśveśecchānuvartinī । mahīyasī brahmayonirmahālakṣmīsamudbhāvā ।। mahāvimānamadhyasthā mahānidrātmahetukā । sarvasādhāraṇī sūkṣmā hyavidyā pāramārthikā ।।
anantarūpānantasthā devī puruṣamohinī । anekākārasaṃsthānā kālatrayavivarjitā ।। brahmajanmā harermūrtirbrahmaviṣṇuśivātmikā । brahmeśaviṣṇujananī brahmākhyā brahmasaṃśrayā ।।
vyaktā prathamajā brāhmī mahatī jñānarūpiṇī । vairāgyaiśvaryadharmātmā brahmamūrtirhṛdisthitā । apāṃyoniḥ svayaṃbhūtirmānasī tattvasaṃbhavā ।। īśvarāṇī ca śarvāṇī śaṅkarārdhaśarīriṇī ।
bhavānī caiva rudrāṇī mahālakṣmīrathāmbikā ।। maheśvarasamutpannā bhuktimuktiphalapradā । sarveśvarī sarvavandyā nityaṃ muditamānasā ।। brahmendropendranamitā śaṅkarecchānuvartinī ।
īśvarārdhāsanagatā maheśvarapativratā ।। sakṛdvibhāvitā sarvā samudrapariśoṣiṇī । pārvatī himavatputrī paramānandadāyinī ।। guṇāḍhyā yogajā yogyā jñānamūrtirvikāsinī ।
sāvitrīkamalā lakṣmīḥ śrīranantorasi sthitā ।। sarojanilayā mudrā yoganidrā surārdinā । sarasvatī sarvavidyā jagajjyeṣṭhā sumaṅgalā ।। vāgdevī varadā vācyā kīrtiḥ sarvārthasādhikā ।
yogīśvarī brahmavidyā mahāvidyā suśobhanā ।। guhyavidyātmavidyā ca dharmavidyātmabhāvitā । svāhā viśvaṃbharā siddhiḥ svadhā medhā dhṛtiḥ śrutiḥ ।। nītiḥ sunītiḥ sukṛtirmādhavī naravāhinī ।
ajā vibhāvarī saumyā bhoginī bhogadāyinī ।। śobhā vaṃśakarī lolā mālinī parameṣṭhinī । trailokyasundarī ramyā sundarī kāmacāriṇī ।। mahānubhāvā sattvasthā mahāmahiṣamardanī ।
padmamālā pāpaharā vicitrā mukuṭānanā ।। niryantrā yantravāhasthā nandinī bhadrakālikā । ādityavarṇā kaumārī mayūravaravāhinī ।। niryantrā yantravāhasthā nandinī bhadrakālikā ।
ādityavarṇā kaumārī mayūravaravāhinī ।। vṛṣāsanagatā gauro mahākālī surārcitā । aditirniyatā raudrī padmagarbhā vivāhanā ।। virūpākṣī lelihānā mahāpuranivāsinī ।
mahāphalānavadyāṅgī kāmapūrā vibhāvarī ।। vicitraratnamukuṭā praṇatārtiprabhañjanī । kauśikī karṣaṇī rātristridaśārtivināśinī ।। bahurūpā surūpā ca virūpā rūpavarjitā ।
bhaktārtiśamanī bhavyā bhavabhāvavināśanī ।। nirguṇā nityavibhavā niḥ sārā nirapatrapā । yaśasvinī sāmagītirbhavāṅganilayālayā ।। dīkṣā vidyādharī dīptā mahendravinipātinī ।
sarvātiśāyinī vidyā sarvasiddhipradāyinī ।। sarveśvarapriyā tārkṣyā samudrāntaravāsinī । akalaṅkā nirādhārā nityasiddhā nirāmayā ।। kāmadhenurbṛhadgarbhā dhīmatī mohanāśinī ।
niḥ saṅkalpā nirātaṅkā vinayā vinayapradā ।। jvālāmālāsahastrāḍhyā devadevī manonmanī । mahābhagavatī durgā vāsudevasamudbhavā ।। mahendropendrabhaginī bhaktigamyā parāvarā ।
jñānajñeyā jarātītā vedāntaviṣayā gatiḥ ।। dakṣiṇā dahanā dāhyā sarvabhūtanamaskṛtā । yogamāyā vibhāvajñā mahāmāyā mahīyasī ।। saṃdhyā sarvasamudbhūtirbrahmavṛkṣāśrayānatiḥ ।
bījāṅkurasamudbhūtirmahāśaktirmahāmatiḥ ।। khyātiḥ prajñā citiḥ saṃvit mahābhogīndraśāyinī । vikṛtiḥ śāṃsarī śāstrī gaṇagandharvasevitā ।। vaiśvānarī mahāśālā devasenā guhapriyā ।
mahārātriḥ śivānandā śacī duḥ svapnanāśinī ।। ijyā pūjyā jagaddhātrī durvijñeyā surūpiṇī । guhāmbikā guṇotpattirmahāpīṭhā marutsutā ।। havyavāhāntarāgādiḥ havyavāhasamudbhavā ।
jagadyonirjaganmātā janmamṛtyujarātigā ।। buddhimātā buddhimatī puruṣāntaravāsinī । tarasvinī samādhisthā trinetrā divisaṃsthitā ।। sarvendriyamanomātā sarvabhūtahṛdi sthitā ।
saṃsāratāriṇī vidyā brahmavādimanolayā ।। brahmāṇī bṛhatī brāhmī brahmabhūtā bhavāraṇiḥ । hiraṇmayī mahārātriḥ saṃsāraparivartikā ।। sumālinī surūpā ca bhāvinī tāriṇī prabhā ।
unmīlanī sarvasahā sarvapratyayasākṣiṇī ।। susaumyā candravadanā tāṇḍavāsaktamānasā । sattvaśuddhikarī śuddhirmalatrayavināśinī ।। jagatpriyā jaganmūrtistrimūrtiramṛtāśrayā ।
nirāśrayā nirāhārā niraṅkuravanodbhavā ।। candrahastā vicitrāṅgī stragviṇī padmadhāriṇī । parāvaravidhānajñā mahāpuruṣapūrvajā ।। vidyeśvarapriyā vidyā vidyujjihvā jitaśramā ।
vidyāmayī sahastrākṣī sahastravadanātmajā ।। sahastraraśmiḥ sattvasthā maheśvarapadāśrayā । kṣālinī sanmayī vyāptā taijasī padmabodhikā ।। mahāmāyāśrayā mānyā mahādevamanoramā ।
vyomalakṣmīḥ siharathā cekitānāmitaprabhā ।। vīreśvarī vimānasthā viśokāśokanāśinī । anāhatā kuṇḍalinā nalinī padmavāsinī ।। sadānandā sadākīrtiḥ sarvabhūtāśrayasthitā ।
vāgdevatā brahmakalā kalātītā kalāraṇiḥ ।। brahmaśrīrbrahmahṛdayā brahmaviṣṇuśivapriyā । vyomaśaktiḥ kriyāśaktirjñānaśaktiḥ parāgatiḥ ।। kṣobhikā bandhikā bhedyā bhedābhedavivarjitā ।
abhinnābhinnasaṃsthānā vaṃśinī vaṃśahāriṇī ।। guhyaśaktirguṇātītā sarvadā sarvatomukhī । bhaginī bhagavatpatnī sakalā kālakāriṇī ।। sarvavit sarvatobhadrā guhyātītā guhāraṇiḥ ।
prakriyā yogamātā ca gaṅgā viśveśvareśvarī ।। kapilā kāpilā kāntākanakābhākalāntarā । puṇyā puṣkariṇī bhoktrī purandarapurassarā ।। poṣaṇī paramaiśvaryabhūtidā bhūtibhūṣaṇā ।
pañcabrahmasamutpattiḥ paramārthārthavigrahā ।। dharmodayā bhānumatī yogijñeya manojavā । manoharā manorakṣā tāpasī vedarūpiṇī ।। vedaśaktirvedamātā vedavidyāprakāśinī ।
yogeśvareśvarī mātā mahāśaktirmanomayī ।। viśvāvasthā viyanmūrtirvidyunmālā vihāyasī । kiṃnarī surabhī vandyā nandinī nandivallabhā ।। bhāratī paramānandā parāparavibhedikā ।
sarvapraharaṇopetā kāmyā kāmeśvareśvarī ।। acintyācintyavibhavā hṛllekhā kanakaprabhā । kūṣmāṇḍī dhanaratnāḍhyā sugandhā gandhāyinī ।। trivikramapadodbhūtā dhanuṣpāṇiḥ śivodayā ।
sudurlabhā dhanādyakṣā dhanyā piṅgalalocanā ।। śāntiḥ prabhāvatī dīptiḥ paṅkajāyatalocanā । ādyā hṛtkamalodbhūtā gavāṃ matā raṇapriyā ।। satkriyā girijā śuddhā nityapuṣṭā nirantarā ।
durgākātyāyanīcaṇḍī carcikā śāntavigrahā ।। hiraṇyavarṇā rajanī jagadyantrapravartikā । mandarādrinivāsā ca śāradā svarṇamālinī ।। ratnamālā ratnagarbhā pṛthvī viśvapramāthinī ।
padmānanā padmanibhā nityatuṣṭāmṛtodbhavā ।। dhunvatī duḥ prakampyā ca sūryamātā dṛṣadvatī । mahendrabhaginī mānyā vareṇyā varadarpitā ।। kalyāṇī kamalā rāmā pañcabhūtā varapradā ।
vācyā vareśvarī vandyā durjayā duratikramā ।। kālarātrirmahāvegā vīrabhadrapriyā hitā । bhadrakālī jaganmātā bhaktānāṃ bhadradāyinī ।। karālā piṅgalākārā nāmabhedāmahāmadā ।
yaśasvinī yaśodā ca ṣaḍadhvaparivartikā ।। śaṅkhinī padminī sāṃkhyā sāṃkhyayogapravartikā । caitrā saṃvatsarārūḍhā jagatsaṃpūraṇīndrajā ।। śumbhāriḥ khecarīsvasthā kambugrīvā kalipriyā ।
khagadhvajī khagārūḍhā parārghyā paramālinī ।। aiśvaryavartmanilayā viraktā garuḍāsanā । jayantī hṛdguhā ramyā gahvireṣṭhā gaṇāgraṇīḥ ।। saṃkalpasiddhā sāmyasthā sarvavijñānadāyinī ।
kalikalpaṣahantrī ca guhyopaniṣaduttamā ।। niṣṭhā dṛṣṭiḥ smṛtirvyāptiḥ puṣṭistuṣṭiḥ kriyāvatī । viśvāmareśvareśānā bhuktirmuktīḥ śivāmṛtā ।। lohitā sarpamālā ca bhīṣaṇī vanamālinī ।
anantaśayanānanyā naranārāyaṇodbhavā ।। nṛsiṃhī daityamathanī śaṅkhacakragadādharā । saṃkarṣaṇasamutpattirambikāpādasaṃśrayā ।। mahājvālā mahāmūrtiḥ sumūrtiḥ sarvakāmadhuk ।
suprabhā sustanā gaurī dharmakāmārthamokṣadā ।। bhrūmadhyanilayā pūrvā purāṇapuruṣāraṇiḥ । mahāvibhūtidā madhyā sarojanayanā samā ।। aṣṭādaśabhujānādyā nīlotpaladalaprabhā ।
sarvaśaktyāsanārūḍhā dharmādharmārthavarjitā ।। vairāgyajñānaniratā nirālokā nirindriyā । vicitragahanādhārā śāśvatasthānavāsinī ।। sthāneśvarī nirānandā triśūlavaradhāriṇī ।
aśeṣadevatāmūrtirdevatā varadevatā । gaṇāmbikā gireḥ putrī niśumbhavinipātinī ।। avarṇa varṇarahitā nivarṇā bījasaṃbhavā । anantavarṇānanyasthā śaṅkarī śāntamānasā ।।
agotrā gomatī goptrī guhyarūpā guṇottarā । gaurgorgavyapriyā gauṇī gaṇeśvaranamaskṛtā ।। satyamātrā satyasaṃdhā trisaṃdhyā saṃdhivarjitā । sarvavādāśrayā saṃkhyā saṃkhyayogasamudbhavā ।।
asaṃkhyeyāprameyākhyā śūnyā śuddhakulodbhavā । bindunādasamutpattiḥ śaṃbhuvāmā śaśiprabhā ।। visaṅgā bhedarahitā manojñā madhusūdanī । mahāśrīḥ śrīsamutpattistamaḥ pāre pratiṣṭhitā ।।
tritattvamātā trividhā susūkṣmapadasaṃśrayā । śāntyatītā malātītā nirvikārā nirāśrayā ।। śivākhyā cittanilayā śivajñānasvarūpiṇī । daityadānavanirmātrī kāśyapī kālakalpikā ।।
śāstrayoniḥ kriyāmūrtiścaturvargapradarśikā । nārāyaṇī narodbhūtiḥ kaumudī liṅgadhāriṇī ।। kāmukī lalitā bhāvā parāparavibhūtidā । parāntajātamahimā baḍavā vāmalocanā ।।
subhadrā devakī sītā vedavedāṅgapāragā । manasvinī manyumātā mahāmanyusamudbhavā ।। amṛtyuramṛtā svāhā puruhūtā puruṣṭutā । aśocyā bhinnaviṣayā hiraṇyarajatapriyā ।।
hiraṇyā rājatī haimī hemābharaṇabhūṣitā । vibhrājamānā durjñeyā jyotiṣṭomaphalapradā ।। mahānidrāsamudbhūtiranidrā satyadevatā । dīrghākakudminī hṛdyā śāntidā śāntivardhinī ।।
lakṣmyādiśaktijananī śakticakrapravartikā । triśaktijananī janyā ṣaḍūrmiparirjitā ।। sudhāmā karmakaraṇī yugāntadahanātmikā । saṃkarṣaṇī jagaddhātrī kāmayoniḥ kirīṭinī ।।
aindrī trailokyanamitā vaiṣṇavī parameśvarī । pradyumnadayitā dāntā yugmadṛṣṭistrilocanā ।। madotkaṭā haṃsagatiḥ pracaṇḍā caṇḍavikramā । vṛṣāveśā viyanmātā vindhyaparvatavāsinī ।।
himavanmerunilayā kailāsagirivāsinī । cāṇūrahantṛtanayā nītijñā kāmarūpiṇī ।। vedavidyāvratasnātā dharmaśīlānilāśanā । vīrabhadrapriyā vīrā mahākālasamudbhavā ।।
