vidyādharapriyā siddhā vidyādharanirākṛtiḥ । āpyāyanī harantī ca pāvanī poṣaṇī khilā ।। mātṛkā manmathodbhūtā vārijā vāhanapriyā । karīṣiṇī sudhāvāṇī vīṇāvādanatatparā ।।
sevitā sevikā sevyā sinīvālī garutmatī । arundhatī hiraṇyākṣī mṛgāṅkā mānadāyinī ।। vasupradā vasumatī vasordhārā vasuṃdharā । dhārādharā varārohā varāvarasahastradā ।।
śrīphalā śrīmatī śrīśā śrīnivāsā śivapriyā । śrīdharā śrīkarī kalyā śrīdharārdhaśarīriṇī ।। anantadṛṣṭirakṣudrā dhātrīśā dhanadapriyā । nihantrī daityasaṅghānāṃ sihikā sihavāhanā ।।
suṣeṇā candranilayā sukīrtiśchinnasaṃśayā । rasajñā rasadā rāmā lelihānāmṛtastravā ।। nityoditā svayañjyotirutsukā mṛtajīvanī । vajradaṇḍā vajrajihvā vaidevī vajravigrahā ।।
maṅgalyā maṅgalā mālā malinā malahāriṇī । gāndharvo gāruḍī cāndrī kambalāśvatarapriyā ।। saudāminī janānandā bhrukuṭīkuṭilānanā । karṇikārakarā kakṣyā kaṃsaprāṇāpahāriṇī ।।
yugandharā yugāvartā trisaṃdhyā harṣavardhanī । pratyakṣadevatā divyā divyagandhā divāparā ।। śakrāsanagatā śākrī sādhvī nārī śavāsanā । iṣṭā viśiṣṭā śiṣṭeṣṭā śiṣṭāśiṣṭaprapūjitā ।।
śatarūpā śatāvartā vinatā surabhiḥ surā । surendramātā sudyumnā suṣumnā sūryasaṃsthitā ।। samīkṣyā satpratiṣṭhā ca nivṛttirjñānapāragā । dharmaśāstrārthakuśalā dharmajñā dharmavāhanā ।।
dharmādharmavinirmātrī dhārmikāṇāṃ śivapradā । dharmaśaktirdharmamayī vidharmā viśvadharmiṇī ।। dharmāntarā dharmameghā dharmapūrvā dhanāvahā । dharmopadeṣṭrī dharmatmā dharmagamyā dharādharā ।।
kāpālī śākalā mūrtiḥ kalā kalitavigrahā । sarvaśaktivinirmuktā sarvaśaktyāśrayāśrayā ।। sarvā sarveśvarī sūkṣmā susūkṣmā jñānarūpiṇī । pradhānapuruṣeśeśā mahādevaikasākṣiṇī ।
sadāśivā viyanmūrtirviśvamūrtiramūrtikā ।। evaṃ nāmnāṃ sahastreṇa stutvāsau himavān giriḥ । bhūyaḥ praṇamya bhītātmā provācedaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। yadetadaiśvaraṃ rūpaṃ ghoraṃ te parameśvari ।
bhīto asmi sāmprataṃ dṛṣṭvā rūpamanyat pradarśaya ।। evamuktātha sā devī tena śailena pārvatī । saṃhṛtya darśayāmāsa svarūpamaparaṃ punaḥ ।। nīlotpaladalaprakhyaṃ nīlotpalasugandhikam ।
dvinetraṃ dvibhujaṃ saumyaṃ nīlālakavibhūṣitam ।। raktapādāmbujatalaṃ suraktakarapallavam । śrīmad viśālasaṃvṛttalalāṭatilakojjvalam ।। bhūṣitaṃ cārusarvāṅgaṃ bhūṣaṇairatikomalam ।
dadhānamurasā mālāṃ viśālāṃ hemanirmitām ।। īṣatsmitaṃ suvimboṣṭhaṃ nūpurārāvasaṃyutam । prasannavadanaṃ divyamanantamahimāspadam ।। tadīdṛśaṃ samālokya svarūpaṃ śailasattamaḥ ।
bhītiṃ saṃtyajya hṛṣṭātmā babhāṣe parameśvarīm ।। adya me saphalaṃ janma adya me saphalaṃ tapaḥ । yanme sākṣāt tvamavyaktāprasannā dṛṣṭigocarā ।। tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ jagat sarvaṃ pradhānādyantvayi sthitam ।
tvayyeva līyate devi tvameva ca parā gatiḥ ।। vadanti kecit tvāmeva prakṛtiṃ prakṛteḥ parām । apare paramārthajñāḥ śiveti śivasaṃśraye ।। tvayi pradhānaṃ puruṣo mahān brahmā tatheśvaraḥ ।
avidyā niyatirmāyā kalādyāḥ śataśo abhavan ।। tvaṃ hi sā paramā śaktiranantā parameṣṭhinī । sarvabhedavinirmuktā sarvebhedāśrayā nijā ।। tvāmadhiṣṭhāya yogeśi mahādevo maheśvaraḥ ।
pradhānādyaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ karoti vikaroti ca ।। tvayaiva saṃgato devaḥ svamānandaṃ samaśnute । tvameva paramānandastvamevānandadāyinī ।। tvamakṣaraṃ paraṃ vyoma mahajjyotirnirañjanam ।
śivaṃ sarvagataṃ sūkṣmaṃ paraṃ brahmā sanātanam ।। tvaṃ śakraḥ sarvadevānāṃ brahmā brahmavidāmasi । vāyurbalavatāṃ devi yogināṃ tvaṃ kumārakaḥ ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ ca vasiṣṭhastvaṃ vyāso vedavidāmasi ।
sāṃkhyānāṃ kapilo devo rudrāṇāmasi śaṅkaraḥ ।। ādityānāmupendrastvaṃ vasūnāṃ caiva pāvakaḥ । vedānāṃ sāmavedastvaṃ gāyatrī chandasāmasi ।। adhyātmavidyā vidyānāṃ gatīnāṃ param gatiḥ ।
māyā tvaṃ sarvaśaktīnāṃ kālaḥ kalayatāmasi ।। oṅkāraḥ sarvaguhyānāṃ varṇānāṃ ca dvijāttamaḥ । āśramāṇāṃ ca gārhasthyamīśvarāṇāṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। puṃsāṃ tvamekaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvabhūtahṛdi sthitaḥ ।
sarvopaniṣadāṃ devi guhyopaniṣaducyate ।। īśānaścāsi kalpānāṃ yugānāṃ kṛtameva ca । ādityaḥ sarvamārgāṇāṃ vācāṃ devi sarasvatī ।। tvaṃ lakṣmīścārurūpāṇāṃ viṣṇurmāyāvināmasi ।
arundhatī satīnāṃ tvaṃ suparṇaḥ patatāmasi ।। sūktānāṃ pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ jyeṣṭhasāma ca sāmasu । sāvitrī cāsi japyānāṃ yajuṣāṃ śatarudriyam ।। parvatānāṃ mahāmerurananto bhogināmasi ।
sarveṣāṃ tvaṃ paraṃ brahma tvanmayaṃ sarvameva hi ।। magocaraṃ nirmalamekarūpam । namāmi satyaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt ।। vedāntavijñānaviniścitārthāḥ ।
tadeva rūpaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye ।। pradhānapuṃyogaviyogahetum । prāṇābhidhānaṃ praṇato asmi rūpam ।। vibhinnasaṃsthaṃ prakṛteḥ parastāt ।
namāmi rūpaṃ puruṣābhidhānam ।। sarvatragaṃ janmavināśahīnam । nato asmi te rūpamaluptabhedam ।। prakṛtyavasthaṃ triguṇātmabījam ।
samanvitaṃ devi nato asmi rūpam ।। vicitrabhedaṃ puruṣaikanātham । nato asmi rūpaṃ jagadaṇḍasaṃjñam ।। svatejasā pūritalokabhedam ।
namāmi rūpaṃ ravimaṇḍalastham ।। sahastrabāhuṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam । nārāyaṇākhyaṃ praṇato asmi rūpam ।। yugāntakālānalakalparūpam ।
namāmi rūpaṃ tava kālasaṃjñam ।। bhogīndramukhyairabhipūjyamānam । nato asmi rūpaṃ tava śeṣasaṃjñam ।। brahmāmṛtānandarasajñamekam ।
nato asmi rūpaṃ tava rudrasaṃjñam ।। surāsurairarcitāpādapadmam । namāmi te rūpamidaṃ namāsi ।। oṃ namaste mahādevi namaste parameśvari ।
namo bhagavatīśāni śivāyai te namo namaḥ ।। tvanmayo ahaṃ tvadādhārastvameva ca gatirmama । tvāmeva śaraṇaṃ yāsye prasīda parameśvari ।। mayā nāsti samo loke devo vādānavo api vā ।
jaganmātaiva matputrī saṃbhūtā tapasā yataḥ ।। eṣā tavāmbikā devi kilābhūta pitṛkanyakā । menāśeṣajaganmāturaho vuṇyasya gauravam ।। pāhi māmamareśāni menayā saha sarvadā ।
namāmi tava pādābjaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ śivām ।। aho me sumahad bhāgyaṃ mahādevīsamāgamāt । ājñāpaya mahādevi kiṃ kariṣyāmi śaṅkari ।। etāvaduktvā vacanaṃ tadā himagirīśvaraḥ ।
saṃprekṣaṇamāṇo girijāṃ prāñjaliḥ pārśvato abhavat ।। atha sā tasya vacanaṃ niśamya jagato araṇiḥ । sasmitaṃ prāha pitaraṃ smṛtvā paśupatiṃ patim ।। śṛṇuṣva caitat paramaṃ guhyamīśvaragocaram ।
upadeśaṃ giriśreṣṭha sevitaṃ brahmavādibhiḥ ।। yanme sākṣāt paraṃ rūpamaiśvaraṃ dṛṣṭamadbhutam । sarvaśaktisamāyuktamanantaṃ prerakaṃ param ।। śāntaḥ samāhitamanā dambhāhaṅkāravarjitaḥ ।
tanniṣṭhastatparo bhūtvā tadeva śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। bhaktyā tvananyayā tāta padbhāvaṃ paramāśritaḥ । sarvayajñatapodānaistadevārcaya sarvadā ।। tadeva manasā paśya tad dhyāyasva japasva ca ।
mamopadeśāt saṃsāraṃ nāśayāmi tavānagha ।। ahaṃ vai matparān bhaktānaiśvaraṃ yogamāsthitān । saṃsārasāgarādasmāduddharāmyacireṇa tu ।। dhyānena karmayogena bhaktyā jñānena caiva hi ।
prāpyāhaṃ te giriśreṣṭha nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ ।। śrutismṛtyuditaṃ samyak karma varṇāśramātmakam । adhyātmajñānasahitaṃ muktaye satataṃ kuru ।। dharmāt saṃjāyate bhaktirbhaktyā saṃprāpyate param ।
śrutismṛtibhyāmudito dharmo yajñādiko mataḥ ।। nānyato jāyate dharmo vedād dharmo hi nirbabhau । tasmānmumukṣurdharmārtho madrūpaṃ vedamāśrayet ।। mamaivaiṣā parā śaktirvedasaṃjñā purātanī ।
ṛgyajuḥ sāmarūpeṇa sargādau saṃpravartate ।। teṣāmeva ca guptyarthaṃ vedānāṃ bhagavānajaḥ । brāhmaṇādīn sasarjātha sve sve karmaṇyayojayat ।। ye na kurvanti tad dharmaṃ tadarthaṃ brahmanirmitam ।
teṣāmadhastād narakāṃstāmistrādīnakalpayat ।। na ca vedād ṛte kiñcicchāstradharmābhidhāyakam । yo anyatraramateso asaunasaṃbhāṣyo dvijātibhiḥ ।। yāni śāstrāṇi dṛśyante loke asmin vividhānitu ।
śrutismṛtiviruddhāni niṣṭhā teṣāṃ hi tāmasī ।। kāpālaṃ pañcarātraṃ ca yāmalaṃ vāmamārhatam । evaṃvidhāni cānyāni mohanārthāni tāni tu ।। ye kuśāstrābhiyogena mohayantīha mānavān ।
mayā sṛṣṭāni śāstrāṇi mohāyaiṣāṃ bhavāntare ।। vedārthavittamaiḥ kāryaṃ yat smṛtaṃ karma vaidikam । tat prayatnena kurvanti matpriyāste hi ye narāḥ ।। varṇānāmanukampārthaṃ manniyogād virāṭ svayam ।
svāyaṃbhuvo manurdhārmān munīnāṃ pūrvamuktavānā ।। śrutvā cānye api munayastanmukhād dharmamuttamam । cakrurdharmapratiṣṭhārthaṃ dharmaśāstrāṇi caiva hi ।। teṣu cāntarhiteṣvevaṃ yugānteṣu maharṣayaḥ ।
brahmaṇo vacanāt tāni kariṣyanti yuge yuge ।। aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni vyāsena kathitāni tu । niyogād brahmaṇo rājaṃsteṣu dharmaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। anyānyupapurāṇāni tacchiṣyaiḥ kathitāni tu ।
yuge yuge atra sarveṣāṃ kartā vai dharmaśāstravit ।। śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chanda eva ca । jyotiḥ śāstraṃ nyāyavidyā mīmāṃsā copabṛṃhaṇam ।। evaṃ caturdaśaitāni vidyāsthānāni sattama ।
caturvedaiḥ sahoktāni dharmo nānyatra vidyate ।। evaṃ paitāmahaṃ dharmaṃ manuvyāsādayaḥ param । sthāpayanti mamādeśād yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। brahmaṇā saha te sarve saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare ।
parasyānte kṛtātmānaḥ praviśanti paraṃ padam ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena dharmārthaṃ vedamāśrayet । dharmeṇa sahitaṃ jñānaṃ paraṃ brahma prakāśayet ।। ye tu saṅgān parityajya māmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
upāsate sadā bhaktyā yogamaiśvaramāsthitāḥ ।। sarvabhūtadayāvantaḥ śāntā dāntā vimatsarāḥ । amānino buddhimantastāpasāḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ ।। maccittā madgataprāṇā majjñānakathane ratāḥ ।
saṃnyāsino gṛhasthāśca vanasthā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। teṣāṃ nityābhiyuktānāṃ māyātattvasamutthitam । nāśayāmi tamaḥ kṛtsnaṃ jñānadīpane mā cirāt ।। te sunirdhūtatamaso jñānenaikena manmayāḥ ।
sadānandāstu saṃsāre na jāyante punaḥ punaḥ ।। tasmāt sarvaprakāreṇa madbhakto matparāyaṇaḥ । māmevārcaya sarvatra menayā saha saṃgataḥ ।। aśakto yadi me dhyātumaiśvaraṃ rūpamavyayam ।
tato me sakalaṃ rūpaṃ kālādyaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। yad yat svarūpaṃ me tāta manaso gocaraṃ bhavet । tanniṣṭhastatparo bhūtvā tadarcanaparo bhava ।। yattu me niṣkalaṃ rūpaṃ cinmātraṃ kevalaṃ śivam ।
sarvopādhivinirmuktamanantamamṛtaṃ param ।। jñānenaikena tallabhyaṃ kleśena paramaṃ padam । jñānameva prapaśyanto māmeva praviśanti te ।। tadbuddhayastadātmānastanniṣṭhāstatparāyaṇāḥ ।
gacchantyapunarāvṛttiṃ jñānanirdhūtakalmaṣāḥ ।। māmanāśritya paramaṃ nirvāṇamamalaṃ padam । prāpyate na hi rājendra tato māṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। ekatvena pṛthaktvena tathā cobhayato api vā ।
māmupāsya mahārāja tato yāsyāsi tatpadam ।। māmanāśritya tat tattvaṃ svabhāvavimalaṃ śivam । jñāyate na hi rājendra tato māṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। tasmāt tvamakṣaraṃ rūpaṃ nityaṃ cārūpamaiśvaram ।
ārādhaya prayatnena tato bandhaṃ prahāsyasi ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā śivaṃ sarvatra sarvadā । samārādhaya bhāvena tato yāsyasi tatpadam ।। na vai paśyanti tat tattvaṃ mohitā mama māyayā ।
anādyanantaṃ paramaṃ maheśvaramajaṃ śivam ।। sarvabhūtātmabhūtasthaṃ sarvādhāraṃ nirañjanam । nityānandaṃ nirābhāsaṃ nirguṇaṃ tamasaḥ param ।। advaitamacalaṃ brahma niṣkalaṃ niṣprapañcakam ।
svasaṃvedyamavedyaṃ tat pare vyomni vyavasthitam ।। sūkṣmeṇa tamasā nityaṃ veṣṭitā mama māyayā । saṃsārasāgare ghore jāyante ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। bhaktyā tvananyayā rājan samyag jñānena caiva hi ।
anveṣṭavyaṃ hi tad brahma janmabandhanivṛttaye ।। ahaṅkāraṃ ca mātsaryaṃ kāmaṃ krodhaṃ parigraham । adharmābhiniveśaṃ ca tyaktvā vairāgyamāsthitaḥ ।। sarvabhūteṣu cātmānaṃ sarvabhūtāni cātmani ।
anvīkṣya cātmanātmānaṃ brahmabhūyāya kalpate ।। brahmabhūtaḥ prasannātmā sarvabhūtābhayapradaḥ । aiśvarīṃ paramāṃ bhaktiṃ vindetānanyagāminīm ।। vīkṣate tat paraṃ tattvamaiśvaraṃ brahmaniṣkalam ।
sarvasaṃsāranirmukto brahmaṇeyavāvatiṣṭhate ।। brahmaṇo hi pratiṣṭhāyaṃ parasya paramaḥ śivaḥ । anantasyāvyayasyaikaḥ svātmādhāro maheśvaraḥ ।। jñānena karmayogena bhaktiyogena vā nṛpa ।
sarvasaṃsāramuktyarthamīśvaraṃ satataṃ śraya ।। eṣa guhyopadeśaste mayā datto girīśvara । anvīkṣya caitadakhilaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ kartumarhasi ।। ahaṃ vai yācitā devaiḥ saṃjātā parameśvarāt ।
vinindya dakṣaṃ pitaraṃ maheśvaravinindakam ।। dharmasaṃsthāpanārthāya tavārādhanakāraṇāt । menādehasamutpannā tvāmeva pitaraṃ śritā ।। sa tvaṃ niyogād devasya brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ ।
pridāsyase māṃ rudrāya svayaṃvarasamāgame ।। tatsaṃbandhācca te rājan sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ । tvāṃ namasyanti vai tāta prasīdati ca śaṅkaraḥ ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena māṃ viddhīśvaragocarām ।
saṃpūjya devamīśānaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja ।। sa evamukto bhagavān devadevyā girīśvaraḥ । praṇamya śirasā devīṃ prāñjaliḥ punarabravīt ।। vistareṇa maheśāni yogaṃ māheśvaraṃ param ।
jñānaṃ caivātmano yogaṃ sādhanāni pracakṣva me ।। tasyaitat paramaṃ jñānamātmayogamanuttamam । yathāvad vyājahāreśāsādhanānica vistarāt ।। niśamya vadanāmbhojād girīndro lokapūjitaḥ ।
lokamātuḥ paraṃ jñānaṃ yogāsakto abhavatpunaḥ ।। pradadau ca maheśāya pārvatīṃ bhāgyagauravāt । niyogād brahmaṇaḥ sādhvīṃ devānāṃ caiva saṃnidhau ।। ya imaṃ paṭhate adhyāyaṃ devyā māhātmyakīrtanam ।
śivasya saṃnidhau bhaktyā sucistadbhāvabhāvitaḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto divyayogasamanvitaḥ । ullaṅghya brahmaṇo lokandevyāḥ sthānamavāpnuyāt ।। yaścaitat paṭhate stotraṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ samīpataḥ ।
devyāḥ samāhitamanāḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। nāmnāmaṣṭasahastraṃ tu devyā yat samudīritam । jñātvār'kamaṇḍalagatāṃ saṃbhāvya parameśvarīm ।। abhyarcya gandhapuṣpādyairbhaktiyogasamanvitaḥ ।
saṃsmaran paramaṃ bhāvaṃ devyā māheśvaraṃ param ।। ananyamānaso nityaṃ japedāmaraṇād dvijaḥ । so antakāle smṛtiṃ labdhvāparaṃ brahmādhigacchati ।। athavā jāyate vipro brāhmaṇānāṃ kule śucau ।
pūrvasaṃskāramāhātmyād brahmavidyāmavāpya saḥ ।। saṃprāpya yogaṃ paramaṃ divyaṃ tat pārameśvaram । śāntaḥ sarvagāto bhūtvā śivasāyujyamānapnuyāt ।। pratyekaṃ cātha nāmāni juhuyāt savanatrayam ।
pūtanādikṛtairdeṣairgrahadoṣaiśca mucyate ।। japed vāharaharnityaṃ saṃvatsaramatandritaḥ । śrīkāmaḥ pārvatīṃ devīṃ pūjayitvā vidhānataḥ ।। saṃpūjya pārśvataḥ śaṃbhuṃ trinetraṃ bhaktisaṃyutaḥ ।
labhate mahatīṃ lakṣmīṃ mahādevaprasādataḥ ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena japtavyaṃ hi dvijātibhiḥ । sarvapāpānodārthaṃ devyā nāma sahastrakam ।। prasaṅgāt kathitaṃ viprā devyā māhātmyamuttamam ।
ataḥ paraṃ prajāsargaṃ bhṛgvādīnāṃ nibodhata ।। bhṛgoḥ khyātyāṃ samutpannā lakṣmīrnārāyaṇapriyā । devau dhātāvidhātārau merorjāmātarau tathā ।। āyatirniyatirmeroḥ kanye caiva mahātmanaḥ ।
dhātāvidhātroste bhārye tayorjātau sutāvubhau ।। prāṇaścaiva mṛkaṇḍuśca mārkaṇḍeyo mṛkaṇḍutaḥ । tathā vedaśirā nāma prāṇasya dyutimān sutaḥ ।। marīcerapi saṃbhūtiḥ paurṇamāsamasūyata ।
kanyācatuṣṭayaṃ caiva sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।। tuṣṭirjyeṣṭhā tathā vṛṣṭiḥ kṛṣṭiścāpacitistathā । virajāḥ parvaścaiva paurṇamāsasya tau sutau ।। kṣamā tu suṣuve putrān pulahasya prajāpateḥ ।
kardamaṃ ca varīyāṃsaṃ sahiṣṇuṃ munisattamam ।। tathaiva ca kanīyāsaṃ taponirdhūtakalpaṣam । anasūyā tathaivātrerjajñe putrānakalpaṣān ।। somaṃ durvāsasaṃ caiva dattātreyaṃ ca yoginam ।
smṛtiścāṅgirasaḥ putrīrjajñe lakṣaṇasaṃyutāḥ ।। sinīvālīṃ kuhūṃ caiva rākāmanumatiṃ tathā । prītyāṃ pulastyo bhagavān dattātrimasṛjat prabhuḥ ।। pūrvajanmani so agastyaḥ smṛtaḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare ।
vedabāhuṃ tathā kanyāṃ sannatiṃ nāma nāmataḥ ।। putrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭisāhastraṃ saṃtatiḥ suṣuve kratoḥ । te cordhvaretasaḥ sarve bālakhilyā iti smṛtāḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaśca tathorjāyāṃ saptaputrānajījanat ।
kanyāṃ ca puṇḍarīkākṣāṃ sarveśobhāsamanvitām ।। rajohaścordhvabāhuśca savanaścānaghastathā । sutapāḥ śukra ityete sapta putrā mahaujasaḥ ।। yo asau rudrātmako vahnirbrahmaṇastanayo dvijāḥ ।
svāhā tasmāt sutān lebhe trīnudārān mahaujasaḥ ।। pāvakaḥ pavamānaśca śuciragniśca te trayaḥ । nirmathyaḥ pavamānaḥ syād vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yaścāsau tapate sūryaḥ śuciragnistvasau smṛtaḥ ।
teṣāṃ tu saṃtatāvanye catvāriṃśca pañca ca ।। pāvakaḥ pavamānaśca śucisteṣāṃ pitā ca yaḥ । ete caikonapañcāśad vahnayaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। sarve tapasvinaḥ proktāḥ sarve yajñeṣu bhāginaḥ ।
rudrātmakāḥ smṛtāḥ sarve tripuṇḍrāṅkitamastakāḥ ।। ayajvānaśca yajvānaḥ pitaro brahmaṇaḥ smṛtāḥ । agniṣvāttā barhiṣado dvidhā teṣāṃ vyavasthitiḥ ।। tebhyaḥ svadhā sutāṃ jajñe menāṃ vaitaraṇīṃ tathā ।
te ubhe brahmavādinyau yoginyau munisattamāḥ ।। asūta menā mainākaṃ krauñcaṃ tasyānujaṃ tathā । gaṅgā himavato jajñe sarvalokaikapāvanī ।। svayogāgnibalād devīṃ lebhe putrīṃ maheśvarīṃ ।
yathāvat kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ devyā māhātmyamuttamam ।। eṣā dakṣasya kanyānāṃ mayāpatyānusaṃtatiḥ । vyākhyātā bhavatāmadya manoḥ sṛṣṭiṃ nibodhata ।। priyavratottānapādau manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya tu ।
dharmajñau sumahāvīryau śatarūpā vyajījanat ।। tatastūttānapādasya dhruvo nāma suto abhavat । bhakto nārāyaṇe deve prāptavān sthānamuttamam ।। dhruvāt śliṣṭiñca bhavyaṃ ca bhāryā śambhurvyajāyata ।
śliṣṭerādhatta succhāyā pañca putrānakalpaṣān ।। vasiṣṭhavacanād devī tapastaptvā suduścaram । ārādhya puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ śālagrāme janārdanam ।। ripuṃ ripuñjayaṃ vipraṃ vṛkalaṃ vṛṣatejasam ।
nārāyaṇaparān śuddhān svadharmaparipālakān ।। riporādhatta bṛhatī cakṣuṣaṃ sarvatejasam । so ajījanat puṣkariṇyāṃ vairaṇyāṃ cākṣuṣaṃ manum । prajāpaterātmajāyāṃ vīraṇasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
manorajāyanta daśa naḍvalāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ । kanyāyāṃ sumahāvīryā vairājasya prajāpateḥ ।। ūruḥ pūruḥ śatadyumnastapasvī satyavāk śuciḥ । agniṣṭudatirātraśca sudyumnaścābhimanyukaḥ ।।
ūrorajanayat putrān ṣaḍāgneyī mahābalān । aṅgaṃ sumanasaṃ svātiṃ kratumaṅgirasaṃ śivam ।। aṅgād veno abhavat paścād bainyo venādajāyata । yo asau pṛthuriti khyātaḥ prajāpālo mahābalaḥ ।।
yena dugdhā mahī pūrvaṃ prājānāṃ hitakāraṇāt । niyogād brahmaṇaḥ sārdhaṃ devendreṇa mahaujasā ।। venaputrasya vitate purā paitāmahe makhe । sūtaḥ paurāṇiko jajñe māyārūpaḥ svayaṃ hariḥ ।।
pravaktā sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ dharmajño guṇavatsalaḥ । taṃ māṃ nitta muniśreṣṭhāḥ pūrvodbhūtaṃ sanātanam ।। asmin manvantare vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ svayam । śrāvayāmāsa māṃ prītyā purāṇaṃ puruṣo hariḥ ।।
madanvaye tu ye sūtāḥ saṃbhūtā vedavarjitāḥ । teṣāṃ purāṇavaktṛtvaṃ vṛttirāsīdajājñayā ।। sa tu vainyaḥ pṛthurdhomān satyasaṃdho jitendriyaḥ । sārvabhaumo mahātejāḥ svadharmaparipālakaḥ ।।
tasya bālyāt prabhṛtyeva bhaktirnārāyaṇe abhavat । govardhanagiriṃ prāpya tapastepe jitendriyaḥ ।। tapasā bhagavān prītaḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ । āgatya devo rājānaṃ prāha dāmodaraḥ svayam ।।
dhramikau rūpasaṃpannau sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varau । matprasādādasaṃdigdhaṃ putrau tava bhaviṣyataḥ । ekamuktvā hṛṣīkeśaḥ svakīyāṃ prakṛtiṃ gataḥ ।। vainyo api vedavidhinā niścalāṃ bhaktimudvahan ।
apālayat svakaṃ rājyaṃ nyāyena madhusūdane ।। acirādeva tanvaṅgo bhāryā tasya sucismitā । khikhaṇḍanaṃ havirdhānamantardhānā vyajāyata ।। śikhaṇḍano abhavat putraḥ suśīla iti viśrutaḥ ।
dhārmiko rūpasaṃpanno vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।। so adhītya vidhivad vedān dharmeṇa tapasi sthitaḥ । matiṃ cakre bhāgyayogāt saṃnyāṃ prati dharmavit ।। sa kṛtvā tīrthasaṃsevāṃ svādhyāye tapasi sthitaḥ ।
jagāma himavatpṛṣṭhaṃ kadācit siddhasevitam ।। tatra dharmapadaṃ nāma dharmasiddhipradaṃ vanam । apaśyad yogināṃ gamyamagamyaṃ brahmavidviṣām ।। tatra mandākinī nāma supuṇyā vimalā nadī ।
padmotpalavanopetā siddhāśramavibhūṣitā ।। sa tasyā dakṣiṇe tīre munīndrairyogibhirvṛtam । supuṇyamāśramaṃ ramyamapaśyat prītisaṃyutaḥ ।। mandākinījale strātvā saṃtarpya pitṛdevatāḥ ।
arcayitvā mahādevaṃ puṣpaiḥ padmotpalādibhiḥ ।। dhyātvārkaṃsaṃsthamīśānaṃ śirasyādhāya cāñjalim । saṃprekṣamāṇo bhāsvantaṃ tuṣṭāva parameśvaram ।। rudrādhyāyena giriśaṃ rudrasya caritena ca ।
anyaiśca vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ śāṃbhavairvedasaṃbhavaiḥ ।। athāsminnantare apaśyat tamāyāntaṃ mahāmunim । śvetāśvataranāmānaṃ mahāpāśupatottamam ।। bhasmasaṃdigdhasavāṅgaṃ kaupīnācchādanānvitam ।
tapasā karṣitātmānaṃ śuklayajñopavītinam ।। samāpya saṃstavaṃ śaṃbhorānandāstrāvilekṣaṇaḥ । vavande śirasā pādau prāñjalirvākyamabravīt ।। dhanyo asmyanugṛhīto asmi yanme sākṣānmunīśvaraḥ ।
yogīśvaro adya bhagavān dṛṣṭo yogavidāṃ varaḥ ।। aho me sumahadbhāgyaṃ tapāṃsi saphalāni me । kiṃ kariṣyāmi śiṣyo ahaṃ tava māṃ pālayānagha ।। so anugṛhyātha rājānaṃ suśīlaṃ śīlasaṃyutam ।
śiṣyatve parijagrāha tapasā kṣīṇakalpaṣam ।। sāṃnyāsikaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ kārayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ । dadau tadaiśvaraṃ jñānaṃ svaśākhāvihitaṃ vratam ।। aśeṣavedasāraṃ tat paśupāśavimocanam ।
antyāśramamiti khyātaṃ brahmādibhiranuṣṭhitam ।। uvāca śiṣyān saṃprekṣya ye tadāśramavāsinaḥ । brāhmaṇān kṣatriyān vaiśyān brahmacaryaparāyaṇān ।। mayā pravartitāṃ śākhāmadhītyaiveha yoginaḥ ।
samāsate mahādevaṃ dhyāyanto niṣkalaṃ śivam ।। iha devo mahādevo ramamāṇaḥ sahomayā । adhyāste bhagavānīśo bhaktānāmanukampayā ।। ihāśeṣajagaddhātā purā nārāyaṇaḥ svayam ।
ārādhayanmahādevaṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। ihaiva devamīśānaṃ devānāmapi daivatam । ārādhya mahatīṃ siddhiṃ lebhire devadānavāḥ ।। ihaiva munayaḥ pūrvaṃ marīcyādyā maheśvaram ।
dṛṣṭvā tapobalājjñānaṃ lebhire sārvakālikam ।। tasmāt tvamapi rājendra tapoyogasamanvitaḥ । tiṣṭha nityaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ tataḥ siddhimavāpsyasi ।। evamābhāṣya viprendro devaṃ dhyātvā pinākinam ।
ācacakṣe mahāmantraṃ yathāvat svārthasiddhaye ।। sarvapāpopaśamanaṃ vedasāraṃ vimuktidam । agnirityādikaṃ puṇyamṛṣibhiḥ saṃpravartitam ।। so api tadvacanād rājā suśīlaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ ।
sākṣāt pāśupato bhūtvā vedābhyāsarato abhavat ।। bhasmoddhūlitasarvāṅgaḥ kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ । śānto dānto jitakrodhaḥ saṃnyāsavidhimāśritaḥ ।। havirdhānastathāgneyyāṃ janayāmāsa satsutam ।
prācīnabarhiṣaṃ nāmnā dhanurvedasya pāragam ।। prācīnabarhirbhāgavān sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ । samudratanayāyāṃ vai daśa putrānajījanat ।। pracetasaste vikhyātā rājānaḥ prathitaijasaḥ ।
adhītavantaḥ svaṃ vedaṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।। daśabhyastu pracetobhyo māriṣāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ । dakṣo jajñe mahābhāgo yaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।। sa tu dakṣo maheśena rudreṇa saha dhīmatā ।
kṛtvā vivādaṃ rudreṇa śaptaḥ prācetaso abhavat ।। samāyāntaṃ mahādevo dakṣaṃ devyā gṛhaṃ haraḥ । dṛṣṭvā yathocitāṃ pūjāṃ dakṣāya pradadau svayam ।। tadā vai tamasāviṣṭaḥ so adikāṃ brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।
pūjāmanarhāmanvicchan jagāma kupito gṛham ।। kadācit svagṛhaṃ prāptāṃ satīṃ dakṣaḥ sudurmanāḥ । bhartrā saha vinindyaināṃ bhartsayāmasā vai ruṣā ।। anye jāmātaraḥ śreṣṭhā bhartustava pinākinaḥ ।
tvamapyasatsutāsmākaṃ gṛhād gaccha yathāgatam ।। tasya tadvākyamākarṇya sā devī śaṅkarapriyā । vinindya pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ dadāhātmānamātmanā ।। praṇamya paśubhartāraṃ bhartāraṃ kṛttivāsasam ।
himavadduhitā sābhūt tapasā tasya toṣitā ।। jñātvā tadbhāgavān rudraḥ prapannārtiharo haraḥ । śaśāpa dakṣaṃ kupitaḥ samāgatyātha tadgṛham ।। tyaktvā dehamimaṃ brahman kṣatriyāṇāṃ kulodbhavaḥ ।
svasyāṃ sutāyāṃ mūḍhātmā putramutpādayiṣyasi ।। evamuktvā mahādevo yayau kālāsaparvatam । svāyaṃbhuvo api kālena dakṣaḥ prācetaso abhavat ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya tu ।
visargaṃ dakṣaparyantaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ pāpanāśanam ।। devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca gandharvoragarakṣasām । utpattiṃ vistarāt sūta brūhi vaivasvate antare ।। sa śaptaḥ śaṃbhunā pūrvaṃ dakṣaḥ prācetaso nṛpaḥ ।
kimakārṣonmahābuddhe śrotumicchāma sāṃpratam ।। vakṣye nārāyaṇenoktaṃ pūrvakalpānuṣaṅgikam । trikālabaddhaṃ pāpaghnaṃ prajāsargasya vistaram ।। sa śaptaḥ śaṃbhunā pūrvaṃ dakṣaḥ prācetaso nṛpaḥ ।
vinindya pūrvavaireṇa gaṅgādvare ayajad bhavam ।। devāśca sarve bhāgārthamāhūtā viṣṇunā saha । sahaiva munibhiḥ sarvairāgatā munipuṅgavāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā devakulaṃ kṛtsnaṃ śaṅkareṇa vināgatam ।
dadhīco nāma viprarṣiḥ prācetasamathābravīt ।। brahmādayaḥ piśācāntā yasyājñānuvidhāyinaḥ । sa devaḥ sāṃprataṃ rudro vidhinā kiṃ na pūjyate ।। sarveṣveva hi yajñeṣu na bhāgaḥ parikalpitaḥ ।
na mantrā bhāryayā sārdhaṃ śaṅkarasyeti nejyate ।। vihasya dakṣaṃ kupito vacaḥ prāha mahāmuniḥ । śṛṇvatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ sarvajñānamayaḥ svayam ।। yataḥ pravṛttirviśveṣāṃ yaścāsya parameśvaraḥ ।
saṃpūjyate sarvayajñairviditvā kila śaṅkaraḥ ।। na hyaṃ śaṅkaro rudraḥ saṃhartā tāmaso haraḥ । nagnaḥ kapālī vikṛto viśvātmā nopapadyate ।। īśvaro hi jagatstraṣṭā prabhurnārāyaṇaḥ svarāṭ ।
sattvātmako asau bhagavānijyate sarvakarmasu ।। kiṃ tvayā bhagavāneṣa sahastrāṃśurna dṛśyate । sarvalokaikasaṃhartā kālātmā parameśvaraḥ ।। yaṃ gṛṇantīha vidvāṃso dhārmikā brahmavādinaḥ ।
so ayaṃ sākṣī tīvrarociḥ kālātmā śāṅkarītanuḥ ।। eṣa rudro mahādevaḥ kaparde ca ghṛṇī haraḥ । ādityo bhagavān sūryo nīlagrīvo vilohitaḥ ।। saṃstūyate sahastrāṃśuḥ sāmagādhvaryuhotṛbhiḥ ।
paśyainaṃ viśvakarmāṇaṃ rudramūrti trayīmayam ।। ya ete dvādaśādityā āgatā yajñabhāginaḥ । sarve sūryā iti jñeyā na hyānyo vidyate raviḥ ।। evamukte tu munayaḥ samāyātā didṛkṣavaḥ ।
bāḍhamityabruvan vākyaṃ tasya sāhāyyakāriṇaḥ ।। tamasāviṣṭamanaso na paśyanti vṛṣadhvajam । sahastraśo atha śataśo bhūya eva vinindyate ।। nindanto vaidikān mantrān sarvabhūtapatiṃ haram ।
apūjayan dakṣavākyaṃ mohitā viṣṇumāyayā ।। devāśca sarve bhāgārthamāgatā vāsavādayaḥ । nāpaśyan devamīśānamṛte nārāyaṇaṃ harim ।। hiraṇyagarbho bhagavān brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ ।
paśyatāmeva sarveṣāṃ kṣaṇādantaradhīyata ।। antarhite bhagavati dakṣo nārāyaṇaṃ harim । rakṣakaṃ jagatāṃ devaṃ jagāma śaraṇaṃ svayam ।। pravartayāmāsa ca taṃ yajñaṃ dakṣo atha nirbhayaḥ ।
rakṣate bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaraṇāgatarakṣakaḥ ।। punaḥ prāha ca taṃ dakṣaṃ dadhīco bhagavānṛṣiḥ । saṃprekṣyarṣigaṇān devān sarvān vai brahmavidviṣaḥ ।। apūjyapūjane caiva pūjyānāṃ cāpyapūjane ।
naraḥ pāpamavāpnoti mahad vai nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। asatāṃ pragraho yatra satāṃ caiva vimānanā । daṇḍo devakṛtastatra sadyaḥ patati dāruṇaḥ ।। evamuktvā tu viprarṣiḥ śaśāpeśvaravidviṣaḥ ।
samāgatān brāhmaṇāṃstān dakṣasāhāyyakāriṇaḥ ।। yasmād bahiṣkṛtā vedā bhavadbhiḥ parameśvaraḥ । vinindito mahādevaḥ śaṅkaro lokavanditaḥ ।। bhaviṣyadhvaṃ trayībāhyāḥ sarve apīśvaravidviṣaḥ ।
nindanto hyaiśvaraṃ mārgaṃ kuśāstrāsaktamānasāḥ ।। mithyādhītasamācārā mithyājñānapralāpinaḥ । prāpya ghoraṃ kaliyugaṃ kalijaiḥ kila pīḍitāḥ ।। tyaktvā tapobalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ gacchadhvaṃ narakān punaḥ ।
bhaviṣyati hṛṣīkeśaḥ svāśrito api parāṅmukhaḥ ।। evamuktvā tu viprarṣirvirarāma taponidhiḥ । jagāma manasā rudramaśeṣāghavināśanam ।। etasminnantare devī mahādevaṃ maheśvaram ।
patiṃ paśupatiṃ devaṃ jñātvaitat prāha sarvadṛk ।। dakṣo yajñena yajate pitā me pūrvajanmani । vinindya bhavato bhāvamātmānaṃ cāpi śaṅkara ।। devāḥ saharṣibhiścāsaṃstatra sāhāyyakāriṇaḥ ।
vināśayāśu taṃ yajñaṃ varamekaṃ vṛṇomyaham ।। evaṃ vijñāpito devyā devo devavaraḥ prabhuḥ । sasarja sahasā rudraṃ dakṣayajñajighāṃsayā ।। sahastraśīrṣapādaṃ ca sahastrākṣaṃ mahābhujam ।
sahastrapāṇiṃ durdharṣaṃ yugāntānalasannibham ।। daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ duṣprekṣyaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam । daṇḍahastaṃ mahānādaṃ śārṅgiṇaṃ bhūtibhūṣaṇam ।। vīrabhadra iti khyātaṃ devadevasamanvitam ।
sa jātamātro deveśamupatasthe kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। tamāha dakṣasya makhaṃ vināśaya śivostviti । vinindya māṃ sa yajate gaṅgādvāre gaṇeśvara ।। tato bandhuprayuktena siṃhenaikena līlayā ।
vīrabhadreṇa dakṣasya vināśamagamat kratuḥ ।। manyunā comayā sṛṣṭā bhadrakālī maheśvarī । tayā ca sārdhaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ samāruhya yayau gaṇaḥ ।। anye sahastraśo rudrā nisṛṣṭāstena dhīmatā ।
romajā iti vikhyātāstasya sāhāyyakāriṇaḥ ।। śūlaśaktigadāhastāṣṭaṅkopalakarāstathā । kālāgnirudrasaṃkāśā nādayanto diśo daśa ।। sarve vṛṣāsanārūḍhāḥ sabhāryāścātibhīṣaṇāḥ ।
samāvṛtya gaṇaśreṣṭhaṃ yayurdakṣamakhaṃ prati ।। sarve śaṃprāpya taṃ deśaṃ gaṅgādvāramiti śrutam । dadṛśuryajñadeśaṃ taṃ dakṣasyāmitatejasaḥ ।। devāṅganāsahastrāḍhyamapsarogītanāditam ।
vīṇāveṇuninādāḍhyaṃ vedavādābhināditam ।। dṛṣṭvā saharṣibhirdevaiḥ samāsīnaṃ prajāpatim । uvāca bhadrayā rudrairvorabhadraḥ smayanniva ।। vayaṃ hyanucarāḥ sarve śarvasyāmitatejasaḥ ।
bhāgābhilapsayā prāptā bhāgān yacchadhvamīpsitān ।। atha cet kasyacidiyamājñā munisurottamāḥ । bhāgo bhavadbhyo deyastu nāsmabhyamiti kathyatām । taṃ brūtājñāpayati yo vetsyāmo hi vayaṃ tataḥ ।।
evamuktā gaṇeśena prajāpatipuraḥ sarāḥ । devā ūcuryajñabhāge na ca mantrā iti prabhum ।। mantrā ūcuḥ surān yūyaṃ tamopahatacetasaḥ । ye nādhvarasya rājānaṃ pūjayadhvaṃ maheśvaram ।।
īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvabhūtatanurharaḥ । pūjyate sarvayajñeṣu sarvābhyudasiddhidaḥ ।। evamuktā apīśānaṃ māyayā naṣṭacetasaḥ । na menire yayurmantrā devān muktvā svamālayam ।।
tataḥ sa rudro bhagavān sabhāryaḥ sagaṇeśvaraḥ । spṛśan karābhyāṃ brahmarṣi dadhīcaṃ prāha devatāḥ ।। mantrāḥ pramāṇaṃ na kṛtā yuṣmābhirbalagarvitaiḥ । yasmāt prasahya tasmād vo nāśayāmyadya garvitam ।।
ityuktvā yajñaśālāṃ tāṃ dadāha gaṇapuṅgavaḥ । gaṇeśvarāśca saṃkruddhā yūpānutpāṭya cikṣipuḥ ।। prastotrā saha hotrā ca aśvaṃ caiva gaṇeśvarāḥ । gṛhītvā bhīṣaṇāḥ sarve gaṅgāstrotasi cikṣipuḥ ।।
vīrabhadro api dīptātmā śakrasyodyacchataḥ karam । vyaṣṭambhayadadīnātmā tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām ।। bhagasya netre cotpāṭya karajāgreṇa līlayā । nihatya muṣṭinā dantān pūṣṇaścaivamapātayat ।।
tathā candramasaṃ devaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā । dharṣayāmāsa balavān smayamāno gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। vahnerhastadvayaṃ chittvā jihvāmutpāṭya līlayā । jaghāna mūrdhni pādena munīnapi munīśvarāḥ ।।
tathā viṣṇuṃ saharuḍaṃ samāyāntaṃ mahābalaḥ । vivyādha niśetairbāṇaiḥ stambhayitvā sudarśanam ।। samālokya mahābāhurāgatya garuḍo gaṇam । jaghāna pakṣaiḥ sahasā nanādāmbunidhiryathā ।।
tataḥ sahastraśo bhadraḥ sasarja garuḍān svayam । vainateyādabhyadhikān garuḍaṃ te pradudruvuḥ ।। tān dṛṣṭvā garuḍo dhīmān palāyata mahājavaḥ । visṛjya mādhavaṃ vegāt tadadbhutamivābhavat ।।
antarhite vainateye bhagavān padmasaṃbhavaḥ । āgatya vārayāmāsa vīrabhadraṃ ca keśavam ।। prasādayāmāsa ca taṃ gauravāt parameṣṭhinaḥ । saṃstūya bhagavānīśaḥ sāmbastatrāgamat svayam ।।
vīkṣya devādhidevaṃ taṃ sāmbaṃ sarvagaṇairvṛtam । tuṣṭāva bhagavān brahmā dakṣaḥ sarve divaukasaḥ ।। viśeṣāt pārvatīṃ devīmīśvarārdhaśarīriṇīm । stotrairnānāvidhairdakṣaḥ praṇamya ca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।
tato bhagavatī devī prahasantī maheśvaram । prasannamānasā rudraṃ vacaḥ prāha ghṛṇānidhiḥ ।। tvameva jagataḥ straṣṭā śāsitā caiva rakṣakaḥ । anugrāhyo bhagavatā dakṣaścāpi divaukasaḥ ।।
tataḥ prahasya bhagavān kaparde nīlalohitaḥ । uvāca praṇatān devān prācetasamatho haraḥ ।। gacchadhvaṃ devatāḥ sarvāḥ prasanno bhavatāmaham । saṃpūjyaḥ sarvayajñeṣu na nindyo ahaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।
tvaṃ cāpi śṛṇu me dakṣa vacanaṃ sarvarakṣaṇam । tyaktvā lokaiṣaṇāmetāṃ madbhakto bhava yatnataḥ ।। bhaviṣyasi gaṇeśānaḥ kalpānte anugrahānmama । tāvat tiṣṭha mamādeśāt svādhikāreṣu nirvṛtaḥ ।।
evamuktvā sa bhagavān sapatnīkaḥ sahānugaḥ । adarśanamanuprāpto dakṣasyāmitatejasaḥ ।। antarhite mahādeve śaṅkare padmasaṃbhavaḥ । vyājahāra svayaṃ dakṣamaśeṣajagato hitam ।।
kiṃ tavāpagato mohaḥ prasanne vṛṣabhadhvaje । yadācaṣṭa svayaṃ devaḥ pālayaitadatandritaḥ ।। sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ hṛdyeṣa vasatīśvaraḥ । paśyantyenaṃ brahmabhūtā vidvāṃso vedavādinaḥ ।।
sa ātmā sarvabhūtānāṃ sa bījaṃ paramā gatiḥ । stūyate vaidikairmantrairdevadevo maheśvaraḥ ।। tamarcayati yo rudraṃ svātmanyekaṃ sanātanam । cetasā bhāvayuktena sa yāti paramaṃ padam ।।
tasmādanādimadhyāntaṃ vijñāya parameśvaram । karmaṇā manasā vācā samārādhaya yatnataḥ ।। yatnāt parihareśasya nindāmātmavināśanīm । bhavanti sarvadoṣāya nindakasya kriyā yataḥ ।।
yastavaiṣa mahāyogī rakṣako viṣṇuravyayaḥ । sa devadevo bhagavān mahādevo na saṃśayaḥ ।। manyante ye jagadyoniṃ vibhinnaṃ viṣṇumīśvarāt । mohādavedaniṣṭhatvāt te yānti narakaṃ narāḥ ।।
vedānuvartino rudraṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ tathā । ekībhāvena paśyanti muktibhājo bhavanti te ।। yo viṣṇuḥ sa svayaṃ rudro yo rudraḥ sa janārdanaḥ । iti matvā yajed devaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।
sṛjatyetajjagat sarvaṃ viṣṇustat paśyatīśvaraḥ । itthaṃ jagat sarvamidaṃ rudranārāyaṇodbhavam ।। tasmāt tyaktvā harernindāṃ viṣṇāvapi samāhitaḥ । samāśrayenmahādevaṃ śaraṇyaṃ brahmavādinām ।।
upaśrutyātha vacanaṃ viriñcasya prajāpatiḥ । jagāma śaraṇaṃ devaṃ gopatiṃ kṛttivāsasam ।। ye anye śāpāgninirdagdhā dadhīcasya maharṣayaḥ । dviṣanto mohitā devaṃ saṃbabhūvuḥ kaliṣvatha ।।
tyaktvā tapobalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ viprāṇāṃ kulasaṃbhavāḥ । pūrvasaṃskāramahātmyād brahmaṇo vacanādiha ।। muktaśāpāstataḥ sarve kalpānte rauravādiṣu । nipātyamānāḥ kālena saṃprāpyādityavarcasam ।
brahmāṇaṃ jagatāmīśamanujñātāḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।। samārādhya tapoyogādīśānaṃ tridaśādhipam । bhaviṣyanti yathā pūrvaṃ śaṅkarasya prasādataḥ ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ dakṣayajñaniṣūdanam ।
śṛṇudhvaṃ dakṣaputrīṇāṃ sarvāsāṃ caiva saṃtatim ।। prajāḥ sṛjeti vyādiṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣaḥ svayaṃbhuvā । sasarja devān gandharvān ṛṣīṃścaivāsuroragān ।। yadāsya sṛjamānasya na vyavardhanta tāḥ prajāḥ ।
tadā sasarja bhūtāni maithunenaiva dharmataḥ ।। asiknyāṃ janayāmāsa vīraṇasya prajāpateḥ । sutāyāṃ dharmayuktāyāṃ putrāṇāṃ tu sahastrakam ।। teṣu putreṣu naṣṭeṣu māyayā nāradasya saḥ ।
ṣaṣṭiṃ dakṣo asṛjat kanyā vairaṇyāṃ vai prajāpatiḥ ।। dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa । viṃśat sapta ca somāya catastro ariṣṭanemine ।। dve caiva bahuputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate ।
dve caivāṅgirase tadvat tāsāṃ vakṣye atha nistaram ।। arundhatī vasurjāmī lambā bhānurmarutvatī । saṃkalpā ca muhūrtā ca sādhyā viśvā ca bhāminī ।। dharmapatnyo daśa tvetāstāsāṃ putrān nibodhata ।
viśvāyā viśvadevāstu sādhyā sādhyānajījanat ।। marutvanto marutvatyāṃ vasavo aṣṭau vasoḥ sutāḥ । bhānostu bhānavaścaiva muhūrtā vai muhūrtajāḥ ।। lambāyāścātha ghoṣo vai nāgavīthī tu jāmijā ।
pṛthivīviṣayaṃ sarvamarundatyāmajāyata । saṃkalpāyāstu saṃkalpo dharmaputrā daśa smṛtāḥ ।। āpo dhruvaśca somaśca dharaścaivānilo analaḥ । pratyūṣaśca prabhāsaśca vasavo aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ ।।
āpasya putro vaitaṇḍyaḥ śramaḥ śrānto dhunistathā । dhruvasya putro bhagavān kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।। somasya bhagavān varcā dharasya draviṇaḥ sutaḥ । purojavo anilasya syādavijñātagatistathā ।।
kumāro hyanalasyāsīt senāpatiriti smṛtaḥ । devalo bhagavān yogī pratyūṣasyābhavat sutaḥ । viśvakarmā prabhāsasya śilpakartā prajāpatiḥ ।। aditirditirdanustadvadariṣṭā surasā tathā ।
surabhirvinatā caiva tāmra krodhavaśā irā । kadrurmuniśca dharmajñā tatputrān vai nibodhata ।। aṃśo dhātā bhagastvaṣṭā mitro atha varuṇor'yamā । vivasvān savitā pūṣā hyaṃśumān viṣṇureva ca ।।
tuṣitā nāma te pūrvaṃ cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ । vaivasvate antare proktā ādityāścāditeḥ sutāḥ ।। ditiḥ putradvayaṃ lebhe kaśyapād balasaṃyutam । hiraṇyakaśipuṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ tathāparam ।।
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityo mahābalaparākramaḥ । ārādhya tapasā devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam । dṛṣṭvālebhevarān divyān stutvāsau vividhaiḥ stavai ।। atha tasya balād devāḥ sarva eva surarṣayaḥ ।
bādhitāstāḍitā jagmurdevadevaṃ pitāmaham ।। śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ devaṃ śaṃbhuṃ sarvajaganmayam । brahmāṇaṃ lokakartāraṃ trātāraṃ puruṣaṃ param । kūṭasthaṃ jagatāmekaṃ purāṇaṃ puruṣottamam ।।
sa yācito devavarairmunibhiśca munīśvarāḥ । sarvadevahitārthāya jagāma kamalāsanaḥ ।। saṃstūyamānaḥ praṇatairmunīndrairamarairapi । kṣīrodasyottaraṃ kūlaṃ yatrāste harirīśvaraḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ jagadyoniṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvaguruṃ śivam । vavande caraṇau mūrdhnā kṛtāñjalirabhāṣata ।। tvaṃ gatiḥ sarvabhūtānāmananto asyakhilātmakaḥ । vyāpī sarvāmaravapurmahāyogī sanātanaḥ ।।
tvamātmā sarvabhūtānāṃ pradhānaṃ prakṛtiḥ parā । vairāgyaiśvaryanirato rāgātīto nirañjanaḥ ।। tvaṃ kartā caiva bhartā ca nihantā suravidviṣām । trātumarhasyananteśa trātā hi parameśvaraḥ ।।
itthaṃ sa viṣṇurbhagavān brahmaṇā saṃprabodhitaḥ । provāconnidrapadmākṣaḥ pītavāsāsuradviṣaḥ ।। kimarthaṃ sumahāvīryāḥ saprajāpatikāḥ surāḥ । imaṃ deśamanuprāptāḥ kiṃ vā kāryaṃ karomi vaḥ ।।
hiraṇyakaśipurnāma brahmaṇo varadarpitaḥ । bādhate bhagavan daityo devān sarvān saharṣibhiḥ ।। avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tvāmṛte puruṣottama । hantumarhasi sarveṣāṃ tvaṃ trātāsi jaganmaya ।।
śrutvā taddaivatairuktaṃ sa viṣṇurlokabhāvanaḥ । vadhāya daityamukhyasya so asṛjat puruṣaṃ svayam ।। meruparvatavarṣmāṇaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayānakam । śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ taṃ prāha garuḍadhvajaḥ ।।
hatvā taṃ daityarājaṃ tvaṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ punaḥ । imaṃ deśaṃ samāgantuṃ kṣipramarhasi pauruṣāt ।। niśamya vaiṣṇavaṃ vākyaṃ praṇamya puruṣottamam । mahāpuruṣamavyaktaṃ yayau daityamahāpuram ।।
vimuñcan bhairavaṃ nādaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ । āruhya garuḍaṃ devo mahāmerurivāparaḥ ।। ākarṇya daityapravarā mahāmegharavopamam । samācacakṣire nādaṃ tadā daityapaterbhayāt ।।
kaścidāgacchati mahān puruṣo devacoditaḥ । vimuñcan bhairavaṃ nādaṃ taṃ jānīmo amarārdana ।। tataḥ sahāsuravarairhiraṇyakaśipuḥ svayam । saṃnaddhaiḥ sāyudhaiḥ putraiḥ prahrādādyaistadā yayau ।।
dṛṣṭvā taṃ garuḍāsīnaṃ sūryakoṭisamaprabham । puruṣaṃ parvatākāraṃ nārāyaṇamivāparam ।। dudruvuḥ kecidanyonmamūcuḥ saṃbhrāntalocanāḥ । ayaṃ sa devo devānāṃ goptā nārāyaṇo ripuḥ ।।
asmākamavyayo nūnaṃ tatsuto vā samāgataḥ । ityuktvā śastravarṣāṇi sasṛjuḥ puruṣāya te । tāni cāśeṣato devo nāśayāmāsa līlayā ।। tadā hiraṇyakaśipoścatvāraḥ prathitaujasaḥ ।
putrā nārāyaṇodbhūtaṃ yuyudhurmeghaniḥ svanāḥ । prahrādaścāpyanuhrādaḥ saṃhrādo hrāda eva ca ।। prahrādaḥ prāhiṇod brāhmamanuhrādo atha vaiṣṇavam । saṃhrādaścāpi kaumāramāgneyaṃ hrāda eva ca ।।
tāni taṃ puruṣaṃ prāpya catvāryastrāṇi vaiṣṇavam । na śekurbādhituṃ viṣṇuṃ vāsudevaṃ yathā tathā ।। athāsau caturaḥ putrān mahābāhurmahābalaḥ । pragṛhya pādeṣu karaiḥ saṃcikṣepa nanāda ca ।।
vimukteṣvatha putreṣu hiraṇyakaśipuḥ svayam । pādena tāḍayāmāsa vegenorasi taṃ balī ।। sa tena pīḍito atyarthaṃ garuḍena tathā'śugaḥ । adṛśyaḥ prayayau tūrṇaṃ yatra nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।
gatvā vijñāpayāmāsa pravṛttamakhilaṃ tathā ।। saṃcintya manasā devaḥ sarvajñānamayo amalaḥ । narasyārdhatanuṃ kṛtvā siṃhasyārdhatanuṃ tathā ।। nṛsiṃhavapuravyakto hiraṇyakaśipoḥ pure ।
āvirbabhūva sahasā mohayan daityapuṅgavān ।। daṃṣṭrākarālo yogātmā yugāntadahanopamaḥ । samāruhyātmanaḥ śaktiṃ sarvasaṃhārakārikām । bhāti nārāyaṇo ananto yathā madhyandine raviḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā nṛsiṃhavapuṣaṃ prahrādaṃ jyeṣṭhaputrakam । vadhāya prerayāmāsa narasihasya so asuraḥ ।। imaṃ nṛsiṃhavapuṣaṃ pūrvasmād bahuśaktikam । sahaiva tvanujaiḥ sarvairnāśayāśu mayeritaḥ ।।
tatsaṃniyogādasuraḥ prahrādo viṣṇumavyayam । yuyudhe sarvayatnena narasiṃhena nirjitaḥ ।। tataḥ saṃcodito daityo hiraṇyākṣastadānujaḥ । dhyātvā paśupaterastraṃ sasarja ca nanāda ca ।।
tasya devādidevasya viṣṇoramitatejasaḥ । na hānimakarodastraṃ yathā devasya śūlinaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā parāhataṃ tvastraṃ prahrādo bhāgyagauravāt । mene sarvātmakaṃ devaṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam ।।
saṃtyajya sarvaśastrāṇi sattvayuktena cetasā । nanāma śirasā devaṃ yogināṃ hṛdayeśayam ।। stutvā nārāyaṇaiḥ stotraiḥ ṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃbhavaiḥ । nivārya pitaraṃ bhrātṛn hiraṇyākṣaṃ tadābravīt ।।
ayaṃ nārāyaṇo anantaḥ śāśvato bhagavānajaḥ । purāṇapuruṣo devo mahāyogī jaganmayaḥ ।। ayaṃ dhātā vidhātā ca svayañjyotirnirañjanaḥ । pradhānapuruṣastattvaṃ mūlaprakṛtiravyayaḥ ।।
īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāmantaryāmī guṇātigaḥ । gacchadhvamenaṃ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇumavyaktamavyayam ।। evamukte sudurbuddhirhiraṇyakaśipuḥ svayam । provāca putramatyarthaṃ mohito viṣṇumāyayā ।।
ayaṃ sarvātmanā vadhyo nṛsiṃho alpaparākramaḥ । samāgato asmadbhavanamidānīṃ kālacoditaḥ ।। vihasya pitaraṃ putro vacaḥ prāha mahāmatiḥ । mā nindasvainamīśānaṃ bhūtānāmekamavyayam ।।
kathaṃ devo mahādevaḥ śāśvataḥ kālavarjitaḥ । kālena hanyate viṣṇuḥ kālātmā kālarūpadhṛk ।। tataḥ suvarṇakaśipurdurātmā vidhicoditaḥ । nivārito api putreṇa yuyodha harimavyayam ।।
saṃraktanayano anto hiraṇyanayanāgrajam । nakhairvidārayāmāsa prahrādasyaiva paśyataḥ ।। hate hiraṇyakaśipau hiraṇyākṣo mahābalaḥ । visṛjya putraṃ prahrādaṃ dudruve bhayavihvalaḥ ।।
anuhrādādayaḥ putrā anye ca śataśo asurāḥ । nṛsiṃhadehasaṃbhūtaiḥ siṃhairnotā yamālayam ।। tataḥ saṃhṛtya tadrūpaṃ harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ । svameva paramaṃ rūpaṃ yayau nārāyaṇāhvayam ।।
gate nārāyaṇe daityaḥ prahrādo asurasattamaḥ । abhiṣekeṇa yuktena hiraṇyākṣamayojayat ।। sa bādhayāmāsa surān raṇe jitvā munīnapi । labdhvāndhakaṃ mahāputraṃ tapasārādhya śaṅkaram ।।
devāñjitvā sadevendrān badhvāca dharaṇīmimām । nītvā rasātalaṃ cakre vandīmindīvaraprabhām ।। tataḥ sabrahmakā devāḥ parimlānamukhaśriyaḥ । gatvā vijñāpayāmāsurviṣṇave harimandiram ।।
sa cintayitvā viśvātmā tadvadhopāyamavyayaḥ । sarvedevamayaṃ śubhraṃ vārāhaṃ vapurādadhe ।। gatvā hiraṇyanayanaṃ hatvā taṃ puruṣottamaḥ । daṃṣṭrayoddhārayāmāsa kalpādau dharaṇīmimām ।।
tyaktvā varāhasaṃsthānaṃ saṃsthāpya ca suradvijān svāmeva prakṛtiṃ divyāṃ yayau viṣṇuḥ paraṃ padam ।। tasmin hate amararipau prahrādau viṣṇutatparaḥ । apālayat svakaṃrājyaṃ bhāvaṃ tyaktvā tadā'suram ।। iyāja vidhivad devān viṣṇorārādhane rataḥ ।
niḥ sapatnaṃ tadā rājyaṃ tasyāsīd viṣṇuvaibhavāt ।। tataḥ kadācidasuro brāhmaṇaṃ gṛhamāgatam । tāpasaṃ nārcayāmāsa devānāṃ caiva māyayā ।। sa tena tāpaso atyarthaṃ mohitenāvamānitaḥ ।
śaśāpāsurarājānaṃ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ ।। yattadvalaṃ samāśritya brāhmaṇānavamanyase । sā bhaktirvaiṣṇavī divyā vināśaṃ te gamiṣyati ।। ityuktvā prayayau tūrṇaṃ prahrādasya gṛhād dvijaḥ ।
mumoha rājyasaṃsaktaḥ so api śāpabalāt tataḥ ।। bādhayāmāsa viprendrān na viveda janārdanam । piturvadhamanusmṛtya krodhaṃ cakre hariṃ prati ।। tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam ।
nārāyaṇasya devasya prahrādasyāmaradviṣaḥ ।। kṛtvā tu sumahad yuddhaṃ viṣṇunā tena nirjitaḥ । purvasaṃskāramāhātmyāt parasmin puruṣe harau । saṃjātaṃ tasya vijñānaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau ।।
tataḥ prabhṛti daityendro hyananyāṃ bhaktimudvahan । nārāyaṇe mahāyogamavāpa puruṣottame ।। hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putre yogasaṃsaktacetasi । avāpa tanmahad rājyamandhako asurapuṅgavaḥ ।।
hiraṇyanetratanayaḥ śaṃbhordehasamudbhavaḥ । mandarasthāmumāṃ devīṃ cakame parvatātmajām ।। purā dāruvane puṇye munayo gṛhamedhinaḥ । īśvarārādhanārthāya tapaśceruḥ sahastraśaḥ ।।
tataḥ kadācinmahati kālayogena dustarā । anāvṛṣṭiratīvogrā hyāsīd bhūtavināśinī ।। sametya sarve munayo gautamaṃ tapasāṃ nidhim । ayācanta kṣudhāviṣṭā āhāraṃ prāṇadhāraṇam ।।
sa tebhyaḥ pradadāvannaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ bahutaraṃ budhaḥ । sarve bubujire viprā nirviśaṅkena cetasā ।। gate tu dvādaśe varṣe kalpānta iva śaṅkarī । babhūva vṛṣṭirmahatī yathāpūrvamabhūjjagat ।।
tataḥ sarve munivarāḥ samāmantrya parasparam । maharṣi gautamaṃ procurgacchāma iti vegataḥ ।। nivārayāmāsa ca tān kañcit kālaṃ yathāsukham । uṣitvā madgṛhe avaśyaṃ gacchadhvamiti paṇḍitāḥ ।।
tato māyāmayīṃ sṛṣṭvā kṛśāṃ gāṃ sarva eva te । samīpaṃ prāpayāmāsugautamasya mahātmanaḥ ।। so anuvīkṣya kṛpāviṣṭastasyāḥ saṃrakṣaṇotsukaḥ । goṣṭhe tāṃ bandhayāmāsa spṛṣṭamātrā mamāra sā ।।
sa śokenābhisaṃtaptaḥ kāryākāryaṃ mahāmuniḥ । na paśyati sma sahasā tādṛśaṃ munayo abruvan ।। govadhyeyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha yāvat tava śarīragā । tāvat te annaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ gacchāmo vayameva hi ।।
tena te muditāḥ santo devadāruvanaṃ śubham । jagmuḥ pāpavaśaṃ nītāstapaścartuṃ yathā purā ।। sa teṣāṃ māyayā jātāṃ govadhyāṃ gautamo muniḥ । kenāpi hetunā jñātvā śaśāpātīvakopanaḥ ।।
bhaviṣyanti trayībāhyā mahāpātakibhiḥ samāḥ । babhūvuste tathā śāpājjāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। sarve saṃprāpya deveśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ viṣṇumavyayam । astuvan laukikaiḥ stotrairucchiṣṭā iva sarvagau ।।
devadevau mahādevau bhaktānāmārtināśanau । kāmavṛttyā mahāyogau pāpānnastrātumarhathaḥ ।। tadā pārśvasthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ saṃprekṣya vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ । kimeteṣāṃ bhavet kāryaṃ prāha puṇyaiṣiṇāmiti ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaraṇyo bhaktavatsalaḥ । gopatiṃ prāha viprendrānālokya praṇatān hariḥ ।। na vedabāhye puruṣe puṇyaleśo api śaṅkara । saṃgacchate mahādeva dharmo vedād vinirbabhau ।।
tathāpi bhaktavātsalyād rakṣitavyā maheśvara । asmābhiḥ sarva eveme gantāro narakānapi ।। tasmād vai vedabāhyānāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya pāpinām । vimohanāya śāstrāṇi kariṣyāmo vṛṣadhvaja ।।
evaṃ saṃbodhito rudro mādhavena murāriṇā । cakāra mohaśāstrāṇi keśavo api śiveritaḥ ।। kāpālaṃ nākulaṃ vāmaṃ bhairavaṃ pūrvapaścimam । pañcarātraṃ pāśupataṃ tathānyāni sahastraśaḥ ।।
sṛṣṭvā tānūcaturdevau kurvāṇāḥ śāstracoditam । patanto niraye ghore bahūn kalpān punaḥ punaḥ ।। jāyanto mānuṣe loke kṣīṇapāpacayāstataḥ । īśvarārādhanabalād gacchadhvaṃ sukṛtāṃ gatim ।
vartadhvaṃ matprasādena nānyathā niṣkṛtirhi vaḥ ।। evamīśvaraviṣṇubhyāṃ coditāste maharṣayaḥ । ādeśaṃ pratyapadyanta śirasāsuravidviṣoḥ ।। cakruste anyāni śāstrāṇi tatra tatra ratāḥ punaḥ ।
śiṣyānadhyāpayāmāsurdarśayitvā phalāni tu ।। mohayanta imaṃ lokamavatīrya mahītale । cakāra śaṅkaro bhikṣāṃ hitāyaiṣāṃ dvijaiḥ saha ।। kapālamālābharaṇaḥ pretabhasmāvaguṇṭhitaḥ ।
vimohayaṃllokamimaṃ jaṭāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitaḥ ।। nikṣipya pārvatīṃ devīṃ viṣṇāvamitatejasi । niyojyāṅgabhavaṃ rudraṃ bhairavaṃ duṣṭanigrahe ।। dattvā nārāyaṇe devīṃ nandinaṃ kulanandinam ।
saṃsthāpya tatra gaṇapān devānindrapurogamān ।। prasthite atha mahādeve viṣṇurviśvatanuḥ svayam । strīrūpadhārī niyataṃ sevate sma maheśvarīm ।। brahmā hutāśanaḥ śakro yamo anye surapuṅgavāḥ ।
siṣevire mahādevīṃ strīveśaṃ śobhanaṃ gatāḥ ।। nandīśvaraśca bhagavān śaṃbhoratyantavallabhaḥ । dvāradeśe gaṇādhyakṣo yathāpūrvamatiṣṭhata ।। etasminnantare daityo hyandhako nāma durmatiḥ ।
āhartukāmo girijāmājagāmātha mandaram ।। saṃprāptamandhakaṃ dṛṣṭvā śaṅkaraḥ kālabhairavaḥ । nyaṣedhayadameyātmā kālarūpadharo haraḥ ।। tayoḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam ।
śūlenorasi taṃ daityamājaghāna vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। tataḥ sahastraśo daityaḥ sasarjāndhakasaṃjñitān । nandiṣeṇādayo daityairandhakairabhinirjitāḥ ।। ghaṇṭākarṇo meghanādaścaṇḍeśaścaṇḍatāpanaḥ ।
vināyako meghavāhaḥ somanandī ca vaidyutaḥ ।। sarve andhakaṃ daityavaraṃ saṃprāpyātibalānvitāḥ । yuyudhuḥ śūlaśaktyṛṣṭigirikūṭaparaśvadhaiḥ ।। bhrāmayitvātha hastābhyāṃ gṛhītacaraṇadvayāḥ ।
daityendreṇātibalinā kṣiptāste śatayojanam ।। tato andhakanisṛṣṭāste śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ । kālasūryapratīkāśā bhairavaṃ tvabhidudruvuḥ ।। hā heti śabdaḥ sumahān babhūvātibhayaṅkaraḥ ।
yuyodha bhairavo rudraḥ śūlamādāya bhīṣaṇam ।। dṛṣṭvāndhakānāṃ subalaṃ durjayaṃ tarjito haraḥ । jagāma śaraṇaṃ devaṃ vāsudevamajaṃ vibhum ।। so asṛjad bhagavān viṣṇurdevīnāṃ śatamuttamam ।
devīpārśvasthito devo vināśāyāmaradviṣām ।। tathāndhakasahastraṃ tu devībhiryamasādanam । nītaṃ keśavamāhātmyāllīlayaiva raṇājire ।। dṛṣṭvā parāhataṃ sainyamandhako api mahāsuraḥ ।
parāṅmukhoraṇāt tasmāt palāyata mahājavaḥ ।। tataḥ krīḍāṃ mahādevaḥ kṛtvā dvādaśavārṣikīm । hitāya loke bhaktānāmājagāmātha mandaram ।। saṃprāptamīśvaraṃ jñātvā sarva eva gaṇeśvarāḥ ।
samāgamyopatasthustaṃ bhānumantamiva dvijāḥ ।। praviśya bhavanaṃ puṇyamayuktānāṃ durāsadam । dadarśa nandinaṃ devaṃ bhairavaṃ keśavaṃ śivaḥ ।। praṇāmapravaṇaṃ devaṃ so anugṛhyātha nandinam ।
āghrāya mūrdhanīśānaḥ keśavaṃ pariṣasvaje ।। dṛṣṭvā devī mahādevaṃ prītivisphāritekṣaṇā । nanāma śirasā tasya pādayorīśvarasya sā ।। nivedya vijayaṃ tasmai śaṅkarāyātha śaṅkarī ।
bhairavo viṣṇumāhātmyaṃ praṇataḥ pārśvago avadat ।। śrutvā tadvijayaṃ śaṃbhurvikramaṃ keśavasya ca । samāste bhagavānīśo devyā saha varāsane ।। tato devagaṇāḥ sarve marīcipramukhā dvijāḥ ।
ājagmurmandaraṃ druṣṭaṃ devadevaṃ trilocanam ।। yena tad vijitaṃ pūrvaṃ devīnāṃ śatamuttamam । samāgataṃ daityasainyamīśdarśanavāñchayā ।। dṛṣṭvā varāsanāsīnaṃ devyā candravibhūṣaṇam ।
praṇemurādarād devyo gāyanti smātilālasāḥ ।। praṇemurgirijāṃ devīṃ vāmapārśve pinākinaḥ । devāsanagataṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam ।। dṛṣṭvā siṃhāsanāsīnaṃ devyā nārāyaṇena ca ।
praṇamya devamīśānaṃ pṛṣṭavatyo varāṅganāḥ ।। kastvaṃ vibhrājase kāntyā keyaṃ bālaraviprabhā । ko anvayaṃ bhti vapuṣā paṅkajāyatalocanaḥ ।। niśamya tāsāṃ vacanaṃ vṛṣendravaravāhanaḥ ।
vyājahāra mahāyogī bhūtādhipatiravyayaḥ ।। ahaṃ nārāyaṇo gaurī jaganmātā sanātanī । vibhajya saṃsthito devaḥ svātmānaṃ bahudheśvaraḥ ।। na me viduḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ devādyā na maharṣayaḥ ।
eko ayaṃ veda viśvātmā bhavānī viṣṇureva ca ।। ahaṃ hi niṣkriyaḥ śāntaḥ kevalo niṣparigrahaḥ । māmeva keśavaṃ devamāhurdevīmathāmbikām ।। eṣa dhātā vidhātā ca kāraṇaṃ kāryameva ca ।
kartā kārayitā viṣṇurbhuktimuktiphalapradaḥ ।। bhoktā pumānaprameyaḥ saṃhartā kālarūpadhṛk । straṣṭā pātā vāsudevo viśvātmā viśvatomukhaḥ ।। kṛṭastho hyakṣaro vyāpī yogī nārāyaṇaḥ svayam ।
tārakaḥ puruṣo hyātmā kevalaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। saiṣā māheśvarī gaurī mama śaktirnirañjanā । sāntā satyā sadānandā paraṃ padamiti śrutiḥ ।। asyāḥ sarvamidaṃ jātamatraiva layameṣyati ।
eṣaiva sarvabhūtānāṃ gatīnāmuttamā gatiḥ ।। tayāhaṃ saṃgato devyā kevalo niṣkalaḥ paraḥ । paśyāmyaśeṣamevedaṃ yastad veda sa mucyate ।। tasmādanādimadvaitaṃ viṣṇumātmānamīśvaram ।
ekameva vijānīdhvaṃ tato yāsyatha nirvṛtim ।। manyante viṣṇumavyaktamātmānaṃ śraddhayānvitāḥ । ye bhinnadṛṣṭyāpīśānaṃ pūjayanto na me priyāḥ ।। dviṣanti ye jagatsūtiṃ mohitā rauravādiṣu ।
pacyamānā na mucyante kalpakoṭiśatairapi ।। tasamādaśeṣabhūtānāṃ rakṣako viṣṇuravyayaḥ । yathāvadiha vijñāya dhyeyaḥ sarvāpadi prabhuḥ ।। śrutvā bhagavato vākyaṃ devyaḥ sarvagaṇeśvarāḥ ।
nemurnārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ devīṃ ca himaśailajām ।। prārthayāmāsurīśāne bhaktiṃ bhaktajanapriye । bhavānīpādayugale nārāyaṇapadāmbuje ।। tato nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ gaṇeśā mātaro api ca ।
na paśyanti jagatsūtiṃ tadbhutamivābhavat ।। tadantare mahādaityo hyandhako manmathārditaḥ । mohito girijāṃ devīmāhartuṃ girimāyayau ।। athānantavapuḥ śrīmān yogī nārāyaṇo amalaḥ ।
tatraivāvirabhūd daityairyuddhāya puruṣottamaḥ ।। yuddhāya viṣṇuṃ gaṇadevamukhyaiḥ । sa kālarudro abhijagāma devaḥ ।। sa devadevaḥ prayayau purastāt ।
jagāma devo api sahastrabāhuḥ ।। vivāhano vāridavarṇavarṇaḥ । strilokadṛṣṭirbhagavānivārkaḥ ।। haraḥ sahastrākṛtirāvirāsīt ।
papāta devopari puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ ।। samāvṛtaṃ devaripurgaṇeśaiḥ । r gaṇairaśeṣairamapapradhānaiḥ ।। sa saṃyuge śaṃbhumanantadhāma ।
vimānamāruhya vihīnasattvaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvāndhakaṃ samayāntaṃ bhagavān garuḍadhvajaḥ । vyājahāra mahādevaṃ bhairavaṃ bhūtibhūṣaṇam ।। hantumarhasi daityeśamandhakaṃ lokakaṇṭakam ।
tvāmṛte bhagavān śakto hantā nānyo asya vidyate ।। tvaṃ hartā sarvalokānāṃ kālātmā hyaiśvarī tanuḥ । stūyate vividhairmantrarvedavidbhirvicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। sa vāsudevasya vaco niśamya bhagavān haraḥ ।
nirīkṣya viṣṇuṃ hanane daityandrasya matiṃ dadhau ।। jagāma devatānīkaṃ gaṇānāṃ harṣamuttamam । stuvanti bhairavaṃ devamantarikṣacarā janāḥ ।। jayānanta mahādeva kālamūrte sanātana ।
tvamagniḥ sarvabhūtānāmantaścarasi nityaśaḥ ।। tvaṃ yatrajñastvaṃ vaṣaṭkārastvaṃ dhātā hariravyayaḥ । tvaṃ brahmā tvaṃ mahādevastvaṃ dhāma paramaṃ padam ।। oṅkāramūrtiryogātmā trayīnetrastrilocanaḥ ।
mahāvibhūtirdeveśo jayāśeṣajagatpate ।। tataḥ kālāgnirudro asau gṛhītvāndhakamīśvaraḥ । triśūlāgreṣu vinyasya prananarta satāṃ gatiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvāndhakaṃ devagaṇāḥ śūlaprotaṃ pitāmahaḥ ।
praṇemurīśvaraṃ devaṃ bhairavaṃ bhavamocakam ।। astuvan munayaḥ siddhā jagurgandharvikiṃnarāḥ । antarikṣe apsaraḥ saṅghā nṛtyantisma manoramāḥ ।। saṃsthāpito athaśūlāgre so andhako dagdhakilbiṣaḥ ।
utpannākhilavijñānastuṣṭāva parameśvaram ।। samāhitā yaṃ vidurīśatattvam । kālaṃ kaviṃ yogaviyogahetum ।। hutāśavaktraṃ jvalanārkarūpam ।
bhavantamekaṃ praṇamāmi rudram ।। vibhāgahīnāmalatattvarūpa । vāyvādibhedairakhilātmarūpa ।। ādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt ।
tvamantako yogigaṇābhijuṣṭaḥ ।। deheṣu dehādiviśeṣahīnaḥ । bhavantamāhuḥ śivameva kecit ।। mānandarūpaṃ praṇavābhidhānam ।
svayaṃ prabho aśeṣaviśeṣahīnaḥ ।। haṃsaḥ prāṇo mṛtyurantāsi yajñaḥ । nīlagrīvaḥ stūyase vedavidbhiḥ ।। pitāmahastvaṃ prapitāmahaśca ।
sadāśivastvaṃ parameśvaro asi ।। parātmane pañcapadāntarāya । sahastraśaktyāsanasaṃsthitāya ।। jagannivāsāya jaganmayāya ।
namo janānāṃ hṛdi saṃsthitāya ।। munīndrasiddhārcitapādayugma । namaḥ parāntāya bhavodbhavāya ।। namo astu te soma sumadhyamāya ।
namo ambikāyāḥ pataye mṛḍāya ।। vedāntavijñānasuniścitāya । namo maheśāya namaḥ śivāya ।। evaṃ stuvantaṃ bhagavān śūlāgrādavaropya tam ।
tuṣṭaḥ provāca hastābhyāṃ spṛṣṭvātha parameśvaraḥ ।। prīto ahaṃ sarvathā daitya stavenānena sāṃpratam । saṃprāpya gāṇapatyaṃ me sannidhāne vasāmaraḥ ।। arogaśchinnasaṃdeho devairapi supūjitaḥ ।
nandīśvarasyānucaraḥ sarvaduḥ khavivarjitaḥ ।। evaṃ vyāhṛtamātre tu devadevena devatāḥ । gaṇeśvarā mahādevamandhakaṃ devasannidhau ।। sahastrasūryasaṃkāśaṃ trinetraṃ candracihnitam ।
nīlakaṇṭhaṃ jaṭāmauliṃ śūlāsaktamahākaram ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ tuṣṭuvurdaityamāścaryaṃ paramaṃ gatāḥ । uvāca bhagavān viṣṇurdevadevaṃ smayanniva ।। sthāne tava mahādeva prabhāvaḥ puruṣo mahān ।
nekṣate ajñānajān doṣān gṛhṇāti ca guṇānapi ।। itīrito atha bhairavo gaṇeśadevapuṅgavaiḥ । sakeśavaḥ sahāndhako jagāma śaṅkarāntikam ।। nirīkṣya devamāgataṃ saśaṅkaraḥ sahāndhakam ।
samādhavaṃ samātṛkaṃ jagāma nirvṛtiṃ haraḥ ।। pragṛhya pāṇineśvaro hiraṇyalocanātmajam । jagāma yatra śailajā vimānamīśavallabhā ।। vilokya sā samāgataṃ bhavaṃ bhavārtihāriṇam ।
avāpa sāndhakaṃ sukhaṃ prasādamandhakaṃ prati ।। athāndhako maheśvarīṃ dadarśa devapārśvagām । papāta daṇḍavatkṣitau nanāma pādapadmayoḥ ।। namāmi devavallabhāmanādimadrijāmimām ।
yataḥ pradhānapūruṣau nihanti yākhilaṃ jagat ।। vibhāti yā śivāsane śivena sākamavyayā । hiraṇmaye atinirmale namāmi tāmimāmajām ।। yadantarākhilaṃ jagajjaganti yānti saṃkṣayam ।
namāmi yatra tāmumāmaśeṣabedavarjitām ।। na jāyate nahīyate na vardhate ca tāmumām । namāmi yā guṇātigā girīśaputrikāmimām ।। kṣamasva devi śailaje kṛtaṃ mayā vimāhataḥ ।
surāsurairyadarcitaṃ namāmi te padāmbujam ।। itthaṃ bhagavatī gaurī bhaktinamreṇa pārvatī । saṃstutā daityapatinā putratve jagṛhe andhakam ।। tataḥ sa mātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ bhairavo rudrasaṃbhavaḥ ।
jagāmānujñayā śaṃbhoḥ pātālaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। yatra sā tāmasī viṣṇormūrtiḥ saṃhārakārikā । samāste hariravyakto nṛsiṃhākṛtirīśvaraḥ ।। tato anantākṛtiḥ śaṃbhuḥ śeṣeṇāpi supūjitaḥ ।
kālāgnirudro bhagavān yuyojātmānamātmani ।। yuñjatastasya devasya sarvā evātha mātaraḥ । bubhukṣitā mahādevaṃ praṇamyāhustriśūlinam ।। bubhukṣitā mahādeva anujñā dīyatāṃ tvayā ।
trailokyaṃ bhakṣayiṣyāmo nānyathā tṛptirastinaḥ ।। etāvaduktvā vacanaṃ mātaro viṣṇusaṃbhavāḥ । bhakṣayāñcakrire sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। tataḥ sa bhairavo devo nṛsiṃhavapuṣaṃ harim ।
dadhyau nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ kṣaṇātprādurabhūddhariḥ ।। vijñāpayāmāsa ca taṃ bhakṣayantīha mātaraḥ । nivārayāśu trailokyaṃ tvadīyā bhagavanniti ।। saṃsmṛtā viṣṇunā devyo nṛsiṃhavapuṣā punaḥ ।
upatasthurmahādevaṃ narasiṃhākṛtiṃ ca tam ।। saṃprāpya sannidhiṃ viṣṇoḥ sarvāḥ saṃhārakārikāḥ । pradaduḥ śaṃbhave śaktiṃ bhairavāyātitejase ।। apaśyaṃstā jagatsūtiṃ nṛsiṃhamatha bhairavam ।
kṣaṇādekatvamāpannaṃ śeṣāhiṃ cāpi mātaraḥ ।। vyājahāra hṛṣīkeśo ye bhaktāḥ śūlapāṇinaḥ । ye ca māṃ saṃsmarantīha pālanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।। mamaiva mūrtiratulā sarvasaṃhārakārikā ।
maheśvarāṃśasaṃbhūtā bhuktimuktipradā tviyam ।। ananto bhagavān kālo dvidhāvasthā mamaiva tu । tāmasī rājasī mūrtirdevadevaścaturmukhaḥ ।। so ayaṃ devo durādharṣaḥ kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।
bhakṣayiṣyati kalpānte rudrātmā nikhilaṃ jagat ।। yā sā vimohikā mūrtirmama nārāyaṇāhvayā । sattvodriktājagat kṛtsnaṃ saṃsthāpayati nityadā ।। sa hi viṣṇuḥ paraṃ brahma paramātmā parā gatiḥ ।
mūlaprakṛtiravyaktā sadānandeti kathyate ।। ityevaṃ bodhitā devyo viṣṇunā viśvamātaraḥ । prapedire mahādevaṃ tameva śaraṇaṃ harim ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ mayāndhakanibarhaṇam ।
māhātmyaṃ devadevasya bhairavasyāmitaujasaḥ ।। andake nigṛhīte vai prahlādasya mahātmanaḥ । virocano nāma suto babhūva nṛpatiḥ purā ।। devāñjitvā sadevendrāna bahūn varṣān mahāsuraḥ ।
pālayāmāsa dharmeṇa trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। tasyaivaṃ vartamānasya kadācid viṣṇucoditaḥ । sanatkumāro bhagavān puraṃ prāpa mahāmuniḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā sihāsanagato brahmaputraṃ mahāsuraḥ ।
nanāmotthāya śirasā prāñjalirvākyamabravīt ।। dhanyo asmyanugṛhīto asmi saṃprāpto me purātanaḥ । yogīśvaro adya bhagavān yato asau brahmavit svayam ।। kimarthamāgato brahman svayaṃ devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।
brūhi me brahmaṇaḥ putra kiṃ kāryaṃ karavāṇyaham ।। so abravīd bhagavān devo dharmayuktaṃ mahāsuram । draṣṭumabhyāgato ahaṃ vai bhavantaṃ bhāgyavānasi ।। sudurlabhā nītireṣā daityānāṃ daityasattama ।
triloke dhārmiko nūnaṃ tvādṛśo anyo na vidyate ।। ityukto asurarājastaṃ punaḥ prāha mahāmunim । dharmāṇāṃ paramaṃ dharmaṃ brūhi me brahmavittama ।। so abravīd bhagavān yogī daityendrāya mahātmane ।
sarvaguhyatamaṃ dharmamātmajñānamanuttamam ।। sa labdhvā paramaṃ jñānaṃ dattvā ca gurudakṣiṇām । nidhāya putre tadrājyaṃ yogābhyāsarato abhavat ।। sa tasya putro matimān balirnāma mahāsuraḥ ।
brahmaṇyo dhārmiko atyarthaṃ vijigye atha purandaram ।। kṛtvā tena mahad yuddhaṃ śakraḥ sarvāmarairvṛtaḥ । jagāma nirjito viṣṇuṃ devaṃ śaraṇamacyutam ।। tadantare aditirdevī devamātā suduḥ khitā ।
daityendrāṇāṃ vadhārthāya putro me syāditi svayam ।। tatāpa sumahad ghoraṃ taporāśistapaḥ param । prapannā viṣṇumavyaktaṃ śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ harim ।। kṛtvā hṛtpadmakiñjalke niṣkalaṃ paramaṃ padam ।
vāsudevamanādyantamānandaṃ vyoma kevalam ।। prasanno bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ । āvirbabhūva yogātmā devamātuḥ puro hariḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā samāgataṃ viṣṇumaditirbhaktisaṃyutā ।
mene kṛtārthamātmānaṃ toṣayāmāsa keśavam ।। jayānantamāhātmyayogābhiyukta । jayāśeṣakalpāmalānandarūpa ।। namo nārasiṃhāya śeṣāya tubhyam ।
namo vāsudevāya tubhyaṃ namaste ।। namo yogagamyāya satyāya tubhyam । namaste varāhāya bhūyo namaste ।। namo vedavijñānadharmābhigamya ।
prabho viśvayone atha bhūyo namaste ।। namo hetave viśvarūpāya tubhyam । śivāyaikarūpāya bhūyo namaste ।। evaṃ sa bhagavān kṛṣṇo devamātrā jaganmayaḥ ।
toṣitaśchandayāmāsa vareṇa prahasanniva ।। praṇamya śirasā bhūmau sā vabre varamuttamam । tvāmeva putraṃ devānāṃ hitāya varaye varam ।। tathāstvityāha bhagavān prapannajanavatsalaḥ ।
dattvā varānaprameyastatraivāntaradhīyata ।। tato bahutithe kāle bhagavantaṃ janārdanam । dadhāra garbhaṃ devānāṃ mātā nārāyaṇaṃ svayam ।। samāviṣṭe hṛṣīkeśe devamāturathodaram ।
utpātā jajñire ghorā balervairocaneḥ pure ।। nirīkṣya sarvānutpātān daityendro bhayavihvalaḥ । prahlādamasuraṃ vṛddhaṃ praṇamyāha pitāmaham ।। pitāmaha mahāprājña jāyante asmatpure adhunā ।
kimutpātā bhavet kāryamasmākaṃ kiṃnimittakāḥ ।। niśamya tasya vacanaṃ ciraṃ dhyātvā mahāsuraḥ । namaskṛtya hṛṣīkeśamidaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। yo yajñairijyate viṣṇuryasya sarvamidaṃ jagat ।
dadhārāsuranāśārthaṃ mātā taṃ tridivaukasām ।। yasmādabhinnaṃ sakalaṃ bhidyate yo akhilādapi । sa vāsudevo devānāṃ māturdehaṃ samāviśat ।। na yasya devā jānanti svarūpaṃ paramārthataḥ ।
sa viṣṇuraditerdehaṃ svecchayādya samāviśat ।। yasmād bhavanti bhūtāni yatra saṃyānti saṃkṣayam । so avatīrṇo mahāyogī purāṇapuruṣo hariḥ ।। na yatra vidyate nāmajātyādiparikalpanā ।
sattāmātrātmarūpo asau viṣṇuraṃśena jāyate ।। yasya sā jagatāṃ mātā śaktistaddharmadhāriṇī । māyā bhagavatī lakṣmīḥ so avatīrṇo janārdanaḥ ।। yasya sā tāmasī mūrtiḥ śaṅkaro rājasī tanuḥ ।
brahmā saṃjāyate viṣṇuraṃśenaikena sattvabhṛt ।। itthaṃ vicintya govindaṃ bhaktinamreṇa cetasā । tameva gaccha śaraṇaṃ tato yāsyasi nirvṛtim ।। tataḥ prahlādavacanād balirvairocanirharim ।
jagāma śaraṇaṃ viśvaṃ pālayāmāsa dharmataḥ ।। kāle prāpte mahāviṣṇuṃ devānāṃ harṣavardhanam । asūta kaśyapāccainaṃ devamātāditiḥ svayam ।। caturbhujaṃ viśālākṣaṃ śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam ।
nīlameghapratīkāśaṃ bhrājamānaṃ śriyāvṛtam ।। upatasthuḥ surāḥ sarve siddhāḥ sādhyāśca cāraṇāḥ । upendramindrapramukhā brahmā carṣigamairvṛtaḥ ।। kṛtopanayano vedānadhyaiṣṭa bhagavān hariḥ ।
samācāraṃ bharadvājāt trilokāya pradarśayan ।। evaṃ hi laukikaṃ mārgaṃ pradarśayati sa prabhuḥ । sa yat pramāṇaṃ kurute lokastadanuvartate ।। tataḥ kālena matimān balirvairocaniḥ svayam ।
yajñairyajñeśvaraṃ viṣṇumarcayāmāsa sarvagam ।। brāhmaṇān pūjayāmāsa dattvā bahutaraṃ dhanam । brahmarṣayaḥ samājagmuryajñavāṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। vijñāya viṣṇurbhagavān bharadvājapracoditaḥ ।
āsthāya vāmanaṃ rūpaṃ yajñadeśamathāgamat ।। kṛṣṇājinopavītāṅga āṣāḍhena virājitaḥ । brāhmaṇo jaṭilo vedānudgiran bhasmamaṇḍitaḥ ।। saṃprāpyāsurarājasya samīpaṃ bhikṣuko hariḥ ।
svapādairvimitaṃ deśamayācata baliṃ tribhiḥ ।। prakṣālya caraṇau viṣṇorbalirbhāsamanvitaḥ । ācāmayitvā bhṛṅgāramādāya svarṇanirmitam ।। prīṇātu devo hariravyayākṛtiḥ ।
nipātayāmāsa jalaṃ suśītalam ।। mathāntarikṣaṃ divamādidevaḥ । prakartukāmaḥ śaraṇaṃ prapannam ।। prājāpatyād brahmalokaṃ jagāma ।
ye tatra loke nivasanti siddhāḥ ।। pitāmahāstoṣayāmāsa viṣṇum । jagāma divyāvaraṇāni bhūyaḥ ।। mahājalaṃ tat puṇyakṛdbhiścajuṣṭam ।
gaṅgetyuktā brahmaṇā vyomasaṃsthā ।। brahmāṇamekaṃ puruṣaṃ svabījam । dṛṣṭvā devāstatra tatra stuvanti ।। mahān balirbhaktiyogena viṣṇum ।
svacetasā yaṃ praṇamanti devāḥ ।। bhūtvā punarvāmano vāsudevaḥ । lokatrayaṃ bhavatā bhāvadattam ।। nipātayāmāsa jalaṃ karāgre ।
trivikramāyāmitavikramāya ।। prahlādasūnoratha śaṅkhapāṇiḥ । pātālamūlaṃ praviśeti bhūyaḥ ।। bhuktvā bhogān devatānāmalabhyān ।
pravekṣyase kalpadāhe punarmām ।। uktvaivaṃ daityasiṃhaṃ taṃ viṣṇuḥ satyaparākramaḥ । purandarāya trailokyaṃ dadau viṣṇururukramaḥ ।। saṃstuvanti mahāyogaṃ siddhā devarṣikinnarāḥ ।
brahmā śakro atha bhagavān rudrādityamarudgaṇāḥ ।। kṛtvaitadadbhutaṃ karma viṣṇurvāmanarūpadhṛk । paśyatāmeva sarveṣāṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। so api daityavaraḥ śrīmān pātālaṃ prāpa coditaḥ ।
prahlādenāsuravarairviṣṇunā viṣṇutatparaḥ ।। apṛcchad viṣṇumāhātmayaṃ bhaktiyogamanuttamam । pūjāvidhānaṃ prahlādaṃ tadāhāsau cakāra saḥ ।। sarasijolacanamīśamaprameyam ।
praṇatagatiṃ praṇidhāya karmayogam ।। eṣa vaḥ kathito viprā vāmanasya parākramaḥ । sa devakāryāṇi sadā karoti puruṣottamaḥ ।। baleḥ putraśataṃ tvāsīnmahābalaparākramam ।
teṣāṃ pradhāno dyutimān bāṇo nāma mahābalaḥ ।। so atīva śaṅkare bhakto rājā rājyamapālayat । trailokyaṃ vaśamānīya bādhayāmāsa vāsavam ।। tataḥ śakrādayo devā gatvocuḥ kṛttivāsasam ।
tvadīyo bādhate hyasmān bāṇo nāma mahāsuraḥ ।। vyāhṛto daivadaiḥ sarvairdevadevo maheśvaraḥ । dadāha bāṇasya puraṃ śareṇaikena līlayā ।। dahyamāne pure tasmin bāṇo rudraṃ triśūlinam ।
yayau śaraṇamīśānaṃ gopatiṃ nīlalohitam ।। mūrdhanyādhāya talliṅgaṃ śāṃbhavaṃ bhītavarjitaḥ । nirgatya tu purāt tasmāt tuṣṭāva parameśvaram ।। saṃstuto bhagavānīśaḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ ।
gāṇapatyena bāṇaṃ taṃ yojayāmāsa bhāvataḥ ।। athābhavan danoḥ putrāstārādyā hyatibhīṣaṇāḥ । tārastathā śambaraśca kapilaḥ śaṅkarastathā । svarbhānurvṛṣaparvā ca prādhānyena prakīrtitāḥ ।।
surasāyāḥ sahastraṃ tu sarpāṇāmabhavad dvijāḥ । anekaśirasāṃ tadvat khecarāṇāṃ mahātmanām ।। ariṣṭā janayāmāsa gandharvāṇāṃ sahastrakam । anantādyā mahānāgāḥ kādraveyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
tāmrā ca janayāmāsa ṣaṭ kanyā dvijapuṅgavāḥ । śukīṃ śyenīṃ ca bhāsīṃ ca sugrīvāṅgṛdhrikāṃ śucim ।। gāstathā janayāmāsa surabhirmahiṣīstathā । irā vṛkṣalatāvallīstṛṇajātīśca sarvaśaḥ ।।
khasā vai yakṣarakṣāṃsi munirapsarasastathā । rakṣogaṇaṃ krodhavaśā janayāmāsa sattamāḥ ।। vinatāyāśca putrau dvau prakhyātau garuḍāruṇau । tayośca garuḍo dhīmān tapastaptvā suduścaram ।
prasādācchūnilaḥ prāpto vāhanatvaṃ hareḥ svayam ।। ārādhya tapasā rudraṃ mahdevaṃ tathāruṇaḥ । sārathye kalpitaḥ pūrvaṃ prītenārkasya śaṃbhunā ।। ete kaśyapadāyādāḥ kīrtitāḥ sthāṇujaṅgamāḥ ।
vaivasvate ante hyasmiñchṛṇvatāṃ pāpanāśanāḥ ।। saptaviṃśat sutāḥ proktāḥ somapatnyaśca suvratāḥ । ariṣṭanemipatnīnāmapatyānīha ṣoḍaśa ।। bahuputrasya viduṣaścatastro vidyutaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
tadvadaṅgirasaḥ putrā ṛṣayo brahmasatkṛtāḥ ।। kuśāśvasya tu devarṣerdevapraharaṇāḥ sutāḥ । ete yugasahastrānte jāyante punareva hi । manvantareṣu niyataṃ tulyaiḥ kāryaiḥ svanāmabhiḥ ।।
etānutpādya putrāṃstu prajāsaṃtānakāraṇāt । kaśyapo gotrakāmastu cacāra sumahat tapaḥ ।। tasya vai tapato atyarthaṃ prādurbhūtau sutāvimau । vatsaraścāsitaścaiva tāvubhau brahmavādinau ।।
vatsarānnaidhruvo jajñe raibhyaśca sumahāyaśāḥ । raibhyasya jajñire raibhyāḥ putrā dyutimatāṃ varāḥ ।। cyavanasya sutā patnī naidhruvasya mahātmanaḥ । sumedhā janayāmāsa putrān vai kuṇḍapāyinaḥ ।।
asitasyaikaparṇāyāṃ brahmiṣṭhaḥ samapadyata । nāmnā vai devalaḥ putro yogācāryo mahātapāḥ ।। śāṇḍilyānāṃ paraḥ śrīmān sarvatattvārthavit sudhīḥ । prasādāt pārvatīśasya yogamuttamamāptavān ।।
śāṇḍilyā naidhru vāraibhyāstrayaḥ pakṣāstu kāśyapāḥ । naraprakṛtayo viprāḥ pulastyasya vadāmi vaḥ ।। tṛṇabindoḥ sutā viprā nāmnā tvilavilā smṛtā । pulastyāya sa rājarṣistāṃ kanyāṃ pratyapādayat ।।
ṛṣistvailavilistasyāṃ viśravāḥ samapadyata । tasya patnyaścatastrastu paulastyakulavardhikāḥ ।। puṣpotkaṭā ca rākā ca kaikasī devavarṇinī । rūpalāvaṇyasaṃpannāstāsāṃ vai śṛṇuta prajāḥ ।।
jyeṣṭhaṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ tasya suṣuve devarūpiṇī । kaikasī janayat putraṃ rāvaṇaṃ rākṣasādhipam ।। kumbhakarṇaṃ śūrpaṇakhāṃ tathaiva ca vibhīṣaṇam । puṣpotkaṭā vyajanayat putrān viśravasaḥ śubhān ।।
mahodaraṃ prahastaṃ ca mahāpārśvaṃ kharaṃ tathā । kumbhīnasīṃ tathā kanyāṃ rākāyāṃ śṛṇuta prajāḥ ।। triśirā dūṣaṇaścaiva vidyujjihvo mahābalaḥ । ityete krūrakarmāṇaḥ paulastyā rākṣasā daśa ।
sarve tapobalotkṛṣṭā rudrabhaktāḥ subhīṣaṇāḥ ।। pulahasya mṛgāḥ putrāḥ sarve vyālāśca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ । bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ sarpāśca śūkarā hastinastathā ।। anapatyaḥ kratustasmin smṛto vaivasvate antare ।
marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ putraḥ svayameva prajāpatiḥ ।। bhṛgorapyabhavacchukro daityācāryo mahātapāḥ । svādhyāyayoganirato harabhakto mahādyutiḥ ।। atreḥ patnyo abhavan bahvyaḥ sodaryāstāḥ pativratāḥ ।
kṛśāśvasya tu viprendrā ghṛtācyāmiti me śrutam ।। sa tāsu janayāmāsa svastyātreyān mahaujasaḥ । vedavedāṅganiratāṃstapasā hatakilbiṣān ।। nāradastu vasiṣṭhāya dadau devīmarundhatīm ।
ūrdhvaretāstatra muniḥ śāpād dakṣasya nāradaḥ ।। haryaśveṣu tu naṣṭeṣu māyayā nāradasya tu । śaśāpa nāradaṃ dakṣaḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ ।। yasmānmama sutāḥ sarve bhavato māyayā dvija ।
kṣayaṃ nītāstvaśeṣeṇa nirapatyo bhaviṣyati ।। arundhatyāṃ vasiṣṭhastu śaktimutpādayat sutam । śakteḥ parāśaraḥ śrīmān sarvajñastapatāṃ varaḥ ।। ārādhya devadeveśamīśānaṃ tripurāntakam ।
lebhe tvapratimaṃ putraṃ kṛṣṇādvaipāyanaṃ prabhum ।। dvaipāyanācchrako jajñe bhagavāneva śaṅkaraḥ । aṃśāṃśenāvatīryorvyāṃ svaṃ prāpa paramaṃ padam ।। śukasyāpyabhavan putrāḥ pañcātyantatapasvinaḥ ।
bhūriśravāḥ prabhuḥ śaṃbhuḥ kṛṣṇo gauraśca pañcamaḥ । kanyā kīrtimatī caiva yogamātā dhṛtavratā ।। ete atra vaṃśyāḥ kathitā brāhmaṇā brahmavādinām । ata ūrdhvaṃ nibodhadhvaṃ kaśyapādrājasaṃtatim ।।
aditiḥ suṣuve putramādityaṃ kaśyapāt prabhum । tasyādityasya caivasīd bhāryāṇāṃ tu catuṣṭayam । saṃjñā rājñī prabhā chāyā putrāṃstāsāṃ nibodhata ।। saṃjñā tvāṣṭrī ca suṣuve sūryānmanumanuttamam ।
yamaṃ ca yamunāṃ caiva rājñī raivatameva ca ।। prabhā prabhātamādityācchāyā sāvarṇamātmajam । śaniṃ ca tapatīṃ caiva viṣṭiṃ caiva yathākramam ।। manostu prathamasyāsan nava putrāstu saṃyamāḥ ।
ikṣvākurnabhagaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireva ca ।। nariṣyantaśca nābhāgo hyariṣṭaḥ kāruṣakastathā । pṛṣadhraśca mahātejā navaite śakrasannibhāḥ ।। ilā jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca somavaṃśavivṛddhaye ।
budhasya gatvā bhavanaṃ somaputreṇa saṃgatā ।। asūta saumyajaṃ devī purūravasamuttamam । pitṝṇāṃ tṛptikartāraṃ budhāditi hi naḥ śrutam ।। saṃprāpya puṃstvamamalaṃ sudyumna iti viśrutaḥ ।
ilā putratrayaṃ lebhe punaḥ strītvamavindata ।। utkalaśca gayaścaiva vinatāśvastathaiva ca । sarve te apratimaprakhyāḥ prapannāḥ kamalodbhavam ।। ikṣvākoścābhavad vīro vikukṣirnāma pārthivaḥ ।
jyeṣṭhaḥ putraśatasyāpi daśa pañca ca tatsutāḥ ।। teṣāñjyeṣṭhaḥ kakutstho abhūt kākutstho hi suyodhanaḥ । suyodhanāt pṛthuḥ śrīmān viśvakaśca pṛthoḥ sutaḥ ।। viśvakādārdrako dhīmān yuvanāśvastu tatsutaḥ ।
sa gokarṇamanuprāpya yuvanāśvaḥ pratāpavān ।। dṛṣṭvā tu gautamaṃ vipraṃ tapantamanalaprabham । praṇamya daṇḍavad bhūmau putrakāmo mahīpatiḥ । apṛcchat karmaṇā kena dhārmikaṃ prāpnuyāt sutam ।।
ārādhya pūrvapuruṣaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam । anādinidhanaṃ devaṃ dhārmikaṃ prāpnuyāt sutam ।। yasya putraḥ svayaṃ brahmā pautraḥ syānnīlalohitaḥ । tamādikṛṣṇamīśānamārādhyāpnoti satsutam ।।
na yasya bhagavān brahmā prabhāvaṃ vetti tattvataḥ । tamārādhya hṛṣīkeśaṃ prāpnuyāddhārmikaṃ sutam ।। sa gautamavacaḥ śrutvā yuvanāśvo mahīpatiḥ । ārādhayanmahāyogaṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam ।।
tasya putro abhavad vīraḥ śrāvastiriti viśrutaḥ । nirmitā yena śrāvastirgauḍadeśe mahāpurī ।। tasmācca bṛhadaśvo abhūt tasmāt kuvalayāśvakaḥ । dhundhumāratvamagamad dhundhuṃ hatvā mahāsuram ।।
dhundhumārasya tanayāstrayaḥ proktā dvijottamāḥ । dṛḍhāśvaścaiva daṇḍāśvaḥ kapilāśvastathaiva ca ।। dṛḍhāśvasya pramodastu haryaśvastasya cātmajaḥ । haryaśvasya nikumbhastu nikumbhāt saṃhatāśvakaḥ ।।
kṛśāśvaśca raṇāśvaśca saṃhatāśvasya vai sutau । yuvanāśvo raṇāśvasya śakratulyabalo yudhi ।। kṛtvā tu vāruṇīmiṣṭimṛṣīṇāṃ vai prasādataḥ । lebhe tvapratimaṃ putraṃ viṣṇubhaktamanuttamam ।
māndhātāraṃ mahāprājñaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam ।। māndhātuḥ purukutso abhūdambarīṣaśca vīryavān । mucukundaśca puṇyātmā sarve śakrasamā yudhi ।। ambarīṣasya dāyādo yuvanāśvo aparaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
harito yuvanāśvasya hāritastatsuto abhavat ।। purukutsasya dāyādastrasadasyurmahāyaśāḥ । narmadāyāṃ samutpannaḥ saṃbhūtistatsuto abhavat ।। viṣṇuvṛddhaḥ sutastasya tvanaraṇyo abhavat paraḥ ।
bṛhadaśavo anaraṇyasya haryaśvastatsuto abhavat ।। so atīva dhārmiko rājā kardamasya prajāpateḥ । prasādāddhārmikaṃ putraṃ lebhe sūryaparāyaṇam ।। sa tu sūryaṃ samabhyarcya rājā vasumanāḥ śubham ।
lebhe tvapratimaṃ putraṃ tridhanvānamarindamam ।। ayajaccāśvamedhena śatrūn jitvā dvijottamāḥ । svādhyāyavān dānaśīlastitikṣurdharmatatparaḥ ।। ṛṣayastu samājagmuryajñavāṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।
vasiṣṭhakaśyapamukhā devāścendrapurogamāḥ ।। tān praṇamya mahārājaḥ papraccha vinayānvitaḥ । samāpya vidhivad yajñaṃ vasiṣṭhādīn dvijottamān ।। kiṃsviccheyaskarataraṃ loke asmin brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥ ।
yajñastapo vā saṃnyāso brūta me sarvavedinaḥ ।। adhītya vedān vidhivat putrānutpādya dharmataḥ । iṣṭvā yajñeśvaraṃ yajñair gaccheda vanamathātmavān ।। ārādhya tapasā devaṃ yoginaṃ parameṣṭhinam ।
pravrajed vidhivad yajñairiṣṭvā pūrvaṃ surottamān ।। yamāhurekaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ parameśvaram । tamārādhya sahastrāṃśuṃ tapasā mokṣamāpnuyāt ।। ajasya nābhāvadhyekamīśvareṇa samarpitam ।
bījaṃ bhagavatā yena sa devastapasejyate ।। yo agniḥ sarvātmako anantaḥ svayaṃbhūrviśvatomukhaḥ । sa rudrastapasogreṇa pūjyate netarairmakhaiḥ ।। yo yajñairijyate devo jātavedāḥ sanātanaḥ ।
sa sarvadaivatatanuḥ pūjyate tapaseśvaraḥ ।। yataḥ sarvamidaṃ jātaṃ yasyāpatyaṃ prajāpatiḥ । tapaḥ sumahadāsthāya pūjyate sa maheśvaraḥ ।। yataḥ pradhānapuruṣau yasya śaktimayaṃ jagat ।
sa devadevastapasā pūjanīyaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। sahastranayano devaḥ sākṣī sa tu prajāpatiḥ । prasīdati mahāyogī pūjitastapasā paraḥ ।। prāptādhyayanayajñas labdhaputrasya caiva hi ।
nāntareṇa tapaḥ kaściddharmaḥ śāstreṣu dṛśyate ।। ityākarṇya sa rājarṣistān praṇamyātihṛṣṭadhīḥ । visarjayitvā saṃpūjya tridhanvānamathābravīt ।। ārādhayiṣye tapasā devamekākṣarāhvayam ।
prāṇaṃ bṛhantaṃ puruṣamādityāntarasaṃsthitam ।। tvaṃ tu dharmarato nityaṃ pālayaitadatandritaḥ । cāturvarṇyasamāyuktamaśeṣaṃ kṣitimaṇḍalam ।। evamuktvā sa tadrājyaṃ nidhāyātmabhave nṛpaḥ ।
jagāmāraṇyamanaghastapaścartumanuttamam ।। himavacchikhare ramye devadāruvane śubhe । kandamūlaphalāhāro munyannairayajat surān ।। saṃvatsaraśataṃ sāgraṃ taponirdhūtakalmaṣaḥ ।
jajāpa manasā devīṃ sāvitrariṃ vedamātaram ।। tasyaivaṃ japato devaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ parameśvaraḥ । hiraṇyagarbho viśvātmā taṃ deśamagamat svayam ।। dṛṣṭvā devaṃ samāyāntaṃ brahmāṇaṃ viśvatomukham ।
nanāma śirasā tasya pādayornāma kīrtayan ।। namo devādhidevāya brahmaṇe paramātmane । hirṇyamūrtaye tubhyaṃ sahastrākṣāya vedhase ।। namo dhātre vidhātre ca namo vedātmamūrtaye ।
sāṃkhyayogādhigamyāya namaste jñānamūrtaye ।। namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ straṣṭre sarvārthavedine । puruṣāya purāṇāya yogināṃ gurave namaḥ ।। tataḥ prasanno bhagavān viriñco viśvabhāvanaḥ ।
varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te varado asmītyabhāṣata ।। japeyaṃ devadeveśa gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram । bhūyo varṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ tāvadāyurbhavenmama ।। bāḍhamityāha viśvātmā samālokya narādhipam ।
spṛṣṭvā karābhyāṃ suprītastatraivāntaradhīyata ।। so api labdhavaraḥ śrīmān jajāpātiprasannadhīḥ । śāntastriṣavaṇasnāyī kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ ।। tasya pūrṇe varṣaśate bhagavānugradīdhitiḥ ।
prādurāsīnmahāyogī bhānormaṇḍalamadhyataḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā vedaviduṣaṃ maṇḍalasthaṃ sanātanam । svayaṃbhuvamanādyantaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vismayaṃ gataḥ ।। tuṣṭāva vaidikairmantraiḥ sāvitryā ca viśeṣataḥ ।
kṣaṇādapaśyat puruṣaṃ tameva parameśvaram ।। caturmukhaṃ jaṭāmaulimaṣṭahastaṃ trilocanam । candrāvayavalakṣamāṇaṃ naranārītanuṃ haram ।। bhāsayantaṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ svaraśmibhiḥ ।
raktāmbaradharaṃ raktaṃ raktamālyānulepanam ।। tadbhāvabhāvito dṛṣṭvā sadbhāvena pareṇa hi । nanāma śirasā rudraṃ sāvitryānena caiva hi ।। namaste nīlakaṇṭhāya bhāsvate parameṣṭhine ।
trayīmayāya rudrāya kālarūpāya hetave ।। tadā prāha mahādevo rājānaṃ prītamānasaḥ । imāni me rahasyāni nāmāni śṛṇu cānagha ।। sarvavedeṣu gītāni saṃsāraśamanāni tu ।
namaskuruṣva nṛpate ebhirmāṃ satataṃ śuciḥ ।। adhyāyaṃ śatarudrīyaṃ yajuṣāṃ sāramuddhṛtam । japasvānanyacetasko mayyāsaktamanā nṛpa ।। brahmacārī mitāhāro bhasmaniṣṭhaḥ samāhitaḥ ।
japedāmaraṇād rudraṃ sa yāti paramaṃ padam ।। ityuktvā bhagavān rudro bhaktānugrahakāmyayā । punaḥ saṃvatsaraśataṃ rājñe hyāyurakalpayat ।। dattvāsmai tat paraṃ jñānaṃ vairāgyaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।
kṣaṇādantardadhe rudrastadadbhutamivābhavat ।। rājāpi tapasā rudraṃ jajāpānanyamānasaḥ । bhasmacchannastriṣavaṇaṃ snātvā śāntaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। japatastasya nṛpateḥ pūrṇe varṣaśate punaḥ ।
yogapravṛttirabhavat kālāt kālātmakaṃ param ।। viveśa tad vedasāraṃ sthānaṃ vai parameṣṭhinaḥ । bhānoḥ sa maṇḍalaṃ śubhraṃ tato yāto maheśvaram ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi rājñaścaritamuttamam ।
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate ।। tridhanvā rājaputrastu dharmeṇāpālayanmahīm । tasya putro abhavad vidvāṃstrayyāruṇa iti smṛtaḥ ।। tasya satyavrato nāma kumāro abhūnmahābalaḥ ।
bhāryā satyadhanā nāma hariścandramajījanat ।। hariścandrasya putro abhūd rohito nāma vīryavān । harito rohitasyātha dhundhustasya suto abhavat ।। vijayaśca sudevaśca dhundhuputrau babhūvatuḥ ।
vijayasyābhavat putraḥ kāruko nāma vīryavān ।। kārukasya vṛkaḥ putrastasmād bāhurajāyata । sagarastasya putrau'bhūd rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।। dve bhārye sagarasyāpi prabhā bhānumatī tathā ।
tābhyāmārādhitaḥ prādādaurvāgnirvaramuttamam ।। ekaṃ bhānumatī putramagṛhṇādasamañjasam । prabhā ṣaṣṭisahastraṃ tu putrāṇāṃ jagṛhe śubhā ।। asamañsasya tanayo hyaṃśumān nāma pārthivaḥ ।
tasya putro dilīpastu dilīpāt tu bhagīrathaḥ ।। yena bhāgīrathī gaṅgā tapaḥ kṛtvāvatāritā । prasādād devadevasya mahādevasya dhīmataḥ ।। bhagīrathasya tapasā devaḥ prītamanā haraḥ ।
babhāra śirasā gaṅgāṃ somānte somabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। bhagīrathasutaścāpi śruto nāma babhūva ha । nābhāgastasya dāyādaḥ sindhudvīpastato abhavat ।। ayutāyuḥ sutastasya ṛtuparṇastu tatsutaḥ ।
ṛtuparṇasya putro abhūt sudāso nāma dhārmikāḥ । saudāsastasya tanayaḥ khyātaḥ kalmāṣapādakaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhastu mahātejāḥ kṣetre kalmāṣapādake । aśmakaṃ janayāmasā tamikṣvākukuladhvajam ।।
aśmakasyotkalāyāṃ tu nakulo nāma pārthivaḥ । sa hi rāmabhayād rājā vanaṃ prāpa suduḥ khitaḥ ।। vibhrat sa nārīkavacaṃ tasmācchataratho abhavat । tasmād bilibiliḥ śrīmānvṛddhaśarmācatatsutaḥ ।।
tasmād viśvasahastasmāt khaṭvāṅga iti viśrutaḥ । dīrghabāhuḥ sutastasya raghustasmādajāyata ।। raghorajaḥ samutpanno rājā daśarathastataḥ । rāmo dāśarathirvoro dharmajño lokaviśrutaḥ ।।
bharato lakṣmaṇaścaiva śatrughnaśca mahābalaḥ । sarve śakrasamā yuddhe viṣṇuśaktisamanvitāḥ । jajñe rāvaṇanāśārthaṃ viṣṇuraṃśena viśvakṛt ।। rāmasya subhagā bhāryā janakasyātmajā śubhā ।
sītā trilokavikhyātā śīlaudāryaguṇānvitā ।। tapasā toṣitā devī janakena girīndrajā । prāyacchajjānakīṃ sītāṃ rāmamevāśritā patim ।। prītaśca bhagavānīśastriśūlī nīlalohitaḥ ।
pradadau śatrunāśārthaṃ janakāyādbhutaṃ dhanuḥ ।। sa rājā janako vidvān dātukāmaḥ sutāmimām । aghoṣayadamitraghno loke asmin dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।। idaṃ dhanuḥ samādātuṃ yaḥ śaknoti jagattraye ।
devo vā dānavo vāpi sa sītāṃ labdhumarhati ।। vijñāya rāmo balavān janakasya gṛhaṃ prabhuḥ । bhañjayāmāsa cādāya gatvāsau līlayaiva hi ।। udvavāha ca tāṃ kanyāṃ pārvatīmiva śaṅkaraḥ ।
rāmaḥ paramadharmātmā senāmiva ca ṣaṇmukhaḥ ।। tato bahutithe kāle rājā daśarathaḥ svayam । rāmaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ sutaṃ vīraṃ rājānaṃ kartumārabhat ।। tasyātha patnī subhagā kaikeyī cārubhāṣiṇī ।
nivārayāmāsa patiṃ prāha saṃbhrāntamānasā ।। matsutaṃ bharataṃ vīraṃ rājānaṃ kartumarhasi । pūrvameva varo yasmād datto me bhavatā yataḥ ।। sa tasyā vacanaṃ śrutvā rājā duḥ khitamānasaḥ ।
bāḍhamityabravīd vākyaṃ tathā rāmo api dharmavit ।। praṇamyātha pituḥ pādau lakṣmaṇena sahācyutaḥ । yayau vanaṃ sapatnīkaḥ kṛtvā samayamātmavān ।। saṃvatsarāṇāṃ catvāri daśa caiva mahābalaḥ ।
uvāsa tatra matimān lakṣmaṇena saha prabhuḥ ।। kadācid vasato araṇye rāvaṇo nāma rākṣasaḥ । parivrājakaveṣeṇa sītāṃ hṛtvā yayau purīm ।। adṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇo rāmaḥ sītāmākulitendriyau ।
duḥ khaśokābhisaṃtaptau babhūvaturarindamau ।। tataḥ kadācit kapinā sugrīveṇa dvijottamāḥ । vānarāṇāmabhūt sakhyaṃ rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ ।। sugrīvasyānugo vīro hanumān nma vānaraḥ ।
vāyuputrau mahātejā rāmasyāsīt priyaḥ sadā ।। sa kṛtvā paramaṃ dhairyaṃ rāmāya kṛtaniścayaḥ । ānayiṣyāmi tāṃ sītāmityuktvā vicacāra ha ।। mahīṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ sītādarśanatatparaḥ ।
jagāma rāvaṇapurīṃ laṅkāṃ sāgarasaṃsthitām ।। tatrātha nirjane deśe vṛkṣmūle śucismitām । apaśyadamalāṃ sītāṃ rākṣasībhiḥ samāvṛtām ।। aśrupūrṇekṣaṇāṃ hṛdyāṃ saṃsmarantīmaninditām ।
rāmamindīvaraśyāmaṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ cātmasaṃsthitam ।। nivedayitvā cātmānaṃ sītāyai rahasi svayam । asaṃśayāya pradadāvasyai rāmāṅgulīyakam ।। dṛṣṭvāṅgulīyakaṃ sītā patyuḥ paramaśobhanam ।
mene samāgataṃ rāmaṃ prītivisphāritekṣaṇā ।। samāśvāsya tadā sītāṃ dṛṣṭvā rāmasya cāntikam । nayiṣye tvāṃ mahābāhuruktvā rāmaṃ yayau punaḥ ।। nivedayitvā rāmāya sītādarśanamātmavān ।
tasthau rāmeṇa purato lakṣmaṇena ca pūjitaḥ ।। tataḥ sa rāmo balavān sārdhaṃ hanumatā svayam । lakṣmaṇena ca yuddhāya buddhiṃ cakre hi rakṣasām ।। kṛtvātha vānaraśatairlaṅkāmārgaṃ mahodadheḥ ।
setuṃ paramadharmātmā rāvaṇaṃ hatavān prabhuḥ ।। sapatnīkaṃ ca sasutaṃ sabhrātṛkamaridamaḥ । ānayāmāsa tāṃ sītāṃ vāyuputrasahāyavān ।। setumadhye mahādevamīśānaṃ kṛttivāsasam ।
sthāpayāmāsa liṅgasthaṃ pūjayāmāsa rāghavaḥ ।। tasya devo mahādevaḥ pārvatyā saha śaṅkaraḥ । pratyakṣameva bhagavān dattavān varamuttamam ।। yat tvayā sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ drakṣyantīha dvijātayaḥ ।
mahāpātakasaṃyuktāsteṣāṃ pāpaṃ vinaśyatu ।। anyāni caiva pāpāni snātasyātra mahodadhau । darśanādeva liṅgasalya nāśaṃ yānti na saṃśayaḥ ।। yāvat sthāsyanti girayo yāvadeṣā ca medinī ।
yāvat setuśca tāvacca sthāsyāmyatra tirohitaḥ ।। snānaṃ dānaṃ japaḥ śrāddhaṃ bhaviṣyatyakṣyaṃ kṛtam । smaraṇādeva liṅgasya dinapāpaṃ praṇaśyati ।। ityuktvā bhagavāñchaṃbhuḥ pariṣvajya tu rāghavam ।
sanandī sagaṇo rudrastatraivāntaradhīyata ।। rāmo api pālayāmāsa rājyaṃ dharmaparāyaṇaḥ । abhiṣikto mahātejā bharatena mahābalaḥ ।। viśeṣāḍh brāhmaṇān sarvān pūjayāmasaceśvaram ।
yajñena yajñahantāramaśvamedhena śaṅkaram ।। rāmasya tanayo jajñe kuśa ityabhiviśrutaḥ । lavaśca sumahābhāgaḥ sarvatattvārthavit sudhīḥ ।। atithistu kuśājjajñe niṣadhastatsuto abhavat ।
nalastu niṣadhasyābhūnnabhastamādajāyata ।। nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīkākhyaḥ kṣemadhanvā ca tatsutaḥ । tasya putro abhavad vīro devānīkaḥ pratāpavān ।। ahīnagustasya suto sahasvāṃstatsuto abhavat ।
tasmāccandrāvalokastu tārāpīḍastu tatsutaḥ ।। tārāpīḍāccandragirirbhānuvittastato abhavat । śrutāyurabhavat tasmādete ikṣvākuvaṃśajāḥ । sarve prādhānyataḥ proktāḥ samāsena dvijottamāḥ ।।
ya imaṃ śṛṇuyānnityamikṣvākorvaṃśamuttamam । sarvapāpavinirmukto svargaloke mahīyate ।। ailaḥ purūravāścātha rājā rājyamapālayat । tasya putrā babhūvurhi ṣaḍindrasamatejasaḥ ।।
āyurmāyuramāvāyurviśvāyuścaiva vīryavān । śatāyuśca śrutāyuśca divyāścaivorvaśīsutāḥ ।। āyuṣastanayā vīrāḥ pañcaivāsan mahaujasaḥ । svarbhānutanayāyāṃ vai prabhāyāmiti naḥ śrutam ।।
nahuṣaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ dharmajño lokaviśrutaḥ । nahuṣasya tu dāyādāḥ ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ ।। utpannāḥ pitṛkanyāyāṃ virajāyāṃ mahābalāḥ । yatiryayātiḥ saṃyātirāyātiḥ pañcako aśvakaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ yayātiḥ pañcānāṃ mahābalaparākramaḥ । devayānīmukhanasaḥ sutāṃ bhāryāmavāpa saḥ । śarmiṣṭhāmāsurīṃ caiva tanayāṃ vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva devayānī vyajāyata ।
druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca śarmiṣṭhā cāpyajījanat ।। so abhyaṣiñcadatikramya jyeṣṭhaṃ yadumaninditam । purumeva kanīyāsaṃ piturvacanapālakam ।। diśi dakṣiṇapūrvasyāṃ turvasuṃ putramādiśat ।
dakṣiṇāparayo rājā yaduṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ nyayojayat । pratīcyāmuttārāyāṃ ca druhyuṃ cānumakalpayat ।। tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā dharmataḥ paripālitā । rājāpi dārasahito navaṃ prāpa mahāyaśāḥ ।।
yadorapyabhavan putrāḥ pañca devasutopamāḥ । sahastrajit tathājyeṣṭhaḥ kroṣaṭurnālo ajitoraghuḥ ।। sahastrajitsutastadvacchatajinnāma pārthivaḥ । sutāḥ śatajito apyāsaṃstrayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।।
haihayaśca hayaścaiva rājā veṇuhayaḥ paraḥ । haihayasyābhavat putro dharma ityabhiviśrutaḥ ।। tasya putro abhavad viprā dharmanetraḥ pratāpavān । dharmanetrasya kīrtistu saṃjitastatsuto abhavat ।।
mahiṣmān saṃjitasyābhūd bhadraśreṇyastadanvayaḥ । bhadraśreṇyasya dāyādo durdamo nāma pārthivaḥ ।। durdamasya suto dhīmān dhanako nāma vīryavān । dhanakasya tu dāyādāścatvāro lokasammatāḥ ।।
kṛtavīryaḥ kṛtāgniśca kṛtavarmā tathaiva ca । kṛtaujāśca caturtho abhūt kārtavīryor'juno abhavat ।। sahastrabāhurdyutimān dhanurvedavidāṃ varaḥ । tasya rāmo abhavanmṛtyurjāmadagnyo janārdanaḥ ।।
tasya putraśatānyāsan pañca tatra mahārathāḥ । kṛtāstrā balinaḥ śūrā dharmātmāno namasvinaḥ ।। śūraśca śūrasenaśca dhṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇastathaiva ca । jayadhvajaśca balavān nārāyaṇaparo nṛpaḥ ।।
śūrasenādayaḥ sarve catvāraḥ prathitaujasaḥ । rudrabhaktā mahātmānaḥ pūjayanti sma śaṅkaram ।। jayadhvajastu matimān devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim । jagāma śaraṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ daivataṃ dharmatatparaḥ ।।
tamūcuritare putrā nāyaṃ dharmastavānagha । īśvarārādhanarataḥ pitāsmākamabhūditi ।। tānabravīnmahātejā eṣa dharmaḥ paro mama । viṣṇoraṃśena saṃbhūtā rājāno yanmahītale ।।
rājyaṃ pālayatāvaśyaṃ bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ । pūjanīyo yato viṣṇuḥ pālako jagato hariḥ ।। sāttvikī rājasī caiva tāmasī ca svayaṃbhuvaḥ । tistrastu mūrtayaḥ proktāḥ sṛṣṭisthityantahetavaḥ ।।
sattvātmā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ saṃsthāpayati sarvadā । sṛjed brahmā rajomūrtiḥ saṃharet tāmaso haraḥ ।। tasmānmahīpatīnāṃ tu rājyaṃ pālayatāmayam । ārādhyo bhagavān viṣṇuḥ keśavaḥ keśimardanaḥ ।।
niśamya tasya vacanaṃ bhrātaro anye manasvinaḥ । procuḥ saṃhārakṛd rudraḥ pūjanīyo mumukṣubhiḥ ।। ayaṃ hi bhagavān rudraḥ sarvaṃ jagadidaṃ śivaḥ । tamoguṇaṃ samāśritya kalpānte saṃharet prabhuḥ ।।
yā sā ghoratarā mūrtirasya tejāmayī parā । saṃhared vidyayā sarvaṃ saṃsāraṃ śūlabhṛt tayā ।। tatastānabravīd rājā vicintyāsau jayadhvajaḥ । sattvena mucyate jantuḥ sattvātmā bhagavān hariḥ ।।
tamūcurbhrātaro rudraḥ sevitaḥ sāttvikairjanaiḥ । mocayet sattvasaṃyuktaḥ pūjayeśaṃ tato haram ।। athābravīd rājaputraḥ prahasan vai jayadhvajaḥ । svadharmo muktaye panthā nānyo munibhiraṣyate ।।
tathā ca vaiṣṇavī śaktirnṛpāṇāṃ devatā sadā । ārādhanaṃ paro dharmo purāreramitaujasaḥ ।। tamabravīd rājaputraḥ kṛṣṇo matimatāṃ varaḥ । yadarjuno asmajjanakaḥ svadharmaṃ kṛtavāniti ।।
