evaṃ vivāde vitate śūraseno abravīd vacaḥ । pramāṇamṛṣayo hyatra brūyuste yat tathaiva tat ।। tataste rājaśārdūlāḥ papracchurbrahmavādinaḥ । gatvā sarve susaṃrabdhāḥ saptarṣoṇāṃ tadāśramam ।।
tānabruvaṃste munayo vasiṣṭhādyā yathārthataḥ । yā yasyābhimatā puṃsaḥ sā hi tasyaiva devatā ।। kintu kāryaviśeṣeṇa pūjitāśceṣṭadā nṛṇām । viśeṣāt sarvadā nāyaṃ niyamo hyanyathā nṛpāḥ ।।
nṛpāṇāṃ daivataṃ viṣṇustathaiva ca purandaraḥ । viprāṇāmagnirādityo brahmā caiva pinākadhṛk ।। devānāṃ daivataṃ viṣṇurdānavānāṃ triśūlabhṛt । gandharvāṇāṃ tathā somo yakṣāṇāmapi kathyate ।।
vidyādharāṇāṃ vāgdevī sādhyānāṃ bhagavānraviḥ । rakṣasāṃ śaṅkaro rudraḥ kiṃnarāṇāṃ ca pārvatī ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ daivataṃ brahmā mahādevaśca śūlabhṛt । manūnāṃ syādumā devī tathā viṣṇuḥ sabhāskaraḥ ।।
gṛhasthānāṃ ca sarve syurbrahmā vai brahmacāriṇām । vaikhānasānāmarkaḥ syād yatīnāṃ ca maheśvaraḥ ।। bhūtānāṃ bhagavān rudraḥ kūṣmāṇḍānāṃ vināyakaḥ । sarveṣāṃ bhagavān brahmā devadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
ityevaṃ bhagavān brahmā svayaṃ devo abhyabhāṣata । tasmājjayadhvajo nūnaṃ viṣṇvārādhanamarhati ।। tān praṇamyātha te jagmuḥ purīṃ paramaśobhanām । pālayāñcakrire pṛthvīṃ jitvā sarvaripūn raṇe ।।
tataḥ kadācid viprendrā videho nāma dānavaḥ । bhīṣaṇaḥ sarvasattvānāṃ purīṃ teṣāṃ samāyayau ।। daṃṣṭrākarālo dīptātmā yugāntadahanopamaḥ । śūlamādāya sūryābhaṃ nādayan vai diśo daśa ।।
tannādaśravaṇānmartyāstatra ye nivasanti te । tatyajurjovitaṃ tvanye dudruvurbhayavihvalāḥ ।। tataḥ sarve susaṃyattāḥ kārtavīryātmajāstadā । yuyudhurdānavaṃ śaktigirikūṭāsimudgaraiḥ ।।
tān sarvān dānavo viprāḥ śūlena prahasanniva । vārayāmāsa ghorātmā kalpānte bhairavo yathā ।। śūrasenādayaḥ pañca rājānastu mahābalāḥ । yuddhāya kṛtasaṃrambhā videhaṃ tvabhidudruvuḥ ।।
śūro astraṃ prāhiṇod raudraṃ śūrasenastu vāruṇam । prājāpatyaṃ tathā kṛṣṇo vāyavyaṃ dhṛṣṇa eva ca ।। jayadhvajaśca kauberamaindramāgneyameva ca । bhañjayāmāsa śūlena tānyastrāṇi sa dānavaḥ ।।
tataḥ kṛṣṇo mahāvīryo gadāmādāya bhīṣaṇām । spṛṣṭvā mantreṇa tarasā cikṣepa na nanāda ca ।। saṃprāpya sā gādāsyoro videhasya śilopamam । na dānavaṃ cālayituṃ śaśākāntakasaṃnibham ।।
dudruvuste bhayagrastā dṛṣṭvā tasyātipauruṣam । jayadhvajastu matimān sasmāra jagataḥ patim ।। viṣṇuṃ grasiṣṇuṃ lokādimaprameyamanāmayam । trātāraṃ puruṣaṃ pūrvaṃ śrīpatiṃ pītavāsasam ।।
tataḥ prādurabhūccakraṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham । ādeśād vāsudevasya bhaktānugrahakāraṇāt ।। jagrāha jagatāṃ yoniṃ smṛtvā nārāyaṇaṃ nṛpaḥ । prāhiṇod vai videhāya dānavebhyo yathā hariḥ ।।
saṃprāpya tasya ghorasya skandhadeśaṃ sudarśanam । pṛthivyāṃ pātayāmāsa śiro adriśikharākṛti ।। tasmin hate devaripau śīrādyā bhrātaro nṛpāḥ । samāyayuḥ purīṃ ramyāṃ bhrātaraṃ cāpyapūjayan ।।
śrutvājagāma bhagavān jayadhvajaparākramam । kārtavīryasutaṃ draṣṭuṃ viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ ।। tamāgatamatho dṛṣṭvā rājā saṃbhrāntamānasaḥ । samāveśyāsane ramye pūjayāmāsa bhāvataḥ ।।
uvāca bhagavān ghoraḥ prasādād bhavato asuraḥ । nipātito mayā saṃkhye videho dānaveśvaraḥ ।। tvadvākyācchinnasaṃdeho viṣṇuṃ satyaparākramam । prapannaḥ śaraṇaṃ tena prasādo me kṛtaḥ śubhaḥ ।।
yakṣyāmi parameśānaṃ viṣṇuṃ padmadalekṣaṇam । kathaṃ kena vidhānena saṃpūjyo harirīśvaraḥ ।। ko ayaṃ nārāyaṇo devaḥ kiṃprabhāvaśca suvrata । sarvametanmamācakṣva paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ।।
yataḥ pravṛttirbhūtānāṃ yasmin sarvamidaṃ jagat । sa viṣṇuḥ sarvabhūtātmā tamāśritya vimucyate ।। svavarṇāśramadharmeṇa pūjyo ayaṃ puruṣottamaḥ । akāmahatabhāvena samārādhyo na cānyathā ।।
etāvaduktvā bhagavāna viśvāmitro mahāmuniḥ । śūrādyaiḥ pūjito viprā jagāmātha svamālayam ।। atha śūrādayo devamayajanta maheśvaram । yajñena yajñagamyaṃ taṃ niṣkāmā rudramavyayam ।।
tān vasiṣṭhastu bhagavān yājayāmāsa sarvavit । gautamo atriragastyaśca sarve rudraparāyaṇāḥ ।। viśvāmitrastu bhagavān jayadhvajamarindamam । yājayāmāsa bhūtādimādidevaṃ janārdanam ।।
tasya yajñe mahāyogī sākṣād devaḥ svayaṃ hariḥ । āvirāsīt sa bhagavān tadadbhutamivābhavat ।। ya imaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ jayadhvajaparākramam । sarvapāpavimuktātmā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
jayadhvajasya putro abhūt tālājaṅgha iti smṛtaḥ । śataputrāstu tasyāsan tālajaṅghāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। teṣāṃ jyeṣṭho mahāvīryo vītihotro abhavannṛpaḥ । vṛṣaprabhṛtayaścānye yādavāḥ puṇyakarmiṇaḥ ।।
vṛṣo vaṃśakarasteṣāṃ tasya putro abhavanmadhuḥ । madhoḥ putraśataṃ tvāsīd vṛṣaṇastasya vaṃśabhāk ।। vītihotrasutaścāpi viśruto ananta ityuta । durjayastasya putro abūt sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ ।।
tasya bhāryā rūpavatī guṇaiḥ sarvairalaṅkṛtā । pativratāsīt patinā svadharmaparipālikā ।। sa kadācinmahābhāgaḥ kālindītīrasaṃsthitām । apaśyadurvaśīṃ devīṃ gāyantīṃ madhurasvanām ।।
tataḥ kāmāhatamanāstatsamīpamupetya vai । provāca suciraṃ kālaṃ devi rantuṃ mayār'hasi ।। sā devī nṛpatiṃ dṛṣṭvā rūpalāvaṇyasaṃyutam । reme tena ciraṃ kālaṃ kāmadevamivāparam ।।
kālāt prabuddho rājā tāmurvaśīṃ prāha śobhanām । gamiṣyāmi purīṃ ramyāṃ hasantī sābravīd vacaḥ ।। na hyanenopabhogena bhavatā rājasundara । prītiḥ saṃjāyate mahyaṃ sthātavyaṃ vatsaraṃ punaḥ ।।
tāmabravīt sa matimān gatvā śīghrataraṃ purīm । āgamiṣyāmi bhūyo atra tanme anujñātumarhasi ।। tamabravīt sā subhagā tathā kuru viśāṃpate । nānyayāpsarasā tāvad rantavyaṃ bhavat punaḥ ।।
omityuktvā yayau tūrṇaṃ purīṃ paramaśobhanām । gatvā pativratāṃ patnīṃ dṛṣṭvā bīto abhavannṛpaḥ ।। saṃprekṣya sā guṇavatī bhāryā tasya pativratā । bhītaṃ prasannayā prāha vācā pīnapayodharā ।।
svāmin kimatra bhavato bhītiradya pravartate । tad brūhi me yathā tattvaṃ na rājñāṃ kīrtaye tvidam ।। sa tasyā vākyamākarṇya lajjāvanatacetanaḥ । novāca kiñcinnṛpatirjñānadṛṣṭyā viveda sā ।।
na bhetavyaṃ tvayā svāmin kāryaṃ pāpaviśodhanam । bhīte tvayi mahārāja rāṣṭraṃ te nāśameṣyati ।। tadā sa rājā dyutimān nirgatya tu purāt tataḥ । gatvā kaṇvāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra mahāmunim ।।
niśamya kaṇvavadanāt prāyaścittavidhiṃ śubham । jagāma himavatpṛṣṭhaṃ samuddiśya mahābalaḥ ।। so apaśyat pathi rājendro gandharvavaramuttamam । bhrājamānaṃ śriyā vyomni bhūṣitaṃ divyamālayā ।।
vīkṣya mālāmamitraghnaḥ sasmārāpsarasāṃ varām । urvaśīṃ tāṃ manaścakre tasyā eveyamarhati ।। so atīva kāmuko rājā gandharveṇātha tena hi । cakāra sumahad yuddhaṃ mālāmādātumudyataḥ ।।
vijitya samare mālāṃ gṛhītvā durjayo dvijāḥ । jagāma tāmapsarasaṃ kālindīṃ draṣṭumādarāt ।। adṛṣṭvāpsarasaṃ tatra kāmabāṇābhipīḍitaḥ । babhrāma sakalāṃ pṛthvīṃ saptadvīpasamanvitām ।।
ākramya himavatpārśvamurvaśīdarśanotsukaḥ । jagāma śailapravaraṃ hemakūṭamiti śrutam ।। tatra tatrāpsarovaryā dṛṣṭvā taṃ siṃhavikramam । kāmaṃ saṃdadhire ghoraṃ bhūṣitaṃ citramālayā ।।
saṃsmarannurvaśīvākyaṃ tasyāṃ saṃsaktamānasaḥ । na paśyati smatāḥ sarvāgiriśṛṅgāṇijagmivān ।। tatrāpyapsarasaṃ divyāmadṛṣṭvā kāmapīḍitaḥ । devalokaṃ mahāmeruṃ yayau devaparākramaḥ ।।
sa tatra mānasaṃ nāma sarastrailokyaviśrutam । bheje śṛṅgāṇyatikramya svabāhubalabhāvitaḥ ।। sa tasya tīre subhagāṃ carantīmatilālasām । dṛṣṭavānanavadyāṅgīṃ tasyai mālāṃ dadau punaḥ ।।
sa mālayā tadā devīṃ bhūṣitāṃ prekṣya mohitaḥ । reme kṛtārthamātmānaṃ jānānaḥ suciraṃ tayā ।। athorvaśī rājavaryaṃ ratānte vākyamabravīt । kiṃ kṛtaṃ bhavatā pūrvaṃ purīṃ gatvā vṛthā nṛpa ।।
sa tasyai sarvamācaṣṭa patnyā yat samudīritam । kaṇvasya darśanaṃ caiva mālāpaharaṇaṃ tathā ।। śrutvaitad vyāhṛtaṃ tena gacchetyāha hitaiṣiṇī । śāpaṃ dāsyati te kaṇvo mamāpi bhavataḥ priyā ।।
tayāsakṛnmahārājaḥ prokto api madamohitaḥ । na tatyajātha tatpārśvaṃ tatra saṃnyastamānasaḥ ।। tatorvaśī kāmarūpā rājñe svaṃ rūpamutkaṭam । suromaśaṃ piṅgalākṣaṃ darśayāmāsa sarvadā ।।
tasyāṃ viraktacetaskaḥ smṛtvā kaṇvābhibhāṣitam । dhiṅmāmiti viniścityatapaḥ kartuṃ samārabhat ।। saṃvatsaradvādaśakaṃ kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ । bhūya eva dvādaśakaṃ vāyubhakṣo abhavannṛpaḥ ।।
gatvā kaṇvāśramaṃ bhītyā tasmai sarvaṃ nyavedayat । vāsamapsarasā bhūyastapoyogamanuttamam ।। vīkṣya taṃ rājaśārdūlaṃ prasanno bhagavānṛṣiḥ । kartukāmo hi nirbojaṃ tasyāghamidamabravīt ।।
gaccha vārāṇasīṃ divyāmīśvarādhyuṣitāṃ purīm । āste mocayituṃ lokaṃ tatra devo maheśvaraḥ ।। snātvā saṃtarpya vidhivad gaṅgāyāndevatāḥ pitṝn । dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaraṃ liṅgaṅkilbiṣānmokṣyase akhilāt ।।
praṇamya śirasā kaṇvamanujñāpya ca durjayaḥ । vārāṇasyāṃ haraṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpānmukto abhavat tataḥ ।। jagāma svapurīṃ śubhrāṃ pālayāmāsa medinīm । yājayāmāsa taṃ kaṇvo yācito ghṛṇayā muniḥ ।।
tasya putro atha matimān supratīka iti śrutaḥ । babhūva jātamātraṃ taṃ rājānamupatasthire ।। urvaśyāṃ ca mahāvīryāḥ sapta devasutopamāḥ । kanyā jagṛhire sarvā jandharvadayitā dvijāḥ ।।
eṣa va kathitaḥ samyak sahastrajita uttamaḥ । vaṃśaḥ pāpaharo nṛṇāṃ kroṣṭorapi nibodhata ।। kroṣṭoreko abhavat putro vṛjinīvāniti śrutiḥ । tasya putro mahān svātiruśadgustatsuto abhavat ।।
uśadgorabhavat putro nāmnā citraratho balī । atha caitrarathirloke śaśabinduriti smṛtaḥ ।। tasya putraḥ pṛthuyaśā rājābhūd dharmatatparaḥ । pṛthukarmā ca tatputrastasmāt pṛthujayo abhavat ।।
pṛthukīrtirabhūt tasmāt pṛthudānastato abhavat । pṛthuśravāstasya putrastasyāsīt pṛthusattamaḥ ।। uśanā tasya putro abūt siteṣustatsuto abhavat । tasyābhūd rukmakavacaḥ parāvṛt tasya sattamāḥ ।।
parāvṛtaḥ suto jajñe jyāmagho lokaviśrutaḥ । tasmād vidarbhaḥ saṃjajñe vidarbhāt krathakaiśikau ।। romapādastṛtīyastu babhrustasyātmajo nṛpaḥ । dhṛtistasyābhavat putraḥ saṃstastasyāpyabhūt sutaḥ ।।
saṃstasya putro balavān nāmnā viśvasahastu saḥ । tasya putro mahāvīryaḥ prajāvān kauśikastataḥ । abhūt tasya suto dhīmān sumantustatsuto analaḥ ।। kaiśikasya sutaścediścaidyāstasyābhavan sutāḥ ।
teṣāṃ pradhāno jyotiṣmān vapuṣmāṃstatsuto abhavat ।। vapuṣmato bṛhanmedhā śrīdevastatsuto abhavat । tasya vītaratho viprā rudrabhakto mahābalaḥ ।। krathasyāpyabhavat kuntī vṛṣṇī tasyābhavat sutaḥ ।
vṛṣṇernivṛttirutpanno daśārhastasya tu dvijāḥ ।। daśārhaputropyāroho jīmūtastatsuto abhavat । jaimūtirabhavad vīro vikṛtiḥ paravīrahā ।। tasya bhīmarathaḥ putraḥ tasmānnavaratho abhavat ।
dānadharmarato nityaṃ samyakśīlaparāyaṇaḥ ।। kadācinmṛgayāṃ yāto dṛṣṭvā rākṣasamūrjitam । dudrāva mahātaviṣṭo bhayena munipuṅgavāḥ ।। anvadhāvata saṃkruddho rākṣasastaṃ mahābalaḥ ।
duryodhano agnisaṃkāśaḥ śūlāsaktamahākaraḥ ।। rājā navaratho bhītyā nātidūrādanuttamam । apaśyat paramaṃ sthānaṃ sarasvatyā sugopitam ।। sa tadvegena mahatā saṃprāpya matimān nṛpaḥ ।
vavande śirasā dṛṣṭvā sākṣād devīṃ sarasvatīm ।। tuṣṭāva vāgbhiriṣṭābhirbaddhāñjaliramitrajit । papāta daṇḍavad bhūmau tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। namasyāmi mahādevīṃ sākṣād devīṃ sarasvatīm ।
vāgdevatāmanādyantāmīśvarīṃ brahmacāriṇīm ।। namasye jagatāṃ yoniṃ yoginīṃ paramāṃ kalām । hiraṇyagarbhamahiṣīṃ trinetrāṃ candraśekharām ।। namasye paramānandāṃ citkalāṃ brahmarūpiṇīm ।
pāhi māṃ parameśāni bhītaṃ śaraṇamāgatam ।। etasminnantare kruddho rājānaṃ rākṣaseśvaraḥ । hantuṃ samāgataḥ sthānaṃ yatra devī sarasvatī ।। samudyamya tadā śūlaṃ praveṣṭuṃ baladarpitaḥ ।
trilokamātustatsthānaṃ śaśāṅkādityasaṃnnibham ।। tadantare mahad bhūtaṃ yugāntādityasannibham । śūlenorasi nirbhidya pātayāmāsa taṃ bhuvi ।। gacchetyāha mahārāja na sthātavyaṃ tvayā punaḥ ।
idānīṃ nirbhayastūrṇaṃ sthāne asmin rākṣaso hataḥ ।। tataḥ praṇamya hṛṣṭātmā rājā navarathaḥ parām । purīṃ jagāma viprendrāḥ purandarapuropamām ।। sthāpayāmāsa deveśīṃ tatra bhaktisamanvitaḥ ।
īje ca vividhairyajñairhemairdevīṃ sarasvatīm ।। tasya cāsīd daśarathaḥ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ । devyā bhakto mahātejāḥ śakunistasya cātmajaḥ ।। tasmāt karambhaḥ saṃbhūto devarāto abhavat tataḥ ।
īje sa cāśvamedhena devakṣatraśca tatsutaḥ ।। madhustasya tu dāyādastasmāt kuruvaśo abhavat । putradvayamabhūt tasya sutrāmā cānureva ca ।। anostu purukutso abhūdaṃśustasya ca rikthabhāk ।
athāṃśoḥ sattvato nāma viṣṇubhaktaḥ pratāpavān । mahātmā dānanirato dhanurvedavidāṃ varaḥ ।। sa nāradasya vacanād vāsudevārcanānvitam । śāstraṃ pravartayāmāsa kuṇḍagolādibhiḥ śrutam ।।
tasya nāmnā tu vikhyātaṃ sāttvataṃ nāma śobhanam । pravartate mahāśāstraṃ kuṇḍādīnāṃ hitāvaham ।। sāttvatastasya putro abhūt sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ । puṇyaśloko mahārājastena vai tatpravartitam ।।
sāttvataḥ sattvasaṃpannaḥ kauśalyāṃ suṣuve sutān । andhakaṃ vai mahābhojaṃ vṛṣṇiṃ devāvṛdhaṃ nṛpam । jyeṣṭhaṃ ca bhajamānākhyaṃ dhanurvedavidāṃ varam ।। teṣāṃ devāvṛdho rājā cacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ ।
putraḥ sarvaguṇopeto mama bhūyāditi prabhuḥ ।। tasya babhruriti khyātaḥ puṇyaśloko abhavannṛpaḥ । dhārmiko rūpasaṃpannastattvajñānarataḥ sadā ।। bhajamānasya sṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānā vijajñire ।
teṣāṃ pradhānau vikhyātau nimiḥ kṛkaṇa eva ca ।। mahābhojakule jātā bhojā vaimārtikāstathā । vṛṣṇeḥ sumitro balavānanamitraḥ śinastathā ।। anamitrādabhūnnighno nighnasya dvau babhūvatuḥ ।
prasenastu mahābhāgaḥ satrājinnāma cottamaḥ ।। anamitrācchinirjajñe kaniṣṭhād vṛṣṇinandanāt । satyavān satyasaṃpannaḥ satyakastatsuto abhavat ।। sātyakiryuyudhānastu tasyāsaṅgo abhavat sutaḥ ।
kuṇistasya suto dhīmāṃstasya putro yugandharaḥ ।। mādrayā vṛṣṇeḥ suto jajñe pṛśnirvai yadunandanaḥ । jajñāte tanayau pṛśneḥ śvaphalkaścitrakaśca ha ।। śvaphalkaḥ kāśirājasya sutāṃ bhāryāmavindata ।
tasyāmajanayat putramakrūraṃ nāma dhārmikam । upamaṅgustathā maṅguranye ca bahavaḥ sutāḥ ।। akrūrasya smṛtaḥ putro devavāniti viśrutaḥ । upadevaśca puṇyātmā tayorviśvapramāthinau ।।
citrakasyābhavat putraḥ pṛthurvipṛthureva ca । aśvagrīvaḥ subāhuśca supārśvakagaveṣaṇau ।। andhakāt kāśyaduhitā lebhe ca caturaḥ sutān । kukuraṃ bhajamānaṃ ca śuciṃ kambalabarhiṣam ।।
kukurasya suto vṛṣṇirvṛṣṇestu tanayo abhavat । kapotaromā vipulastasya putro vilomakaḥ ।। tasyāsīt tumburusakhā vidvān putro nalaḥ kila । khyāyate tasya nāmānuranorānakadundubhiḥ ।।
sa govardhanamāsādya tatāpa vipulaṃ tapaḥ । varaṃ tasmai dadau devo brahmā lokamaheśvaraḥ ।। vaṃśasya cākṣayāṃ kīrti gānayogamanuttamam । gurorabhyadhikaṃ viprāḥ kāmarūpitvameva ca ।।
sa labdhvā varamavyagro vareṇyaṃ vṛṣavāhanam । pūjayāmāsa gānena sthāṇuṃ tridaśapūjitam ।। tasya gānaratasyātha bhagavānambikāpatiḥ । kanyāratnaṃ dadau devo durlabhaṃ tridaśairapi ।।
tayā sa saṅgato rājā gānayogamanuttamam । aśikṣayadamitraghnaḥ priyāṃ tāṃ bhrāntalocanām ।। tasyāmutpādayāmāsa subhujaṃ nāma śobhanam । rūpalāvaṇyasaṃpannāṃ hrīmatīmapi kanyakām ।।
tatastaṃ jananī putraṃ bālye vayasi śobhanam । śikṣayāmāsa vidhivad gānavidyāṃ ca kanyakām ।। kṛtopanayano vedānadhītya vidhivad guroḥ । udvavāhātmajāṃ kanyāṃ gandharvāṇāṃ tu mānasīm ।।
tasyāmutpādayāmāsa pañca putrānanuttamān । vīṇāvādanatattvajñān gānaśāstraviśāradān ।। putraiḥ pautraiḥ sapatnīko rājā gānaviśāradaḥ । pūjayāmāsa gānena devaṃ tripuranāśanam ।।
hrīmatī cāpi yā kanyā śrīrivāyatalocanā । subāhurnāma gandharvastāmādāya yayau purīm ।। tasyāmapyabhavan putrā gandharvasya sutejasaḥ । suṣeṇavīrasugrīvasubhojanaravāhanāḥ ।।
athāsīdabhijit putro vīrastvānakadundubheḥ । punarvasuścābhijitaḥ saṃbabhūvāhukaḥ sutaḥ ।। āhukasyograsenaśca devakaśca dvijottamāḥ । devakasya sutā vīrā jajñire tridaśopamāḥ ।।
devavānupadevaśca sudevo devarakṣitaḥ । teṣāṃ svasāraḥ saptāsan vasudevāya tā dadau ।। vṛkadevopadevā ca tathānyā devarakṣitā । śrīdevā śāntidevā ca sahadevā sahadevā ca suvratā ।
devakī cāpi tāsāṃ tu variṣṭhābhūt sumadhyamā ।। agrasenasya putro abhūnnyagrodhaḥ kaṃsa eva ca । subhūmī rāṣṭrapālaśca tuṣṭimāñchaṅkureva ca ।। bhajamānādabūt putraḥ prakhyāto asau vidūrathaḥ ।
tasya śūraḥ śamistasmāt pratikṣatrastato abhavat ।। svayaṃbhojastatastasmād hṛdikaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ । kṛtavarmātha tatputro devarastatsutaḥ smṛtaḥ । sa śūrastatsuto dhīmān vasudevo atha tatsutaḥ ।।
vasudevāvanmahābāhurvāsudevo jagadguruḥ । babhūva devakīputro devairabhyarthito hariḥ ।। rohiṇī ca mahābhāgā vasudevasya śobhanā । asūta patnī saṃkarṣaṃ rāmaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ halāyudham ।।
sa eva paramātmāsau vāsudevo jaganmayaḥ । halāyudhaḥ svayaṃ sākṣāccheṣaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। bhṛguśāpacchalenaiva mānayan mānuṣīṃ tanum । babhūta tasyāṃ devakyāṃ rohiṇyāmapi mādhavaḥ ।।
umādehasamudbhūtā yoganidrā ca kauśīkī । niyogād vāsudevasya yaśodātanayā hyabhūt ।। ye cānye vasudevasya vāsudevāgrajāḥ sutāḥ । prāgeva kaṃsastān sarvān jaghāna munipuṅgavāḥ ।।
suṣeṇaśca tathodāyī bhadraseno mahābalaḥ । ṛjudāso bhadradāsaḥ kīrtimānapi pūrvajaḥ ।। hateṣveteṣu sarveṣu rohiṇī vasudevataḥ । asūta rāmaṃ lokeśaṃ balabhadraṃ halāyudham ।।
jāte atha rāme devānāmādimātmānamacyutam । asūta devakī kṛṣṇaṃ śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam ।। revatī nāma rāmasya bhāryāsīt suguṇānvitā । tasyāmutpādayāmāsa putrau dvau niśaṭholmukau ।।
ṣoḍaśastrīsahastrāṇi kṛṣṇasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ । babhūvurātmajāstāsu śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ ।। cārudeṣṇaḥ sucāruśca cāruveṣo yaśodharaḥ । cāruśravāścāruyaśāḥ pradyumnaḥ śaṅkha eva ca ।।
rukmiṇya vāsudevasyāṃ mahābalaparākramāḥ । viśiṣṭāḥ sarvaputrāṇāṃ saṃbabhūvurim sutāḥ ।। tān dṛṣṭvā tanayān vīrān raukmiṇeyāñjanārdanam । jāmbavatyabravīt kṛṣṇaṃ bhāryā tasya śucismitā ।।
mama tvaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa viśiṣṭaṃ guṇavattamam । sureśasadṛśaṃ putraṃ dehi dānavasūdana ।। jātbavatyā vacaḥ śrutvā jagannāthaḥ svayaṃ hariḥ । samārebhe tapaḥ kartuṃ taponidhirarindamaḥ ।।
tacchṛṇudhvaṃ muniśreṣṭhā yathāsau devakīsutaḥ । dṛṣṭvā lebhe sutaṃ rudraṃ taptvā tīvraṃ mahat tapaḥ ।। atha devo hṛṣīkeśo bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ । tatāpa ghoraṃ putrārthaṃ nidānaṃ tapasastapaḥ ।।
svecchayāpyavatīrṇo asau kṛtakṛtyo api viśvadhṛk । cacāra svātmano mūlaṃ bodhayan bhāvamaiśvaram ।। jagāma yogibhirjuṣṭaṃ nānāpakṣisamākulam । āśramaṃ tūpamanyorvai munīndrasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
tapattrirājamārūḍhaḥ suparṇamatitejasam । śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiḥ śrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇaḥ ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇaṃ nānāpuṣpopaśobhitam । ṛṣīṇāmāśramairjuṣṭaṃ vedaghoṣanināditam ।।
siṃharkṣaśarabhākīrṇaṃ śārdūlagajasaṃyutam । vimalasvādupānīyaiḥ sarobhirupaśobhitam ।। ārāmairvividhairjuṣṭaṃ devatāyatanaiḥ śubhaiḥ । ṛṣikairṛṣiputraiśca mahāmunigaṇaistathā ।।
vedādhyayanasaṃpannaiḥ sevitaṃ cāgnihotribhiḥ । yogibhirdhyānaniratairnāsāgragatalocanaiḥ ।। upetaṃ sarvataḥ puṇyaṃ jñānibhistattvadarśibhiḥ । nadībhirabhito juṣṭaṃ jāpakairbrahmavādibhiḥ ।।
sevitaṃ tāpasaiḥ puṇyairīśārādhanatatparaiḥ । praśāntaiḥ satyasaṃkalpairniḥ śokairnirupadravaiḥ ।। bhasmāvadātasarvāṅgai rudrajāpyaparāyaṇaiḥ । muṇḍitairjaṭilaiḥ śuddhaistathānyaiśca śikhājaṭaiḥ ।
sevitaṃ tāpasairnitya jñānibhirbrahmacāribhiḥ ।। tatrāśramavare ramye siddhāśramavibhūṣite । gaṅgā bhagavatī nityaṃ vahatyevāghanāśinī ।। sa tānanviṣya viśvātmā tāpasān vītakalmaṣān ।
praṇāmenātha vacasā pūjayāmāsa mādhavaḥ ।। te te dṛṣṭvā jagadyoniṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam । praṇemurbhaktisaṃyuktā yogināṃ paramaṃ gurum ।। stuvanti vaidikairmantraiḥ kṛtvā hṛdi sanātanam ।
procuranyonyamavyaktamādidevaṃ mahāmunim ।। ayaṃ sa bhagavānekaḥ sākṣānnārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ । agacchatyadhunā devaḥ purāṇapuruṣaḥ svayam ।। ayamevāvyayaḥ straṣṭā saṃhartā caiva rakṣakaḥ ।
amūrto mūrtimān bhūtvā munīn draṣṭumihāgataḥ ।। eṣa dhātā vidhātā ca samāgacchati sarvagaḥ । anādirakṣayo ananto mahābhūto maheśvaraḥ ।। śrutvā śrutvā haristeṣāṃ vacāṃsi vacanātigaḥ ।
yayau sa tūrṇaṃ govindaḥ sthānaṃ tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। upaspṛśyātha bhāvena tīrthe tīrthe sa yādavaḥ । cakāra devakīsūnurdevarṣipitṛtarpaṇam ।। nadīnāṃ tīrasaṃsthāni sthāpitāni munīśvaraiḥ ।
liṅgāni pūjayāmāsa śaṃbhoramitatejasaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā samāyāntaṃ yatra yatra janārdanam । pūjayāñcakrire puṣpairakṣataistatra vāsinaḥ ।। samīkṣya vāsudevaṃ taṃ śārṅgaśaṅkhāsidhāriṇam ।
tasthire niścalāḥ sarve śubhāṅgaṃ tannivāsinaḥ ।। yāni tatrārurukṣūṇāṃ mānasāni janārdanam । dṛṣṭvā samīhitānyāsan niṣkrāmanti purāhiram ।। athāvagāhya gaṅgāyāṃ kṛtvā devāditarpaṇam ।
ādāya puṣpavaryāṇi munīndrasyāviśad gṛham ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ yogināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ bhasmoddhūlitavigraham । jaṭācīradharaṃ śāntaṃ nanāma śirasā munim ।। ālokya kṛṣṇamāyāntaṃ pūjayāmāsa tattvavit ।
āsane cāsayāmāsa yogināṃ prathamātithim ।। uvāca vacasāṃ yoniṃ jānīmaḥ paramaṃ padam । viṣṇumavyaktasaṃsthānaṃ śiṣyabhāvena saṃsthitam ।। svāgataṃ te hṛṣīkeśa saphalāni tapāṃsi naḥ ।
yad sākṣādeva viśvātmā madgehaṃ viṣṇurāgataḥ ।। tvāṃ na paśyanti munayo yatanto api hi yoginaḥ । tādṛśasyātha bhavataḥ kimāgamanakāraṇam ।। śrutvopamanyostad vākyaṃ bhagavān keśimardanaḥ ।
vyājahāra mahāyogī vacanaṃ praṇipatya tam ।। bhagavan draṣṭumicchāmi girīśaṃ kṛttivāsasam । saṃprāpto bhavataḥ sthānaṃ bhagavaddarśanotsukaḥ ।। kathaṃ sa bhagavānīśo dṛśyo yogavidāṃ varaḥ ।
mayācireṇa kutrāhaṃ drakṣyāmi tamumāpatim ।। ityāha bhagavānukto dṛśyate parameśvaraḥ । bhaktyā cogreṇa tapasā tatkuruṣveha yatnataḥ ।। iheśvaraṃ devadevaṃ munīndrā brahmavādinaḥ ।
dhyāyanto atrāsate devaṃ jāpinastāpasāśca ye ।। iha devaḥ sapatnīko bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ । krīḍate vividhairbhūtairyogibhiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। ihāśrame purā rudrāt tapastaptvā sudāruṇam ।
lebhe maheśvarād yogaṃ vasiṣṭho bhagavānṛṣiḥ ।। ihaiva bhagavān vyasaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ । dṛṣṭvā taṃ paramaṃ jñānaṃ labdhavānīśvareśvaram ।। ihāśramavare ramye tapastaptvā kapardinaḥ ।
avindat putrakān rudrāt surabhirbhaktisaṃyutā ।। ihaiva devatāḥ pūrvaṃ kālād bhītā maheśvaram । dṛṣṭavanto haraṃ śrīmannirbhayā nirvṛtiṃ yayuḥ ।। ihārādhya mahādevaṃ sāvarṇistapatāṃ varaḥ ।
labdhavān paramaṃ yogaṃ granthakāratvamuttamam ।। pravartayāmāsa śubhāṃ kṛtvā vai saṃhitāṃ dvijaḥ । paurāṇikīṃ supuṇyārthāṃ sacchiṣyeṣu dvijātiṣu ।। ihaiva saṃhitāṃ dṛṣṭvā kāpeyaḥ śāṃśapāyanaḥ ।
mahādevaṃ cakāremāṃ paurāṇīṃ tanniyogataḥ । dvādaśaiva sahastrāṇi ślokānāṃ puruṣottama ।। iha pravartitā puṇyā dvyaṣṭasāhastrikottarā । vāyavīyottaraṃ nāma purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam ।
ihaiva khyāpitaṃ śiṣyaiḥ śāṃśapāyanabhāṣitam ।। yājñavalkyo mahāyogī dṛṣṭvātra tapasā haram । cakāra tanniyogena yogaśāstramanuttamam ।। ihaiva bhṛguṇā pūrvaṃ taptvā vai paramaṃ tapaḥ ।
śukro maheśvarāt putro labdho yogavidāṃ varaḥ ।। tasmādihaiva deveśaṃ tapastaptvā maheśvaram । draṣṭumarhasi viśveśamugraṃ bhīmaṃ kapardinam ।। evamuktvā dadau jñānamupamanyurmahāmuniḥ ।
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kṛṣṇāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe ।। sa tena munivaryeṇa vyāhṛto madhusūdanaḥ । tatraiva tapasā devaṃ rudramārādhayat prabhuḥ ।। bhasmauddhūlitasarvāṅgo muṇḍo valkalasaṃyutaḥ ।
jajāpa rudramaniśaṃ śivaikāhitamānasaḥ ।। tato bahutithe kāle somaḥ somārdhabhūṣaṇaḥ । adṛśyata mahādevo vyomni devyā maheśvaraḥ ।। pinākinaṃ śūlinaṃ devadevam ।
devyā mahādevamasau dadarśa ।। nṛsiṃhacarmāvṛtasarvagātram । sahastrasūryapratimaṃ dadarśa ।। sanātanaṃ yoginamīśitāram ।
prāṇeśvaraṃ śaṃbhumasau dadarśa ।। nendro na cāgnirvaruṇo na mṛtyuḥ । tamādidevaṃ purato dadarśa ।। svātmānamavyaktamanantarūpam ।
śaṅkhāsicakrārpitahastamādyam ।। haṃsādhirūḍhaṃ puruṣaṃ dadarśa । pitāmahaṃ lokaguruṃ divastham ।। nandīśvarādīnamitaprabhāvān ।
kumāramagnipatimaṃ saśākham ।। pracetasaṃ dakṣamathāpi kaṇvam । svāyaṃbhuvaṃ cāpi manuṃ dadarśa ।। baddhāñjalirviṣṇurudārabuddhiḥ ।
svātmanyathātmānamasau vicintya ।। brahmādhipaṃ tvāmṛṣayo vadanti । tvāmeva sarva pravadanti santaḥ ।। saṃhartā dinakaramaṇḍalādhivāsaḥ ।
satvāmekaṃ śaraṇamupaimi devamīśam ।। yogāstvāṃ satatamupāsate hṛdistham । tvāmekaṃ śaraṇamupaimi devamīśam ।। dattvāsau bhavati vimuktaviśvabandhaḥ ।
smṛtvā te padayugalaṃ bhavatprasādāt ।। tattvaṃ jyotiranantamekamacalaṃ satyaṃ paraṃ sarvagam । nityaṃ tvāmahamupaimi satyavibhavaṃviśveśvarantaṃśivam ।। oṃ namo nīlakaṇṭhāya trinetrāya ca raṃhase ।
mahādevāya te nityamīśānāya namo namaḥ ।। namaḥ pinākine tubhyaṃ namo muṇḍāya daṇḍine । namaste vajrahastāya digvastrāya kapardine ।। namo bhairavanādāya kālarūpāya daṃṣṭriṇe ।
nāgayajñopavītāya namaste vahniretase ।। namo astu te girīśāya svāhākārāya te namaḥ । namo muktāṭṭahāsāya bhīmāya ca namo namaḥ ।। namaste kāmanāśāya namaḥ kālapramāthine ।
namo bhairavaveṣāya harāya ca niṣaṅgiṇe ।। namo astu te tryambakāya namaste kṛttivāsase । namo ambikādhipataye paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। namaste vyomarūpāya vyomādhipataye namaḥ ।
naranārīśarīrāya sāṃkhyayogapravartine ।। namo daivatanāthāya devānugataliṅgine । kumāragurave tubhyaṃ devadevāya te namaḥ ।। tamo yajñādhipataye namaste brahmacāriṇe ।
mṛgavyādhāya mahate brahmādhipataye namaḥ ।। namo haṃsāya viśvāya mohanāya namo namaḥ । yogine yogagamyāya yogamāyāya te namaḥ ।। namaste prāṇapālāya ghaṇṭānādapriyāya ca ।
kapāline namastubhyaṃ jyotiṣāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। namo namo namastubhyaṃ bhūya eva namo namaḥ । mahyaṃ sarvātmanā kāmān prayaccha parameśvara ।। evaṃ hi bhaktyā deveśamabhiṣṭūya sa mādhavaḥ ।
papāta pādayorviprā devadevyoḥ sa daṇḍavat ।। utthāpya bhagavān somaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ keśiniṣūdanam । babhāṣe madhuraṃ vākyaṃ meghagambhīraniḥ svanaḥ ।। kimarthaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa tapastaptaṃ tvayāvyaya ।
tvameva dātā sarveṣāṃ kāmānāṃ kāmināmiha ।। tvaṃ hi sā paramā mūrtirmama nārāyaṇāhvayā । nānavāptaṃ tvayā tāta vidyate puruṣottama ।। vettha nārāyaṇānantamātmānaṃ parameśvaram ।
mahādevaṃ mahāyogaṃ svena yogena keśava ।। śrutvā tadvacanaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prahasan vai vṛṣadhvajam । uvāca vīkṣya viśveśaṃ devīṃ ca himaśailajām ।। jñātaṃ hi bhavatā sarvaṃ svena yogena śaṅkara ।
icchāmyātmasamaṃ putraṃ tvadbhaktaṃ dehi śaṅkara ।। tathāstvityāha viśvātmā prahṛṣṭamanasā haraḥ । devīmālokya girijāṃ keśavaṃ pariṣasvaje ।। tataḥ sā jagatāṃ mātā śaṅkarārdhaśarīriṇī ।
vyājahāra hṛṣīkeśaṃ devī himagirīndrajā ।। vatsa jāne tavānantāṃ niścalāṃ sarvadācyuta । ananyāmīśvare bhaktimātmanyapi ca keśava ।। tvaṃ hi nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣāt sarvātmā puruṣottamaḥ ।
prārthito daivataiḥ pūrvaṃ saṃjāto daivakīsutaḥ ।। paśya tvamātmanātmānamātmīyamamalaṃ padam । nāvayorvidyate bheda evaṃ paśyanti sūrayaḥ ।। imānimān varāniṣṭān matto gṛhṇīṣva keśava ।
sarvajñatvaṃ tathaiśvaryaṃ jñānaṃ tat pārameśvaram । īśvare niścalāṃ bhaktimātmanyapi paraṃ balam ।। evamuktastayā kṛṣṇo mahādevyā janārdanaḥ । āśiṣaṃ śirasāhṛṅṇād devo apyāha maheśvaraḥ ।।
kareṇa devyā saha devadevaḥ । r jagāma kailāsagiriṃ girīśaḥ ।। praviśya meruśikharaṃ kailāsaṃ kanakaprabham । rarāma bhagavān somaḥ keśavena maheśvaraḥ ।।
apaśyaṃstaṃ mahātmānaṃ kailāsagirivāsinaḥ । pūjayāñcakrire kṛṣṇaṃ devadevamathācyutam ।। caturbāhumudārāṅgaṃ kālameghasamaprabham । kirīṭinaṃ śārṅgapāṇi śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam ।।
dīrghabāhuṃ viśālākṣaṃ pītavāsasamacyutam । dadhānamurasā mālāṃ vaijayantīmanuttamām ।। bhrājamānaṃ śriyā divyaṃ yuvānamatikomalam । padmāṅghrinayanaṃ cāru susmitaṃ sugatipradam ।।
kadācit tatra līlārthaṃ devakīnandavardhanaḥ । bhrājamānaḥ śrīyā kṛṣṇaścacāra girikandare ।। gandharvāpsarasāṃ mukhyā nāgakanyāśca kṛtsnaśaḥ । siddhā yakṣāśca gandharvāstatra tatra jaganmayam ।।
dṛṣṭvāścaryaṃ paraṃ gatvā harṣādutphullocanāḥ । mumucuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi tasya mūrdhni mahātmanaḥ ।। gandharvakanyakā divyāstadvadapsarasāṃ varāḥ । dṛṣṭvā cakamire kṛṣṇaṃ strastavastravibhūṣaṇāḥ ।।
kāścid gāyanti vividhāṃ gītiṃ gītaviśāradāḥ । saṃprekṣya devakīsūnuṃ sundaryaḥ kāmamohitāḥ ।। kāścidvilāsabahulā nṛtyanti sma tadagrataḥ । saṃprekṣya saṃsthitāḥ kāścit papustadvadanāmṛtam ।।
kāścid bhūṣaṇavaryāṇi svāṅgādādāya sādaram । bhūṣayāñcakrire kṛṣṇaṃ kāminyo lokabhūṣaṇam ।। kāścid bhūṣaṇavaryāṇi samādāya tadaṅgataḥ । svātmānaṃ būṣayāmāsuḥ svātmagairapi mādhavam ।।
kāścidāgatya kṛṣṇasya samīpaṃ kāmamohitāḥ । cucumburvadanāmbhojaṃ harermugdhamṛgekṣaṇāḥ ।। pragṛhya kāścid govindaṃ kareṇa bhavanaṃ svakam । prāpayāmāsurlokādiṃ māyayā tasya mohitāḥ ।।
tāsāṃ sa bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ kāmān kamalalocanaḥ । bahūni kṛtvā rūpāṇi pūrayāmāsa līlayā ।। evaṃ vai suciraṃ kālaṃ devadevapure hariḥ । reme nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān māyayā mohayañjagat ।।
gate bahutithe kāle dvāravatyāṃ nivāsinaḥ । babhūvurvihvalā bhītā govindavirahe janāḥ ।। tataḥ suparṇo balavān pūrvameva visajitaḥ । kṛṣṇena mārgamāṇastaṃ himavantaṃ yayau girim ।।
adṛṣṭvā tatra govindaṃ praṇamya śirasā munim । ājagāmopamanyuṃ taṃ purīṃ dvāravatīṃ punaḥ ।। tadantare mahādaityā rākṣasāścātibhīṣaṇāḥ । ājagmurdvārakāṃ śubhrāṃ bhīṣayantaḥ sahastraśaḥ ।।
sa tān suparṇo balavān kṛṣṇatulyaparākramaḥ । hatvā yuddhena mahatā rakṣati sma purīṃ śubhām ।। etasminneva kāle tu nārado bhagavānṛṣiḥ । dṛṣṭvā kailāsaśikhare kṛṣṇaṃ dvāravatīṃ gataḥ ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nāradamṛṣiṃ sarve tatra nivāsinaḥ । procurnārāyaṇo nāthaḥ kutrāste bhagavān hariḥ ।। sa tānuvāca bhagavān kailasaśikhare hariḥ । ramate adya mahāyogīṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvāhamihāgataḥ ।।
tasyopaśrutya vacanaṃ suparṇaḥ patatāṃ varaḥ । jagāmākāśago viprāḥ kailāsaṃ girimuttamam ।। dadarśa devakīsūnuṃ bhavane ratnamaṇḍite । varāsanasthaṃ govindaṃ devadevāntike harim ।।
upāsyamānamamarairdivyastrībhiḥ samantataḥ । mahādevagaṇaiḥ siddhairyogibhiḥ parivāritam ।। praṇamya daṇḍavad bhūmau suparṇaḥ śaṅkaraṃ śivam । nivedayāmāsa hareḥ pravṛttiṃ dvārake pure ।।
tataḥ praṇamya śirasā śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam । ājagāma purīṃ kṛṣṇaḥ so anujñāto hareṇa tu ।। āruhya kaśyapasutaṃ strīgaṇairabhipūjitaḥ । vacobhiramṛtāsvādairmānito madhusūdanaḥ ।।
vīkṣya yāntamamitraghnaṃ gandharvāpsarasāṃ varāḥ । anvagacchan mahoyogaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।। visarjayitvā viśvātmā sarvā evāṅganā hariḥ । yayau sa tūrṇaṃ govindo divyāṃ dvāravatīṃ purīm ।।
gate muraripau naiva kāminyo munipuṅgavāḥ । niśeva candrarahitā vinā tena cakāśire ।। śrutvā paurajanāstūrṇaṃ kṛṣṇāgamanamuttamam । maṇḍayāñcakrire divyāṃ purīṃ dvāravatīṃ śubhām ।।
patākābhirviśālābhirdhvajai ratnapariṣkṛtaiḥ । lājādibhiḥ purīṃ ramyāṃ bhūṣayāñcakrire tadā ।। avādayanta vividhān vāditrān madhurasvanān । śaṅkhān sahastraśo dadhmurvoṇāvādān vitenire ।।
praviṣṭamātre govinde purīṃ dvāravatīṃ śubhām । agāyan madhuraṃ gānaṃ striyo yauvanaśālinaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā nanṛturīśānaṃ sthitāḥ prāsādamūrdhasu । mumucuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi vasudevasutopari ।।
praviśya bhavanaṃ kṛṣṇa āśīrvādābhivardhitaḥ । varāsane mahāyogī bhāti devībhiranvitaḥ ।। suramye maṇḍape śubhre śaṅkhādyaiḥ parivāritaḥ । ātmajairabhito mukhyaiḥ strīsahastraiśca saṃvṛtaḥ ।।
tatrāsanavare ramye jāmbavatyā sahācyutaḥ । bhrājate mālayā devo yathā devyā samanvitaḥ ।। ājagmurdevagandharvā draṣṭuṃ lokādimavyayam । maharṣayaḥ pūrvajātā mārkaṇḍeyādayo dvijāḥ ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān kṛṣṇo mārkaṇḍeyaṃ samāgatam । nanāmotthāya śirasā svāsanaṃ ca dadau hariḥ ।। saṃpūjya tānṛṣigaṇān praṇāmena mahābhujaḥ । visarjayāmāsa harirdattvā tadabhivāñchitān ।।
tadā madhyāhnasamaye devadevaḥ svayaṃ hariḥ । snātvā śuklāmbaro bhānumupatiṣṭhat kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। jajāpa jāpyaṃ vidhivat prekṣamāṇo divākaram । tarpayāmāsa deveśo deveśo devān munigaṇān pitṝn ।।
praviśya devabhavanaṃ mārkaṇḍeyena caiva hi । pūjayāmāsa liṅgasthaṃ bhūteśaṃ bhūtibhūṣaṇam ।। samāpya niyamaṃ sarvaṃ niyantāsau nṛṇāṃ svayam । bhojayitvā munivaraṃ brāhmaṇānabhipūjya ca ।।
kṛtvātmayogaṃ viprendrā mārkaṇḍeyena cācyutaḥ । kathāḥ paurāṇikīḥ puṇyāścakre putrādibhirvṛtaḥ ।। athaitat sarvamakhilaṃ dṛṣṭvā karma mahāmuniḥ । mārkaṇḍeyo hasan kṛṣṇaṃ babhāṣe madhuraṃ vacaḥ ।।
kaḥ samārādhyate devo bhavatā karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ । brūhi tvaṃ karmabhiḥ pūjyo yogināṃ dhyeya eva ca ।। tvaṃ hi tat paramaṃ brahma nirvāṇamamalaṃ padam । bhārāvataraṇārthāya jāto vṛṣṇikule prabhuḥ ।।
tamabravīnmahābāhuḥ kṛṣṇo brahmavidāṃ varaḥ । śṛṇvatāmeva putrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ prahasanniva ।। bhavatā kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tathyameva na saṃśayaḥ । tathāpi devamīśānaṃ pūjayāmi sanātanam ।।
na me viprāsti kartavyaṃ nānavāptaṃ kathañcana । pūjayāmi tathāpīśaṃ jānannaitat paraṃ śivam ।। na vai paśyanti taṃ devaṃ māyayā mohitā janāḥ । tato ahaṃ svātmano mūlaṃ jñāpayan pūjayāmi tam ।।
na ca liṅgārcanāt puṇyaṃ lokesmin bhītināśanam । tathā liṅge hitāyaiṣāṃ lokānāṃ pūjayecchivam ।। yo ahaṃ talliṅgamityāhurvedavādavido janāḥ । tato ahamātmamīśānaṃ pūjayāmyātmanaiva tu ।।
tasyaiva paramā mūrtistanmayo ahaṃ na saṃśayaḥ । nāvayordyite bhedo vedeṣvevaṃ viniścayaḥ ।। eṣa devo mahādevaḥ sadā saṃsārabhīrubhiḥ । dhyeyaḥ pūjyaśca vandyaśca jñeyo liṅge maheśvaraḥ ।।
kiṃ talliṅgaṃ suraśreṣṭha liṅge saṃpūjyate ca kaḥ । brūhi kṛṣṇa viśālākṣa gahanaṃ hyetaduttamam ।। avyaktaṃ liṅgamityāhurānandaṃ jyotirakṣaram । vedā mahesvaraṃ devamāhurliṅginamavyayam ।।
purā caikārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame । prabodhārthaṃ brahmaṇo me prādurbhūtaḥ svayaṃ śivaḥ ।। tasmāt kālāt samārabhya brahmā cāhaṃ sadaiva hi । pūjayāvo mahādevaṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।
kathaṃ liṅgamabhūt pūrvamaiśvaraṃ paramaṃ padam । prabodhārthaṃ svayaṃ kṛṣṇa vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam ।। āsodekārṇavaṃ ghoramavibhāgaṃ tamomayam । madhye caikārṇave tasmin śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।।
sahastraśīrṣā bhūtvāhaṃ sahastrākṣaḥ sahastrapāt sahastrabāhuryuktātmā śayito ahaṃ sanātanaḥ ।। etasminnantare dūratā paśyami hyamitaprabham । koṭisūryapratīkāśaṃ bhrājamānaṃ śriyāvṛtam ।। caturvaraktraṃ mahāyogaṃ puruṣaṃ kāñcanaprabham ।
kṛṣṇājiradharaṃ devamṛgyajuḥ sāmabhiḥ stutam ।। nimeṣamātreṇa sa māṃ prāpto yogavidāṃ varaḥ । vyājahāra svayaṃ brahmā smayamāno mahādyutiḥ ।। kastvaṃ kuto vā kiṃ ceha tiṣṭhase vaha me prabho ।
ahaṃ kartā hi lokānāṃ svayaṃbhūḥ prapitāmahaḥ ।। evamuktastadā tena brahmaṇāhamuvāca ha । ahaṃ kartāsmi lokānāṃ saṃhartā ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। evaṃ vivāde vitate māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
prabodhārthaṃ paraṃ liṅgaṃ prādurbhūtaṃ śivātmakam ।। kālānalasamaprakhyaṃ jvālāmālāsamākulam । kṣayavṛddhivinirmuktamādimadhyāntavarjitam ।। tato māmāha bhagavānadho gaccha tvamāśu vai ।
antamasya vijānīma ūrdhvaṃ gacche ahamityajaḥ ।। tadāśu samayaṃ kṛtvā gatāvūrdhvamadhaśca dvau । pitāmaho apyahaṃ nāntaṃ jñātavantau samāḥ śatam ।। tato vismayamāpannau bhītau devasya śūlinaḥ ।
māyayā mohitau tasya dhyāyantau viśvamīśvaram ।। proccārantau mahānādamoṅkāraṃ paramaṃ padam । prahvāñjalipuṭopetau śaṃbhuṃ tuṣṭuvatuḥ param ।। brahmaviṣṇū ūcatuḥ ।
anādimalasaṃsārarogavaidyāya śaṃbhave । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।। pralayārṇavasaṃsthāya pralayodbhūtihetave । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।।
jvālāmālāvṛtāṅgāya jvalanastambharūpiṇe । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।। ādimadhyāntahīnāya svabāvāmaladīptaye । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।।
mahādevāya mahate jyotiṣe anantatejase । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।। pradhānapuruṣeśāya vyomarūpāya vedhase । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।।
nirvikārāya satyāya nityāyāmalatejase । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।। vedāntasārarūpāya kālarūpāya dhīmate । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅgamūrtaye ।।
evaṃ saṃstūyamānastu vyakto bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ । bhāti devo mahāyogī sūryakoṭisamaprabhaḥ ।। vaktrakoṭisahastreṇa grasamāna ivāmbaram । sahastrahastacaraṇaḥ sūryasomāgnilocanaḥ ।।
pinākapāṇirbhagavān kṛttivāsāstriśūlabhṛt । vyālayajñopavītaśca meghadundubhiniḥ svanaḥ ।। athovāca mahādevaḥ prīto ahaṃ surasattamau । paśyetaṃ māṃ mahādevaṃ bhayaṃ sarvaṃ pramucyatām ।।
yuvāṃ prasūtau gātrebhyo mama pūrvaṃ sanātanau । ayaṃ me dakṣiṇe pārśve brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । vāmapārśve ca me viṣṇuḥ pālako hṛdaye haraḥ ।। prīto ahaṃ yuvayoḥ samyak varaṃ dadmi yathepsitam ।
evamuktvātha māṃ devo mahādevaḥ svayaṃ śivaḥ । āliṅgya devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ prasādābhimukho abhavat ।। tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasau praṇipatya maheśvaram । ūcatuḥ prekṣya tadvaktraṃ nārāyaṇapitāmahau ।।
yadi prītiḥ samutpannā yadi deyo varaśca nau । bhaktirbhavatu nau nityaṃ tvayi deva maheśvare ।। tataḥ sa bhagavānīśaḥ prahasan parameśvaraḥ । uvāca māṃ mahādevaḥ prītaḥ prītena cetasā ।।
pralayasthitisargāṇāṃ kartā tvaṃ dharaṇīpate । vatsa vatsa hare viśvaṃ pālayaitaccarācaram ।। tridhā bhinno asmyahaṃ viṣṇo brahmaviṣṇuharākhyayā । sargarakṣālayaguṇairnirguṇo api nirañjanaḥ ।।
saṃmohaṃ tyaja bho viṣṇo pālayainaṃ pitāmaham । bhaviṣyatyeṣa bhagavāṃstava putraḥ sanātanaḥ ।। ahaṃ ca bhavato vaktrāt kalpādau ghorarūpadhṛk । śūlapāṇirbhaviṣyāmi krodhajastava putrakaḥ ।।
evamuktvā mahādevo brahmāṇaṃ munisattama । anugṛhya ca māṃ devastatraivāntaradhīyata ।। tataḥ prabhṛti lokeṣu liṅgārcā supratiṣṭhitā । liṅga tallayanād brahman brahmaṇaḥ paramaṃ vapuḥ ।।
etalliṅgasya māhātmyaṃ bhāṣitaṃ te mayānagha । etad budhyanti yogajñā na devā na ca dānavāḥ ।। etaddhi paramaṃ jñānamavyaktaṃ śivasaṃjñitam । yena sūkṣmamacintyaṃ tat paśyanti jñāna vakṣuṣaḥ ।।
tasmai bhagavate nityaṃ namaskāraṃ prakurmahe । mahādevāya rudrāya devadevāya liṅgine ।। namo vedarahasyāya nīlakaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ । vibhīṣaṇāya śāntāya sthāṇave hetave namaḥ ।।
brahmaṇe vāmadevāya trinetrāya mahīyase । śaṅkarāya maheśāya girīśāya śivāya ca ।। namaḥ kuruṣva satataṃ dhyāyasva manasā haram । saṃsārasāgarādasmādacirāduttariṣyasi ।।
evaṃ sa vāsudevena vyāhṛto munipuṅgavaḥ । jagāma manasā devamīśānaṃ viśvatomukham ।। praṇamya śirasā kṛṣṇamanujñāto mahāmuniḥ । jagāma cepsitaṃ deśaṃ devadevasya śūlinaḥ ।।
ya imaṃ śrāvayennityaṃ liṅgādhyāyamanuttamam । śṛṇuyād vā paṭhed vāpi sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। śrutvā sakṛdapi hyetat tapaścaraṇamuttamam । vāsudevasya viprendrāḥ pāpaṃ muñciti mānavaḥ ।।
japed vāharaharnityaṃ brahmaloke mahīyate । evamāha mahāyogī kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ ।। tato labdhavaraḥ kṛṣṇo jāmbavatyāṃ maheśvarāt । ajījananmahātmānaṃ sāmbamātmajamuttamam ।।
pradyumnasyāpyabhūt putro hyaniruddho mahābalaḥ । tāvubhau guṇasaṃpannau kṛṣṇasyaivāpare tanū ।। hatvā ca kaṃsaṃ narakamanyāṃśca śataśo asurān । vijitya līlayā śakraṃ jitvā bāṇaṃ mahāsuram ।।
sthāpayitvā jagat kṛtsnaṃ loke dharmāṃśca śāśvatān । cakre nārāyaṇo gantuṃ svasthānaṃ buddhimuttamām ।। etasminnantare viprā bhṛgvādyāḥ kṛṣṇamīśvaram । ājagmurdvārakāṃ draṣṭuṃ kṛtakāryaṃ sanātanam ।।
sa tānuvāca viśvātmā praṇipatyābhipūjya ca । āsaneṣūpaviṣṭān vai saha rāmeṇa dhīmatā ।। gamiṣye tat paraṃ sthānaṃ svakīyaṃ viṣṇusaṃjñitam । kṛtāni sarvakāryāṇi prasīdadhvaṃ munīśvarāḥ ।।
idaṃ kaliyugaṃ ghoraṃ saṃprāptamadhunāśubham । bhaviṣyanti janāḥ sarve hyasmin pāpānuvartinaḥ ।। pravartayadhvaṃ majjñānaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāvaham । yeneme kalijaiḥ pāpairmucyante hi dvijottamāḥ ।।
ye māṃ janāḥ saṃsmaranti kalau sakṛdapi prabhum । teṣāṃ naśyatu tat pāpaṃ bhaktānāṃ puruṣottame ।। yer'cayiṣyantimāṃ bhaktyā nityaṃ kaliyuge dvijāḥ । vidhānā vedadṛṣṭena te gamiṣyanti tat padam ।।
ye brāhmaṇā vaṃśajātā yuṣmākaṃ vai sahastraśaḥ । teṣāṃ nārāyaṇe bhaktirbhaviṣyati kalau yuge ।। parāt parataraṃ yānti nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ । na te tatra gamiṣyanti ye dviṣanti maheśvaram ।।
dhyānaṃ homaṃ tapastaptaṃ jñānaṃ yajñādiko vidhiḥ । teṣāṃ vinaśyati kṣipraṃ ye nindanti pinākinam ।। yo māṃ samāśrayennityamekāntaṃ bhāvamāśritaḥ । vinindya devamīśānaṃ sa yāti narakāyutam ।।
tasmāt sā parihartavyā nindā paśupatau dvijāḥ । karmaṇā manasā vācā tadbhakteṣvapi yatnataḥ ।। ye tu dakṣādhvare śaptā dadhīyena dvijottamāḥ । bhaviṣyanti kalau bhaktaiḥ parihāryāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
dviṣanto devamīśānaṃ yuṣmākaṃ vaṃśasaṃbhavāḥ । śaptāśca gautamenorvyāṃ na saṃbhāṣyā dvijottamaiḥ ।। ityevamuktāḥ kṛṣṇena sarva eva maharṣayaḥ । omityuktvā yayustūrṇaṃsvāni sthānāni sattamāḥ ।।
tato nārāyaṇaḥ kṛṣṇo līlayaiva jaganmayaḥ । saṃhṛtya svakulaṃ sarvaṃ yayau tat paramaṃ padam ।। ityeṣa vaḥ samāsena rājñāṃ vaṃśo anukīrtitaḥ । na śakyo vistarād vaktuṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotumicchatha ।।
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi vaṃśānāṃ kathanaṃ śubham । sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate ।। kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliśceti caturyugam । eṣāṃ svabhāvaṃ sūtādya kathayasva samāsataḥ ।।
gate nārāyaṇe kṛṣṇe svameva paramaṃ padam । pārthaḥ paramadharmātmā pāṇḍavaḥ śatrutāpanaḥ ।। kṛtvā cevottaravidhiṃ śokena mahatāvṛtaḥ । apaśyat pathi gacchantaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ munim ।।
śiṣyaiḥ praśiṣyairabhitaḥ saṃvṛtaṃ brahmavādinam । papāta daṇḍavad bhūmau tyaktvā śokaṃ tadār'junaḥ ।। uvāca paramaprītaḥ kasmād deśānmahāmune । idānīṃ gacchasi kṣipraṃ kaṃ vā deśaṃ prati prabho ।।
saṃdarśanād vai bhavataḥ śoko me vipulo gataḥ । idānīṃ mama yat kāryaṃ brūhi padmadalekṣaṇa ।। tamuvāca mahāyogī kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ svayam । upaviśya nadītire śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto muniḥ ।।
idaṃ kaliyugaṃ ghoraṃ saṃprāptaṃ pāṇḍunandana । tato gacchāmi devasya vārāṇasīṃ mahāpurīm ।। asmin kaliyuge ghore lokāḥ pāpānuvartinaḥ । bhaviṣyanti mahāpāpā varṇāśramavivarjitāḥ ।।
nānyat paśyāmi jantūnāṃmuktvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm । sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ prāyaścittaṃ kalau yuge ।। kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca sarveṣveteṣu vai narāḥ । bhaviṣyanti mahātmāno dhārmikāḥ satyavādinaḥ ।।
tvaṃ hi lokeṣu vikhyāto dhṛtimāñ janavatsalaḥ । pālayādya paraṃ dharmaṃ svakīyaṃ mucyase bhayāt ।। evamukto bhagavatā pārthaḥ parapurañjayaḥ । pṛṣṭavān praṇipatyāsau yugadharmān dvijottamāḥ ।।
tasmai provāca sakalaṃ muniḥ satyavatīsutaḥ । praṇamya devamīśānaṃ yugadharmān sanātanān ।। vakṣyāmi te samāsena yugadharmān nareśvara । na śakyate mayā pārtha vistareṇābhibhāṣitum ।।
ādyaṃ kṛtayugaṃ proktaṃ tatastretāyugaṃ budhaiḥ । tṛtīyaṃ dvāparaṃ pārtha caturthaṃ kalirucyate ।। dhyānaṃ paraṃ kṛtayuge tretāyāṃ jñānamucyate । dvāpare yajñamevāhurdānameva kalau yuge ।।
brahmā kṛtayuge devastretāyāṃ bhagavān raviḥ । dvāpare daivataṃ viṣṇuḥ kalau rudro maheśvaraḥ ।। brahmā viṣṇustathā sūryaḥ sarva eva kaliṣvapi । pūjyate bhagavān rudraścaturṣvapi pinākadhṛk ।।
ādye kṛtayuge dharmaścatuṣpādaḥ sanātanaḥ । tretāyuge tripādaḥ syād dvipādo dvāpare sthitaḥ । tripādahīnastiṣye tu sattāmātreṇa tiṣṭhati ।। kṛte tu mithunotpattirvṛttiḥ sākṣād rasollasā ।
prajāstṛptāḥ sadā sarvāḥ sadānandāśca bhoginaḥ ।। adhamottamatvaṃ nāstyāsāṃ nirviśeṣāḥ purañjaya । tulyamāyuḥ sukhaṃ rūpaṃ tāsāṃ tasmin kṛte yuge ।। viśokāḥ sattvabahulā ekāntabahulāstathā ।
dhyānaniṣṭhāstaponiṣṭhā mahādevaparāyaṇāḥ ।। tā vai niṣkāmacāriṇyo nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ । parvatodadhivāsinyo hyaniketaḥ parantapa ।। rasollāsā kālayogāt tretākhye naśyate tataḥ ।
tasyāṃ siddhau praṇaṣṭāyāmanyā siddhiravartata ।। apāṃ saukṣmye pratihate tadā meghātmanā tu vai । meghebhyaḥ stanayitnubhyaḥ pravṛttaṃ vṛṣṭisarjanam ।। sakṛdeva tayā vṛṣṭyā saṃyukte pṛthivītale ।
prādurāsaṃstadā tāsāṃ vṛkṣā vai gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ ।। sarvapratyupayogastu tāsāṃ tebhyaḥ prajāyate । vartayanti sma tebhyastāstretāyugamukhe prajāḥ ।। tataḥ kālena mahatā tāsāmeva viparyatāt ।
rāgalobhātmako bhāvastadā hyākasmiko abhavat ।। viparyayeṇa tāsāṃ tu tena tatkālabhāvinā । praṇaśyanti tataḥ sarve vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ ।। tatasteṣu pranaṣṭeṣu vibhrāntā maithunodbhavāḥ ।
abhidhyāyanti tāṃ siddhiṃ satyābhidhyāyinastadā ।। prādurbabhūvustāsāṃ tu vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ । vastrāṇi te prasūyante phalānyābharaṇāni ca ।। teṣveva jāyate tāsāṃ gandhavarṇarasānvitam ।
amākṣikaṃ mahāvīryaṃ puṭake puṭake madhu ।। tena tā vartayanti sma tretāyugamukhe prijāḥ । hṛṣṭapuṣṭāstayā siddhyā sarvā vai vigatajvarāḥ ।। tataḥ kālāntareṇaiva punarlobhāvṛtāstadā ।
vṛkṣāṃstān paryagṛhṇanta madhu cāmākṣikaṃ balāt ।। tāsāṃ tenāpacāreṇa punarlobhakṛtena vai । praṇaṣṭāmadhunā sārdhaṃ kalpavṛkṣāḥ kvacit kvacit ।। śītavarṣātapaistīvrai statastā duḥ khitā bhṛśam ।
dvandvaiḥ saṃpīḍyamānāstu cakrurāvaraṇāni ca ।। kṛtvā dvandvapratīghātān vārtopāyamacintayan । naṣṭeṣu madhunā sārdhaṃ kalpavṛkṣeṣu vai tadā ।। tataḥ prādurbabhau tāsāṃ siddhistretāyuge punaḥ ।
vārtāyāḥ sādhikā hyanyā vṛṣṭistāsāṃ nikāmataḥ ।। tāsāṃ vṛṣṭyūdakānīha yāni nimnairgatāni tu । avahan vṛṣṭisaṃtatyā strotaḥ sthānāni nimnagāḥ ।। ye punastadapāṃ stokā āpannāḥ pṛthivītale ।
apāṃ bhūṇeśca saṃyogādoṣadhyastāstadābhavan ।। aphālakṛṣṭāścānuptā grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa । ṛtupuṣpaphalaiścaiva vṛkṣagulmāśca jajñire ।। tataḥ prādurabhūt tāsāṃ rāgo lobhaśca sarvaśaḥ ।
avaśyaṃ bhāvinār'the na tretāyugavaśena vai ।। tatastāḥ paryagṛhṇanta nadīkṣetrāṇi parvatān । vṛkṣagulmauṣadhīścaiva prasahya tu yathābalam ।। viparyayeṇa tāsāṃ tā oṣadhyo viviśurmahīm ।
pitāmahaniyogena dudoha pṛthivīṃ pṛthuḥ ।। tatastā jagṛhuḥ sarvā anyonyaṃ krodhamūrchitāḥ । vasudāradhanādyāṃstu balāt kālabalena tu ।। maryādāyāḥ pratiṣṭhārthaṃ jñātvaitad bhagavānajaḥ ।
sasarja kṣatriyān brahmā brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya ca ।। varṇāśramavyavasthāṃ ca tretāyāṃ kṛtavān prabhuḥ । yajñapravartanaṃ caiva paśuhiṃsāvivarjitam ।। dvāpareṣvatha vidyante matibhedāḥ sadā nṛṇām ।
rāgo lobhastathā yuddhaṃ tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ ।। eko vedaścatuṣpādastretāsviha vidhīyate । vedavyāsaiścaturdhā tu vyasyate dvāparādiṣu ।। ṛṣiputraiḥ punarbhedād bhidyante dṛṣṭivibhramaiḥ ।
mantrabrāhmaṇavinyāsaiḥ svaravarṇaviparyayaiḥ ।। saṃhitā ṛgyajuḥ sāmnāṃ saṃhanyante śrutarṣibhiḥ । sāmānyād vaikṛtāccaivadṛṣṭibhedaiḥ kvacit kvacit ।। brāhmaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāṇi mantrapravacanāni ca ।
itihāsapurāṇāni dharmaśāstrāṇi suvrata ।। avṛṣṭirmaraṇaṃ caiva tathaiva vāyādhyupadravāḥ । vāṅmanaḥ kāyajairduḥ sairnirvedo jāyate nṛṇām ।। nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥ khamokṣavicāraṇā ।
vicāraṇācca vairāgyaṃ vairāgyād doṣadarśanam ।। doṣāṇāṃ darśanāccaiva dvāpare jñānasaṃbhavaḥ । eṣā rajastamoyuktā vṛttirvai dvāpare smṛtā ।। ādye kṛte tu dharmo asti sa tretāyāṃ pravartate ।
dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge ।। tiṣye māyāmasūyāṃ ca vadhaṃ caiva tapasvinām । sādhayanti narā nityaṃ tamasā vyākulīkṛtāḥ ।। kalau pramārako rogaḥ satataṃ kṣud bhayaṃ tathā ।
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ deśānāṃ ca viparyayaḥ ।। adhārmikā anācārā mahākopālpacetasaḥ । anṛtaṃ vadanti te lubdhāstiṣye jātāḥ suduḥ prajāḥ ।। duriṣṭairduradhītaiśca durācārairdurāgamaiḥ ।
viprāṇāṃ karmadoṣaiśca prajānāṃ jāyate bhayam ।। nādhīyate kalau vedān na yajanti dvijātayaḥ । yajantyanyāyato vedān paṭhante cālpabuddhayaḥ ।। śūdrāṇāṃ mantrayaunaiśca saṃbandho brāhmaṇaiḥ saha ।
bhaviṣyati kalau tasmiñ śayanāsanabhojanaiḥ ।। rājānaḥ sūdrabhūyiṣṭhā brāhmaṇān bādhayanti ca । bhrūṇahatyā vīrahatyā prajāyete nareśvara ।। snānaṃ homaṃ japaṃ dānaṃ devatānāṃ tathār'canam ।
anyāni caiva karmāṇi na kurvanti dvijātayaḥ ।। vinindanti mahādevaṃ brāhmaṇān puruṣottamam । āmnāyadharmaśāstrāṇi purāṇāni kalau yuge ।। kurvantyavedadṛṣṭāni karmāṇi vividhāni tu ।
svadharme abhirucirnaiva brāhmaṇānāṃ prijāyate ।। kuśīlacaryāḥ pāṣaṇḍairvṛthārūpaiḥ samāvṛtāḥ । bahuyācanako loko bhaviṣyati parasparam ।। aṭṭaśūlā janapadāḥ śivaśūlāścatuṣpathāḥ ।
pramadāḥ keśaśūlinyo bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।। śukladantājinākhyāśca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāyavāsasaḥ । śūdrā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti yugānte samupasthite ।। śasyacaurā bhaviṣyanti tathā cailābhimarṣiṇaḥ ।
caurāścaurasya hartāro harturhartā tathāparaḥ ।। duḥ khapracuratālpāyurdehotsādaḥ sarogatā । adharmābhiniveśitvāt tamovṛttaṃ kalau smṛtam ।। kāṣāyiṇo atha nirgranthāstathā kāpālikāśca ye ।
vedavikrayiṇaścānye tīrthavikrayiṇaḥ pare ।। āsanasthān dvijān dṛṣṭvā na calantyalpabuddhayaḥ । tāḍayanti dvijendrāṃśca śūdrā rājopajīvinaḥ ।। uccāsanasthāḥ śūdrāstu dvijamadhye parantapa ।
jñātvā na hiṃsate rājā kalau kālabalena tu ।। puṣpaiśca hasitaiścaiva tathānyairmaṅgalairdvijāḥ । śūdrānabhyarcayantyalpaśrutabhagyabalānvitāḥ ।। na prekṣante arcitāṃścāpi śūdrā dvijavarān nṛpa ।
sevāvasaramālokya dvāri tiṣṭhanti ca dvijāḥ ।। vāhanasthān samāvṛtya śūdrāñ śūdropajīvinaḥ । sevante brāhmaṇāstatra stuvanti stutibhiḥ kalau ।। adhyāpayanti vai vedāñ śūdrāñ śūdropajīvinaḥ ।
paṭhanti vaidikān mantrān nāstikyaṃ ghoramāśritāḥ ।। tapoyajñaphalānāṃ ca vikretāro dvijottamāḥ । yatayaśca bhaviṣyanti śataśo atha sahastraśaḥ ।। nāśayanti hyadhītāni nādhigacchanti cānagha ।
gāyanti laukikairgānairdaivatāni narādhipa ।। vāmapāśupatācārāstathā vai pāñcarātrikāḥ । bhaviṣyanti kalau tasmin brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāstathā ।। jñānakarmaṇyuparate loke niṣkriyatāṃ gate ।
kīṭamūṣakasarpāśca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān ।। kurvānti cāvatārāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ kuleṣu vai । dadhīcaśāpanirdagdhāḥ purā dakṣādhvare dvijāḥ ।। nindanti ca mahādevaṃ tamasāviṣṭacetasaḥ ।
vṛthā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti kalau tasmin yugāntike ।। ye cānye śāpanirdagdhā gautamasya mahātmanaḥ । sarve te ca bhaviṣyanti brāhmaṇādyāḥ svajātiṣu ।। vinindanti hṛṣīkeśaṃ brāhmaṇān brahmavādinaḥ ।
vedabāhyavratācārā durācārā vṛthāśramāḥ ।। mohayanti janān sarvān darśayitvā phalāni ca । tamasāviṣṭamanaso vaiḍālavṛttikādhamāḥ ।। kalau rudro mahādevo lokānāmīśvaraḥ paraḥ ।
na devatā bhavennṛṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca daivatam ।। kariṣyatyavatārāṇi śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ । śrautasmārtapratiṣṭhārthaṃ bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। upadekṣyati tajjñānaṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ brahmasaṃjñitam ।
sarvavedāntasāraṃ hi dharmān vedanidarśitān ।। ye taṃ viprā niṣevante yena kenopacārataḥ । vijityakalijān doṣān yānti te paramaṃ padam ।। anāyāsena sumahat puṇyamāpnoti mānavaḥ ।
anekadoṣaduṣṭasya kalereṣa mahān guṇaḥ ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena prāpya māheśvaraṃ yugam । viśeṣād brāhmaṇo rudramīśānaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajet ।। ye namanti virūpākṣamīśānaṃ kṛttivāsasam ।
prasannacetaso rudraṃ te yānti paramaṃ padam ।। yathā rudranamaskāraḥ sarvakarmaphalo dhruvam । anyadevanamaskārānna tatphalamavāpnuyāt ।। evaṃvidhe kaliyuge doṣāṇāmekaśodhanam ।
mahādevanamaskāro dhyānaṃ dānamiti śrutiḥ ।। tasmādanīśvarānanyān tyaktvā devaṃ maheśvaram । samāśrayed virūpākṣaṃ yadīcchet paramaṃ padam ।। nārcayantīha ye rudraṃ śivaṃ tridaśavanditam ।
teṣāṃ dānaṃ tapo yajño vṛthā jīvitameva ca ।। namo rudrāya mahate devadevāya śūline । tryambakāya trinetrāya yogināṃ gurave namaḥ ।। namo astu vāmadevāya mahādevāya vedhase ।
śaṃbhave sthāṇave nityaṃ śivāya parameṣṭhine । namaḥ śomāya rudrāya mahāgrāsāya hetave ।। prapadye ahaṃ virūpākṣaṃ śaraṇyaṃ brahmacāriṇam । mahādevaṃ mahāyogamīśānaṃ cāmbikāpatim ।।
yogināṃ yogadātāraṃ yogamāyāsamāvṛtam । yogināṃ kurumācāryaṃ yogigamyaṃ pinākinam ।। saṃsāratāraṇaṃ rudraṃ brahmāṇaṃ brahmaṇo adhipam । śāśvataṃ sarvagaṃ brahmaṇyaṃ brāhmaṇapriyam ।।
kapardinaṃ kālamūrtimamūrti parameśvaram । ekamūrti mahāmūrti vedavedyaṃ divaspatim ।। nīlakaṇṭhaṃ viśvamūrti vyāpinaṃ viśvaretasam । kālāgniṃ kāladahanaṃ kāmadaṃ kāmanāśanam ।।
namasye giriśaṃ devaṃ candrāvayavabhūṣaṇam । vilohitaṃ lelihānamāhityaṃ parameṣṭhinam । ugraṃ paśupatiṃ bhīmaṃ bhāskaraṃ tamasaḥ param ।। ityetallakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yugānāṃ vai samāsataḥ ।
atītānāgatānāṃ vai yāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ ।। manvantareṇa caikena sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi vai । vyākhyātāni na saṃdehaḥ kalpaḥ kalpena caiva hi ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣu vai ।
tulyābhimāninaḥ sarve nāmarūpairbhavantyuta ।। evamukto bhagavatā kirīṭī śvetavāhanaḥ । babhāra paramāṃ bhaktimīśāne avyabhicāriṇīm ।। namaścakāra tamṛṣiṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ prabhum ।
sarvajñaṃ sarvakartāraṃ skṣād viṣṇuṃ vyavasthitam ।। tamuvāca punarvyāsaḥ pāthaṃ parapurañjayam । karābhyāṃ suśubhābhyāṃ ca saṃspṛśya praṇataṃ muniḥ ।। dhanyo asyanugṛhīto asi tvādṛśo anyo na vidyate ।
trailokye śaṅkare nūnaṃ bhaktaḥ parapurañjaya ।। dṛṣṭavānasi taṃ devaṃ viśvākṣaṃ viśvatomukham । pratyakṣameva sarveśaṃ rudraṃ sarvajagadgurum ।। jñānaṃ tadaiśvaraṃ divyaṃ yathāvad viditaṃ tvayā ।
svayameva hṛṣīkeśaḥ prītyovāca sanātanaḥ ।। gaccha gaccha svakaṃ sthānaṃ na śokaṃ kartumarhasi । vrajasva parayā bhaktyā śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ śivam ।। evamuktvā sa bhagavānanugṛhyārjunaṃ prabhuḥ ।
jagāma śaṅkarapurīṃ samārādhayituṃ bhavam ।। pāṇḍaveyo api tad vākyāt saṃprāpya śaraṇaṃ śivam । saṃtyajya sarvakarmāṇi tadbhaktiparamo abhavat ।। nārjunena samaḥ śaṃbhorbhaktyā bhūto bhaviṣyati ।
muktvā satyavatīsūnuṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vā devakīsutam ।। tasmai bhagavate nityaṃ namaḥ satyāya dhīmate । pārāśaryāya munaye vyāsāyāmitatejase ।। kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ sākṣād viṣṇureva sanātanaḥ ।
ko hyanyastattvato rudraṃ vetti taṃ parameśvaram ।। namaḥ kurudhvaṃ tamṛṣiṃ kṛṣṇaṃ satyavatīsutam । pārāśaryaṃ mahātmānaṃ yoginaṃ viṣṇumavyayam ।। evamuktāstu munayaḥ sarva eva samīhitāḥ ।
preṇemustaṃ mahātmānaṃ vyāsaṃ satyavatīsutam ।। prāpya vārāṇasīṃ divyāṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ । kimakārṣonmahābuddhiḥ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।। prāpya vārāṇasī divyāmupaspṛśya mahāmuniḥ ।
pūjayāmāsa jāhnavyāṃ devaṃ viśveśvaraṃ śivam ।। tamāgataṃ puniṃ dṛṣṭvā tatra ye nivasanti vai । pūjayāñcakrire vyāsaṃ munayo munipuṅgavam ।। papracchuḥ praṇatāḥ sarve kathāḥ pāpavināśanīḥ ।
mahādevāśrayāḥ puṇyā mokṣadharmān sanātanān ।। sa cāpi kathayāmāsa sarvajño bhagavānṛṣiḥ । māhātmyaṃ devadevasya dharmān vedanidarśitān ।। teṣāṃ madhye munīndrāṇāṃ vyāsaśiṣyo mahāmuniḥ ।
pṛṣṭavān jaiminirvyāsaṃ gūḍhamarthaṃ sanātanam ।। bhagavan saṃśayaṃ tvekaṃ chettumarhasi tattvataḥ । na vidyate hyaviditaṃ bhavatā paramarṣiṇā ।। kecid dhyānaṃ praśaṃsanti dharmamevāpare janāḥ ।
anye sāṃkhyaṃ tathā yogaṃ tapastvanye maharṣayaḥ ।। brahmacaryamatho maunamanye prāharmaharṣayaḥ । ahiṃsāṃ satyamapyanye saṃnyāsamapare viduḥ ।। kecid dayāṃ praśaṃsanti dānamadhyayanaṃ tathā ।
tīrthayātrāṃ tathā kecidanye cendriyanigraham ।। kimeteṣāṃ bhavejjyāyaḥ prabrūhi munipuṅgava । yadi vā vidyate apyanyad guhyaṃ tadvaktumarhasi ।। śrutvā sa jaiminervākyaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ ।
prāha gambhīrayā vācā praṇamya vṛṣaketanam ।। sādhu sādhu mahābhāga yatpṛṣṭaṃ bhavatā mune । vakṣye guhyatamād guhyaṃ śruṇvantvanye maharṣayaḥ ।। īśvareṇa purā proktaṃ jñānametat sanātanam ।
gūḍhamaprājñavidviṣṭaṃ sevitaṃ sūkṣmadarśibhiḥ ।। nāśraddadhāne dātavyaṃ nābhakte parameṣṭhinaḥ । na vedavidviṣu śubhaṃ jñānanānāṃ jñānamuttamam ।। meruśṛṅge purā devamīśānaṃ tripuradviṣam ।
devāsanagatā devī mahādevamapṛcchata ।। devadeva mahādeva bhaktānāmārtināśana । kathaṃ tvāṃ puruṣo devamacirādeva paśyati ।। sāṃkhyayogastathā dhyānaṃ karmayogo atha vaidikaḥ ।
āyāsabahulā loke yāni cānyāni śaṅkara ।। yena vibrāntacittānāṃ yogināṃ karmiṇāmapi । dṛśyo hi bhagavān sūkṣmaḥ sarveṣāmatha dehinām ।। etad guhyatamaṃ jñānaṃ gūḍhaṃ brahmādisevitama ।
hitāya sarvabhaktānāṃ brūhi kāmāṅganāśana ।। avācyametad vijñānaṃ jñānamajñairbahiṣkṛtam । vakṣye tava yathā tattvaṃ yaduktaṃ paramarṣibhiḥ ।। paraṃ guhyatamaṃ kṣetraṃ mama vārāṇasī purī ।
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ saṃsārārṇavatāriṇī ।। tatra bhaktā mahādevi madīyaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ । nivasanti mahātmānaḥ paraṃ niyamamāsthitāḥ ।। uttamaṃ sarvatīrthānāṃ sthānānāmuttamaṃ ca tat ।
jñānānāmuttamaṃ jñānamavimuktaṃ paraṃ mama ।। sthānāntaraṃ pavitrāṇi tīrthānyāyatanāni ca । śmaśānasaṃsthitānyeva divyabhūmigatāni ca ।। bhūrloke naiva saṃlagnamantarikṣe mamālayam ।
ayuktāstanna paśyanti yuktāḥ paśyanti cetasā ।। śmasānametad vikhyātamavimuktamiti śrutam । kālo bhūtvā jagadidaṃ saṃharāmyatra sundari ।। devīdaṃ sarvaguhyānāṃ sthānaṃ priyatamaṃ mama ।
madbhaktāstatra gacchanti māmeva praviśanti te ।। dattaṃ japtaṃ hutaṃ ceṣṭaṃ tapastaptaṃ kṛtaṃ ca yat । dhyānamadhyayanaṃ jñānaṃ sarvaṃ tatrākṣayaṃ bhavet ।। janmāntarasahastreṣu yatpāpaṃ pūrvasaṃcitam ।
avimuktaṃ praviṣṭasya tatsarvaṃ vrajati kṣayam ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrā ye varṇasaṃkarāḥ । striyo mlecchāśca ye cānye saṃkīrṇāḥ pāpayonayaḥ ।। koṭāḥ pipīlikāścaiva ye cānye mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ।
kālena nidhanaṃ prāptā avimukte varānane ।। candrārdhamaulayastryakṣā mahāvṛṣabhavāhanāḥ । śive mama pure devi jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।। nāvimukte mṛtaḥ kaścinnarakaṃ yāti kilbiṣī ।
īśvarānugṛhītā hi sarve yānti parāṃ gatim ।। mokṣaṃ sudurlabhaṃ matvā saṃsāraṃ cātibhīṣaṇam । aśmanā caraṇau hatvā vārāṇasyāṃ vasennaraḥ ।। durlabhā tapasā cāpi pūtasya parameśvari ।
yatra tatra vipannasya gatiḥ saṃsāramokṣaṇī ।। prasādājjāyate hyetanmama śailendranandini । aprabuddhā na paśyanti mama māyāvimohitāḥ ।। avimuktaṃ na sevanti mūḍhā ye tamasāvṛtāḥ ।
viṇmūtraretasāṃ madhye te vasanti punaḥ punaḥ ।। hanyamāno api yo vidvān vased vighnaśatairapi । sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra gatvā na śocati ।। janmamṛtyujarāmuktaṃ paraṃ yāti śivālayam ।
apunarmaraṇānāṃ hi sā gatirmokṣakāṅkṣiṇām । yāṃ prāpya kṛtakṛtyaḥ syāditi manyanti paṇḍatāḥ ।। na dānairna tapobhiśca na yajñairnāpi vidyayā । prāpyate gatirutkṛṣṭā yāvimukte tu labhyate ।।
nānāvarṇā vivarṇāśca caṇḍālādyā jugupsitāḥ । kilbiṣaiḥ pūrṇadehā ye viśiṣṭaiḥ pātakaistathā । bheṣajaṃ paramaṃ teṣāmavimuktaṃ vidurbudhāḥ ।। avimuktaṃ paraṃ jñānamavimuktaṃ paraṃ padam ।
avimuktaṃ paraṃ tattvamavimuktaṃ paraṃ śivam ।। kṛtvā vai naiṣṭhikīṃ dīkṣāmavimukte vasanti ye । teṣāṃ tatparamaṃ jñānaṃ dadāmyante paraṃ padam ।। prāyāgaṃ naimiṣaṃ puṇyaṃ śrīśailo atha mahālayaḥ ।
kedāraṃ bhadrakarṇaṃ ca gayā puṣkarameva ca ।। kurukṣetraṃ rudrakoṭirnarmadāmrātakeśvaram । śāligrāmaṃ ca kubjāmraṃ kokāmukhamanuttamam । prabhāsaṃ vijayeśānaṃ gokarṇaṃ bhadrakarṇakam ।।
etāni puṇyasthānāni trailokye viśrutāni ha । na yāsyanti paraṃ mokṣaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ yathā mṛtāḥ ।। vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣeṇa gaṅgā tripathagāminī । praviṣṭā nāśayet pāpaṃ janmāntaraśataiḥ kṛtam ।।
anyatra sulabhā gaṅgā śrāddhaṃ dānaṃ tapo japaḥ । vratāni sarvamevaitad vārāṇasyāṃ sudurlabham ।। yajeta juhuyānnityaṃ dadātyarcayate amarān । vāyubhakṣaśca satataṃ vārāṇasyāṃ stito naraḥ ।।
yadi pāpo yadi śaṭho yadi vādhārmiko naraḥ । vārāṇasīṃ samāsādya punāti sakalaṃ naraḥ ।। vārāṇasyāṃ mahādevaṃ yer'cayanti stuvanti vai । sarvapāpavinirmuktāste vijñeyā gaṇeśvarāḥ ।।
anyatra yogajñānābhyāṃ saṃnyāsādathavānyataḥ । prāpyate tat paraṃ sthānaṃ sahastreṇaiva janmanā ।। ye bhaktā devadeveśe vārāṇasyāṃ vasanti vai । te vindanti paraṃ mokṣamekenaiva tu janmanā ।।
yatra yogastathā jñānaṃ muktirekena janmanā । avimuktaṃ samāsādya nānyad gacchet tapovanam ।। yato mayā na muktaṃ tadavimuktaṃ tataḥ smṛtam । tadeva guhyaṃ guhyānāmetad vijñāya mucyate ।।
jñānājñānābhiniṣṭhānāṃ paramānandamicchatām । yā gatirvihitā subhru sāvimukte mṛtasya tu ।। yāni caivāvimuktasya dehe tūktāni kṛtsnaśaḥ । purī vārāṇasī tebhyaḥ sthānebhyo hyadhikāśubhā ।।
yatra sākṣānmahādevo dehānte svayamīśvaraḥ । vyācaṣṭe tārakaṃ brahma tatraiva hyavimuktakam ।। yat tat parataraṃ tattvamavimuktamiti śrutam । ekena janmanā devi vārāṇasyāṃ tadāpnuyāt ।।
bhrūmadhye nābhimadhye ca hṛdaye caiva mūrdhani । yathāvimuktāditye vārāṇasyāṃ vyavasthitam ।। varaṇāyāstathā cāsyā madhye vārāṇasī purī । tatraiva saṃsthitaṃ tattvaṃ nityamevāvimuktakam ।।
vārāṇasyāḥ paraṃ sthānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati । yatra nārāyaṇo devo mahādevo diveśvaraḥ ।। tatra devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ । upāsate māṃ satataṃ devadevaṃ pitāmaham ।।
mahāpātakino ye ca ye tebhyaḥ pāpakṛttamāḥ । vārāṇasīṃ samāsādya te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।। tasmānmumukṣurniyato vased vai maraṇāntikam । vārāṇasyāṃ mahādevājjñānaṃ labdhvā vimucyate ।।
kintu vighnā bhaviṣyanti pāpopahatacetasaḥ । tato naiva caret pāpaṃ kāyena manasā girā ।। etad rahasyaṃ vedānāṃ purāṇānāṃ ca suvratāḥ । avimuktāśrayaṃ jñānaṃ na kaścid vetti tattvataḥ ।।
devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca śṛṇvatāṃ parameṣṭhinām । devyai devena kathitaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam ।। yathā nārāyaṇaḥ śreṣṭho devānāṃ puruṣottamaḥ । yatheśvarāṇāṃ giriśaḥ sthānānāṃ caitaduttamam ।।
yaiḥ samārādhito rudraḥ pūrvasminneva janmani । te vindanti paraṃ kṣetramavimuktaṃ śivālayam ।। kalikalmaṣasaṃbhūtā yeṣāmupahatā matiḥ । na teṣāṃ vedituṃ śakyaṃ sthānaṃ tat parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
ye smaranti sadā kālaṃ vindanti ca purīmimām । teṣāṃ vinaśyati kṣipramihāmutra ca pātakam ।। yāni ceha prakurvanti pātakāni kṛtālayāḥ । nāśayet tāni sarvāṇi devaḥ kālatanuḥ śivaḥ ।।
āgacchatāmidaṃ sthānaṃ sevituṃ mokṣakāṅkṣiṇām । mṛtānāṃ ca punarjanam na bhūyo bhavasāgare ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena vārāṇasyāṃ vasennaraḥ । yogī vāpyathavāyogī pāpī vā puṇyakṛttamaḥ ।।
na vedavacanāt pitrorna caiva guruvādataḥ । matirutkramaṇīyā syādavimuktagatiṃ prati ।। ityevamuktvā bhagavān vyāso vedavidāṃ varaḥ । sahaiva śiṣyapravarairvārāṇasyāṃ cacāra ha ।।
sa śiṣyaiḥ saṃvṛto dhīmān gururdvaipāyano muniḥ । jagāma vipulaṃ liṅgamoṅkāraṃ muktidāyakam ।। tatrābhyarcya mahādevaṃ śiṣyaiḥ saha mahāmuniḥ । provāca tasya māhātmyaṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।
idaṃ tad vimalaṃ liṅgamoṅkāraṃ nāma śobhanam । asya smaraṇamātreṇa mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।। etat parataraṃ jñānaṃ pañcayatanamuttamam । sevitaṃ sūribhirnityaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ vimokṣadam ।।
atra sākṣānmahādevaḥ pañcāyatanavigrahaḥ । ramate bhagavān rudro jantūnāmapavargadaḥ ।। yat tat pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ pañcārthamiti śabdyate । tadetad vimalaṃ liṅgamoṅkāre samavasthitam ।।
śāntyatītā tathā śāntirvidyā caiva parā kalā । pratiṣṭhā ca nivṛttiśca pañcārthaṃ liṅgamaiśvaram ।। pañcānāmapi devānāṃ brahmādīnāṃ sadāśrayam । oṅkārabodhakaṃ liṅgaṃ pañcāyatanamucyate ।।
saṃsmaredaiśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ pañcāyatanamavyayam । dehānte tatparaṃ jyotirānandaṃ viśate budhaḥ ।। atra devarṣayaḥ pūrvaṃ siddhā brahmarṣayastathā । upāsya devamīśānaṃ prāptavantaḥ paraṃ padam ।।
matsyodaryāstaṭe puṇyaṃ sthānaṃ guhyatamaṃ śubham । gocarmamātraṃ viprendrā oṅkāreśvaramuttamam ।। kṛttivāseśvaraṃ liṅgaḥ madhyameśvaramuttamam । viśveśvaraṃ tathoṅkāraṃ kapardeśvarameva ca ।।
etāni guhyaliṅgāni vārāṇasyāṃ dvijottamāḥ । na kaścidiha jānāti vinā śaṃbhoranugrahāt ।। evamuktvā yayau kṛṣṇaḥ pārāśaryo mahāmuniḥ । kṛttivāseśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ draṣṭuṃ devasya śūlinaḥ ।।
samabhyarcya tathā śiṣyairmāhātmyaṃ kṛttivāsasaḥ । kathayāmāsa śiṣyebhyo bhagavān brahmavittamaḥ ।। asmin sthāne purā daityo hastī bhūtvā bhavāntikam । brāhmaṇān hantumāyāto ye atra nityamupāsate ।।
teṣāṃ liṅgānmahādevaḥ prādurāsīt trilocanaḥ । rakṣaṇārthaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaktānāṃ bhaktavatsalaḥ ।। hatvā gajākṛtiṃ daityaṃ śūlenāvajñayā haraḥ । vasastasyākarot kṛttiṃ kṛttivāseśvarastataḥ ।।
atra siddhiṃ parāṃ prāptā munayo munipuṅgavāḥ । tenaiva ca śarīreṇa prāptāstat paramaṃ padam ।। vidyā vidyeśvarā rudrāḥ śivāye ca prakīrtitāḥ । kṛttivāseśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ nityamāvṛtya saṃsthitāḥ ।।
jñātvā kaliyugaṃ ghoramadharmabahulaṃ janāḥ । kṛttivāsaṃ na muñcanti kṛtārthāste na saṃśayaḥ ।। janmāntarasahastreṇa mokṣo anyatrāpyate na vā । ekena janmanā mokṣaḥ kṛttivāse tu labhyate ।।
ālayaḥ sarvasiddhānāmetat sthānaṃ vadanti hi । gopitaṃ devadevena mahādevena śaṃbhunā ।। yuge yuge hyatra dāntā brāhmaṇā vedapārāgāḥ । upāsate mahādevaṃ japanti śatarudriyam ।।
stuvanti satataṃ devaṃ tryambakaṃ kṛttivāsasam । dhyāyanti hṛdaye devaṃ sthāṇuṃ sarvāntaraṃ śivam ।। ye vārāṇasyāṃ nivasanti viprāḥ । ye kṛttivāsaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannāḥ ।।
sudurlabhaṃ viprakuleṣu janma । dhyāyanti citte yatayo maheśam ।। vārāṇasīmadhyagatā munindrāḥ । stuvanti rudraṃ praṇamanti śaṃbhum ।।
sthāṇuṃ prapadye giriśaṃ purāṇam । jāne mahādevamanekarūpam ।। samābhāṣya munīn dhīmān devadevasya śūlinaḥ । jagāma liṅgaṃ tad draṣṭuṃ kapardeśvaramavyayam ।।
snātvā tatra vidhānena tarpayitvā pitṝn dvijāḥ । piśācamocane tīrthe pūjayāmāsa śūlinam ।। tatrāścaryamapaśyaṃste munayo guruṇā saha । menire kṣetramāhātmyaṃ praṇemurgiriśaṃ haram ।।
kaścidabhyājagāmedaṃ śārdūlo ghorarūpadhṛk । mṛgīmekāṃ bhakṣayituṃ kapardeśvaramuttamam ।। tatra sā bhītahṛdayā kṛtvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam । dhāvamānā susaṃbhrāntā vyāghrasya vaśamāgatā ।।
tāṃ vidārya nakhaistīkṣṇaiḥ śārdūlaḥ sumahābalaḥ । jagāma cānyaṃ vijanaṃ deśaṃ dṛṣṭvā munīśvarān ।। mṛtamātrā ca sā bālā kapardeśāgrato mṛgī । adṛśyata mahājvālā vyomni sūryasamaprabhā ।।
trinetrā nīlakaṇṭhā ca śaśāṅkāṅkitamūrdhajā । vṛṣādhirūḍhā puruṣaistādṛśaireva saṃvṛtā ।। puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ vimuñcinti khecarāstasya mūrdhani । gaṇeśvaraḥ svayaṃ bhūtvā na dṛṣṭastatkṣaṇāt tataḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvaitadāścaryavaraṃ jaiminipramukhā dvijāḥ । kapardeśvaramāhātmyaṃ papracchurgurumacyutam ।। teṣāṃ provāca bhagavān devāgre copaviśya saḥ । kapardeśasya māhātmyaṃ praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam ।।
idaṃ devasya talliṅgaṃ kapardośvaramuttamam । smṛtvaivāśeṣapāpaughaṃ kṣipramasya vimuñcati ।। kāmakrodhādayo doṣā vārāṇasīnivāsinām । vighnāḥ sarve vinaśyanti kapardeśvarapūjanāt ।।
tasmāt sadaiva draṣṭavyaṃ kapardeśvaramuttamam । pūjitavyaṃ prayatnena stotavyaṃ vaidikaiḥ stavaiḥ ।। dhyāyatāmatra niyataṃ yogināṃ śāntacetasām । jāyate yogasaṃsiddhiḥ sā ṣaṇmāse na saṃśayaḥ ।।
brahmahatyādayaḥ pāpā vinaśyantyasya pūjanāt । piśācamocane kuṇḍe snātasyātra samīpataḥ ।। asmin kṣetre purā viprāstapasvī śaṃsitavrataḥ । śaṅkukarṇa iti khyātaḥ pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram ।
jajāpa rudramaniśaṃ praṇavaṃ brahmarūpiṇam ।। puṣpadhūpādibhiḥ stotrairnamaskāraiḥ pradakṣiṇaiḥ । uvāsa tatra yogātmā kṛtvā dīkṣāṃ tu naiṣṭhikīma ।। kadācidāgataṃ pretaṃ paśyati sma kṣudhānvitam ।
asthicarmapinaddhāṅgaṃ niḥ śvasantaṃ muhurmuhuḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā sa muniśreṣṭhaḥ kṛpayā parayā yutaḥ । provāca ko bhavān kasmād deśād deśamimaṃśritaḥ ।। tasmai piśācaḥ kṣudhayā pīḍyamāno abravīd vacaḥ ।
pūrvajanmanyahaṃ vipro dhanadhānyasamanvitaḥ । putrapautrādibhiryuktaḥ kuṭumbabharaṇotsukaḥ ।। na pūjitā mayā devā gāvo apyatithayastathā । na kadācit kṛtaṃ puṇyamalpaṃ vā svalpameva vā ।।
ekadā bhagavān devo govṛṣeśvaravāhanaḥ । viśveśvaro vārāṇasyāṃ dṛṣṭaḥ spṛṣṭe namaskṛtaḥ ।। tadācireṇa kālena pañcatvamahamāgataḥ । na dṛṣṭaṃ nanmayā ghoraṃ yamasya vadanaṃ mune ।।
īdṛśīṃ yonimāpannaḥ paiśācīṃ kṣudhayānvitaḥ । pipāsayādhunākrānto na jānāmi hitāhitam ।। yadi kañcit samuddhartumupāyaṃ paśyasi prabho । kuruṣva taṃ namastubhyaṃ tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।
ityuktaḥ śaṅkukarṇo atha piśācamidamabravīt । tvādṛśo na hi loke asmin vidyate puṇyakṛttamaḥ ।। yat tvayā bhagavān pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭo viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ । saṃspṛṣṭo vandito bhūyaḥ ko anyastvatsadṛśo bhuvi ।।
tena karmavipākena deśametaṃ samāgataḥ । snānaṃ kuruṣva śīghraṃ tvamasmin kuṇḍe samāhitaḥ । yenemāṃ kutsitāṃ yoniṃ kṣiprameva prahāsyasi ।। dayālunā devavaraṃ trinetram ।
cakre samādhāya mano avagāham ।। mamāra divyābharaṇopapannaḥ । śaśāṅkacihnāṅkitacārumauliḥ ।। samāvṛto yogibhairaprameyaiḥ ।
yathodaye bhānuraśeṣadevaḥ ।। nṛtyanti divyāpsaraso abhirāmāḥ । gandharvavidyādharakiṃnarādyāḥ ।। ravāpya bodhaṃ bhagavātprasādāt ।
trayīmayaṃ yatra vibhāti rudraḥ ।। muniḥ prahṛṣṭo manasā maheśam । praṇamya tuṣṭāva kapardinaṃ tam ।। goptāramekaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।
mādityamagniṃ kapilādhirūḍham ।। hiraṇmayaṃ yoginamādimantam । mahāmuniṃ brahmamayaṃ pavitram ।। sahastrabāhuṃ namasaḥ parastāt ।
hiraṇyagarbhādhipatiṃ trinetram ।। yenāvṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ śivena । praṇamya nityaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye ।। svayaṃprabhaṃ citpatimekarudram ।
namaskariṣye na yato anyadasti ।। labdhvā samādhiṃ paramārthabhūtāḥ । taṃ brahmapāraṃ bhavataḥ svarūpam ।। r na saṃdṛśe tiṣṭhati yatsvarūpam ।
svayaṃbhuvaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye ।। sabrahmavijñānamabhedamekam । sabrahmapāraṃ praṇato asmi nityam ।। vivartate yaṃ praṇamanti devāḥ ।
kālaṃ bṛhantaṃ bhavataḥ svarūpam ।। sthāṇuṃ prapadye giriśaṃ purārim । pinākinaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi ।। stutvaivaṃ śaṅkukarṇo asau bhagavantaṃ kapardinam ।
papāta daṇḍavad bhūmau proccaran praṇavaṃ param ।। tatkṣaṇāt paramaṃ liṅgaṃ prādurbhūtaṃ śivātmakam । jñānamānandamadvaitaṃ koṭikālāgnisannibham ।। śaṅkukarṇo atha muktātmā tadātmā sarvago amalaḥ ।
nililye vimale liṅge tadbhutamivābhavat ।। etad rahasyamākhyātaṃ māhātmyaṃ vaḥ kapardinaḥ । na kaścid vetti tamasā vidvānapyatra muhyati ।। ya imāṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśinīm ।
bhaktaḥ pāpaviśuddhātmā rudrasāmīpyamāpnuyāt ।। paṭhecca satataṃ śuddho brahmapāraṃ mahāstavam । prātarmadhyāhnasamaye sa yogaṃ prāpnuyāt param ।। ihaiva nityaṃ vatsyāmo devadevaṃ kapardinam ।
drakṣyāmaḥ satataṃ devaṃ pūjayāmo atha śūlinam ।। ityuktvā bhagavān vyāsaḥ śiṣyaiḥ saha mahāmuniḥ । uvāsa tatra yuktātmā pūjayan vai kapardinam ।। uṣitvā tatra bhagavān kapardeśāntike punaḥ ।
draṣṭuṃ yayau madhyameśaṃ bahuvarṣagaṇān prabhuḥ ।। tatra mandākinīṃ puṇyāmṛṣisaṅganiṣevitām । nadīṃ vimalapānīyāṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭo abhavanmuniḥ ।। sa tāmanvīkṣya munibhiḥ saha dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ ।
cakāra bhāvapūtātmā snānaṃ snānavidhānavit ।। saṃtarpya vidhivad devānṛṣīn pitṛgaṇāṃstathā । pūjayāmāsa lokādiṃ puṣpairnānāvidhairbhavam ।। praviśya śiṣyapravaraiḥ sārdhaṃ satyavatīsutaḥ ।
madhyameśvaramīśānamarcayāmāsa śūlinam ।। tataḥ pāśupatāḥ śāntā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ । draṣṭuṃ samāgatā rudraṃ madhyameśvaramīśvaram ।। oṅkārāsaktamanaso vedādhyayanatatparāḥ ।
jaṭilā muṇḍitāścāpi śuklayajñopavītinaḥ ।। kaupīnavasanāḥ kecidapare cāpyavāsasaḥ । brahmacaryaratāḥ śāntā vedāntajñānatatparāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā dvaipāyanaṃ viprāḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtaṃ munim ।
pūjayitvā yathānyāyamidaṃ vacanamabruvan ।। ko bhavān kuta āyātaḥ saha śiṣyairmahāmune । procuḥ pailādayaḥ śiṣyāstānṛṣīn brahmabhāvitān ।। ayaṃ satyavatīsūnuḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ ।
vyāsaḥ svayaṃ hṛṣīkeśo yena vedāḥ pṛthak kṛtāḥ ।। yasya devo mahādevaḥ sākṣādeva pinākadhṛk । aṃśāṃśenābhavat putro nāmnā śuka iti prabhuḥ ।। yaḥ sa sākṣānmahādevaṃ sarvabhāvena śaṅkaram ।
prapannaḥ parayā bhaktyā yasya tajjñānamaiśvaram ।। tataḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve hṛṣṭasarvatanūruhāḥ । nemuravyagramanasaḥ procuḥ satyavatīsutam ।। bhagavan bhavatā jñātaṃ vijñānaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
prisādād devadevasya yat tanmāheśvaraṃ param ।। tadvadāsmākamavyaktaṃ rahasyaṃ guhyamuttamam । kṣipraṃ paśyema taṃ devaṃ śrutvā bhagavato mukhāt ।। visarjayitvā tāñchiṣyān sumantupramukhāṃstataḥ ।
provāca tatparaṃ jñānaṃ yogibhyo yogavittamaḥ ।। tatkṣaṇādeva vimalaṃ saṃbhūtaṃ jyotiruttamam । līnāstatraiva te viprāḥ kṣaṇādantaradhīyata ।। tataḥ śiṣyān samāhūya bhagavān brahmavittamaḥ ।
provāca madhyameśasya māhātmyaṃ pailapūrvakān ।। asmin sthāne svayaṃ devo devyā saha maheśvaraḥ । ramate bhagavān nityaṃ rudraiśca parivāritaḥ ।। atra pūrvaṃ hṛṣīkeśo viśvātmā devakīsutaḥ ।
uvāsa vatsaraṃ kṛṣṇaḥ sadā pāśupatairvṛtaḥ ।। bhasmoddhūlitasarvāṅgo rudrādhyayanatatparaḥ । ārādhayan hariḥ śaṃbhuṃ kṛtvā pāśupataṃ vratam ।। tasya te bahavaḥ śiṣyā brahmacaryaparāyaṇāḥ ।
labdhvā tadvacanājjñānaṃ dṛṣṭavanto maheśvaram ।। tasya devo mahādevaḥ pratyakṣaṃ nīlalohitaḥ । dadau kṛṣṇāsya bhagavāna varado varamuttamam ।। yer'cayiṣyanti govindaṃ madbhaktā vidhipūrvakam ।
teṣāṃ tadaiśvaraṃ jñānamutpatsyati jaganmaya ।। namasyor'cayitavyaśca dhyātavyo matparairjanaiḥ । bhaviṣyasi na saṃdeho matprasādād dvijātibhiḥ ।। ye atra drakṣyanti deveśaṃ snātvā rudraṃ pinākinam ।
brahmahatyādikaṃ pāpaṃ teṣāmāśu vinaśyati ।। prāṇāṃstyajanti ye martyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api । te yānti tat paraṃ sthānaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। dhanyāstu khalu te viprā mandākinyāṃ kṛtodakāḥ ।
arcayanti mahādevaṃ madhyameśvaramīśvaram ।। snānaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ śrāddhaṃ piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ tviha । ekaikaśaḥ kṛtaṃ viprāḥ punātyāsaptamaṃ kulam ।। saṃnihatyāmupaspṛśya rāhugraste divākare ।
yat phalaṃ labhate martyastasmād daśaguṇaṃ tviha ।। evamuktvā mahāyogī madhyameśānti ke prabhuḥ । uvāsa suciraṃ kālaṃ pūjayan vai maheśvaram ।। tataḥ sarvāṇi guhyāni tīrthānyāyatanāni ca ।
jagāma bhagavān vyāso jaiminipramukhairvṛtaḥ ।। prayāgaṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ prayāgādadhikaṃ śubham । viśvarūpaṃ tathā tīrthaṃ tālatīrthamanuttamam ।। ākāśākhyaṃ mahātīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ caivārṣabhaṃ param ।
svarnolaṃ ca mahātīrthaṃ gaurītīrthamanuttamam ।। prājāpatyaṃ tathā tīrthaṃ svargadvāraṃ tathaiva ca । jambukeśvaramityuktaṃ dharmākhyaṃ tīrthamuttamam ।। gayātīrthaṃ mahātīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ caiva mahānadī ।
nārāyaṇaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ vāyutīrthamanuttamam ।। jñānatīrthaṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ vārāhaṃ tīrthamuttamam । yamatīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ tīrthaṃ saṃvartakaṃ śubham ।। agnitīrthaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ kalaśeśvaramuttamam ।
nāgatīrthaṃ somatīrthaṃ sūryatīrthaṃ tathaiva ca ।। parvatākhyaṃ mahāguhyaṃ maṇikarṇamanuttamam । ghaṭotkacaṃ tīrthavaraṃ śrītīrthaṃ ca pitāmaham ।। gaṅgātīrthaṃ tu deveśaṃ yayātestīrthamuttamam ।
kāpilaṃ caiva someśaṃ brahmatīrthamanuttamam ।। atra liṅgaṃ purānīya brahmā snātuṃ yadā gataḥ । tadānīṃ sthāpayāmāsa viṣṇustalliṅgamaiśvaram ।। tataḥ snātvā samāgatya brahmā provāca taṃ harim ।
mayānītamidaṃ liṅgaṃ kasmāt sthāpitavānasi ।। tamāha viṣṇustvatto api rudre bhaktirdṛḍhā mama । tasmāt pratiṣṭhitaṃ liṅgaṃnāmnā tava bhaviṣyati ।। bhūteśvaraṃ tathā tīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ dharmasamudbhavam ।
gandharvatīrthaṃ paramaṃ vāhneyaṃ tīrthamuttamam ।। daurvāsikaṃ vyomatīrthaṃ candratīrthaṃ dvijottamāḥ । citrāṅgadeśvaraṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyaṃ vidyādhareśvaram ।। kedāratīrthamugrākhyaṃ kālañjaramanuttamam ।
sārasvataṃ prabhāsaṃ ca bhadrakarṇaṃ hradaṃ śubham ।। laukikākhyaṃ mahātīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ caiva vṛṣadhvajam । hiraṇyagarbhaṃ goprekṣyaṃ tīrthaṃ caiva vṛṣadhvajam ।। upaśāntaṃ śivaṃ caiva vyāghreśvaramanuttamam ।
trilocanaṃ mahātīrthaṃ lolārkaṃ cottarāhvayam ।। kapālamocanaṃ tīrthaṃ brahmahatyāvināśanam । śukreśvaraṃ mahāpuṇyamānandapuramuttamam ।। evamādīni tīrthāni prādhānyāt kathitāni tu ।
na śakyaṃ vistarād vaktuṃ tīrthasaṃkhyā dvijāttamāḥ ।। teṣu sarveṣu tīrtheṣu snātvābhyarcya pinākinam । upoṣya tatra tatrāsau pārāśaryo mahāmuniḥ ।। tarpayitvā pitṝn devān kṛtvā piṇḍapridānakam ।
jagāma punarevāpi yatra viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ ।। snātvābhyarcya paraṃ liṅgaṃ śiṣyaiḥ saha mahāmuniḥ । uvāca śiṣyān dharmātmā svān deśān gantumarhathā ।। te praṇamya mahātmānaṃ jagmuḥ pailādayo dvijāḥ ।
vāsaṃ ca tatra niyato vārāṇasyāṃ cakāra saḥ ।। śānto dāntastriṣavaṇaṃsnātvābhyarcya pinākinam । bhaikṣāhāro viśuddhātmā brahmacaryaparāyaṇaḥ ।। kadācid vasatā tatra vyāsenāmitatejasā ।
bhramamāṇena bhikṣā tu naiva labdhā dvijottamāḥ ।। tataḥ krodhāvṛtatanurnarāṇāmiha vāsinām । vighnaṃ sṛjāmi sarveṣāṃ yena siddhirvihīyate ।। tatkṣaṇe sā mahādevī śaṅkarārdhaśarīriṇī ।
prādurāsīt svayaṃ prītyā veṣaṃ kṛtvā tu mānuṣam ।। bho bho vyāsa mahābuddhe śaptavyā bhavatā na hi । gṛhāṇa bhikṣāṃ mattastvamuktvaivaṃ pradadau śivā ।। uvāca ca mahādevī krodhanastvaṃ bhavān yataḥ ।
iha kṣetre na vastavyaṃ kṛtaghno asi tvayā sadā ।। evamuktaḥ sa bhagavān dhyānājjñātvā parāṃ śivām । uvāca praṇato bhūtvā stutvā ca pravaraiḥ stavaiḥ ।। caturdaśyāmathāṣṭamyāṃ praveśaṃ dehi śāṅkari ।
evamastvityanujñāya devī cāntaradhīyata ।। evaṃ sa bhagavān vyāso mahāyogī purātanaḥ । jñātvā kṣetraguṇān sarvān sthitastasyātha pārśvataḥ ।। evaṃ vyāsaṃ sthitaṃ jñātvā kṣetraṃ sevanti paṇḍitāḥ ।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena vārāṇasyāṃ vasennaraḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhedavimuktasya māhātmyaṃ śṛṇuyādapi । śrāvayed vā dvijān śāntān so apiyātiparāṅgatim ।। śrāddhe vā daivike kārye rātrāvahani vā dvijāḥ ।
nadīnāṃ caiva tīreṣu devatāyataneṣu ca ।। snātvā samāhitamanā dambhamātsaryavarjitaḥ । japedīśaṃ namaskṛtya sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। māhātmyamavimuktasya yathāvat tadudīritam ।
idānīṃ tu prayāgasya māhātmyaṃ brūhi suvrata ।। yāni tīrthāni tatraiva viśrutāni mahānti vai । idānīṃ kathayāsmākaṃ sūta sarvārthavid bhavān ।। śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve vistareṇa bravīmi vaḥ ।
prayāgasya ca māhātmyaṃ yatra devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। mārkaṇḍeyena kathitaṃ kaunteyāya mahātmane । yathā yudhiṣṭhirāyaitat tadvakṣye bhavatāmaham ।। nihatya kauravāna sarvān bhrātṛbhiḥ saha pārthivaḥ ।
śokena mahātāviṣṭā mumoha sa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। acireṇātha kālena mārkaṇḍeyo mahātapāḥ । saṃprāpto hāstinapuraṃ rājadvāre sa tiṣṭhati ।। dvārapālo api taṃ dṛṣṭvā rājñaḥ kathitavān drutam ।
mārkaṇḍeyo draṣṭumicchaṃstvāmāste dvāryasau muniḥ ।। tvarito dharmaputrastu dvārametyāha tatparam । svāgataṃ te mahāprājña svāgataṃ te mahāmune ।। adya me saphalaṃ janma adya me tāritaṃ kulam ।
adya me pitarastuṣṭāstvayi tuṣṭe mahāmune ।। siṃhāsanamupasthāpya pādaśaucārcanādibhiḥ । yudhiṣṭhiro mahātmeti pūjayāmāsa taṃ munim ।। mārkaṇḍeyastatastuṣṭaḥ provāca sa yudhiṣṭhiram ।
kimarthaṃ muhyase vidvan sarvaṃ jñātvāhamāgataḥ ।। tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā praṇamyāha mahāmunim । kathaya tvaṃ samāsena yena mucyeta kilbiṣaiḥ ।। nihatā vahavo yuddhe puṃso niraparādhinaḥ ।
asmābhiḥ kauravaiḥ sārdhaṃ prasaṅgānmunipuṅgava ।। yena hiṃsāsamudbhūtājjanmāntarakṛtādapi । mucyate pātakādasmāt tad bhavān vaktumarhati ।। śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yanmāṃ pṛcchasi bhārat ।
prayāgagamanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ narāṇāṃ pāpanāśanam ।। tatra devo mahādevo rudro viśvāmareśvaraḥ । samāste bhagavān brahmā svayaṃbhūrapi daivadaiḥ ।। bhagavañcchrotumicchāmi prayāgagamane phalam ।
mṛtānāṃ kā gatistatra snātānāmapi kiṃ phalam ।। ye vasanti prayāge tu brūhi teṣāṃ tu kiṃ phalam । bhavatā viditaṃ hyetat tanme brūhi namo astu te ।। kathayiṣyāmi te vatsa yā ceṣṭā yacca tatphalam ।
purā maharṣibhiḥ samyak kathyamānaṃ mayā śrutam ।। etat prajāpatikṣetraṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam । atra snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste apunarbhavāḥ ।। tatra brahmādayo devā rakṣāṃ kurvanti saṃgatāḥ ।
bahūnyanyāni tīrthāni sarvapāpāpahāni tu ।। kathituṃ neha śaknomi bahuvarṣaśatairapi । saṃkṣepeṇa pravakṣyāmi prayāgasyeha kīrtanam ।। ṣaṣṭirdhanuḥ sahastrāṇi yāni rakṣanti jāhnavīm ।
yamunāṃ rakṣati sadā savitā saptavāhanaḥ ।। prayāge tu viśeṣeṇa svayaṃ vasati vāsavaḥ । maṇḍalaṃ rakṣati hariḥ sarvadevaiśca sammitam ।। nyagrodhaṃ rakṣate nityaṃ śūlapāṇirmaheśvaraḥ ।
sthānaṃ rakṣanti vai devāḥ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham ।। svakarmaṇāvṛto loko naiva gacchati tatpadam । svalpaṃ svalpataraṃ pāpaṃ yadā tasya narādhipa । prayāgaṃ smaramāṇasya sarvamāyāti saṃkṣayam ।।
darśanāt tasya tīrthasya nāma saṃkīrtanādapi । muttikālambhanād vāpi naraḥ pāpāt pramucyate ।। pañca kuṇḍāni rājendra yeṣāṃ madhye tu jāhnavī । prayāgaṃ viśataḥ puṃsaḥ pāpaṃ naśyati tatkṣaṇāt ।।
yojanānāṃ sahastreṣu gaṅgāṃ yaḥ smarate naraḥ । api duṣkṛtakarmāsau labhate paramāṃ gatim ।। kīrtanānmucyate pāpād dṛṣṭvā bhadrāṇi paśyati । tathopaspṛśya rājendra svargaloke mahīyate ।।
vyādhito yadi vā dīnaḥ krūddho vāpi bhavennaraḥ । gaṅgāyamunamāsādya tyajet prāṇān prayatnataḥ ।। dīptakāñcanavarṇābhairvimānairbhānuvarṇibhiḥ । īpsitāṃllabhate kāmān vadanti munipuṅgavāḥ ।।
sarvaratnamayairdivyairnānādhvajasamākulaiḥ । varāṅganāsamākīrṇairmodate śubhalakṣaṇaḥ ।। gītavāditranirghoṣaiḥ prasuptaḥ pratibudhyate । yāvanna smarate janma tāpat svarge mahīyate ।।
tasmāt svargāt paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣīṇakarmā narottama । hiraṇyaratnasaṃpūrṇe samṛddhe jāyate kule ।। tadeva smarate tīrthaṃ smaraṇāt tatra gacchati । deśastho yadi vāraṇye videśe yadi vā gṛhe ।।
prayāgaṃ smaramāṇastu yastu prāṇān parityajet । brahmalokamavāpnoti vadanti munipuṅgavāḥ ।। sarvakāmaphalā vṛkṣā mahī yatra hiraṇmayī । ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhāstatra loke sa gacchati ।।
strīsahastrākule ramye mandākinyāstaṭe śubhe । modate munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ svakṛteneha karmaṇā ।। siddhacāraṇagandharvaiḥ pūjyate divi daivataiḥ । tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo jambudvīpapatirbhavet ।।
tataḥ śubhāni karmāṇi cintayānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ । guṇavān vittasaṃpanno bhavatīha na saṃśayaḥ । karmaṇā manasā vācā satyadharmapratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। gaṅgāyamunayormadhye yastu grāmaṃ pratīcchati ।
suvarṇamatha muktāṃ vā tathaivānyān pratigrahān ।। svakārye pitṛkārye vā devatābhyarcane api vā । niṣphalaṃ tasya tat tīrthaṃ yāvat tatphalamaśnute ।। atastīrthe na gṛhṇīyāt puṇyeṣvāyataneṣu ca ।
nimitteṣu ca sarveṣu apramatto dvijo bhavet ।। kapilāṃ pāṭalāvarṇāṃ yastu dhenuṃ prayacchati । svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ cailakaṇṭhāṃ payasvinīm ।। yāvad romāṇi tasyā vai santi gātreṣu sattama ।
tāvad varṣasahastrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate ।। kathayiṣyāmi te vatsa tīrthayātrāvidhikramam । ārṣeṇa tu vidhānena yathā dṛṣṭaṃ yathā śrutam ।। prayāgatīrthayātrārtho yaḥ prayāti naraḥ kvacit ।
balīvardaṃ samārūḍhaḥ śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam ।। narake vasate ghore samāḥ kalpaśatāyutam । tato nivartate ghoro gavāṃ krodho hi dāruṇaḥ । salilaṃ ca na gṛhṇanti pitarastasya dehinaḥ ।।
yastu putrāṃstathā bālān snāpayet pāyayet tathā । yathātmanā tathā sarvān dānaṃ vipreṣu dāpayet ।। aiśvaryāllobhamohād vā gacched yānena yo naraḥ । niṣphalaṃ tasya tat tīrthaṃ tasamādyānaṃ vivarjayet ।।
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye yastu kanyāṃ prayacchati । ārṣeṇa tu vivāhena yathā vibhavavistaram ।। na sa paśyati taṃ ghoraṃ narakaṃ tena karmaṇā । uttarān sa kurūn gatvā modate kālamakṣayam ।।
vaṭamūlaṃ samāśritya yastu prāṇān parityajet । sarvalokānatikramya rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। tatra brahmādayo devā diśaśca sadigīśvarāḥ । lokapālāśca siddhāśca pitaro lokasaṃmatāḥ ।।
sanatkumārapramukhāstathā brahmarṣayo apare । nāgāḥ supārṇāḥ siddhāśca tathā nityaṃ samāsate । hariśca bhagavānāste prajāpatipuraskṛtaḥ ।। gaṅgāyamunayormadhye pṛthivyā jaghanaṃ smṛtam ।
prayāgaṃ rājaśārdūla triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।। tatrābhiṣekaṃ yaḥ kuryāt saṃgame saṃśitavrataḥ । tulyaṃ phalavāpnoti rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ ।। na mātṛvacanāt tāta na lokavacanādapi ।
matirutkramaṇīyā te prayāgagāmanaṃ prati ।। daśa tīrtha sahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭyastathāpare । teṣāṃ sānnidhyamatraiva tīrthānāṃ kurunandana ।। yā gatiryogayuktasya sattvasthasya manīṣiṇaḥ ।
sā gatistyajataḥ prāṇān gaṅgāyamunasaṃgame ।। na te jīvanti loke asmin yatra tatra yudhiṣṭhira । ye prayāgaṃ na saṃprāptāstriṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।। evaṃ dṛṣṭvā tu tat tīrthaṃ prayāgaṃ paramaṃ padam ।
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ śaśāṅka iva rāhuṇā ।। kambalāśvatarau nāgau yamunādakṣiṇe taṭe । tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।। tatra gatvā naraḥ sthānaṃ mahādevasya dhīmataḥ ।
ātmānaṃ tārayet pūrvaṃ daśātītān daśāparān ।। kṛtvābhiṣekaṃ tu naraḥ so aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet । svargalokamavāpnoti yāvadāhūtasaṃplavam ।। pūrvapārśve tu gaṅgāyāstrailokyakhyātimān nṛpa ।
avacaḥ sarvasāmudraḥ pratiṣṭhānaṃ ca viśrutam ।। brahmacārī jitakrodhastrirātraṃ yadi tiṣṭhati । sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā so aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। uttareṇa pratiṣṭhānaṃ bhāgīrathyāstu savyataḥ ।
haṃsaprapatanaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam ।। aśvamedhaphalaṃ tatra smṛtamātrāt tu jāyate । yāvaccandraśca sūryaśca tāvat svarge mahīyate ।। urvaśīpuline ramye vipule haṃsapāṇḍure ।
parityajatiyaḥ prāṇān śṛṇu tasyāpi yat phalam ।। ṣaṣṭivarṣasahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭivarṣaśatāni ca । āste sa pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ svargaloke narādhipa ।। athaṃ saṃdhyāvaṭe ramye brahmacārī jitendriyaḥ ।
naraḥ śucirupāsīta brahmalokamavāpnuyāt ।। koṭitīrthaṃ samāśritya yastu prāṇān parityajet । koṭivarṣasahastrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।। yatra gaṅgā mahābhāgā bahutīrthatapovanā ।
siddhakṣetraṃ hi tajjñeyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। kṣitau tārayate martyān nāgāṃstārayate apyadhaḥ । divi tārayate devāṃstena tripathagā smṛtā ।। yāvadasthīni gaṅgāyāṃ tiṣṭhanti puruṣasya tu ।
tāvad varṣasahastrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।। tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ nadīnāṃ paramā nadī । mokṣadā sarvabhūtānāṃ mahāpātakināmapi ।। sarvatra sulabhā gaṅgā triṣu sthāneṣu durlabhā ।
gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṃgame ।। sarveṣāme bhūtānāṃ pāpopahatacetasām । gatimanveṣamāṇānāṃ nāsti gaṅgāsamā gatiḥ ।। pavitrāṇāṃ pavitraṃ ca maṅgalānāṃ ca maṅgalam ।
māheśvarāt paribhraṣṭā sarvapāpaharā śubhā ।। kṛte yuge tu tīrthāni tretāyāṃ puṣkaraṃ param । dvāpare tu kurukṣetraṃ kalau gaṅgāṃ viśiṣyate ।। gaṅgāmeva niṣeveta prayāge tu viśeṣataḥ ।
nānyat kaliyugodbhūtaṃ malaṃ hantuṃ suduṣkṛtam ।। akāmo vā sakāmo vā gaṅgāyāṃ yo vipadyate । sa mṛto jāyate svarge narakaṃ ca na paśyati ।। ṣaṣṭistīrthasahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭistīrthaśatāni ca ।
māghamāse gamiṣyanti gaṅgāyamunasaṃgamam ।। gavāṃ śatasahastrasya samyag dattasya yat phalam । prayāge māghamāse tu tryahaṃ snātasya tat phalam ।। gaṅgāyamunayormadhye kārṣāgniṃ yastu sādhayet ।
ahīnāṅgo apyarogaśca pañcendriyasamanvitaḥ ।। yāvanti romakūpāṇi tasya gātreṣu mānada । tāvad varṣasahastrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।। tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo jambūdvīpapatirbhavet ।
sa bhuktvā vipulān bhogāṃstat tīrthaṃ bhajate punaḥ ।। jalapraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryāt saṃgame lokaviśrute । rāhugrasto yathā somo vimuktaḥ sarvapātakaiḥ ।। somalokamavāpnoti somena saha modate ।
ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣaśatāni ca ।। svargataḥ śakraloke asau munigandharvasevitaḥ । tato bhraṣṭastu rājendra samṛddhe jāyate kule ।। adhaḥ śirāstvayodhārāmurdhvapādaḥ pibennaraḥ ।
