śataṃ varṣasahastrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।। tasmād bhraṣṭastu rājendra agnihotrī bhavennaraḥ । bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogāṃstat tīrthaṃ bhajate punaḥ ।। yaḥ svadehaṃ vikarted vā śakunibhyaḥ prayacchati ।
vihagairupabhuktasya śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam ।। śataṃ varṣasahastrāṇi somaloke mahīyate । tatastasmāt paribhraṣṭo rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ।। guṇavān rūpasaṃpanno vidvān supriyavākyavān ।
bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogāṃstatatīrthaṃ bhajate punaḥ ।। uttare yamunātīre prayāgasya tu dakṣiṇe । ṛṇapramocanaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ tu paramaṃ smṛtam ।। ekarātroṣitaḥ snātvā ṛṇaistatra pramucyate ।
sūryalokamavāpnoti anṛṇaśca sadā bhavet ।। tapanasya sutā devī triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā । samāgatā mahābhāgā yamunā yatra nimnagā ।। yenaiva niḥ sṛtā gaṅgā tenaiva yamunā gatā ।
yojanānāṃ sahastreṣu kīrtanāt pāpanāśanī ।। tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca yamunāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira । sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ punātyāsaptamaṃ kulam । prāṇāṃstyajati yastatra sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।
agnitīrthamiti khyātaṃ yamunādakṣiṇa taṭe । paścime dharmarājasya tīrthaṃ tvanarakaṃ smṛtam । tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste apunarbhavāḥ ।। kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ snātvā saṃtarpayecchuciḥ ।
dharmarājaṃ mahāpāpairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। daśa tīrthasahastrāṇi triṃśatkoṭyastathāparāḥ । prayāge saṃsthitāni syurevamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।। tistraḥ koṭyor'dhakoṭī ca tīrthānāṃ vāyurabravīt ।
divi bhūmyantarikṣe ca tatsarvaṃ jāhnavī smṛtā ।। yatra gaṅgā mahābhāgā sa deśastat tapovanam । siddhikṣetraṃ tu tajjñeyaṃ gaṅgātīrasamāśritam ।। yatra devo mahādevo devyā saha maheśvaraḥ ।
āste vaṭeśvaro nityaṃ tat tīrthaṃ tat tapovanam ।। idaṃ satyaṃ dvijātīnāṃ sādhūnāmātmajasya ca । suhṛdāṃ ca japet karṇe śiṣyasyānugatasya tu ।। idaṃ dhanyamidaṃ svargyamidaṃ medhyamidaṃ sukham ।
idaṃ puṇyamidaṃ ramyaṃ pāvanaṃ dharmyamuttamam ।। maharṣoṇāmidaṃ guhyaṃ sarvapāpapramocanam । atrādhītya dvijo adhyāyaṃ nirmalatvamavāpnuyāt ।। yaścedaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ tīrthaṃ puṇyaṃ sadā śuciḥ ।
jātismaritvaṃ labhate nākapṛṣṭhe ca modate ।। prāpyante tānitīrthāni sadbhiḥ śiṣṭānudarśibhiḥ । snāhi tīrtheṣu kauravya na ca vakramatirbhava ।। evamuktvā sa bhagavān mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmuniḥ ।
tīrtāni kathayāmāsa pṛthivyāṃ yāni kānicit ।। bhūsamudrādisaṃsthānaṃ pramāṇaṃ jyotiṣāṃ sthitam । pṛṣṭaḥ provāca sakalamuktvātha prayayo muniḥ ।। ya idaṃ kalyamutthāya paṭhate atha śṛṇoti vā ।
mucyate sarvapāpebhyo rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। evamuktāstu munayo naimiṣīyā mahāmatim । papracchuruttaraṃ sūtaṃ pṛthivyādivinirṇayam ।। kathito bhavatā sūta sargaḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ śubhaḥ ।
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmastrilokasyāsya maṇḍalam ।। yāvantaḥ sāgarā dvīpāstathā varṣāṇi parvatāḥ । vanāni saritaḥ sūryagrahāṇāṃ sthitireva ca ।। yadādhāramidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ yeṣāṃ pṛthvī purā tviyam ।
nṛpāṇāṃ tatsamāsena sūta vaktumihārhasi ।। vakṣye devādidevāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave । namaskṛtvāprameyāya yaduktaṃ tena dhīmatā ।। svāyaṃbhuvasya tu manoḥ prāgukto yaḥ priyavrataḥ ।
putrastasyābhavan putrāḥ prajāpatisamā daśa ।। agnīdhraścāgnibāhuśca vapuṣmān dyutimāṃstathā । medhā medhātithirhavyaḥ savanaḥ putra eva ca ।। jyotiṣmān daśamasteṣāṃ mahābalaparākramaḥ ।
dhārmiko dānanirataḥ sarvabhūtānukampakaḥ ।। medhāgnibāhuputrāstu trayo yogaparāyaṇāḥ । jātismarā mahābhāgā na rājye dadhire matim ।। priyavrato abhyaṣiñcad vai saptadvīpeṣu sapta tān ।
jambudvīpeśvaraṃ putramagnīdhramakaronnṛpaḥ ।। plakṣdvīpeśvaraścaiva tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ । śālmaleśaṃ vapuṣmantaṃ narendramabhiṣiktavān ।। jyotiṣmantaṃ kuśadvīpe rājānaṃ kṛtavān prabhuḥ ।
dyutimantaṃ ca rājānaṃ krauñcadvīpe samādiśat ।। śākadvīpeśvaraṃ cāpi havyaṃ cakre priyavrataḥ । puṣkarādhipatiṃ cakre savanaṃ ca prajāpatiḥ ।। puṣkare savanasyāpi mahāvītaḥ suto abhavat ।
dhātikiścaiva dvāvetau putrau putravatāṃ varau ।। mahāvītaṃ smṛtaṃ varṣaṃ tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ । nāmnā tu dhātakeścāpi dhātakīkhaṇḍamucyate ।। śākadvīpeśvarasyātha havyasyāpyabhavan sutāḥ ।
jaladaśca kumāraśca sukumāro maṇīcakaḥ । kusumottaro atha modākiḥ saptamaḥ syānmahādrumaḥ ।। jaladaṃ jaladasyātha varṣaṃ prathamamucyate । kumārasya tu kaumāraṃ tṛtīyaṃ sukumārakam ।।
maṇīcakaṃ caturthaṃ tu pañcamaṃ kusumottaram । modākaṃ ṣaṣṭhamityuktaṃ saptamaṃ tu mahādrumam ।। krauñcadvīpeśvarasyāpi sutā dyutimato abhavan । kuśalaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ dvitīyastu manoharaḥ ।।
uṣṇastṛtīyaḥ saṃproktaścaturthaḥ pravaraḥ smṛtaḥ । andhakāro muniścaiva dundubhiścaiva saptamaḥ । teṣāṃ svanāmabhirdeśāḥ krauñcadvīpāśrayāḥ śubhāḥ ।। jyotiṣmataḥ kuśadvīpe saptaivāsan mahaujasaḥ ।
udbhedo veṇumāṃścaivāśvaratho lambano dhṛtiḥ । ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākāraścāpi saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। svanāmacihnitān yatra tathā varṣāṇi suvratāḥ । jñeyāni sapta tānyeṣu dvīpeṣvevaṃ na yo mataḥ ।।
śālmaladvīpanāthasya sutāścāsan vapuṣmataḥ । śvetaśca haritaścaiva jīmūto rohitastathā । vaidyutau mānasaścaiva saptamaḥ suprabho mataḥ ।। plakṣadvīpeśvarasyāpi sapta medhātitheḥ sutāḥ ।
jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayasteṣāṃ śiśiraśca sukhodayaḥ । ānandaśca śivaścaiva kṣemakaśca dhruvastathā ।। plakṣadvīpādiṣu jñeyaḥ śākadvīpāntikeṣu vai । varṇāśramavibhāgena svadharmo muktaye dvijāḥ ।।
jambudvīpeśvarasyāpi putrāstvāsan mahābalāḥ । agnīdhrasya dvijaśreṣṭhāstannāmāni nibodhata ।। nābhiḥ kiṃpuruṣaścaiva tathā haririlāvṛtaḥ । ramyo hiraṇvāṃśca kururbhadrāśvaḥ ketumāhalakaḥ ।।
jambudvīpeśvaro rājā sa cāgnīdhro mahāmatiḥ । vibhajya navadhā tebhyo yathānyāyaṃ dadau punaḥ ।। nābhestu dakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ himāhvaṃ pradadau punaḥ । hemakūṭaṃ tato varṣaṃ dadau kiṃpuruṣāya tu ।।
tṛtīyaṃ naiṣadhaṃ varṣaṃ haraye dattavān pitā । ilāvṛtāya pradadau merumadhyamilāvṛtam ।। nīlācalāśritaṃ varṣaṃ ramyāya pradadau pitā । śvetaṃ yaduttaraṃ varṣaṃ pitrā dattaṃ hiraṇvate ।।
yaduttaraṃ śṛṅgavato varṣaṃ tat kuruve dadau । meroḥ pūrveṇa yad varṣaṃ bhadrāśvāya nyavedayat । gandhamādanavarṣaṃ tu ketumālāya dattavān ।। varṣeṣveteṣu tān putrānabhiṣicya narādhipaḥ ।
saṃsārakaṣṭatāṃ jñātvā tapastepe vanaṃ gataḥ ।। himāhvayaṃ tu yasyaitannābherāsīnmahātmanaḥ । tasyarṣabho abhavat putro marudevyāṃ mahādyutiḥ ।। ṛṣabhād bharato jajñe vīraḥ putraśatāgrajaḥ ।
so abhiṣicyarṣabhaḥ putraṃ bharataṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ । vānaprasthāśramaṃ gatvā tapastepe yathāvidhi ।। tapasā karṣito atyarthaṃ kṛśo dhamanisaṃtataḥ । jñānayogarato bhūtvā mahāpāśupato abhavat ।।
sumatirbharatasyābhūt putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ । sumatestaijasastasmādindridyumno vyajāyata ।। parameṣṭhī sutastasmāt pratīhārastadanvayaḥ । pratiharteti vikhyāta utpannastasya cātmajaḥ ।।
bhavastasmādathodgīthaḥ prastāvastatsuto abhavat । pṛthustatastato rakto raktasyāpi gayaḥ sutaḥ ।। naro gayasya tanayastasya putro virāḍabhūt । tasya putro mahāvīryo dhīmāṃstasmādajāyata ।।
mahānto api tataścābhūd bhauvanastatsuto abhavat । tvaṣṭā tvaṣṭuśca virajo rajastasyāpyabhūt sutaḥ ।। śatajid rajasastasya jajñe putraśataṃ dvijāḥ । teṣāṃ pradhāno balavān viśvajyotiriti smṛtaḥ ।।
ārādhya devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ kṣemakaṃ nāma pārthivam । asūta putraṃ dharmajñaṃ mahābāhumarindamam ।। ete purastād rājāno mahāsattvā mahaujasaḥ । eṣāṃ vaṃśaprasūtaiśca bhukteyaṃ pṛthivī purā ।।
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepeṇa dvijottamāḥ । trailokyasyāsya mānaṃ vo na śakyaṃ vistareṇa tu ।। bhūrloko atha bhuvarlokaḥ svarloko atha mahastataḥ । janastapaśca satyaṃ ca lokāstvaṇḍodbhavā matāḥ ।।
sūryācandramasoryāvat kiraṇairavabhāsate । tāvad bhūrloka ākhyātaḥ purāṇe dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।। yāvatpramāṇo bhūrloko vistarāt parimaṇḍalāt । bhuvarloko api tāvānsyānmaṇḍalād bhāskarasya tu ।।
ūrdhvaṃyanmaṇḍalād vyomadhruvoyāvadvyavasthitaḥ । svarlokaḥ sa samākhyātastatra vāyostu nemayaḥ ।। āvahaḥ pravahaścaiva tathaivānuvahaḥ paraḥ । saṃvaho vivahaścātha tadūrdhvaṃ syāt parāvahaḥ ।।
tathā parivahaścordhvaṃ vāyorvai sapta nemayaḥ । bhūmeryojanalakṣe tu bhānorvai maṇḍalaṃ sthitam ।। lakṣe divākarasyāpi maṇḍalaṃ śaśinaḥ smṛtam । nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ tallakṣeṇa prakāśate ।।
dvelakṣe hyuttare viprā budho nakṣatramaṇḍalāt । tāvatpramāṇabhāge tu budhasyāpyuśanāḥ sthitaḥ ।। aṅgārako api śukrasya tatpramāṇo vyavasthitaḥ । lakṣadvayena bhaumasya sthito devapurohitaḥ ।।
saurirdvilakṣeṇa guror grahāṇāmatha maṇḍalam । saptarṣimaṇḍalaṃ tasmāllakṣamātre prikāśate ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ maṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ lakṣamātre sthito dhruvaḥ । meḍhībhūtaḥ samastasya jyotiścakrasya vai dhruvaḥ ।
tatra dharmaḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇurnārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ ।। navayojanasāhastro viṣkambhaḥ savituḥ smṛtaḥ । triguṇastasya vistāro maṇḍalasya pramāṇataḥ ।। dviguṇastasya vistārād vistāraḥ śaśinaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
tulyastayostu svarbhānurbhūtvādhastāt prasarpati ।। addhṛtya pṛthivīcchāyāṃ nirmito maṇḍalākṛtiḥ । svarbhānostu vṛhat sthānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ yat tamomayam ।। candrasya ṣoḍaśo bhāgo bhārgavasya vidhīyate ।
bhārgavāt pādahīnastu vijñeyo vai bṛhaspatiḥ ।। bṛhaspateḥ pādahīnau vakrasaurāvubhau smṛtau । vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva pādahīnastayorbudhaḥ ।। tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi vapuṣmantīha yāni vai ।
budhena tāni tulyāni vistārānmaṇḍalāt tathā ।। tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparāt । śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve caiva yojane ।। sarvāvaranikṛṣṭāni tārakāmaṇḍalāni tu ।
yojanānyardhamātrāṇi tebhyo hrasvaṃ na vidyate ।। upariṣṭāt trayasteṣāṃ grahā ye dūrasarpiṇaḥ । sauro aṅgirāśca vakraśca jñeyā mandavicāriṇaḥ ।। tebhyo adhastācca catvāraḥ punaranye mahāgrahāḥ ।
sūryaḥ saumo budhaścaiva bhārgavaścaiva śīghragāḥ ।। dakṣiṇāyanamārgastho yadā carati raśmimān । tadā sarvagrahāṇāṃ sa sūryo adhastāt prasarpati ।। vistīrṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā tasyordhvaṃ carate śaśī ।
nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ somādūrdhvaṃ prasarpati ।। nakṣatrebhyo budhaścordhvaṃ budhādūrdhvaṃ tu bhārgavaḥ । vakrastu bhārgavādūrdhvaṃ vakrādūrdhvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ।। tasmācchanaiścaro apuyūrdhvaṃ tasmāt saptarṣimaṇḍalam ।
ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva saptānāndhru vaścordhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ ।। yojanānāṃ sahastrāṇi bhāskarasya ratho nava । īṣādaṇḍastathaiva syād dviguṇo dvijasattamāḥ ।। sārdhakoṭistathā sapta niyutānyadhikāni tu ।
yojanānāṃ tu tasyākṣastatra cakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। trinābhimati pañcāre ṣaṣṇeminyakṣayātmake । saṃvatsarameya kṛtsnaṃ kālacakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। catkāriṃśat sahastrāṇi dvitīyo akṣo vivasvataḥ ।
pañcānyāni tu sārdhāni syandanasya dvijottamāḥ ।। akṣapramāṇamubhayoḥ pramāṇaṃ tadyugārdhayoḥ । hrasvo akṣastadyugārdhena dhruvādhāre rathasya tu ।। dvitīye akṣe tu taccakraṃ saṃsthitaṃ mānasācale ।
hayāśca sapta chandāṃsi tannāmāni nibodhata ।। gāyatrī ca bṛhatyuṣṇik jagatī paṅktireva ca । anaṣṭup triṣṭubityuktāśchandāṃsi harayo hareḥ ।। mānasopari māhendrī prācyāṃ diśi mahāpurī ।
dakṣiṇe na yamasyātha varuṇasya tu paścime ।। uttareṇa tu somasya tannāmāni nibodhata । amarāvatī saṃyamanī sukhā caiva vibhā kramāt ।। kāṣṭhāṃ gato dakṣiṇataḥ kṣipteṣuriva sarpati ।
jyotiṣāṃ cakramādāya devadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। divasasya ravirmadhye sarvakālaṃ vyavasthitaḥ । saptadvīpeṣu viprendrā niśāmadhyasya saṃmukham ।। udayāstamane caiva sarvakālaṃ tu saṃmukhe ।
aśeṣāsu diśāsveva tathaiva vidiśāsu ca ।। kulālacakraparyanto bhramanneṣa yatheśvaraḥ । karotyahastathā rātriṃ vimuñcan medinīṃ dvijāḥ ।। divākarakarairetat pūritaṃ bhuvanatrayam ।
trailokyaṃ kathitaṃ sadbhirlokānāṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। ādityamūlamakhilaṃ trilokaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ । bhavatyasmāt jagat kṛtsnaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। rudrendropendracandrāṇāṃ viprendrāṇāṃ divaukasām ।
dyutirdyutimatāṃ kṛtsnaṃ yattejaḥ sārvalaukikam ।। sarvātmā sarvalokeśo mahādevaḥ prajāpatiḥ । sūrya eva trilokasya mūlaṃ paramadaivatam ।। dvādaśānye tathādityā devāste ye adhikāriṇaḥ ।
nirvahanti padaṃ tasya tadaṃśā viṣṇumūrtayaḥ ।। gandharvadevoragakinvannarādyāḥ । śchandomayaṃ brahmamayaṃ purāṇam ।। sa ratho adhiṣṭhito devairādityairvasubhistathā ।
gandharvairapsarobhiśca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ ।। dhātār'yamātha mitraśca varuṇaḥ śakra eva ca । vivasvānatha pūṣā ca parjanyaścāṃśureva ca ।। bhagastvaṣṭā ca viṣṇuśca dvādaśaite divākarāḥ ।
āpyāyanti vai bhānuṃ vasantādiṣu vai kramāt ।। pulastyaḥ pulahaścātrirvasiṣṭhaścāṅgirā bhṛguḥ । bharadvājo gautamaśca kaśyapaḥ kratureva ca ।। jamadagniḥ kauśikaśca munayo brahmavādinaḥ ।
stuvanti devaṃ vividhaiśchandobhiste yathākramam ।। rathakṛcca rathaujśca rathacitraḥ subāhukaḥ । rathasvano atha varuṇaḥ suṣeṇaḥ senajit tathā ।। tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiśca rathajit satyajit tathā ।
grāmaṇyo devadevasya kurvate abhīśusaṃgraham ।। atha hetiḥ prahetiśca pauruṣeyo vadhastathā । sarpo vyāghrastathāpaśca vāto vidyud divākaraḥ ।। brahmopetaśca viprendrā yajñopetastathaiva ca ।
rākṣasapravarā hyete prayānti purataḥ kramāt ।। vāsukiḥ kaṅkanīraśca takṣakaḥ sarpapuṅgavaḥ । elāpatraḥ śaṅkhapālastathairāvatasaṃjñitaḥ ।। dhanañjayo mahāpadmastathā karkoṭako dvijāḥ ।
kambalāśvataraścaiva vahantyenaṃ yathākramam ।। tumbururnārado hāhā hūhūrviśvāvasustathā । ugraseno vasurucirarvāvasurathāparaḥ ।। citrasenastathorṇāyurdhṛtarāṣṭro dvijottamāḥ ।
sūryavarcā dvādaśaite gandharvā gāyatāṃ varāḥ । gāyanti vividhairgānairbhānuṃ ṣaḍjādibhiḥ kramāt ।। kratusthalāpsarovaryā tathānyā puñjikasthalā । menakā sahajanyā ca pramlocā ca dvijottamāḥ ।।
anumlocā ghṛtīcī ca viśvācī corvaśī tathā । anyā ca pūrvacittiḥ syādanyā caiva tilottamā ।। tāṇḍavairvividhairenaṃ vasantādiṣu vai kramāt । toṣayanti mahādevaṃ bhānumātmānamavyayam ।।
evaṃ devā vasantyarke dvau dvau māsau krameṇa tu । sūryamāpyāyayantyete tejasā tejasāṃ nidhim ।। grathitaiḥ svairvacobhistu stuvanti munayo ravim । gandharvāpsarasaścainaṃ nṛtyageyairupāsate ।।
grāmaṇīyakṣabhūtāni kurvate abhīṣusaṃgraham । sarpā vahanti deveśaṃ yātudhānāḥ prayānti ca ।। bālakhilyā nayantyastaṃ parivāryodayād ravim । ete tapanti varṣanti bhānti vānti sṛjanti ca ।
bhūtānāmaśubhaṃ karma vyapohantīha kīrtitāḥ ।। ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti divi sānugāḥ । vimāne ca sthito nityaṃ kāmage vātaraṃhasi ।। varṣantaśca tapantaśca hlādayantaśca vai prajāḥ ।
gopayantīha bhūtāni sarvāṇīhāyugakṣayāt ।। eteṣāmeva devānāṃ yathāvīryaṃ yathātapaḥ । yathāyogaṃ yathāsattvaṃ sa eṣa tapati prabhuḥ ।। ahorātravyavasthānakāraṇaṃ sa prajāpatiḥ ।
pitṛdevamanuṣyādīn sa sadāpyāyed raviḥ ।। tatra devo mahādevo bhāsvān sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ । bhāsate vedaviduṣāṃ nīlagrīvaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। sa eṣa devo bhagavān parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ ।
sthānaṃ tad vidurādityaṃ vedajñā vedavigraham ।। evameṣa mahādevo devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ । karoti niyataṃ kālaṃ kālātmā hyaiśvarī tanuḥ ।। tasya ye raśmayo viprāḥ sarvalokapradīpakāḥ ।
teṣāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ punaḥ sapta raśmayo grahayonayaḥ ।। suṣumno harikeśaśca viśvakarmā tathaiva ca । viśvavyacāḥ punaścānyaḥ saṃyadvasurataḥ paraḥ ।। arvāvasuriti khyātaḥ svarāḍanyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।
supumnaḥ sūryaraśmistu puṣṇāti śiśiradyutim ।। tiryagūrdhvapracāro asau suṣumnaḥ paripaṭhyate । harikeśastu yaḥ prokto raśmirnakṣatrapoṣakaḥ ।। viśvakarmā tathā raśmirbudhaṃ puṣṇāti sarvadā ।
viśvavyacāstu yo raśmiḥ śukraṃ puṣṇāti nityadā ।। saṃyadvasuriti khyātaḥ sa puṣṇāti ca lohitam । vṛhaspatiṃ prapuṣṇāti raśmirarvāvasuḥ prabhoḥ । śanaiścaraṃ prapuṣṇāti saptamastu surāṭ tathā ।।
evaṃ sūryaprabhāvena sarvā nakṣatratārakāḥ । vardhante vardhitā nityaṃ nityamāpyāyayanti ca ।। divyānāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca naiśānāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ । ādānānnityamādityastejasāṃ tamasāṃ prabhuḥ ।।
ādatte sa tu nāḍīnāṃ sahastreṇa samantataḥ । nādeyāṃścaiva sāmudrān kūpyāṃścaiva sahastradṛk । sthāvarāñjaṅgamāṃścaiva yacca kulyādikaṃ payaḥ ।। tasya raśmisahastraṃ tacchītavarṣoṣṇanistravam ।
tāsāṃ catuḥ śataṃ nāḍyo varṣante citramūrtayaḥ ।। vandanāścaiva yājyāśca ketanā bhūtanāstathā । amṛtā nāma tāḥ sarvā raśmayo vṛṣṭisarjanāḥ ।। himodvāhāśca tā nāḍyo raśmayastriśataṃ punaḥ ।
raśmyo meṣyaśca pauṣyaśca hlādinyo himasarjanāḥ । candrāstā nāmataḥ sarvāḥ pītābhāḥ syurgabhastayaḥ ।। śukrāśca kakubhaścaiva gāvo viśvabhṛtastathā । śukrāstā nāmataḥ sarvāstrividhā gharmasarjanāḥ ।।
samaṃ bibharti tābhiḥ sa manuṣyapitṛdevatāḥ । manuṣyānauṣadheneha svadhayā ca pitṝnapi । amṛtena surān sarvāṃstribhistrariṃstarpayatyasau ।। vasante graiṣmike caiva śataiḥ sa tapati tribhiḥ ।
śaradyapi ca varṣāsu caturbhaiḥ saṃpravarṣati । hemante śiśire caiva himamutsṛjati tribhiḥ ।। varuṇo māghamāse tu sūryaḥ pūṣā tu phalgune । caitre māsi bhavedaṃśo dhātā vaiśākhatāpanaḥ ।।
jyeṣṭhāmūle bhavedindraḥ āṣāḍhe savitā raviḥ । vivasvān śrāvaṇe māsi prauṣṭhapadyāṃ bhagaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। parjanyo aśvayuji tvaṣṭākārtike māsi bhāskaraḥ । mārgaśīrṣa bhavenmitraḥ pauṣe viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
pañcaraśmisahastrāṇi varuṇasyārkakarmaṇi । ṣaḍbhiḥ sahastraiḥ pūṣā tu devoṃśaḥ saptabhistathā ।। dhātāṣṭabhiḥ sahastraistu navabhistu śatakratuḥ । vivasvān daśabhiḥ pāti pātyekādaśabhirbhagaḥ ।।
saptabhistapate mitrastvaṣṭā caivāṣṭabhistapet । aryamā daśabhaiḥ pāti parjanyo navabhistapet । ṣaḍbhī raśmisahastraistu viṣṇustapati viśvasṛk ।। vasante kapilaḥ sūryo grīṣme kāñcanasaprabhaḥ ।
śveto varṣāsu varṇena pāṇḍuraḥ śaradi prabhuḥ । hemante tāmravarṇaḥ syācchiśire lohito raviḥ ।। oṣadhīṣu balaṃ dhatte svadhāmapi pitṛṣvatha । sūryo amaratvamamṛte trayaṃ triṣu niyacchati ।।
anye cāṣṭau grahā jñeyāḥ sūryeṇādhiṣṭhitā dvijāḥ । candramāḥ somaputraśca śukraścaiva bṛhaspatiḥ । bhaumo mandastathā rāhuḥ ketumānapi cāṣṭamaḥ ।। sarve dhruve nibaddhā vai grahāste vātaraśmibhiḥ ।
bhrāmyamāṇā yathāyogaṃ bhramantyanudivākaram ।। alātacakravad yānti vātacakreritā dvijāḥ । yasmād vahati tān vāyuḥ pravahastena sa smṛtaḥ ।। rathastricakraḥ somasya kundābhāstasya vājinaḥ ।
vāmadakṣiṇato yuktā daśa tena niśākaraḥ ।। vīthyāśrayāṇi carati nakṣatrāṇi raviryathā । hrāsavṛddhī ca viprendrā dhruvādhārāṇi sarvadā ।। sa somaḥ śuklapakṣe tu bhāskare parataḥ sthite ।
āpūryate parasyāntaḥ satataṃ divasakramāt ।। kṣīṇāyitaṃ suraiḥ somamāpyāyati nityadā । ekena raśminā viprāḥ suṣumnākhyena bhāskaraḥ ।। eṣā sūryasya vīryeṇa somasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ ।
paurṇamāsyāṃ sa dṛśyeta saṃpūrṇe divasakramāt ।। saṃpūrṇamardhamāsena taṃ somamamṛtātmakam । pibanti devatā viprā yataste amṛtabhojanāḥ ।। tataḥ pañcadaśe bhāge kiñcicchiṣṭe kalātmake ।
aparāhṇe pitṛgaṇā jaghanyaṃ paryupāsate ।। pibanti dvikalaṃ kālaṃ śiṣṭā tasya kalā tuyā । sudhāmṛtamayīṃ puṇyāṃ tāmandoramṛtātmikām ।। niḥ sṛtaṃ tadamāvāsyāṃ gabhastibhyaḥ svadhāmṛtam ।
māsatṛptimapāpyagryāṃ pitaraḥ santi nirvṛtāḥ ।। na somasya vināśaḥ syāt sudhā devaistu pīyate । evaṃ sūryanimittasya kṣayo vṛddhiśca sattamāḥ ।। somaputrasya cāṣṭābhirvājibhirvāyuvegibhiḥ ।
vārijaiḥ syandano yuktastenāsau yāti sarvataḥ ।। śukrasya bhūmijairaśvaiḥ syandano daśabhirvṛtaḥ । aṣṭabiścātha bhaumasya ratho haimaḥ suśobhanaḥ ।। bṛhaspaterathāṣṭāśvaḥ syandano hemanirmitaḥ ।
rathastamomayo aṣṭāśvo mandasyāyasanirmitaḥ । svarbhānorbhāskarāreśca tathā ṣaḍbhirhayairvṛtaḥ ।। ete mahāgrahāṇāṃ vai samākhyātā rathā nava । sarve dhruve mahābhāgā nibaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ ।।
graharkṣatārādhiṣṇyāni dhruve baddhānyeśeṣataḥ । bhramanti bhrāmayantyenaṃ sarvāṇyanilaraśmibhiḥ ।। dhruvādūrdhvaṃ maharlokaḥ koṭiyojanavistṛtaḥ । kalpādhikāriṇastatra saṃsthitā dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।।
janaloko maharlokāt tathā koṭidvayātamakaḥ । sanandanādayastatra saṃsthitā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।। jalokāt tapolokaḥ koṭitrayasamanvitaḥ । vairājāstatra vai devāḥ sthitā dāhavivarjitāḥ ।।
prājāpatyāt satyalokaḥ koṭiṣaṭkena saṃyutaḥ । apunarmārakāstatra brahmalokastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। atra lokagururbrahmā viśvātmā viśvatomukhaḥ । āste sa yogibhirnityaṃ pītvā yogāmṛtaṃ param ।।
viśanti yatayaḥ śāntā naiṣṭhikā brahmacāriṇaḥ । yoginastāpasāḥ siddhā jāpakāḥ parameṣṭhinam ।। dvāraṃ tadyogināmekaṃ gacchatāṃ paramaṃ padam । tatra gatvā na śocanti sa viṣṇuḥ sa ca śaṅkaraḥ ।।
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ puraṃ tasya durāsadam । na me varṇayituṃ śakyaṃ jvālāmālāsamākulam ।। tatra nārāyaṇasyāpi bhavanaṃ brahmaṇaḥ pure । śete tatra hariḥ śrīmān māyī māyāmayaḥ paraḥ ।।
sa viṣṇulokaḥ kathitaḥ punarāvṛttivarjitaḥ । yānti tatra mahātmāno ye prapannā janārdanam ।। ūrdhvaṃ tad brahmasadanāt puraṃ jyotirmayaṃ śubham । vahninā ca parikṣiptaṃ tatrāste bhagavān bhavaḥ ।।
devyā saha mahādevaścintyamāno manīṣibhiḥ । yogibhiḥ śatasāhastrairbhūtai rudraiśca saṃvṛtaḥ ।। tatra te yānti niyatā dvijā vai brahmacāriṇaḥ । madādevaparāḥ śāntāstāpasā brahmavādinaḥ ।।
nirmamā nirahaṅkārāḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ । drakṣyanti brahmaṇā yuktā rudralokaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ ।। ete sapta mahālokāḥ pṛthivyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ । mahātalādayaścādhaḥ pātālāḥ santi vai dvijāḥ ।।
mahātalaṃ ca pātālaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam । prāsādairvividhaiḥ śubhrairdevatāyatanairyutam ।। anantena ca saṃyuktaṃ mucukundena dhīmatā । nṛpeṇa balinā caiva pātālasvargavāsinā ।।
śailaṃ rasātalaṃ viprāḥ śārkaraṃ hi talātalam । pītaṃ sutalamityuktaṃ nitalaṃ vidrumaprabham । sitaṃ hi vitalaṃ proktaṃ talaṃ caiva sitetaram ।। suparṇena muniśreṣṭhāstathā vāsukinā śubham ।
rasātalamiti khyātaṃ tathānyaiśca niṣevitam ।। virocanahiraṇyākṣatakṣakādyaiśca sevitam । talātalamiti khyātaṃ sarvaśobhāsamanvitam ।। vainateyādibhiścaiva kālanemipurogamaiḥ ।
pūrvadevaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ sutalaṃ ca tathāparaiḥ ।। nitalaṃ yavanādyaiśca tārakāgnimukhaistathā । mahāntakādyairnāgaiśca prahmādenāsureṇa ca ।। vitalaṃ caiva vikhyātaṃ kambalāhīndrasevitam ।
mahājambhena vīreṇa hayagrīveṇa vai tathā ।। śaṅkukarṇena saṃbhinnaṃ tathā namucipūrvakaiḥ । tathānyairvivadhairnāgaistalaṃ caiva suśobhanam ।। teṣāmadhastānnarakā māyādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
pāpinasteṣu pacyante na te varṇayituṃ kṣamāḥ ।। pātālānāmadhaścāste śeṣākhyā vaiṣṇavī tanuḥ । kālāgnirudro yogātmā nārasiṃho api mādhavaḥ ।। yo anantaḥ paṭhyete devo nāgarūpī janārdanaḥ ।
tadādhāramidaṃ sarvaṃ sa kālāgnimapāśritaḥ ।। tamāviśya mahāyogī kālastadvadanotthitaḥ । viṣajvālāmayo ante asau jagat saṃharati svayam ।। sahastramāyo apratimaḥ saṃhartā śaṅkarodbhavaḥ ।
tāmasī śāṃbhavī mūrtiḥ kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।। etad brahmāṇḍamākhyātaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃ mahat । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhūrlokasyāsya nirṇayam ।। jambudvīpaḥ pradhāno ayaṃ plakṣaḥ śālmala eva ca ।
kuśaḥ krauñcaśca śākaśca puṣkaraścaiva saptamaḥ ।। ete sapta mahādvīpāḥ samudraiḥ saptabhirvṛtāḥ । dvīpād dvīpo mahānuktaḥ sāgarādapi sāgaraḥ ।। kṣārodekṣurasodaśca surodaśca ghṛtodakaḥ ।
dadhyodaḥ kṣīrasalilaḥ svādūdaśceti sāgarāḥ ।। pañcāśatkoṭivistīrṇā sasamudrā dharā smṛtā । dvīpaiśca saptabhiryuktā yojanānāṃ samāsataḥ ।। jambūdvīpaḥ samastānāṃ dvīpānāṃ madhyataḥ śubhaḥ ।
tasya madhye mahāmerurviśrutaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ ।। caturaśītisāhastro yojanaistasya cocchrayaḥ । praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastāddvātriṃśanmūrdhni vistṛtaḥ ।। mūle ṣoḍaśasāhastro vistārastasya sarvataḥ ।
bhūpadmāsyāsya śailo asau karṇikātvena saṃsthitaḥ ।। himavān hemakūṭaśca niṣadhaścāsya dakṣiṇe । nīlaḥ śvetaśca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ ।। lakṣapramāṇau dvau madhye daśahīnāstathā pare ।
sahastradvitayocchrāyāstāvadvistāriṇaśca te ।। bhārataṃ dakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ tataḥ kiṃpuruṣaṃ smṛtam । harivarṣaṃ tathaivānyanmerordakṣiṇato dvijāḥ ।। ramyakaṃ cottaraṃ varṣaṃ tasyaivānuhiraṇmayam ।
uttarāḥ kuravaścaiva yathaite bharatāstathā ।। navasāhastramekaikameteṣāṃ dvijasattamāḥ । ilāvṛtaṃ ca tanmadhye tanmadhye merurucchritaḥ ।। meroścaturdiśaṃ tatra navasāhastravistṛtam ।
ilāvṛtaṃ mahābhāgāścātvārastatra parvatāḥ । viṣkambhā racitā meroryojanāyutamucchritāḥ ।। pūrveṇa mandaro nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ । vipulaḥ paścime pārśve supārśvaścottare smṛtaḥ ।।
kadambasteṣu jambuśca pippalo vaṭa eva ca । jambūdvīpasya sā jambūrnāmaheturmaharṣayaḥ ।। mahāgajapramāṇāni jambvāstasyāḥ phalāni ca । patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvataḥ ।।
rasena tasyāḥ prakhyātā tatra jambūnadīti vai । sarit pravartate cāpi pīyate tatra vāsibhiḥ ।। na svedo na ca daurgandhyaṃ na jarā nendriyakṣayaḥ । tatpānāt susthamanasāṃ narāṇāṃ tatra jāyate ।।
tīramṛttatra saṃprāpya vāyunā suviśoṣitā । jāmbūnadākhyaṃ bhavati suvarṇaṃ siddhabhūṣaṇam ।। bhadrāśvaḥ pūrvato meroḥ ketumālaśca paścime । varṣe dve tu muniśreṣṭhāstayormadhye ilāvṛtam ।।
vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ pūrve dakṣiṇe gandhamādanam । vaibhrājaṃ paścime vidyāduttare saviturvanam ।। aruṇodaṃ mahābhadramasitodaṃ ca mānasam । sarāṃsyetāni catvāri devayogyāni sarvadā ।।
sitāntaśca kumudvāṃśca kururī mālyavāṃstathā । vaikaṅko maṇiśailaśca ṛkṣavāṃścācalottamāḥ ।। mahānīlo atha rucakaḥ sabindurmandarastathā । veṇumāṃścaiva meghaśca niṣadho devaparvataḥ ।
ityete devaracitāḥ siddhāvāsāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। aruṇodasya sarasaḥ pūrvataḥ kesarācalaḥ । trikūṭaśikharaścaiva pataṅgo rucakastathā ।। niṣadho vasudhāraśca kaliṅgastriśikhaḥ śubhaḥ ।
samūlo vasudhāraśca kuravaścaiva sānumān ।। tāmrātaśca viśālaśca kumudo veṇurvataḥ । ekaśṛṅgo mahāśailo gajaśailaḥ piśācakaḥ ।। pañcaśailo atha kailāso himavāṃśacācalottamaḥ ।
ityete devacaritā utkaṭāḥ parvatottamāḥ ।। mahābhadrasya saraso dakṣiṇe kesarācalaḥ । śikhivāsaśca vaidūryaḥ kapilo gandhamādanaḥ ।। jārudhiśca sugandhiśca śrīśṛṅgaścācalottamaḥ ।
supārśvaśca supakṣaśca kaṅkaḥ kapila eva ca ।। piñjaro bhadraśailaśca surasaśca mahābalaḥ । añjano madhumāṃstadvat kumudo mukuṭastathā ।। sahastraśikharaścaiva pāṇḍuraḥ kṛṣṇa eva ca ।
pārijāto mahāśailastathaiva kapilodakaḥ ।। suṣeṇaḥ puṇḍarīkaśca mahāmeghastathaiva ca । ete parvatarājānaḥ siddhagandharvasevitāḥ ।। asitodasya sarasaḥ paścime kesarācalaḥ ।
śaṅkhakūṭo atha vṛṣabho haṃso nāgastathā paraḥ ।। kālāñjanaḥ śukraśailo nīlaḥ kamala eva ca । puṣpakaśca sumeghaśca vārāho virajāstathā । mayūraḥ kapilaścaiva mahākapila eva ca ।।
ityete devagandharvasiddhasaṅghaniṣevitāḥ । saraso mānasasyeha uttare kesarācalāḥ ।। eteṣāṃ śailamukhyānāmantareṣu yathākramam । santi caivāntaradroṇyaḥ sarāṃsi ca vanāni ca ।।
vasanti tatra munayaḥ siddhāśca brahmabhāvitāḥ । prasannāḥ śāntarajasaḥ sarvaduḥ khavivarjitāḥ ।। caturdaśasahastraṇi yojanānāṃ mahāpurī । merorupari vikhyātā devadevasya vedhasaḥ ।।
tatrāste bhagavān brahmā viśvātmā viśvabhāvanaḥ । upāsyamāno yogīndrairmunīndropendraśaṅkaraiḥ ।। tatra deveśvareśānaṃ viśvātmānaṃ prajāpatim । sanatkumāro bhagavānupāste nityameva hi ।।
sa siddhairṛṣigandharvaiḥ pūjyamānaḥ surairapi । samāste yogayuktatmā pītvā tatparamāmṛtam ।। tatra devādidevasya śaṃbhoramitatejasaḥ । dīptamāyatanaṃ śubhraṃ purastād brahmaṇaḥ sthitam ।।
divyakāntisamāyuktaṃ caturdhāraṃ suśobhanam । maharṣigaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ brahmavidbhirniṣevitam ।। devyā saha mahādevaḥ śaśāṅkārkāgnilocanaḥ । ramate tatra viśveśaḥ pramathaiḥ pramatheśvaraḥ ।।
tatra vedavidaḥ śāntā munayo brahmacāriṇaḥ । pūjayanti mahādevaṃ tāpasāḥ satyavādinaḥ ।। teṣāṃ sākṣānmahādevo munīnāṃ brahmavādinām । gṛhṇāti pūjāṃ śirasā pārvatyā parameśvaraḥ ।।
tatraiva parvatavare śakrasya paramā purī । nāmnāmarāvatī pūrve sarvaśobhāsamanvitā ।। tamindramapsaraḥ saṅghā gandharvā gītatatparāḥ । upāsate sahastrākṣaṃ devāstatra sahastraśaḥ ।।
ye dhārmikā vedavido yāgahomaparāyaṇāḥ । teṣāṃ tat paramaṃ sthānaṃ devānāmapi durlabham ।। tasya dakṣiṇadigbhāge vahneramitatejasaḥ । tejovatī nāma purī divyāścaryasamanvitā ।।
tatrāste bhagavān vahnirbhrājamānaḥ svatejasā । japināṃ homināṃ sthānaṃ dānavānāṃ durāsadam ।। dakṣiṇe parvatavare yamasyāpi mahāpurī । nāmnā saṃyamanī divyā siddhagandharvasevitā ।।
tatra vaivasvataṃ devaṃ devādyāḥ paryupāsate । sthānaṃ tat satyasaṃdhānāṃ loke puṇyakṛtāṃ nṛṇām ।। tasyāstu paścime bhāge nirṛtestu mahātmanaḥ । rakṣovatī nāma purī rākṣasaiḥ sarvato vṛtā ।।
tatra taṃ nirṛtiṃ devaṃ rākṣasāḥ paryupāsate । gacchanti tāṃ dharmaratā ye vai tāmasavṛttayaḥ ।। paścime parvatavare varuṇasya mahāpurī । nāmnā suddhavatī puṇyā sarvakāmardhisaṃyutā ।।
tatrāpsarogaṇaiḥ siddhaiḥ sevyamāno amarādhipaḥ । āste sa varuṇo rājā tatra gacchanti ye ambudāḥ । tīrthayātrāparī nityaṃ ye ca loke adhamarṣiṇaḥ ।। tasyā uttaradigbhāge vāyorapi mahāpurī ।
nāmnā gandhavatī puṇyā tatrāste asau prabhañjanaḥ ।। apsarogaṇagandharvaiḥ sevyamāno amaraprabhuḥ । prāṇāyāmaparāmartyāsthānantadyānti śāśvatam ।। tasyāḥ pūrveṇa digbhāge somasya paramā purī ।
nāmnā kāntimatī śubhrā tatra somo virājate ।। tatra ye bhoganiratā svadharmaṃ puryapāsate । teṣāṃ tad racitaṃ sthānaṃ nānābhogasamanvitam ।। tasyāśca pūrvadigbhāge śaṅkarasya mahāpurī ।
nāmnā yaśovatī puṇyā sarveṣāṃ sudurāsadā ।। tatreśānasya bhavanaṃ rudraviṣṇutanoḥ śubham । ghameśvarasya vipulaṃ tatrāste sa gaṇairvṛtaḥ ।। tatra bhogābhilipsūnāṃ bhaktānāṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
nivāsaḥ kalpitaḥ pūrvaṃ devadevena śūlinā ।। viṣṇupādād viniṣkrāntā plāvayitvendumaṇḍalam । samantād brahmaṇaḥ puryāṃ gaṅgā patati vai divaḥ ।। sā tatra patitā dikṣu caturdhā hyabhavad dvijāḥ ।
sītā cālakanandā ca sucakṣurbhadranāmikā ।। pūrveṇa sītā śailāt tu śailaṃ yātyantarikṣataḥ । tataśca pūrvavarṣeṇa bhadrāśvenaiti cārṇavam ।। tathaivālakanandā ca dakṣiṇādetya bhāratam ।
prayāti sāgaraṃ bhittvā saptabhedā dvijottamāḥ ।। sucakṣuḥ paścimagirīnatītya sakalāṃstathā । paścimaṃ ketumālākhyaṃ varṣaṃ gatvaiti cārṇavam ।। bhadrā tathottaragirīnuttarāṃśca tathā kurūn ।
atītya cottarāmbhodhiṃ samabhyeti maharṣayaḥ ।। ānīlaniṣadhāyāmau mālyavān gandhamādanaḥ । tayormadhyagato meruḥ karṇikākārasaṃsthitaḥ ।। bhāratāḥ ketumālāśca bhadrāśvāḥ kuravastathā ।
patrāṇi lokapadmasya maryādāśailabāhyataḥ ।। jaṭharo devakūṭaśca maryādāparvatāvubhau । dakṣiṇottaramāyāmāvānīlaniṣadhāyatau ।। gandhamādanakailāsau pūrvapaścāyatāvubhau ।
aśītiyojanāyāmāvarṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।। niṣadhaḥ pāriyātraśca maryādāparvatāvimau । meroḥ paścimadigbhāge yathāpūrvau tathā sthitau ।। triśṛṅgo jārudhaistadvaduttare varṣaparvatau ।
pūrvapaścāyatāvetau arṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।। maryādāparvatāḥ proktā aṣṭāviha mayā dvijāḥ । jaṭharādyāḥ sthitā meroścaturdikṣu maharṣayaḥ ।। ketumāle narāḥ kālāḥ sarve panasabhojanāḥ ।
striyaścotpalapatrābhā jīvanti ca varṣāyutam ।। bhadrāśve puruṣāḥ śuklāḥ striyaścandrāṃśusannibhāḥ । daśa varṣasahastrāṇi jīvante āmrabhojanāḥ ।। ramyake puruṣā nāryo ramante rajataprabhāḥ ।
daśavarṣasahastrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca । jīvanti caiva sattvasthā nyagrodhaphalabhojanāḥ ।। hiraṇmaye hiraṇyābhāḥ sarve ca lakucāśanāḥ । ekādaśasahastrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca ।
jīvanti puruṣā nāryo devalokasthitā iva ।। trayodaśasahastrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca । jīvanti kuruvarṣe tu śyāmāṅgāḥ kṣīrabhojanāḥ ।। sarve mithunajātāśca nityaṃ sukhaniṣevinaḥ ।
candradvīpe mahādevaṃ yajanti satataṃ śivam ।। tathā kiṃpuruṣe viprā mānavā hemasannibhāḥ । daśavarṣahastrāṇi jīvanti plakṣabhojanāḥ ।। yajanti satataṃ devaṃ caturmūrti caturmukham ।
dhyāne manaḥ samādhāya sādaraṃ bhaktisaṃyutāḥ ।। tathā ca harivarṣe tu mahārajatasannibhāḥ । daśavarṣasahastrāṇi jīvantīkṣurasāśinaḥ ।। tatra nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ viśvayoniṃ sanātanam ।
upāsate sadā viṣṇuṃ mānavā viṣṇubhāvitāḥ ।। tatra candraprabhaṃ śubhraṃ śuddhasphaṭikanirmitam । vimānaṃ vāsudevasya pārijātavanāśritam ।। caturdhāramanopamyaṃ catustoraṇasaṃyutam ।
prākārairdaśabhiryuktaṃ durādharṣaṃ sudurgamam ।। sphāṭikairmaṇḍapairyuktaṃ devarājagṛhopamam । svarṇastambhasahastraiśca sarvataḥ samalaṅkṛtam ।। hemasopānasaṃyuktaṃ nānāratnopaśobhitam ।
divyasiṃhāsanopetaṃ sarvaśobhāsamanvitam ।। sarobhiḥ svādupānīyairnadībhiścopaśobhitam । nārāyaṇaparaiḥ śuddhairvedādhyayanatatparaiḥ ।। yogibhiśca samākīrṇaṃ dhyāyadbhiḥ puruṣaṃ harim ।
stuvadbhiḥ satataṃ mantrairnamasyadbhiśca mādhavam ।। tatra devādidevasya viṣṇoramitatejasaḥ । rājānaḥ sarvakālaṃ tu mahimānaṃ prakurvate ।। gāyanti caiva nṛtyanti vilāsinyo manoramāḥ ।
striyo yauvanaśālinyaḥ sadā maṇḍanatatparāḥ ।। ilāvṛte padmavarṇā jambūphalarasāśinaḥ । trayodaśa sahastrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ vai sthirāyuṣaḥ ।। bhārate tu striyaḥ puṃso nānāvarṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
nānādevārcane yuktā nānākarmāṇi kurvate । paramāyuḥ smṛtaṃ teṣāṃ śataṃ varṣāṇi suvratāḥ ।। nānāhārāśca jīvanti puṇyapāpanimittataḥ । navayojanasāhastraṃ varṣametat prakīrtitam ।
karmabhūmiriyaṃ viprā narāṇāmadhikāriṇām ।। mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimānṛkṣaparvataḥ । vindhyaśca pāriyātraśca saptātra kulaparvatāḥ ।। indradyumnaḥ kaśerumāṃstāmravarṇo gabhastimān ।
nāgadvīpastathā saumyo gandharvastvatha vāruṇaḥ ।। ayaṃ tu navamasteṣāṃ dvīpaḥ sāgarasaṃvṛtaḥ । yojanānāṃ sahastraṃ tu dvīpo ayaṃ dakṣiṇottaraḥ ।। pūrve kirātāstasyānte paśicame yavanāstathā ।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśya madhye śūdrāstathaiva ca ।। ijyāyuddhavaṇijyābhirvartayantyatra mānavāḥ । stravante pāvanā nadyaḥ parvatebhyo viniḥ sṛtāḥ ।। śatadruścandrabhāgā ca sarayūryamunā tathā ।
irāvatī vitastā ca vipāśā devikā kuhūḥ ।। gomatī dhūtapāpā ca bāhudā ca dṛṣadvatī । kauśikī lohitā caiva himavatpādaniḥ sṛtāḥ ।। vedasmṛtirvedavatī vrataghnī tridivā tathā ।
parṇāśā vandanā caiva sadānīrā manoramā ।। carmaṇvatī tathā dūryā vidiśā vetravatyapi । śigruḥ svaśilpāpi tathā pāriyātrāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। narmadā surasā śoṇa daśārṇā ca mahānadī ।
mandākinī citrakūṭā tāmasī ca piśācikā ।। citrotpalā vipāśā ca mañjulā vāluvāhinī । ṛkṣavatpādajā nadyaḥ sarvapāpaharā nṛṇām ।। tāpī payoṣṇī nirvindhyā śīghrodā ca mahānadī ।
veṇyā vaitaraṇī caiva balākā ca kumudvatī ।। toyā caiva mahāgairī durgā cāntaḥ śilā tathā । vindhyapādaprasūtāstā nadyaḥ puṇyajalāḥ śubhāḥ ।। sodāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇā varṇā ca matsarī ।
tuṅgabhdrā suprayogā kāverī ca dvijottamāḥ । dakṣiṇāpathagā nadyaḥ sahyapādaviniḥ sṛtāḥ ।। ṛtumālā tāmraparṇo puṣpavatyutpalāvatī । malayānniḥ sṛtā nadyaḥ sarvāḥ śītajalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
ṛṣikulyā trisāmā ca mandagā mandagāminī । rūpā pālāsinī caiva ṛṣikā vaṃśakāriṇī । śuktimatpādasaṃjātāḥ sarvapāpaharā nṛṇām ।। āsāṃ nadyupanadyaśca śataśo dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।
sarvapāpaharāḥ puṇyāḥ snānadānādikarmasu ।। tāsvime kurupāñcālā madhyadeśādayo janāḥ । pūrvadeśādikāścaiva kāmarūpanivāsinaḥ ।। puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgāmagadhā dākṣiṇātyāścakṛtsnaśaḥ ।
tathāparāntāḥ saurāṣṭrāḥ śūdrābhīrāstathār'budāḥ ।। mālakā mālavāścaiva pāriyātranivāsinaḥ । sauvīrāḥ saindhavā hūṇā śālvāḥ kalpanivāsinaḥ ।। madrā rāmāstathāmbaṣṭhāḥ pārasīkāstathaiva ca ।
āsāṃ pibanti salilaṃ vasanti saritāṃ sadā ।। catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni kavayo abruvan । kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliścānyatra na kvacit ।। yāni kiṃpuruṣādyāni varṣāṇyaṣṭau maharṣayaḥ ।
na teṣu śoko nāyāso nodvegaḥ kṣudbhayaṃ na ca ।। svasthāḥ prajā nirātaṅkāḥ sarvaduḥ khavivarjitāḥ । ramanti vividhairbhāvaiḥ sarvāśca sthirayauvanāḥ ।। hemakūṭagireḥ śṛṅge mahākūṭaiḥ suśobhanam ।
sphāṭikaṃ devadevasya vimānaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। atha devādidevasya bhūteśasya triśūlinaḥ । devāḥ siddhagaṇā yakṣāḥ pūjāṃ nityaṃ prakurvate ।। sa devo giriśaḥ sārdhaṃ mahādevyā maheśvaraḥ ।
bhūtaiḥ parivṛto nityaṃ bhāti tatra pinākadhṛk ।। vibhaktacāruśikharaḥ kailāso yatra parvataḥ । nivāsaḥ koṭiyakṣāṇāṃ kuberasya ca dhīmataḥ । tatrāpi devadevasya bhavasyāyatanaṃ mahat ।।
mandākinī tatra divyā ramyā suvimalodakā । nadī nānāvidhaiḥ padmairanekaiḥ samalaṅkṛtā ।। devadānavagandharvayakṣarākṣasakiṃnaraiḥ । upaspṛṣṭajalā nityaṃ supuṇyā sumanoramā ।।
anyāśca nadyaḥ śataśaḥ svarṇapadmairalaṅkṛtāḥ । tāsāṃ kūleṣu devasya sthānāni parameṣṭhinaḥ । devarṣigaṇajuṣṭāni tathā nārāyaṇasya ca ।। sitāntaśikhare cāpi pārijātavanaṃ śubham ।
tatra śakrasya vipulaṃ bhavanaṃ ratnamaṇḍitam । sphāṭikastambhasaṃyuktaṃ hemagopurasaṃyutam ।। tatrātha devadevasya viṣṇorviśvāmareśituḥ । supuṇyaṃ bhavanaṃ ramyaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam ।।
tatra nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān lakṣmyā saha jagatpatiḥ । āste sarvāmaraśreṣṭhaḥ pūjyamānaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। tathā ca vasudhāre tu vasūnāṃ ratnamaṇḍitam । sthānānāmaṣṭakaṃ puṇyaṃ durādharṣaṃ suradviṣām ।।
ratnadhāre girivare saptarṣoṇāṃ mahātmanām । saptāśramāṇi puṇyāni siddhāvāsayutāni tu ।। tatra haimaṃ caturdvāraṃ vajranīlādimaṇḍitam । supuṇyaṃ sumahat sthānaṃ brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।
tatra devarṣayo viprāḥ siddhā brahmarṣayo apare । upāsate sadā devaṃ pitāmahamajaṃ param ।। sa taiḥ saṃpūjito nityaṃ devyā saha caturmukhaḥ । āste hitāya lokānāṃ śāntānāṃ paramā gatiḥ ।।
athaikaśṛṅgaśikhare mahāpadmairalaṅkṛtam । svacchāmṛtajalaṃ puṇyaṃ sugandhaṃ sumahat saraḥ ।। jaigīṣavyāśramaṃ tatra yogīndrairupaśobhitam । tatrāsau bhagavān nityamāste śiṣyaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।
praśāntadoṣairakṣudrairbrahmavidbhirmahātmabhiḥ ।। śaṅkho manoharaścaiva kauśikaḥ kṛṣṇa eva ca । sumanā vedanādaśca śiṣyāstasya pradhānataḥ ।। sarve yogaratāḥ śāntā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ ।
upāsate mahāvīryā brahmavidyāparāyaṇāḥ ।। teṣāmanugrihārthāya yatīnāṃ śāntacetasām । sānnidhyaṃ kurute bhūyo devyā saha maheśvaraḥ ।। anyānicāśramāṇi syustasmin girivarottame ।
munīnāṃ yuktamanasāṃ sarāṃsi saritastathā ।। teṣu yogaratā viprā jāpakāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ । brahmaṇyāsaktamanaso ramante jñānatatparāḥ ।। ātmanyātmānamādhāya śikhāntāntaramāsthitam ।
dhāyāyanti devamīśānaṃ yena sarvamidaṃ tatam ।। sumeghe vāsavasthānaṃ sahastrādityasaṃnibham । tatrāste bhagavānindraḥ śacyā saha sureśvaraḥ ।। gajaśaile tu durgāyā bhavanaṃ maṇitāraṇam ।
āste bhagavatī durgā tatra sākṣānmaheśvarī ।। upāsyamānā vividhaiḥ śaktibhedairitastataḥ । pītvā yogāmṛtaṃ labdhvā sākṣādānandamaiśvaram ।। sunīlasya gireḥ śṛṅge nānādhātusamujjvale ।
rākṣasānāṃ purāṇi syuḥ sarāṃsi śataśo dvijāḥ ।। tathā puraśataṃ viprāḥ śataśṛṅge mahācale । sphāṭikastambhasaṃyuktaṃ yakṣāṇāmamitaujasām ।। śvetodaragireḥ śṛṅge suparṇasya mahātmanaḥ ।
prākāragopuropetaṃ maṇitoraṇamaṇḍitam ।। sa tatra garuḍaḥ śrīmān sākṣād viṣṇurivāparaḥ । dhyātvāste tat paraṃ jyotirātmānaṃ viṣṇumavyayam ।। anyacca bhavanaṃ puṇyaṃ śrīśṛṅge munipuṅgavāḥ ।
śrīdevyāḥ sarvaratnāḍhyaṃ haimaṃ sumaṇitoraṇam ।। tatra sā paramā śaktirviṣṇoratimanoramā । anantavibhavā lakṣmīrjagatsaṃmohanotsukā ।। adhyāste devagandharvasiddhacāraṇavanditā ।
vicintya jagatoyoniṃ svaśaktikiraṇojjvalā ।। tatraiva devadevasya viṣṇorāyatanaṃ mahat । sarāṃsi tatra catvāri vicitrakamalāśrayā ।। tathā sahastraśikhare vidyādharapurāṣṭakam ।
ratnasopānasaṃyuktaṃ sarobhiścopaśobhitam ।। nadyo vimalapānīyāścitranīlotpalākarāḥ । karṇikāravanaṃ dvivyaṃ tatrāste śaṅkaromayā ।। pāriyātre mahāśaile mahālakṣmyāḥ puraṃ śubham ।
ramyaprāsādasaṃyuktaṃ ghaṇṭācāmarabhūṣitam ।। nṛtyadbhirapsaraḥ saṅghairitaścetaśca śobhitam । mṛdaṅgamurajodghuṣṭaṃ vīṇāveṇunināditam ।। gandharvakiṃnarākīrṇaṃ saṃvṛtaṃ siddhapuṅgavaiḥ ।
bhāsvadbhittisamākīrṇaṃ mahāprāsādasaṃkulam ।। gaṇeśvarāṅganājuṣṭaṃ dhārmikāṇāṃ sudarśanam । tatra sā vasate devī nityaṃ yogaparāyaṇā ।। mahālakṣmīrmahādevī triśūlavaradhāriṇī ।
trinetrā sarvaśasaktībhiḥ saṃvṛtā sadasanmayā । paśyanti tatra munayaḥ siddhā ye brahmavādinaḥ ।। supārśvasyottare bhāge sarasvatyāḥ purottamam । sarāṃsi siddhajuṣṭāni devabhogyāni sattamāḥ ।।
pāṇḍurasya gireḥ śṛṅge vicitradrumasaṃkule । sandharvāṇāṃ puraśataṃ divyastrībhiḥ samāvṛtam ।। teṣu nityaṃ madotsiktā varanāryastathaiva ca । krīḍanti muditā nityaṃ vilāsairbhogatatparāḥ ।।
añjanasya gireḥ śṛṅge nārīṇāṃ puramuttamam । vasanti tatrāpsaraso rambhādyā ratilālasāḥ ।। citrasenādayo yatra samāyāntyarthinaḥ sadā । sā purī sarvaratnāḍhyā naikaprastravaṇairyutā ।।
anekāni purāṇi syuḥ kaumude cāpi suvratāḥ । rudrāṇāṃ śāntarajasāmīśvarārpitacetasām ।। teṣu rudrā mahāyogā maheśāntaracāriṇaḥ । samāsate paraṃ jyotirārūḍhāḥ sthānamuttamam ।।
piñjarasya gireḥ śṛṅge gaṇeśānāṃ puratrayam । nandīśvarasya kapile tatrāste suyaśā yatiḥ ।। tathā ca jārudhaiḥ śṛṅge devadevasya dhīmataḥ । dīptamāyatanaṃ puṇyaṃ bhāskarasyāmitaujasaḥ ।।
tasyaivottaradigbhāge candrasthānamanuttamam । ramate tatra ramyo asau bhagavān śītadīdhitiḥ ।। anyacca bhavanaṃ divyaṃ haṃsaśaile maharṣayaḥ । sahastrayojanāyāmaṃ suvarṇamaṇitoraṇam ।।
tatrāste bhagavān brahmā siddhasaṅghairabhiṣṭutaḥ । sāvitryā saha viśvātmā vāsudevādibhiryutaḥ ।। tasya dakṣiṇadigbhāge siddhānāṃ puramuttamam । sanandanādayo yatra vasanti munipuṅgavāḥ ।।
pañcaśailasya śikhare dānavānāṃ puratrayam । nātidūreṇa tasyātha daityacāryasya dhīmataḥ ।। sugandhaśailaśikhare saridbhirupaśobhitam । kardamasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ tatrāste bhagavānṛṣiḥ ।।
tasyaiva pūrvadigbhāge kiñcid vai dakṣiṇāśrite । sanatkumāro bhagavāṃstatrāste brahmavittamaḥ ।। sarveṣveteṣu śaileṣu tatānyeṣu munīśvarāḥ । sarāṃsi vimalā nadyo devānāmālayāni ca ।।
siddhaliṅgāni puṇyāni munibhiḥ sthāpitāni tu । vanyānyāśramavaryāṇi saṃkhyātuṃ naiva śaknuyām ।। eṣa saṃkṣepataḥ prokto jambūdvīpasya vistaraḥ । na śakyaṃ vistarād vaktuṃ mayā varṣaśatairapi ।।
jambūdvīpasya vistārād dviguṇena samantataḥ । saṃveṣṭayitvā kṣārodaṃ plakṣadvīpo vyavasthitaḥ ।। plakṣadvīpe ca viprendrāḥ saptāsan kulaparvatāḥ । ṛjvāyatāḥ suparvāṇaḥ siddhasaṅghaniṣevitāḥ ।।
gomedaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ dvitīyaścandra ucyate । nārādo dundubhiścaiva somaśca ṛṣabhastathā । vaibhrājaḥ saptamaḥ prokto brahmaṇo atyantavallabhaḥ ।। tatra devarṣigandharvaiḥ siddhaiśca bhagavānajaḥ ।
upāsyate sa viśvātmā sākṣī sarvasya viśvasṛk ।। teṣu puṇyā janapadā nādhayo vyādhayo na ca । na tatra pāpakartāraḥ puruṣā vā kathañcana ।। teṣāṃ nadyaśca saptaiva varṣāṇāṃ tu samudragāḥ ।
tāsu brahmarṣayo nityaṃ pitāmahapupāsate ।। anutaptā śikhī caiva vipāpā tridivā kṛtā । amṛtā sukṛtā caiva nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। kṣudranadyastvasaṃkhyātāḥ sarāṃsi subahūnyapi ।
na caiteṣu yugāvasthā puruṣā vai cirāyuṣaḥ ।। āryakāḥ kuravāścaiva vidaśā bhāvinastathā । brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdrāstasmin dvīpe prakīrtitāḥ ।। ijyate bhagavān somo varṇaistatra nivāsibhiḥ ।
teṣāṃ ca somasāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। sarve dharmaparā nityaṃ nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ । pañcavarṣasahastrāṇi jīvanti ca nirāmayāḥ ।। plakṣadvīpapramāṇaṃ tu dviguṇena samantataḥ ।
saṃveṣṭyekṣurasāmbhodhiṃ śālmaliḥ saṃvyavasthitaḥ ।। sapta varṣāṇi tatrāpi saptaiva kulaparvatāḥ । ṛjvāyatāḥ suparvāṇaḥ sapta nadyaśca suvratāḥ ।। kumudaśconnataścaiva tṛtīyaśca balāhakaḥ ।
droṇaḥ kaṅkastu mahiṣaḥ kakudvān sapta parvatāḥ ।। yonī toyā vitṛṣṇā ca candrā śuklā vimocanī । nivṛttiścaiti tā nadyaḥ smṛtā pāpaharā nṛṇām ।। na teṣu vidyate lobhaḥ krodho vā dvijasattamāḥ ।
na caivāsti yugāvasthā janā jīvantyanāmayāḥ ।। yajanti satataṃ tatra varṇā vāyuṃ sanātanam । teṣāṃ tasyātha sāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ ca salokatā ।। kapilā brāhmaṇāḥ proktā rājānaścāruṇāstathā ।
pītā vaiśyāḥ smṛtāḥ kṛṣṇā dvīpe asmin vṛṣalā dvijāḥ ।। śālmalasya tu vistārād dviguṇena samantataḥ । saṃveṣṭya tu surodābdhiṃ kuśadvīpo vyavasthitaḥ ।। vidrumaścaiva hemaśca dyutimān puṣpavāṃstathā ।
kuśeśayo hariścātha mandaraḥ sapta parvatāḥ ।। dhutapāpā śivā caiva pavitrā saṃmatā tathā । vidyudambhā mahī ceti nadyastatra jalāvahāḥ ।। anyāśca śataśoviprā nadyo maṇijalāḥ śubhāḥ ।
tāsu brahmāṇamīśānaṃ devādyāḥ paryupāsate ।। brāhmaṇā draviṇo viprāḥ kṣatriyāḥ śuṣmiṇastathā । vaiśyāḥ snehāstu mandehāḥ śūdrāstatra prakīrtitāḥ ।। sarve vijñānasaṃpannā maitrādiguṇasaṃyutāḥ ।
yathoktakāriṇaḥ sarve sarve bhūtahite ratāḥ ।। yajanti vividhairyajñairbrahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam । teṣāṃ ca brahmasāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ ca salokatā ।। kuśadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇena samantataḥ ।
krauñcadvīpastato viprā veṣṭayitvā ghṛtodadhim ।। krauñco vāmanakaścaiva tṛtīyaścāndhakārakaḥ । devāvṛcca vivindaśca puṇḍarīkastathaiva ca । nāmnā ca saptamaḥ proktaḥ parvato dundubhisvanaḥ ।।
gaurī kumudvitī caiva saṃdhyā rātrirmanojavā । khyātiśca puṇḍarīkāca nadyaḥ prādhānyataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। puṣkarāḥ puṣkalā dhanyāstiṣyāstasya krameṇa vai । brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścaiva dvijottamāḥ ।।
arcayanti mahādevaṃ yajñadānasamādhibhiḥ । vratopavāsairvividhairhemaiḥ svādhyāyatarpaṇaiḥ ।। teṣāṃ vai rudrasāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ cātidurlabham । salokatā ca sāmīpyaṃ jāyate tatprasādataḥ ।।
krauñcadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇena samantataḥ । śākadvīpaḥ sthito viprā āveṣṭya dadhisāgaram ।। udayo raivataścaiva śyāmāko astagiristathā । āmbikeyastathā ramyaḥ keśarī ceti parvatāḥ ।।
sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī reṇukā tathā । ikṣukā dhenukā caiva gabhastiśceti nimnagāḥ ।। āsāṃ pibantaḥ salilaṃ jīvante tatra mānavāḥ । anāmayā hyaśokāśca rāgadveṣavivarjitāḥ ।।
magāśca magadhāścaiva mānavā mandagāstathā । brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścātra krameṇa tu ।। yajanti satataṃ devaṃ sarvalokaikasākṣiṇam । vratopavāsairvividhairdevadevaṃ divākaram ।।
teṣāṃ sūryeṇa sāyujyaṃ sāmīpyaṃ ca sarūpatā । salokatā ca viprendrā jāyate tatprasādataḥ ।। śākadvīpaṃ samāvṛtya kṣīrodaḥ sāgaraḥ sthitaḥ । śvetadvīpaśca tanmadhye nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।।
tatra puṇyā janapadā nānāścaryasamanvitāḥ । śvetāstatra narā nityaṃ jāyante viṣṇutatparāḥ ।। nādhayo vyādhayastatra jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ na ca । krodhalobhavinirmuktā māyāmātsaryavarjitāḥ ।।
nityapuṣṭā nirātaṅkā nityānandāśca bhoginaḥ । nārāyaṇaparāḥ sarve nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।। kecid dhyānaparā nityaṃ yoginaḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ । kecijjapanti tapyanti kecid vijñānino apare ।।
anye nirbojayogena brahmabhāvena bhāvitāḥ । dhyāyanti tat paraṃ vyoma vāsudevaṃ paraṃ padam ।। ekāntino nirālambā mahābhāgavatāḥ pare । paśyanti paramaṃ brahma viṣṇavākhyaṃ tamasaḥ paraṃ ।।
sarve caturbhujākārāḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharāḥ । supītavāsasaḥ sarve śrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasaḥ ।। anye maheśvaraparāstripuṇḍrāṅkitamastakāḥ । svayogodbhūtakiraṇā mahāgaruḍavāhanāḥ ।।
sarvaśaktisamāyuktā nityānandāśca nirmalāḥ । vasanti tatra puruṣā viṣṇorantaracāriṇaḥ ।। tatra nārāyaṇasyānyad durgamaṃ duratikramam । nārāyaṇaṃ nāma puraṃ vyāsādyairupaśobhitam ।।
hemaprākārasaṃsuktaṃ sphāṭikairmaṇḍapairyutam । prabhāsahastrakalilaṃ durādharṣaṃ suśobhanam । harmyaprākārasaṃyuktamaṭṭālakasamākulam ।। hemagopurasāhastrairnānāratnopaśobhitaiḥ ।
śubhrāstaraṇasaṃyuktaṃ vicitraiḥ samalaṅkṛtam ।। nandanairvividhākāraiḥ stravantībhīśca śobhitam । sarobhiḥ sarvato yuktaṃ vīṇāveṇunināditam ।। patākābhirvicitrābhiranekābhiśca śobhitam ।
vīthībhiḥ sarvato yuktaṃ sopānai ratnabhūṣitaiḥ ।। nārīśatasahastrāḍhyaṃ divyagoyasamanvitam । haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇaṃ cakravākopaśobhitam । caturdvāramanaupamyamagamyaṃ devavidviṣām ।।
tatra tatrāpsaraḥ saṅdhairnṛtyadbhirupaśobhitam । nānāgītavidhānajñairdevānāmapi durlabhaiḥ ।। nānāvilāsasaṃpannaiḥ kāmukairatikomalaiḥ । prabhūtacandravadanairnūpurārāvasaṃyutaiḥ ।।
īṣatsmitaiḥ subimboṣṭhairbālamugdhamṛgekṣaṇaiḥ । aśeṣavibhavopetairbhūṣitaistanumadhyamaiḥ ।। surājahaṃsacalanaiḥ suveṣairmadhurasvanaiḥ । saṃlāpālāpakuśalairdivyābharaṇabhūṣaitaiḥ ।।
stanabhāravinamraiśca madaghūrṇitalocanaiḥ । nānāvarṇavicitrāṅgairnānābhogaratipriyaiḥ ।। praphullakusumodyānairitaścetaśca śobhitam । asaṃkhyeyaguṇaṃ śuddhamāgamyaṃ tridaśairapi ।।
śrīmatpavitraṃ devasya śrīpateramitaujasaḥ । tasya madhye atitejaskamuccaprākāratoraṇam ।। sthānaṃ pad vaiṣṇavaṃ divyaṃ yogināmapi durlabham । tanmadhye bhagavānekaḥ puṇḍarīkadaladyutiḥ ।
śete aśeṣajagatsūtiḥ śeṣāhiśayane hariḥ ।। vicintyamāno yogīndraiḥ sanandanapurogamaiḥ । svātmānandāmṛtaṃ pītvā paraṃ tat tamasaḥ param ।। supītavasano ananto mahāmāyo mahābhujaḥ ।
kṣīrodakanyayā nityaṃ gṛhītacaraṇadvayaḥ ।। sā ca devī jagadvandyā pādamūle haripriyā । samāste tanmanā nityaṃ pītvā nārāyaṇāmṛtam ।। na tatrādhārmikā yānti na ca devāntarāśrayāḥ ।
vaikuṇṭhaṃ nāma tat sthānaṃ tridaśairapi vanditam ।। na me atra bhavati prajñā kṛtsnaśastannirūpaṇe । etāvacchakyate vaktuṃ nārāyaṇapuraṃ hi tat ।। sa eva paramaṃ brahma vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ ।
śete nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān māyayā mohayañjagat ।। nārāyaṇādidaṃ jātaṃ tasminneva vyavasthitam । tamevābhyeti kalpānte sa eva paramā gatiḥ ।। śākadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇena vyavasthitaḥ ।
kṣīrārṇavaṃ samāśritya dvīpaḥ puṣkarasaṃvṛtaḥ ।। eka evātra viprendrāḥ parvato mānasottaraḥ । yojanānāṃ sahastrāṇi sārdhaṃ pañcāśaducchritaḥ । tāvadeva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।।
sa eva dvīpaḥ paścārdhe mānasottarasaṃjñitaḥ । eka eva mahāsānuḥ saṃniveśād dvidhā kṛtaḥ ।। tasmin dvīpe smṛtau dvau tu puṇyau janapadau śubhau । aparau mānasasyātha parvatasyānumaṇḍalau ।
mahāvītaṃ smṛtaṃ varṣaṃ dhātakīkhaṇḍameva ca ।। svādūdakenodadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ । tasmin dvīpe mahāvṛkṣo nyagrodho amarapūjitaḥ ।। tasmin nivasati brahmā viśvātmā viśvabhāvanaḥ ।
tatraiva muniśārdūlāḥ śivanārāyaṇālayaḥ ।। vasatyatra mahādevo haror'ddhahariravyayaḥ । saṃpūjyamāno brahmādyaiḥ kumārādyaiśca yogibhiḥ । gandharvaiḥ kinnarairyakṣairīśvaraḥ kṛṣṇapiṅgalaḥ ।।
svasthāstatra prajāḥ sarvā brahmaṇā sadṛśatviṣaḥ । nirāmayā viśokāśca rāgadveṣavivarjitāḥ ।। satyānṛte na tatrāstāṃ nottamādhamamadhyamāḥ । na varṇāśramadharmāśca na nadyo na ca parvatāḥ ।।
pareṇa puṣkarasyātha sthito mahān । svādūdakasamudrastu samantād dvijasattamāḥ ।। pareṇa tasya mahatī dṛśyate lokasaṃsthitiḥ । kāñcanī dviguṇā bhūmiḥ sarvā caiva śilopamā ।।
tasyāḥ pareṇa śailastu maryādātmātmamaṇḍalaḥ । prakāśaścāprakāśaśca lokālokaḥ sa ucyate ।। yojanānāṃ sahastrāṇi daśa tasyocchrayaḥ smṛtaḥ । tāvāneva ca vistāro lokāloko mahāgiriḥ ।।
samāvṛtya tu taṃ śailaṃ sarvato vai tamaḥ sthitam । tamaścāṇḍakaṭāhena samantāt pariveṣṭitam ।। etai sapta mahālokāḥ pātālāḥ saptakīrtitāḥ । brahmāṇḍasyaiṣa vistāraḥ saṃkṣepeṇa mayoditaḥ ।।
aṇḍānāmīdṛśānāṃ tu koṭyo jñeyāḥ sahastraśaḥ । sarvagatvāt pradhānasya kāraṇasyāvyayātmanaḥ ।। aṇḍeṣveteṣu sarveṣu bhuvanāni caturdaśa । tatra tatra caturvaktrā rudrā nārāyaṇādayaḥ ।।
daśottaramathaikaikamaṇḍāvaraṇasaptakam । samantāt saṃsthitaṃ viprā yatra yānti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। anantamekamavyaktanādinidhanaṃ mahat । atītya vartate sarvaṃ jagat prakṛtirakṣaram ।।
anantatvamanantasya yataḥ saṃkhyā na vidyate । tadavyaktamiti jñeyaṃ tad brahma paramaṃ padam ।। ananta eṣa sarvatra sarvasthāneṣu paṭhyate । tasya pūrvaṃ mayāpyuktaṃ yattanmāhātmyamavyayam ।।
gataḥ sa eṣa sarvatra sarvasthāneṣu vartate । bhūmau rasātale caiva ākāśe pavane anale । arṇaveṣu ca sarveṣu divi caiva na saśayaḥ ।। tathā tamasi sattve ca eṣa eva mahādyutiḥ ।
anekadhā vibhaktāṅgaḥ krīḍate puruṣottamaḥ ।। maheśvaraḥ paro avyaktādaṇḍamavyaktasaṃbhavam । aṇḍād brahmā samutpannastena sṛṣṭamidaṃ jagat ।। atītānāgatānīha yāni manvantarāṇi tu ।
tāni tvaṃ kathayāsmākaṃ vyāsāṃśca dvāpare yuge ।। vedaśākhāpraṇayanaṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ । tathāvatārān dharmārthamīśānasya kalau yuge ।। kiyanto devadevasya śiṣyāḥ kaliyugeṣu vai ।
etat sarvaṃ samāsena sūta vaktumihārhasi ।। manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvaṃ tataḥ svārociṣo manuḥ । uttamastāmasaścaiva raivataścākṣuṣastathā ।। ṣaḍete manavo atītāḥ sāṃprataṃ tu raveḥ sutaḥ ।
vaivasvato ayaṃ yasyaitat saptamaṃ vartate antaram ।। svāyaṃbhuvaṃ tu kathitaṃ kalpādāvantaraṃ mayā । ata ūrdhvaṃ nibodhadhvaṃ manoḥ svārociṣasya tu ।। pārāvatāśca tuṣitā devāḥ svārociṣe antare ।
vipaścinnāma devendro babhūvāsurasūdanaḥ ।। ūrjastambhastathā prāṇo dānto atha vṛṣabhastathā । timiraścārvarīvāṃśca sapta saptarṣayo abhavan ।। caitrakiṃpuruṣādyāśca sutāḥ svārociṣasya tu ।
dvitīyamatadākhyātamantaraṃ śṛṇu cottaram ।। tṛtīye apyantare viprā uttamo nāma vai manuḥ । suśāntistatra devendro babhūvāmitrakarṣaṇaḥ ।। sudhāmānastathā satyāḥ śivāścātha pratardanāḥ ।
vaśavartinaśca pañcaite gaṇā dvādaśakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। rajordhvaścordhvabāhuśca sabalaścānayastathā । sutapāḥ śukra ityete sapta saptarṣayo abhavan ।। tāmasasyāntare devāḥ surā vāharayastathā ।
satyāśca sudhiyaścaiva saptaviṃśatikā gaṇāḥ ।। śibirindrastathaivāsīcchatayajñopalakṣaṇaḥ । babhūva śaṅkare bhakto mahādevārcane rataḥ ।। jyotirdharmā pṛthuḥ kāvyaścaitrognirvanakastathā ।
pīvarastvṛṣayo hyete sapta tatrāpi cāntare ।। pañcame cāpi viprendrā raivato nāma nāmataḥ । manurvasuśca tatrendro babhūvāsuramardanaḥ ।। amitābhā bhūtarayā vaikuṇṭhāḥ svacchamedhasaḥ ।
ete devagaṇāstatra caturdaśa caturdaśa ।। hiraṇyaromā vedaśrīrūrdhvabāhustathaiva ca । vedabāhuḥ sudhāmā ca parjanyaśca mahāmuniḥ । ete saptarṣayo viprāstatrāsan raivate antare ।।
svārociṣaścottamaśca tāmaso raivatastathā । priyavratānvayā hyete catvāro manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhe manvantare cāsīccākṣuṣastu manurdvijāḥ । manojavastathaivendro devānapi nibodhataḥ ।।
ādyāḥ prasūtā bhāvyāśca pṛthugāśca divaukasaḥ । mahānubhāvā lekhyāśca pañcaite hyaṣṭakā gaṇāḥ ।। sumedhā virajāścaiva haviṣmānuttamo madhuḥ । atināmā sahiṣṇuśca saptāsannṛṣayaḥ śubhāḥ ।।
vivasvataḥ suto viprāḥ śrāddhadevo mahādyutiḥ । manuḥ sa vartate dhīmān sāṃprataṃ saptame antare ।। ādityā vasavo rudrā devāstatra marudgaṇāḥ । purandarastathaivendro babhūva paravīrahā ।।
vasiṣṭhaḥ kaśyapaścātrirjamadagniśca gautamaḥ । viśvāmitro bharadvājaḥ sapta saptarṣayo abhavan ।। viṣṇuśaktiranaupamyā sattvodriktā sthitā sthitau । tadaṃśabhūtā rājānaḥ sarve ca tridivaukasaḥ ।।
svāyaṃbhuve antare pūrvamākūtyāṃ mānasaḥ sutaḥ । ruceḥ prajāpateryajñastadaṃśenābhavad dvijāḥ ।। tataḥ punarasau devaḥ prāpte svārociṣe antare । tuṣitāyāṃ samutpannastuṣitaiḥ saha daivataiḥ ।।
auttame apyantare viṣṇuḥ satyaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ । satyāyāmabhavat satyaḥ satyarūpo janārdanaḥ ।। tāmasasyāntare caiva saṃprāpte punareva hi । haryāyāṃ haribhirdevairharirevābhavaddhariḥ ।।
raivate apyantare caiva saṃbhūtyāṃ mānaso abhavat । saṃbhūto mānasaiḥ sārdhaṃ devaiḥ saha mahādyutiḥ ।। cākṣuṣe apyantare caiva vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ । vikuṇṭhāyāmasau jajñe vaikuṇṭhairdaivataiḥ saha ।।
manvantare atra saṃprāpte tathā vaivasvate antare । vāmanaḥ kaśyapād viṣṇuradityāṃ saṃbabhūva ha ।। tribhiḥ kramairimāṃllokāñjitvā yena mahātmanā । purandarāya trailokyaṃ dattaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam ।।
ityetāstanavastasya sapta manvantareṣu vai । sapta caivābhavan viprā yābhiḥ saṃrakṣitāḥ prajāḥ ।। yasmād viṣṭamidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ vāmanena mahātmanā । tasmāt sa vai smṛto viṣṇurviśerdhātoḥ praveśanāt ।।
eṣa sarvaṃ sṛjatyādau pāti hanti ca keśavaḥ । bhūtāntarātmā bhagavān nārāyaṇa iti śrutiḥ ।। ekāṃśena jagat sarvaṃ vyāpya nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ । caturdhā saṃsthito vyāpī saguṇo nirguṇo api ca ।।
ekā bhagavato mūrtirjñānarūpā śivāmalā । vāsudevābhidhānā sā guṇātītā suniṣkalā ।। dvitīyā kālasaṃjñānyā tāmasī śeṣasaṃjñitā । nihanti sakalaṃ cānte vaiṣṇavī paramā tanuḥ ।।
sattvodriktā tathaivānyā pradyumneti ca saṃjñitā । jagat sthāpayate sarvaṃ sa viṣṇuḥ prakṛtirdhruvā ।। caturtho vāsudevasya mūrtirbrāhmīti saṃjñitā । rājasī cāniruddhākhyā pradyumnaḥ sṛṣṭikārikā ।।
yaḥ svapityakhilaṃ bhūtvā pradyumnena saha prabhuḥ । nārāyaṇākhyo brahmāsau prijāsargaṃ karoti saḥ ।। yā sā nārāyaṇatanuḥ pradyumnākhyā munīśvarāḥ । tayā saṃmohayed viśvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।।
saiva sarvajagatsūtiḥ prakṛtiḥ parikīrtitā । vāsudevo hyanantātmā kevalo nirguṇo hariḥ ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣaḥ kālastattvatrayamanuttamam । vāsudevātmakaṃ nityametad vijñāya mucyate ।।
ekaṃ cedaṃ catuṣpādaṃ caturdhā punaracyutaḥ । bibheda vāsudevo asau pradyumno hariravyayaḥ ।। kṛṣṇadvaipāyano vyāso viṣṇurnārāyaṇaḥ svayam । apāntaratamāḥ pūrvaṃ svecchayā hyabhavaddhariḥ ।।
anādyantaṃ paraṃ brahma na devā narṣayo viduḥ । eko ayaṃ veda bhagavān vyāso nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। ityetad viṣṇumāhātmyamuktaṃ vo munipuṅgavāḥ । etat satyaṃ punaḥ satyamevaṃ jñātvā na muhyati ।।
asmin manvantare pūrvaṃ vartamāne mahān vibhuḥ । dvāpare prathame vyāso manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo mataḥ ।। bibheda bahudhā vedaṃ niyogād brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ । dvitīye dvāpare caiva vedavyāsaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
tṛtīye cośanā vyāsaścaturthe syād bṛhaspatiḥ । savitā pañcame vyāsaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। saptame ca tathaivendro vasiṣṭhaścāṣṭame mataḥ । sārasvataśca navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ ।।
ekādaśe tu trivṛṣaḥ śatatejāstataḥ paraḥ । trayodaśe tathā dharmastarakṣustu caturdaśe ।। tryāruṇirvai pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśe tu dhanañjayaḥ । kṛtañjayaḥ saptadaśe hyaṣṭādaśe ṛtañjayaḥ ।।
tato vyāso bharadvājastasmādūrdhvaṃ tu gautamaḥ । rājaśravāścaikaviṃśastasmācchuṣmāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ।। tṛṇabindustrayoviṃśe vālmīkistatparaḥ smṛtaḥ । pañcaviśe tathā śaktiḥ ṣaḍviṃśe tu parāśaraḥ ।।
saptaviṃśe tathā vyāso jātūkarṇo mahāmuniḥ । aṣṭāviṃśe punaḥ prāpte hyasmin vai dvāpare dvijāḥ । parāśarasuto vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano abhavat ।। sa eva sarvavedānāṃ purāṇānāṃ pradarśakaḥ ।
pārāśaryo mahāyogī kṛṣṇadvaipāyano hariḥ ।। ārādhya devamīśānaṃ dṛṣṭvā sāmbaṃ trilocanam । tatprasādādasau vyāsaṃ vedānāmakarot prabhuḥ ।। atha śiṣyān prijagrāha caturo vedapāragān ।
jaiminiṃ ca sumantuṃ ca vaiśampāyanameva ca । pailaṃ teṣāṃ caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ māṃ mahāmuniḥ ।। ṛgvedaśrāvakaṃ pailaṃ jagrāha sa mahāmuniḥ । yajurvedapravaktāraṃ vaiśampāyanameva ca ।।
jaiminiṃ sāmavedasya śrāvakaṃ sonvapadyata । tathaivātharvavedasya sumantumṛṣisattamam । itihāsapurāṇāni pravaktuṃ māmayojayat ।। eka āsīdyajurvedastaṃ caturdhā vyakalpayat ।
cāturhetramabhūd yasmiṃstena yajñamathākarot ।। ādhvaryavaṃ yajurbhiḥ syādṛgbhirhetraṃ dvijottamāḥ । audgātraṃ sāmabhiścakre brahmatvaṃ cāpyatharvabhiḥ ।। tataḥ sa ṛca uddhṛtya ṛgvedaṃ kṛtavān prabhuḥ ।
yajūṃṣi ca yajurvedaṃ sāmavedaṃ ca sāmabhiḥ ।। ekaviṃśatibhedena ṛgvedaṃ kṛtavān purā । śākhānāṃ tu śatenaiva yajurvedamathākarot ।। sāmavedaṃ sahastreṇa śākhānāṃ prabibheda saḥ ।
atharvāṇamatho vedaṃ bibheda navakena tu ।। bhedairaṣṭādaśairvyāsaḥ purāṇaṃ kṛtavān prabhuḥ । so ayamekaścatuṣpādo vedaḥ pūrvaṃ purātanāt ।। oṅkāro brahmaṇo jātaḥ sarvadoṣaviśodhanaḥ ।
vedavedyo hi bhagavān vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। sa gīyate paro vede yo vedainaṃ sa vedavit । etat parataraṃ brahma jyotirānandamuttamam ।। vedavākyoditaṃ tattvaṃ vāsudevaḥ paraṃ padam ।
vedavedyamimaṃ vetti vedaṃ vedaparo muniḥ ।। avedaṃ paramaṃ vetti vedaniṣṭhaḥ sadeśvaraḥ । sa vedavedyo bhagavān vedamūrtirmaheśvaraḥ । sa eva vedo vedyaśca tamevāśritya mucyate ।।
ityedakṣaraṃ vedyamoṅkāraṃ vedamavyayam । avedaṃ ca vijānāti pārāśaryo mahāmuniḥ ।। vedavyāsāvatārāṇi dvāpare kathitāni tu । mahādevāvatārāṇi kalau śṛṇuta suvratāḥ ।।
ādye kaliyuge śveto devadevo mahādyutiḥ । nāmnā hitāya viprāṇāmabhūd vaivasvate antare ।। himavacchikhare ramye chagale parvatottame । tasya śiṣyāḥ śikhāyuktā vabhūvuramitaprabhāḥ ।।
śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ । catvāraste mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ ।। subhāno damanaścātha suhotraḥ kaṅkaṇastathā । lokākṣiratha yogīndro jaigīṣavyastu saptame ।।
aṣṭame dadhivāhaḥ syānnavame vṛṣabhaḥ prabhuḥ । bhṛgustu daśame proktastasmādugraḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। dvādaśe atriḥ samākhyāto balī cātha trayodaśe । caturdaśe gautamastu vedaśīrṣā tataḥ param ।।
gokarṇaścābhavat tasmād guhāvāsaḥ śikhaṇḍyatha । jaṭāmālyaṭṭahāsaśca dāruko lāṅgalī kramāt ।। śvetastathā paraḥ śūlī ḍiṇḍī muṇḍī ca vai kramāt । sahiṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca nakulīśo antime prabhuḥ ।।
vaivasvate antare śaṃbhoravatārāstriśūlinaḥ । aṣṭāviṃśatirākhyātā hyante kaliyuge prabhoḥ । tīrthe kāyāvatāre syād deveśo nakulīśvaraḥ ।। tatra devādidevasya catvāraḥ sutapodhanāḥ ।
śiṣyā babhūvuścānyeṣāṃ pratyekaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। prasannamanaso dāntā aiśvarīṃ bhaktimāśritāḥ । krameṇa tān pravakṣyāmi yogino yogavittamān ।। śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ ।
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaśca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃstathā । vikeśaśca viśokaśca viśāpaśśāpanāśanaḥ ।। sumukho durmukhaścaiva durdamo duratikramaḥ । sanaḥ sanātanaścaiva mukāraśca sanandanaḥ ।।
dālabhyaśca mahāyogī dharmātmano mahaujasaḥ । sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhapātraja eva ca ।। sārasvatastathā megho ghanavāhaḥ suvāhanaḥ । kapilaścāsuriścaiva voḍhuḥ pañcaśikho muniḥ ।।
parāśaraśca gargaśca bhārgavaścāṅgirāstathā । balabandhurnirāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgastapodhanaḥ ।। lambodaraśca lambaśca lāmbākṣo lambakeśakaḥ । sarvajñaḥ samabuddhiśca sādhyaḥ satyastathaiva ca ।।
śudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vasiṣṭho virajāstathā । atrirugrastathā caiva śravaṇo atha śraviṣṭhakaḥ ।। kuṇiśca kuṇibāhuśca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ । kaśyapohyuśanā caiva cyavano atha bṛhaspatiḥ ।।
utathyo vāmadevaśca mahākāyo mahānilaḥ । vācaśravāḥ supīkaśca śyāvāśvaḥ sapathīśvaraḥ ।। hariṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo lokākṣiḥ kuthumistathā । sumanturvarcarī vidvān kabandhaḥ kuśikandharaḥ ।।
plakṣo dārbhāyaṇiścaiva ketumān gautamastathā । bhallāpī madhupiṅgaśca śvetaketustaponidhiḥ ।। uśijo bṛhadukthaśca devalaḥ kapireva ca । śālihotro agniveśyaśca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ ।।
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaśca kumbhaścaiva pravāhakaḥ । ulūko vidyutaścaiva śādvalo hyāśvalāyanaḥ ।। akṣapādaḥ kumāraśca ulūko vatsa eva ca । kuśikaścaiva gargaśca mitrako ṛṣya eva ca ।।
śiṣyā ete mahātmānaḥ sarvovarteṣu yoginām । vimalā brahmabhūyiṣṭhā jñānayogaparāyaṇāḥ ।। kurvanti cāvatārāṇi brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya hi । yogeśvarāṇāmādeśād vedasaṃsthāpanāya vai ।।
ye brāhmaṇāḥ saṃsmaranti namasyanti ca sarvadā । tarpayantyarcayantyetān brahmavidyāmavāpnuyuḥ ।। idaṃ vaivasvataṃ proktamantaraṃ vistareṇa tu । bhaviṣyati ca sāvarṇo dakṣasāvarṇa eva ca ।।
daśamo brahmasāvarṇo dharmasāvarṇa eva ca । dvādaśo rudrasāvarṇo rocamānastrayodaśaḥ । bhautyaścaturdaśaḥ prokto bhaviṣyā manavaḥ kramāt ।। ayaṃ vaḥ kathito hyaṃśaḥ pūrvo nārāyaṇeritaḥ ।
bhūtabhavyairvartamānairākhyānairupabṛṃhitaḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi śrāvayed vā dvijottamān । sa sarvapāpanirmukto brahmaṇā saha modate ।। paṭhed devālaye snātvā nadītīreṣu caiva hi ।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya bhāvena puruṣottamam ।। namo devādidevāya devānāṃ paramātmane । puruṣāya purāṇāya viṣṇave kūrmarūpiṇe ।। bhavatā kathitaḥ samyak sargaḥ svāyaṃbhuvastataḥ ।
brahmāṇḍasyāsya vistāro manvantaraviniścayaḥ ।। tatreśvareśvaro devo varṇibhirdharmatatparaiḥ । jñānayogaratairnityamārādhyaḥ kathitastvayā ।। tadvadāśeṣasaṃsāraduḥ khanāśamanuttamam ।
jñānaṃ brahmaikaviṣayaṃ yena paśyema tatparam ।। tvaṃ hi nārāyaṇātsākṣāt kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāt prabho । avāptākhilavijñānastattvāṃ pṛcchāmahe punaḥ ।। śrutvā munīnāṃ tad vākyaṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ prabhum ।
sūtaḥ paurāṇikaḥ smṛtvā bhāṣituṃ hyupacakrame ।। athāsminnantare vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ svayam । ājagāma muniśreṣṭhā yatra satraṃ samāsate ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā vedavidvāṃsaṃ kālameghasamadyutim ।
vyāsaṃ kamalapatrākṣaṃ praṇemurdvijapuṅgavāḥ ।। papāta daṇḍavad bhūmau dṛṣṭvāsau romaharṣaṇaḥ । pradakṣiṇīkṛtya guruṃ prāñjaliḥ pārśvago abhavat ।। pṛṣṭāste anāmayaṃ viprāḥ śaunakādyā mahāmunim ।
samāśvāsyāsanaṃ tasmai tadyogyaṃ samakalpayan ।। athaitānabravīd vākyaṃ parāśarasutaḥ prabhuḥ । kaccinna tapaso hāniḥ svādhyāyasya śrutasya ca ।। tataḥ sa sūtaḥ svaguruṃ praṇamyāha mahāmunim ।
jñānaṃ tad brahmaviṣayaṃ munīnāṃ vaktumarhasi ।। ime hi munayaḥ śāntāstāpasā dharmatatparāḥ । śuśrūṣā jāyate caiṣāṃ vaktumarhasi tattvataḥ ।। jñānaṃ vimuktidaṃ divyaṃ yanme sākṣāt tvayoditam ।
munīnāṃ vyāhṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ viṣṇunā kūrmarūpiṇā ।। śrutvā sūtasya vacanaṃ muniḥ satyavatīsutaḥ । praṇamya śirasā rudraṃ vacaḥ prāha sukhāvaham ।। vakṣye devo mahādevaḥ pṛṣṭo yogīśvaraiḥ purā ।
sanatkumārapramukhaiḥ svayaṃ yatsamabhāṣata ।। sanatkumāraḥ sanakastathaiva ca sanandanaḥ । aṅgirā rudrasahito bhṛguḥ paramadharmavit ।। kaṇādaḥ kapilo yogī vāmadevo mahāmuniḥ ।
śukro vasiṣṭho bhagavān sarve saṃyatamānasāḥ ।। parasparaṃ vicāryaite saṃśayāviṣṭacetasaḥ । taptavantastapo ghoraṃ puṇye badarikāśrame ।। apaśyaṃste mahāyogamṛṣiṃ dharmasutaṃ śucim ।
nārāyaṇamanādyantaṃ nareṇa sahitaṃ tadā ।। saṃstūya vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ sarve vedasamudbhavaiḥ । praṇemurbhaktisaṃyuktā yogino yogavittamam ।। vijñāya vāñchitaṃ teṣāṃ bhagavānapi sarvavit ।
prāha gambhīrayā vācā kimarthaṃ tapyate tapaḥ ।। abruvan hṛṣṭamanaso viśvātmānaṃ sanātanam । sākṣānnārāyaṇaṃ devamāgataṃ siddhisūcakam ।। vayaṃ saṃśayamāpannāḥ sarve vai brahmavādinaḥ ।
bhavantamekaṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannāḥ puruṣottamam ।। tvaṃ hi tad vettha paramaṃ sarvajño bhagavānṛṣiḥ । nārāyaṇaḥ svayaṃ sākṣāt purāṇo avyaktapūruṣaḥ ।। nahyanyo vidyate vettā tvāmṛte parameśvara ।
śuśrūṣāsmākamakhilaṃ saṃśayaṃ chettumarhasi ।। kiṃ kāraṇamidaṃ kṛtsnaṃ ko anusaṃsarate sadā । kaścidātmā ca kā muktiḥ saṃsāraḥ kiṃnimittakaḥ ।। kaḥ saṃsārayatīśānaḥ ko vā sarvaṃ prapaśyati ।
kiṃ tat parataraṃ brahma sarvaṃ no vaktumarhasi ।। evamukte tu munayaḥ prāpaśyan puruṣottamam । vihāya tāpasaṃ rūpaṃ saṃsthitaṃ svena tejasā ।। vibhrājamānaṃ vimalaṃ prabhāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitam ।
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ devaṃ taptajāmbūnadaprabham ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ śārṅgahastaṃ śriyāvṛtam । na dṛṣṭastatkṣaṇādeva narastasyaiva tejasā ।। tadantare mahādevaḥ śaśāṅkāṅkitaśekharaḥ ।
prasādābhimukho rudraḥ prādurāsīnmaheśvaraḥ ।। nirīkṣya te jagannāthaṃ trinetraṃ candrabhūṣaṇam । tuṣṭuvurhṛṣṭamanaso bhaktyā taṃ parameśvaram ।। jayeśvara mahādeva jaya bhūtapate śiva ।
jayāśeṣamunīśāna tapasābhiprapūjita ।। sahasramūrte viśvātman jagadyantrapravartaka । jayānanta jagajjanmatrāṇasaṃhārakāraṇa ।। sahasracaraṇeśāna śaṃbho yogīndravandita ।
jayāmbikāpate deva namaste parameśvara ।। saṃstuto bhagavānīśastryambako bhaktavatsalaḥ । samāliṅgya hṛṣīkeśaṃ prāha gambhīrayā girā ।। kimarthaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa munīndrā brahmavādinaḥ ।
imaṃ samāgatā deśaṃ kiṃ vā kāryaṃ mayācyuta ।। ākarṇya bhagavadvākyaṃ devadevo janārdanaḥ । prāha devo mahādevaṃ prasādābhimukhaṃ sthitam ।। ime hi munayo deva tāpasāḥ kṣīṇakalmaṣāḥ ।
abhyāgatā māṃ śaraṇaṃ samyagdarśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। yadi prasanno bhagavān munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām । sannidhau mama tajjñānaṃ divyaṃ vaktumihārhasi ।। tvaṃ hi vettha svamātmānaṃ na hyanyo vidyate śiva ।
tatastvamātmanātmānaṃ munīndrebhyaḥ pradarśaya ।। evamuktvā hṛṣīkeśaḥ provāca munipuṅgavān । pradarśayan yogasiddhiṃ nirīkṣya vṛṣabhadhvajam ।। saṃdarśanānmaheśasya śaṅkarasyātha śūlinaḥ ।
kṛtārthaṃ svayamātmānaṃ jñātumarhatha tattvataḥ ।। praṣṭumarhatha viśveśaṃ pratyakṣaṃ purataḥ sthitam । mamaiva sannidhāveṣa yathāvad vaktumīśvaraḥ ।। niśamya viṣṇuvacanaṃ praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam ।
sanatkumārapramukhāḥ pṛcchanti sma maheśvaram ।। athāsminnantare divyamāsanaṃ vimalaṃ śivam । kimapyacintyaṃ gaganādīśvarārhaṃ samudbabhau ।। tatrāsasāda yogātmā viṣṇunā saha viśvakṛt ।
tejasā pūrayan viśvaṃ bhāti devo maheśvaraḥ ।। taṃ te devādideveśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ brahmavādinaḥ । vibhrājamānaṃ vimale tasmin dadṛśurāsane ।। yaṃ prapaśyantiyogasthāḥ svātmanyātmānamīśvaramā ।
ananyatejasaṃ śāntaṃ śivaṃ dadṛśire kila ।। yataḥ prasūtirbhūtānāṃ yatraitat pravilīyate । tamāsanasthaṃ bhūtānāmīśaṃ dadṛśire kila ।। yadantarā sarvametad yato abhinnamidaṃ jagat ।
sa vāsudevamāsīnaṃ tamīśaṃ dadṛśuḥ kila ।। provāca pṛṣṭo bhagavān munīnāṃ parameśvaraḥ । nirīkṣya puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ svātmayogamanuttamam ।। tacchṛṇudhvaṃ yathānyāyamucyamānaṃ mayānaghāḥ ।
praśāntamānasāḥ sarve jñānamīśvarabhāṣitam ।। avācyametad vijñānamātmaguhyaṃ sanātanam । yanna devā vijānanti yatanto api dvijātayaḥ ।। idaṃ jñānaṃ samāśritya brahmabhūtā dvijottamāḥ ।
na saṃsāraṃ prapadyante pūrve api brahmavādinaḥ ।। guhyād guhyatamaṃ sākṣād gopanīyaṃ prayatnataḥ । vakṣye bhaktimatāmadya yuṣmākaṃ brahmavādinām ।। ātmāyaḥ kevalaḥ svasthaḥ śāntaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।
asti sarvāntaraḥ sākṣāccinmātrastamasaḥ paraḥ ।। so antaryāmī sa puruṣaḥ sa prāṇaḥ sa maheśvaraḥ । sa kālo agnistadavyaktaṃ sa evedamiti śrutiḥ ।। asmād vijāyate viśvamatraiva pravilīyate ।
sa māyī māyayā baddhaḥ karoti vividhāstanūḥ ।। na cāpyayaṃ saṃsarati na ca saṃsārayet prabhuḥ । nāyaṃ pṛthvī na salilaṃ na tejaḥ pavano nabhaḥ ।। na prāṇe na mano avyaktaṃ na śabdaḥ sparśa eva ca ।
na rūparasagandhāśca nāhaṃ kartā na vāgapi ।। na pāṇipādau no pāyurna copasthaṃ dvijottamāḥ । na kartā na ca bhoktā vā na ca prakṛtipūruṣau । na māyā naiva ca prāścaitanyaṃ paramārthataḥ ।।
yathā prakāśatamasoḥ sambandho nopapadyate । tadvadaikyaṃ na saṃbandhaḥ prapañcaparamātmanoḥ ।। chāyātapau yathā loke parasparavilakṣaṇau । tadvat prapañcapuruṣau vibhinnau paramārthataḥ ।।
yadyātmā malino asvastho vikārī syāt svabhāvataḥ । nahi tasya bhavenmuktirjanmāntaraśatairapi ।। paśyanti munayo yuktāḥ svātmānaṃ paramārthataḥ । vikārahīnaṃ nirduḥ khamānandātmānamavyayam ।।
ahaṃ kartā sukhī duḥ khī kṛśaḥ sthūleti yā matiḥ । sā cāhaṅkārakartṛtvādātmanyāropyate janaiḥ ।। vadanti vedavidvāṃsaḥ sākṣiṇaṃ prakṛteḥ param । bhoktāramakṣaraṃ śuddhaṃ sarvatra samavasthitam ।।
tasmādajñānamūlo hi saṃsāraḥ sarvadehinām । ajñānādanyathā jñānaṃ tacca prakṛtisaṃgatam ।। nityoditaḥ svayaṃ jyotiḥ sarvagaḥ puruṣaḥ paraḥ । ahaṅkārāvivekena kartāhamiti manyate ।।
paśyanti ṛṣayo avyaktaṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmakam । pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ buddhvā kāraṇaṃ brahmavādinaḥ ।। tenāyaṃ saṃgato hyātmā kūṭastho api nirañjanaḥ । svātmānamakṣaraṃ brahma nāvabuddhyeta tattvataḥ ।।
anātmanyātmavijñānaṃ tasmād duḥ khaṃ tathetaram । ragadveṣādayo doṣāḥ sarve bhrāntinibandhanāḥ ।। karmaṇyasya bhaved doṣaḥ puṇyāpuṇyamiti sthitiḥ । tadvaśādeva sarveṣāṃ sarvadehasamudbhavaḥ ।।
nityaḥ sarvatrago hyātmā kūṭastho doṣavarjitaḥ । ekaḥ sa bhidyate śaktyā māyayā na svabhāvataḥ ।। tasmādadvaitamevāhurmunayaḥ paramārthataḥ । bhedo vyaktasvabhāvena sā ca māyātmasaṃśrayā ।।
yathā hi dhūmasaṃparkānnākāśo malino bhavet । antaḥ karaṇajairbhāvairātmā tadvanna lipyate ।। yathā svaprabhayā bhāti kevalaḥ sphaṭiko amalaḥ । upādhihīno vimalastathaivātmā prakāśate ।।
jñānasvūpamevāhurjagadetad vicakṣaṇāḥ । arthasvarūpamevājñāḥ paśyantyanye kudṛṣṭayaḥ ।। kūṭastho nirguṇo vyāpī caitanyātmā svabhāvataḥ । dṛśyate hyartharūpeṇa puruṣairbhrāntidṛṣṭibhiḥ ।।
yathā saṃlakṣyate raktaḥ kevalaḥ sphaṭiko janaiḥ । raktikādyupadhānena tadvat paramapūruṣaḥ ।। tasmādātmākṣaraḥ śuddho nityaḥ sarvagato avyayaḥ । upāsitavyo mantavyaḥ śrotavyaśca mumukṣubhiḥ ।।
yadā manasi caitanyaṃ bhāti sarvatragaṃ sadā । yogino avyavadhānena tadā saṃpadyate svayam ।। yadā sarvāṇi būtāni svātmanyevābhipaśyati । sarvabhūteṣu cātmānaṃ brahma saṃpadyate tadā ।।
yadā sarvāṇi bhūtāni samādhistho na paśyati । ekībhūtaḥ pareṇāsau tadā bhavati kevalaḥ ।। yadā sarve pramucyante kāmā ye asya hṛdi sthitāḥ । tadāsāvamṛtībhūtaḥ kṣemaṃ gacchati paṇḍitaḥ ।।
yadā bhūtapṛthagbhāvamekasthamanupaśyati । tata eva ca vistāraṃ brahma saṃpadyate tadā ।। yadā paśyati cātmānaṃ kevalaṃ paramārthataḥ । māyāmātraṃ jagat kṛtsnaṃ tadā bhavati nirvṛtaḥ ।।
yadā janmajarāduḥ khavyādhīnāmekabheṣajam । kevalaṃ brahmavijñānaṃ jāyate asau tadā śivaḥ ।। yathā nadīnadā loke sāgareṇaikatāṃ yayuḥ । tadvadātmākṣareṇāsau niṣkalenaikatāṃ vrajet ।।
tasmād vijñānamevāsti na prapañco na saṃsṛtiḥ । ajñānenāvṛtaṃ loko vijñānaṃ tena muhyati ।। tajjñānaṃ nirmalaṃ sūkṣmaṃ nirvikalpaṃ yadavyayam । ajñānamitarat sarvaṃ vijñānamiti me matam ।।
etad vaḥ paramaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ bhāṣitaṃ jñānamuttamam । sarvavedāntasāraṃ hi yogastatraikacittatā ।। yogāt saṃjāyate jñānaṃ jñānād yogaḥ pravartate । yogajñānābhiyuktasya nāvāpyaṃ vidyate kvacit ।।
yadeva yogino yānti sāṃkhyaistadadhigamyate । ekaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca yaḥ paśyati sa tattvavit ।। anye ca yogino viprā aiśvaryāsaktacetasaḥ । majjanti tatra tatraiva na tvātmaiṣāmiti śrutiḥ ।।
yattat sarvagataṃ divyamaiśvaryamacalaṃ mahat । jñānayogābhiyuktastu dehānte tadavāpnuyāt ।। eṣa ātmāhamavyakto māyāvī parameśvaraḥ । kīrtitaḥ sarvavedeṣu sarvātmā sarvatomukhaḥ ।।
sarvakāmaḥ sarvarasaḥ sarvagandho ajaro amaraḥ । sarvataḥ pāṇipādo ahamantaryāmī sanātanaḥ ।। apāṇipādo javano grahītā hṛdi saṃsthitaḥ । acakṣurapi paśyāmi tathākarṇaḥ śṛṇomyaham ।।
vedāhaṃ sarvamevedaṃ na māṃ jānāti kaścana । prāhurmahāntaṃ puruṣaṃ māmekaṃ tattvadarśinaḥ ।। paśyanti ṛṣayo hetumātmanaḥ sūkṣmadarśinaḥ । nirguṇāmalarūpasya yattadaiśvaryamuttamam ।।
yanna devā vijānanti mohitā mama māyayā । vakṣye samāhitā yūyaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ brahmavādinaḥ ।। nāhaṃ praśāstā sarvasya māyātītaḥ svabhāvataḥ । prerayāmi tathāpīdaṃ kāraṇaṃ sūrayo viduḥ ।।
yanme guhyatamaṃ dehaṃ sarvagaṃ tattvadarśinaḥ । praviṣṭā mama sāyujyaṃ labhante yogino avyayam ।। teṣāṃ hi vaśamāpannā māyā me viśvarūpiṇī । labhante paramāṃ śuddhiṃ nirvāṇaṃ te mayā saha ।।
na teṣāṃ punarāvṛttiḥ kalpakoṭiśatairapi । prasādānmama yogīndrā etad vedānuśāsanam ।। nāputraśiṣyayogibhyo dātavyaṃ brahmavādibhiḥ । maduktametad vijñānaṃ sāṃkhyayogasamāśrayam ।।
avyaktādabhavat kālaḥ pradhānaṃ puruṣaḥ paraḥ । tebhyaḥ sarvamidaṃ jātaṃ tasmād brahmamayaṃ jagat ।। sarvataḥ pāṇipādaṃ tat sarvato akṣiśiromukham । sarvataḥ śrutimalloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।।
sarvendriyaguṇābhāsaṃ sarvendriyavivarjitam । sarvādhāraṃ sadānandamavyaktaṃ dvaitavarjitam ।। sarvopamānarahitaṃ pramāṇātītagocaram । nirvikalpaṃ nirābhāsaṃ sarvāvāsaṃ parāmṛtam ।।
abhinnaṃ bhinnasaṃsthānaṃ śāśvataṃ dhru vamavyayam । nirguṇaṃ paramaṃ vyoma tajjñānaṃ sūrayo viduḥ ।। sa ātmā sarvabhūtānāṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ paraḥ । so ahaṃ sarvatragaḥ śānto jñānātmā parameśvaraḥ ।।
mayā tatamidaṃ viśvaṃ jagadavyaktamūrtinā । matsthāni sarvabhūtāni yastaṃ veda sa vedavit ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ caiva tattvadvayamudāhṛtam । tayoranādiruddiṣṭaḥ kālaḥ saṃyojakaḥ paraḥ ।।
trayametadanādyantamavyakte samavasthitam । tadātmakaṃ tadanyat syāt tadrūpaṃ māmakaṃ viduḥ ।। mahadādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ saṃprasūte akhilaṃ jagat । yā sā prakṛtiruddiṣṭā mohinī sarvadehinām ।।
puruṣaḥ prakṛtistho hi bhuṅkteyaḥ prākṛtān guṇān । ahaṅkāravimuktatvāt procyate pañcaviṃśakaḥ ।। ādyo vikāraḥ prakṛtermahānātmeti kathyate । vijñānaśaktirvijñātā hyahaṅkārastadutthitaḥ ।।
eka eva mahānātmā so ahaṅkāro abhidhīyate । sa jīvaḥ so antarātmeti gīyate tattvacintakaiḥ ।। tena vedayate sarvaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca janmasu । sa vijñānātmakastasya manaḥ syādupakārakam ।।
tenāvivekatastasmāt saṃsāraḥ puruṣasya tu । sa cāvivekaḥ prakṛtau saṅgāt kālena so abhavat ।। kālaḥ sṛjati bhūtāni kālaḥ saṃharati prajāḥ । sarve kālasya vaśagā na kālaḥ kasyacid vaśe ।।
so antarā sarvamevedaṃ niyacchati sanātanaḥ । procyate bhagavān prāṇaḥ sarvajñaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। sarvendriyebhyaḥ paramaṃ mana āhurmanīṣiṇaḥ । manasaścāpyahaṅkāramahaṅkārānmahān paraḥ ।।
mahataḥ paramavyaktamavyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ । puruṣād bhagavān prāṇastasya sarvamidaṃ jagat ।। prāṇāt parataraṃ vyoma vyomātīto agnirīśvaraḥ । so ahaṃ sarvatragaḥ śānto jñānātmā parameśvaraḥ ।
nāsti mattaḥ paraṃ bhūtaṃ māṃ vijñāya vimucyate ।। nityaṃ hi nāsti jagati bhūtaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam । ṛte māmekamavyaktaṃ vyomarūpaṃ maheśvaram ।। so ahaṃ sṛjāmi sakalaṃ saṃharāmi sadā jagat ।
māyī māyāmayo devaḥ kālena saha saṅgataḥ ।। matsannidhāveṣa kālaḥ karoti sakalaṃ jagat । niyojayatyanantātmā hyetad vedānuśāsanam ।। vakṣye samāhitā yūyaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ brahmavādinaḥ ।
māhātmyaṃ devadevasya yenedaṃ saṃpravartate ।। nāhaṃ tapobhirvividhairna dānena na cejyayā । śakyo hi puruṣairjñātumṛte bhaktimanuttamām ।। ahaṃ hi sarvabhāvānāmantastiṣṭhāmi sarvagaḥ ।
māṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ loko na jānāti munīśvarāḥ ।। yasyāntarā sarvamidaṃ yo hi sarvāntaraḥ paraḥ । so ahandhātā vidhātā ca kālo agnirviśvatomukhaḥ ।। na māṃ paśyanti munayaḥ sarve api tridivaukasaḥ ।
brahmā ca manavaḥ śakro ye cānye prathitaujasaḥ ।। gṛṇanti satataṃ vedā māmekaṃ parameśvaram । yajanti vividhairagniṃ brāhmaṇā vaidikairmakhaiḥ ।। sarve lokā namasyanti brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
dhyāyanti yogino devaṃ bhūtādhipatimīśvaram ।। ahaṃ hi sarvahaviṣāṃ bhoktā caiva phalapradaḥ । sarvadevatanurbhūtvā sarvātmā sarvasaṃsthitaḥ ।। māṃ paśyantīha vidvāṃśo dhārmikā vedavādinaḥ ।
teṣāṃ sannihito nityaṃ ye bhaktyā māmupāsate ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā dhārmikā māmupāsate । teṣāṃ dadāmi tat sthānamānandaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। anye api ye vikarmasthāḥ śūdrādyā nīcajātayaḥ ।
bhaktimantaḥ pramucyante kālena mayi saṃgatāḥ ।। na madbhaktā vinaśyanti madbhaktā vītakalmaṣāḥ । ādāvetat pratijñātaṃ na me bhaktaḥ praṇaśyati ।। yo vai nindati taṃ mūḍho devadevaṃ sa nindati ।
yo hi taṃ pūjayed bhaktyā sa pūjayati māṃ sadā ।। patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ madārādhanakāraṇāt । yo me dadāti niyataḥ sa me bhaktaḥ priyo mataḥ ।। ahaṃ hi jagatāmādau brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam ।
vidhāya dattavān vedānaśeṣānātmaniḥ sṛtān ।। ahameva hi sarveṣāṃ yogināṃ gururavyayaḥ । dhārmikāṇāṃ ca goptāhaṃ nihantā vedavidviṣām ।। ahaṃ vai sarvasaṃsārānmocako yogināmiha ।
saṃsāraheturevāhaṃ sarvasaṃsāravarjitaḥ ।। ahameva hi saṃhartā straṣṭāhaṃ paripālakaḥ । māyāvī māmīkā śaktirmāyā lokavimohinī ।। mamaiva ca parā śaktiryā sā vidyeti gīyate ।
nāśayāmi tayā māyāṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitaḥ ।। ahaṃ hi sarvaśaktīnāṃ pravartakanivartakaḥ । ādhārabhūtaḥ sarvāsāṃ nidhānamamṛtasya ca ।। ekā sarvāntarā śaktiḥ karoti vividhaṃ jagat ।
āsthāya brahmāṇo rūpaṃ manmayī madadhiṣṭhitā ।। anyā ca śaktirvipulā saṃsthāpayati me jagat । bhūtvā nārāyaṇo ananto jagannātho jaganmayaḥ ।। tṛtīyā mahatī śaktirnihanti sakalaṃ jagat ।
tāmasī me samākhyātā kālākhyā rudrarūpiṇī ।। dhyānena māṃ prapaśyanti kecijjñānena cāpare । apare bhaktiyogena karmayogena cāpare ।। sarveṣāmeva bhaktānāmiṣṭaḥ priyataro mama ।
yo hi jñānena māṃ nityamārādhayati nānyathā ।। anye ca ye trayo bhaktā madārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ । te api māṃ prāpnuvantyeva nāvartante ca vai punaḥ ।। mayā tatamidaṃ kṛtsanaṃ pradhānapuruṣātmakam ।
mayyeva saṃsthitaṃ viśvaṃ mayā saṃpreryate jagat ।। nāhaṃ prerayitā viprāḥ paramaṃ yogamāśritaḥ । prerayāmi jagatkṛtsnametadyo veda so amṛtaḥ ।। paśyāmyaśeṣamevedaṃ vartamānaṃ svabhāvataḥ ।
karoti kālo bhagavān mahāyogeśvaraḥ svayam ।। yogaḥ saṃprocyate yogī māyā śāstreṣu sūribhiḥ । yogeśvaro asau bhagavān mahādevo mahān prabhuḥ ।। mahattvaṃ sarvatattvānāṃ paratvāt parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
procyate bhagavān brahmā mahān brahmamayo amalaḥ ।। yo māmevaṃ vijānāti mahāyogeśvareśvaram । so avikalpena yogena yujyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। so ahaṃ prerayitā devaḥ paramānandamāśritaḥ ।
nṛtyāmi yogī satataṃ yastad veda sa vedavit ।। iti guhyatamaṃ jñānaṃ sarvavedeṣu niṣṭhitam । prasannacetase deyaṃ dhārmikāyāhitāgnaye ।। etāvaduktvā bhagavān yogināṃ parameśvaraḥ ।
nanarta paramaṃ bhāvamaiśvaraṃ saṃpradarśayan ।। taṃ te dadṛśurīśānaṃ tejasāṃ paramaṃ nidhim । nṛtyamānaṃ mahādevaṃ viṣṇunā gagane amale ।। yaṃ viduryogatattvajñā yogino yatamānasāḥ ।
tamīśaṃ sarvabhūtānāmākaśe dadṛśuḥ kila ।। yasya māyāmayaṃ sarvaṃ yenedaṃ preryate jagat । nṛtyamānaḥ svayaṃ viprairviśveśaḥ khalu dṛśyate ।। yat pādapaṅkajaṃ smṛtvā puruṣo ajñānajaṃ bhayam ।
jahati nṛtyamānaṃ taṃ bhūteśaṃ dadṛśuḥ kila ।। yaṃ vinidrā jitaśvāsāḥ śāntā bhaktisamanvitāḥ । jyotirmayaṃ prapaśyanti sa yogī dṛśyate kila ।। yo ajñānānmocayet kṣipraṃ prasanno bhaktavatsalaḥ ।
tameva mocakaṃ rudramākāśe dadṛśuḥ param ।। sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ sahasracaraṇākṛtim । sahasrabāhuṃ jaṭilaṃ candrārdhakṛtaśekharam ।। vasānaṃ carma vaiyāghraṃ śūlāsaktamahākaram ।
daṇḍapāṇiṃ trayīnetraṃ sūryasomāgnilocanam ।। brahmāṇḍaṃ tejasā svena sarvamāvṛtya ca sthitam । daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ durdharṣaṃ sūryakoṭisamaprabham ।। aṇḍasthaṃ cāṇḍabāhyasthaṃ bāhyamabhyantaraṃ param ।
sṛjantamanalajvālaṃ dahantamakhilaṃ jagat । nṛtyantaṃ dadṛśurdevaṃ viśvakarmāṇamīśvaram ।। mahādevaṃ mahāyogaṃ devānāmapi daivatam । paśūnāṃ patimīśānaṃ jyotiṣāṃ jyotiravyayam ।।
pinākinaṃ viśālākṣaṃ bheṣajaṃ bhavarogiṇām । kālātmānaṃ kālakālaṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।। umāpatiṃ virūpākṣaṃ yogānandamayaṃ param । jñānavairāgyanilayaṃ jñānayogaṃ sanātanam ।।
śāśvataiśvaryavibhavaṃ dharmādhāraṃ durāsadam । mahendropendranamitaṃ maharṣigaṇavanditam ।। ādhāraṃ sarvaśaktīnāṃ mahāyogeśvareśvaram । yogināṃ paramaṃ brahma yogināṃ yogavanditam ।
yogināṃ hṛdi tiṣṭhantaṃ yogamāyāsamāvṛtam ।। kṣaṇena jagato yoniṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam । īśvareṇaikatāpannamapaśyan brahmavādinaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā tadaiśvaraṃ rūpaṃ rudranārāyaṇātmakam ।
kṛtārthaṃ menire santaḥ svātmānaṃ brahmavādinaḥ ।। sanātanaścaiva sanandanaśca । maharṣiratriḥ kapilo marīciḥ ।। taṃ padmanābhāśritavāmabhāgam ।
baddhvāñjaliṃ sveṣu śiraḥsu bhūyaḥ ।। antaḥśarīre nihitaṃ guhāyām । ānandapūrṇāyatamānasāste ।। prāṇeśvaraṃ rudramanantayogam ।
pracetasaṃ brahmamayaṃ pavitram ।। dāntāḥ śāntā vimalaṃ rukmavarṇam । kaviṃ parebhyaḥ paramaṃ tatparaṃ ca ।। sarvātmabhūstvaṃ paramāṇubhūtaḥ ।
stvāmeva sarvaṃ pravadanti santaḥ ।। tvatto adhijātaḥ puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ । yathāvidhānaṃ sakalaṃ sasarja ।। stvayyevānte saṃsthitiṃ te labhante ।
nṛtyantaṃ sve hṛdaye sanniviṣṭam ।। māyāvī tvaṃ jagatāmekanāthaḥ । yogātmānaṃ citpatiṃ divyanṛtyam ।। nṛtyantaṃ te mahimānaṃ smarāmaḥ ।
brahmānandamanubhūyānubhūya ।। tvamakṣaraṃ prakṛtau gūḍharūpam । svayaṃprabhaṃ bhavato yatprakāśam ।। namanti tvāmṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇadoṣāḥ ।
viśanti tvāṃ yatayo brahmaniṣṭhāḥ ।। tvāmevaikaṃ bodhayatyekarūpam । steṣāṃ śāntiḥ śāśvatī netareṣām ।। brahmā viśvaṃ parameṣṭhī variṣṭhaḥ ।
svayaṃ jyotiracalo nityamuktaḥ ।। tvaṃ pālayasyakhilaṃ viśvarūpaḥ । namāmastvāṃ śaraṇaṃ saṃprapannāḥ ।। prāṇaṃ bṛhantaṃ harimagnimīśam ।
dhātāramādityamanekarūpam ।। tvamasya viśvasya paraṃ nidhānam । sanātanastvaṃ puruṣottamo asi ।। tvameva rudro bhagavānadhīśaḥ ।
sarveśvarastvaṃ parameśvaro asi ।। mādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt । khaṃ brahma śūnyaṃ prakṛtiṃ nirguṇaṃ ca ।। yadavyayaṃ nirmalamekarūpam ।
tadantarā yatpratibhāti tattvam ।। parāyaṇaṃ brahmatanuṃ pavitram । prasīda bhūtādhipate maheśa ।। saṃsārabījaṃ vilayaṃ prayāti ।
prasādayāmo vayamekamīśam ।। kālāya sarvāya harāya tubhyam । namo agnaye deva namaḥ śivāya ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān devaḥ kapardī vṛṣavāhanaḥ ।
saṃhṛtya paramaṃ rūpaṃ prakṛtistho abhavad bhavaḥ ।। te bhavaṃ bhūtabhavyeśaṃ pūrvavat samavasthitam । dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ vismitā vākyamabruvan ।। bhagavan bhūtabhavyeśa govṛṣāṅkitaśāsana ।
dṛṣṭvā te paramaṃ rūpaṃ nirvṛtāḥ sma sanātana ।। bhavatprasādādamale parasmin parameśvare । asmākaṃ jāyate bhaktistvayyevāvyabhicāriṇī ।। idānīṃ śrotumicchāmo māhātmyaṃ tava śaṅkara ।
bhūyo api tava yannityaṃ yāthātmyaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। sa teṣāṃ vākyamākarṇya yogināṃ yogasiddhidaḥ । prāhaḥ gambhīrayā vācā samālokya ca mādhavam ।। śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve yathāvat parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
vakṣyāmīśasya māhātmyaṃ yattadvedavido viduḥ ।। sarvalokaikanirmātā sarvalokaikarakṣitā । sarvalokaikasaṃhartā sarvātmāhaṃ sanātanaḥ ।। sarveṣāmeva vastūnāmantaryāmī pitā hyaham ।
madhye cāntaḥ sthitaṃ sarvaṃ nāhaṃ sarvatra saṃsthitaḥ ।। bhavadbhiradbhutaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yatsvarūpaṃ tu māmakam । mamaiṣā hyupamā viprā māyayā darśitā mayā ।। sarveṣāmeva bhāvānāmantarā samavasthitaḥ ।
prerayāmi jagat kṛtsnaṃ kriyāśāktiriyaṃ mama ।। yayedaṃ ceṣṭate viśvaṃ tatsvabhāvānuvarti ca । so ahaṃ kālo jagat kṛtsnaṃ prerayāmi kalātmakam ।। ekāṃśena jagat kṛtsnaṃ karomi munipuṅgavāḥ ।
saṃharāmyekarūpeṇa dvidhāvasthā mamaiva tu ।। ādimadhyāntanirmukto māyātattvapravartakaḥ । kṣobhayāmi ca sargādau pradhānapuruṣāvubhau ।। tābhyāṃ saṃjāyate viśvaṃ saṃyuktābhyāṃ parasparam ।
mahadādikrameṇaiva mama tejo vijṛmbhate ।। yo hi sarvajagatsākṣī kālacakrapravartakaḥ । hiraṇyagarbho mārtaṇḍaḥ so api maddehasaṃbhavaḥ ।। tasmai divyaṃ svamaiśvaryaṃ jñānayogaṃ sanātanam ।
dattavānātmajān vedān kalpādau caturo dvijāḥ ।। sa manniyogato devo brahmā madbhāvabhāvitaḥ । divyaṃ tanmāmakaiśvaryaṃ sarvadā vahati svayam ।। sa sarvalokanirmātā manniyogena sarvavit ।
bhūtvā caturmukhaḥ sargaṃ sṛjatyevātmasaṃbhavaḥ ।। yo api nārāyaṇo ananto lokānāṃ prabhavāvyayaḥ । mamaiva paramā mūrtiḥ karoti paripālanam ।। yo antakaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ rudraḥ kālātmakaḥ prabhuḥ ।
madājñayāsau satataṃ saṃhariṣyati me tanuḥ ।। havyaṃ vahati devānāṃ kavyaṃ kavyāśināmapi । pākaṃ ca kurute vahniḥ so api macchakticoditaḥ ।। bhuktamāhārajātaṃ ca pacate tadaharniśam ।
vaiśvānaro agnirbhagavānīśvarasya niyogataḥ ।। yo api sarvāmbhasāṃ yonirvaruṇo devapuṅgavaḥ । so api saṃjīvayet kṛtsnamīśasyaiva niyogataḥ ।। yo antastiṣṭhati bhūtānāṃ bahirdevaḥ prabhañjanaḥ ।
madājñayāsau bhūtānāṃ śarīrāṇi bibharti hi ।। yo api saṃjīvano nṝṇāṃ devānāmamṛtākaraḥ । somaḥ sa manniyogena coditaḥ kila vartate ।। yaḥ svabhāsā jagat kṛtsnaṃ prakāśayati sarvadā ।
