sūryo vṛṣṭiṃ vitanute śāstreṇaiva svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।। yo apyaśeṣajagacchāstā śakraḥ sarvāmareśvaraḥ । yajvanāṃ phalado devo vartate asau madājñayā ।। yaḥ praśāstā hyasādhūnāṃ vartate niyamādiha ।
yamo vaivasvato devo devadevaniyogataḥ ।। yo api sarvadhanādhyakṣo dhanānāṃ saṃpradāyakaḥ । so apīśvaraniyogena kubero vartate sadā ।। yaḥ sarvarakṣasāṃ nāthastāmasānāṃ phalapradaḥ ।
manniyogādasau devo vartate nirṛtiḥ sadā ।। vetālagaṇabhūtānāṃ svāmī bhogaphalapradaḥ । īśānaḥ kila bhaktānāṃ so api tiṣṭhanmamājñayā ।। yo vāmadevo aṅgirasaḥ śiṣyo rudragaṇāgraṇīḥ ।
rakṣako yogināṃ nityaṃ vartate asau madājñayā ।। yaśca sarvajagatpūjyo vartate vighnakārakaḥ । vināyako dharmanetā so api madvacanāt kila ।। yo api brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho devasenāpatiḥ prabhuḥ ।
skando asau vartate nityaṃ svayaṃbhūrvidhicoditaḥ ।। ye ca prajānāṃ patayo marīcyādyā maharṣayaḥ । sṛjanti vividhaṃ lokaṃ parasyaiva niyogataḥ ।। yā ca śrīḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ dadāti vipulāṃ śriyam ।
patnī nārāyaṇasyāsau vartate madanugrahāt ।। vācaṃ dadāti vipulāṃ yā ca devī sarasvatī । sāpīśvaraniyogena coditā saṃpravartate ।। yāśeṣapuruṣān ghorānnarakāt tārayiṣyati ।
sāvitrī saṃsmṛtā devī devājñānuvidhāyinī ।। pārvatī paramā devī brahmavidyāpradāyinī । yāpi dhyātā viśeṣeṇa sāpi madvacanānugā ।। yo anantamahimānantaḥ śeṣo aśeṣāmaraprabhuḥ ।
dadhāti śirasā lokaṃ so api devaniyogataḥ ।। yo agniḥ saṃvartako nityaṃ vaḍavārūpasaṃsthitaḥ । pibatyakhilamambhodhimīśvarasya niyogataḥ ।। ye caturdaśa loke asmin manavaḥ prathitaujasaḥ ।
pālayanti prajāḥ sarvāste api tasya niyogataḥ ।। ādityā vasavo rudrā marutaśca tathāśvinau । anyāśca devatāḥ sarvā macchāstreṇaiva dhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। gandharvā garuḍā ṛkṣāḥ siddhāḥ sādhyāścacāraṇāḥ ।
yakṣarakṣaḥ piśācāśca sthitāḥ śāstre svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।। kalākāṣṭhānimeṣāśca muhūrtā divasāḥ kṣapāḥ । ṛtavaḥ pakṣamāsāśca sthitāḥ śāstre prajāpateḥ ।। yugamanvantarāṇyeva mama tiṣṭhanti śāsane ।
parāścaiva parārdhāśca kālabhedāstathā pare ।। caturvidhāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca । niyogādeva vartante devasya paramātmanaḥ ।। pātālāni ca sarvāṇi bhuvanāni ca śāsanāt ।
brahmāṇḍāni ca vartante sarvāṇyeva svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।। atītānyapyasaṃkhyāni brahmāṇḍāni mamājñayā । pravṛttāni padārthaughaiḥ sahitāni samantataḥ ।। brahmāṇḍāni bhaviṣyanti saha vastubhirātmagaiḥ ।
vahiṣyanti sadaivājñāṃ parasya paramātmanaḥ ।। bhūmirāpo analo vāyuḥ khaṃ mano buddhireva ca । bhūtādirādiprakṛtirniyoge mama vartate ।। yāśeṣajagatāṃ yonirmohinī sarvadehinām ।
māyā vivartate nityaṃ sāpīśvaraniyogataḥ ।। yo vai dehabhṛtāṃ devaḥ puruṣaḥ paṭhyate paraḥ । ātmāsau vartate nityamīśvarasya niyogataḥ ।। vidhūya mohakalilaṃ yayā paśyati tat padam ।
sāpi vidyā maheśasya niyogavaśavartinī ।। bahunātra kimuktena mama śaktyātmakaṃ jagat । mayaiva preryate kṛtsnaṃ mayyeva pralayaṃ vrajet ।। ahaṃ hi bhagavānīśaḥ svayaṃ jyotiḥ sanātanaḥ ।
paramātmā paraṃ brahma matto hyanyanna vidyate ।। ityetat paramaṃ jñānaṃ yuṣmākaṃ kathitaṃ mayā । jñātvā vimucyate janturjanmasaṃsārabandhanāt ।। śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve prabhāvaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
yaṃ jñātvā puruṣo mukto na saṃsāre patet punaḥ ।। parāt parataraṃ brahma śāśvataṃ niṣkalaṃ dhruvam । nityānandaṃ nirvikalpaṃ taddhāma paramaṃ mama ।। ahaṃ brahmavidāṃ brahmā svayaṃbhūrviśvatomukhaḥ ।
māyāvināmahaṃ devaḥ purāṇo hariravyayaḥ ।। yogināmasmyahaṃ śaṃbhuḥ strīṇāṃ devī girīndrajā । ādityānāmahaṃ viṣṇurvasūnāmasmi pāvakaḥ ।। rudrāṇāṃ śaṅkaraścāhaṃ garuḍaḥ patatāmaham ।
airāvato gajendrāṇāṃ rāmaḥ śastrabhṛtāmaham ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ ca vasiṣṭho ahaṃ devānāṃ ca śatakratuḥ । śilpināṃ viśvakarmāhaṃ prahlādo asmyamaradviṣām ।। munīnāmapyahaṃ vyāso gaṇānāṃ ca vināyakaḥ ।
vīrāṇāṃ vīrabhadro ahaṃ siddhānāṃ kapilo muniḥ ।। parvatānāmahaṃ merurnakṣatrāṇāṃ ca candramāḥ । vajraṃ praharaṇānāṃ ca vratānāṃ satyamasmyaham ।। ananto bhogināṃ devaḥ senānīnāṃ ca pāvakiḥ ।
āśramāṇāṃ ca gārhasthamīśvarāṇāṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। mahākalpaśca kalpānāṃ yugānāṃ kṛtamasmyaham । kuberaḥ sarvayakṣāṇāṃ gaṇeśānāṃ ca vīrakaḥ ।। prajāpatīnāṃ dakṣo ahaṃ nirṛtiḥ sarvarakṣasām ।
vāyurbalavatāmasmi dvīpānāṃ puṣkaro asmyaham ।। mṛgendrāṇāṃ ca siṃho ahaṃ yantrāṇāṃ dhanureva ca । vedānāṃ sāmavedo ahaṃ yajuṣāṃ śatarudriyam ।। sāvitrī sarvajapyānāṃ guhyānāṃ praṇavo asmyaham ।
sūktānāṃ pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ jyeṣṭhasāma ca sāmasu ।। sarvavedārthaviduṣāṃ manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo asmyaham । brahmāvartastu deśānāṃ kṣetrāṇāmavimuktakam ।। vidyānāmātmavidyāhaṃ jñānānāmaiśvaraṃ param ।
bhūtānāmasmyahaṃ vyoma sattvānāṃ mṛtyureva ca ।। pāśānāmasmyahaṃ māyā kālaḥ kalayatāmaham । gatīnāṃ muktirevāhaṃ pareṣāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। yaccānyadapi loke asmin sattvaṃ tejobalādhikam ।
tatsarvaṃ pratijānīdhvaṃ mama tejovijṛmbhitam ।। ātmānaḥ paśavaḥ proktāḥ sarve saṃsāravartinaḥ । teṣāṃ patirahaṃ devaḥ smṛtaḥ paśupatirbudhaiḥ ।। māyāpāśena badhnāmi paśūnetān svalīlayā ।
māmeva mocakaṃ prāhuḥ paśūnāṃ vedavādinaḥ ।। māyāpāśena baddhānāṃ mocako anyo na vidyate । māmṛte paramātmānaṃ bhūtādhipatimavyayam ।। caturviṃśatitattvāni māyā karma guṇā iti ।
ete pāśāḥ paśupateḥ kleśāśca paśubandhanāḥ ।। mano buddhirahaṅkāraḥ khānilāgnijalāni bhūḥ । etāḥ prakṛtayastvaṣṭau vikārāśca tathāpare ।। śrotraṃ tvakcakṣuṣī jihvā ghrāṇaṃ caiva tu pañcamam ।
pāyūpasthaṃ karau pādau vāk caiva daśamī matā ।। śabdaḥ sparśaśca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhastathaiva ca । trayoviṃśatiretāni tattvāni prākṛtāni tu ।। caturviṃśakamavyaktaṃ pradhānaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam ।
anādimadhyanidhanaṃ kāraṇaṃ jagataḥ param ।। sattvaṃ rajastamaśceti guṇatrayamudāhṛtam । sāmyāvasthitimeteṣāmavyaktaṃ prakṛtiṃ viduḥ ।। sattvaṃ jñānaṃ tamo ajñānaṃ rajo miśramudāhṛtam ।
guṇānāṃ buddhivaiṣamyād vaiṣamyaṃ kavayo viduḥ ।। dharmādharmāviti proktau pāśau dvau bandhasaṃjñitau । mayyarpitāni karmāṇi nibandhāya vimuktaye ।। avidyāmasmitāṃ rāgaṃ dveṣaṃ cābhiniveśakam ।
kleśākhyānacalān prāhuḥ pāśānātmanibandhanān ।। eteṣāmeva pāśānāṃ māyā kāraṇamucyate । mūlaprakṛtiravyaktā sā śaktirmayi tiṣṭhati ।। sa eva mūlaprakṛtiḥ pradhānaṃ puruṣo api ca ।
vikārā mahadādīni devadevaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। sa eva pāśaḥ paśavaḥ sa eva । tamāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।। anyad guhyatamaṃ jñānaṃ vakṣye brāhmaṇapuṅgavāḥ ।
yenāsau tarate janturghoraṃ saṃsārasāgaram ।। ahaṃ brahmamayaḥ śāntaḥ śāśvato nirmalo avyayaḥ । ekākī bhagavānuktaḥ kevalaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। mama yonirmahad brahma tatra garbhaṃ dadhāmyaham ।
mūlaṃ māyābhidhānaṃ tu tato jātamidaṃ jagat ।। pradhānaṃ puruṣo hyatmā mahān bhūtādireva ca । tanmātrāṇi mahābhūtānīndriyāṇi ca jajñire ।। tato aṇḍamabhavaddhaimaṃ sūryakoṭisamaprabham ।
tasmin jajñe mahābrahmā macchaktyā copabṛṃhitaḥ ।। ye cānye bahavo jīvā manmayāḥ sarva eva te । na māṃ paśyanti pitaraṃ māyayā mama mohitāḥ ।। yāśca yoniṣu sarvāsu saṃbhavanti hi mūrtayaḥ ।
tāsāṃ māyā parā yonirmāmeva pitaraṃ viduḥ ।। yo māmevaṃ vijānāti bījinaṃ pitaraṃ prabhum । sa dhīraḥ sarvalokeṣu na mohamadhigacchati ।। īśānaḥ sarvavidyānāṃ bhūtānāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।
oṅkāramūrtirbhagavānahaṃ brahmā prajāpatiḥ ।। samaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu tiṣṭhantaṃ parameśvaram । vinaśyatsvavinaśyantaṃ yaḥ paśyati sa paśyati ।। samaṃ paśyan hi sarvatra samavasthitamīśvaram ।
na hinastyātmanātmānaṃ tato yāti parāṅgatim ।। viditvā sapta sūkṣmāṇi ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ca maheśvaram । pradhānaviniyogajñaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati ।। svatantratā nityamaluptaśaktiḥ ।
ṣaḍāhuraṅgāni maheśvarasya ।। sūkṣmāṇyāhuḥ sapta tattvātmakāni । bandhaḥ prokto viniyogo api tena ।। vedeṣūktā kāraṇaṃ brahmayoniḥ ।
nmaheśvaraḥ puruṣaḥ satyarūpaḥ ।। vyomavyāpī vedavedyaḥ purāṇaḥ । bījaṃ viśvaṃ deva ekaḥ sa eva ।। tvekātmānaṃ kecidanyattathāhuḥ ।
mahādevaḥ procyate vedavidbhiḥ ।। prabhuṃ purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ viśvarūpam । sa buddhimān buddhimatītya tiṣṭhati ।। niṣkalo nirmalo nityo niṣkriyaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।
tanno vada mahādeva viśvarūpaḥ kathaṃ bhavān ।। nāhaṃ viśvo na viśvaṃ ca māmṛte vidyate dvijāḥ । māyānimittamatrāsti sā cātmānamapāśritā ।। anādinidhanā śaktirmāyāvyaktasamāśrayā ।
tannimittaḥ prapañco ayamavyaktādabhavat khalu ।। avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ prāhurānandaṃ jyotirakṣaram । ahameva paraṃ brahma matto hyanyanna vidyate ।। tasmānme viśvarūpatvaṃ niścitaṃ brahmavādibhiḥ ।
ekatve ca pṛthaktve ca proktametannidarśanam ।। ahaṃ tat paramaṃ brahma paramātmā sanātanaḥ । akāraṇaṃ dvijāḥ prokto na doṣo hyātmanastathā ।। anantā śaktayo avyakte māyādyāḥ saṃsthitā dhruvāḥ ।
tasmin divi sthitaṃ nityamavyaktaṃ bhāti kevalam ।। yābhistallakṣyate bhinnamabhinnaṃ tu svabhāvataḥ । ekayā mama sāyujyamanādinidhanaṃ dhruvam ।। puṃso abhūdanyayā bhūtiranyayā tattirohitam ।
anādimadhyaṃ tiṣṭhantaṃ yujyate avidyayā kila ।। tadetat paramaṃ vyaktaṃ prabhāmaṇḍalamaṇḍitam । tadakṣaraṃ paraṃ jyotistad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। tatra sarvamidaṃ protamotaṃ caivākhilaṃ jagat ।
tadeva ca jagat kṛtsnaṃ tad vijñāya vimucyate ।। yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha । ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvān vibheti na kutaścana ।। mādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt ।
nityānandī bhavati brahmabhūtaḥ ।। yajjyotiṣāṃ jyotirekaṃ divistham । ātmānandī bhavati brahmabhūtaḥ ।। brahmānandamamṛtaṃ viśvadhāma ।
yatra gatvā na nivarteta bhūyaḥ ।। yadarciṣi pravibhātīva tejaḥ । vibhrājamānaṃ vimalaṃ vyoma dhāma ।। ātmanyātmānamanubhūyānubhūya ।
brahmānandī bhagavānīśa eṣaḥ ।। sarvavyāpī sarvabhūtāntarātmā । teṣāṃ śāntiḥ śāśvatī netareṣām ।। sarvānanaśirogrīvaḥ sarvabhūtaguhāśayaḥ ।
sarvavyāpī ca bhagavān na tasmādanyadiṣyate ।। ityetadaiśvaraṃ jñānamuktaṃ vo munipuṅgavāḥ । gopanīyaṃ viśeṣeṇa yogināmapi durlabham ।। aliṅgamekamavyaktaṃ liṅgaṃ brahmeti niścitam ।
svayañjyotiḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ pare vyomni vyavasthitam ।। avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattadakṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam । nirguṇaṃ śuddhavijñānaṃ tad vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ ।। tanniṣṭhāḥ śāntasaṃkalpā nityaṃ tadbhāvabhāvitāḥ ।
paśyanti tat paraṃ brahma yattalliṅgamiti śrutiḥ ।। anyathā nahi māṃ draṣṭuṃ śakyaṃ vai munipuṅgavāḥ । nahi tad vidyate jñānaṃ yatastajjñāyate param ।। etattatparamaṃ jñānaṃ kevalaṃ kavayo viduḥ ।
ajñānamitarat sarvaṃ yasmānmāyāmayaṃ jagat ।। yajjñānaṃ nirmalaṃ sūkṣmaṃ nirvikalpaṃ yadavyayam । mamātmāsau tadevemiti prāhurvipaścitaḥ ।। ye apyanekaṃ prapaśyanti te api paśyanti tatparam ।
āśritāḥ paramāṃ niṣṭhāṃ buddhvaikaṃ tattvamavyayam ।। ye punaḥ paramaṃ tattvamekaṃ vānekamīśvaram । bhaktyā māṃ saṃprapaśyanti vijñeyāste tadātmakāḥ ।। sākṣādeva prapaśyanti svātmānaṃ parameśvaram ।
nityānandaṃ nirvikalpaṃ satyarūpamiti sthitiḥ ।। bhajante paramānandaṃ sarvagaṃ yattadātmakam । svātmanyavasthitāḥ śāntāḥ pare avyakte parasya tu ।। eṣā vimuktiḥ paramā mama sāyujyamuttamam ।
nirvāṇaṃ brahmaṇā caikyaṃ kaivalyaṃ kavayo viduḥ ।। tasmādanādimadhyāntaṃ vastvekaṃ paramaṃ śivam । sa īśvaro mahādevastaṃ vijñāya vimucyate ।। na nakṣatrāṇi tapano nota vidyut ।
tannityabhāsamacalaṃ sadvibhāti ।। śuddhaṃ bṛhantaṃ paramaṃ yadvibhāti । paśyanti tattvamacalaṃ yat sa īśaḥ ।। śuddhaṃ vadanti puruṣaṃ sarvavedāḥ ।
dhāyāyanti vedārthaviniścitārthāḥ ।। prāṇo anilo gaganaṃ nota buddhiḥ । vibhāti devaḥ śiva eva kevalaḥ ।। jñānāmṛtaṃ sarvavedeṣu gūḍham ।
yuñjīta yogaṃ prayato hyajasram ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaṃ paramadurlabham । yenātmānaṃ prapaśyanti bhānumantamiveśvaram ।। yogāgnirdahati kṣipramaśeṣaṃ pāpapañjaram ।
prasannaṃ jāyate jñānaṃ sākṣānnirvāṇasiddhidam ।। yogātsaṃjāyate jñānaṃ jñānād yogaḥ pravartate । yogajñānābhiyuktasya prasīdati maheśvaraḥ ।। ekakālaṃ dvikālaṃ vā trikālaṃ nityameva vā ।
ye yuñjantīha madyogaṃ te vijñeyā maheśvarāḥ ।। yogastu dvividho jñeyo hyabhāvaḥ prathamo mataḥ । aparastu mahāyogaḥ sarvayogottamottamaḥ ।। śūnyaṃ sarvanirābhāsaṃ svarūpaṃ yatra cintyate ।
abhāvayogaḥ sa prokto yenātmānaṃ prapaśyati ।। yatra paśyati cātmānaṃ nityānandaṃ nirañjanam । mayaikyaṃ sa mahāyogo bhāṣitaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। ye cānye yogināṃ yogāḥ śrūyante granthavistare ।
sarve te brahmayogasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। yatra sākṣāt prapaśyanti vimuktā viśvamīśvaram । sarveṣāmeva yogānāṃ sa yogaḥ paramo mataḥ ।। sahasraśo atha śataśo ye ceśvarabahiṣkṛtāḥ ।
na te paśyanti māmekaṃ yogino yatamānasāḥ ।। prāṇāyāmastathā dhyānaṃ pratyāhāro atha dhāraṇā । samādhiśca muniśreṣṭhā yamo niyama āsanam ।। mayyekacittatāyogo vṛttyantaranirodhataḥ ।
tatsādhanānyaṣṭadhā tu yuṣmākaṃ kathitāni tu ।। ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryāparigrahau । yamāḥ saṃkṣepataḥ proktāścittaśuddhipradā nṛṇām ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā sarvabhūteṣu sarvadā ।
akleśajananaṃ proktaṃ tvahiṃsā paramarṣibhiḥ ।। ahiṃsāyāḥ paro dharmo nāstyahiṃsā paraṃ sukham । vidhinā yā bhaveddhiṃsā tvahiṃsaiva prakīrtitā ।। satyena sarvamāpnoti satye sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
yathārthakathanācāraḥ satyaṃ proktaṃ dvijātibhiḥ ।। paradravyāpaharaṇaṃ cauryād vātha balena vā । steyaṃ tasyānācaraṇādasteyaṃ dharmasādhanam ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā sarvāvasthāsu sarvadā ।
sarvatra maithunatyāgaṃ brahmacaryaṃ pracakṣate ।। dravyāṇāmapyanādānamāpadyapi yathecchayā । aparigraha ityāhustaṃ prayatnena pālayet ।। tapaḥ svādhyāyasaṃtoṣāḥ śaucamīśvarapūjanam ।
samāsānniyamāḥ proktā yogasiddhipradāyinaḥ ।। upavāsaparākādikṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ । śarīraśoṣaṇaṃ prāhustāpasāstapa uttamam ।। vedāntaśatarudrīyapraṇavādijapaṃ budhāḥ ।
sattvaśuddhikaraṃ puṃsāṃ svādhyāyaṃ paricakṣate ।। svādhyāyasya trayo bhedā vācikopāṃśumānasāḥ । uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyaṃ prāhurvedārthavedinaḥ ।। yaḥ śabdabodhajananaḥ pareṣāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ sphuṭam ।
svādhyāyo vācikaḥ prokta upāṃśoratha lakṣaṇam ।। oṣṭhayoḥ spandamātreṇa parasyāśabdabodhakaḥ । upāṃśureṣa nirdiṣṭaḥ sāhasro vācikājjapaḥ ।। yatpadākṣarasaṅgatyā parispandanavarjitam ।
cintanaṃ sarvaśabdānāṃ mānasaṃ taṃ japaṃ viduḥ ।। yadṛcchālābhato nityamalaṃ puṃso bhavediti । yā dhīstāmṛṣayaḥ prāhuḥ saṃtoṣaṃ sukhalakṣaṇam ।। bāhyamābhyantaraṃ śaucaṃ dvidhā proktaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।
mṛjjalābhyāṃ smṛtaṃ bāhyaṃ manaḥśuddhirathāntaram ।। stutismaraṇapūjābhirvāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ । suniścalā śive bhaktiretadīśvarapūjanam ।। yamāḥ saniyamāḥ proktāḥ prāṇāyāmaṃ nibodhata ।
prāṇaḥ svadehajo vāyurāyāmastannirodhanam ।। uttamādhamamadhyatvāt tridhāyaṃ pratipāditaḥ । sa eva dvividhaḥ proktaḥ sagarbho agarbha eva ca ।। mātrādvādaśako mandaścaturviṃśatimātrikaḥ ।
madhyamaḥ prāṇasaṃrodhaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśanmātrikottamaḥ ।। prasvedakampanotthānajanakatvaṃ yathākramam । mandamadhyamamukhyānāmānandāduttamottamaḥ ।। sagarbhamāhuḥ sajapamagarbhaṃ vijapaṃ budhāḥ ।
etad vai yogināmuktaṃ prāṇāyāmasya lakṣaṇam ।। savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ śirasā saha । trirjapedāyataprāṇaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa ucyate ।। recakaḥ pūrakaścaiva prāṇāyāmo atha kumbhakaḥ ।
procyate sarvaśāstreṣu yogibhiryatamānasaiḥ ।। recako ajastraniśvāsāt pūrakastannirodhataḥ । sāmyena saṃsthitiryā sā kumbhakaḥ parigīyate ।। indriyāṇāṃ vicaratāṃ viṣayeṣu svabhāvataḥ ।
nigrahaḥ procyate sadbhiḥ pratyāhārastu sattamāḥ ।। hṛtpuṇḍarīke nābhyāṃ vā mūrdhni parvatamastake । evamādiṣu deśeṣu dhāraṇā cittabandhanam ।। deśāvasthitimālambya buddheryā vṛttisaṃtatiḥ ।
vṛttyantarairasaṃsṛṣṭā taddhyānaṃ sūrayo viduḥ ।। ekākāraḥ samādhiḥ syād deśālambanavarjitaḥ । pratyayo hyarthamātreṇa yogasādhanamuttamam ।। dhāraṇā dvādaśāyāmā dhyānaṃ dvādaśadhāraṇāḥ ।
dhyānaṃ dvādaśakaṃ yāvat samādhirabhidhīyate ।। āsanaṃ svastikaṃ proktaṃ padmamardhāsanaṃ tathā । sādhanānāṃ ca sarveṣāmetatsādhanamuttamam ।। ūrvorupari viprendrāḥ kṛtvā pādatale ubhe ।
samāsītātmanaḥ padmametadāsanamuttamam ।। ekaṃ pādamathaikasmin vinyasyoruṇi sattamāḥ । āsītārdhāsanamidaṃ yogasādhanamuttamam ।। ubhe kṛtvā pādatale jānūrvorantareṇa hi ।
samāsītātmanaḥ proktamāsanaṃ svastikaṃ param ।। adeśakāle yogasya darśanaṃ hi na vidyate । agnyabhyāse jale vāpi śuṣkaparṇacaye tathā ।। jantuvyāpte śmaśāne ca jīrṇagoṣṭhe catuṣpathe ।
saśabde sabhaye vāpi caityavalmīkasaṃcaye ।। aśubhe durjanākrānte maśakādisamanvite । nācared dehabādhe vā daurmanasyādisaṃbhave ।। sugupte suśubhe deśe guhāyāṃ parvatasya tu ।
nadyāstīre puṇyadeśe devatāyatane tathā ।। gṛhe vā suśubhe ramye vijane jantuvarjite । yuñjīta yogī satatamātmānaṃ matparāyaṇaḥ ।। namaskṛtya tu yogīndrān saśiṣyāṃśca vināyakam ।
guruṃ caivātha māṃ yogī yuñjīta susamāhitaḥ ।। āsanaṃ svastikaṃ baddhvā padmamardhamathāpi vā । nāsikāgre samāṃ dṛṣṭimīṣadunmīlitekṣaṇaḥ ।। kṛtvātha nirbhayaḥ śāntastyaktvā māyāmayaṃ jagat ।
svātmanyavasthitaṃ devaṃ cintayet parameśvaram ।। śikhāgre dvādaśāṅgulye kalpayitvātha paṅkajam । dharmakandasamudbhūtaṃ jñānanālaṃ suśobhanam ।। aiśvaryāṣṭadalaṃ śvetaṃ paraṃ vairāgyakarṇikam ।
cintayet paramaṃ kośaṃ karṇikāyāṃ hiraṇmayam ।। sarvaśaktimayaṃ sākṣād yaṃ prāhurdivyamavyayam । oṅkāravācyamavyaktaṃ raśmijālasamākulam ।। cintayet tatra vimalaṃ paraṃ jyotiryadakṣaram ।
tasmin jyotiṣi vinyasyasvātmānaṃ tadabhedataḥ ।। dhyāyītākāśamadhyasthamīśaṃ paramakāraṇam । tadātmā sarvago bhūtvā na kiñcidapi cintayet ।। etad guhyatamaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyānāntaramathocyate ।
cintayitvā tu pūrvoktaṃ hṛdaye padmamuttamam ।। ātmānamatha kartāraṃ tatrānalasamatviṣam । madhye vahniśikhākāraṃ puruṣaṃ pañcaviṃśakam ।। cintayet paramātmānaṃ tanmadhye gaganaṃ param ।
oṅkarabodhitaṃ tattvaṃ śāśvataṃ śivamacyutam ।। avyaktaṃ prakṛtau līnaṃ paraṃ jyotiranuttamam । tadantaḥ paramaṃ tattvamātmādhāraṃ nirañjanam ।। dhyāyīta tanmayo nityamekarūpaṃ maheśvaram ।
viśodhya sarvatattvāni praṇavenāthavā punaḥ ।। saṃsthāpya mayi cātmānaṃ nirmale parame pade । plāvayitvātmano dehaṃ tenaiva jñānavāriṇā ।। madātmā manmayo bhasma gṛhītvā hyagnihotrajam ।
tenoddhṛtya tu sarvāṅgamagnirityādimantrataḥ । cintayet svātmanīśānaṃ paraṃ jyotiḥ svarūpiṇam ।। eṣa pāśupato yogaḥ paśupāśavimuktaye । sarvavedāntasāro ayamatyāśramamiti śrutiḥ ।।
etat parataraṃ guhyaṃ matsāyujyopapādakam । dvijātīnāṃ tu kathitaṃ bhaktānāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।। brahmacaryamahiṃsā ca kṣamā śaucaṃ tapo damaḥ । saṃtoṣaḥ satyamāstikyaṃ vratāṅgāni viśeṣataḥ ।।
ekenāpyatha hīnena vratamasya tu lupyate । tasmādātmaguṇopeto madvrataṃ voḍhumarhati ।। vītarāgabhayakrodhā manmayā māmupāśritāḥ । bahavo anena yogena pūtā madbhāvamāgatāḥ ।।
ye yathā māṃ prapadyante tāṃstathaiva bhajāmyaham । jñānayogena māṃ tasmād yajeta parameśvaram ।। athavā bhaktiyogena vairāgyeṇa pareṇa tu । cetasā bodhayuktena pūjayenmāṃ sadā śuciḥ ।।
sarvakarmāṇi saṃnyasya bhikṣāśī niṣparigrahaḥ । prāpnoti mama sāyujyaṃ guhyametanmayoditam ।। adveṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ maitraḥ karuṇa eva ca । nirmamo nirahaṅkāro yo madbhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥ ।।
saṃtuṣṭaḥ satataṃ yogī yatātmā dṛḍhaniścayaḥ । mayyarpitamano buddhiryo madbhaktaḥ sa me priyaḥ ।। yasmānnodvijate loko lokānnodvijate ca yaḥ । harṣāmarṣabhayodvegairmukto yaḥ sa hi me priyaḥ ।।
anapekṣaḥ śucirdakṣa udāsīno gatavyathaḥ । sarvārambhaparityāgī bhaktimān yaḥ sa me priyaḥ ।। tulyanindāstutirmaunī saṃtuṣṭo yena kenacit । aniketaḥ sthiramatirmadbhakto māmupaiṣyati ।।
sarvakarmāṇyapi sadā kurvāṇo matparāyaṇaḥ । matprasādādavāpnoti śāśvataṃ paramaṃ padam ।। cetasā sarvakarmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya matparaḥ । nirāśīrnirmamo bhūtvā māmekaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajet ।।
tyaktvā karmaphalāsaṅgaṃ nityatṛpto nirāśrayaḥ । karmaṇyabhipravṛtto api naiva tena nibadhyate ।। nirāśīryatacittātmā tyaktasarvaparigrahaḥ । śārīraṃ kevalaṃ karma kurvannāpnoti tatpadam ।।
yadṛcchālābhatuṣṭasya dvandvātītasya caiva hi । kurvato matprasādārthaṃ karma saṃsāranāśanam ।। manmanā mannamaskāro madyājī matparāyaṇaḥ । māmupaiṣyati yogīśaṃ jñātvā māṃ parameśvaram ।।
madbuddhayo māṃ satataṃ bodhayantaḥ parasparam । kathayantaśca māṃ nityaṃ mama sāyujyamāpnuyuḥ ।। evaṃ nityābhiyuktānāṃ māyeyaṃ karmasānvagam । nāśayāmi tamaḥ kṛtsnaṃ jñānadīpena bhāsvatā ।।
madbuddhayo māṃ satataṃ pūjayantīha ye janāḥ । teṣāṃ nityābhiyuktānāṃ yogakṣemaṃ vahāmyaham ।। ye anye ca kāmabhogārthaṃ yajante hyanyadevatāḥ । teṣāṃ tadantaṃ vijñeyaṃ devatānugataṃ phalam ।।
ye cānyadevatābhaktāḥ pūjayantīha devatāḥ । madbhāvanāsamāyuktā mucyante te api bhāvataḥ ।। tasmādanīśvarānanyāṃstyaktvā devānaśeṣataḥ । māmeva saṃśrayedīśaṃ sa yāti paramaṃ padam ।।
tyaktvā putrādiṣu snehaṃ niḥ śoko niṣparigrahaḥ । yajeccāmaraṇālliṅge viraktaḥ parameśvaram ।। ye arcayanti sadā liṅgaṃ tyaktvā bhogānaśeṣataḥ । ekena janmanā teṣāṃ dadāmi paramaiśvaram ।।
parānandātmakaṃ liṅgaṃ kevalaṃ sannirañjanam । jñānātmakaṃ sarvagataṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam ।। ye cānye niyatā bhaktā bhāvayitvā vidhānataḥ । yatra kvacana talliṅgamarcayanti maheśvaram ।।
jale vā vahnimadhye vāvyomni sūrye athavānyataḥ । ratnādau bhāvayitveśamarcayelliṅgamaiśvaram ।। sarvaṃ liṅgamayaṃ hyetat sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam । tasmālliṅge arcayedīśaṃ yatra kvacana śāśvatam ।।
agnau kriyāvatāmapsu vyomni sūrye manīṣiṇām । kāṣṭhādiṣveva mūrkhāṇāṃ hṛdi liṅgantuyoginām ।। yadyanutpannavijñāno viraktaḥ prītisaṃyutaḥ । yāvajjīvaṃ japed yuktaḥ praṇavaṃ brahmaṇo vapuḥ ।।
athavā śatarudrīyaṃ japedāmaraṇād dvijaḥ । ekākī yatacittātmā sa yāti paramaṃ padam ।। vased vāmaraṇād vipro vārāṇasyāṃ samāhitaḥ । so apīśvaraprasādena yāti tat paramaṃ padam ।।
tatrotkramaṇakāle hi sarveṣāmeva dehinām । dadāti tat paraṃ jñānaṃ yena mucyeta bandhanāt ।। varṇāśramavidhiṃ kṛtsnaṃ kurvāṇo matparāyaṇaḥ । tenaiva janmanā jñānaṃ labdhvā yāti śivaṃ padam ।।
ye api tatra vasantīha nīcā vā pāpayonayaḥ । sarve taranti saṃsāramīśvarānugrahād dvijāḥ ।। kintu vighnā bhaviṣyanti pāpopahatacetasām । dharmaṃ samāśrayet tasmānmuktaye niyataṃ dvijāḥ ।।
etad rahasyaṃ vedānāṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasya cit । dhārmikāyaiva dātavyaṃ bhaktāya brahmacāriṇe ।। ityetaduktvā bhagavānātmayogamanuttamam । vyājahāra samāsīnaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam ।।
mayaitad bhāṣitaṃ jñānaṃ hitārthaṃ brahmavādinām । dātavyaṃ śāntacittebhyaḥ śiṣyebhyo bhavatā śivam ।। uktvaivamatha yogīndrānabravīd bhagavānajaḥ । hitāya sarvabhaktānāṃ dvijātīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
bhavanto api hi majjñānaṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ vidhipūrvakam । upadekṣyanti bhaktānāṃ sarveṣāṃ vacanānmama ।। ayaṃ nārāyaṇo yo ahamīśvaro nātra saṃśayaḥ । nāntaraṃ ye prapaśyanti teṣāṃ deyamidaṃ param ।।
mamaiṣā paramā mūrtirnārāyaṇasamāhvayā । sarvabhūtātmabhūtasthā śāntā cākṣarasaṃjñitā ।। ye tvanyathā prapaśyanti loke bhedadṛśo janāḥ । na te māṃ saṃprapaśyanti jāyante ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।
ye tvimaṃ viṣṇumavyaktaṃ māṃ vā devaṃ maheśvaram । ekībhāvena paśyanti na teṣāṃ punarudbhavaḥ ।। tasmādanādinidhanaṃ viṣṇumātmānamavyayam । māmeva saṃprapaśyadhvaṃ pūjayadhvaṃ tathaiva hi ।।
ye anyathā māṃ prapaśyanti matvemaṃ devatāntaram । te yānti narakān ghorān nāhaṃ teṣuvyavasthitaḥ ।। mūrkhaṃ vā paṇḍitaṃ vāpi brāhmaṇaṃ vā madāśrayam । mocayāmi śvapākaṃ vā na nārāyaṇanindakam ।।
tasmādeṣa mahāyogī madbhaktaiḥ puruṣottamaḥ । arcanīyo namaskāryo matprītijananāya hi ।। evamuktvā samāliṅgya vāsudevaṃ pinākadhṛk । antarhito abhavat teṣāṃ sarveṣāmeva paśyatām ।।
nārāyaṇo api bhagavāṃstāpasaṃ veṣamuttamam । jagrāha yoginaḥ sarvāṃstyaktvā vai paramaṃ vapuḥ ।। jñātaṃ bhavadbhiramalaṃ prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ । sākṣādeva maheśasya jñānaṃ saṃsāranāśanam ।।
gacchadhvaṃ vijvarāḥ sarve vijñānaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ । pravartayadhvaṃ śiṣyebhyo dhārmikebhyo munīśvarāḥ ।। idaṃ bhaktāya śāntāya dhārmikāyāhitāgnaye । vijñānamaiśvaraṃ deyaṃ brāhmaṇāya viśeṣataḥ ।।
evamuktvā sa viśvātmā yogināṃ yogavittamaḥ । nārāyaṇo mahāyogī jagāmādarśanaṃ svayam ।। te api devādideveśaṃ namaskṛtya maheśvaram । nārāyaṇaṃ ca bhūtādiṃ svāni sthānāni bhejire ।।
sanatkumāro bhagavān saṃvartāya mahāmuniḥ । dattavānaiśvaraṃ jñānaṃ so api satyavratāya tu ।। sanandano api yogīndraḥ pulahāya maharṣaye । pradadau gautamāyātha pulaho api prajāpatiḥ ।।
aṅgirā vedaviduṣe bharadvājāya dattavān । jaigīṣavyāya kapilastathā pañcaśikhāya ca ।। parāśaro api sanakāt pitā me sarvatattvadṛk । lebhetatparamaṃ jñānaṃ tasmād vālmīkirāptavān ।।
mamovāca purā devaḥ satīdehabhavāṅgajaḥ । vāmadevo mahāyogī rudraḥ kila pinākadhṛk ।। nārāyaṇo api bhagavān devakītanayo hariḥ । arjunāya svayaṃ sākṣāt dattavānidamuttamam ।।
yadahaṃ labdhavān rudrād vāmadevādanuttamam । viśeṣād giriśe bhaktistasmādārabhya me abhavat ।। śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ rudraṃ prapanno ahaṃ viśeṣataḥ । bhūteśaṃ giraśaṃ sthāṇuṃ devadevaṃ triśūlinam ।।
bhavanto api hi taṃ devaṃ śaṃbhuṃ govṛṣavāhanam । prapadyadhvaṃ sapatnīkāḥ saputrāḥ śaraṇaṃ śivam ।। vartadhvaṃ tatprasādena karmayogena śaṅkaram । pūjayadhvaṃ mahādevaṃ gopatiṃ bhūtibhūṣaṇam ।।
evamukte atha munayaḥ śaunakādyā maheśvaram । praṇemuḥ śāśvataṃ sthāṇuṃ vyāsaṃ satyavatīsutam ।। abruvan hṛṣṭamanasaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ prabhum । sākṣādeva hṛṣīkeśaṃ sarvalokamaheśvaram ।।
bhavatprasādādacalā śaraṇye govṛṣadhvaje । idānīṃ jāyate bhaktiryā devairapi durlabhā ।। kathayasva muniśreṣṭha karmayogamanuttamam । yenāsau bhagavānīśaḥ samārādhyo mumukṣubhiḥ ।।
tvatsaṃnidhāveṣa sūtaḥ śṛṇotu bhagavadvacaḥ । tadvadākhilalokānāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ dharmasaṃgraham ।। yaduktaṃ devadevena viṣṇunā kūrmarūpiṇā । pṛṣṭena munibhiḥ pūrvaṃ śakreṇāmṛtamanthane ।।
śrutvā satyavatīsūnuḥ karmayogaṃ sanātanam । munīnāṃ bhāṣitaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ provāca susamāhitaḥ ।। ya imaṃ paṭhate nityaṃ saṃvādaṃ kṛttivāsasaḥ । sanatkumārapramukhaiḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
śrāvayed vā dvijān śuddhān brahmacaryaparāyaṇān । yo vā vicārayedarthaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। yaścaitacchṛṇuyānnityaṃ bhaktiyukto dṛḍhavrataḥ । sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena paṭhitavyo manīṣibhiḥ । śrotavyaścātha mantavyo viśeṣād brāhmaṇaiḥ sadā ।। śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve vakṣyamāṇaṃ sanātanam । karmayogaṃ brāhmaṇānāmātyantikaphalapradam ।।
āmnāyasiddhamakhilaṃ brihmaṇānupradarśitam । ṛṣīṇāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ pūrvaṃ manurāha prajāpatiḥ ।। sarvapāpaharaṃ puṇyamṛṣisaṅghairniṣevitam । samāhitadhiyo yūyaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ gadato mama ।।
kṛtopanayano vedānadhīyīta dvijottamāḥ । garbhāṣṭame aṣṭame vābde svasūtroktavidhānataḥ ।। daṇḍī ca mekhalī sūtrī kṛṣṇājinadharo muniḥ । bhikṣāhāro guruhito vīkṣamāṇo gururmukham ।।
kārpāsamupavītārthaṃ nirmitaṃ brahmaṇā purā । brāhmaṇānāṃ trivit sūtraṃ kauśaṃ vā vastrameva vā ।। sadopavītī caiva syāt sadā baddhaśikho dvijaḥ । anyathā yat kṛtaṃ karma tad bhavatyayathākṛtam ।।
vasedavikṛtaṃ vāsaḥ kārpāsaṃ vā kaṣāyakam । tadeva paridhānīyaṃ śuklamacchidramuttamam ।। uttaraṃ tu samākhyātaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ śubham । abhāve gavyamajinaṃ rauravaṃ vā vidhīyate ।।
uddhṛtya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ savye bāhau samarpitam । upavītaṃ bhavennityaṃ nivītaṃ kaṇṭhasajjane ।। savyaṃ bāhuṃ samuddhṛtya dakṣiṇe tu dhṛtaṃ dvijāḥ । prācīnāvītamityuktaṃ pitrye karmaṇi yojayet ।।
agnyagāre gavāṃ goṣṭhe home japye tathaiva ca । svādhyāye bhojane nityaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca sannidhau ।। upāsane gurūṇāṃ ca saṃdhyayoḥ sādhusaṃgame । upavītī bhavennityaṃ vidhireṣa sanātanaḥ ।।
mauñjī trivṛt samā ślakṣaṇā kāryā viprasya mekhalā । muñjābhāve kuśenāhurgranthinaikena vā tribhiḥ ।। dhārayed bailvapālāśau daṇḍau keśāntakau dvijaḥ । yajñārhavṛkṣajaṃ vātha saumyamavraṇameva ca ।।
sāyaṃ prātardvijaḥ saṃdhyāmupāsīta samāhitaḥ । kāmāllobhād bhayānmohāt tyaktena patito bhavet ।। agnikāryaṃ tataḥ kuryāt sāyaṃ prātaḥ prasannadhīḥ । snātvā saṃtarpayed devānṛṣīn pitṛgaṇāṃstathā ।।
devatābhyarcanaṃ kuryāt puṣpaiḥ patreṇa vāmbubhiḥ । abhivādanaśīlaḥ syānnityaṃ vṛddheṣu dharmataḥ ।। asāvahaṃ bho nāmeti samyak praṇatipūrvakam । āyurārogyasiddhyarthaṃ tandrādiparivarjitaḥ ।।
āyuṣṇān bhava saumyeti vācyo vipro abhivādane । akāraścāsya nāmno ante vācyaḥ pūrvākṣaraḥ plutaḥ ।। na kuryād yo abhivādasya dvijaḥ pratyabhivādanam । nābhivādyaḥ sa viduṣā yathā śūdrastathaiva saḥ ।।
vyatyastapāṇinā kāryamupasaṃgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ । savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇaḥ ।। laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ cāpi tathādhyātmikameva vā । ādadīta yato jñānaṃ taṃ pūrvamabhivādayet ।।
nodakaṃ dhārayed bhaikṣaṃ puṣpāṇi samidhastathā । evaṃvidhāni cānyāni na daivādyeṣu karmasu ।। brāhmaṇaṃ kuśalaṃ pṛcchet kṣatrabandhumanāmayam । vaiśyaṃ kṣemaṃ samāgamya śūdramārogyameva tu ।।
upādhyāyaḥ pitā jyeṣṭho bhrātā caiva mahīpatiḥ । mātulaḥ śvaśurastrātā mātāmahapitāmahau । varṇajyeṣṭhaḥ pitṛvyaśca puṃso atra guravaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। mātā mātāmahī gurvo piturmātuśca sodarāḥ ।
śvaśrūḥ pitāmahījyeṣṭhā dhātrī ca guravaḥ striyaḥ ।। ityukto guruvargo ayaṃ mātṛtaḥ pitṛto dvijāḥ । anuvartanameteṣāṃ manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ ।। guruṃ dṛṣṭvā samuttiṣṭhedabhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।
naitairupaviśet sārdhaṃ vivadennātmakāraṇāt ।। jīvitārthamapi dveṣād gurubhirnaiva bhāṣaṇam । udito api guṇairanyairgurudveṣī patatyadhaḥ ।। gurūṇāmapi sarveṣāṃ pūjyāḥ pañca viśeṣataḥ ।
teṣāmādyāstrayaḥ śreṣṭhāsteṣāṃ mātā supūjitā ।। yo bhāvayati yā sūte yena vidyopadiśyate । jyeṣṭho bhrātā ca bhartā ca pañcaite guravaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ātmanaḥ sarvayatnena prāṇatyāgena vā punaḥ ।
pūjanīyā viśeṣeṇa pañcaite bhūtimicchatā ।। yāvat pitā ca mātā ca dvāvetau nirvikāriṇau । tāvat sarvaṃ parityajya putraḥ syāt tatparāyaṇaḥ ।। pitā mātā ca suprītau syātāṃ putraguṇairyadi ।
sa putraḥ sakalaṃ dharmamāpnuyāt tena karmaṇā ।। nāsti mātṛsamaṃ daivaṃ nāsti pitṛsamo guruḥ । tayoḥ pratyupakāro api na kathañcana vidyate ।। tayornityaṃ priyaṃ kuryāt karmaṇā manasā girā ।
na tābhyāmananujñāto dharmamanyaṃ samācaret ।। varjayitvā muktiphalaṃ nityaṃ naimittikaṃ tathā । dharmasāraḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ pretyānantaphalapradaḥ ।। samyagārādhya vaktāraṃ visṛṣṭastadanujñayā ।
śiṣyo vidyāphalaṃ bhuṅkte pretya cāpadyate divi ।। yo bhrātaraṃ pitṛsamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ mūrkho avamanyate । tena doṣeṇa sa pretya nirayaṃ ghoramṛcchati ।। puṃsā vartmaniviṣṭena pūjyo bhartā tu sarvadā ।
yāti dātari loke asmin upakārāddhi gauravam ।। yenarā bhartṛpiṇḍārthaṃ svān prāṇān saṃtyajanti hi । teṣāmathākṣayāṃllokān provāca bhagavān manuḥ ।। mātulāṃśca pitṛvyāṃśca śvaśurānṛtvijo gurūn ।
asāvahamiti brūyuḥ pratyutthāya yavīyasaḥ ।। avācyo dīkṣito nāmnā yavīyānapi yo bhavet । bhobhavatpūrvakaṃ tvenamabhibhāṣeta dharmavit ।। abhivādyāśca pūjyaśca śirasā vandya eva ca ।
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyādyaiśca śrīkāmaiḥ sādaraṃ sadā ।। nābhivādyāstu vipreṇa kṣatriyādyāḥ kathañcana । jñānakarmaguṇopetā yadyapyete bahuśrutāḥ ।। brāhmaṇaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ svasti kuryāditi sthitiḥ ।
savarṇeṣu savarṇānāṃ kāryamevābhivādanam ।। gururagnirdvijātīnāṃ varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇo guruḥ । patireko guruḥ strīṇāṃ sarvatrābhyāgato guruḥ ।। vidyā karma vayo bandhurvittaṃ bhavati pañcamam ।
mānyasthānāni pañcāhuḥ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ gurūttarāt ।। pañcānāṃ triṣu varṇeṣu bhūyāṃsi balavanti ca । yatra syuḥ so atra mānārhaḥ śūdro api daśamīṃ gataḥ ।। panthā deyo brāhmaṇāya striyai rājñe hyacakṣuṣe ।
vṛddhāya bhārabugnāya rogiṇe durbalāya ca ।। bhikṣāmāhṛtya śiṣṭānāṃ gṛhebhyaḥ prayato anvaham । nivedya gurave aśnīyād vāgyatastadanujñayā ।। bhavatpūrvaṃ cared bhaikṣyamupanīto dvijottamaḥ ।
bhavanmadhyaṃ tu rājanyo vaiśyastu bhavaduttaram ।। mātaraṃ vā svasāraṃ vā māturvā bhaginīṃ nijām । bhikṣeta bhikṣāṃ prathamaṃ yā cainaṃ na vimānayet ।। sajātīyagṛheṣveva sārvavarṇikameva vā ।
bhaikṣyasya caraṇaṃ proktaṃ patitādiṣu varjitam ।। vedayajñairahīnānāṃ praśastānāṃ svakarmasu । brahmacaryāhared bhaikṣaṃ gṛhebhyaḥ prayato anvaham ।। guroḥ kule na bhikṣeta na jñātikulabandhuṣu ।
alābhe tvanyagehānāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ vivarjayet ।। sarvaṃ vā vicared grāmaṃ pūrvoktānāmasaṃbhave । niyamya prayato vācaṃ diśastvanavalokayan ।। samāhṛtya tu tad bhaikṣaṃ yāvadarthamamāyayā ।
bhuñjīta prayato nityaṃ vāgyato ananyamānasaḥ ।। bhaikṣyeṇa vartayennityaṃ naikānnādī bhaved vratī । bhaikṣyeṇa vratino vṛttirupavāsasamā smṛtā ।। pūjayedaśanaṃ nityamadyāccaitadakutsayan ।
dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyet prasīdecca pratinandecca sarvaśaḥ ।। anārogyamanāyuṣyamasvargyaṃ cātibhojanam । apuṇyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ tasmāt tatparivarjayet ।। prāṅmukho annāni bhuñjīta sūryābhimukha eva vā ।
nādyādudaṅmukho nityaṃ vidhireṣa sanātanaḥ ।। prakṣālya pāṇipādau ca bhuñjāno dvirupaspṛśet । śucau deśe samāsīno bhuktvā ca dvirupaspṛśet ।। bhuktvā pītvā ca suptvā ca snātvā rathyopasarpaṇe ।
oṣṭhāvalamokau spṛṣṭvā vāso viparidhāya ca ।। retomūtrapurīṣāṇāmutsarge ayuktabhāṣaṇe । ṣṭhīvitvādhyayanārambhe kāsaśvāsāgame tathā ।। catvaraṃ vā śmaśānaṃ vā samākramya dvijottamaḥ ।
saṃdhyayorubhayostadvadācānto apyācamet punaḥ ।। caṇḍālamlecchasaṃbhāṣe strīśūdrocchiṣṭabhāṣaṇe । ucchiṣṭaṃ puruṣaṃ spṛṣṭvā bhojyaṃ cāpi tathāvidham । ācāmedaśrupāte vā lohitasya tathaiva ca ।।
bhojane saṃdhyayoḥ snātvā pītvā mūtrapurīṣayoḥ । ācānto apyācamet suptvā sakṛtsakṛdathānyataḥ ।। agnergavāmathālambhe spṛṣṭvā prayatameva vā । strīṇāmathātmanaḥ sparśe nīvīṃ vā paridhāya ca ।।
upaspṛśejjalaṃ vārdraṃ tṛṇaṃ vā bhūmimeva vā । keśānāṃ cātmanaḥ sparśe vāsaso akṣālitasya ca ।। anuṣṇābhiraphenābiraduṣṭābhiśca dharmataḥ । śaucepsuḥ sarvadācāmedāsīnaḥ prāgudaṅmukhaḥ ।।
śiraḥ prāvṛtya kaṇṭhaṃ vā muktakacchasikho api vā । akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucamācānto apyaśucirbhavet ।। sopānatko jalastho vā noṣṇīṣī vācamed budhaḥ । na caiva varṣadhārābhirna tiṣṭhan noddhṛtodakaiḥ ।।
naikahastārpitajalairvinā sūtreṇa vā punaḥ । na pādukāsanastho vā bahirjānurathāpi vā ।। na jalpan na hasan prekṣan śayānaḥ prahva eva ca । nāvīkṣitābhiḥ phenādyairupetābhirathāpi vā ।।
śūdrāśucikaronmuktairna kṣārābhistathaiva ca । na caivāṅgulibhiḥ śabdaṃ na kurvan nānyamānasaḥ ।। na varṇarasaduṣṭābhirna caiva pradarodakaiḥ । na pāṇikṣubhitābhirvā na bahiṣkakṣa eva vā ।।
hṛdgābhiḥ pūyate vipraḥ kaṇṭhyābhiḥ kṣatriyaḥ śuciḥ । prāśitābhistathāvaiśyaḥ strīśūdrau sparśato antataḥ ।। aṅguṣṭhamūlāntarato rekhāyāṃ brāhmamucyate । antarāṅguṣṭhadeśinyo pitṝṇāṃ tīrthamuttamam ।।
kaniṣṭhāmūlataḥ paścāt prājāpatyaṃ pracakṣate । aṅgulyagre smṛtaṃ daivaṃ tadevārṣaṃ prakīrtitam ।। mūle vā daivamārṣaṃ syādāgneyaṃ madhyataḥ smṛtaṃ । tadeva saumikaṃ tīrthametajjñātvā na muhyati ।।
brāhmeṇaiva tu tīrthena dvijo nityamupaspṛśet । kāyena vātha daivena tu pitryeṇa vai dvijāḥ ।। triḥ prāśnīyādapaḥ pūrvaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prayatastataḥ । saṃmṛjyāṅguṣṭhamūlena mukhaṃ vai samupaspṛśet ।।
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu spṛśennetradvayaṃ tataḥ । tarjanyaṅguṣṭhayogena spṛśennāsāpṛṭadvayam ।। kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayogena śravaṇe samupaspṛśet । sarvāsāmatha yogena hṛdayaṃ tu talena vā ।
saṃspṛśed vā śirastadvadaṅguṣṭhenāthavā dvayam ।। triḥ prāśnīyād yadambhastu suprītāstena devatāḥ । brahmā viṣṇurmaheśaśca bhavantītyanuśuśrumaḥ ।। gaṅgā ca yamunā caiva prīyete parimārjanāt ।
saṃspṛṣṭayorlocanayoḥ prīyete śaśibhāskarau ।। nāsatyadastrau prīyete spṛṣṭe nāsāpuṭadvaye । karṇayoḥ spṛṣṭayostadvat prīyete cānilānalau ।। saṃspṛṣṭe hṛdaye cāsya prīyante sarvadevatāḥ ।
mūrdhni saṃsparśanādekaḥ prītaḥ sa puruṣo bhavet ।। nocchiṣṭaṃ kurvate mukhyā vipruṣo aṅgaṃ nayanti yāḥ । dantavad dantalagneṣu jihvāsparśe aśucirbhavet ।। spṛśānti bindavaḥ pādau ya ācāmayataḥ parān ।
bhūmigaiste samā jñeyā na tairaprayato bhavet ।। maduparke ca some ca tāmbūlasya ca bhakṣaṇe । phalamūle cekṣudaṇḍe na doṣaṃ prāha ve manuḥ ।। pracaraṃścānnapāneṣu dravyahasto bhavennaraḥ ।
bhūmau nikṣipya tad dravyamācamyābhyukṣayet tu tat ।। taijasaṃ vai samādāya yadyucchiṣṭo bhaved dvijaḥ । bhūmau nikṣipya tad dravyamācamyābhyukṣayet tu tat ।। yadyamatraṃ samādāya bhaveduccheṣaṇānvitaḥ ।
anidhāyaiva tad dravyamācāntaḥ śucitāmiyāt । vastrādiṣu vikalpaḥ syāt tatsaṃspṛṣṭvācamediha ।। araṇye anudake rātrau cauravyāghrākule pathi । kṛtvā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā dravyahasto na duṣyati ।।
nidhāya dakṣiṇe karṇe brahmasūtramudaṅmukhaḥ । ahni kuryācchakṛnmūtraṃ rātrau ced dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ।। antardhāya mahīṃ kāṣṭhaiḥ patrairloṣṭhatṛṇena vā । prāvṛtya ca śiraḥ kuryād viṇmūtrasya visarjanam ।।
chāyākūpanadīgoṣṭhacaityāmbhaḥ pathi bhasmasu । agnau caiva śmaśāne ca viṇmūtre na samācaret ।। na gomaye na kṛṣṭe vā mahāvṛkṣe na śāḍvale । na tiṣṭhan vā na nirvāsā na ca parvatamastake ।।
na jīrṇadevāyatane na valmīke kadācana । na sasattveṣu garteṣu na gacchan vā samācaret ।। tuṣāṅgārakapāleṣu rājamārge tathaiva ca । na kṣetre na vile vāpi na tīrthe na catuṣpathe ।।
nodyānodasamīpe vā noṣare na parāśucau । na sopānatpāduko vā chatrī vā nāntarikṣake ।। na caivābhimukhe strīṇāṃ gurubrāhmaṇayorgavām । na devadevālayayorapāmapi kadācana ।।
na jyotīṃṣi nirīkṣanvānasaṃdhyābhimukho apivā । pratyādityaṃ pratyanalaṃ pratisomaṃ tathaiva ca ।। āhṛtya mṛttikāṃ kūlāllepagandhāpakarṣaṇam । kuryādatandritaḥ śaucaṃ viśuddhairuddhṛtodakaiḥ ।।
nāharenmṛttikāṃ vipraḥ pāṃśulānna ca kardamāt । na mārgānnoṣarād deśācchaucaśiṣṭāṃ parasya ca ।। na devāyatanāt kūpād grāmānna ca jalāt tathā । upaspṛśet tato nityaṃ pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ ।।
evaṃ daṇḍādibhiryuktaḥ śaucācārasamanvitaḥ । āhūto adhyayanaṃ kuryād vīkṣamāṇo gurormukham ।। nityamudyatapāṇiḥ syāt sādhvācāraḥ susaṃyataḥ । āsyatāmiti coktaḥ sannāsītābhimukhaṃ guroḥ ।।
pratiśravaṇasaṃbhāṣe śayāno na samācaret । nāsīno na ca bhuñjāno na tiṣṭhanna parāṅmukhaḥ ।। nīcaṃ śayyāsanaṃ cāsya sarvadā gurusannidhau । gurostu cakṣurviṣaye na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet ।।
nodāharedasya nāma parokṣamapi kevalam । na caivāsyānukurvota gatibhāṣaṇaceṣṭitam ।। guroryatra parīvādo nindā cāpi pravartate । karṇaiṃ tatra pidhātavyau gantavyaṃ vā tato anyataḥ ।।
dūrastho nārcayedenaṃ na kruddho nāntike striyāḥ । na caivāsyottaraṃ brūyāt sthito nāsīta sannidhau ।। udakumbhaṃ kuśān puṣpaṃ samidho asyāharet sadā । mārjanaṃ lepanaṃ nityamaṅgānāṃ vai samācaret ।।
nāsya nirmālyaśayanaṃ pādukopānahāvapi । ākramedāsanaṃ cāsya chāyādīn vā kadācana ।। sādhayed dantakāṣṭhādīn labdhaṃ cāsmai nivedayet । anāpṛcchya na gantavyaṃ bhavet priyahite rataḥ ।।
na pādau sārayedasya saṃnidhāne kadācana । jṛmbhitaṃ hasitaṃ caiva kaṇṭhaprāvaraṇaṃ tathā । varjayet sannidhau nityamavasphocanameva ca ।। yathākālamadhīyīta yāvanna vimanā guruḥ ।
āsītādho guroḥ kūrce phalake vā samāhitaḥ ।। āsane śayane yāne naiva tiṣṭhet kadācana । dhāvantamanudhāveta gacchantamanugacchati ।। go aśvoṣṭrayānaprāsādaprastareṣu kaṭeṣu ca ।
āsīta guruṇā sārdhaṃ śilāphalakanauṣu ca ।। jitendriyaḥ syāt satataṃ vaśyātmākrodhanaḥ śuciḥ । prayuñjīta sadā vācaṃ madhurāṃ hitabhāṣiṇīm ।। gandhamālyaṃ rasaṃ kalyāṃ śuktaṃ prāṇivihiṃsanam ।
abhyaṅgaṃ cāñcanopānacchatradhāraṇameva ca ।। kāmaṃ lobhaṃ bhayaṃ nidrāṃ gītavāditranartanam । ātarjanaṃ parīvādaṃ strīprekṣālambhanaṃ tathā । paropaghātaṃ paiśunyaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet ।।
udakumbhaṃ sumanaso gośakṛnmṛttikāṃ kuśān । āhared yāvadarthāni bhaikṣyaṃ cāharahaścaret ।। kṛtaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ sarvaṃ varjyaṃ paryuṣitaṃ ca yat । anṛtyadarśo satataṃ bhaved gītādiniḥ spṛhaḥ ।।
nādityaṃ vai samīkṣeta na cared dantadhāvanam । ekāntamaśucistrībhiḥ śūdrāntyairabhibhāṣaṇam ।। gurūcchiṣṭaṃ bheṣajārthaṃ prayuñjīta na kāmataḥ । kalāpakarṣaṇasnānaṃ nācareddhi kadācana ।।
na kuryānmānasaṃ vipro gurostyāge kadācana । mohādvā yadi vā lobhāt tyaktena patito bhavet ।। laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ cāpi tathādhyātmikameva ca । ādadīta yato jñānaṃ na taṃ druhyet kadācana ।।
gurorapyavaliptasya kāryākāryamajānataḥ । utpathapratipannasya manustyāgaṃ samabravīt ।। gurorgurau sannihite guruvad bhaktimācaret । na cātisṛṣṭo guruṇā svān gurūnabivādayet ।।
vidyāguruṣvetadeva nityā vṛttiḥ svayoniṣu । pratiṣedhatsu cādharmāddhitaṃ copadiśatsvapi ।। śreyaḥsu guruvad vṛttiṃ nityameva samācaret । guruputreṣu dāreṣu guroścaiva svabandhuṣu ।।
bālaḥ samānajanmā vā śiṣyo vā yajñakarmaṇi । adhyāpayan gurusuto guruvanmānamarhati ।। utsādanaṃ vai gātrāṇāṃ snāpanocchiṣṭabhojane । na kuryād guruputrasya pādayoḥ śaucameva ca ।।
guruvat paripūjyāstu savarṇā guruyoṣitaḥ । asavarṇāstu saṃpūjyāḥ pratyutthānābhivādanaiḥ ।। abhyañjanaṃ snāpanaṃ ca gātrotsādanameva ca । gurupatnyā na kāryāṇi keśānāṃ ca prasādhanam ।।
gurupatnī tu yuvatī nābhivādyeha pādayoḥ । kurvota vandanaṃ bhūmyāmasāvahamiti bruvan ।। viproṣya pādagrahaṇamanvahaṃ cābhivādanam । gurudāreṣu kurvota satāṃ dharmamanusmaran ।।
mātṛṣvasā mātulānī śvaśrūścātha pitṛṣvasā । saṃpūjyā gurupatnīva samāstā gurubhāryayā ।। bhrāturbhāryopasaṃgrāhyā savarṇāhanyahanyapi । viproṣya tūpasaṃgrāhyā jñātisaṃbandhiyoṣitaḥ ।।
piturbhaginyāṃ mātuśca jyāyasyāṃ ca svasaryapi । mātṛvad vṛttimātiṣṭhenmāt tābhyo garīyasī ।। evamācārasaṃpannamātmavantamadāmbhikam । vedamadhyāpayed dharmaṃ purāṇāṅgāni nityaśaḥ ।।
saṃvatsaroṣite śiṣye gururjñānamanirdiśan । harate duṣkṛtaṃ tasya śiṣyasya vasato guruḥ ।। ācāryaputraḥ śuśrūṣurjñānado dhārmikaḥ śuciḥ । śakto annador'tho svaḥsādhuradhyāpyā daśa dharmataḥ ।।
kṛtajñaśca tathādrohī medhāvī śubhakṛnnaraḥ । āptaḥ priyo atha vidhivat ṣaḍadhyāpyā dvijātayaḥ । eteṣu brahmaṇo dānamanyatra tu yathoditān ।। ācamya saṃyato nityamadhīyīta udaṅmukhaḥ ।
upasaṃgṛhya tatpādau vīkṣamāṇo gurormukham । adhīṣva bho iti brūyād virāmo astviti cāramet ।। prākkūlān paryupāsīnaḥ pavitraiścaiva pāvitaḥ । prāṇāyāmaistribhiḥ pūtastata oṅkāramarhati ।।
brāhmaṇaḥ praṇavaṃ kuryādante ca vidhivad dvijaḥ । kuryādadhyayanaṃ nityaṃ sa brahmāñjalipūrvataḥ ।। sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vedaścakṣuḥ sanātanam । adhīyītāpyayaṃ nityaṃ brāhmaṇyāccyavate anyathā ।।
yo adhīyīta ṛco nityaṃ kṣīrāhutyā sa devatāḥ । prīṇāti tarpayantyenaṃ kāmaistṛptāḥ sadaiva hi ।। yajūṃṣyadhīte niyataṃ dadhnā prīṇāti devatāḥ । sāmānyadhīte prīṇāti ghṛtāhutibhiranvaham ।।
atharvāṅgiraso nityaṃ madhvā prīṇāti devatāḥ । dharmāṅgāni purāṇāni māṃsaistarpayate surān ।। apāṃ samīpe niyato naityakaṃ vidhimāśritaḥ । gāyatrīmapyadhīyīta gatvāraṇyaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।
sahasraparamāṃ devīṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām । gāyatrīṃ vai japennityaṃ japayajñaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। gāyatrīṃ caiva vedāṃśca tulayātolayat prabhuḥ । ekataścaturo vedān gāyatrīṃ ca tathaikataḥ ।।
oṅkāramāditaḥ kṛtvā vyāhṛtīstadanantaram । tato adhīyīta sāvitrīmekāgraḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ ।। purākalpe samutpannā bhūrbhuvaḥsvaḥ sanātanāḥ । mahāvyāhṛtayastistraḥ sarvāśubhanibarhaṇāḥ ।।
pradhānaṃ puruṣaḥ kālo viṣṇurbrahmā maheśvaraḥ । sattvaṃ rajastamastistraḥ kramād vyāhṛtayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। oṅkārastat paraṃ brahma sāvitrī syāt tadakṣaram । eṣa mantro mahāyogaḥ sārāt sāra udāhṛtaḥ ।।
yo adhīte ahanyahanyetāṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram । vijñāyārthaṃ brahmacārī sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। gāyatrī vedajananī gāyatrī lokapāvanī । na gāyatryāḥ paraṃ japyametad vijñāya mucyate ।।
śrāvaṇasya tu māsasya paurṇamāsyāṃ dvijottamāḥ । āṣāḍhyāṃ proṣṭhapadyāṃ vā vedopākaraṇaṃ smṛtam ।। utsṛjya grāmanagaraṃ māsān vipror'ddhapañcamān । adhīyīta śucau deśe brahmacārī samāhitaḥ ।।
puṣye tu chandasāṃ kuryād bahirutsarjanaṃ dvijaḥ । māghaśuklasya vā prāpte pūrvāhne prathame ahani ।। chandāṃsyūrdhvamathobhyasyecchuklapakṣeṣu vai dvijaḥ । vedāṅgāni purāṇāni kṛṣṇapakṣe ca mānavam ।।
imān nityamanadhyāyānadīyāno vivarjayet । adhyāpanaṃ ca kurvāṇo hyabhyasyannapi yatnataḥ ।। karṇaśrave anile rātrau divā pāṃśusamūhane । vidyutstanitavarṣeṣu maholkānāṃ ca saṃplave ।
ākālikamanadhyāyameteṣvāha prajāpatiḥ ।। etānabhyuditān vidyād yadā prāduṣkṛtāgniṣu । tadā vidyādanadhyāyamanṛtau cābhradarśane ।। nirghāte bhūmicalane jyotiṣāṃ copasarjane ।
etānākālikān vidyādanadhyāyānṛtāvapi ।। prāduṣkṛteṣvagniṣu tu vidyutstanitanisvane । sajyotiḥ syādanadhyāyaḥ śeṣarātrau yathā divā ।। nityānadhyāya eva syād grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca ।
dharmanaipuṇyakāmānāṃ pūtigandhe ca nityaśaḥ ।। antaḥ śavagate grāme vṛṣalasya ca sannidhau । anadhyāyo rudyamāne samavāye janasya ca ।। udake madhyarātre ca viṇmūtre ca visarjane ।
ucchiṣṭaḥ śrāddhabuk caiva manasāpi na cintayet ।। pratigṛhya dvijo vidvānekodiṣṭasya ketanam । tryahaṃ na kīrtayed brahma rājño rāhośca sūtake ।। yāvadeko anudiṣṭasya sneho gandhaśca tiṣṭhati ।
viprasya viduṣo dehe tāvad brahma na kīrtayet ।। śayānaḥ prauḍhapādaśca kṛtvā caivāvasakthikām । nādhīyītāmiṣaṃ jagdhvā sūtakānnādyameva ca ।। nīhāre bāṇaśabde ca saṃdhyayorubhayorapi ।
amāvāsyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyaṣṭamīṣu ca ।। upākarmaṇi cotsarge trirātraṃ kṣapaṇaṃ smṛtam । aṣṭakāsu tvahorātraṃ ṛtvantyāsu ca rātriṣu ।। mārgaśīrṣe tathā pauṣe māghamāse tathaiva ca ।
tistro aṣṭakāḥ samākhyātā kṛṣṇapakṣetu sūribhiḥ ।। śleṣmātakasya chāyāyāṃ śālmalermadhukasya ca । kadācidapi nādhyeyaṃ kovidārakapitthayoḥ ।। samānavidye ca mṛte tathā sabrahmacāriṇi ।
ācārye saṃsthite vāpi trirātraṃ kṣapaṇaṃ smṛtam ।। chidrāṇyetāni viprāṇāṃye anadhyāyaḥ prakīrtitāḥ । hiṃsanti rākṣasāsteṣu tasmādetān vivarjayet ।। naityake nāstyanadhyāyaḥ saṃdhyopāsana eva ca ।
upākarmaṇi karmānte homamantreṣu caiva hi ।। ekāmṛcamathaikaṃ vā yajuḥ sāmāthavā punaḥ । aṣṭakādyāsvadhīyīta mārute cātivāyati ।। anadhyāyastu nāṅgeṣu netihāsapurāṇayoḥ ।
na dharmaśāstreṣvanyeṣu parvaṇyetāni varjayet ।। eṣa dharmaḥ samāsena kīrtito brahmacāriṇām । brahmaṇābhihitaḥ pūrvamṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।। yo anyatra kurute yatnamanadhītya śrutiṃ dvijaḥ ।
sa saṃmūḍho na saṃbhāṣyo vedabāhyo dvijātibhiḥ ।। na vedapāṭhamātreṇa saṃtuṣṭo vai bhaved dvijaḥ । pāṭhamātrāvasannastu paṅke gauriva sīdati ।। yo adhītya vidhivad vedaṃ vedārthaṃ na vicārayet ।
sasānvayaḥ śūdrakalpaḥ pātratāṃ na prapadyate ।। yadi tvātyantikaṃ vāsaṃ kartumicchati vai gurau । yuktaḥ paricaredenamāśarīravimokṣaṇāt ।। gatvā vanaṃ vā vidhivajjuhuyājjātavedasam ।
adhīyīta sadā nityaṃ brahmaniṣṭhaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। sāvitrīṃ śatarudrīyaṃ vedāntāṃśca viśeṣataḥ । abhyaset satataṃ yukte bhasmasnānaparāyaṇaḥ ।। vedāgame samyagiheritaṃ vaḥ ।
svāyaṃbhuvo yanmanurāha devaḥ ।। yo anutiṣṭhati vidhiṃ vidhānavit । yāti tat padamanāmayaṃ śivam ।। vedaṃ vedau tathā vedān vedān vā caturo dvijāḥ ।
adhītya cādhigamyārthaṃ tataḥ snāyād dvijottamaḥ ।। gurave tu varaṃ dattvā snāyīta tadanujñayā । cīrṇavrato atha yuktātmā saśaktaḥ snātumarhati ।। vaiṇavīṃ dhārayed yaṣṭimantarvāsastathottaram ।
yajñopavītadvitayaṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum ।। chatraṃ coṣṇīṣamamalaṃ pāduke cāpyupānahau । raukme ca kuṇḍale vedaṃ kṛttakeśanakhaḥ śuciḥ ।। svādhyāye nityayuktaḥ syād bahirmālyaṃ na dhārayet ।
anyatrakāñcanād vipronaraktāṃ bibhṛyāt strajam ।। śuklāmbaradharo nityaṃ sugandhaḥ priyadarśanaḥ । na jīrṇamalavadvāsā bhaved vai vibhave sati ।। na raktamulbaṇaṃ cānyadhṛtaṃ vāso na kuṇḍikām ।
nopānahau strajaṃ cātha pāduke ca prayojayet ।। upavītamalaṅkāraṃ darbhān kṛṣṇājināni ca । nāpasavyaṃ parīdadhyād vāso na vikṛtaṃ vaset ।। āhared vidhivad dārān sadṛśānātmanaḥ śubhān ।
rūpalakṣaṇasaṃyuktān yonidoṣavivarjitān ।। amātṛgotraprabhavāmasamānarṣigotrajām । āhared brāhmaṇo bhāryāṃ śīlaśaucasamanvitām ।। ṛtukālābhigāmī syād yāvat putro abhijāyate ।
varjayet pratiṣiddhāni prayatnena dināni tu ।। ṣaṣṭhyaṣṭamīṃ pañcadaśīṃ dvādaśīṃ ca caturdaśīm । brahmacārī bhavennityaṃ tadvajjanmatrayāhani ।। ādadhītāvasathyāgniṃ juhuyājjātavedasam ।
vratāni snātako nityaṃ pāvanāni ca pālayet ।। vedoditaṃ svakaṃ karma nityaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ । akurvāṇaḥ patatyāśu narakānatibhīṣaṇān ।। abyaset prayato vedaṃ mahāyajñān na hāpayet ।
kuryād gṛhyāṇi karmāṇi saṃdhyopāsanameva ca ।। sakhyaṃ samādhaikaiḥ kuryādupeyādīśvaraṃ sadā । daivatānyapi gaccheta kuryād bhāryābhipoṣaṇam ।। na dharmaṃ khyāpayed vidvān na pāpaṃ gūhayedapi ।
kurvotātmahitaṃ nityaṃ sarvabhūtānikampakaḥ ।। vayasaḥ karmaṇor'thasya śrutasyābhijanasya ca । veṣavāgbuddhisārūpyamācaran vicaret sadā ।। śrutismṛtyuditaḥ samyak sādhubhiryaśca sevitaḥ ।
tamācāraṃ niṣeveta nehetānyatra karhicit ।। yenāsya pitaro yātā yena yātāḥ pitāmahāḥ । tena yāyāt satāṃ mārgaṃ tena gacchan na riṣyati ।। nityaṃ svādhyāyaśīlaḥ syānnityaṃ yajñopavītavān ।
satyavādī jitakrodho brahmabhūyāya kalpate ।। saṃdhyāsnānaparo nityaṃ brahmayajñuparāyaṇaḥ । anasūyī mṛdurdānto gṛhasthaḥ pretya vardhate ।। vītarāgabhayakrodho lobhamohavivarjitaḥ ।
sāvitrījāpyanirataḥ śrāddhakṛnmucyate gṛhī ।। mātāpitrorhite yukto gobrāhmaṇahite rataḥ । dānto yajvā devabhakto brahmaloke mahīyate ।। trivargasevī satataṃ devatānāṃ ca pūjanam ।
kuryādaharaharnityaṃ namasyet prayataḥ surān ।। vibhāgaśīlaḥ satataṃ kṣamāyukto dayālukaḥ । gṛhasthastu samākhyāto na gṛheṇa gṛhī bhavet ।। kṣamā dayā ca vijñānaṃ satyaṃ caiva damaḥ śamaḥ ।
adhyātmanirataṃ jñānametad brāhmaṇalakṣaṇam ।। etasmānna pramādyeta viśeṣeṇa dvijottamaḥ । yathāśaktiṃ caran karma ninditāni vivarjayet ।। vidhūya mohakalilaṃ labdhvā yogamanuttamam ।
gṛhastho mucyate bandhāt nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। vigarhātikramākṣepahiṃsābandhavadhātmanām । anyamanyusamutthānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ marṣaṇaṃ kṣamā ।। svaduḥ kheṣviva kāruṇyaṃ paraduḥ kheṣu sauhṛdāt ।
dayeti munayaḥ prāhuḥ sākṣād dharmasya sādhanam ।। caturdaśānāṃ vidyānāṃ dhāraṇaṃ hi yatārthataḥ । vijñānamiti tad vidyād yena dharmo vivardhate ।। adhītya vidhivad vidyāmarthaṃ caivopalabhya tu ।
dharmakāryānnivṛttaścenna tad vijñānamiṣyate ।। satyena lokāñjayati satyaṃ tatparamaṃ padam । yathābhūtapravād tu satyamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।। damaḥ śarīroparamaḥ śamaḥ prajñāprisādajaḥ ।
adhyātmamakṣaraṃ vidyād yatra gatvā na śocati ।। yayā sa devo bhagavān vidyayā vedyate paraḥ । sākṣād devo mahādevastajjñānamiti kīrtitam ।। tanniṣṭhastatparo vidvānnityamakrodhanaḥ śuciḥ ।
mahāyajñaparo vipro labhate tadanuttamam ।। dharmasyāyatanaṃ yatnāccharīraṃ paripālayet । na hi dehaṃ vinā rudraḥ puruṣairvidyate paraḥ ।। nityadharmārthakāmeṣu yujyeta niyato dvijaḥ ।
na dharmavarjitaṃ kāmamarthaṃ vā manasā smaret ।। sīdannapi hi dharmeṇa na tvadharmaṃ samācaret । dharmo hi bhagavān devo gatiḥ sarveṣu jantuṣu ।। bhūtānāṃ priyakārī syāt na paradrohakarmadhīḥ ।
na vedadevatānindāṃ kuryāt taiśca na saṃvaset ।। yastvimaṃ niyataṃ vipro dharmādhyāyaṃ paṭhecchuciḥ । adhyāpayet śrāvayed vā brahmaloke mahīyate ।। na hiṃsyāt sarvabhūtāninānṛtaṃ vāvadet kvacit ।
nāhitaṃ nāpriyaṃ vākyaṃ na stenaḥ syād kadācana ।। tṛṇaṃ vā yadi vā śākaṃ mṛdaṃ vā jalameva vā । parasyāpaharañjanturnarakaṃ pratipadyate ।। na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇīyānna śūdrapatitādapi ।
na cānyasmādaśaktaśca ninditān varjayed budhaḥ ।। nityaṃ yācanako na syāt punastaṃ naiva yācayet । prāṇānapaharatyevaṃ yācakastasya durmatiḥ ।। na devadravyahārī syād viśeṣeṇa dvijottamaḥ ।
brahmasvaṃ vā nāpaharedāpadyapi kadācana ।। na viṣaṃ viṣamityāhurbrahmasvaṃ viṣamucyate । devasvaṃ cāpi yatnena sadā pariharet tataḥ ।। puṣpe śākrodake kāṣṭhe tathā mūle phale tṛṇe ।
adattādānamasteyaṃ manuḥ prāha prajāpatiḥ ।। grahītavyāni puṣpāṇi devārcanavidhau dvijāḥ । naikasmādeva niyatamananujñāya kevalam ।। tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ prakāśaṃ vai hared budhaḥ ।
dharmārthaṃ kevalaṃ viprā hyanyathā patito bhavet ।। tilamudgayavādīnāṃ muṣṭirgrāhyā pathi sthitaiḥ । kṣudhārtairnānyathā viprā dharmavidbhiriti sthitiḥ ।। na dharmasyāpadeśena pāpaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caret ।
vratena pāpaṃ pracchādya kurvan strīśūdradambhanam ।। pretyeha cedṛśo vipro garhyate brahmavādibhiḥ । chadmanācaritaṃ yacca vrataṃ rakṣāṃsi gacchati ।। aliṅgī liṅgiveṣeṇa yo vṛttimupajīvati ।
sa liṅgināṃ haredenastiryagyonau ca jāyate ।। baiḍālavratinaḥ pāpā loke dharmavināśakāḥ । sadyaḥ patanti pāpeṣu karmaṇastasya tat phalam ।। pāṣaṇḍino vikarmasthān vāmācārāṃstathaiva ca ।
pañcarātrān pāśupatān vāṅmātreṇāpi nārcayet ।। vedanindāratān martyān devanindāratāṃstathā । dvijanindāratāṃścaiva manasāpi na cintayet ।। yājanaṃ yonisaṃbandhaṃ sahavāsaṃ ca bhāṣaṇam ।
kurvāṇaḥ patate jantustasmād yatnena varjayet ।। devadrohād gurudrohaḥ koṭikoṭiguṇādhikaḥ । jñānāpavādo nāstikyaṃ tasmāt koṭiguṇādhikam ।। gobhiśca daivatairvipraiḥ kṛṣyā rājopasevayā ।
kulānyakulatāṃ yānti yāni hīnāni dharmataḥ ।। kuvivāhaiḥ kriyālopairvedānadhyayanena ca । kulānyakulatāṃ yānti brāhmaṇātikrameṇa ca ।। anṛtāt pāradāryācca tathābhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇāt ।
aśrautadharmācaraṇāt kṣipraṃ naśyati vai kulam ।। aśrotriyeṣu vai dānād vṛṣaleṣu tathaiva ca । vihitācārahīneṣu kṣipraṃ naśyati vai kulam ।। nādhārmikairvṛte grāme na vyādhibahule bhṛśam ।
na śūdrarājye nivasenna pāṣaṇḍajanairvṛte ।। himavadvindhyayormadhye pūrvapaścimayoḥ śubham । muktvā samudrayordeśaṃ nānyatra nivased dvijaḥ ।। kṛṣṇo vā yatra carati mṛgo nityaṃ svabhāvataḥ ।
puṇyāśca viśrutā nadyastatra vā nivased dvijaḥ ।। ardhakrośānnadīkūlaṃ varjayitvā dvijottamaḥ । nānyatra nivaset puṇyaṃ nāntyajagrāmasannidhau ।। na saṃvasecca patitairna caṇḍālairna pukkasaiḥ ।
na mūrkhairnāvaliptaiśca nāntyairnāntyāvasāyibhiḥ ।। ekaśayyāsanaṃ paṅktirbhāṇḍapakvānnamiśraṇam । yājanādhyāpane yonistathaiva sahabhojanam ।। sahādhyāyastu daśamaḥ sahayājanameva ca ।
ekādaśa samuddiṣṭā doṣāḥ sāṅkaryasaṃjñitāḥ ।। samīpe vā vyavasthānāt pāpaṃ saṃkramate nṛṇām । tasmāt sarvaprayatnena sāṅkaryaṃ parivarjayet ।। ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭā ye na spṛśanti parasparam ।
bhasmanā kṛtamaryādā na teṣāṃ saṃkaro bhavet ।। agninā bhasmanā caiva salilenāvasekataḥ । dvāreṇa stambhamārgeṇa ṣaḍbhiḥ paṅktirvibhidyate ।। na kuryācchuṣkavairāṇi vivādaṃ ca na paiśunam ।
parakṣetre gāṃ dhayantīṃ na cācakṣīta kasyacit । na saṃvadet sūtake ca na kañcinmarmaṇi spṛśet ।। na sūryapariveṣaṃ vā nendracāpaṃ śavāgnikam । parasmai kathayed vidvān śaśinaṃ vā kadācana ।।
na kuryād bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ virodhaṃ bandhubhistathā । ātmanaḥ pratikūlāni pareṣāṃ na samācaret ।। tithiṃ pakṣasya na brūyāt na nakṣatrāṇi nirdiśet । nodakyāmabhibhāṣeta nāśuciṃ vā dvijottamaḥ ।।
na devaguruviprāṇāṃ dīyamānaṃ tu vārayet । na cātmānaṃ praśaṃsed vā paranindāṃ ca varjayet । vedanindāṃ devanindāṃ prayatnena vivarjayet ।। yastu devānṛṣīn viprānvedān vā nindati dvijaḥ ।
na tasya niṣkṛtirdṛṣṭā śāstreṣviha munīśvarāḥ ।। nindayed vai guruṃ devaṃ vedaṃ vā sopabṛṃhaṇam । kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ raurave pacyate naraḥ ।। tūṣṇīmāsīta nindāyāṃ na brūyāt kiñciduttaram ।
karṇau pidhāya gantavyaṃ na caitānavalokayet ।। varjayed vai rahasyāni pareṣāṃ gūhayed budhaḥ । vivādaṃ svajanaiḥ sārdhaṃ na kuryād vai kadācana ।। na pāpaṃ pāpināṃ brūyādapāpaṃ vā dvijāttamāḥ ।
satenatulyadoṣaḥ syānmithyā dvirdeṣavān bhavet ।। yāni mithyābhiśastānāṃ patantyaśrūṇi rodanāt । tāniputrān paśūnghninti teṣāṃ mithyābhiśaṃsinām ।। brihmahatyāsurāpāne steyagurvaṅganāgame ।
dṛṣṭaṃ viśodhanaṃ vṛddhairnāsti mithyābhiśaṃsane ।। nekṣetodyantamādityaṃ śaśinaṃ cānimittataḥ । nāstaṃ yāntaṃ na vāristhaṃ nopasṛṣṭaṃ na maghyagam । tirohitaṃ vāsasā vā nādarśāntaragāminam ।।
na nagnāṃ striyamīkṣeta puruṣaṃ vā kadācana । na ca mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā na ca saṃspṛṣṭamaithunam । nāśuciḥ sūryasomādīn grahānālokayed budhaḥ ।। patitavyaṅgacaṇḍālānucchiṣṭān nāvalokayet ।
nābhibhāṣeta ca paramucchiṣṭo vāvaguṇṭhitaḥ ।। na paśyet pretasaṃsparśaṃ na kruddhasya gurormukham । na tailodakayośchāyāṃ na patnīṃ bhojane sati । nāmuktabandhanāṅgāṃ vā nonmattaṃ mattameva vā ।।
nāśnīyāt bhāryayā sārdhaṃnaināmīkṣeta cāśnatīm । kṣuvantīṃ jṛmbhamāṇāṃ vā nāsanasthāṃ yathāsukham ।। nodake cātmano rūpaṃ na kūlaṃ śvabhrameva vā । na laṅghayecca mūtraṃ vā nādhitiṣṭhet kadācana ।।
na śūdrāya matiṃ dadyāt kṛśaraṃ pāyasaṃ dadhi । nocchiṣṭaṃ vā madhu ghṛtaṃ na ca kṛṣṇājinaṃ haviḥ ।। na caivāsmai vrataṃ dadyānna ca dharmaṃ vaded budhaḥ । na ca krodhavaśaṃ gacched dveṣaṃ rāgaṃ ca varjayet ।।
lobhaṃ dambhaṃ tathā yatnādasūyāṃ jñānakutsanam । īrṣyāṃ madaṃ tathā śokaṃ mohaṃ ca parivarjayet ।। na kuryāt kasyacit pīḍāṃ sutaṃ śiṣyaṃ ca tāḍayet । na hīnānupaseveta na ca tīkṣṇamatīn kvacit ।।
nātmānaṃ cāvamanyeta dainyaṃ yatnena varjayet । na viśiṣṭānasatkuryāt nātmānaṃ vā śaped budhaḥ ।। na nakhairvilikhed bhūmiṃ gāṃ ca saṃveśayenna hi । na nadīṣu nadīṃ brūyāt parvateṣu ca parvatān ।।
āvāse bhojane vāpi na tyajet hasayāyinam । nāvagāhedapo nagno vahniṃ nātivrajet padā ।। śiro abhyaṅgāvaśiṣṭena tailenāṅgaṃ na lepayet । na sarpaśastraiḥ krīḍeta svāni khāni na saṃspṛśet ।
romāṇi ca rahasyāni nāśiṣṭena saha vrajet ।। na pāṇipādavāṅnetracāpalyaṃ samupāśrayet । na śiśnodaracāpalyaṃ na ca śravaṇayoḥ kvacit ।। na cāṅganakhavādaṃ vai kuryānnāñjalinā pibet ।
nābhihanyājjalaṃ padbhyāṃ pāṇinā vā kadācana ।। na śātayediṣṭakābhiḥ phalāni na phalena ca । na mlecchabhāṣāṃ śikṣeta nākarṣecca padāsanam ।। na bhedanamavasphoṭaṃ chedanaṃ vā vilekhanam ।
kuryād vimardanaṃ dhīmān nākasmādeva niṣphalam ।। notsaṅgebhakṣayed bhakṣyaṃ vṛthā ceṣṭāṃ ca nācaret । na nṛtyedathavā gāyenna vāditrāṇi vādayet ।। na saṃhatābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kaṇḍūyedātmanaḥ śiraḥ ।
na laukikaiḥ stavairdevāṃstoṣayed bāhyajairapi ।। nākṣaiḥ krīḍenna dhāveta nāpsu viṇmūtramācaret । nocchiṣṭaḥ saṃviśennityaṃ na nagnaḥ snānamācaret ।। na gacchenna paṭhed vāpi na caiva svaśiraḥ spṛśet ।
na dantairnakharomāṇi chindyāt suptaṃ na bodhayet ।। na bālātapamāsevet pretadhūmaṃ vivarjayet । naikaḥ supyācchūnyagṛhe svayaṃ nopānahau haret ।। nākāraṇād vā niṣṭhīvenna bāhubhyāṃ nadīṃ taret ।
na pādakṣālanaṃ kuryāt pādenaiva kadācana ।। nāgnau pratāpayet pādau na kāṃsye dhāvayed budhaḥ । nābhiprāsarayed devaṃ brāhmaṇān gāmathāpi vā । vāyvagniguruviprān vā sūryaṃ vā śaśinaṃ prati ।।
aśuddhaḥ śayanaṃ yānaṃ svādhyāyaṃ snānavāhanam । bahirniṣkramaṇaṃ caiva na kurvota kathañcana ।। svapnamadhyayanaṃ snānamudvartaṃ bhojanaṃ gatim । ubhayoḥ saṃdhyayornityaṃ madhyāhne caiva varjayet ।।
na spṛśet pāṇinocchiṣṭo viprogobrāhmaṇānalān । na cāsanaṃ padā vāpi na devapratimāṃ spṛśet ।। nāśuddho agniṃ paricarenna devān kīrtayedṛṣīn । nāvagāhedagādhāmbu dhārayennānimittataḥ ।।
na vāmahastenoddhatya pibed vaktreṇa vā jalam । nottaredanupaspṛśya nāpsu retaḥ samutsṛjet ।। amedhyaliptamanyad vā lohitaṃ vā viṣāṇi vā । vyatikramenna stravantīṃ nāpsu maithunamācaret ।
caityaṃ vṛkṣaṃ na vai chindyānnāpsu ṣṭhīvanamācaret ।। nāsthibhasmakapālāni na keśānna ca kaṇṭakān । tuṣāṅgārakarīṣaṃ vā nādhitiṣṭhet kadācana ।। na cāgniṃ laṅghayed dhīmān nopadadhyādadhaḥ kvacit ।
na cainaṃ pādataḥ kuryānmukhena na dhamed budhaḥ ।। na kūpamavaroheta nāvekṣetāśuciḥ kvacit । agnau na ca kṣipedagniṃ nādbhiḥ praśamayet tathā ।। suhṛnmaraṇamārtiṃ vā na svayaṃ śrāvayet parān ।
apaṇyaṃ kūṭapaṇyaṃ vā vikraye na prayojayet ।। na vahniṃ mukhaniśvāsair jvālayennāśucirbudhaḥ । puṇyasthānodakasthāne sīmāntaṃ vā kṛṣenna tu ।। na bhindyāt pūrvasamayamabhyupetaṃ kadācana ।
parasparaṃ paśūn vyālān pakṣiṇo nāvabodhayet ।। parabādhaṃ na kurvota jalavātātapādibhiḥ । kārayitvā svakarmāṇi kārūn paścānna vañcayet । sāyaṃprātar gṛhadvārān bhikṣārthaṃ nāvaghaṭṭayet ।।
bahirmālyaṃ bahirgandhaṃ bhāryayā saha bhojanam । vigṛhya vādaṃ kudvārapraveśaṃ ca vivarjayet ।। na khādanbrāhmaṇastiṣṭhenna jalped vā hasan budhaḥ । svamagniṃ naiva hastena spṛśennāpsu ciraṃ vaset ।।
na pakṣakeṇopadhamenna śūrpeṇa na pāṇinā । mukhe naiva dhamedagniṃ mukhādagnirajāyata ।। parastriyaṃ na bhāṣeta nāyājyaṃ yājayed dvijaḥ । naikaścaret sabhāṃ vipraḥ samavāyaṃ ca varjayet ।।
na devāyatanaṃ gacchet kadācid vāpradakṣiṇam । na vījayed vā vastreṇa na devāyatane svapet ।। naiko adhvānaṃ prapadyeta nādhārmikajanaiḥ saha । na vyādhidūṣitairvāpi na śūdraiḥ patitena vā ।।
nopānadvarjito vātha jalādirahitastathā । na rātrau nāriṇā sārdhaṃ na vinā ca kamaṇḍalum । nāgnigobrāhmaṇādīnāmantareṇa vrajet kvacit ।। na vatsatantrīṃ vitatāmatikrāmet kvacid dvijaḥ ।
na ninded yoginaḥ siddhān vratino vāyatīṃstathā ।। devatāyatanaṃ prājño devānāṃ caiva satriṇām । nākrāmet kāmataśchāyāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca gorapi ।। svāṃ tu nākramayecchāyāṃ patitādyairna rogibhiḥ ।
nāṅgārabhasmakeśādiṣvadhitiṣṭhet kadācana ।। varjayenmārjanīreṇuṃ snānavastraghacodakam । na bhakṣayedabhakṣyāṇi nāpeyaṃ ca pibed dvijaḥ ।। nādyācchūdrasya vipro annaṃ mohād vā yadi vānyataḥ ।
sa śūdrayoniṃ vrajati yastu bhuṅkte hyanāpadi ।। ṣaṇmāsān yo dvijo bhuṅkte śūdrasyānnaṃ vigarhitam । jīvanneva bhavecchūdro mṛtaḥ śvā cābhijāyate ।। brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrasya ca munīśvarāḥ ।
yasyānnenodarasthena mṛtastadyonimāpnuyāt ।। rājānnaṃ nartakānnaṃ ca takṣṇo annaṃ carmakāriṇaḥ । gaṇānnaṃ gaṇikānnaṃ ca ṣaṇḍhānnaṃ caiva varjayet ।। cakropajīvirajakataskaradhvajināṃ tathā ।
gāndharvalohakārānnaṃ sūtakānnaṃ ca varjayet ।। kulālacitrakarmānnaṃ vārdhuṣeḥ patitasya ca । paunarbhavacchatrikayorabhiśastasya caiva hi ।। suvarṇakāraśailūṣavyādhabaddhāturasya ca ।
cikitsakasya caivānnaṃ puṃścalyā daṇḍikasya ca ।। stenanāstikayorannaṃ devatānindakasya ca । somavikrayiṇaścānnaṃ śvapākasya viśeṣataḥ ।। bhāryājitasya caivānnaṃ yasya copapatirgṛhe ।
utsṛṣṭasya kadaryasya tathaivocchiṣṭabhojinaḥ ।। apāṅktyānnaṃ ca saṅghānnaṃ śastrājīvasya caiva hi । klībasaṃnyāsinoścānnaṃ mattonmattasya caiva hi । bhītasya ruditasyānnamavakruṣṭaṃ parikṣutam ।।
brahmadviṣaḥ pāparuceḥ śrāddhānnaṃ sūtakasya ca । vṛthāpākasya caivānnaṃ śāvānnaṃ śvaśurasya ca ।। aprajānāṃ tu nārīṇāṃ bhṛtakasya tathaiva ca । kārukānnaṃ viśeṣeṇa śastravikrayiṇastathā ।।
śauṇḍānnaṃ ghāṭikānnaṃ ca bhiṣajāmannameva ca । viddhaprajananasyānnaṃ parivittyannameva ca ।। punarbhuvo viśeṣeṇa tathaiva didhiṣūpateḥ । avajñātaṃ cāvadhūtaṃ saroṣaṃ vismayānvitam ।
gurorapi na bhoktavyamannaṃ saṃskāravarjitam ।। duṣkṛtaṃ hi manuṣyasya sarvamanne vyavasthitam । yo yasyānnaṃ samaśnāti sa tasyāśnāni kilbiṣam ।। ārdhikaḥ kulamitraśca svagopālaśca nāpitaḥ ।
ete śūdreṣu bhojyānnā yaścātmānaṃ nivedayet ।। kuśīlavaḥ kumbhakāraḥ kṣetrakarmaka eva ca । ete śūdreṣu bhojyānnā dattvā svalpaṃ paṇaṃ budhaiḥ ।। pāyasaṃ snehapakvaṃ yad gorasaṃ caiva saktavaḥ ।
piṇyākaṃ caiva tailaṃ ca śūdrād grāhyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ ।। vṛntākaṃ nālikāśākaṃ kusumbhāśmantakaṃ tathā । palāṇḍuṃ laśunaṃ śuktaṃ niryāsaṃ caiva varjayet ।। chatrākaṃ viḍvarāhaṃ ca śelaṃ peyūṣameva ca ।
vilayaṃ sumukhaṃ caiva kavakāni ca varjayet ।। gṛñjanaṃ kiṃśukaṃ caiva kakubhāṇḍaṃ tathaiva ca । udumbaramalābuṃ ca jagdhvā patati vai dvijaḥ ।। vṛthā kṛśarasaṃyāvaṃ pāyasāpūpameva ca ।
anupākṛtamāṃsaṃ ca devānnāni havīṃṣi ca ।। yavāgūṃ mātuliṅgaṃ ca matsyānapyanupākṛtān । nīpaṃ kapitthaṃ plakṣaṃ ca prayatnena vivarjayet ।। piṇyākaṃ coddhṛtasnehaṃ devadhānya tathaiva ca ।
rātrau ca tilasaṃbaddhaṃ prayatnena dadhi tyajet ।। nāśnīyāt payasā takraṃ na bījānyupajīvayet । kriyāduṣṭaṃ bhāvaduṣṭamasatsaṃsargi varjayet ।। keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca sahṛllekhaṃ ca nityaśaḥ ।
śvāghrātaṃ ca punaḥ siddhaṃ caṇḍālāvekṣitaṃ tathā ।। udakyayā ca patitairgavā cāghrātameva ca । anarcitaṃ puryuṃ ṣitaṃ paryāyānnaṃ ca nityaśaḥ ।। kākakukkuṭasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ kṛmibhiścaiva saṃyutam ।
manuṣyairapyavaghrātaṃ kuṣṭhinā spṛṣṭameva ca ।। na rajasvalayā dattaṃ na puṃścālyā saroṣayā । malabadvāsasā vāpi paravāso atha varjayet ।। vivatsāyāśca goḥ kṣīramauṣṭraṃ vānirdaśaṃ tathā ।
āvikaṃ sandhinīkṣīramapeyaṃ manurabravīt ।। balākaṃ haṃsadātyūhaṃ kalaviṅkaṃ śukaṃ tathā । kuraraṃ ca cakoraṃ ca jālapādaṃ ca kokilam ।। vāyasaṃ khañjarīṭaṃ ca śyenaṃ gṛdhraṃ tathaiva ca ।
ulūkaṃ cakravākaṃ ca bhāsaṃ pārāvatānapi । kapotaṃ ṭiṭṭibhaṃ caiva grāmakukkuṭameva ca ।। siṃhavyāghraṃ ca mārjāraṃ śvānaṃ śūkarameva ca । śṛgālaṃ markaṭaṃ caiva gardabhaṃ ca na bhakṣayet ।।
na bhakṣayet sarvamṛgān pakṣiṇo anyān vanecarān । jalecarān sthalacarān prāṇinaśceti dhāraṇā ।। godhā kūrmaḥ śaśaḥ śvāvicchalyakaśceti sattamāḥ । bhakṣyāḥ pañcanakhā nityaṃ manurāha prijāpatiḥ ।।
matsyān saśalkān bhuñjīyān māṃsaṃ rauravamevaca । nivedya devatābhyastu brāhmaṇebhyastu nānyathā ।। mayūraṃ tittiraṃ caiva kapotaṃ ca kapiñjalam । vādhrīṇasaṃ bakaṃ bhakṣyaṃ mīnahaṃsaparājitāḥ ।।
śapharaṃ siṃhatuṇḍaṃ ca tathā pāṭhīnarohitau । matsyāścaite samuddiṣṭā bhakṣaṇāya dvijottamāḥ ।। prokṣitaṃ bhakṣayedeṣāṃ māṃsaṃ ca dvijakāmyayā । yathāvidhi niyuktaṃ ca prāṇānāmapi cātyaye ।।
bhakṣayennaiva māṃsāni śeṣabhojī na lipyate । auṣadhārthamaśaktau vā niyogād yajñakāraṇāt ।। āmantritastu yaḥ śrāddhe daive vā māṃsamutsṛjet । yāvanti paśuromāṇi tāvato narakān vrajet ।।
adeyaṃ cāpyapeyaṃ ca tathaivāspṛśyameva ca । dvijātīnāmanālokyaṃ nityaṃ madyamiti sthitiḥ ।। tasmāt sarvaprakāreṇa madyaṃ nityaṃ vivarjayet । pītvā patati karmabhyastvasaṃbhāṣyo bhaved dvijaḥ ।।
bhakṣayitvā hyabhakṣyāṇi pītvāpeyānyapi dvijaḥ । nādhikārī bhavet tāvad yāvad tanna jahātyadhaḥ ।। tasmāt pariharennityamabhakṣyāṇi prayatnataḥ । apeyāni ca vipro vai tathā ced yāti rauravam ।।
ahanyahani kartavyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ mahāmune । tadācakṣvākhilaṃ karma yena mucyeta bandhanāt ।। vakṣye samāhitā yūyaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ gadato mama । ahanyahani kartavyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ kramād vidhim ।।
brāhme muhūrte tūtthāya dharmamarthaṃ ca cintayet । kāyakleśaṃ tadudbhūtaṃ dhyāyīta manaseśvaram ।। uṣaḥ kāle atha saṃprāpte kṛtvā cāvaśyakaṃ budhaḥ । snāyānnadīṣu suddhāsu śaucaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi ।।
prātaḥ snānena pūyante ye api pāpakṛto janāḥ । tasmāt sarvaprayatnena prātaḥ snānaṃ samācaret ।। prātaḥ snānaṃ praśaṃsanti dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakaraṃ śubham । ṛṣīṇāmṛṣitā nityaṃ prātaḥ snānānna saṃśayaḥ ।।
mukhe suptasya satataṃ lālā yāḥ saṃstravanti hi । tato naivācaret karma akṛtvā snānamāditaḥ ।। alakṣmīḥ kālakarṇo ca duḥ svapnaṃ durvicintitam । prātaḥ snānena pāpāni pūyante nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
na ca snānaṃ vinā puṃsāṃ pāvanaṃ karma susmṛtam । home japye viśeṣeṇa tasmāt snānaṃ samācaret ।। aśaktāvaśiraskaṃ vā snānamasya vidhīyate । ārdreṇa vāsasā vātha mārjanaṃ kāpilaṃ smṛtam ।।
asāmarthye samutpanne snānamevaṃ samācaret । brāhmādīni yathāśaktau snānānyāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।। brāhmamāgneyamuddiṣṭaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyameva ca । vāruṇaṃ yaugikaṃ tadvat ṣoḍhā snānaṃ prakīrtitam ।।
brāhmaṃ tu mārjanaṃ mantraiḥ kuśaiḥ sodakabindubhiḥ । āgneyaṃ bhasmanā pādamastakāddehadhūlanam ।। gavāṃ hi rajasā proktaṃ vāyavyaṃ snānamuttamam । yattu sātapavarṣeṇa snānaṃ tad divyamucyate ।।
vāruṇaṃ cāvagāhastu mānasaṃ tvātmavedanam । yaugikaṃ snānamākhyātaṃ yogo viṣṇuvicintanam ।। ātmatīrthamiti khyātaṃ sevitaṃ brahmavādibhiḥ । manaḥ śucikaraṃ puṃsāṃ nityaṃ tat snānamācaret ।।
śaktaśced vāruṇaṃ vidvān prājāpatyaṃ tathaiva ca । prakṣālya dantakāṣṭhaṃ vai bhakṣayitvā vidhānataḥ ।। ācamya prayato nityaṃ snānaṃ prātaḥ samācaret । madhyāṅgulisamasthaulyaṃ dvādaśāṅgulasaṃmitam ।।
satvacaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ syāt tadagreṇa tu dhāvayet । kṣīravṛkṣasamudbhūtaṃ mālatīsaṃbhavaṃ śubham । apāmārgaṃ ca bilvaṃ ca karavīraṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। varjayitvā ninditāni gṛhītvaikaṃ yathoditam ।
parihṛtya dinaṃ pāpaṃ bhakṣayed vai vidhānavit ।। notpāṭayeddantakāṣṭaṃnāṅgulyā dhāvayet kvacit । prakṣālya bhaṅktvā tajjahyācchucaudeśe samāhitaḥ ।। snātvā saṃtarpayed devānṛṣīn pitṛgaṇāṃstathā ।
ācamya mantravannityaṃ punarācamya vāgyataḥ ।। saṃmārjya mantrairātmānaṃ kuśaiḥ sodakabindubhiḥ । āpo hiṣṭhā vyāhṛtibhiḥ sāvitryā vāruṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। oṅkāravyāhṛtiyutāṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram ।
japtvā jalāñjaliṃ dadyād bhāskaraṃ prati tanmanāḥ ।। prākkūleṣu samāsīno darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ । prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyet saṃdhyāmiti śrutiḥ ।। yā saṃdhyā sā jagatsūtirmāyātītā hi niṣkalā ।
aiśvarī tu parāśaktistattvatrayasamudbhavā ।। dhyātvār'kamaṇḍalagatāṃ sāvitrīṃ vai japan budhaḥ । prāṅmukhaḥ satataṃ vipraḥ saṃdhyopāsanamācaret ।। saṃdhyāhīno aśucirnityamanarhaḥ sarvakarmasu ।
yadanyat kurute kiñcinna tasya phalamāpnuyāt ।। ananyacetasaḥ śāntā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ । upāsya vidhivat saṃdhyāṃ prāptāḥ pūrvaṃ parāṃ gatim ।। yo anyatra kurute yatnaṃ dharmakārye dvijottamaḥ ।
vihāya saṃdhyāpraṇatiṃ sa yāti narakāyutam ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena saṃdhyopāsanamācaret । upāsito bhavet tena devo yogatanuḥ paraḥ ।। sahasraparamāṃ nityaṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām ।
sāvitrariṃ vai japed vidvān prāṅmukhaḥ prayataḥ sthitaḥ ।। athopatiṣṭhedādityamudayantaṃ samāhitaḥ । mantraistu vividhaiḥ saurerṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃbhavaiḥ ।। upasthāya mahāyogaṃ devadevaṃ divākaram ।
kurvota praṇatiṃ bhūmau mūrdhnā tenaiva mantrataḥ ।। oṃ khakholkāya śāntāya kāraṇatrayahetave । nivedayāmi cātmānaṃ namaste jñānarūpiṇe । namaste ghṛṇine tubhyaṃ sūryāya brahmarūpiṇe ।।
tvameva brahma paramamāpo jyotī raso amṛtam । bhūrbhuvaḥ svastvamoṅkāraḥ sarve rudrāḥ sanātanāḥ । puruṣaḥ sanmaho atastvāṃ praṇamāmi kapardinam ।। tvameva viśvaṃ bahudhā sadasat sūyate ca yat ।
namo rudrāya sūryāya tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। pracetase namastubhyaṃ namo mīḍhuṣṭamāya te । namo namaste rudrāya tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। hiraṇyabāhave tubhyaṃ hiraṇyapataye namaḥ ।
ambikāpataye tubhyamumāyāḥ pataye namaḥ ।। namo astu nīlagrīvāya namastubhyaṃ pinākine । vilohitāya bhargāya sahasrākṣāya te namaḥ ।। namo haṃsāya te nityamādityāya namo astu te ।
namaste vajrahastāya tryambakāya namo astu te ।। prapadye tvāṃ virūpākṣaṃ mahāntaṃ parameśvaram । hiraṇmayaṃ gṛhe guptamātmānaṃ sarvadehinām ।। namasyāmi paraṃ jyotirbrahmāṇaṃ tvāṃ parāṃ gatim ।
viśvaṃ paśupatiṃ bhīmaṃ naranārīśarīriṇam ।। namaḥ sūryāya rudrāya bhāsvate parameṣṭhine । ugrāya sarvabhaktāya tvāṃ prapadye sadaiva hi ।। etad vai sūryahṛdayaṃ japtvā stavamanuttamam ।
prātaḥ kāle atha madhyāhne namaskuryād divākaram ।। idaṃ putrāya śiṣyāya dhārmikāya dvijātaye । pradeyaṃ sūryahṛdayaṃ brahmaṇā tu pradarśitam ।। sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ vedasārasamudbhavam ।
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitaṃ puṇyamṛṣisaṅghairniṣevitam ।। athāgamya gṛhaṃ vipraḥ samācamya yathāvidhi । prajvālya vihniṃ vidhivajjuhuyājjātavedasam ।। ṛtvikputro atha patnī vā śiṣyo vāpi sahodaraḥ ।
prāpyānujñāṃ viśeṣeṇa juhuyurvā yatāvidhi ।। pavitrapāṇiḥ pūtātmā śuklāmbaradharottaraḥ । ananyamānaso vahniṃ juhuyāt saṃyatendriyaḥ ।। vinā darbheṇa yatkarma vinā sūtreṇa vā punaḥ ।
rākṣasaṃ tadbhavet sarvaṃ nāmutreha phalapradam ।। daivatāni namaskuryād deyasārānnivedayet । dadyāt puṣpādikaṃ teṣāṃ vṛddhāṃścaivābhivādayet ।। guruṃ caivāpyupāsīta hitaṃ cāsya samācaret ।
vedābhyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryāt prayatnācchaktito dvijaḥ ।। japedadhyāpayecchiṣyān dhārayecca vicārayet । avekṣeta ca śāstrāṇi dharmādīni dvijottamaḥ । vaidikāṃścaiva nigamān vedāṅgāni veśiṣataḥ ।।
upeyādīśvaraṃ cātha yogakṣemaprasiddhaye । sādhayed vividhānarthān kuṭumbārthe tato dvijaḥ ।। tato madhyāhnasamaye snānārthaṃ mṛdamāharet । puṣpākṣatān kuśatilān gomayaṃ śuddhameva ca ।।
nadīṣu devakhāteṣu taḍāgeṣu saraḥsu ca । snānaṃ samācarennityaṃ gartaprastravaṇeṣu ca ।। parakīyanipāneṣu na snāyād vai kadācana । pañcapiṇḍān samuddhṛtya snāyād vāsaṃbhave punaḥ ।।
mṛdaikayā śiraḥ kṣālyaṃ dvābhyāṃ nābhestathopari । adhaśca tisṛbhiḥ kāyaṃ pādau ṣaḍbhistathaiva ca ।। mṛttikā ca samuddiṣṭā tvārdrāmalakamātrikā । gomayasya pramāṇaṃ tat tenāṅgaṃ lepayet tataḥ ।।
lepayitvā tu tīrasthastalliṅgaireva mantrataḥ । prakṣālyācamya vidhivat tataḥ snāyāt samāhitaḥ ।। abhimantrya jalaṃ mantraistalliṅgairvāruṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ । bhāvapūtastadavyaktaṃ dhyāyan vai viṣṇumavyayam ।।
āpo nārāyaṇodbhūtāstā evāsyāyanaṃ punaḥ । tasmānnārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ snānakāle smared budhaḥ ।। procya soṃkāramādityaṃ trirnimajjejjalāśaye । ācāntaḥ punarācāmenmantreṇānena mantravit ।।
antaścarasi bhūteṣu guhāyāṃ viśvato mukhaḥ । tvaṃ yajñastvaṃ vaṣaṭkāra āpo jyotī raso amṛtam ।। drupadāṃ vā trirabhyasyed vyāhṛtipraṇavānvitām । sāvitrīṃ vā japed vidvān tathā caivāghamarṣaṇam ।।
tataḥ saṃmārjanaṃ kuryādāpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ । idamāpaḥ pravahata vyāhṛtibhistathaiva ca ।। tato abhimantrya tat tīrthamāpo hiṣṭhādimantrakaiḥ । antarjalagato magno japet triraghamarṣaṇam ।।
tripadāṃ vātha sāvitrīṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam । āvartayed vā praṇavaṃ devaṃ vā saṃsmareddharim ।। drupadādiva yo mantro yajurvede pratiṣṭhitaḥ । antarjale trirāvartya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
apaḥ pāṇau samādāya japtvā vai mārjane kṛte । vinyasya mūrdhni tat toyaṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।। yathāśvamedhaḥ kraturāṭ sarvapāpāpanodanaḥ । tathāghamarṣaṇaṃ sūktaṃ sarvapāpāpanodanam ।।
athopatiṣṭhedādityaṃ mūrdhni puṣpānvitāñjalim । prakṣipyālokayed devamudvayaṃ tamasaspari ।। udutyaṃ citramityete taccakṣuriti mantrataḥ । haṃsaḥ śuciṣadetena sāvitryā ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
anyaiśca vaidikairmantraiḥ sauraiḥ pāpapraṇāśanaiḥ । sāvitrīṃ vai japet paścājjapayajñaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ ।। vividhāni pavitrāṇi guhyavidyāstathaiva ca । śatarudrīyamatharvaśiraḥ saurāṃśca śaktitaḥ ।।
prākkūleṣu samāsīnaḥ kuśeṣu prāṅmukhaḥ śuciḥ । tiṣṭhaṃścedīkṣamāṇor'kaṃ japyaṃ kuryāt samāhitaḥ ।। sphāṭikendrākṣarudrākṣaiḥ putrajīvasamudbhavaḥ । kartavyā tvakṣamālā syāduttarāduttamā smṛtā ।।
japakāle na bhāṣeta nānyāni prekṣayed budhaḥ । na kampayecchirogrīvāṃ dantānnaiva prakāśayet ।। guhyakā rākṣasā siddhā haranti prasabhaṃ yataḥ । ekānte suśubhe deśe tasmājjapyaṃ samācaret ।।
caṇḍālāśaucapatitān dṛṣṭvācamya punarjapet । taireva bhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā snātvā caiva japet punaḥ ।। ācamya prayato nityaṃ japedaśucidarśane । saurān mantrān śaktito vai pāvamānīstu kāmataḥ ।।
yadi syāt klinnavāsā vai vārimadhyagato japet । anyathā tu śucau bhūmyāṃ darbheṣu susamāhitaḥ ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ samāvṛtya namaskṛtvā tataḥ kṣitau । ācamya ca yathāśāstraṃ śaktyā svādhyāyamācaret ।।
tataḥ saṃtarpayed devānṛṣīn pitṛgaṇāṃstathā । adāvoṅkāramuccārya namo ante tarpayāmi vaḥ ।। devān brahmaḥṛṣīṃścaiva tarpayedakṣatodakaiḥ । tilodakaiḥ pitṝn bhaktyā svasūtroktavidhānataḥ ।।
anvārabdhena savyena pāṇinā dakṣiṇena tu । devarṣostarpayed dhīmānudakāñjalibhiḥ pitan ।। yajñopavītī devānāṃ nivītī ṛṣītarpaṇe । prācīnāvītī pitrye tu svena tīrthena bhāvataḥ ।।
niṣpīḍya snānavastraṃ tu samācamya ca vāgyataḥ । svairmantrairarcayed devān puṣpaiḥ patrairathāmbubhiḥ ।। brahmāṇaṃ śaṅkaraṃ sūryaṃ tathaiva madhusūdanam । anyāṃścābhimatān devān bhaktyā cākrodhano atvaraḥ ।।
pradadyād vātha puṣpāṇi sūktena pauruṣeṇa tu । āpo vā devatāḥ sarvāstena samyak samarcitāḥ ।। dhyātvā praṇavapūrvaṃ vai daivatāni samāhitaḥ । namaskāreṇa puṣpāṇi vinyased vai pṛthak pṛthak ।।
na viṣṇvārādhanāt puṇyaṃ vidyate karma vaidikam । tasmādanādimadhyāntaṃ nityamārādhayeddharim ।। tadviṣṇoriti mantreṇa sūktena puruṣeṇa tu । naitābhyāṃ sadṛśo mantro sūktena puruṣeṇa tu ।
naitābhyāṃ sadṛśo mantro vedeṣūktaścaturṣvapi ।। nivedayeta svātmānaṃ viṣṇāvamalatejasi । tadātmā tanmanāḥ śāntastadviṣṇoriti mantrataḥ ।। athavā devamīśānaṃ bhagavantaṃ sanātanam ।
ārādhayenmahādevaṃ bhāvapūto maheśvaram ।। mantreṇa rudrāgāyatryā praṇavenātha vā punaḥ । īśānenātha vā rudraistryambakena samāhitaḥ ।। puṣpaiḥ patrairathādbhirvā candanādyairmaheśvaram ।
uktvā namaḥ śivāyeti mantreṇānena yojayet ।। namaskuryānmahādevaṃ ṛtaṃ satyamitiśvaram । nivedayīta svātmānaṃ yo brahmāṇamitīśvaram ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ dvijaḥ kuryāt pañca brahmāṇi vai japan ।
dhyāyīta devamīśānaṃ vyomamadhyagataṃ śivam ।। athāvalokayedarkaṃ haṃsaḥ suciṣadityṛcā । kuryāt pañca mahāyajñān gṛhaṃ gatvā samāhitaḥ ।। devayajñaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ tathaiva ca ।
mānuṣyaṃ brahmayajñaṃ ca pañca yajñān pracakṣate ।। yadi syāt tarpaṇādarvāk brahmayajñaḥ kṛto na hi । kṛtvā manuṣyayajñaṃ vai tataḥ svādhyāyamācaret ।। agneḥ paścimato deśe bhūtayajñānta eva vā ।
kuśapuñje samāsīnaḥ kuśapāṇiḥ samāhitaḥ ।। śālāgnau laukike vāgnau jale bhūbhyāmathāpivā । vaiśvadevaṃ tataḥ kuryād devayajñaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ ।। yadi syāllaukike pakvaṃ tato annaṃ tatra hūyate ।
śālāgnau tatra devānnaṃ vidhireṣa sanātanaḥ ।। devebhyastu hutādannāccheṣād bhūtabaliṃ haret । bhūtayajñaḥ sa vai jñeyo bhūtidaḥ sarvadehinām ।। śvabhyaśca śvapacebhyaśca patitādibhya eva ca ।
dadyād bhūmau baliṃ tvannaṃ pakṣibhyo atha dvijottamaḥ ।। sāyaṃ cānnasya siddhasya patnyamantraṃ baliṃ haret । bhūtayajñastvayaṃ nityaṃ sāyaṃ prātarvidhīyate ।। ekaṃ tu bhojayed vipraṃ pitṝnuddiśya sattamam ।
nityaśrāddhaṃ taduddiṣṭaṃ pitṛyajño gatipradaḥ ।। uddhṛtya vā yathāśakti kiñcidannaṃ samāhitaḥ । vedatattvārthaviduṣe dvijāyaivopapādayet ।। pūjayedatithiṃ nityaṃ namasyedarcayed dvijam ।
manovākkarmabhiḥ śāntamāgataṃ svagṛha tataḥ ।। hantakāramathāgraṃ vā bhikṣāṃ vā śaktito dvijaḥ । dadyādatithaye nityaṃ budhyeta parameśvaram ।। bhikṣāmāhurgrāsamātramagraṃ tasyāścaturguṇam ।
puṣkalaṃ hantakāraṃ tu taccaturguṇamucyate ।। godohamātraṃ kālaṃ vai pratīkṣyo hyatithiḥ svayam । abhyāgatān yathāśakti pūjayedatithiṃ yathā ।। bhikṣāṃ vai bhikṣave dadyād vidhivad brahmacāriṇe ।
dadyādannaṃ yathāśakti tvarthibhyo lobhavarjitaḥ ।। sarveṣāmapyalābhe tu annaṃ gobhyo nivedayet । bhuñjīta bandhubhiḥ sārdhaṃ vāgyato annamakutsayan ।। akṛtvā tu dvijaḥ pañca mahāyajñān dvijottamāḥ ।
bhṛñjīta cet sa mūḍhātmā tiryagyoniṃ sagacchati ।। vedābhyāso anvahaṃ śaktyā mahāyajñakriyā kṣamā । nāśayatyāśu pāpāni devānāmarcanaṃ tathā ।। yo mohādathavālasyādakṛtvā devatārcanam ।
bhuṅkte sa yāti narakān śūkareṣvabhijāyate ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena kṛtvā karmāṇi vai dvijāḥ । bhuñjīta svajanaiḥ sārdhaṃ sayāti paramāṃ gatim ।। prāṅmukho annāni bhuñjīta sūryābhimukha eva vā ।
āsīnastvāsane śuddhe bhūmyāṃ pādau nidhāya tu ।। āyuṣyaṃ prāṅmukho bhuṅkte yaśasyaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ । śriyaṃ pratyaṅmukho bhuṅkte ṛtaṃ bhuṅkte udaṅmukhāḥ ।। pañcārdre bhojanaṃ kuryād bhūmau pātraṃ nidhāya tu ।
upavāsena tattulyaṃ manurāha prajāpatiḥ ।। upalipte śucau deśe pādau prakṣālya vai karau । ācamyārdrānano akrodhaḥ pañcārdre bhojanaṃ caret ।। mahāvyahṛtibhistvannaṃ paridhāyodakena tu ।
amṛtopastaraṇamasītyāpośānakriyāṃ caret ।। svāhāpraṇavasaṃyuktāṃ prāṇāyādyāhutiṃ tataḥ । apānāya tato hutvā vyānāya tadanantaram ।। udānāya tataḥ kuryāt samānāyeti pañcamīm ।
vijñāya tattvameteṣāṃ juhuyādātmani dvijaḥ ।। śeṣamannaṃ yathākāmaṃ bhuñjītavyaṃ janairyutam । dhyātvā tanmanasā devamātmānaṃ vai prajāpatim ।। amṛtāpidhānamasītyupariṣṭādapaḥ pibet ।
ācāntaḥ punarācāmedāyaṃ gauriti mantrataḥ ।। drupadāṃ vā trirāvartya sarvapāpapraṇāśanīm । prāṇānāṃ granthirasītyālabhed hṛdayaṃ tataḥ ।। ācamyāṅguṣṭhamātreti pādāṅguṣṭhe atha dakṣiṇe ।
niḥ stravayed hastajalamūrdhvahastaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। hutānumantraṇaṃ kuryāt śraddhāyāmiti mantrataḥ । athākṣareṇa svātmānaṃ yojayed brahmaṇeti hi ।। sarveṣāmeva yāgānāmātmayāgaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ ।
yo anena vidhinā kuryāt sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ kṣayam ।। yajñopavītī bhuñjīta straggandhālaṅkṛtaḥ śuciḥ । sāyaṃprāparnāntarā vai saṃdhyāyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ ।। nādyāt sūryagrahāt pūrvamahni sāyaṃ śaśigrahāt ।
grahakāle ca nāśnīyāt snātvāśnīyāt tu muktayoḥ ।। mukte śaśini bhuñjīta yadi na syānmahāniśā । amuktayorastaṅgatayoradyād dṛṣṭvā pare ahani ।। nāśnīyāt prekṣamāṇānāmapradāyaiva durmatiḥ ।
na yajñaśiṣṭādand vā na kruddho nānyamānasaḥ ।। ātmārthaṃ bhojanaṃ yasya ratyarthaṃ yasya maithunam । vṛtyarthaṃ yasya cādhītaṃ niṣphalaṃ tasya jīvitam ।। yadbhuṅkte veṣṭitaśirā yacca bhuṅkte udaṅmukhaḥ ।
sopānatkaśca yad bhuṅkte sarvaṃ vidyāt tadāsuram ।। nārdharātre na madhyāhne nājīrṇe nārdravastradhṛk । na ca bhinnāsanagato na śayānaḥ sthito api vā ।। na bhinnabhājane caiva na bhūmyāṃ na ca pāṇiṣu ।
nocchiṣṭo ghṛtamādadyānna mūrdhānaṃ spṛśedapi ।। na brahma kīrtayan vāpi na niḥ śeṣaṃ na bhāryayā । nāndhakāre na cākāśe na ca devālayādiṣu ।। naikavastrastu bhuñjīta na yānaśayanasthitaḥ ।
na pādukānirgato atha na hasan vilapannapi ।। bhuktvaivaṃ sukhamāsthāya tadannaṃ pariṇāmayet । itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedārthānupabṛṃhayet ।। tataḥ saṃdhyāmupāsīta pūrvoktavidhinā dvijaḥ ।
āsīnastu japed devīṃ gāyatrīṃ paścimāṃ prati ।। na tiṣṭhati tu yaḥ purvāṃ nāste saṃdhyāṃ tu paścimām । sa śūdreṇa samo loke sarvadharmavivarjitaḥ ।। hutvāgniṃ vidhivanmantrairbhuktvā yajñāvaśiṣṭakam ।
sabhṛtyabāndhavajanaḥ svapecchuṣkapado niśi ।। nottarābhimukhaḥ svapyāt paścimābhimukho na ca । na cākāśe na nagno vā nāśucirnāsane kvacit ।। na śīrṇāyāṃ tu khaṭvāyāṃ śūnyāgāre na caiva hi ।
nānuvaṃśaṃ na pālāśe śayane vā kadācana ।। ityetadakhilenoktamahanyahani vai mayā । brāhmaṇānāṃ kṛtyajātamapavargaphalapradam ।। nāstikyādathavālasyāt brāhmaṇo na karoti yaḥ ।
sa yāti narakān ghorān kākayonau ca jāyate ।। nānyo vimuktaye panthā muktvāśramavidhiṃ svakam । tasmāt karmāṇi kurvota tuṣṭaye parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। atha śrāddhamamāvāsyāṃ prāpya kāryaṃ dvijottamaiḥ ।
piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ bhaktyā bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।। piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kṣīṇe rājani śasyate । aparāhne dvijātīnāṃ praśastenāmiṣeṇa ca ।। pratipatprabhṛti hyanyāstithayaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣake ।
caturdaśīṃ varjayitvā praśastā hyuttarottarāḥ ।। amāvāsyāṣṭakāstistraḥ pauṣamāsādiṣu triṣu । tistraścānvaṣṭakāḥ puṇyā māghī pañcadaśī tathā ।। trayodaśī maghāyuktā varṣāsu tu viśeṣataḥ ।
śasyāpākaśrāddhakālā nityāḥ proktā dine dine ।। naimittikaṃ tu kartavyaṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ । bāndhavānāṃ ca maraṇe nārakī syādato anyathā ।। kāmyāni caiva śrāddhāni śasyānte grahaṇādiṣu ।
ayane viṣuve caiva vyatīpāte apyanantakam ।। saṃkrāntyamakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ tathā janmadineṣvapi । nakṣatreṣu ca sarveṣu kāryaṃ kāmyaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। svargaṃ ca labhate kṛtvā kṛttikāsu dvijottamaḥ ।
apatyamatha rohiṇyāṃ saumye tu brahmavarcasam ।। raudrāṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ siddhimārdrāyāṃ śauryameva ca । punarvasau tathā bhūmiṃ śriyaṃ puṣye tathaiva ca ।। sarvān kāmāṃstathā sārpe pitrye saubhāgyameva ca ।
aryamṇe tu dhanaṃ vindyāt phālgunyāṃ pāpanāśanam ।। jñātiśraiṣṭhyaṃ tathā haste citrāyāṃ ca bahūn sutān । vāṇijyasiddhiṃ svātau tu viśākhāsu suvarṇakam ।। maitre bahūni mitrāṇi rājyaṃ śākre tathaiva ca ।
mūle kṛṣiṃ labhed yānasiddhimāpye samudrataḥ ।। sarvān kāmān vaiśvadeve śraiṣṭhyaṃ tu śravaṇe punaḥ । śraviṣṭhāyāṃ tathā kāmān vāruṇe ca paraṃ balam ।। ajaikapāde kupyaṃ syādahirbudhne gṛhaṃ śubham ।
revatyāṃ bahavo gāvo hyaśvinyāṃ turagāṃstathā । yāmye atha jīvanaṃ tat syādyadi śrāddhaṃ prayacchati ।। ādityavāre tvārogyaṃ candre saubhāgyameva ca । kauje sarvatra vijayaṃ sarvān kāmān budhasya tu ।।
vidyāmabhīṣṭā jīve tu dhanaṃ vai bhārgave punaḥ । śamaiśvare labhedāyuḥ pratipatsu sutān śubhān ।। kanyakāṃ vai dvitīyāyāṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ tu vandinaḥ । paśūnkṣudrāṃścaturthyāṃ tu pañcamyāṃśobhanān sutān ।।
ṣaṣṭyāṃ dyūtaṃ kṛṣiṃ cāpi saptamyāṃ labhate naraḥ । aṣṭamyāmapi vāṇijyaṃ labhate śrāddhadaḥ sadā ।। syānnavamyāmekakhuraṃ daśamyāṃ dvikhuraṃ bahu । ekādaśyāṃ tathā rūpyaṃ brahmavarcasvinaḥ sutān ।।
dvādaśyāṃ jātarūpaṃ ca rajataṃ kupyameva ca । jñātiśraiṣṭhyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ tu kruprajāḥ । pañcadaśyāṃ sarvakāmānāpnoti śrāddhadaḥ sadā ।। tasmācchrāddhaṃ na kartavyaṃ caturdaśyāṃ dvijātibhiḥ ।
śastreṇa tu hatānāṃ vai tatra śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet ।। dravyabrāhmaṇasaṃpattau na kālaniyamaḥ kṛtaḥ । tasmād bhogāpavargārthaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryurdvijātayaḥ ।। karmārambheṣu sarveṣu kuryādābhyudayaṃ punaḥ ।
putrajanmādiṣu śrāddhaṃ pārvaṇaṃ parvaṇi smṛtam ।। ahanyahani nityaṃ syāt kāmyaṃ naimittikaṃ punaḥ । ekoddiṣṭādi vijñeyaṃ vṛddhiśrāddhaṃ tu pārvaṇam ।। etat pañcavidhaṃ śrāddhaṃ manunā parikīrtitam ।
yātrāyāṃ ṣaṣṭhamākhyātaṃ tatprayatnena pālayet ।। śuddhaye saptamaṃ śrāddhaṃ brahmaṇā paribhāṣitam । daivikaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ śrāddhaṃ yatkṛtvā mucyate bhayāt ।। saṃdhyārātryorna kartavyaṃ rāhoranyatra darśanāt ।
deśānāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa bhavet puṇyamanantakam ।। gaṅgāyāmakṣayaṃ śrāddhaṃ prayāge amarakaṇṭake । gāyanti pitaro gāthāṃ kīrtayanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। eṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrāḥ śīlavanto guṇānvitāḥ ।
teṣāṃ tu samavetānāṃ yadyeko api gāyāṃ vrajet ।। gayāṃ prāpyānuṣaṅgeṇa yadi śrāddhaṃ samācaret । tāritāḥ pitarastena sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। varāhaparvate caiva gaṅgāyāṃ vai viśeṣataḥ ।
vārāṇasyāṃ viśeṣeṇa yatra devaḥ svayaṃ haraḥ ।। gaṅgādvāre prabhāse ca bilvake nīlaparvate । kurukṣetre ca kubjāmre bhṛgutuṅge mahālaye ।। kedāre phalgutīrthe ca naimiṣāraṇya eva ca ।
sarasvatyāṃ viśeṣeṇa puṣkareṣu viśeṣataḥ ।। narmadāyāṃ kuśāvarte śrīśaile bhadrakarṇake । vetravatyāṃ vipāśāyāṃ godāvaryāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। evamādiṣu cānyeṣu tīrtheṣu pulineṣu ca ।
