nadīnāṃ caiva tīreṣu tuṣyanti pitaraḥ sadā ।। vrīhibhiśca yavairmāṣairadbhirmūlaphalena vā । śyāmākaiśca yavaiḥ śākairnovāraiśca priyaṅgubhiḥ । gaudhūmaiśca tilairmudgairmāsaṃ prīṇayate pitṝn ।।
āmrān pāne ratānikṣūn mṛdvīkāṃśca sadāḍimān । vidāryāśca bharaṇḍāśca śrāddhakāle prādapayet ।। lājān madhuyutān dadyāt saktūn śarkarayā saha । dadyācchrāddhe prayatnena śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukān ।।
dvau māsau matsyamāṃsena trīn māsān hāriṇenatu । aurabhreṇātha caturaḥ śākuneneha pañca tu ।। ṣaṇmāsāṃśchāgamāṃsena pārṣatenātha sapta vai । aṣṭāveṇasya māṃsena rauraveṇa navaiva tu ।।
daśamāsāṃstu tṛpyanti varāhamahiṣāmiṣaiḥ । śaśakūrmaryormāṃsena māsānekādaśaiva tu ।। saṃvatsaraṃ tu gavyena payasā pāyasena tu । vārdhroṇasasya māṃsena tṛptirdvādaśavārṣikī ।।
kālaśākaṃ mahāśalkaṃ khaṅgalohāmiṣaṃ madhu । ānantyāyaiva kalpante munyannāni ca sarvaśaḥ ।। krītvā labdhvā svayaṃ vātha mṛtānāhṛtya vā dvijaḥ । dadyācchrāddhe prayatnena tadasyākṣayamucyate ।।
pippalīṃ kramukaṃ caiva tathā caiva masūrakam । kūṣmāṇḍālābuvārtākān bhūstṛṇaṃ surasaṃ tathā ।। kusumbhapiṇḍamūlaṃ vai tandulīyakameva ca । rājamāṣāṃstathā kṣīraṃ māhiṣaṃ ca vivarjayet ।।
kodravān kovidārāṃścapālakyān maricāṃstathā । varjayet sarvayatnena śrāddhakāle dvijottamaḥ ।। snātvā yathoktaṃ saṃtarpya pitṝṃścandrakṣaye dvijaḥ । piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt saumyamanāḥ śuciḥ ।।
pūrvameva parīkṣeta brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam । tīrthaṃ tad havyakavyānāṃ pradāne cātithiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ye somapā virajaso dharmajñāḥ śāntacetasaḥ । vratino niyamasthāśca ṛtukālābhigāminaḥ ।।
pañcāgnirapyadhīyāno yajurvedavideva ca । bahvṛcaśca trisauparṇastrimadhurvātha yo bhavet ।। triṇāciketacchandogo jyeṣṭhasāmaga eva ca । atharvaśiraso adhyetā rudrādhyāyī viśeṣataḥ ।।
agnihotraparo vidvān nyāyavicca ṣaḍaṅgavit । mantrabrāhmaṇaviccaiva yaśca syād dharmapāṭhakaḥ ।। ṛṣivratī ṛṣīkaśca tathā dvādaśavārṣikaḥ । brahmadeyānusaṃtāno garbhaśuddhaḥ sahasradaḥ ।।
cāndrāyaṇavratacaraḥ satyavādī purāṇavit । gurudevāgnipūjāsu prasakto jñānatatparaḥ ।। vimuktaḥ sarvato dhīro brahmabhūto dvijottamaḥ । mahādevārcanarato vaiṣṇavaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ।।
ahiṃsānirato nityamapratigrahaṇastathā । satriṇo dānaniratā vijñeyāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ।। yuvānaḥ śrotriyāḥ svasthā mahāyajñaparāyaṇāḥ । sāvitrījāpaniratā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ।।
kulīnāḥ śrutavantaśca śīlavantastapasvinaḥ । agnicitsnātakā viprā vijñeyāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ।। mātāpitrorhite yuktaḥ prātaḥ snāyī tathā dvijaḥ । adhyātmavinmunirdānto vijñeyaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ।।
jñānaniṣṭho mahāyogī vedāntārthavicintakaḥ । śraddhāluḥ śrāddhanirato brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ।। vedavidyārataḥ snāto brahmacaryaparaḥ sadā । atharvaṇo mumukṣuśca brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ।।
asamānapravarako hyasagotrastathaiva ca । asaṃbandhī ca vijñeyo brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ।। bhojayed yoginaṃ pūrvaṃ tattvajñānarataṃ yatim । alābhe naiṣṭhikaṃ dāntamupakurvāṇakaṃ tathā ।।
tadalābhe gṛhasthaṃ tu mumukṣuṃ saṅgavarjitam । sarvālābhe sādhakaṃ vā gṛhasthamapi bhojayet ।। prakṛterguṇatattvajño yasyāśnāti yatirhaviḥ । phalaṃ vedavidāṃ tasya sahasrādatiricyate ।।
tasmād yatnena yogīndramīśvarajñānatatparam । bhojayed havyakavyeṣu alābhāditarān dvijān ।। eṣa vai prathamaḥ kalpaḥ pridāne havyakavyayoḥ । anukalpastvayaṃ jñeyaḥ sadā sadbhiranuṣṭhitaḥ ।।
mātāmahaṃ mātulaṃ ca svastrīyaṃ śvaśuraṃ gurum । dauhitraṃ viṭpatiṃ bandhumṛtvigyājyau ca bhojayet ।। na śrāddhe bhojayenmitraṃ dhanaiḥ kāryo asya saṃgrahaḥ । paiśācī dakṣiṇā sā hi naivāmutra phalapradā ।।
kāma śrāddhe arcayenmitraṃ nābhirūpamapi tvarim । dviṣatā hi havirbhuktaṃ bhavati pretya niṣphalam ।। brāhmaṇo hyanadhīyānastṛṇāgniriva śāmyati । tasmai havyaṃ na dātavyaṃ na hi bhasmani hūyate ।।
yatheriṇe bījamuptvā na vaptā labhate phalam । tathānṛce havirdattvā na dātā labhate phalam ।। yāvato grasate piṇḍān havyakavyeṣvamantravit । tāvato grasate pretya dīptān sthūlāṃstvayoguḍān ।।
api vidyākulairyuktā hīnavṛttā narādhamāḥ । yatraite bhuñjate havyaṃ tad bhavedāsura dvijāḥ ।। yasya vedaśca vedī ca vicchidyete tripūruṣam । sa vai durbrāhmaṇo nārhaḥ śrāddhādiṣu kadācana ।।
śūdrapreṣyo bhṛto rājño vṛṣalo grāmayājakaḥ । badhabandhopajīvī ca ṣaḍete brahmabandhavaḥ ।। dattānuyogān vṛtyarthaṃ patitān manurabravīt । vedavikrāyiṇo hyete śrāddhādiṣu vigarhitāḥ ।।
śrutivikrayiṇo ye tu parapūrvāsamudbhavāḥ । asamānān yājayanti patitāste prakīrtitāḥ ।। asaṃskṛtādhyāpakā ye bhṛtyā vādhyāpayanti ye । adhīyate tathā vedān patitāste prakīrtitāḥ ।।
vṛddhaśrāvakanirgranthāḥ pañcarātravido janāḥ । kāpālikāḥ pāśupatāḥ pāṣaṇḍā ye ca tadvidhāḥ ।। yasyāśnanti havīṃṣyete durātmānastu tāmasāḥ । na tasya tad bhavecchrāddhaṃ pretya ceha phalapradam ।।
anāśramo yo dvijaḥ syādāśramī vā nirarthakaḥ । mithyāśramī ca te viprā vijñeyāḥ paṅktidūṣakāḥ ।। duścarmā kunakhī kuṣṭhī śvitrī ca śyāvadantakaḥ । viddhaprajananaścaiva stenaḥ klībo atha nāstikaḥ ।।
madyapo vṛṣalīsakto vīrahā didhiṣūpatiḥ । āgāradāhī kuṇḍāśī somavikrayiṇo dvijāḥ ।। parivettā tathā hiṃstraḥ parivittirnirākṛtiḥ । paunarbhavaḥ kusīdī ca tathā nakṣatradarśakaḥ ।।
gītavāditranirato vyādhitaḥ kāṇa eva ca । hīnāṅgaścātiriktāṅgo hyavakīrṇistathaiva ca ।। kanyādūṣī kuṇḍagolau abhiśasto atha devalaḥ । mitradhruk piśunaścaiva nityaṃ bhāryānuvartakaḥ ।।
mātāpitrorgurostyāgī dāratyāgī tathaiva ca । gotrabhid bhraṣṭaśaucaśca kāṇḍaspṛṣṭastathaiva ca ।। anapatyaḥ kūṭasākṣī yācako raṅgajīvakaḥ । samudrayāyī kṛtahā tathā samayabhedakaḥ ।।
devanindāparaścaiva vedanindāratastathā । dvijanindārataścaite varjyāḥ śrāddhādikarmasu ।। kṛtaghnaḥ piśunaḥ krūro nāstiko vedanindakaḥ । mitradhruk kuhakaścaiva viśeṣāt paṅktidūṣakāḥ ।।
sarve punarabhojyānnāstvadānārhāśca karmasu । brahmabhāvanirastāśca varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।। śūdrānnarasapuṣṭāṅgaḥ saṃdhyopāsanavarjitaḥ । mahāyajñavihīnaśca brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktidūṣakaḥ ।।
adhītanāśanaścaiva snānahomavivarjitaḥ । tāmaso rājasaścaiva brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktidūṣakaḥ ।। bahunātra kimuktena vihitān ye na kurvate । ninditānācarantyete varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
gomayenodakairbhūmiṃ śodhayitvā samāhitaḥ । saṃnipātya dvijān sarvān sādhubhiḥ saṃnimantrayet ।। śvo bhaviṣyati me śrāddhaṃ pūrvedyurabhipūjya ca । asaṃbhave paredyurvā yathoktairlakṣaṇairyutān ।।
tasya te pitaraḥ śrutvā śrāddhakālamupasthitam । anyonyaṃ manasā dhyātvā saṃpatanti manojavāḥ ।। brāhmaṇaiste sahāśnanti pitaro hyantarikṣagāḥ । vāyubhūtāstu tiṣṭhanti bhuktvā yānti parāṃ gatim ।।
āmantritāśca te viprāḥ śrāddhakāla upasthite । vaseyurniyatāḥ sarve brahmacaryaparāyaṇāḥ ।। akrodhano atvaro amattaḥ satyavādī samāhitaḥ । bhāraṃ maithunamadhvānaṃ śrāddhakṛd varjayejjapam ।।
āmantrito brāhmaṇo vā yo anyasmai kurute kṣaṇam । sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ sūkaratvāṃ prāyāti ca ।। āmantrayitvā yo mohādanyaṃ cāmantrayed dvijam । sa tasmādadhikaḥ pāpī viṣṭhākīṭo abhijāyate ।।
śrāddhe nimantrito vipro maithunaṃ yo adhigacchati । brahmahatyāmavāpnoti tiryagyonau ca jāyate ।। nimantritastu yo vipro hyadhvānaṃ yāti durmatiḥ । bhavanti pitarastasya taṃ māsaṃ pāṃśubhojanāḥ ।।
nimantritastu yaḥ śrāddhe prakuryāt kalahaṃ dvijaḥ । bhavanti tasya tanmāsaṃ pitaro malabhojanāḥ ।। tasmānnimantritaḥ śrāddhe niyatātmā bhaved dvijaḥ । akrodhanaḥ śaucaparaḥ kartā caiva jitendriyaḥ ।।
śvobhūte dakṣiṇāṃ gatvā diśaṃ darbhān samāhitaḥ । samūlānāhared vāri dakṣiṇāgrān sunirmalān ।। dakṣiṇāpravaṇaṃ snigdhaṃ vibhaktaṃ śubhalakṣaṇam । śuciṃ deśaṃ viviktaṃ ca gomayenopalepayet ।।
nadītīreṣu tīrtheṣu svabhūmau caiva sānuṣu । vivikteṣu ca tuṣyanti dattena pitaraḥ sadā ।। pārakye bhūmibhāge tu pitṝṇāṃ naiva nirvapet । svāmibhistad vihanyeta mohād yat kriyate naraiḥ ।।
aṭavyaḥ parvatāḥ puṇyāstīrthānyāyatanāni ca । sarvāṇyasvāmikānyāhurna hi teṣu parigrahaḥ ।। tilān pravikiret tatra sarvato bandhayedajān । asuropahataṃ sarvaṃ tilaiḥ śuddhyatyajena vā ।।
tato annaṃ bahusaṃskāraṃ naikavyañjanamacyutam । coṣyapeyasamṛddhaṃ ca yathāśaktyā prakalpayet ।। tato nivṛtte madhyāhne luptalomanakhān dvijān । abhigamya yathāmārgaṃ prayacched dantadhāvanam ।।
tailamabhyañjanaṃ snānaṃ snānīyaṃ ca pṛthagvidham । pātrairaudumbarairdadyād vaiśvadaivatyapūrvakam ।। tataḥ snātvā nivṛttebhyaḥ pratyutthāyakṛtāñjaliḥ । pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca saṃprayacched yathākramam ।।
ye cātra viśvedevānāṃ viprāḥ pūrvaṃ nimantritāḥ । prāṅmukhānyāsanānyeṣāṃ tridarbhopahitāni ca ।। dakṣiṇāmukhayuktāni pitṝṇāmāsanāni ca । dakṣiṇāgraikadarbhāṇi prokṣitāni tilodakaiḥ ।।
teṣūpaveśayedetānāsanaṃ spṛśya sa dvijam । āsadhvamiti saṃjalpan āsanāste pṛthak pṛthak ।। dvau daive prāṅmukhau pitrye trayaścodaṅmukhāstathā । ekaikaṃ vā bhavet tatra devamātāmaheṣvapi ।।
satkriyāṃ deśakālau ca śaucaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpadam । pañcaitān vistaro hanti tasmānneheta vistaram ।। api vā bhojayedekaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam । śrutaśīlādisaṃpannamalakṣaṇavivarjitam ।।
uddhṛtya pātre cānnaṃ tat sarvasmāt prakṛtāt punaḥ । devatāyatane cāsmai nivedyānyatpravartayet ।। prāsyedagnau tadannaṃ tu dadyād vā brahmacāriṇe । tasmādekamapi śreṣṭhaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ bhojayed dvijam ।।
bhikṣuko brahmacārī vā bhojanārthamupasthitaḥ । upaviṣṭeṣu yaḥ śrāddhe kāmaṃ tamapi bhojayet ।। atithiryasya nāśnāti na tacchrāddhaṃ praśasyate । tasmāt prayatnācchrāddheṣu pūjyā hyatithayo dvijaiḥ ।।
ātithyarahite śrāddhe bhuñjate ye dvijātayaḥ । kākayoniṃ vrajantyete dātā caiva na saṃśayaḥ ।। hīnāṅgaḥ patitaḥ kuṣṭhī vraṇī pukkasanāstikau । kukkuṭāḥ śūkarāḥ śvāno varjyāḥ śrāddheṣu dūrataḥ ।।
bībhatsumaśuciṃ nagnaṃ mattaṃ dhūrtaṃ rajasvalām । nīlakāṣāyavasanaṃ pāṣaṇḍāṃśca vivarjayet ।। yat tatra kriyate karma paitṛkaṃ brāhmaṇān prati । tatsarvameva kartavyaṃ vaiśvadaivatyapūrvakam ।।
yathopaviṣṭān sarvāṃstānalaṅkuryād vibhūṣaṇaḥ । stragdāmabhiḥ śiroveṣṭairdhūpavāso anulepanaiḥ ।। tatastvāvāhayed devān brāhmaṇānāmanujñayā । udaṅmukho yathānyāyaṃ viśve devāsa ityṛcā ।।
dve pavitre gṛhītvātha bhājane kṣālite punaḥ । śaṃ no devyā jalaṃ kṣiptvā yavo asīti yavāṃstathā ।। yā divyā iti mantraṇa haste tvarghaṃ vinikṣipet । pradadyād gandhamālyāni dhūpādīni ca śaktitaḥ ।।
apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pitṝṇāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ । āvāhanaṃ tataḥ kuryāduśantastvetyṛcā budhaḥ ।। āvāhya tadanujñāto japedāyantu nastataḥ । śaṃ no devyodakaṃ pātre tilo asīti tilāṃstathā ।।
kṣiptvā cārghaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ dattvā hasteṣu vai punaḥ । saṃstravāṃśca tataḥ sarvān pātre kuryāt samāhitaḥ । pitṛbhyaḥ sthānametena nyubjaṃ pātraṃ nidhāpayet ।। agnau kariṣyetyādāya pṛcchatyannaṃ ghṛtaplutam ।
kuruṣvetyabhyanujñāto juhuyādupavītavān ।। yajñopavītinā homaḥ kartavyaḥ kuśapāṇinā । prācīnāvītinā pitryaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ tu homavat ।। dakṣiṇaṃ pātayejjānuṃ devān paricaran pumān ।
pitṛṇāṃ paricaryāsu pātayeditaraṃ tathā ।। somāya vai pitṛmate svadhā nama iti bruvan । agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadheti juhuyāt tataḥ ।। agnyabhāve tu viprasya pāṇāvevopapādayet ।
mahādevāntike vātha goṣṭhe vā susamāhitaḥ ।। tatastairabhyanujñāto gatvā vai dakṣiṇāṃ diśam । gomayenopatipyorvoṃ sthānaṃ kṛtvā tu saikatam ।। maṇḍalaṃ caturastraṃ vā dakṣiṇāvanataṃ śubham ।
trirullikhet tasya madhyaṃ darbheṇaikena caiva hi ।। tataḥ saṃstīrya tatsthāne darbhān vaidakṣiṇāgrakān । trīn piṇḍān nirvapet tatra haviḥ śeṣātsamāhitaḥ ।। nyupya piṇḍāṃstu taṃ hastaṃ nimṛjyāllepabhāginām ।
teṣu darbheṣvathācamya trirāyamya śanairasūn । tadannaṃ tu namaskuryāt pitṝneva ca mantravit ।। udakaṃ ninayeccheṣaṃ śanaiḥ piṇḍāntike punaḥ । avajighrecca tān piṇḍān yathānyuptān samāhitaḥ ।।
atha piṇḍāvaśiṣṭānnaṃ vidhinā bhojayed dvijān । māṃsānyapūpān vividhān dadyāt kṛsarapāyasam ।। sūpaśākaphalānīkṣūn payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ madhu । annaṃ caiva yathākāmaṃ vividhaṃ bhakṣyapeyakam ।।
yad yadiṣṭaṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ tatsarvaṃ vinivedayet । dhānyāṃstilāṃśca vividhān śarkarā vividhāstathā ।। uṣṇamannaṃ dvijātibhyo dātavyaṃ śreya icchatā । anyatra phalamūlebhyaḥ pānakebhyastathaiva ca ।।
nāśrūṇi pātayejjātu na kupyennānṛtaṃ vadet । na pādena spṛśedannaṃ na caitadavadhūnayet ।। krodhena caiva yat dattaṃ yad bhuktaṃ tvarayā punaḥ । yātudhānā vilumpanti jalpatā copapāditam ।।
svinnagātro na tiṣṭheta sannidhau tu dvijanmanām । na cātra śyenakākādīn pakṣiṇaḥ pratiṣedhayet । tadrūpāḥ pitarastatra samāyānti bubhukṣavaḥ ।। na dadyāt tatra hastena pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ tathā ।
na cāyasena pātreṇa na caivāśraddhayā punaḥ ।। kāñcanena tu pātreṇa rājataudumbareṇa vā । dattamakṣayatāṃ yāti khaḍgena ca viśeṣataḥ ।। pātre tu mṛṇmaye yo vai śrāddhe bhojayate pitan ।
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ bhoktā caiva purodhasaḥ ।। na paṅktyāṃ viṣamaṃ dadyānna yācenna ca dāpayet । yācitā dāpitā dātā narakān yānti dāruṇān ।। bhuñjīran vāgyatāḥ śiṣṭā na brūyuḥ prākṛtān guṇān ।
tāvaddhi pitaro aśnanti yāvannoktā havirguṇāḥ ।। nāgrāsanopaviṣṭastu bhuñjota prathamaṃ dvijaḥ । bahūnāṃ paśyatāṃ so ajñaḥ paṅktyā harati kilbiṣam ।। na kiñcid varjayecchrāddhe niyuktastu dvijottamaḥ ।
na māṃsaṃ pratiṣedheta na cānyasyānnamīkṣayet ।। yo nāśnāti dvijo māṃsaṃ niyuktaḥ pitṛkarmaṇi । sa pretya paśutāṃ yāti saṃbhavānekaviṃśatim ।। svādhyāyaṃ śrāvayedeṣāṃ dharmaśāstrāṇi caiva hi ।
itihāsapurāṇāni śrāddhakalpāṃśca śobhanān ।। tato annamutsṛjed bhukte agrato vikiran bhuvi । pṛṣṭvā tṛptāḥ stha ityevaṃ tṛptānācāmayet tataḥ ।। ācāntānanujānīyādabhito ramyatāmiti ।
svadhāstviti ca taṃ brūyurbrāhmaṇāstadanantaram ।। tato bhuktavatāṃ teṣāmannaśeṣaṃ nivedayet । yathā brūyustathā kuryādanujñātastu vai dvijaiḥ ।। pitrye svadita ityeva vākyaṃ goṣṭheṣu sūnṛtam ।
saṃpannamityabhyudaye daive rocata ityapi ।। visṛjya brāhmaṇāṃstān vai daivapūrvaṃ tu vāgyataḥ । dakṣiṇāṃ diśamākāṅ kṣanyācetemān varān pitṝn ।। dātāro no abhivardhantāṃ vedāḥ saṃtatireva ca ।
śraddhā ca no mā vyagamad bahudeyaṃ ca nosttviti ।। piṇḍāṃstu go ajaviprebhyo dadyādagnau jale api vā । madhyamaṃ tu tataḥ piṇḍamadyāt patnī sutārthinī ।। prakṣālya hastāvācamya jñātīn śeṣeṇa toṣayet ।
jñātiṣvapi catuṣṭeṣu svān bhṛtyān bhojayot tataḥ । paścāt svayaṃ ca patnībhiḥ śeṣamannaṃ samācaret ।। nodvāsayet taducchiṣṭaṃ yāvannāstaṅgato raviḥ । brahmacārī bhavetāṃ tu dampatī rajanīṃ tu tām ।।
dattvā śrāddhaṃ tathā bhuktvā sevate yastu maithunam । mahārauravamāsādya kīṭayoniṃ vrajet punaḥ ।। śucirakrodhanaḥ śāntaḥ satyavādī samāhitaḥ । svādhyāyaṃ ca tathādhvānaṃ kartā bhoktā ca varjayet ।।
śrāddhaṃ bhuktvā paraśrāddhaṃ bhuñjate ye dvijātayaḥ । mahāpātikibhistulyā yānti te narakān bahūn ।। eṣa vo vihitaḥ samyak śrāddhakalpaḥ sanātanaḥ । āmena vartayennityamudāsīno atha tattvavit ।।
anagniradhvago vāpi tathaiva vyasanānvitaḥ । āmaśrāddhaṃ dvijaḥ kuryād vidhijñaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ । tenāgnau karaṇaṃ kuryāt piṇḍāṃstenaiva nirvapet ।। yo anena vidhinā śrāddhaṃ kuryāt saṃyatamānasaḥ ।
vyapetakalpaṣo nityaṃ yogināṃ vartate padam ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena śrāddhaṃ kuryād dvijottamaḥ । ārādhito bhavedīśastena samyak sanātanaḥ ।। api mūlairphalairvāpi prakuryānnirdhano dvijaḥ ।
tilodakaistarpayed vā pitṝn snātvā samāhitaḥ ।। na jīvatpitṛko dadyāddhomāntaṃ cābhidhīyate । yeṣāṃ vāpi pitā dadyāt teṣāṃ caike pracakṣate ।। pitā pitāmahaścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ ।
yo yasya mriyate tasmai deyaṃ nānyasya tena tu ।। bhojayed vāpi jīvantaṃ yathākāmaṃ tu bhaktitaḥ । na jīvantamatikramya dadāti śrūyate śrutiḥ ।। dvyāmuṣyāyaṇiko dadyād bījikṣetrikayoḥ samam ।
ṛkyādardhaṃ samādadyānniyogotpādito yadi ।। aniyuktaḥ suto yaśca śulkato jāyate tviha । pradadyād bījine piṇḍaṃ kṣetriṇe tu tato anyathā ।। dvau piṇḍau nirvapet tābhyāṃ kṣetriṇe bījine tathā ।
kīrtayedatha caikasmin bījinaṃ kṣetriṇaṃ tataḥ ।। mṛtāhani tu kartavyamekodiṣṭaṃ vidhānataḥ । aśauce sve parikṣīṇe kāmyaṃ vai kāmataḥ punaḥ ।। pūrvāhne caiva kartavyaṃ śrāddhamabhyudayārthinā ।
devavatsarvameva syād yavaiḥ kāryā tilakriyā ।। darbhāśca ṛjavaḥ kāryā yugmān vai bhojayed dvijān । nāndīmukhāstu pitaraḥ prīyantāmiti vācayet ।। mātṛśrāddhaṃ tu pūrvaṃ syāt pitṝṇāṃ syādanantaram ।
tato mātāmahānāṃ tu vṛddhau śrāddhatrayaṃ smṛtam ।। davapūrvaṃ pradadyād vai na kuryādapradakṣiṇam । prāṅmukho nirvapet piṇḍānupavītī samāhitaḥ ।। pūrvaṃ tu mātaraḥ pūjyā bhaktyā vai sagaṇeśvarāḥ ।
sthaṇḍileṣu vicitreṣu pratimāsu dvijātiṣu ।। puṣperdhūpaiśca naivedyairgandhādyairbhūṣaṇairapi । pūjayitvā mātṛgaṇaṃ kūryācchrāddhatrayaṃ budhaḥ ।। akṛtvā mātṛyāgaṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pariveṣayet ।
tasya krodhasamāviṣṭā hiṃsāmicchanti mātaraḥ ।। daśāhaṃ prāhurāśaucaṃ sapiṇḍeṣu vipaścitaḥ । mṛteṣu vātha jāteṣu brāhmaṇānāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। nityāni caiva karmāṇi kāmyāni ca viśeṣataḥ ।
nakuryād vihitaṃ kiñcit svādhyāyaṃ manasāpica ।। śucīnakrodhanān bhūmyān śālāgnau bhāvayed dvijān । śuṣkānnena phalairvāpi vaitānaṃ juhuyāt tathā ।। na spṛśeyurimānanye na ca tebhyaḥ samāharet ।
caturthe pañcame vāhni saṃsparśaḥ kathito budhaiḥ ।। sūtake tu sapiṇḍānāṃ saṃsparśo na praduṣyati । sūtakaṃ sūtikāṃ caiva varjayitvā nṛṇāṃ punaḥ ।। adhīyānastathā yajvā vedavicca pitā bhavet ।
saṃspṛśyāḥ sarva evaite snānānmātā daśāhataḥ ।। daśāhaṃ nirguṇe proktamaśaucaṃ cātinirguṇe । ekadvitriguṇairyuktaṃ catustryekadinaiḥ śuciḥ ।। daśāhāt tu paraṃ samyagadhīyīta juhoti ca ।
caturthe tasya saṃsparśaṃ manurāha prajāpatiḥ ।। kriyāhīnasya mūrkhasya mahārogiṇa eva ca । yatheṣṭācaraṇasyāhurmaraṇāntamaśauvakam ।। trirātraṃ daśarātraṃ vā brāhmaṇānāmaśaucakam ।
prāksaṃskārāt trirātraṃ syāt tasmādūrdhvaṃ daśāhakam ।। ūnadvivārṣike prete mātāpitrostadiṣyate । trirātreṇa śucistvanyo yadi hyatyantanirguṇaḥ ।। adantajātamaraṇe pitrorekāhamiṣyate ।
jātadante trirātraṃ syād yadi syātāṃ tu nirguṇau ।। ādantajananāt sadya ācaulādekarātrakam । trirātramaupanayanāt sapiṇḍānāmudāhṛtam ।। jātamātrasya bālasya yadi syānmaraṇaṃ pituḥ ।
mātuśca sūtakaṃ tat syāt pitā syāt spṛśya eva ca ।। sadyaḥ śaucaṃ sapiṇḍānāṃ kartavyaṃ sodarasya ca । ūrdhvaṃ daśāhādekāhaṃ sodaro yadi nirguṇaḥ ।। athordhvaṃ dantajananāt sapiṇḍānāmaśaucakam ।
ekarātraṃ nirguṇānāṃ cailādūrdhvaṃ trirātrakam ।। adantajātamaraṇaṃ saṃbhaved yadi sattamāḥ । ekarātraṃ sapiṇḍānāṃ yadi te atyantanirguṇāḥ ।। vratādeśāt sapiṇḍānāmarvāk snānaṃ vidhīyate ।
sarveṣāmeva guṇināmūrdhvaṃ tu viṣamaṃ punaḥ ।। arvāk ṣaṇmāsataḥ strīṇāṃ yadi syād garbhasaṃstravaḥ । tadā māsasamaistāsāmaśaucaṃ divasaiḥ smṛtam ।। tata ūrdhvaṃ tu patane strīṇāṃ dvādaśarātrikam ।
sadyaḥ śaucaṃ sapiṇḍānāṃ garbhastrāvācca vā tataḥ ।। garbhacyutāvahorātraṃ sapiṇḍe atyantanirguṇe । yatheṣṭācaraṇe jñātau trirātramiti niścayaḥ ।। yadi syāt sūtake sūtirmaraṇe vā mṛtirbhavet ।
śeṣeṇaiva bhavecchuddhirahaḥ śeṣe trirātrakam ।। maraṇotpattiyoge tu maraṇācchuddhiriṣyate । aghavṛddhimadāśaucamūrghvaṃ cet tena śudhyati ।। atha cet pañcamīrātrimatītya parato bhavet ।
aghavṛddhimadāśaucaṃ tadā pūrveṇa śudhyati ।। deśāntaragataṃ śrutvā sūtakaṃ śāvameva tu । tāvadaprayato martyo yāvaccheṣaḥ samāpyate ।। atīte sūtake proktaṃ sapiṇḍānāṃ trirātrakam ।
tathaiva maraṇe snānamūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarād yadi ।। vedāntaviccādhīyāno yo agnimān vṛttikarṣitaḥ । sadyaḥ śaucaṃ bhavet tasya sarvāvasthāsu sarvadā ।। strīṇāmasaṃskṛtānāṃ tu pradānāt pūrvataḥ sadā ।
sapiṇḍānāṃ trirātraṃ syāt saṃskāre bhartureva hi ।। ahastvadattakanyānāmaśaucaṃ maraṇe smṛtam । ūnadvivarṣānmaraṇe sadyaḥ śaucamudāhṛtam ।। ādantāt sodare sadya ācaulādekarātrakam ।
āpradānāt trirātraṃ syād daśarātramataḥ param ।। mātāmahānāṃ maraṇe trirātraṃ syādaśaucakam । ekodakānāṃ maraṇe sūtake caitadeva hi ।। pakṣiṇī yonisambandhe bāndhaveṣu tathaiva ca ।
ekarātraṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ gurau sabrahmacāriṇi ।। prete rājani sajyotiryasya syād viṣaye sthitiḥ । gṛhe mṛtāsu dattāsu kanyakāsu tryahaṃ pituḥ ।। parapūrvāsu bhāryāsu putreṣu kṛtakeṣu ca ।
trirātraṃ syāt tathācārye svabhāryāsvanyagāsu ca ।। ācāryaputre patnyāṃ ca ahorātramudāhṛtam । ekāhaṃ syādupādhyāye svagrāme śrotriye api ca ।। trirātramasapiṇḍeṣu svagṛhe saṃsthiteṣu ca ।
ekāhaṃ cāsvavarye syādekarātraṃ tadiṣyate ।। trirātraṃ śvaśrūmaraṇe śvaśure vai tadeva hi । sadyaḥ śaucaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ sagotre saṃsthite sati ।। śuddhyed vipro daśāhena dvādaśāhena bhūmipaḥ ।
vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudyati ।। kṣatraviṭśūdradāyādā ye syurviprasya bāndhavāḥ । teṣāmaśauce viprasya daśāhācchuddhiriṣyate ।। rājanyavaiśyāvapyevaṃ hīnavarṇāsu yoniṣu ।
svameva śaucaṃ kuryātāṃ viśuddhyarthamasaṃśayam ।। sarve tūttaravarṇānāmaśaucaṃ kuryurādṛtāḥ । tadvarṇavidhidṛṣṭena svaṃ tu śaucaṃ svayoniṣu ।। ṣaḍrātraṃ vā trirātraṃ syādekarātraṃ krameṇa hi ।
vaiśyakṣatriyaviprāṇāṃ śūdreṣvāśaucameva tu ।। ardhamāso atha ṣaḍrātraṃ trirātraṃ dvijapuṅgavāḥ । śūdrakṣatriyaviprāṇāṃ vaiśyeṣvāśaucamiṣyate ।। ṣaḍrātraṃ vai daśāhaṃ ca viprāṇāṃ vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ ।
aśaucaṃ kṣatriye proktaṃ krameṇa dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।। śūdraviṭkṣatriyāṇāṃ tu brāhmaṇe saṃsthite sati । daśarātreṇa śuddhiḥ syādityāha kamalodbhavaḥ ।। asapiṇḍaṃ dvijaṃ pretaṃ vipro nirhṛtya bandhuvat ।
aśitvā ca sahoṣitvā daśarātreṇa śudhyati ।। yadyannamatti teṣāṃ tu trirātreṇa tataḥ śuciḥ । anadannannamahnaiva na ca tasmin gṛhe vaset ।। sodakeṣvetadeva syānmāturāpteṣu bandhuṣu ।
daśāhena śavasparśe sapiṇḍaścaiva śudhyati ।। yadi nirharati pretaṃ prolabhākrāntamānasaḥ । daśāhena dvijaḥ śudhyed dvādaśāhena bhūmipaḥ ।। ardhamāsena vaiśyastu śūdro māsena śudhyati ।
ṣaḍrātreṇāthavā sarve trirātreṇāthavā punaḥ ।। anāthaṃ caiva nirhṛtya brāhmaṇaṃ dhanavarjitam । snātvā saṃprāśya tu ghṛtaṃ śudhyanti brāhmaṇādayaḥ ।। avaraśced varaṃ varṇamavaraṃ vā varo yadi ।
aśauce saṃspṛśet snehāt tadāśaucena śudhyati ।। pretībhūtaṃ dvijaṃ vipro yo anugacchata kāmataḥ । snātvā sacailaṃ spṛṣṭvāgniṃ ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati ।। ekāhāt kṣatriye śuddhirvaiśye syācca dvyahena tu ।
śūdre dinatrayaṃ proktaṃ prāṇāyāmaśataṃ punaḥ ।। anasthisaṃcite śūdre rauti ced brāhmaṇaḥ svakaiḥ । trirātraṃ syāt tathāśaucamekāhaṃ tvanyathā smṛtam ।। asthisaṃcayanādarvāgekāhaṃ kṣatravaiśyayoḥ ।
anyathā caiva sajyotirbrāhmaṇe snānameva tu ।। anasthisaṃcit vipre brāhmaṇo rauti cet tadā । snānenaiva bhavecchuddhiḥ sacailena na saṃśayaḥ ।। yastaiḥ sahāśanaṃ kuryācchayanādīni caiva hi ।
bāndhavo vāparo vāpi sa daśāhena śudhyati ।। yasteṣāmannamaśnāti sakṛdevāpi kāmataḥ । tadāśauce nivṛtte asau snānaṃ kṛtvā viśudhyati ।। yāvattadannamaśnāti durbhikṣopahato naraḥ ।
tāvantyahānyaśaucaṃ syāt prāyaścittaṃ tataścaret ।। dāhādyaśaucaṃ kartavyaṃ dvijānāmagnihotriṇām । sapiṇḍānāṃ tu maraṇe maraṇāditareṣu ca ।। sapiṇḍatā ca puruṣe saptame vinivartate ।
samānodakabhāvastu janmanāmnoravedane ।। pitā pitāmahaścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ । lepabhājastrayaścātmā sāpiṇḍyaṃ sāptapauruṣaṇ ।। aprattānāṃ tathā strīṇāṃ sāpiṇḍyaṃ sāptapauruṣam ।
ūḍhānāṃ bhartusāpiṇḍyaṃ prāha devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। ye caikajātā bahavo bhinnayonaya eva ca । bhinnavarṇāstu sāpiṇḍyaṃ bhavet teṣāṃ tripūruṣam ।। kāravaḥ śilpino vaidyā dāsīdāsāstathaiva ca ।
dātāro niyamī caiva brahmavidbrahmacāriṇau ।। satriṇo vratinastāvat sadyaḥ śaucā udāhṛtāḥ । rājā caivābhiṣiktaśca prāṇasatriṇa eva ca ।। yajñe vivāhakāle ca devayāge tathaiva ca ।
sadyaḥ śaucaṃ samākhyātaṃ durbhikṣe cāpyupadrave ।। ḍimbāhavahatānāṃ ca vidyutā pārthivairdvijaiḥ । sadyaḥ śaucaṃ samākhyātaṃ sarpādimaraṇe tathā ।। agnau maruprapatane vīrādhvanyapyanāśake ।
brāhmaṇārthe ca saṃnyaste sadyaḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate ।। naiṣṭhikānāṃ vanasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām । nāśaucaṃ kīrtyate sadbhiḥ patite ca tathā mṛte ।। patitānāṃ na dāhaḥ syānnāntyeṣṭirnāsthisaṃcayaḥ ।
na cāśrupātapiṇḍau vā kāryaṃ śrāddhādi kaṅkvacit ।। vyāpādayet tathātmānaṃ svayaṃ yo agniviṣādibhiḥ । vihitaṃ tasya nāśaucaṃ nāgnirnāpyudakādikam ।। atha kaścit pramādena mriyate agniviṣādibhiḥ ।
tasyāśaucaṃ vidhātavyaṃ kāryaṃ caivodakādikam ।। jāte kumāre tadahaḥ kāmaṃ kuryāt pratigraham । hiraṇyadhānyagovāsastilānnaguḍasarpiṣām ।। phalāni puṣpaṃ śākaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ kāṣṭhameva ca ।
toyaṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ tailamauṣadhaṃ kṣīrameva ca । āśaucināṃ gṛhād grāhyaṃ śuṣkānnaṃ caiva nityaśaḥ ।। āhitāgniryathānyāyaṃ dagdhavyastribhiragnibhiḥ । anāhitāgnirgṛhyeṇa laukikenetaro janaḥ ।।
dehābhāvāt palāśaistu kṛtvā pratikṛtiṃ punaḥ । dāhaḥ kāryo yathānyāyaṃ sapiṇḍaiḥ śraddhayānvitaiḥ ।। sakṛtprasiñcantyudakaṃ nāmagotreṇa vāgyatāḥ । daśāhaṃ bāndhavaiḥ sārdhaṃ sarve caivārdravāsasaḥ ।।
piṇḍaṃ pratidinaṃ dadyuḥ sāyaṃ prātaryathāvidhi । pretāya ca gṛhadvāri caturthe bhojayed dvijān ।। dvitīye ahani kartavyaṃ kṣurakarma sabāndhavaiḥ । caturthe bāndhavaiḥ sarvairasthanāṃ saṃcayanaṃ bhavet ।
pūrvaṃ tu bhojayed viprānayugmān śraddhayā śucīn ।। pañcame navame caiva tathaivaikādaśe ahani । ayugmān bhojayed viprān navaśrāddhaṃ tu tadviduḥ ।। ekādaśe ahni kurvota pretamuddiśya bhāvataḥ ।
dvādaśe vātha kartavyamanindye tvathavāhani । ekaṃ pavitramekor'ghaḥ piṇḍapātraṃ tathaiva ca ।। evaṃ mṛtāhni kartavyaṃ pratimāsaṃ tu vatsaram । sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ proktaṃ pūrṇe saṃvatsare punaḥ ।।
kuryāccatvāri pātrāṇi pretādīnāṃ dvijottamāḥ । pretārthaṃ pitṛpātreṣu pātramāsecayet tataḥ ।। ye samānā iti dvābhyāṃ piṇḍānapyevameva hi । sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ devapūrvaṃ vidhīyate ।।
pitṝnāvāhayet tatra punaḥ pretaṃ ca nirdiśet । ye sapiṇḍīkṛtāḥ pretāna teṣāṃ syāt pṛthakkriyāḥ । yastu kuryāt pṛthak piṇḍaṃ pitṛhā so abhijāyate ।। mṛte pitari vai putraḥ piṇḍamabdaṃ samācaret ।
dadyāccānnaṃ sodakumbhaṃ pratyahaṃ pretadharmataḥ ।। pārvaṇena vidhānena saṃvatsarikamiṣyate । pratisaṃvatsaraṃ kāryaṃ vidhireṣa sanātanaḥ ।। mātāpitroḥ sutaiḥ kāryaṃ piṇḍadānādikaṃ ca yat ।
patnī kuryāt sutābhāve patnya bhāve sahodahaḥ ।। anenaiva vidhāne jīvan vā śrāddhamācaret । kṛtvā dānādikaṃ sarvaṃ śraddhāyuktaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। eṣa vaḥ kathitaḥ samyag gṛhasthānāṃ kriyāvidhiḥ ।
strīṇāṃ tu bhartṛśuśrūṣā dharmo nānya iheṣyate ।। svadharmaparamo nityamīśvirārpitamānasaḥ । prāpnoti tat paraṃ sthānaṃ yaduktaṃ vedavādibhiḥ ।। agnihotraṃ tu juhuyādādyante aharniśoḥ sadā ।
darśena caiva pakṣānte paurṇamāsena caiva hi ।। śasyānte navaśasyeṣṭyā tathartvante dvijo adhvaraiḥ । paśunā tvayanasyānte samānte saumikairmakhaiḥ ।। nāniṣṭvā navaśasyeṣṭyā paśunā vāgnimān dvijaḥ ।
navānnamadyānmāṃsaṃ vā dīrghamāyurjijīviṣuḥ ।। navenānnena cāniṣṭvā paśuhavyena cāganyaḥ । prāṇānevāttumicchanti navānnāmiṣagṛddhinaḥ ।। sāvitrān śāntihomāṃśca kuryāt parvasu nityaśaḥ ।
pitṝṃścaivāṣṭakāsvarcan nityamanvaṣṭakāsu ca ।। eṣa dharmaḥ paro nityamapadharmo anya ucyate । trayāṇāmiha varṇānāṃ gṛhasthāśramavāsinām ।। nāstikyādathavālasyād yo agnīn nādhātumicchati ।
yajeta vā na yajñena sa yāti narakān bahūn ।। tāmistramandhatāmistraṃ mahārauravarauravau । kumbhīpākaṃ vaitaraṇīmasipatravanaṃ tathā ।। anyāṃśca narakān ghorān saṃprāpyānte sudurmatiḥ ।
antyajānāṃ kule viprāḥ śūdrayonau ca jāyate ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena brāhmaṇo hi viśeṣataḥ । ādhāyāgniṃ viśuddhātmā yajeta parameśvaram ।। agnihotrāt paro dharmo dvijānāṃ neha vidyate ।
tasmādārādhayennityamagnihotreṇa śāśvatam ।। yaścādhāyāgnimālasyānna yaṣṭuṃ devamicchati । so asau mūḍho na saṃbhāṣyaḥ kiṃ punarnāstiko janaḥ ।। yasya traivārṣikaṃ bhaktaṃ paryāptaṃ bhṛtyavṛttaye ।
adhikaṃ cāpi vidyeta sa somaṃ pātumarhati ।। eṣa vai sarvayajñānāṃ somaḥ prathama iṣyate । somenārādhayed devaṃ somalokamaheśvaram ।। na somayāgādadhiko maheśārādhane kratuḥ ।
samo vā vidyate tasmāt somenābhyarcayet param ।। pitāmahena viprāṇāmādāvabhihitaḥ śubhaḥ । dharmo vimuktaye sākṣācchrautaḥ smārto dvidhā punaḥ ।। śrautastretāgnisaṃbandhāt smārtaḥ pūrvaṃ mayoditaḥ ।
śreyaskaratamaḥ śrautastasmācchrautaṃ samācaret ।। ubhāvabhihitau dharmau vedādeva viniḥ sṛtau । śiṣṭācārastṛtīyaḥ syācchratismṛtyoralābhataḥ ।। dharmeṇābhigato yaistu vedaḥ saparibṛṃhaṇaḥ ।
te śiṣṭā brāhmaṇāḥ proktā nityamātmaguṇānvitāḥ ।। teṣāmabhimato yaḥ syāccetasā nityameva hi । sa dharmaḥ kathitaḥ sadbhirnānyeṣāmiti dhāraṇā ।। purāṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca vedānāmupabṛṃhaṇam ।
ekasmād brahmavijñānaṃ dharmajñānaṃ tathaikataḥ ।। dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ tatpramāṇataraṃ smṛtam । dharmaśāstraṃ purāṇaṃ tad brahmajñāne parā pramā ।। nānyato jāyate dharmo brahmavidyā ca vaidikī ।
tasmād dharmaṃ purāṇaṃ ca śraddhātavyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ ।। eṣa vo abhihitaḥ kṛtsno gṛhasthāśramavāsinaḥ । dvijāteḥ paramo dharmo vartanāni nibodhata ।। dvividhastu gṛhī jñeyaḥ sādhakaścāpyasādhakaḥ ।
adhyāpanaṃ yājanaṃ ca pūrvasyāhuḥ pratigraham । kusīdakṛṣivāṇijyaṃ prakurvotāsvayaṅkṛtam ।। kṛṣerabhāvād vāṇijyaṃ tadabhāvāt kusīdakam । āpatkalpo hyaṃ jñeyaḥ pūrvokto mukhya iṣyate ।।
svayaṃ vā karṣaṇaṃ kuryād vāṇijyaṃ vā kusīdakam । kaṣṭā pāpīyasī vṛttiḥ kusīdaṃ tad vivarjayet ।। kṣātravṛttiṃ parāṃ prahurna svayaṃ karṣaṇaṃ dvijaiḥ । tasmāt kṣātreṇa varteta vartanenāpadi dvijaḥ ।।
tena cāvāpyajīvaṃstu vaiśyavṛttiṃ kṛṣiṃ vrajet । na kathañcana kurvota brāhmaṇaḥ karma karṣaṇam ।। labdhalābhaḥ pitṝn devān brāhmaṇāṃścāpi pūjayet । te tṛptāstasya taṃ doṣaṃ śamayanti na saṃśayaḥ ।।
devebhyaśca pitṛbhyaśca dadyād bhāgaṃ tu viṃśakam । triṃśadbhāgaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ kṛṣiṃ kurvan na duṣyati ।। vaṇik pradadyād dviguṇaṃ kusīdī triguṇaṃ punaḥ । kṛṣīvalo na doṣeṇa yujyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
śiloñchaṃ vāpyādadīta gṛhasthaḥ sādhakaḥ punaḥ । vidyāśilpādayastvanye bahavo vṛttihetavaḥ ।। asādhakastu yaḥ prokto gṛhasthāśramasaṃsthitaḥ । śiloñche tasya kathite dve vṛttī paramarṣibhiḥ ।।
amṛtenāthavā jīvenmṛtenāpyathavā yadi । ayācitaṃ syādamṛtaṃ mṛtaṃ bhekṣaṃ tu yācitam ।। kuśūladhānyako vā syāt kumbhīdhānyaka eva vā । tryahaihiko vāpi bhavedaśvastanika eva ca ।।
caturṇāmapi caiteṣāṃ dvijānāṃ gṛhamedhinām । śreyān paraḥ paro jñeyo dharmato lokajittamaḥ ।। ṣaṭkarmaiko bhavatyeṣāṃ tribhiranyaḥ pravartate । dvābhyāmekaścaturthastu brahmasatreṇa jīvati ।।
vartayaṃstu śiloñchābhyāmagnihotraparāyaṇaḥ । iṣṭīḥ pārvāyaṇāntīyāḥ kevalā nirvapet sadā ।। na lokavṛtiṃ varteta vṛttihetoḥ kathañcana । ajihmāmaśaṭhāṃ śuddhāṃ jīved brāhmaṇajīvikām ।।
yācitvā vāpi sadbhyo annaṃ pitṝndevāṃstu toṣayet । yācayed vā śuciṃ dāntaṃ na tṛpyeta svayaṃ tataḥ ।। yastu dravyārjanaṃ kṛtvā gṛhasthastoṣayenna tu । devān pitṛṃśca vidhinā śunāṃ yoniṃ vrajatyasau ।।
dharmaścārthaśca kāmaśca śreyo mokṣaścatuṣṭayam । dharmāviruddhaḥ kāmaḥ syād brāhmaṇānāṃ tu netaraḥ ।। yor'tho dharmāya nātmārthaḥ sor'tho anarthastathetaraḥ । tasmādarthaṃ samāsādya dadyād vai juhuyād yajet ।।
athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dānadharmamanuttamam । brahmaṇābhihitaṃ pūrvamṛṣīṇāṃ brahmavādinām ।। arthānāmudite pātre śraddhayā pratipādanam । dānamityabhinirdiṣṭaṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।।
yad dadāti viśiṣṭebhyaḥ śraddhayā parayā yutaḥ । tad vai vittamahaṃ manye śeṣaṃ kasyāpi rakṣati ।। nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ trividhaṃ dānamucyate । caturthaṃ vimalaṃ proktaṃ sarvadānottamottamam ।।
ahanyahani yat kiñcid dīyate anupakāriṇe । anuddiśya phalaṃ tasmād brāhmaṇāya tu nityakam ।। yat tu pāpopaśāntyarthaṃ dīyate viduṣāṃ kare । naimittikaṃ taduddiṣṭaṃ dānaṃ sadbhiranuṣṭhitam ।।
apatyavijayaiśvaryasvargārthaṃ yat pradīyate । dānaṃ tat kāmyamākhyātamṛṣibhirdharmacintakaiḥ ।। yadīśvaraprīṇanārthaṃ brahmavitsu pradīyate । cetasā dharmayuktena dānaṃ tad vimalaṃ śivam ।।
dānadharmaṃ niṣeveta pātramāsādya śaktitaḥ । utpatsyate hi tatpātraṃ yat tārayati sarvataḥ ।। kuṭumbabhaktavasanād deyaṃ yadatiricyate । anyathā dīyate yaddhi na tad dānaṃ phalapradam ।।
śrotriyāya kulīnāya vinītāya tapasvine । vṛttasthāya daridrāya pradeyaṃ bhaktipūrvakam ।। yastu dadyānmahīṃ bhaktyā brāhmaṇāyāhitāgnaye । sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra gatvā na śocati ।।
ikṣubhiḥ saṃtatāṃ bhumiṃ yavagodhūmaśalinīm । dadāti vedaviduṣe yaḥ sa bhūyo na jāyate ।। gocarmamātrāmapi vā yo bhūmiṃ saṃprayacchati । brāhmaṇāya daridrāya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
bhūmidānāt paraṃ dānaṃ vidyate neha kiñcana । annadānaṃ tena tulyaṃ vidyādānaṃ tato adhikam ।। yo brāhmaṇāya śāntāya śucaye dharmaśāline । dadāti vidyāṃ vidhinā brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
dadyādaharahastvannaṃ śraddhayā brahmacāriṇe । sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaṇaḥ sthānamāpnuyāt ।। gṛhasthāyānnadānena phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ । āmamevāsya dātavyaṃ dattvāpnoti parāṃ gatim ।।
vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ tu brāhmaṇān sapta pañca vā । upoṣya vidhinā śāntaḥ śuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ ।। pūjayitvā tilaiḥ kṛṣṇairmadhunā na viśeṣataḥ । gandhādibhiḥ samabhyarcya vācayed vā svyaṃ vadet ।।
prīyatāṃ dharmarājeti yad vā manasi vartate । yāvajjīvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva naśyati ।। kṛṣṇājine tilān kṛttvā hiraṇyaṃ madhusarpiṣī । dadāti yastu viprāya sarvaṃ tarati duṣkṛtam ।।
kṛtānnamudakumbhaṃ ca vaiśākhyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ । nirdiśya dharmarājāya viprebhyo mucyate bhayāt ।। suvarṇatilayuktaistu brāhmaṇān sapta pañca vā । tarpayedudapātraistu brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।।
māghamāse tu viprastu dvādaśyāṃ samupoṣitaḥ । śuklāmvaradharaḥ kṛṣṇaistilairhutvā hutāśanam ।। pradadyād brāhmaṇebhyastu tilāneva samāhitaḥ । janmaprabhṛti yatpāpaṃ sarvaṃ tarati vai dvijaḥ ।।
amāvasyāmanuprāpya brāhmaṇāya tapasvine । yatkicid devadeveśaṃ dadyāccoddiśya śaṅkaram ।। prīyatāmīśvaraḥ somo mahādevaḥ sanātanaḥ । saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva naśyati ।।
yastu kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ snātvā devaṃ pinākinam । ārādhayed dvijamukhe na tasyāsti punarbhavaḥ ।। kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ viśeṣeṇa dhārmikāya dvijātaye । snātvābhyarcya yathānyāyaṃ pādaprakṣālanādibhiḥ ।।
prīyatāṃ me mahādevo dadyād dravyaṃ svakīyakam । sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim ।। dvijaiḥ kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ viśeṣataḥ । amāvāsyāyāṃ bhaktaistu pūjanīyastrilocanaḥ ।।
ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāro dvādaśyāṃ puruṣottamam । arcayed bāhmaṇamukhe sa gacchet paramaṃ padam ।। eṣā tithirvaiṣṇavīṃ syād dvādaśī śuklapakṣake । tasyāmārādhayed devaṃ prayatnena janārdanam ।।
yatkiñcid devamīśānamuddiśya brāhmaṇe śucau । dīyate viṣṇave vāpi tadanantaphalapradam ।। yo hi yāṃ devatāmicchet samārādhayituṃ naraḥ । brāhmaṇān pūjayed yatnāt satasyāṃ toṣayet tataḥ ।।
dvijānāṃ vapurāsthāya nityaṃ tiṣṭhanti devatāḥ । pūjyante brāhmaṇālābhe pratimādiṣvapi kvacit ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena tat tat phalamabhīpsatā । dvijeṣu devatā nityaṃ pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ ।।
vibhūtikāmaḥ satataṃ pūjayed vai purandaram । brahmavarcasakāmastu brahmāṇaṃ brahmakāmukaḥ ।। ārogyakāmo atha raviṃ dhanakāmo hutāśanam । karmaṇāṃ siddhikāmastu pūjayed vai vināyakam ।।
bhogakāmastu śaśinaṃ balakāmaḥ samīraṇam । mumukṣuḥ sarvasaṃsārāt prayatnenārcayeddharim ।। yastu yogaṃ tathā mokṣamanvicchejjñānamaiśvaram । sor'cayed vai virūpākṣaṃ prayatneneśvareśvaram ।।
ye vāñchanti mahāyogān jñānāni ca maheśvaram । te pūjayanti bhūteśaṃ keśavaṃ cāpi bhoginaḥ ।। vāridastṛptimāpnoti sukhamakṣayyamannadaḥ । tilapradaḥ prajāmiṣṭāṃ dīpadaścakṣuruttamam ।।
bhūmidaḥ sarvamāpnoti dīrghamāyurhiraṇyadaḥ । gṛhado agryāṇi veśmāni rūpyado rūpamuttamam ।। vāsodaścandrasālokyamaśvisālokyamaśvadaḥ । anaḍudaḥ śriyaṃ puṣṭāṃ godo vradhnasya viṣṭapam ।।
yānaśayyāprado bhāryāmaiśvaryamabhayapradaḥ । dhānyadaḥ śāśvataṃ saukhyaṃ brahmado brahmasātmyatām ।। dhānyānyapi yathāśakti vipreṣu pratipādayet । vedavitsu viśiṣṭeṣu pretya svargaṃ samaśnute ।।
gavāṃ ghāsapradānena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate । indhanānāṃ pradānena dīptāgnirjāyate naraḥ ।। phalamūlāni śākāni bhojyāni vividhāni ca । pradadyād brāhmaṇebhyastu mudā yuktaḥ sadā bhavet ।।
auṣadhaṃ snehamāhāraṃ rogiṇe rogaśāntaye । dadāno rogarahitaḥ sukhī dīrghāyureva ca ।। asipatravanaṃ mārgaṃ kṣuradhārāsamanvitam । tīvritāpaṃ ca tarati chatropānatprado naraḥ ।।
yad yadiṣṭatamaṃ loke yaccāpi dayitaṃ gṛhe । tattad guṇavate deyaṃ tadevākṣyamicchatā ।। apane viṣuve caiva grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ । saṃkrāntyādiṣu kāleṣu dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ।।
prayāgādiṣu tīrtheṣu puṇyeṣvāyataneṣu ca । dattvā cākṣayamāpnoti nadīṣu ca vaneṣu ca ।। dānadharmāt paro dharmo bhūtānāṃ neha vidyate । tasmād viprāya dātavyaṃ śrotriyāya dvijātibhiḥ ।।
svagāyurbhūtikāmena tathā pāpopaśāntaye । mumukṣuṇā ca dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyastathānvaham ।। dīyamānaṃ tu yo mohād goviprāgnisureṣu ca । nivārayati pāpātmā tiryagyoniṃ vrajet tu saḥ ।।
yastu dravyārjanaṃ kṛtvā nārcayed brāhmaṇān surān । sarvasvamapahṛtyainaṃ rājā rāṣṭrāt pravāsayet ।। yastu durbhikṣavelāyāmannādyaṃ na prayacchati । mriyamāṇeṣu vipreṣu brāhmaṇaḥ sa tu garhitaḥ ।।
na tasmāt pratigṛhṇīyurna viśeyuśca tena hi । aṅkayitvā svakād rāṣṭrāt taṃ rājā vipravāsayet ।। yastvasadbhyo dadātīha svadravyaṃ dharmasādhanam । sa pūrvābhyadhikaḥ pāpī narake pacyate naraḥ ।।
svādhyāyavanto ye viprā vidyāvanto jitendriyāḥ । satyasaṃyamasaṃyuktāstebhyo dadyād dvijottamāḥ ।। subhuktamapi vidvāṃsaṃ dhārmikaṃ bhojayed dvijam । na tu mūrkhamavṛttasthaṃ daśarātramupoṣitam ।।
sannikṛṣṭamatikramya śrotriyaṃ yaḥ prayacchati । sa tena karmaṇā pāpī dahatyāsaptamaṃ kulam ।। yadisyādadhiko vipraḥ śīlavidyādibhiḥ svayam । tasmai yatnena dātavyaṃ atikramyāpi sannidhim ।।
yo arcitaṃ pratigṛhṇīyād dadyādarcitameva ca । tāvubhau gacchataḥ svargaṃ narakaṃ tu viparyaye ।। na vāryapi prayaccheta nāstike haituke api ca । pāṣaṇḍeṣu ca sarveṣu nāvedavidi dharmavit ।।
apūpaṃ ca hiraṇyaṃ ca gāmaśvaṃ pṛthivīṃ tilān । avidvān pratigṛhṇāno bhasmī bhavati kāṣṭhavat ।। dvijātibhyo dhanaṃ lipset praśastebhyo dvijottamaḥ । api vā jātimātrebhyo na tu śūdrāt kathañcana ।।
vṛttisaṅkocamanvicchenneheta dhanavistaram । dhanalobhe prasaktastu brāhmaṇyādeva hīyate ।। vedānadhītya sakalān yajñāṃścāvāpya sarvaśaḥ । na tāṃ gatimavāpnoti saṅkocād yāmavāpnuyāt ।।
pratigraharucirna syāt yātrārthaṃ tu samāharet । sthityarthādadhikaṃ gṛhṇan brāhmaṇo yātyadhogatim ।। yastu yācanako nityaṃ na sa svargasya bhājanam । udvejayati bhūtāni yathā caurastathaiva saḥ ।।
gurūn bhṛtyāṃścojjihīrṣurarciṣyan devatātithīn । sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyānna tu tṛpyet svayaṃ tataḥ ।। evaṃ gṛhastho yuktātmā devatātithipūjakaḥ । vartamānaḥ saṃyātātmā yāti tat paramaṃ padam ।।
putre nidhāya vā sarvaṃ gatvāraṇyaṃ tu tattvavit । ekākī vicarennityamudāsīnaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। eṣa vaḥ kathito dharmo gṛhasthānāṃ dvijottamāḥ । jñātvānutiṣṭhenniyataṃ tathānuṣṭhāpayed dvijān ।।
gṛhadharmeṇa samarcayedajastram । prakṛtiṃ yāti paraṃ na yāti janma ।। evaṃ gṛhāśrame sthitvā dvitīyaṃ bhāgamāyuṣaḥ । vānaprasthāśramaṃ gacchet sadāraḥ sāgnireva ca ।।
nikṣipya bhāryāṃ putreṣu gacched vanamathāpi vā । dṛṣṭvāpatyasya cāpatyaṃ jarjarīkṛtavigrahaḥ ।। śuklapakṣasya pūrvāhne praśaste cottarāyaṇe । gatvāraṇyaṃ niyamavāṃstapaḥ kuryāt samāhitaḥ ।।
phalamūlāni pūtāni nityamāhāramāharet । yatāhāro bhavet tena pūjayet pitṛdevatāḥ ।। pūjayitvātithiṃ nityaṃ snātvā cābhyarcayet surān । gṛhādāhṛtya cāśnīyādaṣṭau grāsān samāhitaḥ ।।
jaṭāśca bibhṛyānnityaṃ nakharomāṇi notsṛjet । svādhyāyaṃ sarvadā kuryānniyacched vācamanyataḥ ।। agnihotraṃ ca juhuyāt pañcayajñān samācaret । munyannaiṃrvividhairmedhyaiḥ śākamūlaphalena vā ।।
cīravāsā bhavennityaṃ snāyāt triṣavaṇaṃ śuciḥ । sarvabhūtānukampī syāt pratigrahavivarjitaḥ ।। darśena paurṇamāsena yajet niyataṃ dvijaḥ । ṛkṣeṣvāgrayaṇe caiva cāturmāsyāni cāharet ।
uttarāyaṇaṃ ca kramaśo dakṣasyāyanameva ca ।। vāsantaiḥ śāradairmedhyairmunyannaiḥ svayamāhṛtaiḥ । puroḍāśāṃścarūṃścaiva vidhivannirvapet pṛthak ।। devatābhyaśca tad hutvā vanyaṃ medhyataraṃ haviḥ ।
śeṣaṃ samupabhuñjīta lavaṇaṃ ca svayaṃ kṛtam ।। varjayenmadhumāṃsāni bhaumāni kavakāni ca । bhūstṛṇaṃ śigrukaṃ caiva śleṣmātakaphalāni ca ।। na phālakṛṣṭamaśnīyādutsṛṣṭamapi kenacit ।
na grāmajātānyārto api puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca ।। śrāvaṇenaiva vidhinā vahniṃ paricaret sadā । na druhyet sarvabhūtāni nirdvandvo nirbhayo bhavet ।। na naktaṃ kiñcidaśnīyād rātrau dhyānaparo bhavet ।
jitendriyo jitakrodhastattvajñānavicintakaḥ । brahmacārī bhavennityaṃ na patnīmapi saṃśrayet ।। yastu patnyā vanaṃ gatvā maithunaṃ kāmataścaret । tad vrataṃ tasya lupyeta prāyaścittīyate dvijaḥ ।।
tatra yo jāyate garbho na saṃspṛśyo dvijātibhiḥ । na hi vede adhikāro asya tadvaṃśepyevameva hi ।। adhaḥ śayīta satataṃ sāvitrījāpyatatparaḥ । śaraṇyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ saṃvibhāgaparaḥ sadā ।।
parivādaṃ mṛṣāvādaṃ nidrālasyaṃ vivarjayet । ekāgniraniketaḥ syāt prokṣitāṃ bhūmimāśrayet ।। mṛgaiḥ saha cared vāsaṃ taiḥ sahaiva ca saṃvaset । śilāyāṃ śarkarāyāṃ vā śayīta susamāhitaḥ ।।
sadyaḥ prakṣālako vā syānmāsasaṃcayiko api vā । ṣaṇmāsanicayo vā syāt samānicaya eva vā ।। tyajedāśvayuje māsi saṃpannaṃ pūrvasaṃcitam । jīrṇāni caiva vāsāṃsi śākamūlaphalāni ca ।।
dantolūkhaliko vāsyāt kāpotīṃ vṛttimāśrayet । aśmakuṭṭo bhaved vāpi kālapakvabhugeva vā ।। naktaṃ cānna samaśnīyād divā cāhṛtya śaktitaḥ । caturthakāliko vā syāt syādvāpyaṣṭamakālikaḥ ।।
cāndrāyaṇavidhānairvā śukle kṛṣṇe ca vartayet । pakṣe pakṣe samaśnīyād yavāgūṃ kvathitāṃ sakṛt ।। puṣpamūlaphalairvāpi kevalairvartayet sadā । svābhāvikaiḥ svayaṃ śīrṇairvaikhānasamate sthitaḥ ।।
bhūmau vā parivarteta tiṣṭhed vā prapadairdinam । sthānāsanābhyāṃ viharenna kvacid dhairyamutsṛjet ।। grīṣme pañcatapāśca syād varṣāsvabhrāvakāśakaḥ । ārdravāsāstu hemante kramaśo vardhayaṃstapaḥ ।।
upaspṛśya triṣavaṇaṃ pitṛdevāṃśca tarpayet । ekapādena tiṣṭheta marīcīn vā pibet tadā ।। pañcāgnirdhūmapo vā syāduṣmapaḥ somapo api vā । payaḥ pibecchuklapakṣe kṛṣṇāpakṣe tu gomayam ।
śīrṇaparṇāśano vā syāt kṛcchrair vā vartayet sadā ।। yogābhyāsarataśca syād rudrādhyāyī bhavet sadā । atharvaśiraso adhyetā vedāntābhyāsatatparaḥ ।। yamān seveta satataṃ niyamāṃścāpyatandritaḥ ।
kṛṣṇājinī sottarīyaḥ śuklayajñopavītavān ।। atha cāgnīn samāropya svātmani dhyānatatparaḥ । anagniraniketaḥ syānmunirmokṣaparo bhavet ।। tāpaseṣveva vipreṣu yātrikaṃ bhaikṣamāharet ।
gṛhamedhiṣu cānyeṣu dvijeṣu vanavāsiṣu ।। grāmādāhṛtya vāśnīyādaṣṭau grāsān vane vasan । pratigṛhya puṭenaiva pāṇinā śakalena vā ।। vividhāścopaniṣada ātmasaṃsiddhaye japet ।
vidyāviśeṣān sāvitrīṃ rudrādhyāyaṃ tathaiva ca ।। mahāprāsthānikaṃ cāsau kuryādanaśanaṃ tu vā । agnipraveśamanyad vā brarhmārpaṇavidhau sthitaḥ ।। saṃśrayedaśivapuñjanāśanam ।
yāti yatra jagato asya saṃsthitiḥ ।। evaṃ vanāśrame sthitvā tṛtīyaṃ bhāgamāyuṣaḥ । caturthamāyuṣo bhāgaṃ saṃnyāsena nayet kramāt ।। agnīnātmanī saṃsthāpya dvijaḥ pravrajito bhavet ।
yogābhyāsarataḥ śānto brahmavidyāparāyaṇaḥ ।। yadā manasi saṃjātaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ sarvavastuṣu । tadā saṃnyāsamicchecca patitaḥ syād viparyaye ।। prājāpatyāṃ nirūpyeṣṭimāgneyīmathavā punaḥ ।
dāntaḥ pakvakaṣāyo asau brahmāśramamupāśrayet ।। jñānasaṃnyāsinaḥ kecid vedasaṃnyāsinaḥ pare । karmasaṃnyāsinastvanye trividhāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। yaḥ sarvasaṅganirmukto nirdvandvaścaiva nirbhayaḥ ।
procyate jñānasaṃnyāsī svātmanyeva vyavasthitaḥ ।। vedamevābhyasennityaṃ nirāśī niṣparigrahaḥ । procyate vedasaṃnyāsī mumukṣurvijitendriyaḥ ।। yastvagnīnātmasātkṛtvā brahmārpaṇaparo dvijaḥ ।
jñeyaḥ sa karmasaṃnyāsī mahāyajñaparāyaṇaḥ ।। trayāṇāmapi caiteṣāṃ jñānī tvabhyadhiko mataḥ । na tasya vidyate kāryaṃ na liṅgaṃ vā vipaścitaḥ ।। nirmamo nirbhayaḥ śānto nirdvandvaḥ parṇabhojanaḥ ।
jīrṇakaupīnavāsāḥ syānnagno vā dhyānatatparaḥ ।। brahmacārī mitāhāro grāmādannaṃ samāharet । adhyātmamatirāsīta nirapekṣo nirāmiṣaḥ ।। ātmanaiva sahāyena sukhārthaṃ vicarediha ।
nābhinandeta maraṇaṃ nābhinandeta jīvitam ।। kālameva pratīkṣeta nideśaṃ bhṛtako yathā । nādhyetavyaṃ na vaktavyaṃ śrotavyaṃ na kadācana । evaṃ jñātvā paro yogī brahmabhūyāya kalpate ।।
ekavāsāthavā vidvān kaupīnācchādanastathā । muṇḍī śikhī vātha bhavet tridaṇḍī niṣparigrahaḥ । kāṣāyavāsāḥ satataṃ dhyānayogaparāyaṇaḥ ।। grāmānte vṛkṣamūle vā vased devālaye api vā ।
samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca tathā mānāpamānayoḥ । bhaikṣyeṇa vartayennityaṃ naikānnādī bhavet kvacit ।। yastu mohena vālasyādekānnādī bhaved yatiḥ । na tasya niṣkṛtiḥ kācid dharmaśāstreṣu kathyate ।।
rāgadveṣavimuktātmā samaloṣṭāśmakāñcanaḥ । prāṇihaṃsānivṛttaśca maunī syāt sarvanispṛhaḥ ।। dṛṣṭipūtaṃ nyaset pādaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet । satyapūtāṃ vaded vāṇīṃ manaḥ pūtaṃ samācaret ।।
naikatra nivased deśe varṣābhyo anyatra bhikṣukaḥ । snānaśaucarato nityaṃ kamaṇḍalukaraḥ śuciḥ ।। brahmacaryarato nityaṃ vanavāsarato bhavet । mokṣaśāstreṣu nirato brahmasūtrī jitendriyaḥ ।।
dambhāhaṅkāranirmukto nindāpaiśunyavarjitaḥ । ātmajñānaguṇopeto yatirmokṣamavāpnuyāt ।। abhyaset satataṃ vedaṃ praṇavākhyaṃ sanātanam । snātvācamya vidhānena śucirdevālayādiṣu ।।
yajñopavītī śāntātmā kuśapāṇiḥ samāhitaḥ । dhautakāṣāyavasano bhasmacchannatanūrahaḥ ।। adhiyajñaṃ brahma japedādhidaivikameva ca । ādhyātmikaṃ ca satataṃ vedāntābhihitaṃ ca yat ।।
putreṣu vātha nivasan brahmacārī yatirmuniḥ । vedamevābhyasennityaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ tapaḥ param । kṣamā dayā ca satoṣo vratānyasya viśeṣataḥ ।।
vedāntajñānaniṣṭho vā pañca yajñān samāhitaḥ । kuryādaharahaḥ snātvā bhikṣānnenaiva tena hi ।। homamantrāñjapennityaṃ kāle kāle samāhitaḥ । svādhyāyaṃ cānvahaṃ kuryāt sāvitrīṃ saṃdhyayorjapet ।।
dhyāyīta satataṃ devamekānte parameśvaram । ekānnaṃ varjayennityaṃ kāmaṃ krodhaṃ parigraham ।। ekavāsā dvivāsā vā śikhī yajñopavītavān । kamaṇḍalukaro vidvān tridaṇḍī yāti tatparam ।।
evaṃ svāśramaniṣṭhānāṃ yatīnāṃ niyatātmanām । bhaikṣeṇa vartanaṃ proktaṃ phalamūlairathāpi vā ।। ekakālaṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ na prasajyeta vistare । bhaikṣe prasakto hi yatirviṣayeṣvapi sajjati ।।
saptāgāraṃ cared bhaikṣamalābhāt tu punaścaret । prakṣālya pātre bhuñjīyādadbhiḥ prakṣālayet tu tat ।। athavānyadupādāya pātre bhuñjīta nityaśaḥ । bhuktvā tat saṃtyajet pātraṃ yātrāmātramalolupaḥ ।।
vidhūme sannamusale vyaṅgāre bhuktavajjane । vṛtte śarāvasaṃpāte bhikṣāṃ nityaṃ yatiścaret ।। godohamātraṃ tiṣṭheta kālaṃ bhikṣuradhomukhaḥ । bhikṣetyuktvā sakṛt tūṣṇīmaśnīyād vāgyataḥ śuciḥ ।।
prakṣālya pāṇipādau ca samācamya yathāvidhi । āditye darśayitvānnaṃ bhuñjīta prāṅmukhottaraḥ ।। hutvā prāṇāhutīḥ pañca grāsānaṣṭau samāhitaḥ । ācamya devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ dhyāyīta parameśvaram ।।
alābuṃ dārupātraṃ ca mṛṇmayaṃ vaiṇavaṃ tataḥ । catvāri yatipātrāṇi manurāha prajāpatiḥ ।। prāgrātre pararātre ca madhyarātre tathaiva ca । saṃdhyāsvahni viśeṣeṇa cintayennityamīśvaram ।।
kṛtvā hṛtpadmanilaye viśvākhyaṃ viśvasaṃbhavam । ātmānaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ parastāt tamasaḥ sthitam ।। sarvasyādhārabhūtānāmānandaṃ jyotiravyayam । pradhānapuruṣātītamākāśaṃ dahanaṃ śivam ।।
tadantaḥ sarvabhāvānāmīśvaraṃ brahmarūpiṇam । dhyāyedanādimadvaitamānandādiguṇālayam ।। mahāntaṃ paramaṃ brahma puruṣaṃ satyamavyayam । sitetarāruṇākāraṃ maheśaṃ viśvarūpiṇam ।।
oṅkārānte atha cātmānaṃ saṃsthāpya paramātmani । ākāśe devamīśānaṃ dhyāyītākāśamadhyagam ।। kāraṇaṃ sarvabhāvānāmānandaikasamāśrayam । purāṇaṃ puruṣaṃ śaṃbhuṃ dhyāyan mucyeta bandhanāt ।।
yadvā guhāyāṃ prakṛtau jagatsaṃmohanālaye । vicintya paramaṃ vyoma sarvabhūtaikakāraṇam ।। jīvanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yatra lokaḥ pralīyate । ānandaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sūkṣmaṃ yat paśyanti mumukṣavaḥ ।।
tanmadhye nihitaṃ brahma kevalaṃ jñānalakṣaṇam । anantaṃ satyamīśānaṃ vicintyāsīta saṃyataḥ ।। guhyād guhyatamaṃ jñānaṃ yatīnāmetadīritam । yo anutiṣṭhenmaheśena so aśnute yogamaiśvaram ।।
tasmād dhyānarato nityamātmavidyāparāyaṇaḥ । jñānaṃ samabhyased brāhmaṃ yena mucyeta bandhanāt ।। matvā pṛthak svamātmānaṃ sarvasmādeva kevalam । ānandamajaraṃ jñānaṃ dhyāyīta ca punaḥ param ।।
yasmāt bhavanti bhūtāni yad gatvā neha jāyate । sa tasmādīśvaro devaḥ parasmād yo adhitiṣṭhati ।। yadantare tad gaganaṃ śāśvataṃ śivamavyayam । yadaṃśastatparo yastu sa devaḥ syānmaheśvaraḥ ।।
vratāni yāni bhikṣūṇāṃ tathaivopavratāni ca । ekaikātikrame teṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate ।। upetya ca striyaṃ kāmāt prāyaścittaṃ samāhitaḥ । prāṇāyāmasamāyuktaṃ kuryāt sāṃtapanaṃ śuciḥ ।।
tataścareta niyamāt kṛcchraṃ saṃyatamānasaḥ । punarāśramamāgamya cared bhiśruratandritaḥ ।। na dharmayuktamanṛtaṃ hinastīti manīṣiṇaḥ । tathāpi ca na kartavyaṃ prasaṅgo hyeṣa dāruṇaḥ ।।
ekarātropavāsaśca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā । uktvānṛtaṃ prakartavyaṃ yatinā dharmalipsunā ।। paramāpadgatenāpi na kāryaṃ steyamanyataḥ । steyādabhyadhikaḥ kaścinnāstyadharma iti smṛtiḥ ।
hiṃsā caiṣāparā diṣṭā yā cātmajñānanāśikā ।। yadetad draviṇaṃ nāma prāṇa hyete bahiśvarāḥ । sa tasya harati prāṇān yo yasya harate dhanam ।। evaṃ kṛtvā sa duṣṭātmā bhinnavṛtto vratāccyutaḥ ।
bhūyo nirvedamāpannaścareccāndrāyaṇavratam ।। vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena saṃvatsaramiti śrutiḥ । bhūyo nirvedamāpannaścared bhikṣuratandritaḥ ।। akasmādeva hiṃsāṃ tu yadi bhikṣuḥ samācaret ।
kuryātkṛchrātikṛcchraṃ tu cāndrāyaṇamathāpi vā ।। skandedindriyadaurbalyāt striyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yatiryadi । tena dhārayitavyā vai prāṇāyāmāstu ṣoḍaśa । divāskande trirātraṃ syāt prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā ।।
ekānne madhumāṃse ca navaśrāddhe tathaiva ca । pratyakṣalavaṇe coktaṃ prājāpatyaṃ viśodhanam ।। dhyānaniṣṭhasya satataṃ naśyate sarvapātakam । tasmānmaheśvaraṃ jñātvā tasya dhyānaparo bhavet ।।
yad brahma paramaṃ jyotiḥ pratiṣṭhākṣaramadvayam । yo antarātra paraṃ brahma sa vijñeyo maheśvaraḥ ।। eṣa devo mahādevaḥ kevalaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ । tadevākṣaramadvaitaṃ tadādityāntaraṃ param ।।
yasmānmahīyate devaḥ svadhāmni jñānasaṃjñite । ātmayogāhvaye tattve mahādevastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। nānyad devānmahādevād vyatiriktaṃ prapaśyati । tamevātmānamanveti yaḥ sa yāti paraṃ padam ।।
manyate ye svamātmānaṃ vibhinnaṃ parameśvarāt । na te paśyanti taṃ devaṃ vṛthā teṣāṃ pariśramaḥ ।। ekameva paraṃ brahma vijñeyaṃ tattvamavyayam । sa devastu mahādevo naitad vijñāya badhyate ।।
tasmād yateta niyataṃ yatiḥ saṃyatamānasaḥ । jñānayogarataḥ śānto mahādevaparāyaṇaḥ ।। eṣa vaḥ kathito vipro yatīnāmāśramaḥ śubhaḥ । pitāmahena vibhunā munīnāṃ pūrvamīritam ।।
nāputraśiṣyayogibhyo dadyādidamanuttamam । jñānaṃ svayaṃbhuvā proktaṃ yatidharmāśrayaṃ śivam ।। paśupatiparitoṣe yad bhavedekahetuḥ । praṇihitamanaso ye nityamevācaranti ।।
ataḥ paraṃ pravalakṣyāmi prāyaścittavidhiṃ śubham । hitāya sarvaviprāṇāṃ doṣāṇāmapanuttaye ।। akṛtvā vihitaṃ karma kṛtvā ninditameva ca । doṣamāpnoti puruṣaḥ prāyaścittaṃ viśodhanam ।।
prāyaścittamakṛtvā tu na tiṣṭhed brāhmaṇaḥ kvacit । yad brūyurbrāhmaṇāḥ śāntā vidvāṃsastatsamācaret ।। vedārthavittamaḥ śānto dharmakāmo agnimān dvijaḥ । sa eva syāt paro dharmo yameko api vyavasyati ।।
anāhitāgnayo viprāstrayo vedārthapāragāḥ । yad brūyurdharmakāmāste tajjñeyaṃ dharmasādhanam ।। anekadharmaśāstrajñā ūhāpohaviśāradāḥ । vedādhyayanasaṃpannāḥ saptaite parikīrtitāḥ ।।
mīmāṃsājñānatattvajñā vedāntakuśalā dvijāḥ । ekaviṃśatisaṃkhyātāḥ prayāścittaṃ vadanti vai ।। brahmahā madyapaḥ steno gurutalpaga eva ca । mahāpātakinastvete yaścaitaiḥ saha saṃvaset ।।
saṃvatsaraṃ tu patitaiḥ saṃsargaṃ kurute tu yaḥ । yānaśayyāsanairnityaṃ jānan vai patito bhavet ।। yājanaṃ yonisaṃbandhaṃ tathaivādhyāpanaṃ dvijaḥ । kṛtvā sadyaḥ patejjñānāt saha bhojanameva ca ।।
avijñāyātha yo mohāt kuryādadhyāpanaṃ dvijaḥ । saṃvatsareṇa patati sahādhyayanameva ca ।। brahmāhā dvādaśābdāni kuṭiṃ kṛtvā vane vaset । bhaikṣamātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ kṛtvā śavaśirodhvajam ।।
brāhmaṇāvasathān sarvān devāgārāṇi varjayet । vinindan svayamātmānaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ ca saṃsmaran ।। asaṃkalpitayogyāni saptāgārāṇi saṃviśet । vidhūme śanakairnityaṃ vyaṅgāre bhuktavajjane ।।
ekakālaṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ doṣaṃ vikhyāpayan nṛṇām । vanyamūlaphalairvāpi vartayed dhairyamākṣitaḥ ।। kapālapāṇiḥ khaṭvāṅgī brahmacaryaparāyaṇaḥ । pūrṇe tu dvādaśe varṣe brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।।
akāmataḥ kṛte pāpe prāyaścittamidaṃ śubham । kāmato maraṇācchuddhirjñeyā nānyena kenacit ।। kuryādanaśanaṃ vātha bhṛgoḥ patanameva vā । jvalantaṃ vā viśedagniṃ jalaṃ vā praviśet svayam ।।
brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā samyak prāṇān parityajet । brahmahatyāpanodārthamantarā vā mṛtasya tu ।। dīrghāmayānvitaṃ vipraṃ kṛtvānāmayameva tu । dattvā cānnaṃ sa durbhikṣe brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।।
aśvamedhāvabhṛthake snātvā vā śudhyate dvijaḥ । sarvasvaṃ vā vedavide brāhmaṇāya pradāya tu ।। sarasvatyāstvaruṇayā saṃgame lokaviśrute । śudhyet triṣavaṇasnānāt trirātropoṣito dvijaḥ ।।
gatvā rāmeśvaraṃ puṇyaṃ snātvā caiva mahodadhau । brahmacaryādibhiryukto dṛṣṭvā rudraṃ vimucyate ।। kapālamocanaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ devasya śūlinaḥ । snātvābhyarcya pitṝn bhaktyā brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।।
yatra devādidevena bharaveṇāmitaujasā । kapālaṃ sthāpitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। samabhyarcya mahādevaṃ tatra bhairavarūpiṇam । tarpapitvā pitṝn snātvā mucyate brahmahatyayā ।।
kathaṃ devena rudreṇa śaṅkareṇāmitaujasā । kapālaṃ brahmaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ sthāpitaṃ dehajaṃ bhuvi ।। śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ puṇyāṃ kathāṃ pāpapraṇāśanīm । māhātmyaṃ devadevasya mahādevasya dhīmataḥ ।।
purā pitāmahaṃ devaṃ meruśṛṅge maharṣayaḥ । procuḥ praṇamya lokādiṃ kimekaṃ tattvamavyayam ।। sa māyayā maheśasya mohito lokasaṃbhavaḥ । avijñāya paraṃ bhāvaṃ svātmānaṃ prāha dharṣiṇam ।।
ahaṃ dhātā jagadyoniḥ svayaṃbhūreka īśvaraḥ । anādimatparaṃ brahma māmabhyarcya vimucyate ।। ahaṃ hi sarvadevānāṃ pravartakanivartakaḥ । na vidyate cābhyadhiko matto lokeṣu kaścana ।।
tasyaivaṃ manyamānasya jajñe nārāyaṇāṃśajaḥ । provāca prahasan vākyaṃ roṣatāmravilocanaḥ ।। kiṃ kāraṇamidaṃ brahman vartate tava sāṃpratam । ajñānayogayuktasya na tvetaducitaṃ tava ।।
ahaṃ dhātā hi lokānāṃ yajño nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ । na māmṛte asya jagato jīvanaṃ sarvadā kvacit ।। ahameva paraṃ jyotirahameva parā gatiḥ । matpreritena bhavatā sṛṣṭaṃ bhuvanamaṇḍalam ।।
evaṃ vivadatormohāt parasparajayaiṣiṇoḥ । ājagmuryatra tau devau vedāścatvāra eva hi ।। anvīkṣya devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ yajñātmānaṃ ca saṃsthitam । procuḥ saṃvignahṛdayā yāthātmyaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
yasyāntaḥ sthāni bhūtāni yasmātsarvaṃ pravartate । yadāhustatparaṃ tattvaṃ sa devaḥ syānmaheśvaraḥ ।। yo yajñairakhilairīśo yogena ca samarcyate । yamāhurīśvaraṃ devaṃ sa devaḥ syāt pinākadhṛk ।।
yenedaṃ bhrāmyate cakraṃ yadākāśāntaraṃ śivam । yogibhirvidyate tattvaṃ mahādevaḥ sa śaṅkaraḥ ।। yaṃ prapaśyanti yogeśaṃ yatanto yatayaḥ param । maheśaṃ puruṣaṃ rudraṃ sa devo bhagavān bhavaḥ ।।
evaṃ sa bhagavān brahmā vedānāmīritaṃ śubham । śrutvāha prahasan vākyaṃ viśvātmāpi vimohitaḥ ।। kathaṃ tatparamaṃ brahma sarvasaṅgavivarjitam । ramate bhāryayā sārdhaṃ pramathaiścātigarvitaiḥ ।।
itirite atha bhagavān praṇavātmā sanātanaḥ । amūrto mūrtimān bhūtvā vacaḥ prāha pitāmaham ।। na hyeṣa bhagavān patnyā svātmano vyatiriktayā । kadācid ramate rudrastādṛśo hi maheśvaraḥ ।।
ayaṃ sa bhagavānīśaḥ svayañjyotiḥ sanātanaḥ । svānandabhūtā kathitā devī nāgantukā śivā ।। ityevamukte api tadā yajñamūrterajasya ca । nājñānamagamannāśamīśvarasyaiva māyayā ।।
tadantare mahājyotirviriñco viśvabhāvanaḥ । prāpaśyadadbhutaṃ divyaṃ pūrayan gaganāntaram ।। tanmadhyasaṃsthaṃ vimalaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tejasojjvalam । vyomamadhyagataṃ divyaṃ prādurāsīd dvijottamāḥ ।।
sa dṛṣṭvā vadanaṃ divyaṃ mūrdhni lokapitāmahaḥ । tena tanmaṇjalaṃ ghoramālokayadaninditam ।। prajajvālātikopena brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃ śiraḥ । kṣaṇādadṛśyata mahān puruṣo nīlalohitaḥ ।।
triśūlapiṅgalo devo nāgayajñopavītavān । taṃ prāha bhagavān brahmā śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam ।। jānāmi bhavataḥ pūrvaṃ lalāṭādeva śaṅkara । prādurbhāvaṃ maheśān māmeva śaraṇaṃ vraja ।।
śrutvā sagarvavacanaṃ padmayoneratheśvaraḥ । prāhiṇot puruṣaṃ kālaṃ bhairavaṃ lokadāhakam ।। sa kṛtvā sumahad yuddhaṃ brahmaṇā kālabhairavaḥ । cakarta tasya vadanaṃ viriñcasyātha pañcamam ।।
nikṛttavadano devo brahmā devena śaṃbhunā । mamāra ceśayogena jīvitaṃ prāpa viśvasṛk ।। athānupaśyad giriśaṃ maṇḍalāntarasaṃsthitam । samāsīnaṃ mahādevyā mahādevaṃ sanātanam ।।
bhujaṅgarājavalayaṃ candrāvayavabhūṣaṇam । koṭisūryapratīkāśaṃ jaṭājūṭavirājitam ।। śārdūlacarmavasanaṃ divyamālāsamanvitam । triśūlapāṇiṃ duṣprekṣyaṃ yoginaṃ bhūtibhūṣaṇam ।।
yamantarā yoganiṣṭhāḥ prapaśyanti hṛdīśvaram । tamādidevaṃ brahmāṇaṃ mahādevaṃ dadarśa ha ।। yasya sā paramā devī śaktirākāśasaṃsthitā । so anantaiśvaryayogātmā maheśo dṛśyate kila ।।
yasyāśeṣajagad bījaṃ vilayaṃ yāti mohanam । sakṛtpraṇāmamātreṇa sa rudraḥ khalu dṛśyate ।। yo atha nācāraniratān svabhaktāneva kevalam । vimocayati lokānāṃ nāyako dṛśyate kila ।।
yasya vedavidaḥ śāntā nirdvandvā brahmacāriṇaḥ । vidanti vimalaṃ rūpaṃ sa śaṃbhurdṛśyate kila ।। yasya brahmādayo devā ṛṣayo brahmavādinaḥ । arcayanti sadā liṅgaṃ viśveśaḥ khalu dṛśyate ।।
yasyāśeṣajagad bījaṃ vilayaṃ yāti mohanam । sakṛtpraṇāmamātreṇa sa rudraḥ khalu dṛśyate ।। vidyāsahāyo bhagavān yasyāsau maṇḍalāntaram । hiraṇyagarbhaputro asāvīśvaro dṛśyate kila ।।
yasyāśeṣajagatsūtirvijñānatanurīśvarī । na muñcati sadā pārśvaṃ śaṅkaro asāvadṛśyata ।। puṣpaṃ vā yadi vā patraṃ yatpādayugale jalam । dattvā tarati saṃsāraṃ rudro asau dṛśyate kila ।।
tatsannidhāne sakalaṃ niyacchati sanātanaḥ । kālaḥ kila sa yogātmā kālakālo hi dṛśyate ।। jīvanaṃ sarvalokānāṃ trilokasyaiva bhūṣaṇam । somaḥ sa dṛśyate devaḥ somo yasya vibhūṣaṇam ।।
devyā saha sadā sākṣād yasya yogaḥ svabhāvataḥ । gīyate paramā muktiḥ sa yogī dṛśyate kila ।। yogino yogatattvajñā viyogābhimukhāniśam । yogaṃ dhyāyanti devyāsau sa yogī dṛśyate kila ।।
so anuvīkṣya mahādevaṃ mahādevyā sanātanam । varāsane samāsīnamavāpa paramāṃ smṛtim ।। labdhvā māheśvarīṃ divyāṃ saṃsmṛtiṃ bhagavānajaḥ । toṣayāmāsa varadaṃ somaṃ somavibhūṣaṇam ।।
namo devāya mahate mahādevyai namo namaḥ । namaḥ śivāya śāntāya śivāyai śāntaye namaḥ ।। oṃ namo brahmaṇe tubhyaṃ vidyāyai te namo namaḥ । namo mūlaprakṛtaye maheśāya namo namaḥ ।।
namo vijñānadehāya cintāyai te namo namaḥ । namaste kālakālāya īśvarāyai namo namaḥ ।। namo namo astu rudrāya rudrāṇyai te namo namaḥ । namo namaste kāmāya māyāyai ca namo namaḥ ।।
niyantre sarvakāryāṇāṃ kṣobhikāyai namo namaḥ । namo astu te prakṛtaye namo nārāyaṇāya ca ।। yogādāyai namastubhyaṃ yogināṃ gurave namaḥ । namaḥ saṃsāranāśāya saṃsārotpattaye namaḥ ।।
nityānandāya vibhave namo astvānandamūrtaye । namaḥ kāryavihīnāya viśvaprakṛtaye namaḥ ।। oṅkāramūrtaye tubhyaṃ tadantaḥ saṃsthitāya ca । namaste vyomasaṃsthāya vyomaśaktyai namo namaḥ ।।
iti somāṣṭakeneśaṃ praṇanāma pitāmahaḥ । papāta daṇḍavad bhūmau gṛṇan vai śatarudriyam ।। atha devo mahādevaḥ praṇatārtiharo haraḥ । provācotthāpya hastābhyāṃ prato asmi tava sāṃpratam ।।
dattvāsau paramaṃ yogamaiśvaryamatulaṃ mahat । provācāgre sthitaṃ devaṃ nīlalohitamīśvaram ।। eṣa brahmāsya jagataḥ saṃpūjyaḥ prathamaḥ sutaḥ । ātmano rakṣaṇīyaste gururjyeṣṭhaḥ pitā tava ।।
ayaṃ purāṇapuruṣo na hantavyastvayānagha । svayogaiśvaryamāhātmyānmāmeva śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। ayaṃ ca yajño bhagavān sagarvo bhavatānagha । śāsitavyo viriñcasya dhāraṇīyaṃ śirastvayā ।।
brahmahatyāpanodārthaṃ vrataṃ lokāya darśayan । carasva satataṃ bhikṣāṃ saṃsthāpaya suradvijān ।। ityetaduktvā vacanaṃ bhagavān parameśvaraḥ । sthānaṃ svābhāvikaṃ divyaṃ yayau tatparamaṃ padam ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavānīśaḥ kaparde nīlalohitaḥ । grāhayāmāsa vadanaṃ brahmaṇaḥ kālabhairavam ।। cara tvaṃ pāpanāśārthaṃ vrataṃ lokahitāvaham । kapālahasto bhagavān bhikṣāṃ gṛhṇātu sarvataḥ ।।
uktvaivaṃ prāhiṇot kanyāṃ brahmahatyāmiti śrutām । daṃṣṭrākarālavadanāṃ jvālāmālāvibhūṣaṇām ।। yāvad vārāṇasīṃ divyāṃ purīmeṣa gamiṣyati । tāvat tvaṃ bhīṣaṇe kālamanugaccha trilocanam ।।
evamābhāṣya kālāgniṃ prāha devo maheśvaraḥ । aṭasva nikhilaṃ lokaṃ bhikṣārtho manniyogataḥ ।। yadā drakṣyasi deveśaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam । tadāsau vakṣyati spaṣṭamupāyaṃ pāpaśodhanam ।।
sa devadevatāvākyamākarṇya bhagavān haraḥ । kapālapāṇirviśvātmā cacāra bhuvanatrayam ।। āsthāya vikṛtaṃ veṣaṃ dīpyamānaṃ svatejasā । śrīmat pavitramatulaṃ jaṭājūṭavirājitam ।।
koṭisūryapratīkāśaiḥ pramathaiścātigarvitaiḥ । bhāti kālāgninayano mahādevaḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।। pītvā kadamṛtaṃ divyamānandaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ । līlāvilāsūbahulo lokānāgacchatīśvaraḥ ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā kālavadanaṃ śaṅkaraṃ kālabhairavam । rūpalāvaṇyasaṃpannaṃ nārīkulamagādanu ।। gāyanti vividhaṃ gītaṃ nṛtyanti purataḥ prabhoḥ । sasmitaṃ prekṣya vadanaṃ cakrurbhrūbhaṅgameva ca ।।
sa devadānavādīnāṃ deśānabhyetya śūladhṛk । jagāma viṣṇorbhavanaṃ yatrāste madhusūdanaḥ ।। nirīkṣya divyabhavanaṃ śaṅkaro lokaśaṅkaraḥ । sahaiva bhūtapravaraiḥ praveṣṭumupacakrame ।।
avijñāya paraṃ bhāvaṃ divyaṃ tatpārameśvaram । nyavārayat triśūlāṅkaṃ dvārapālo mahābalaḥ ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiḥ pītavāsā mahābhujaḥ । viṣvaksena iti khyāto viṣṇoraṃśasamudbhavaḥ ।।
athainaṃ śaṅkaragaṇo yuyudhe viṣṇusaṃbhavam । bhīṣaṇo bhairavādeśāt kālavega iti śrutaḥ ।। vijitya taṃ kālavegaṃ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ । rudrāyābhimukhaṃ raudraṃ cikṣepa ca sudarśanam ।।
atha devo mahādevastripurāristriśūlabhṛt । tamāpatantaṃ sāvajñamālokayadamitrajit ।। tadantare mahadbhūtaṃ yugāntadahanopamam । śūlenorasi nirbhidya pātayāmāsa taṃ bhuvi ।।
sa śūlābhihato atyarthaṃ tyaktvā svaṃ paramaṃ balam । tatyāja jīvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā mṛtyuṃ vyādhihatā iva ।। nihatya viṣṇupuruṣaṃ sārdhaṃ pramathapuṅgavaiḥ । viveśa cāntaragṛhaṃ samādāya kalevaram ।।
nirīkṣya jagato hetumīśvaraṃ bhagavān hariḥ । śiro lalāṭāt saṃbhidya raktadhārāmapātayat ।। gṛhāṇa bhagavan bhikṣāṃ madīyāmamitadyute । na vidyate anābhyuditā tava tripuramardana ।।
na saṃpūrṇaṃ kapālaṃ tad brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ । divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu sā ca dhārā pravāhitā ।। athābravīt kālarudraṃ harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ । saṃstūya vaidikairmantrairbahumānapuraḥ saram ।।
kimarthametad vadanaṃ brahmaṇo bhavatā dhṛtam । provāca vṛttamakhilaṃ bhagavān parameśvaraḥ ।। samāhūya hṛṣīkeśo brahmahatyāmathācyutaḥ । prārthayāmāsa deveśo vimuñceti triśūlinam ।।
na tatyājātha sā pārśvaṃ vyāhṛtāpi murāriṇā । ciraṃ dhyātvā jagadyoniḥ śaṅkaraṃ prāha sarvavit ।। vrajasva bhagavan divyāṃ purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ śubhām । yatrākhilajagaddoṣaṃ kṣipraṃ nāśayatāśvaraḥ ।।
tataḥ śarvāṇi guhyāni tīrthānyāyatanāni ca । jagāma līlayā devo lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। saṃstūyamānaḥ pramathairmahāyogairitastataḥ । nṛtyamāno mahāyogī hastanyastakalevaraḥ ।।
tamabhyadhāvad bhagavān harirnārāyaṇaḥ svayam । athāsthāyāparaṃ rūpaṃ nṛtyadarśanalālasaḥ ।। nirīkṣamāṇo novindaṃ vṛṣendrāṅkitaśāsanaḥ । sasmito anantayogātmā nṛtyati sma punaḥ punaḥ ।।
atha sānucaro rudraḥ saharirdharmavāhanaḥ । bheje mahādevapurīṃ vārāṇasīmiti śrutām ।। praviṣṭamātre deveśe brahmahatyā kapardini । hā hetyuktvā sanādaṃ sā pātālaṃ prāpa duḥ khitā ।।
praviśya paramaṃ sthānaṃ kapālaṃ brahmaṇo haraḥ । gaṇānāmagrato devaḥ sthāpayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ ।। sthāpayitvā mahādevo dadau tacca kalevaram । uktvā sajīvamastvīśo viṣṇave sa ghṛṇānidhiḥ ।।
ye smaranti mamājastraṃ kāpālaṃ veṣamuttamam । teṣāṃ vinaśyati kṣipramihāmutra ca pātakam ।। āgamya tīrthapravare snānaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ । tarpayitvā pitṝn devān mucyate brahmahatyayā ।।
aśāśvataṃ jagajjñātvā ye asmin sthāne vasanti vai । dehānte tat paraṃ jñānaṃ dadāmi paramaṃ padam ।। itīdamuktvā bhagavān samāliṅgya janārdanam । sahaiva pramatheśānaiḥ kṣaṇādantaradhīyata ।।
sa labdhvā bhagavān kṛṣṇo viṣvaksenaṃ triśūlinaḥ । svaṃ deśamagat tūrṇaṃ gṛhītvāṃ paramaṃ vapuḥ ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam । kapālamocanaṃ tīrthaṃ sthāṇoḥ priyakaraṃ śubham ।।
ya imaṃ paṭhate adhyāyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ samīpataḥ । vācikairmānasaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikaiśca vimucyate ।। surāpastu surāṃ taptāmagnivarṇāṃ svayaṃ pibet । tayā sa kāye nirdagdhe mucyate tu dvijottamaḥ ।।
gomūtramagnivarṇaṃ vā gośakṛdrasameva vā । payo ghṛtaṃ jalaṃ vātha mucyate pātakāt tataḥ ।। jalārdravāsāḥ prayato dhyātvā nārāyaṇaṃ harim । brahmahatyāvrataṃ cātha caret tatpāpaśāntaye ।।
suvarṇasteyakṛd vipro rājānamabhigamya tu । svakarma khyāpayan brūyānmāṃ bhavānanuśāstviti ।। gṛhītvā musalaṃ rājā sakṛd hanyāt tataḥ svayam । vadhe tu śuddhyate steno brāhmaṇastapasaiva vā ।।
skandhenādāya musalaṃ lakuṭaṃ vāpi khādiram । śaktiṃ cobhayatastīkṣṇāmāyasaṃ daṇḍameva vā ।। rājā tena ca gantavyo muktakeśena dhāvatā । ācakṣāṇena tatpāpamevaṅkarmāsmi śādhi mām ।।
śāsanād vā vimokṣād vā stenaḥ steyād vimucyate । aśāsitvā tu taṃ rājāstenasyāpnoti kilbiṣam ।। tapasāpanunutsustu suvarṇasteyajaṃ malam । cīravāsā dvijo araṇye cared brahmahaṇo vratam ।।
snātvāśvamedhāvabhṛthe pūtaḥ syādathavā dvijaḥ । pradadyād vātha viprebhyaḥ svātmatulyaṃ hiraṇyakam ।। cared vā vatsaraṃ kṛcchraṃ brahmacaryaparāyaṇaḥ । brāhmaṇaḥ svarṇahārī tu tatpāpasyāpanuttaye ।।
gurorbhāryāṃ samāruhya brāhmaṇaḥ kāmamohitaḥ । avagūhet striyaṃ taptāṃ dīptāṃ kārṣṇāyasīṃ kṛtām ।। svayaṃ vā śiśnavṛṣaṇāvutkṛtyādhāya cāñcalau । ātiṣṭhed dakṣiṇāmāśāmānipātādajihmagaḥ ।।
gurvarthaṃ vā hataḥ śuddhyeccared vā brahmahā vratam । śākhāṃ vā kaṇṭakopetāṃ pariṣvajyātha vatsaram । adhaḥ śayīta niyato mucyate gurutalpagaḥ ।। kṛcchraṃ vābdaṃ cared vipraścīravāsāḥ samāhitaḥ ।
aśvamedhāvabhṛthake snātvā vā śuddhyate naraḥ ।। kāle aṣṭame vā bhuñjāno brahmacārī sadāvratī । sthānāsanābhyāṃ viharaṃstrirahno abhyupayannapaḥ ।। adhaḥ śāyī tribhirvarṣaistad vyapohati pātakam ।
cāndrāyaṇāni vā kuryāt pañca catvāri vā punaḥ ।। patitaiḥ saṃprayuktānāmatha vakṣyāmi niṣkṛtim । patitena tu saṃsargaṃ yo yena kurute dvijaḥ । sa tatpāpāpanodārthaṃ tasyaiva vratamācaret ।।
taptakṛcchraṃ cared vātha saṃvatsaramatandritaḥ । ṣāṇmāsike tu saṃsarge prāyaścittārdhamarhati ।। ebhirvratairapohanti mahāpātakino malam । puṇyatīrthābhigamanāt pṛthivyāṃ vātha niṣkṛtiḥ ।।
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ steyaṃ gurvaṅganāgamaḥ । kṛtvā taiścāpi saṃsargaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ kāmakārataḥ ।। kuryādanaśanaṃ vipraḥ puṇyatīrthe samāhitaḥ । jvalantaṃ vā viśedagniṃ dhyātvā devaṃ kapardinam ।।
na hyanyā niṣkṛtirdṛṣṭā munibhirdharmavādibhiḥ । tasmāt puṇyeṣu tīrtheṣu dahed vāpi svadehakam ।। gatvā duhitaraṃ vipraḥ svasāraṃ vā snuṣāmapi । praviśejjvalanaṃ dīptaṃ matipūrvamiti sthitiḥ ।।
mātṛṣvasāṃ mātulānīṃ tathaiva ca pitṛṣvasām । bhāgineyīṃ samāruhya kuryāt kṛcchrātikṛcchrakau ।। cāndrāyaṇaṃ ca kurvota tasya pāpasya śāntaye । dhyāyan devaṃ jagadyonimanādinidhanaṃ param ।।
bhrātṛbhāryāṃ samāruhya kuryāt tatpāpaśāntaye । cāndrāyaṇāni catvāri pañca vā susamāhitaḥ ।। paitṛṣvastreyīṃ gatvā tu svastreyāṃ mātureva ca । mātulasya sutāṃ vāpi gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ।।
sakhibhāryāṃ samāruhya gatvā śyālīṃ tathaiva ca । ahorātroṣito bhūtvā taptakṛcchraṃ samācaret ।। udakyāgamane viprastrirātreṇa viśudhyati । cāṇḍālīgamane caiva taptakṛcchratrayaṃ viduḥ ।
saha sāṃtapanenāsya nānyathā niṣkṛtiḥ smṛtā ।। mātṛgotrāṃ samāsādya samānapravarāṃ tathā । cādrāyaṇena śudhyeta prayatātmā samāhitaḥ ।। brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇīṃ gatvā gṛcchramekaṃ samācaret ।
kanyakāṃ dūṣayitvā tu careccāndrāyaṇavratam ।। amānuṣīṣu puruṣa udakyāyāmayoniṣu । retaḥ siktvā jale caiva kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret ।। bandhakīgamane viprastrirātreṇa viśuddhyati ।
gavi bhathunamāsevya careccāndrāyaṇavratam ।। ajāvī maithunaṃ kṛtvā prājāpatyaṃ cared dvijaḥ । patitāṃ ca striyaṃ gatvā tribhiḥ kṛcchrai rviśuddhyati ।। pulkasīgamane caiva kracchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ।
naṭīṃ śailūṣakīṃ caiva rajakīṃ veṇujīvinīm । gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ kuryāt tathā carmopajīvinīm ।। brahāmacārī striyaṃ gacchet kathañcitkāmamohitaḥ । saptagāraṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ vasitvā gardabhājinam ।।
upaspṛśet triṣavaṇaṃ svapāpaṃ parikīrtayan । saṃvatsareṇa caikena tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate ।। brahmahatyāvrataṃ vāpi ṣaṇmāsānācared yamī । mucyate hyavakīrṇo tu brāhmaṇānumate sthitaḥ ।।
saptarātramakṛtvā tu bhaikṣacaryāgnipūjanam । retasaśca samutsarge prāyaścittaṃ samācaret ।। oṅkārapūrvikābhistu mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ sadā । saṃvatsaraṃ tu bhuñjāno naktaṃ bhikṣāśanaḥ śuciḥ ।।
sāvitrīṃ ca japeccaiva nityaṃ krodhavivarjitaḥ । nadītīreṣu tīrtheṣu tasmāt pāpād vimucyate ।। hatvā tu kṣatriyaṃ vipraḥ kuryād brahmahaṇo vratam । akāmato vai ṣaṇmāsān dadyān pañcaśataṃ gavām ।।
abdaṃ careta niyato vanavāsī samāhitaḥ । prājāpatyaṃ sāntapanaṃ taptakṛcchraṃ tu vā svayam ।। pramāpyākāmato vaiśyaṃ kuryāt saṃvatsaradvayam । gosahasraṃ sapādaṃ ca dadyād brahmahaṇo vratam ।
kṛcchrātikṛcchrau vā kuryāccāndrāyaṇamathāvi vā ।। saṃvatsaraṃ vrataṃ kuryācchūdraṃ hatvā pramādataḥ । gosahasrārdhapādaṃ ca dadyāt tatpāpaśāntaye ।। aṣṭau varṣāṇi ṣaṭ trīṇi kuryād brahmahaṇo vratam ।
hatvā tu kṣatriyaṃ vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ caiva yathākramam ।। nihatya brāhmaṇīṃ viprastvaṣṭavarṣaṃ vrataṃ caret । rājanyāṃ varṣaṣaṭkaṃ tu vaiśyāṃ saṃvatsaratrayam । vatsareṇa viśuddhyeta śūdrāṃ hatvā dvijottamaḥ ।।
vaiśyāṃ hatvā pramādena kiñcid dadyād dvijātaye । antyajānāṃ vadhe caiva kuryāccāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam । parākeṇāthavā śuddhirityāha bhagavānajaḥ ।। maṇḍūkaṃ nakulaṃ kākaṃ dandaśūkaṃ ca mūṣikam ।
śvānaṃ hatvā dvijaḥ kuryāt ṣoḍaśāṃśaṃ vrataṃ tataḥ ।। payaḥ pibet trirātraṃ tu śvānaṃ hatvā suyantritaḥ । mārjāraṃ vātha nakulaṃ yojanaṃ vādhvano vrajet । kṛcchraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ tu kuryādaśvavadhe dvijaḥ ।।
abhrīṃ kārṣṇāyasīṃ dadyāt sarpaṃ hatvā dvijottamaḥ । palālabhāraṃ ṣaṇḍaṃ ca saisakaṃ caikamāṣakam ।। dhṛtakumbhaṃ varāhaṃ ca tiladroṇaṃ ca tittirim । śukaṃ dvihāyanaṃ vatsaṃ krauñcaṃ hatvā trihāyanam ।।
hatvā haṃsaṃ balākāṃ ca bakaṃ barhiṇameva ca । vānaraṃ śyenabhāsau ca sparśayed brāhmaṇāya gām ।। kravyādāṃstu mṛgān hatvā dhenuṃ dadyāt payasvinīm । akravyādān vatsatarīmuṣṭraṃ hatvā tu kṛṣṇalam ।।
kiñcideva tu viprāya dadyādasthimatāṃ vadhe । anasthnāṃ caiva hiṃsāyāṃ prāṇāyāmena śudhyati ।। phaladānāṃ tu vṛkṣāṇāṃ chedane japyamṛkśatam । gulmavallīlatānāṃ tu puṣpitānāṃ ca vīrudhām ।।
anyeṣāṃ caiva vṛkṣāṇāṃ sarasānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ । phalapuṣpodbhavānāṃ ca ghṛtaprāśo viśodhanam ।। hastināṃ ca vadhe dṛṣṭaṃ taptakṛcchraṃ viśodhanam । cāndrāyaṇaṃ parākaṃ vā gāṃ hatvā tu pramādataḥ ।
matipūrvaṃ vadhe cāsyāḥ prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate ।। manuṣyāṇāṃ tu haraṇaṃ kṛtvā strīṇāṃ gṛhasya ca । vāpīkūpajalānāṃ ca śudhyeccāndrāyaṇena tu ।। dravyāṇāmalpasārāṇāṃ steyaṃ kṛtvānyaveśmataḥ ।
caret sāṃtapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ tanniryātyātmaśuddhaye ।। dhānyānnadhanacauryaṃ tu kṛtvā kāmād dvijottamaḥ । svajātīyagṛhādeva kṛcchrārdhena viśuddhyati ।। bhakṣabhojyāpaharaṇe yānaśayyāsanasya ca ।
puṣpamūlaphalānāṃ ca pañcagavyaṃ viśodhanam ।। tṛṇakāṣṭhadrumāṇāṃ ca śuṣkānnasya guḍasya ca । cailacarmāmiṣāṇāṃ ca trirātraṃ syādabhojanam ।। maṇimuktāpravālānāṃ tāmrasya rajatasya ca ।
ayaḥ kāṃsyopalānāṃ ca dvādaśāhaṃ kaṇāśanam ।। kārpāsakīṭajorṇānāṃ dviśaphaikaśaphasya ca । pakṣigandhauṣadhīnāṃ ca rajvāścaiva tryahaṃ payaḥ ।। naramāṃsāśanaṃ kṛtvā cāndrāyaṇamathācaret ।
kākaṃ caiva tathā śvānaṃ jagdhvā hastinameva ca । varāhaṃ kukkuṭaṃ cātha taptakṛcchreṇa śudhyati ।। kravyādānāṃ ca māṃsāni purīṣaṃ mūtrameva ca । gogomāyukapīnāṃ ca tadeva vratamācaret ।
upoṣya dvādaśāhaṃ tu kūṣmāṇḍairjuhuyād ghṛtam ।। nakulolūkamārjāraṃ jagdhvā sāṃtapanaṃ caret । śvāpadoṣṭrakharāñjagdhvā taptakṛcchreṇa śuddhyati । vratavaccaiva saṃskāraṃ pūrveṇa vidhinaiva tu ।।
bakaṃ caiva balākaṃ ca haṃsaṃ kāraṇḍavaṃ tathā । cakravākaṃ plavaṃ jagghvā dvādaśāhamabhojanam ।। kapotaṃ ṭiṭṭibhaṃ caiva śukaṃ sārasameva ca । ulūkaṃ jālapādaṃ ca jagdhvāpyetad vrataṃ caret ।।
śiśumāraṃ tathā cāṣaṃ matsyamāṃsaṃ tathaiva ca । jagdhvā caiva kaṭāhārametadeva cared vratam ।। kokilaṃ caiva matsyāṃśca maṇḍukaṃ bhujagaṃ tathā । gomūtrayāvakāhāro māsenaikena śuddhyati ।।
jalecarāṃśca jalajān prattudānnakhaviṣkirān । raktapādāṃstathā jagdhvā saptāhaṃ caitadācaret ।। śuno māṃsaṃ śuṣkamāṃsamātmārthaṃ ca tathā kṛtam । bhuktvā māsaṃ caredetat tatpāpasyāpanuttaye ।।
vārtākaṃ bhustṛṇaṃ śigruṃ khukhuṇḍaṃ karakaṃ tathā । prājāpatyaṃ carejjagdhvā śaṅkhaṃ kumbhīkameva ca ।। palāṇḍuṃ laśunaṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret । nālikāṃ taṇḍulīyaṃ ca prājāpatyena śuddhyati ।।
aśmāntakaṃ tathā potaṃ taptakṛcchreṇa śuddhyati । prājāpatyena śuddhiḥ syāt kakkubhāṇḍasya bhakṣaṇe ।। alābuṃ kiṃśukaṃ caiva bhuktvā caitad vrataṃ caret । udumbaraṃ ca kāmena taptakṛcchreṇa śuddhyati ।।
vṛthā kṛsarasaṃyāvaṃ pāyasāpūpasaṃkulam । bhuktvā caivaṃ vidhaṃ tvannaṃ trirātreṇa viśuddhyati ।। pītvā kṣīrāṇyapeyāni brahmacārī samāhitaḥ । gomūtrayāvakāhāro māsenaikena śuddhyati ।।
anirdaśāhaṃ gokṣīraṃ māhiṣaṃ cājameva ca । saṃdhinyāśca vivatsāyāḥ piban kṣīramidaṃ caret ।। eteṣāṃ ca vikārāṇi pītvā mohena mānavaḥ । gomūtrayāvakāhāraḥ saptarātreṇa śuddhyati ।।
bhuktvā caiva navaśrāddhe mṛtake sūtake tathā । cāndrāyaṇena śuddhyeta brāhmaṇastu samāhitaḥ ।। yasyāgnau hūyate nityaṃ na yasyāgraṃ na dīyate । cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret samyak tasyānnaprāśane dvijaḥ ।।
abhojyānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ bhuktvā cānnamupaskṛtam । antāvasāyināṃ caiva taptakṛcchreṇa śuddhyati ।। cāṇḍālānnaṃ dvijo bhuktvā samyak cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret । buddhipūrvaṃ tu kṛcchrābdaṃ punaḥ saṃskārameva ca ।।
asurāmadyapānena kuryāccāndrāyaṇavratam । abhojyānnaṃ tu bhuktvā ca prājāpatyena śuddhyati ।। viṇmūtrapāśanaṃ kṛtvā retasaścaitadācaret । anādiṣṭeṣu caikāhaṃ sarvatra tu yathārthataḥ ।।
viḍvarāhakharoṣṭrāṇāṃ gomāyoḥ kapikākayoḥ । prāśya mūtrapurīṣāṇi dvijaścāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ।। ajñānāt prāśya viṇmūtraṃ surāsaṃspṛṣṭameva ca । punaḥ saṃskāramarhanti trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ ।।
kravyādāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ caiva prāśya mūtrapurīṣakam । mahāsāṃtapanaṃ mohāt tathā kuryād dvijottamaḥ । bhāsamaṇḍūkakurare viṣkire kṛcchramācaret ।। prājāpatyena śuddhyeta brāhāmaṇocchiṣṭabhojane ।
kṣatriye taptakṛcchraṃ syād vaiśye caivātikṛcchrakam । śūdrocchiṣṭaṃ dvijo bhuktvā kuryāccāndrāyaṇavratam ।। surābhāṇḍodare vāri pītvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret । śunocchiṣṭaṃ dvijo bhuktvā trirātreṇa viśuddhyati ।
gomūtrayāvakāhāraḥ pītaśeṣaṃ ca rāgavān ।। apo mūtrapurīṣādyairdūṣitāḥ prāśayed yadā । tadā sāṃtapanaṃ proktaṃ vrataṃ pāpaviśodhanam ।। cāṇḍālakūpabhāṇḍeṣu yadi jñānāt pibejjalam ।
caret sāṃtapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ brāhmaṇaḥ pāpaśodhanam ।। cāṇḍālena tu saṃspṛṣṭaṃ pītvā vāri dvijottamaḥ । trirātreṇa viśuddhyeta pañcagavyena caiva hi ।। mahāpātakisaṃsparśe bhuṅkte asnātvā dvijo yadi ।
buddhipūrvaṃ tu mūḍhātmā taptakṛcchraṃ samācaret ।। spṛṣṭvā mahāpātakinaṃ cāṇḍālaṃ vā rajasvalām । pramādād bhojanaṃ kṛtvā trirātreṇa viśuddhyati ।। snānārhe yadi bhuñjīta ahorātreṇa śuddhyati ।
buddhipūrvaṃ tu kṛcchreṇa bhagavānāha padmajaḥ ।। śuṣkaparyuṣitādīni gavādipratidūṣitam । bhuktvopavāsaṃ kurvota kṛcchrapādamathāpi vā ।। saṃvatsarānte kṛcchraṃ tu cared vipraḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
ajñātabhuktaśuddhyarthaṃ jñātasya tu viśeṣataḥ ।। vrātyānāṃ yajanaṃ kṛtvā pareṣāmantyakarma ca । abhicāramahīnaṃ ca tribhiḥ kṛcchrairviśuddhyati ।। brāhmaṇādihatānāṃ tu kṛtvā dāhādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।
gomūtrayāvakāhāraḥ prājāpatyena śuddhyati ।। tailābhyakto athavā kuryād yadi mūtrapurīṣake । ahorātreṇa śuddhyeta śmaśrukarma ca maithunam ।। ekāhena vivāhāgniṃ parihārya dvijottamaḥ ।
trirātreṇa viśaddhyeta trirātrāt ṣaḍahaṃ punaḥ ।। daśāhaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā parihārya pramādataḥ । kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ kuryāt tatpāpasyāpanuttaye ।। patitād dravyamādāya tadutsargeṇa śuddhyati ।
caret sāṃtapanaṃ kṛcchramityāha bhagavān prabhuḥ ।। anāśakanivṛttāstu pravrajyāvasitāstathā । careyustrīṇi kṛcchrāṇi trīṇi cāndrāyaṇāni ca ।। punaśca jātakarmādisaṃkāraiḥ saṃskṛtā dvijāḥ ।
śuddhyeyustad vrataṃ samyak careyurdharmavardhanāḥ ।। anupāsitasaṃdhyastu tadaharyāpako vaset । anaśnan saṃyatamanā rātrau ced rātrimeva hi ।। akṛtvā samidādhānaṃ śuciḥ snātvā samāhitaḥ ।
gāyatryaṣṭasahasrasya japyaṃ kuryād viśuddhaye ।। upāsīta na cet saṃdhyāṃ gṛhastho api pramādataḥ । snātvā viśuddhyate sadyaḥ pariśrāntastu saṃyamāt ।। vedoditāni nityāni karmāṇi ca vilopya tu ।
snātakavratalopaṃ tu kṛtvā copavased dinam ।। saṃvatsaraṃ caret kṛcchramagnyutsādī dvijottamaḥ । cāndrāyaṇaṃ cared vrātyo gopradānena śuddhyati ।। nāstikyaṃ yadi kurvota prājāpatyaṃ cared dvijaḥ ।
devadrohaṃ gurudrohaṃ taptakṛcchreṇa śuddhyati ।। uṣṭrayānaṃ samāruhya kharayānaṃ ca kāmataḥ । trirātreṇa viśuddhyet tu nagno vā praviśejjalam ।। ṣaṣṭhānnakālatāmāsaṃ saṃhitājapa eva ca ।
homāśca śākalā nityamapāṅktānāṃ viśodhanam ।। nīlaṃ raktaṃ vasitvā ca brāhmaṇo vastrameva hi । ahorātroṣitaḥ snātaḥ pañcagavyena śuddhyati ।। vedadharmapurāṇānāṃ caṇḍālasya tu bhāṣaṇe ।
cāndrāyaṇena śuddhiḥ syānna hyanyā tasya niṣkṛtiḥ ।। udbandhanādinihataṃ saṃspṛśya brāhmaṇaḥ kvacit । cāndrāyaṇena śuddhiḥ syāt prājāpatyena vā punaḥ ।। ucchiṣṭo yadyanācāntaścāṇḍālādīn spṛśed dvijaḥ ।
pramādād vai japet snātvā gāyatryaṣṭasahasrakam ।। drupadānāṃ śataṃ vāpi brahmacārī samāhitaḥ । trirātropoṣitaḥ samyak pañcagavyena śuddhyati ।। caṇḍālapatitādīṃstu kāmād yaḥ saṃspṛśed dvijaḥ ।
ucchiṣṭastatra kurvota prājāpatyaṃ viśuddhaye ।। cāṇḍālasūtakaśavāṃstathā nārīṃ rajasvalām । spṛṣṭvā snāyād viśuddhyarthaṃ tatspṛṣṭaṃ patitiṃ tathā ।। cāṇḍālasūtakaśavaiḥ saṃspṛṣṭaṃ saṃspṛśed yadi ।
pramādāt tata ācamya japaṃ kuryāt samāhitaḥ ।। tat spṛṣṭasparśinaṃ spṛṣṭvā buddhipūrvaṃ dvijottamaḥ । ācamet tad viśuddhyarthaṃ prāha devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। bhuñjānasya tu viprasya kadācit saṃstraved gudam ।
kṛtvā śaucaṃ tataḥ snāyādupoṣya juhuyād ghṛtam ।। cāṇḍālāntyaśavaṃ spṛṣṭvā kṛcchraṃ kuryād viśuddhaye । spṛṣṭvābhyaktastvasaṃspṛśyamahorātreṇa śuddhyati ।। surāṃ spṛṣṭvā dvijaḥ kuryāt prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ śuciḥ ।
palāṇḍuṃ laśunaṃ caiva ghṛtaṃ prāśya tataḥ śuciḥ ।। brāhmaṇastu śunā daṣṭastryahaṃ sāyaṃ payaḥ pibet । nābherūrdhvaṃ tu daṣṭasya tadeva dviguṇaṃ bhavet ।। syādetat triguṇaṃ bāhvormūrdhni ca syāccaturguṇam ।
snātvā japed vā sāvitrīṃ śvabhirdaṣṭo dvijottamaḥ ।। anirvartya mahāyajñān yo bhuṅkte tu dvijottamaḥ । anāturaḥ sati dhane kṛcchrārdhena sa śuddhyati ।। āhitāgnirupasthānaṃ na kuryād yastu parvaṇi ।
ṛtau na gacched bhāryāṃ vā so api kṛcchrārdhamācaret ।। vinādbhirapsu nāpyārtaḥ śarīraṃ sanniveśya ca । sacailo jalamāplutya gāmālabhya viśuddhyati ।। buddhipūrvaṃ tvabhyudito japedantarjale dvijaḥ ।
gāyatryaṣṭasahasraṃ tu tryahaṃ copavased vratī ।। anugamyecchayā śūdraṃ pretībhūtaṃ dvijottamaḥ । gāyatryaṣṭasahasraṃ ca japyaṃ kuryānnadīṣu ca ।। kṛtvā tu śapathaṃ vipro viprasya vadhasaṃyutam ।
mṛṣaiva yāvakānnena kuryāccāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam ।। paṅktyāṃ viṣamadānaṃ tu kṛtvā kṛcchreṇa śuddhyati । chāyāṃ śvapākasyāruhya snātvā saṃprāśayed ghṛtam ।। īkṣedādityamaśucirdṛṣṭvāgniṃ candrameva vā ।
mānuṣaṃ cāsthi saṃspṛśya snānaṃ kṛtvā viśuddhyati ।। kṛtvā tu mithyādhyayanaṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ tu vatsaram । kṛtaghno brāhmaṇagṛhe pañca saṃvatsaraṃ vratī ।। huṅkāraṃ brāhmaṇasyoktvā tvaṅkāraṃ ca garīyasaḥ ।
snātvānaśnannahaḥ śeṣaṃ praṇipatya prasādayet ।। tāḍayitvā tṛṇenāpi kaṇṭhaṃ baddhvāpi vāsasā । vivāde vāpi nirjitya praṇipatya prasādayet ।। avagūrya caret kṛcchramatikṛcchraṃ nipātane ।
kṛcchrātikṛcchrau kurvota viprasyotpādya śoṇitam ।। gurorākrośamanṛtaṃ kṛtvā kuryād viśodhanam । ekarātraṃ trirātraṃ vā tatpāpasyāpanuttaye ।। devarṣoṇāmabhimukhaṃ ṣṭhīvanākrośane kṛte ।
ulmukena dahejjihvāṃ dātavyaṃ ca hiraṇyakam ।। devodyāne tu yaḥ kuryānmūtroccāraṃ sakṛd dvijaḥ । chindyācchiśnaṃ tu śuddhyarthaṃ careccāndrāyaṇaṃ tu vā ।। devatāyatane mūtraṃ kṛtvā mohād dvijottamaḥ ।
śiśnasyotkartanaṃ kṛtvā cāndrāyaṇamathācaret ।। devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca devānāṃ caiva kutsanam । kṛtvā samyak prakurvota prājāpatyaṃ dvijottamaḥ ।। taistu saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā snātvā devān samarcayet ।
dṛṣṭvā vīkṣeta bhāsvantaṃ smvatvā viśeśvaraṃ smaret ।। yaḥ sarvabhūtādhipatiṃ viśveśānaṃ vinindati । na tasya niṣkṛtiḥ śakyā kartuṃ varṣaśatairapi ।। cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret pūrvaṃ kṛcchraṃ caivātikṛcchrakam ।
prapannaḥ śaraṇaṃ devaṃ tasmāt pāpād vimucyate ।। sarvasvadānaṃ vidhivat sarvapāpaviśodhanam । cāndrāyaṇaṃ cavidhinā kṛcchraṃ caivātikṛcchrakam ।। puṇyakṣetrābhigamanaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam ।
devatābhyarcanaṃ nṝṇāmaśeṣāghavināśanam ।। amāvasyāṃ tithiṃ prāpya yaḥ samārādhayecchivam । brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ mahādevaṃ tathā kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm ।
saṃpūjya brāhmaṇamukhe sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। trayodaśyāṃ tathā rātrau sopahāraṃ trilocanam । dṛṣṭveśaṃ prathame yāme mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।। upoṣitaścaturdaśyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe samāhitaḥ ।
yamāca dharmarājāya mṛtyave cāntakāya ca ।। vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhūtakṣayāya ca । pratyekaṃ tilasaṃyuktān dadyāt saptodakāñjalīn । snātvā nadyāṃ tu pūrvāhne mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।।
brahmacaryamadhaḥ śayyāmupavāsaṃ dvijārcanam । vrateṣveteṣu kurvota śāntaḥ saṃyatamānasaḥ ।। amāvasyāyāṃ brahmāṇaṃ samuddiśya pitāmaham । brāhmaṇāṃstrīn samabhyarcya mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।।
ṣaṣṭhyāmupoṣito devaṃ śuklapakṣe samāhitaḥ । saptamyāmarcayed bhānuṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।। bharaṇyāṃ ca caturthyāṃ ca śanaiścaradine yamam । pūjayet saptajanmotthairmucyate pātakairnaraḥ ।।
ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāraḥ samabhyarcya janārdanam । dvādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣasya mahāpāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। tapo japastīrthasevā devabrāhmaṇapūjanam । grahaṇādiṣu kāleṣu mahāpātakaśodhanam ।।
yaḥ sarvapāpayukto api puṇyatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ । niyamena tyajet prāṇān sa mucyet sarvapātakaiḥ ।। brahmaghnaṃ vā kṛtaghnaṃ vā mahāpātakadūṣitam । bhartāramuddharennārī praviṣṭā saha pāvakam ।।
etadeva paraṃ strīṇāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidurbudhāḥ । sarvapāpasamudbhūtau nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। pativratā tu yā nārī bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇotsukā । na tasyā vidyate pāpamiha loke paratra ca ।।
pativratā dharmaratā rudrāṇyeva na saṃśayaḥ । nāsyāḥ parābhavaṃ kartuṃ śaknotīha janaḥ kvacit ।। yathā rāmasya subhagā sītā trailokyaviśrutā । patnī dāśaratherdevī vijigye rākṣaseśvaram ।।
rāmasya bhāryāṃ vimalāṃ rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ । sītāṃ viśālanayanāṃ cakame kālacoditaḥ ।। gṛhītvā māyayā veṣaṃ carantīṃ vijane vane । samāhartuṃ matiṃ cakre tāpasaḥ kila kāminīm ।।
vijñāya sā ca tadbhāvaṃ smṛtvā dāśarathiṃ patim । jagāma śaraṇaṃ vahnimāvasathyaṃ śucismitā ।। upatasthe mahāyogaṃ sarvadoṣavināśanam । kṛtāñjalī rāmapatnī śākṣāt patimivācyutam ।।
namasyāmi mahāyogaṃ kṛtāntaṃ gahanaṃ param । dāhakaṃ sarvabhūtānāmīśānaṃ kālarūpiṇam ।। namasye pāvakaṃ devaṃ sākṣiṇaṃ viśvatomukham । ātmānaṃ dīptavapuṣaṃ sarvabhūtahṛdī sthitam ।।
prapadye śaraṇaṃ vahniṃ brahmaṇyaṃ brahmarūpiṇam । bhūteśaṃ kṛttivasanaṃ śaraṇyaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। oṃ prapadye jaganmūrtiṃ prabhavaṃ sarvatejasām । mahāyogeśvaraṃ vahnimādityaṃ parameṣṭhinam ।।
prapadye śaraṇaṃ rudraṃ mahāgrāsaṃ triśūlinam । kālāgniṃ yogināmīśaṃ bhogamokṣaphalapradam ।। prapadye tvāṃ virūpākṣaṃ bhurbhuvaḥ svaḥ svarūpiṇam । hiraṇyamaye gṛhe guptaṃ mahāntamamitaujasam ।।
vaiśvānaraṃ prapadye ahaṃ sarvabhūteṣvavasthitam । havyakavyavahaṃ devaṃ prapadye vahnimīśvaram ।। prapadye tatparaṃ tattvaṃ vareṇyaṃ savituḥ svayam । bhargamagniparaṃ jyotī rakṣa māṃ havyavāhana ।।
iti vahnyaṣṭakaṃ japtvā rāmapatnī yaśasvinī । dhyāyantī manasā tasthau rāmamunmīlitekṣaṇā ।। athāvasathyād bhagavān havyavāho maheśvaraḥ । āvirāsīt sudīptātmā tejasā pradahanniva ।।
svaṣṭvā māyāmayīṃ sītāṃ sa rāvaṇavadhepsayā । sītāmādāya dharmiṣṭhāṃ pāvako antaradhīyata ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tādṛśīṃ sītāṃ rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ । samādāya yayau laṅkāṃ sāgarāntarasaṃsthitām ।।
kṛtvātha rāvaṇavadhaṃ rāmo lakṣmaṇasaṃyutaḥ । masādāyābhavat sītāṃ śaṅkākulitamānasaḥ ।। sā pratyayāya bhūtānāṃ sītā māyāmīya punaḥ । viveśa pāvakaṃ dīptaṃ dadāha jvalano api tām ।।
dagdhvā māyāmayīṃ sītāṃ bhagavānugradīdhitiḥ । rāmāyādarśayat sītāṃ pāvako abhūt surapriyaḥ ।। pragṛhya bhartuścaraṇau karābhyāṃ sā sumadhyamā । cakāra praṇatiṃ bhūmau rāmāya janakātmajā ।।
dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭamanā rāmo vismayākulalocanaḥ । nanāma vahniṃ sirasā toṣayāmāsa rāghavaḥ ।। uvāca vahnerbhagavān kimeṣā varavarṇinī । dagdhā bhagavatā pūrvaṃ dṛṣṭā matpārśvamāgatā ।।
