tamāha devo lokānāṃ dāhako havyavāhanaḥ । yathāvṛttaṃ dāśarathiṃ bhūtānāmeva sannidhau ।। iyaṃ sā mithileśena pārvatīṃ rudravallabhām । ārādhya labdhā tapasā devyāścātyantavallabhā ।।
bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇopetā suśīleyaṃ pativratā । bhavānīpārśvamānītā mayā rāvaṇakāmitā ।। yā nītā rākṣaseśena sītā bhagavatāhṛtā । mayā māyāmayī sṛṣṭā rāvaṇasya vadhāya sā ।।
tadarthaṃ bhavatā duṣṭo rāvaṇo rākṣaseśvaraḥ । mayopasaṃhṛtā caiva hato lokavināśanaḥ ।। gṛhāṇa vimalāmenāṃ jānakīṃ vacanānmama । paśya nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ svātmānaṃ prabhavāvyayam ।।
ityuktvā bhagavāṃścaṇḍo viścārcirviśvatomukhaḥ । mānito rāghaveṇāgnirbhūtaiścāntaradhīyata ।। etate pativratānāṃ vaiṃ māhātmyaṃ kathitaṃ mayā । strīṇāṃ sarvāghaśamanaṃ prāyaścittamidaṃ smṛtam ।।
aśeṣapāpayuktastu puruṣo api susaṃyataḥ । svadehaṃ puṇyatīrtheṣu tyaktvā mucyeta kilbiṣāt ।। pṛthivyāṃ sarvatīrtheṣu snātvā puṇyeṣu vā dvijaḥ । mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ samastairapi pūruṣaḥ ।।
ityeṣa mānavo dharmo yuṣmākaṃ kathito mayā । maheśārādhanārthāya jñānayogaṃ ca śāśvatam ।। yo anena vidhinā yuktaṃ jñānayogaṃ samācaret । sa paśyati mahādevaṃ nānyaḥ kalpaśatairapi ।।
sthāpayed yaḥ paraṃ dharmaṃ jñānaṃ tatpārameśvaram । na tasmādadhiko loke sa yogī paramo mataḥ ।। ya saṃsthāpayituṃ śakto na kuryānmohito janaḥ । sa yogayukto api munirnātyarthaṃ bhagavatpriyaḥ ।।
tasmāt sadaiva dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ । dharmayukteṣu śānteṣu śraddhayā cānviteṣu vai ।। yaḥ paṭhed bhavatāṃ nityaṃ saṃvādaṃ mama caiva hi । sarvapāpavinirmukto gaccheta paramāṃ gatim ।।
śrāddhe vā daivike kārye brāhmaṇānāṃ ca sannidhau । paṭheta nityaṃ sumanāḥ śrotavyaṃ ca dvijātibhiḥ ।। yor'thaṃ vicārya yuktātmā śrāvayed brāhmaṇān śucīn । sa doṣakañcukaṃ tyaktvā yāti devaṃ maheśvaram ।।
etāvaduktvā bhagavān vyāsaḥ satyavatīsutaḥ । samāśvāsya munīn sūtaṃ jagāma ca yathāgatam ।। tīrthāni yāni loke asmin viśrutāni māhanti ca । tāni tvaṃ kathayāsmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa sāṃpratam ।।
śṛṇudhvaṃ kathayiṣye ahaṃ tīrthāni vividhāni ca । kathitāni purāṇeṣu munibhirbrahmavādibhiḥ ।। yatra snānaṃ japo homaḥ śrāddhadānādikaṃ kṛtam । ekaikaśo muniśreṣṭhāḥ punātyāsaptamaṃ kulam ।।
pañcayojanavistīrṇaṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ । prayāgaṃ prathitaṃ tīrthaṃ tasya māhātmyamīritam ।। anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ kurūṇāṃ devavanditam । ṛṣīṇāmāśramairjuṣṭaṃ sarvapāpaviśodhanam ।।
tatra snātvā viśuddhātmā dambhamātsaryavarjitaḥ । dadāti yatkiñcidapi punātyubhayataḥ kulam ।। gayātīrthaṃ paraṃ guhyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ cāti vallabham । kṛtvā piṇḍapradānaṃ tu na bhūyo jāyate naraḥ ।।
sakṛd gayābhigamanaṃ kṛtvā piṇḍaṃ dadāti yaḥ । tāritāḥ pitarastena yāsyanti paramāṃ gatim ।। tatra lokahitārthāya rudreṇa paramātmanā । śilātale padaṃ nyastaṃ tatra pitṝn prasādayet ।।
gayābhigamanaṃ kartuṃ yaḥ śakto nābhigacchati । śocanti pitarastaṃ vai vṛthā tasya pariśramaḥ ।। gāyanti pitaro gāthāḥ kīrtayanti maharṣayaḥ । gayāṃyāsyatiyaḥ kaścit so asmān saṃtārayiṣyati ।।
yadi syāt pātakopetaḥ svadharmarativarjitaḥ । gayāṃ yāsyati vaṃśyo yaḥ so asmān saṃtārayiṣyati ।। eṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrāḥ śīlavanto guṇānvitāḥ । teṣāṃ tu samavetānāṃ yadyeko api gayāṃ vrajet ।।
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena brāhmaṇastu viśeṣataḥ । pradadyād vidhivat piṇḍān gayāṃ gatvā samāhitaḥ ।। dhanyāstu khalu te martyā gayāyāṃ piṇḍadāyinaḥ । kulānyubhayataḥ sapta samuddhṛtyāpnuyāt param ।।
anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ siddhāvāsamudāhṛtam । prabhāsamiti vikhyātaṃ yatrāste bhagavān bhavaḥ ।। tatra snānaṃ tapaḥ śrāddhaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca pūjanam । kṛtvā lokamavāpnoti brahmaṇo akṣayyamuttamam ।।
tīrthaṃ traiyambakaṃ nāma sarvadevanamaskṛtam । pūjayitvā tatra rudraṃ jyotiṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet ।। suvarṇākṣaṃ mahādevaṃ samabhyarcya kapardinam । brāhmaṇān pūjayitvā tu gāṇapatyaṃ labhed dhruvam ।।
someśvaraṃ tīrthavaraṃ rudrasya parameṣṭhinaḥ । sarvavyādhiharaṃ puṇyaṃ rudrasālokyakāraṇam ।। tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ vijayaṃ nāma śobhanam । tatra liṅgaṃ maheśasya vijayaṃ nāma viśrutam ।।
ṣaṇmāsān niyatāhāro brahmacārī samāhitaḥ । uṣitvā tatra viprendrā yāsyanti paramaṃ padam ।। anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ pūrvadeśe suśobhanam । ekāmraṃ devadevasya gāṇapatyaphalapradam ।।
dattvātra śivabhaktānāṃ kiñcicchaśvanmahīṃ śubhām । sārvabhaumo bhaved rājā mumukṣurmokṣamāpnuyāt ।। mahānadījalaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam । grahaṇe samupaspṛśya mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।।
anyā ca virajā nāma nadī trailokyaviśrutā । tasyāṃ snātvā naro viprā brahmaloke mahīyate ।। tīrthaṃ nārāyaṇasyānyannāmnā tu puruṣottamam । tatra nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmānāste paramapūruṣaḥ ।।
pūjayitvā paraṃ viṣṇuṃ snātvā tatra dvijottamaḥ । brāhmaṇān pūjayitvā tu viṣṇulokamavāpnuyāt ।। tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ gokarṇaṃ nāma viśrutam । sarvapāpaharaṃ śaṃbhornivāsaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā liṃṅgaṃ tu devasya gokarṇeśvaramuttamam । īpsitāṃllabhate kāmān rudrasya dayito bhavet ।। uttaraṃ cāpi gokarṇaṃ liṅgaṃ devasya śūlinaḥ । mahādevasyārcayitvā śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।
tatra devo mahādevaḥ sthāṇurityabhiviśrutaḥ । taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate tatkṣaṇānnaraḥ ।। anyat kubjāmramatulaṃ sthānaṃ viṣṇormahātmanaḥ । saṃpūjya puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ śvetadvīpe mahīyate ।।
yatra nārāyaṇo devo rudreṇa tripurāriṇā । kṛtvā yajñasya mathanaṃ dakṣasya tu visarjitaḥ ।। samantād yojanaṃ kṣetraṃ siddharṣigaṇavanditam । puṇyamāyatanaṃ viṣṇostatrāste puruṣottamaḥ ।।
anyat kokāmukhaṃ viṣṇostīrthamadbhutakarmaṇaḥ । mṛto atra pātakairmukto viṣṇusārūpyamāpnuyāt ।। śālagrāmaṃ mahātīrthaṃ viṣṇoḥ prītivivardhanam । prāṇāṃstatra narastyaktvā hṛṣīkeṣaṃ prapaśyati ।।
aśvatīrthamiti khyātaṃ siddhāvāsaṃ supāvanam । āste hayaśirā nityaṃ tatra nārāyaṇaḥ svayam ।। tīrthaṃ trailokyavikhyātaṃ brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ । puṣkaraṃ sarvapāpaghnaṃ mṛtānāṃ brahmalokadam ।।
manasā saṃsmared yastu puṣkaraṃ vai dvijottamaḥ । pūyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ śakreṇa saha modate ।। tatra devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ । upāsate siddhasaṅghā brahmaṇaṃ padmasaṃbhavam ।।
tatra strātvā bhavecchuddho brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinam । pūjayitvā dvijavarān brahmāṇaṃ saṃprapaṣyati ।। tatrābhigamya deveśaṃ puruhūtamaninditam । surūpo jāyate martyaḥ sarvān kāmānavāpnuyāt ।।
saptasārasvataṃ tīrthaṃ brahmādyaiḥ sevitaṃ param । pūjayitvā tatra rudramaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। yatra maṅkaṇako rudraṃ prapannaḥ parameśvaram । ārādhayāmāsa haraṃ pañcakṣaraparāyaṇaḥ ।।
namaḥ śivāyeti muniḥ japan pañcākṣaraṃ param । ārādhayāmāsa śivaṃ tapasā govṛṣadhvajam ।। prajajvālātha tapasā munirmaṅkaṇakastadā । nanarta harṣavegena jñātvā rudraṃ samāgatam ।।
taṃ prāha bhagavān rudraḥ kimarthaṃ nartitaṃ tvayā । dṛṣṭvāpi devamīśānaṃ nṛtyati sma punaḥ punaḥ ।। so anvīkṣya bhagavānīśaḥ sagarvaṃ garvaśāntaye । svakaṃ dehaṃ vidāryāsmai bhasmarāśimadarśayat ।।
paśyemaṃ maccharīrotthaṃ bhasmarāśiṃ dvijottama । māhātmyametat tapasastvādṛśo anyo api vidyate ।। yat sagarvaṃ hi bhavatā nartitaṃ munipuṅgava । na yuktaṃ tāpasasyaitat tvattopyatrādhiko hyaham ।।
ityābhāṣya muniśreṣṭhaṃ sa rudraḥ kila viśvadṛk । āsthāya paramaṃ bhāvaṃ nanarta jagato haraḥ ।। sahasraśīrṣā bhūtvā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt । daṃṣṭrākarālavadano jvālāmālī bhayaṅkaraḥ ।।
so anvapaśyadaśeṣasya pārśve tasya triśūlinaḥ । viśālalocanamekāṃ devīṃ cāruvilāsinīm । sūryāyutasamaprakhyāṃ prasannavadanāṃ śivām ।। sasmitaṃ prekṣya viśveśaṃ tiṣṭhantīmamitadyutim ।
dṛṣṭvā saṃtrastahṛdayo vepamāno munīśvaraḥ । nanāma śirasā rudraṃ rudrādhyāyaṃ japan vaśī ।। prasanno bhagavānīśastryambako bhaktavatsalaḥ । pūrvaveṣaṃ sa jagrāha devī cāntarhitābhavat ।।
āliṅgya bhaktaṃ praṇataṃ devadevaḥ svayaṃśivaḥ । na bhetavyaṃ tvayā vatsa prāha kiṃ te dadāmyaham ।। praṇamya mūrdhnā giriśaṃ haraṃ tripurasūdanam । vijñāpayāmāsa tadā hṛṣṭaḥ praṣṭumanā muniḥ ।।
namo astu te mahādeva maheśvara namo astu te । kimetad bhagavadrūpaṃ sughoraṃ viśvatomukham ।। kā ca sā bhagavatpārśve rājamānā vyavasthitā । antarhiteva sahasā sarvamicchāmi veditum ।।
ityukte vyājahāramaṃ tathā maṅkaṇakaṃ haraḥ । maheśaḥ svātmano yogaṃ devīṃ ca tripurānalaḥ ।। ahaṃ sahasranayanaḥ sarvātmā sarvatomukhaḥ । dāhakaḥ sarvapāpānāṃ kālaḥ kālakaro haraḥ ।।
mayaiva preryate kṛtsnaṃ cetanācetanātmakam । so antaryāmī sa puruṣo hyahaṃ vai puruṣottamaḥ ।। tasya sā paramā māyā prakṛtistriguṇātmikā । procyate munirbhiśaktirjagadyoniḥ sanātanī ।।
sa eṣa māyayā viśvaṃ vyāmohayati viśvavit । nārāyaṇaḥ paro avyakto māyārūpa iti śrutiḥ ।। evametajjagat sarvaṃ sarvadā sthāpayāmyaham । yojayāmi prakṛtyāhaṃ puruṣaṃ pañcaviṃśakam ।।
tathā vai saṃgato devaḥ kūṭasthaḥ sarvago amalaḥ । sṛjatyaśeṣamevedaṃ svamūrteḥ prakṛterajaḥ ।। sa devo bhagavān brahmā viśvarūpaḥ pitāmahaḥ । tavaitat kathitaṃ samyak straṣṭvatvaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।।
eko ahaṃ bhagavān kalo hyanādiścāntakṛd vibhuḥ । samāsthāya paraṃ bhāvaṃ prokto rudro manīṣibhiḥ ।। mama vai sāparā śaktirdevī vidyeti viśrutā । dṛṣṭā hi bhavatā nūnaṃ vidyādehastvahaṃ tataḥ ।।
evametāni tattvāni pradhānapuruṣeśvarāḥ । viṣṇurbrahmā ca bhagavān rudraḥ kāla iti śrutiḥ ।। trayametadanādyantaṃ brahmaṇyeva vyavasthitam । tadātmakaṃ tadavyaktaṃ tadakṣaramiti śrutiḥ ।।
ātmānandaparaṃ tattvaṃ cinmātraṃ paramaṃ padam । ākāśaṃ niṣkalaṃ brahma tasmādanyanna vidyate ।। evaṃ vijñāya bhavatā bhaktiyogāśrayeṇa tu । saṃpūjyo vandanīyo ahaṃ tatastaṃ paśya śāśvatam ।।
etāvaduktvā bhagavāñjagāmādarśanaṃ haraḥ । tatraiva bhaktiyogena rudrāmārādhayanmuniḥ ।। etat pavitramatulaṃ tīrthaṃ brahmarṣisevitam । saṃsevya brāhmaṇo vidvān mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।।
anyat pavitraṃ vipulaṃ tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam । rudrakoṭiriti khyātaṃ rudrasya parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। purā puṇyatame kāle devadarśanatatparāḥ । koṭibrahmarṣayo dāntāstaṃ deśamagaman param ।।
ahaṃ drakṣyāmi giriśaṃ pūrvameva pinākinam । anyo anyaṃ bhaktiyuktānāṃ vyāghāto jāyate kila ।। teṣāṃ bhaktiṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā giriśo yogināṃ guruḥ । koṭirūpo abhavad rudro rudrakoṭistataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
te sma sarve mahādevaṃ haraṃ giriguhāśayam । paśyantaḥ pārvatīnāthaṃ hṛṣṭapuṣṭadhiyo abhavan ।। anādyantaṃ mahādevaṃ pūrvamevāhamīśvaram । dṛṣṭavāniti bhaktyā te rudranyastadhiyo abhavan ।।
athāntarikṣe vimalaṃ paśyanti sma mahattaram । jyotistatraiva te sarve abhilaṣantaḥ paraṃ padam ।। etat sadeśādhyuṣitaṃ tīrthaṃ puṇyatamaṃ śubham । dṛṣṭvā rudraṃ samabhyarcya rudrasāmīpyamāpnuyāt ।।
anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ nāmnā madhuvanaṃ smṛtam । tatra gatvā niyamavānindrasyārdhāsanaṃ labhet ।। athānyatpuṣpanagarī deśaḥ puṇyatamaḥ śubhaḥ । tatra gatvā pitṝn pūjya kulānāṃ tārayecchatam ।।
kālañjaraṃ mahātīrthaṃ loke rudro maheśvaraḥ । kālaṃ jaritavān devo yatra bhaktipriyo haraḥ ।। śveto nāma śive bhakto rājarṣipravaraḥ purā । tadāśīstannamaskāraḥ pūjayāmāsa śūlinam ।।
saṃsthāpya vidhinā liṅgaṃ bhaktiyogapuraḥ saraḥ । jajāpa rudramaniśaṃ tatra saṃnyastamānasaḥ ।। sa taṃ kālo atha dīptātmā śūlamādāya bhīṣaṇam । netumabhyāgato deśaṃ sa rājā yatra tiṣṭhati ।।
vīkṣya rājā bhayāviṣṭaḥ śūlahastaṃ samāgatam । kālaṃ kālakaraṃ ghoraṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ caṇḍadīdhitim ।। ubābhyāmatha hastābhyāṃ spṛṭvāsau liṅgamaiśvaram । nanāma śirasā rudraṃ jajāpa śatarudriyam ।।
japantamāha rājānaṃ namantamasakṛd bhavam । ehyehīti puraḥ sthitvā kṛtāntaḥ prahasanniva ।। tamuvāca bhayāviṣṭo rājā rudraparāyaṇaḥ । ekamīśārcanarataṃ vihāyānyaṃ niṣūdaya ।।
ityuktavantaṃ bhagavānabravīd bhītamānasam । rudrārcanarato vānyo madvaśe ko na tiṣṭhati ।। evamuktvā sa rājānaṃ kālo lokaprakālanaḥ । babandha pāśai rājāpi jajāpa śatarudriyam ।।
tejorāśiṃ bhūtabhartuḥ purāṇam । prādurbhūtaṃ saṃsthitaṃ saṃdadarśa ।। devyā devaṃ candralekhojjvalāṅgam । mene cāsmannātha āgacchatīti ।।
kālo rudraṃ devadevyā maheśam । rājarṣistaṃ netumabhyājagāma ।। devo rudro bhūtabhartā purāṇaḥ । dehītīmaṃ kālamūce mameti ।।
kālātmāsau manyamānaḥ svabhāvam । kruddho rudramabhidudrāva vegāt ।। so anvīkṣyānte viśvamāyāvidhijñaḥ । śvetasyainaṃ paśyato vyājaghāna ।।
mamāra so atibhīṣaṇo maheśapādaghātitaḥ । rarāja devatāpatiḥ sahomayā pinākadhṛk ।। nirīkṣya devamīśvaraṃ prahṛṣṭamānaso haram । nanāma sāmbamavyayaṃ sa rājapuṅgavastadā ।।
namo bhavāya hetave harāya viśvasaṃbhave । namaḥ śivāya dhīmate namo apavargadāyine ।। namo namo namo astu te mahāvibhūtaye namaḥ । vibhāgahīnarūpiṇe namo narādhipāya te ।।
namo astu te gaṇeśvara prapannaduḥ khanāśana । anādinityabhūtaye varāhaśṛṅgadhāriṇe ।। namo vṛṣadhvajāya te kapālamāline namaḥ । namo mahānaṭāya te namo vṛṣadhvajāya te ।।
athānugṛhya śaṅkaraḥ praṇāmatatparaṃ nṛpam । svagāṇapatyamavyayaṃ sarūpatāmatho dadau ।। sahomayā sapārṣadaḥ sarājapuṅgavo haraḥ । munīśasiddhavanditaḥ kṣaṇādadṛśyatāmagāt ।।
kāle maheśābhihate lokanāthaḥ pitāmahaḥ । ayācata varaṃ rudraṃ sajīvo ayaṃ bhavatviti ।। nāsti kaścidapīśāna doṣaleśo vṛṣadhvaja । kṛtāntasyaiva bhavatā tatkārye viniyojitaḥ ।।
sa devadevavacanād devadeveśvaro haraḥ । tathāstvityāha viśvātmā so api tādṛgvidho abhavat ।। ityetat paramaṃ tīrthaṃ kālañjaramiti śrutam । gatvābhyarcya mahādevaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ sa vindati ।।
idanamanyate paraṃ sthānaṃ guhyād guhyatamaṃ mahat । mahādevasya devasya mahālayamiti śrutam ।। tatra devādidevena rudreṇa tripurāriṇā । śilātale padaṃ nyastaṃ nāstikānāṃ nidarśanam ।।
tatra puśupatāḥ śāntā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ । upāsate mahādevaṃ vedādhyayanatatparāḥ ।। snātvā tatra padaṃ śārvaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhaktipuraḥ saram । namaskṛtvātha śirasā rudrasāmīpyamāpnuyāt ।।
anyacca devadevasya sthānaṃ śaṃbhormahātmanaḥ । kedāramiti vikhyātaṃ siddhānāmālayaṃ śubham ।। tatra snātvā mahādevamabhyarcya vṛṣaketanam । pītvā caivodakaṃ śuddhaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।।
śrāddhadānādikaṃ kṛtvā hyakṣyaṃ labhate phalam । dvijātipravarairjuṣṭaṃ yogibhiryatamānasaiḥ ।। tīrthaṃ plakṣāvataraṇaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam । tatrābhyarcya śrīnivāsaṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।।
anyaṃ magadharājasya tīrthaṃ svargagatipradam । akṣayaṃ vindati svargaṃ tatra gatvā dvijottamaḥ ।। tīrthaṃ kanakhalaṃ puṇyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam । yatra devena rudreṇa yajño dakṣasya nāśitaḥ ।।
tatra gaṅgāmupaspṛśya śucirbhāvasamanvitaḥ । mucyate sarvapāpaistu brahmalokaṃ labhenmṛtaḥ ।। mahātīrthamiti khyātaṃ puṇyaṃ nārāyaṇapriyam । tatrābhyarcya hṛṣīkeśaṃ śvetadvīpaṃ nigacchati ।।
anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ nāmnā śrīparvataṃ śubham । tatra prāṇān parityajya rudrasya dayito bhavet ।। tatra sannihito rudro devyā saha maheśvaraḥ । snānapiṇḍādikaṃ tatra kṛtamakṣayyamuttamam ।।
godāvarī nadī puṇyā sarvapāpavināśanī । tatra snātvā pitṝn devāṃstarpayitvā yathāvidhi । sarvapāpavisuddhātmā gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।। pavitrasalilā puṇyā kāverī vipulā nadī ।
tasyāṃ snātvodakaṃ kṛtvā mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ । trirātropoṣitenātha ekarātroṣitena vā ।। dvijātīnāṃ tu kathitaṃ tīrthānāmiha sevanam । yasya vāṅmanaso śuddhe hastapādau ca saṃsthitau ।
alolupo brahmacāro tīrthānāṃ phalamāpnuyāt ।। svāmitīrthaṃ mahātīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam । tatra sannihito nityaṃ skando amaranamaskṛtaḥ ।। snātvā kumāradhārāyāṃ kṛtvā devāditarpaṇam ।
ārādhya ṣaṇmukhaṃ devaṃ skandena saha modate ।। nadī trailokyavikhyātā tāmraparṇoti nāmataḥ । tatra snātvā pitṝn bhaktyā tarpayitvā yathāvidhi । pāpakartṝnapi pitṝstārayennātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
candratīrthamiti khyātaṃ kāveryāḥ prabhave akṣayam । tīrthaṃ tatra bhaved vastuṃ mṛtānāṃ svargatirdhruvā ।। vindhyapāde prapaśyanti devadevaṃ sadāśivam । bhaktyā ye te na paśyanti yamasya sadanaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
devikāyāṃ vṛṣo nāma tīrthaṃ siddhaniṣevitam । tatra snātvodakaṃ datvā yogasiddhiṃ ca vindati ।। daśāśvamedhikaṃ tīrthaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam । daśānāmaśvamedhānāṃ tatrāpnoti phalaṃ naraḥ ।।
puṇḍarīkaṃ mahātīrthaṃ brāhmaṇairupasevitam । tatrābhigamya yuktātmā pauṇḍarīkaphalaṃ labhet ।। tīrthebhyaḥ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ brahmatīrthamiti śrutam । brahmāṇamarcayitvā tu brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
sarasvatyā vinaśanaṃ plakṣaprastravaṇaṃ śubham । vyāsatīrthaṃ paraṃ tīrthaṃ mainākaṃ ca nagottamam । yamunāprabhavaṃ caiva sarvapāpaviśodhanam ।। pitṝṇāṃ duhitā devī gandhakālīti viśrutā ।
tasyāṃ snātvā divaṃ yāti mṛto jātismaro bhavet ।। kuberatuṅgaṃ pāpaghnaṃ siddhacāraṇasevitam । prāṇāṃstatra parityajya kuberānucaro bhavet ।। umātuṅgamiti khyātaṃ yatra sā rudravallabhā ।
tatrābhyarcya mahādevīṃ kosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।। bhṛgutuṅge tapastaptaṃ śrāddhaṃ dānaṃ tathā kṛtam । kulānyubhayataḥ sapta punātīti śrutirmama ।। kāśyapasya mahātīrthaṃ kālasarpiriti śrutam ।
tatra śrāddhāni deyāni nityaṃ pāpakṣayecchayā ।। daśārṇāyāṃ tathā dānaṃ śrāddhaṃ homastathā japaḥ । akṣayaṃ cāvyayaṃ caiva kṛtaṃ bhavati sarvadā ।। tīrthaṃ dvijātibhirjuṣṭaṃ nāmnā vai kurujāṅgalam ।
dattvā tu dānaṃ vidhivad brahmaloke mahīyate ।। vaitaraṇyāṃ mahātīrthe svarṇavedyāṃ tathaiva ca । dharmapṛṣṭhe ca sarasi brahmaṇaḥ parame śubhe ।। bharatasyāśrame puṇye puṇye śrāddhavaṭe śubhe ।
mahāhrade ca kauśikyāṃ dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ।। muñjapṛṣṭhe padaṃ nyastaṃ mahādevena dhīmatā । hitāya sarvabhūtānāṃ nāstikānāṃ nidarśanam ।। alpenāpi tu kālena naro dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।
pāpmānamutsṛjatyāśu jīrṇāṃ tvacamivoragaḥ ।। nāmnā kanakanandeti tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam । udīcyāṃ muñjapṛṣṭhasya brahmarṣigaṇasevitam ।। tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti saśarīrā dvijātayaḥ ।
dattaṃ cāpi sadā śrāddhamakṣayaṃ samudāhṛtam । ṛṇaistribhirnaraḥ snātvā mucyate kṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ ।। mānase sarasi snātvā śakrasyārdhāsanaṃ labhet । uttaraṃ mānasaṃ gatvā siddhiṃ prāpnotyanuttamām ।।
tasmānnirvartayecchrāddhaṃ yathāśakti yathābalam । kāmān salabhate divyān mokṣopāyaṃ ca vindati ।। parvato himavānnāma nānādhātuvibhūṣitaḥ । yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi so aśītistvāyato giriḥ ।
siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇo devarṣigaṇasevitaḥ ।। tatra puṣkariṇī ramyā suṣumnā nāma nāmataḥ । tatra gatvā dvijo vidvān brahmahatyāṃ vimuñcati ।। śrāddhaṃ bhavati cākṣayyaṃ tatra dattaṃ mahodayam ।
tārayecca pitṝn samyag daśa pūrvān daśāparān ।। sarvatra himavān puṇyo gaṅgā puṇyā samantataḥ । nadyaḥ samudragāḥ puṇyāḥ samudraśca viśeṣataḥ ।। badaryāśramamāsādya mucyate kalikalmaṣāt ।
tatra nārāyaṇo devo nareṇāste sanātanaḥ ।। akṣayaṃ tatra dānaṃ syāt japyaṃ vāpi tathāvidham । mahādevapriyaṃ tīrthaṃ pāvanaṃ tad viśeṣataḥ । tārayecca pitṝn sarvān dattvā śrāddhaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।
devadāruvanaṃ puṇyaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam । mahādevena devena tatra dattaṃ mahad varaṃ ।। mohayitvā munīn sarvān punastaiḥ saṃprapūjitaḥ । prasanno bhagavānīśo munīndrān prāha bhāvitān ।।
ihāśramavare ramye nivasiṣyatha sarvadā । madbhāvanāsamāyuktāstataḥ siddhimavāpsyatha ।। ye atra māmarcayantīha loke dharmaparā janāḥ । teṣāṃ dadāmi paramaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ hi śāśvatam ।।
atra nityaṃ vasiṣyāmi saha nārāyaṇena ca । prāṇāniha narastyaktvā na bhūyo janma vindati ।। saṃsmaranti ca ye tīrthaṃ deśāntaragatā janāḥ । teṣāṃ ca sarvapāpāni nāśayāmi dvijottamāḥ ।।
śrāddhaṃ dānaṃ tapo homaḥ piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ tathā । dhyānaṃ japaśca niyamaḥ sarvamatrākṣayaṃ kṛtam ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena draṣṭavyaṃ hi dvijātibhiḥ । devadāruvanaṃ puṇyaṃ mahādevaniṣevitam ।।
yatresvaro mahādevo viṣṇurvā puruṣottamaḥ । tatra sannihitā gaṅgātīrthānyāyatanāni ca ।। kathaṃ dāruvanaṃ prāpto bhagavān govṛṣadhvajaḥ । mohayāmāsa viprendrān sūta vaktumihārhasi ।।
purā dāruvan ramye devasiddhaniṣevite । saputradārā munayastapaśceruḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। pravṛttaṃ vividhaṃ karma prakurvāṇā yathāvidhi । yajanti vividhairyajñaistapanti ca maharṣayaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ pravṛttivinyastacetasāmatha śūladhṛk । khyāpayan sa mahādoṣaṃ yayau dāruvanaṃ haraḥ ।। kṛtvā viśvaguruṃ viṣṇuṃ pārśve devo maheśvaraḥ । yayau nivṛttavijñānasthāpanārthaṃ ca śaṅkaraḥ ।।
āsthāya vipulaṃ veśamūnaviṃśativatsaraḥ । līlālaso mahābāhuḥ pīnāṅgaścārulocanaḥ ।। cāmīkaravapuḥ śrīmān pūrṇacandranibhānanaḥ । mattamātaṅgagāmano digvāsā jagadīśvaraḥ ।।
kuśeśayamayīṃ mālaṃ sarvaratnairalaṅkṛtām । dadhāno bhagavānīśaḥ samāgacchati sasmitaḥ ।। yo anantaḥ puruṣo yonirlokānāmavyayo hariḥ । strīveṣaṃ viṣṇurāsthāya so anugacchati śūlinam ।।
sampūrṇacandravadanaṃ pīnonnatapayodharam । śucismitaṃ suprasannaṃ raṇannupurakadvayam ।। supītavasanaṃ divyaṃ śyāmalaṃ cārulocanam । udārahaṃsacalanaṃ vilāsi sumanoharam ।।
evaṃ sa bhagavānīśo devadāruvane haraḥ । cacāra hariṇā bhikṣāṃ māyayā mohayan jagat ।। dṛṣṭvā carantaṃ viśveśaṃ tatra tatra pinākinam । māyayā mohitā nāryo devadevaṃ samanvayuḥ ।।
vistrastavastrābharaṇāstyaktvā lajjāṃ pativratāḥ । sahaiva tena kāmārtā vilāsinyaścarantihi ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ putrakā ye syuryuvāno jitamānasāḥ । anvagacchan hṛṣīkeśaṃ sarve kāmaprapīḍitāḥ ।।
nārīgaṇā māyinamekamīśam । micchantyathāliṅganamācaranti ।। gāyanti gītāni munīśaputrāḥ । bhrūbhaṅgamanye vicaranti tena ।।
māyī murārirmanasi praviṣṭaḥ । māyānubhūyanta itiva samyak ।। sa mādhavaḥ strīgaṇamadhyaviṣṭaḥ । yathaikaśaktyā saha devadevaḥ ।।
tadā virūḍhaḥ punareva bhūyaḥ । tadīśavṛttāmṛtamādidevaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā nārīkulaṃ rudraṃ putrāṇāmapi keśavam । mohayantaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ kopaṃ saṃdadhire bhṛśam ।।
atīva paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ procurdevaṃ kapardinam । śeṣuśca śāpairvividhairmāyayā tasya mohitāḥ ।। tapāṃsi teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratyāhanyanta śaṅkare । yathādityaprakāśena tārakā nabhasi sthitāḥ ।।
te bhagnatapaso viprāḥ sametya vṛṣabhadhvajam । ko bhavāniti deveśaṃ pṛcchanti sma vimohitāḥ ।। so abravīd bhagavānīśastapaścartumihāgataḥ । idānīṃ bhāryayā deśe bhavadbhiriha suvratāḥ ।।
tasya te vākyamākarṇya bhṛgvādyā munipuṅgavāḥ । ūcurgṛhītvā vasanaṃ tyaktvā bhāryāṃ tapaścara ।। athovāca vihasyeśaḥ pinākī nīlalohitaḥ । saṃprekṣya jagato yoniṃ pārśvasthaṃ ca janārdanam ।।
kathaṃ bhavadbhiruditaṃ svabhāryāpoṣaṇotsukaiḥ । tyaktavyā mama bhāryeti dharmajñaiḥ śāntamānasaiḥ ।। vyabhicāraratā nāryaḥ saṃtyājyāḥ patineritāḥ । asmābhireṣā subhagā tādṛśī tyāgamarhati ।।
na kadācidiyaṃ viprā manasāpyanyamicchati । nāhamenāmapi tathā vimuñcāmi kadācana ।। dṛṣṭvā vyabhicarantīha hyasmābhiḥ puruṣādhama । uktaṃ hyasatyaṃ bhavatā gamyatāṃ kṣiprameva hi ।।
evamukte mahādevaḥ satyameva mayeritam । bhavatāṃ pratibhātyeṣetyuktvāsau vicacāra ha ।। so agacchaddhariṇā sārdhaṃ munindrasya mahātmanaḥ । vasiṣṭhasyāśramaṃ puṇyaṃ bhikṣārtho parameśvaraḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā samāgataṃ devaṃ bhikṣamāṇamarundhatī । vasiṣṭhasya priyā bhāryā pratyudgamya nanāma nam ।। prakṣālya pādau vimalaṃ dattvā cāsanamuttamam । saṃprekṣya śithilaṃ gātramabhighātahataṃ dvijaiḥ ।
saṃdhayāmāsa bhaiṣajyairviṣṇā vadanā satī ।। cakāra mahatīṃ pūjāṃ prārthayāmāsa bhāryayā । ko bhavān kuta āyātaḥ kimācāro bhavāniti । uvāca tāṃ mahādevaḥ siddhānāṃ pravaro asmyaham ।।
yadetanmaṇḍalaṃ śuddhaṃ bhāti brahmamayaṃ sadā । eṣaiva devatā mahyaṃ dhārayāmi sadaiva tat ।। hatyuktvā prayayau śrīmānanugṛhya pativratām । tāḍayāñcakrire daṇḍairloṣṭibhirmuṣṭibhidvijāḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā carantaṃ giriśaṃ nagnaṃ vikṛtalakṣaṇam । procuretad bhavāṃlliṅgamutpāṭayatu durmate ।। tānabravīnmahāyogī kariṣyāmīti śaṅkaraḥ । yuṣmākaṃ māmake liṅge yadi dveṣo abhijāyate ।।
ityuktvotpāṭayāmāsa bhagavān bhaganetrahā । nāpaśyaṃstatkṣaṇeneśaṃ keśavaṃ liṅgameva ca ।। tadotpātā babhūvurhi lokānāṃ bhayaśaṃsinaḥ । na rājate sahasrāṃśuścacāla pṛthivī punaḥ ।
niṣprabhāśca grahāḥ sarve cukṣubhe ca mahodadhiḥ ।। apaśyaccānusūyātreḥ svapnaṃ bhāryā pativratā । kathayāmāsa viprāṇāṃ bhayādākulitekṣaṇā ।। tejasā bhāsayan kṛtsnaṃ nārāyaṇasahāyavān ।
bhikṣamāṇaḥ śivo nūnaṃ dṛṣṭo asmākaṃ gṛheṣviti ।। tasyā vacanamākarṇya śaṅkamānā maharṣayaḥ । sarve jagmurmahāyogaṃ brahmāṇaṃ viśvasaṃbhavam ।। upāsyamānamamalairyogibhirbrahmavittamaiḥ ।
caturvedairmūrtimadbhiḥ sāvitryā sahitaṃ prabhum ।। āsīnamāsane ramye nānāścaryasamanvite । prabhāsahasrakalile jñānaiśvaryādisaṃyute ।। vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā sastitaṃ śubhralocanam ।
caturmukhaṃ mahābāhuṃ chandomayamajaṃ param ।। vilokya vedapuruṣaṃ prasannavadanaṃ śubham । śirobhirdharaṇīṃ gatvā toṣayāmāsurīśvaram ।। tān prasannamanā devaścaturmūrtiścaturmukhaḥ ।
vyājahāra muniśreṣṭhāḥ kimāgamanakāraṇam ।। tasya te vṛttamakhilaṃ brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ । jñāpayāñcakrire sarve kṛtvā śirasi cāñjalim ।। kaścid dāruvanaṃ puṇyaṃ puruṣo atīvaśobhanaḥ ।
bhāryayā cārusarvāṅgyā praviṣṭo nagna eva hi ।। mohayāmāsa vapuṣā nārīṇāṃ kulamīśvaraḥ । kanyakānāṃ priyā cāsya dūṣayāmāsa putrakān ।। asmābhirvividhāḥ śāpāḥ pradattāśca parāhatāḥ ।
tāḍito asmābhiratyarthaṃ liṅgantu vinipātitam ।। antarhitaśca bhagavān sabhāryo liṅgameva ca । utpātāścābhavan ghorāḥ sarvabhūtabhayaṅkarāḥ ।। ka eṣa puruṣo deva bhītāḥ sma puruṣottama ।
bhavantameva śaraṇaṃ prapannā vayamacyuta ।। tvaṃ hi vetsi jagatyasmin yatkiñcidapi ceṣṭitam । anugraheṇa viśveśa tadasmānanupālaya ।। vijñāpito munigaṇairviśvātmā kamalodbhavaḥ ।
dhyātvā devaṃ triśūlāṅkaṃ kṛtāñjalirabhāṣata ।। hā kaṣṭaṃ bhavatāmadya jātaṃ sarvārthanāśanam । dhigbalaṃ dhik tapaścaryā mithyaiva bhavatāmiha ।। saṃprāpya puṇyasaṃskārānnidhīnāṃ paramaṃ nidhim ।
upekṣitaṃ vṛthācārairbhavadbhiriha mohitaiḥ ।। kāṅkṣante yogino nityaṃ yatanto yatayo nidhim । yameva taṃ samāsādya hā bhavadbhirupekṣitam ।। yajanti yajñairvividhairyatprāptyairvedavādinaḥ ।
mahānidhiṃ samāsādya hā bhavadbhirupekṣitam ।। yaṃ samāsādya devānaimaiśvaryamakhilaṃ jagat । tamāsādyākṣayanidhiṃ hā bhavadbhirupekṣitam ।। yatsamāpattijanitaṃ viśveśatvamidaṃ mama ।
tadevopekṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā nidhānaṃ bhāgyavarjitaiḥ ।। yasmin samāhitaṃ divyamaiśvaryaṃ yat tadavyayam । tamāsādya nidhiṃ brāhma hā bhavadbhirvṛthākṛtam ।। eṣa devo mahādevo vijñeyastu maheśvaraḥ ।
na tasya paramaṃ kiñcit padaṃ samadhigamyate ।। devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ cāpi śāśvataḥ । sahasrayugaparyante pralaye sarvadehinām । saṃharatyeṣa bhagavān kālo bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ ।।
eṣa caiva prajāḥ sarvāḥ sṛjatyekaḥ svatejasā । eṣa cakrī ca vajrī ca śrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇaḥ ।। yogī kṛtayuge devastretāyāṃ yajña ucyate । dvāpare bhagavān kālo dharmaketuḥ kalau yuge ।।
rudrasya mūrtayastistro yābhirviśvamidaṃ tatam । tamo hyagnī rajo brahmā sattvaṃ viṣṇuriti prabhuḥ ।। mūrtiranyā smṛtā cāsya digvāsā vai śivā dhruvā । yatra tiṣṭhati tad brahma yogena tu samanvitam ।।
yā cāsya pārśvagā bhāryā bhavadbhirabhivīkṣitā । sā hi nārāyaṇo devaḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ ।। tasmāt sarvamidaṃ jātaṃ tatraiva ca layaṃ vrajet । sa eva mohayet kṛtsnaṃ sa eva paramā gatiḥ ।।
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt । ekaśṛṅgo mahānātmā purāṇo aṣṭākṣaro hariḥ ।। caturvedaścaturmūrtistrimūrtistriguṇaḥ paraḥ । ekamūrtirameyātmā nārāyaṇa iti śrutiḥ ।।
ṛtasya garbho bhagavānāpo māyātanuḥ prabhuḥ । stūyate vividhairmantrairbrāhmaṇairdharmamokṣibhiḥ ।। saṃhṛtya sakalaṃ viśvaṃ kalpānte puruṣottamaḥ । śete yogāmṛtaṃ pītvā yat tad viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।।
na jāyate na mriyate vardhate na ca viśvasṛk । mūlaprakṛtiravyaktā gīyate vaidikairajaḥ ।। tato niśāyāṃ vṛttāyāṃ sisṛkṣurakhilañjagat । ajasya nābhau tad bījaṃ kṣipatyeṣa maheśvaraḥ ।।
taṃ māṃ vitta mahātmānaṃ brahmāṇaṃ viśvato mukham । mahāntaṃ puruṣaṃ viśvamapāṃ garbhamanuttamam ।। na taṃ vidātha janakaṃ mohitāstasya māyayā । devadevaṃ mahādevaṃ bhūtānāmīśvaraṃ haram ।।
eṣa devo mahādevo hyanādirbhagavān haraḥ । viṣṇunā saha saṃyuktaḥ karoti vikaroti ca ।। na tasya vidyate kāryaṃ na tasmād vidyate param । sa vedān pradadau pūrvaṃ yogamāyātanurmama ।।
sa māyī māyayā sarvaṃ karoti vikaroti ca । tameva muktaye jñātvā vrajeta śaraṇaṃ bhavam ।। itīritā bhagavatā marīcipramukhā vibhum । praṇamya devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ pṛcchanti sma suduḥ khitāḥ ।।
kathaṃ paśyema taṃ devaṃ punareva pinākinam । brūhi viśvāmareśāna trātā tvaṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇām ।। yad dṛṣṭaṃ bhavatā tasya liṅgaṃ bhuvi nipātitam । talliṅgānukṛtīśasya kṛtvā liṅgamanuttamam ।।
pūjayadhvaṃ sapatnīkāḥ sādaraṃ putrasaṃyutāḥ । vaidikaireva niyamairvividhairbrahmacāriṇaḥ ।। saṃsthāpya śāṅkarairmantrairṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃbhavaiḥ । tapaḥ paraṃ samāsthāya gṛṇantaḥ śatarudriyam ।।
samāhitāḥ pūjayadhvaṃ saputrāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ । sarve prāñjalayo bhūtvā śūlapāṇiṃ prapadyatha ।। tato drakṣyatha deveśaṃ durdarśamakṛtātmabhiḥ । yaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvamajñānamadharmaśca praṇaśyati ।।
tataḥ praṇamya varadaṃ brahmāṇamamitaujasam । jagmuḥ saṃhṛṣṭamanaso devadāruvanaṃ punaḥ ।। ārādhayitumārabdhā brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā । ajānantaḥ paraṃ devaṃ vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ ।।
sthaṇḍileṣu vicitreṣu parvatānāṃ guhāsu ca । nadīnāṃ ca vivikteṣu pulineṣu śubheṣu ca ।। śaivālabhojanāḥ kecit kecidantarjaleśayāḥ । kecidabhrāvakāśāstu pādāṅguṣṭhāgraviṣṭhitāḥ ।।
danto alūkhalinastvanye hyaśmakuṭṭāstathā pare । śākaparṇāśinaḥ kecit saṃprakṣālā marīcipāḥ ।। vṛkṣamūlaniketāśca śilāśayyāstathā pare । kālaṃ nayanti tapasā pūjayanto maheśvaram ।।
tatasteṣāṃ prasādārthaṃ prapannārtiharo haraḥ । cakā bhagavān buddhiṃ prabodhāya vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।। devaḥ kṛtayuge hyasmin śṛṅge himavataḥ śubhe । devadāruvanaṃ prāptaḥ prasannaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।
bhasmapāṇḍuradigdhāṅgo nagno vikṛtalakṣaṇaḥ । ulmukavyagrahastaśca raktapiṅgalalocanaḥ ।। kvacicca hasate raudraṃ kvacid gāyati vismitaḥ । kvacinnṛtyati śṛṅgārī kvacidrauti muhurmuhuḥ ।।
āśrame abhyāgato bhikṣāṃ yācate ca punaḥ punaḥ । māyāṃ kṛtvātmano rūpaṃ devastad vanamāgataḥ ।। kṛtvā girisutāṃ gaurīṃ pārśvedevaḥ pinākadhṛk । sā ca pūrvavad deveśī devadāruvanaṃ gatā ।।
dṛṣṭvā samāgataṃ devaṃ devyā saha kapardinam । praṇemuḥ śirasā bhūmau toṣayāmāsurīśvaram ।। vaidikairvividhairmantraiḥ sūktairmāheśvaraiḥ śubhaiḥ । atharvaśirasā cānye rudrādyairbrahmabhirbhavam ।।
namo devādidevāya mahādevāya te namaḥ । tryambakāya namastubhyaṃ triśūlavaradhāriṇe ।। namo digvāsase tubhyaṃ vikṛtāya pinākine । sarvapraṇatadehāya svayamapraṇatātmane ।।
antakāntakṛte tubhyaṃ sarvasaṃharaṇāya ca । namo astu nṛtyaśīlāya namo bhairavarūpiṇe ।। naranārīśarīrāya yogināṃ gurave namaḥ । namo dāntāya śāntāya tāpasāya harāya ca ।।
vibhīṣaṇāya rudrāya namaste kṛttivāsase । namaste lelihānāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ ।। aghoraghorarūpāya vāmadevāya vai namaḥ । namaḥ kanakamālāya devyāḥ priyakarāya ca ।।
gaṅgāsaliladhārāya śambhave parameṣṭhine । namo yogādhipataye brahmādhipataye namaḥ ।। prāṇāya ca namastubhyaṃ namo bhasmāṅgarāgine । namaste ghanavāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe vahniretase ।।
brahmaṇaśca śiro hartre namaste kālarūpiṇe । āgatiṃ te na janīmo gatiṃ naiva ca naiva ca । viśveśvara mahādeva yo asi so asi namo astu te ।। namaḥ pramathanāthāya dātre ca śubhasaṃpadām ।
kapālapāṇaye tubhyaṃ namo mīḍhuṣṭamāya te । namaḥ kanakaliṅgāya vāriliṅgāya te namaḥ ।। namo vahnyarkaliṅgāya jñānaliṅgāya te namaḥ । namo bhujaṅgahārāya karṇikārapriyāya ca ।
kirīṭine kuṇḍaline kālakālāya te namaḥ ।। vāmadeva maheśāna devadeva trilocana । kṣamyatāṃ yatkṛtaṃ mohāt tvameva śaraṇaṃ hi naḥ ।। caritāni vicitrāṇi guhyāni gahanāni ca ।
brahmādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ durvijñeyo asi śaṅkara ।। ajñānād yadi vā jñānād yatkiñcitkurute naraḥ । tatsarvaṃ bhagavānena kurute yogamāyayā ।। evaṃ stutvā mahādevaṃ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।
ūcuḥ praṇamya giriśaṃ paśyāmastvāṃ yathā purā ।। teṣāṃ saṃstavamākarṇya somaḥ momavibhūṣaṇaḥ । svameva paramaṃ rūpaṃ darśayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ ।। taṃ te dṛṣṭvātha giriśaṃ devyā saha pinākinam ।
yathā pūrvaṃ sthitā viprāḥ praṇemurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। tataste munayaḥ sarve saṃstūya ca maheśvaram । bhṛgvaṅgirovasiṣṭhāstu viśvāmitrastathaiva ca ।। gautamo atriḥ sukeśaśca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।
marīciḥ kaśyapaścāpi saṃvartaśca mahātapāḥ । praṇamya devadeveśamidaṃ vacanamabruvan ।। kathaṃ tvāṃ devadeveśa karmayogena vā prabho । jñānena vātha yogena pūjayāmaḥ sadaiva hi ।।
kena vā devamārgeṇa saṃpūjyo bhagavāniha । kiṃ tat sevyamasevyaṃ vā sarvametad bravīhi naḥ ।। etad vaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi gūḍhaṃ gahanamuttamam । brahmaṇe kathitaṃ pūrvamādāveva maharṣayaḥ ।।
sāṃkhyayogo dvidhā jñeyaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ hi sādhanam । yogena sahitaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ vimuktidam ।। na kevalena yogena dṛśyate puruṣaḥ paraḥ । jñānaṃ tu kevalaṃ samyagapavargaphalapradam ।।
bhavantaḥ kevalaṃ yogaṃ samāśritya vimuktaye । vihāya sāṃkhyaṃ vimalamakurvanta pariśramam ।। etasmāt kāraṇād viprānṛṇāṃ kevaladharmiṇām । āgato ahamimaṃ deśaṃ jñāpayan mohasaṃbhavam ।।
tasmād bhavadbhirvimalaṃ jñānaṃ kaivalyasādhanam । jñātavyaṃ hi prayatnena śrotavyaṃ dṛśyameva ca ।। ekaḥ sarvatrago hyātmā kevalaścitimātrakaḥ । ānando nirmalo nityaṃ syādetat sāṃkhyadarśanam ।।
etadeva paraṃ jñānameṣa mokṣo atra gīyate । etat kaivalyamamalaṃ brahmabhāvaśca varṇitaḥ ।। āśritya caitat paramaṃ tanniṣṭhāstatparāyaṇāḥ । paśyanti māṃ mahātmāno yatayo viśvamīśvaram ।।
etat tat paramaṃ jñānaṃ kevalaṃ sannirañjanam । ahaṃ hi vedyo bhagavān mama mūrtiriyaṃ śivā ।। bahūni sādhanānīha siddhaye kathitāni tu । teṣāmabhyadhikaṃ jñānaṃ māmakaṃ dvijapuṅgavāḥ ।।
jñānayogaratāḥ śāntā māmeva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ । ye hi māṃ bhasmaniratā dhyāyanti satataṃ hṛdi ।। madbhaktiparamā nityaṃ yatayaḥ kṣīṇakalmaṣāḥ । nāśayāmyacirāt teṣāṃ ghoraṃ saṃsārasāgaram ।।
praśāntaḥ saṃyatamanā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaḥ । brahmacaryarato nagno vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret ।। nirmitaṃ hi mayā pūrvaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ param । guhyād guhyatamaṃ sūkṣmaṃ vedasāraṃ vimuktaye ।।
yad vā kaupīnavasanaḥ syād vaikavasano muniḥ । vedābhyāsarato vidvān dhyāyet paśupatiṃ śivam ।। eṣa pāśupato yogaḥ sevanīyo mumukṣubhiḥ । bhasmacchannairhi satataṃ niṣkāmairiti viśrutiḥ ।।
vītarāgabhayakrodhā manmayā māmupāśritāḥ । bahavo anena yogena pūtā madbhāvamāgatāḥ ।। anyāni caiva śāstrāṇi loke asmin mohanānitu । vedavādaviruddhāni mayaiva kathitāni tu ।।
vāmaṃ pāśupataṃ somaṃ lākulaṃ caiva bhairavam । asevyametat kathitaṃ vedavāhyaṃ tathetaram ।। vedamurtirahaṃ viprā nānyaśāstrārthavedibhiḥ । jñāyate matsvarūpaṃ tu muktvā vedaṃ sanātanam ।।
sthāpayadhvamidaṃ mārgaṃ pūjayadhvaṃ maheśvaram । acirādaiśvaraṃ jñānamutpatsyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। mayi bhaktiśca vipulā bhavatāmastu sattamāḥ । dhyātamātro hi sānnidhyaṃ dāsyāmi munisattamāḥ ।।
ityuktvā bhagavān somastatraivāntaradhīyata । to api dāruvane tasmin pūjayanti sma śaṅkaram । brahmacaryaratāḥ śāntā jñānayogaparāyaṇāḥ ।। sametya te mahātmāno munayo brahmavādinaḥ ।
vitenire bahūn vādānnadhyātmajñānasaṃśrayān ।। kimasya jagato mūlamātmā cāsmākameva hi । ko api syāt sarvabhāvānāṃ heturīśvara eva ca ।। ityevaṃ manyamānānāṃ dhyānamārgāvalambinām ।
āvirāsīnmahādevī devī girivarātmajā ।। koṭisūryapratīkāśā jvālāmālāsamāvṛtā । svabhābhirvimalābhistu pūrayantī nabhastalam ।। jvālāsahasrāntarasanniviṣṭām ।
jānanti te tat paramasya bījam ।। gatistathātmā gaganābhidhānā । tasyāmathaite munayaśca viprāḥ ।। tadantare devamaśeṣahetum ।
rudraṃ bṛhantaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।। praṇemurānandamavāpuragryam । dāvirbabhau janmavināśahetu ।। sarvātmikā sarvaniyāmikā ca ।
vyomābhidhānā divi rājatīva ।। nmaheśvaraḥ śiva eko atha rudraḥ । māyāmathāruhya sa devadevaḥ ।। māyī rudraḥ sakalo niṣkalaśca ।
metajjñātvā hyamṛtatvaṃ vrajanti ।। devyā bhargaḥ saha devādidevaḥ । vanaukasaste punareva rudram ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ devadevaviceṣṭitam ।
devadāruvane pūrvaṃ purāṇe yanmayā śrutam ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyānnityaṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ । śrāvayed vā dvijān śāntān sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। eṣā puṇyatamā devī devagandharvasevitā ।
narmadā lokavikhyātā tīrthānāmuttamā nadī ।। tasyāḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ māhātmyaṃ mārkaṇḍeyena bhāṣitam । yudhiṣṭhirāya tu śubhaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।। śrutāstu vividhā dharmāstvatprasādānmahāmune ।
māhātmyaṃ ca prayāgasya tīrthāni vividhāni ca ।। narmadā sarvatīrthānāṃ mukhyā hi bhavateritā । tasyāstvidānīṃ māhātmyaṃ vaktumarhasi sattama ।। narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā rudradehād viniḥ sṛtā ।
tārayet sarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। narmadāyāstu māhātmyaṃ purāṇe yanmayā śrutam । idānīṃ tatpravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanāḥ śubham ।। puṇyā kanakhale gaṅgā kurukṣetre sarasvatī ।
grāme vā yadi vāraṇye puṇyā sarvatra narmadā ।। tribhiḥ sārasvataṃ toyaṃ saptāhena tu yāmunam । sadyaḥ punāti gāṅgeyaṃ darśanādeva nārmadam ।। kaliṅgadeśapaścārdhe parvate amarakaṇṭake ।
puṇyā ca triṣu lokeṣu ramaṇīyā manoramā ।। sadevāsuragandharvā ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ । tapastaptvā tu rājendra siddhiṃ tu paramāṃ gatāḥ ।। tatra snātvā naro rājan niyamastho jitendriyaḥ ।
upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ kulānāṃ tārayecchatam ।। yojanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ śrūyate sariduttamā । vistāreṇa tu rājendra yojanadvayamāyatā ।। ṣaṣṭitīrthasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭikoṭyastathaiva ca ।
parvatasya samantāt tu tiṣṭhantyamarakaṇṭake ।। brahmacārī śucirbhūtvā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ । sarvahiṃsānivṛttastu sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। evaṃ sarvasamācāro yastu prāṇān samutsṛjet ।
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ rājan śṛṇuṣvāvahito nṛpa ।। śatavarṣasahasrāṇi svarge modati pāṇḍava । sapsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇo divyastrīparivāritaḥ ।। divyagandhānuliptaśca divyapuṣpopaśobhitaḥ ।
krīḍate devaloke tu daivataiḥ saha modate ।। tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ । gṛhaṃ tu labhate asau vai nānāratnasamanvitam ।। stambhairmaṇimayairdivyairvajravaidūryabhūṣitam ।
ālekhyavāhanaiḥ śubhrairdāsīdāsasamanvitam ।। rājarājeśvaraḥ śrīmān sarvastrījanavallabhaḥ । jīved varṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ tatra bhogasamanvitaḥ ।। agnipraveśe atha jale athavānaśane kṛte ।
anivartikā gatistasya pavanasyāmbare yathā ।। paścime parvatataṭe sarvapāpavināśanaḥ । hrado jaleśvaro nāma triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ ।। tatra piṇḍapradānena saṃdhyopāsanakarmaṇā ।
daśavarṣāṇi pitarastarpitāḥ syurna saṃśayaḥ ।। dakṣiṇe narmadākūle kapilākhyā mahānadī । saralārjunasaṃcchannā nātidūre vyavasthitā ।। sā tu puṇyā mahābhāgā triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā ।
tatra koṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ tīrthānāṃ tu yudhiṣṭhira ।। tasmiṃstīrthe tu ye vṛkṣāḥ patitāḥ kālaparyayāt । narmadātoyasaṃspṛṣṭāste yānti paramāṃ gatim ।। dvitīyā tu mahābhāgā viśalyakaraṇī śubhā ।
tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā viśalyo bhavati kṣaṇāt ।। kapilā ca viśalyā ca śrūyate rājasattama । īśvareṇa purā proktā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। anāśakaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa ।
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। tatra snātvā naro rājannaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet । ye vasantyuttare kūle rudraloke vasanti te ।। sarasvatyāṃ ca gaṅgāyāṃ narmadāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।
samaṃ snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca yathā me śaṅkaro abravīt ।। parityajati yaḥ praṇān parvate amarakaṇṭake । varṣakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ rudraloke mahīyate ।। narmadāyāṃ jalaṃ puṇyaṃ phenormisamalaṅkṛtam ।
pavitraṃ śirasā vandya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। narmadā sarvataḥ puṇyā brahmahatyāpahāriṇī । ahorātropavāsena mucyate brahmahatyayā ।। jāleśvaraṃ tīrthavaraṃ sarvapāpavināśanam ।
tatra gatvā niyamavān sarvakāmāṃllabhennaraḥ ।। candrasūryoparāge tu gatvā hyamarakaṇṭakam । aśvamedhād daśaguṇaṃ puṇyamāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। eṣa puṇyo girivaro devagandharvasevitaḥ ।
nānādrumalatākīrṇo nānāpuṣpopaśobhitaḥ ।। tatra saṃnihito rājan devyā saha maheśvaraḥ । brahmā viṣṇustathā cendro vidyādharagaṇaiḥ saha ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt parvataṃ hyamarakaṇṭakam ।
pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānaḥ ।। kāverī nāma vipulā nadī kalpaṣanāśinī । tatra snātvā mahādevamarcayed vṛṣabhadhvajam । saṃgame narmadāyāstu rudraloke mahīyate ।।
narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā sarvapāpavināśinī । munibhiḥ kathitā pūrvamīśvareṇa svayaṃbhuvā ।। munibhiḥ saṃstutā hyeṣā narmadā pravarā nadī । rudragātrād viniṣkrāntā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।
sarvapāpaharā nityaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtā । saṃstutā devagandharvairapyarobhistathaiva ca ।। uttare caiva tatkūle tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam । nāmnā bhadreśvaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham ।
tatra snātvā naro rājan daivataiḥ saha mohate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthamāmrātakeśvaram । tatra snātvā naro rājan gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।। tato aṅgāreśvaraṃ gacchenniyato niyatāśanaḥ ।
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudraloke mahīyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra kedāraṃ nāma puṇyadam । tatra snātvodakaṃ kṛtvā sarvān kāmānavāpnuyāt ।। pippaleśaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpavināśanam ।
tatra snātvā mahārāja rudraloke mahīyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra vimaleśvaramuttamam । tatra prāṇān parityajya rudralokamavāpnuyāt ।। tataḥ puṣkariṇīṃ gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret ।
snātamātro narastatra indrasyārdhāsanaṃ labhet ।। tato gaccheta rājendra śūlabhedamiti śrutam । tatra snātvārcayed devaṃ gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।। tato gaccheta rājendra balitīrthamanuttam ।
tatra snātvā naro rājan sihāsanapatirbhavet ।। śakratīrthaṃ tato gacchet kūle caiva tu dakṣiṇe । upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ snānaṃ kṛtvā yathāvidhi ।। ārādhayenmahāyogaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim ।
gosahasraphalaṃ prāpya viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। ṛṣitīrthaṃ tato gatvā sarvapāpaharaṃ nṛṇām । snātamātro narastatra śivaloke mahīyate ।। nāradasya tu tatraiva tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam ।
snātamātro narastatra gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।। yatra taptaṃ tapaḥ pūrvaṃ nāradena surarṣiṇā । pratīstasya dadau yogaṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ ।। brahmaṇā nirmitaṃ liṅgaṃ brahmeśvaramiti śrutam ।
yatra snātvā naro rājan brahmaloke mahīyate ।। ṛṇatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sa ṛṇānmucyate dhruvam । maheśvaraṃ tato gacchet paryāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam ।। bhīmeśvaraṃ tato gacchet sarvavyādhivināśanam ।
snātamātro narastatra sarvaduḥkhaiḥ pramucyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra piṅgaleśvaramuttamam । ahorātropavāsena trirātraphalamāpnuyāt ।। tasmiṃmastīrthe tu rājendra kapilāṃ yaḥ prayacchati ।
yāvanti tasyā romāṇi tatprasūtikuleṣu ca । tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate ।। yastu prāṇaparityāgaṃ kuryāt tatra narādhipa । akṣayaṃ modate kālaṃ yāvaccandradivākarau ।।
narmadātaṭamāśritya tiṣṭhante ye tu mānavāḥ । te mṛtāḥ svargamāyānti santaḥ sukṛtino yathā ।। tato dīpteśvaraṃ gacched vyāsatīrthaṃ tapovanam । nivartitā purā tatra vyāsabhītā mahānadī ।
huṅkāritā tu vyāsena dakṣiṇena tato gatā ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ tu yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe yudhiṣṭhira । prītastasya bhaved vyāso vāñchitaṃ labhate phalam ।। tato gaccheta rājendra ikṣunadyāstu saṃgamam ।
trailokyaviśrutaṃ puṇyaṃ tatra sannihitaḥ śivaḥ । tatra stanātvā naro rājan gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।। skandatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpapraṇāśanam । ājanmanaḥ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ snātastīvraṃ vyapohati ।।
tatra devāḥ sagandharvā bhavātmajamanuttamam । upāsate mahātmānaṃ skandaṃ śaktidhiraṃ prabhum ।। tato gacchedāṅgirasaṃ snānaṃ tatra samācaret । gosahasraphalaṃ prāpya rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
aṅgirā yatra deveśaṃ brahmaputro vṛṣadhvajam । tapasārādhya viśveśaṃ labdhavān yogamuttamam ।। kuśatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpapraṇāśanam । snānaṃ tatra prakurvota aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।।
koṭitīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpapraṇāśanam । tatra strātvā naro rājyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। candrabhāgāṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret । snātamātro narastatra somaloke mahīyate ।।
narmadādakṣiṇe kūle saṃgameśvaramuttamam । tatra snātvā naro rājan sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet ।। narmadāyottare kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam । ādityāyatanaṃ ramyamīśvareṇa tu bhāṣitam ।।
tatra snātvā tu rājendra dattvā dānaṃ tu śaktitaḥ । tasya tīrthaprabhāveṇa labhate cākṣayaṃ phalam ।। daridrā vyādhitā ye tu ye ca duṣkṛtakāriṇaḥ । mucyante sarvapāpebhyaḥ sūryalokaṃ prayānti ca ।।
mārgeśvaraṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret । snātamātro narastatra svargalokamavāpnuyāt ।। tataḥ paścimato gacchenmarudālayamuttamam । tatra snātvā tu rājendra śucirbhūtvā prayatnataḥ ।।
kāñcanaṃ tu dvijo dadyād yathāvibhavavistaram । puṣpakeṇa vimānena vāyulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। tato gaccheta rājendra ahalyātīrthamuttamam । snānamātrādapsarobhirmodate kālamakṣayam ।।
caitramāse tu saṃprāpte śuklapakṣe trayodaśī । kāmadevadine tasminnahalyāṃ yastu pūjayet ।। yatra tatra narotpanno varastatra priyo bhavet । strīvallabho bhavecchrīmān kāmadeva ivāparaḥ ।।
ayodhyāṃ tu samāsādya tīrthaṃ śakrasya viśrutam । snātamātro narastatra gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।। somatīrthaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret । snātamātro narastatra sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
somagrahe tu rājendra pāpakṣayakaraṃ bhavet । trailokyaviśrutaṃ rājan somatīrthaṃ mahāphalam ।। yastu cāndrāyaṇaṃ kuryāt tatra tīrthe samāhitaḥ । sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā somalokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
agnipraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryāt somatīrthe narādhipa । jale cānaśanaṃ vāpi nāsau martyo abhijāyate ।। stambhatīrthaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret । snātamātro narastatra somaloke mahīyate ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra viṣṇutīrthamanuttamam । yodhanīpuramākhyātaṃ viṣṇoḥ sthānamanuttamam ।। asurā yodhitāstatra vāsudevena koṭiśaḥ । tatra tīrthaṃ samutpannaṃ viṣṇuśrīko bhavediha ।
ahorātropavāsena brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।। narmadādakṣiṇe kūle tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam । kāmatīrthamiti khyātaṃ yatra kāmor'cayad bhavam ।। tasmiṃstīrthe naraḥ snātvā upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ ।
kusumāyudharūpeṇa rudroloke mahīyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra brahmatīrthamanuttamam । umāhakamiti khyātaṃ tatra saṃtarpayet pitṝn ।। paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ śrdhaṃ kuryād yathāvidhi ।
gajarūpā śilā tatra toyamadhye vyavasthitā ।। tasmiṃstu dāpayet piṇḍān vaiśākhyāntu viśeṣataḥ । snātvā samāhitamanā dambhamātsaryavarjitaḥ । tṛpyanti pitarastasya yāvat tiṣṭhati medinī ।।
siddheśvaraṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret । snātamātro narastatra gāṇapatyapadaṃ labhet ।। tato gaccheta rājendra liṅgo yatra janārdanaḥ । tatra snātvā tu rājendra viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।।
yatra nārāyaṇo devo munonāṃ bhāvitātmanām । svātmānaṃ darśayāmāsa liṅgaṃ tat paramaṃ padam ।। aṅkolaṃ tu tato gacchet sarvapāpavināśanam । snānaṃ dānaṃ ca tatraiva brāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojanam ।
piṇḍapridānaṃ ca kṛtaṃ pretyānantaphalapradam ।। traiyambakena toyena yaścaruṃ śrapayet tataḥ । aṅkolamūle dadyācca piṇḍāṃścaiva yathāvidhi । tāritāḥ pitarastena tṛpyantyācandratārakam ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra tāpaseśvaramuttamam । tatra snātvā tu rājendra prāpnuyāt tapasaḥ phalam ।। śuklatīrthaṃ tato gacchet sarvapāpavināśanam । nāsti tena sama tīrthaṃ narmadāyāṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।।
darśanāt sparśanāt tasya snānadānatapojapāt । homāccaivopavāsācca śuklatīrthe mahat phalam ।। yojanaṃ tat smṛtaṃ kṣetraṃ devagandharvasevitam । śuklatīrthamiti khyātaṃ sarvapāpavināśanam ।।
pādapāgreṇa dṛṣṭena brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati । devyā saha sadā bhargastatra tiṣṭhati śaṅkaraḥ ।। kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ vaiśākhe māsi suvrata । kailāsāccābhiniṣkramya tatra sannihito haraḥ ।।
devadānavagandharvāḥ siddhavidyādharāstathā । gaṇāścāpsarasāṃ nāgāstatra tiṣṭhanti puṅgava ।। rajakena yathā vastraṃ śuklaṃ bhavati vāriṇā । ājanmani kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śuklatīrthe vyapohati ।
snānaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ śrāddhamanantaṃ tatra dṛśyate ।। śuklatīrthāt paraṃ tīrthaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati । pūrve vayasi karmāṇi kṛtvā pāpāni mānavaḥ । ahorātropavāsena śuklatīrthe vyapohati ।।
kārtikasya tu māsasya kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī । ghṛtena snāpayed devamupoṣya parameśvaram । ekaviṃśatkulopeto na cyavedaiśvarāt padāt ।। tapasā brahmacaryeṇa yajñadānena vā punaḥ ।
na tāṃ gatimavāpnoti śuklatīrthe tu yāṃ labhet ।। śuklatīrthaṃ mahātīrthamṛṣisiddhaniṣevitam । tatra snātvā naro rājan punarjanma na vindati ।। ayane vā caturdaśyāṃ saṃkrāntau viṣuve tathā ।
snātvā tu sopavāsaḥ san vijitātmā samāhitaḥ ।। dānaṃ dadyād yathāśakti prīyetāṃ hariśaṅkarau । etat tīrthaprabhāveṇa sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ।। anāthaṃ durgataṃ vipraṃ nāthavantamathāpi vā ।
udvādayati yastīrthe tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ।। yāvat tadromasaṃkhyā tu tatprasūtikuleṣu ca । tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra yamatīrtha manuttamam ।
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ māghamāse yudhiṣṭhira । snānaṃ kṛtvā naktabhījī na paśyed yonisaṅkaṭam ।। tato gaccheta rājendra eraṇḍītīrthamuttamam । saṃgame tu naraḥ snāyādupavāsaparāyaṇaḥ ।
brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayedekaṃ koṭirbhavati bhojitāḥ ।। eraṇḍīsaṃgame snātvā bhaktibhāvāt turañjitaḥ । mṛttikāṃ śirasi sthāpya avagāhya ca tajjalam । narmadodakasaṃmiśraṃ mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthaṃ kārṇāṭikeśvaram । gaṅgāvatarate tatra dine puṇye na saṃśayaḥ ।। tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca dattvā caiva yathāvidhi । sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
nanditīrthaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret । prīyate tasya nandīśaḥ somaloke mahīyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthaṃ tvanarakaṃ śubham । tatra snātvā naro rājan narakaṃ naiva paśyati ।।
tasmiṃstīrthe tu rājendra svānyasthīni vinikṣipet । rūpavān jāyate loke dhanabhogasamanvitaḥ ।। tato gaccheta rājendra kapilātīrtha muttamam । tatra snātvā naro rājan gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।।
jyeṣṭhamāse tu saṃprāpte caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ । tatropoṣya naro bhaktyā dadyād dīpaṃ ghṛtena tu ।। ghṛtena snāpayed rudraṃ saghṛtaṃ śrīphalaṃ dahet । ghaṇṭābharaṇasaṃyuktāṃ kapilāṃ vai pradāpayet ।।
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ । śivatulyabalo bhūtvā śivavat krīḍate ciram ।। aṅgārakadine prāpte caturthyāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ । snāpayitvā śivaṃ dadyād brāhmaṇebhyastu bhojanam ।।
sarvabhogasamāyukto vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ । gatvā śakrasya bhavanaṃ śakreṇa saha modate ।। tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo dhanavān bhogavān bhavet । aṅgārakanavamyāṃ tu amāvāsyāṃ tathaiva ca ।
snāpayet tatra yatnena rūpavān subhago bhavet ।। tato gaccheta rājendra gaṇeśvaramanuttamam । śrāvaṇe māsī saṃprāpte kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśī ।। snātamātro narastatra rudraloke mahīyate ।
pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā mucyate asāvṝṇatrayāt ।। gaṅgeśvarasamīpe tu gaṅgāvadanamuttamam । akāmo vā sakāmo vā tatra snātvā tu mānavaḥ । ājanmajanitaiḥ pāpairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
tasya vai paścime deśe samīpe nātidūrataḥ । daśāśvamedhikaṃ tīrthaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।। upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ māsi bhādrapade śubhe । amāvasyāṃ naraḥ snātvā pūjayed vṛṣabhadhvajam ।।
kāñcanena vimānena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā । gatvā rudrapuraṃ ramyaṃ rudreṇa saha modate ।। sarvatra sarvadivase snānaṃ tatra samācaret । pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kuryādaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra bhṛgutīrtha manuttamam । tatra devo bhṛguḥ purvaṃ rudramārādhayat purā ।। darśanāt tasya devasya sadyaḥ pāpāt pramucyate । etat kṣetraṃ suvipulaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।
tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste apunarbhavāḥ । upānahostathā yugmaṃ deyamannaṃ sakāñcanam । bhojanaṃ ca yathāśakti tadasyākṣayamucyate ।। kṣaranti sarvadānāni yajñadānaṃ tapaḥ kriyā ।
akṣayaṃ tat tapastaptaṃ bhṛgutīrthe yudhiṣṭhira ।। tasyaiva tapasogreṇa tuṣṭena tripurāriṇā । sānnidhyaṃ tatra kathitaṃ bhṛgutīrthe yudhiṣṭhira ।। tato gaccheta rājendra gautameśvaramuttamam ।
yatrārādhya triśūlāṅkaṃ gautamaḥ siddhimāpnuyāt ।। tatra snātvā naro rājan upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ । kāñcanena vimānena brahmaloke mahīyate ।। vṛṣotsargaṃ tato gacchecchāśvataṃ padamāpnuyāt ।
na jānanti narā mūḍhā viṣṇormāyāvimohitāḥ ।। dhautapāpaṃ tato gacched dhautaṃ yatra vṛṣeṇa tu । narmadāyāṃ sthitaṃ rājan sarvapātakanāśanam । tatra tīrthe naraḥ snātvā brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ।।
tatra tīrthe tu rājendra prāṇatyāgaṃ karoti yaḥ । caturbhujastrinetraśca haratulyabalo bhavet ।। vaset kalpāyutaṃ sāgraṃ śivatulyaparākramaḥ । kālena mahatā jātaḥ pṛthivyāmekarāḍ bhavet ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra haṃsatīrtha manuttamam । tatra snātvā naro rājan brahmaloke mahīyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra siddho yatra janārdanaḥ । varāhatīrtha mākhyātaṃ viṣṇulokagatipradam ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra candratīrthamanuttamam । paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣeṇa snānaṃ tatra samācaret । snātamātro narastatra candraloke mahīyate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra kanyātīrthamanuttamam ।
śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ snānaṃ tatra samācaret । snātamātro narastatra pṛthivyāmekarāḍ bhavet ।। devatīrtha tato gacchet sarvadevanamakṛtam । tatra snātvā ca rājendra daivataiḥ saha modate ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra śikhitīrthamanuttamam । yat tatra dīyate dānaṃ sarvaṃ koṭiguṇaṃ bhavet ।। tato gaccheta rājendra tīrthaṃ paitāmahaṃ śubham । yattatra kriyate śrāddhaṃ sarvaṃ tadakṣayaṃ bhavet ।।
sāvitrītīrthamāsādya yastu prāṇān parityajet । vidhūya sarvapāpāni brahmaloke mahīyate ।। manoharaṃ tu tatraiva tīrthaṃ paramaśobhanam । tatra snātvā naro rājan daivataiḥ saha modate ।।
tato gaccheta rājendra mānasaṃ tīrthamuttamam । snātvā tatra naro rājan rudraloke mahīyate ।। svargabinduṃ tato gacchettīrthaṃ devanamaskṛtam । tatra snātvā naro rājan durgatiṃ naiva gacchati ।।
apsareśaṃ tato gacchet snānaṃ tatra samācaret । krīḍate nākalokastho hyapsarobhiḥ sa modate ।। tato gaccheta rājendra bhārabhūtimanuttamam । upoṣitor'cayedīśaṃ rudraloke mahīyate ।
asmiṃstīrthe mṛto rājan gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।। kārtike māsi deveśamarcayet pārvatīpatim । aśvamedhād daśaguṇaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। vṛṣabhaṃ yaḥ prayaccheta tatra kundendusaprabham ।
vṛṣayuktena yānena rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। etat tīrthaṃ samāsādya yastu prāṇān parityajet । sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। jalapraveśaṃ yaḥ kuryāt tasmiṃstīrthe narādhipa ।
haṃsayuktena yānena svargalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। eraṇḍyā narmadāyāstu saṃgamaṃ lokaviśrutam । tatra tīrthaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।। upavāsaparo bhūtvā nityaṃ vrataparāyaṇaḥ ।
tatra snātvā tu rājendra mucyate brahmahatyayā ।। tato gaccheta rājendra narmadodadhisaṃgamam । jamadagniriti khyātaḥ siddho yatra janārdanaḥ ।। tatra snātvā naro rājan narmadodadhisaṃgame ।
triguṇaṃ cāśvamedhasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। tato gaccheta rājendra piṅgaleśvaramuttamam । tatra snātvā naro rājan rudraloke mahīyate ।। tatropavāsaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā paśyeta vimaleśvaram ।
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ hitvā yāti śivālayam ।। tato gaccheta rājendra ālikātīrthamuttamam । upoṣya rajanīmekāṃ niyato niyatāśanaḥ । asya tīrthasya māhātmyānmucyate brahmahatyayā ।।
etāni tava saṃkṣepāt prādhānyāt kathitāni tu । na śakyā vistarād vaktuṃ saṃkhyā tīrtheṣupāṇḍava ।। eṣā pavitrā vimalā nadī trailokyaviśrutā । narmadā saritāṃ śreṣṭhā mahādevasya vallabhā ।।
manasā saṃsmaredyastu narmadāṃ vai yudhiṣṭhira । cāndrāyaṇaśataṃ sāgraṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। aśraddadhānāḥ puruṣā nāstikyaṃ ghoramāśritāḥ । patanti narake ghore ityāha parameśvaraḥ ।।
narmadāṃ sevate nityaṃ svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ । tena puṇyā nadī jñeyā brahmahatyāpahāriṇī ।। idaṃ trailokyavikhyātaṃ tīrthaṃ naimiśamuttamam । mahādevapriyakaraṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ।।
mahādevaṃ didṛkṣūṇāmṛṣīṇaṇāṃ parameṣṭhinām । brahāmaṇā nirmitaṃ sthānaṃ tapastaptuṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। marīcayo atrayo viprā vasiṣṭhāḥ kratavastathā । bhṛgavo aṅgirasaḥ pūrvā brahmāṇaṃ kamalodbhavam ।।
sametya sarvavaradaṃ caturmūrti caturmukham । pṛcchanti praṇipatyainaṃ viśvakarmāṇamacyutam ।। bhagavan devamīśānaṃ bhargamekaṃ kapardinam । kenopāyena paśyāmo brūhi devanamaskṛtam ।।
satraṃ sahasramāsadhvaṃ vāṅmanodoṣavarjitāḥ । deśaṃ ca vaḥ pravakṣyāmi yasmin deśe cariṣyatha ।। uktvā manomayaṃ cakraṃ sa sṛṣṭvā tānuvāca ha । kṣiptametanmayā cakramanuvrajata mā ciram ।
yatrāsya nemiḥ śīryeta sa deśaḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ ।। tato mumoca taccakraṃ te ca tatsamanuvrajan । tasya vai vrajataḥ kṣipraṃ yatra nemiraśīryata । naimisaṃ tatsmṛtaṃ nāmnā puṇyaṃ sarvatra pūjitam ।।
siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ yakṣagandharvasevitam । sthānaṃ bhagavataḥ śaṃbhoretannaimiśamuttamam ।। atra devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ । tapastaptvā purā devā lebhire pravarān varān ।।
imaṃ deśaṃ samāśritya ṣaṭkulīyāḥ samāhitāḥ । satreṇārādhya deveśaṃ dṛṣṭavanto maheśvaram ।। atra dānaṃ tapastaptaṃ snānaṃ japyādikaṃ ca yat । ekaikaṃ pāvayet pāpaṃ saptajanmakṛtaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
atra pūrvaṃ sa bhagavānṛṣīṇāṃ satramāsatām । provāca vāyurbrahmāṇḍaṃ purāṇaṃ brahmabhāṣitam ।। atra devo mahādevo rudrāṇyā kila viśvakṛt । ramate adhyāpi bhagavān pramathaiḥ parivāritaḥ ।।
atra prāṇān parityajya niyamena dvijātayaḥ । brahmalokaṃ gamiṣyanti yatra gatvā na jāyate ।। anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ jāpyeśvaramitiśrutam । jajāpa rudramaniśaṃ yatra nandī mahāgaṇaḥ ।।
prītastasya mahādevo devyā saha pinākadhṛk । dadāvātmasamānatvaṃ mṛtyuvañcanameva ca ।। abhūdṛṣiḥ sa dharmātmā śilādo nāma dharmavit । ārādhayanmahādevaṃ putrārthaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam ।।
tasya varṣasahasrānte tapyamānasya viśvakṛt । śarvaḥ somo gaṇavṛto varado asmītyabhāṣata ।। sa vavre varamīśānaṃ vareṇyaṃ girijāpatim । ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnaṃ dehi putraṃ tvayā samam ।।
tathāstvityāha bhagavān devyā saha maheśvaraḥ । paśyatastasya viprarṣerantardhānaṃ gato haraḥ ।। tato yiyakṣuḥ svāṃ bhūmiṃ śilādo dharmavittamaḥ । cakarṣa lāṅgalenorvoṃ bhittvādṛśyata śobhanaḥ ।।
saṃvartakānalaprakhyaḥ kumāraḥ prahasanniva । rūpalāvaṇyasaṃpannastejasā bhāsayan diśaḥ ।। kumāratulyo apratimo meghagambhīrayā girā । śilādaṃ tāta tāteti prāha nandī punaḥ punaḥ ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nandanaṃ jātaṃ śilādaḥ pariṣasvaje । munibhyo darśayāmāsa ye tadāśramavāsinaḥ ।। jātakarmādikāḥ sarvāḥ kriyāstasya cakāra ha । upanīya yathāśāstraṃ vedamadhyāpayat sutam ।।
adhītavedo bhagavān nandī matimanuttamām । cakre maheśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ jeṣye mṛtyumiti prabhum ।। sa gatvā saritaṃ puṇyāmekāgraśraddhayānvitaḥ । jajāpa rudramaniśaṃ maheśāsaktamānasaḥ ।।
tasya koṭyāṃ tu pūrṇāyāṃ śaṅkaro bhaktavatsalaḥ । āgatya sāmbaḥ sagaṇo varado asmītyuvāca ha ।। sa vavre punarevāhaṃ japeyaṃ koṭimīśvaram । tāvadāyurmahādeva dehīti varamīśvara ।।
evamastviti saṃprocya devo apyantaradhīyata । jajāpa koṭiṃ bhagavān bhūyastadgatamānasaḥ ।। dvitīyāyāṃ ca koṭyāṃ vai saṃpūrṇāyāṃ vṛṣadhvajaḥ । āgatya varado asmīti prāha bhūtagaṇairvṛtaḥ ।।
tṛtīyāṃ japtumicchāmi koṭiṃ bhūyo api śaṅkara । tathāstvityāha viśvātmā devo apyantaradhīyata ।। koṭitraye atha saṃpūrṇe devaḥ prītamanā bhṛśam । āgatya varado asmīti prāha bhūtagaṇairvṛtaḥ ।।
japeyaṃ koṭimanyāṃ vai bhūyo api tava tejasā । ityukte bhagavānāha na japtavyaṃ tvayā punaḥ ।। amaro jarayā tyakto mama pārśvagataḥ sadā । mahāgaṇapatirdevyāḥ putro bhava maheśvaraḥ ।।
yogīśvaro yoganetā gaṇānāmīśvareśvaraḥ । sarvalokādhipaḥ śrīmān sarvajño madbalānvitaḥ ।। jñānaṃ tanmāmakaṃ divyaṃ hastāmalakavat tava । ābhūtasaṃplavasthāyī tato yāsyasi matpadam ।।
etaduktvā mahādevo gaṇānāhūya śaṅkaraḥ । abhiṣekeṇa yuktena nandīśvaramayojayat ।। udvāhayāmāsa ca taṃ svayameva pinākadhṛk । marutāṃ ca śubhāṃ kanyāṃ suyaśeti ca viśrutām ।।
etajjapyeśvaraṃ sthānaṃ devadevasya śūlinaḥ । yatra tatra mṛto martyo rudraloke mahīyate ।। anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ japyeśvarasamīpataḥ । nāmnā pañcanadaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।
trirātropoṣitastatra pūjayitvā maheśvaram । sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudraloke mahīyate ।। anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ śaṅkarasyāmitaujasaḥ । mahābhairavamityuktaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ।।
tīrthānāṃ ca paraṃ tīrthaṃ vitastā paramā nadī । sarvapāpaharā puṇyā svayameva girīndrajā ।। tīrthaṃ pañcatapaṃ nāma śaṃbhoramitatejasaḥ । yatra devādidevena cakrārthaṃ pūjito bhavaḥ ।।
piṇḍadānādikaṃ tatra pretyānantaphalapradam । mṛtastatrāpi niyamād brahmaloke mahīyate ।। kāyāvarohaṇaṃ nāma mahādevālayaṃ śubham । yatra māheśvarā dharmā munibhiḥ saṃpravartitāḥ ।।
śrāddhaṃ dānaṃ tapo homa upavāsastathākṣayaḥ । parityajati yaḥ prāṇān rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। anyacca tīrthapravaraṃ kanyātīrthamiti śrutam । tatra gatvā tyajet prāṇāṃllokān prāpnoti śāśvatān ।।
jāmadagnyasya tu śubhaṃ rāmasyākliṣṭakarmaṇaḥ । tatra snātvā tīrtha vare gosahasraphalaṃ labhet ।। mahākālamiti khyātaṃ tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam । gatvā prāṇān parityajya gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt ।।
guhyād guhyatamaṃ tīrthaṃ nakulīśvaramuttamam । tatra sannihitaḥ śrīmān bhagavān nakulīśvaraḥ ।। himavacchikhare ramye gaṅgādvāre suśobhane । devyā saha mahādevo nityaṃ śiṣyaiśca saṃvṛtaḥ ।।
tatra snātvā mahādevaṃ pūjayitvā vṛṣadhvajam । sarvapāpairvimucyeta mṛtastajjñānamāpnuyāt ।। anyacca devadevasya sthānaṃ puṇyatamaṃ śubham । bhīmeśvaramiti khyātaṃ gatvā muñcati pātakam ।।
tathānyaccaṇḍavegāyāḥ saṃbhedaḥ pāpanāśanaḥ । tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca mucyate brahmahatyayā ।। sarveṣāmapi caiteṣāṃ tīrthānāṃ paramā purī । nāmnāvārāṇasī divyā koṭikoṭyayutādhikā ।।
tasyāḥ purastānmāhātmyaṃ bhāṣitaṃ vo mayā tviha । nānyatra labhyate muktiryogināpyekajanmanā ।। ete prādhānyataḥ proktā deśāḥ pāpaharā nṛṇām । gatvā saṃkṣālayet pāpaṃ janmāntaraśataiḥ kṛtam ।।
yaḥ svadharmān parityajya tīrthasevāṃ karoti hi । na tasya phalate tīrthamahi loke paratra ca ।। prāyaścittī ca vidhurastathā pāpacaro gṛhī । prakuryāt tīrthasaṃsevāṃ ye cānye tādṛśā janāḥ ।।
sahāgnirvā sapatnīko gacchet tīrthāni yatnataḥ । sarvapāpavinirmukto yathoktāṃ gatimāpnuyāt ।। ṛṇāni trīṇyapākṛtya kuryād vā tīrthasevanam । vidhāya vṛttiṃ putrāṇāṃ bhāryāṃ teṣu nidhāya ca ।।
prāyaścittaprasaṅgena tīrthamāhātmyamīritam । yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ।। etadākarṇya vijñānaṃ nārāyaṇamukheritam । kūrmarūpadharaṃ devaṃ papracchurmunayaḥ prabhum ।।
kathitā bhavatā dharmā mokṣajñānaṃ savistaram । lokānāṃ sargavistāraṃ vaṃśamanvantarāṇi ca ।। pratisargamidānīṃ no vaktumarhasī mādhava । bhūtānāṃ bhūtabhavyeśa yathā pūrvaṃ tvayoditam ।।
śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavān kūrmarūpadhṛk । vyājahāra mahāyogī bhūtānāṃ pratisaṃcaram ।। nityo naimittikaścaiva prākṛtātyantikau tathā । caturdhāyaṃ purāṇe asmin procyate pratisaṃcaraḥ ।।
yo ayaṃ saṃdṛśyate nityaṃ loke bhūtakṣayastviha । nityaḥ saṃkīrtyate nāmnā munibhiḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ ।। brāhmo naimittiko nāma kalpānte yo bhaviṣyati । trailokyasyāsya kathitaḥ pratisargo manīṣibhiḥ ।।
mahādādyāṃ viśeṣāntaṃ yadā saṃyāti saṃkṣayam । prākṛtaḥ pratisargo ayaṃ procyate kālacintakaiḥ ।। jñānādātyantikaḥ prokto yoginaḥ paramātmani । pralayaḥ pratisargo ayaṃ kālacintāparairdvijaiḥ ।।
ātyantikaśca kathitaḥ pralayo atra sasādhanaḥ । naimittikamidānīṃ vaḥ kathayiṣye samāsataḥ ।। caturyugasahasrānte saṃprāpte pratisaṃcare । svātmasaṃsthāḥ prajāḥ kartuṃ pratipede prajāpatiḥ ।।
tato bhavatyanāvṛṣṭistīvrā sā śatavārṣikī । bhūtakṣayakarī ghorā sarvabhūtakṣayaṅkarī ।। tato yānyalpasārāṇi sattvāni pṛthivītale । tāni cāgre pralīyante bhūmitvamupayānti ca ।।
saptaraśmiratho bhūtvā samuttiṣṭhan divākaraḥ । asahyaraśmirbhavati pibannambho gabhastibhiḥ ।। tasya te raśmayaḥ sapta pibantyambu mahārṇave । tenāhāreṇa tā dīptāḥ sūryāḥ sapta bhavantyuta ।।
tataste raśmayaḥ sapta sūryā bhūtvā caturdiśam । caturlokamidaṃ sarvaṃ dahanti śikhinastathā ।। vyāpnuvantaśca te viprāstūrdhvaṃ cādhaśca raśmibhiḥ । dīpyante bhāskarāḥ sapta yugāntāgnipratāpinaḥ ।।
te sūryā vāriṇā dīptā bahusāhastraraśmayaḥ । khaṃ samāvṛtya tiṣṭhanti nirdahanto vasuṃdharām ।। tatasteṣāṃ pratāpena dahyamānā vasuṃdharā । sādrinadyarṇavadvīpā nisnehā samapadyata ।।
dīptābhiḥ saṃtatābhiśca raśmibhirvai samantataḥ । adhaścordhvaṃ ca lagnābhistiryak caiva samāvṛtam ।। sūryāgninā pramṛṣṭānāṃ saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ parasparam । ekatvamupayātānāmekajvālaṃ bhavatyuta ।।
sarvalokapraṇāśaśca so agnirbhūtvā sukuṇḍalī । caturlokamidaṃ sarvaṃ nirdahatyātmatejasā ।। tataḥ pralīne sarvasmiñ jaṅgame sthāvare tathā । nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmiḥ kūrmapṛṣṭhā prakāśate ।।
ambarīṣamivābhāti sarvamāpūritaṃ jagat । sarvameva tadarcirbhiḥ pūrṇaṃ jājvalyate punaḥ ।। pātāle yāni sattvāni mahodadhigatāni ca । tatastāni pralīyante bhūmitvamupayānti ca ।।
dvīpāṃśca parvatāṃścaiva varṣāṇyatha mahodadhīn । tān sarvān bhasmasāt kṛtvā saptātmā pāvakaḥ prabhuḥ ।। samudrebhyo nadībhyaśca pātālebhyaśca sarvaśaḥ । pibannapaḥ samiddho agniḥ pṛthivīmāśrito jvalan ।।
tataḥ saṃvartakaḥ śailānatikramya mahāṃstathā । lokān dahati dīptātmā rudratejovijṝmbhitaḥ ।। sa dagdhvā pṛthivīṃ devo rasātalamaśoṣayat । adhastāt pṛthivīṃ dagdhvā divamūrdhvaṃ dahiṣyati ।।
yojanānāṃ śatānīha sahasrāṇyayutāni ca । uttiṣṭhanti śikhāstasya vahneḥ saṃvartakasya tu ।। gandharvāṃśca piśācāṃśca sayakṣoragarākṣasān । tadā dahatyasau dīptaḥ kālarudrapracoditaḥ ।।
bhūrlokaṃ ca bhuvarlokaṃ svarlokaṃ ca tathā mahaḥ । dahedaśeṣaṃ kālāgniḥ kālo viśvatanuḥ svayam ।। vyāpteṣveteṣu lokeṣu tiryagūrdhvamathāgninā । tat tejaḥ samanuprāpya kṛtsnaṃ jagadidaṃ śanaiḥ ।
ayoguḍanibhaṃ sarvaṃ tadā caikaṃ prakāśate ।। tato gajakulonnādāstaḍidbhiḥ samalaṅkṛtāḥ । uttiṣṭhanti tadā vyomni ghorāḥ saṃvartakā ghanāḥ ।। kecinnīlotpalaśyāmāḥ kecit kumudasannibhāḥ ।
dhūmravarṇāstathā kecit kecit pītāḥ payodharāḥ ।। kecid rāsabhavarṇāstu lākṣārasanibhāstathā । śaṅkhakundanibhāścānye jātyañjananibhāḥ pare ।। manaḥ śilābhāstvanye ca kapotasadṛśāḥ pare ।
indragopanibhāḥ keciddharitālanibhāstathā । indracāpanibhāḥ keciduttiṣṭhanti ghanā divi ।। kecit parvatasaṃkāśāḥ kecid gajakulopamāḥ । kūṭāṅgāranibhāścānye kecinmīnakulodvahāḥ ।
bahūrūpā ghorūpā ghorasvaraninādinaḥ ।। tadā jaladharāḥ sarve pūrayanti nabhaḥ sthalam । tataste jaladā ghorā rāviṇo bhāskarātmajāḥ । saptadhā saṃvṛtātmānastamagniṃ śamayantyuta ।।
tataste jaladā varṣaṃ muñcantīha mahaughavat । sughoramaśivaṃ sarvaṃ nāśayanti ca pāvakam ।। pravṛṣṭe ca tadātyarthamambhasā pūryate jagat । adbhistejobhibhūtatvāt tadāgniḥ praviśatyapaḥ ।।
naṣṭe cāgnau varṣaśataiḥ payodāḥ kṣayasaṃbhavāḥ । plāvayanto atha bhuvanaṃ mahājalaparistravaiḥ ।। dhārābhiḥ pūrayantīdaṃ codyamānāḥ svayaṃbhuvā । atyantasalilaughaiśca velā iva mahodadhiḥ ।।
sādridvīpā tathā pṛthvī jalaiḥ saṃcchādyate śanaiḥ । ādityaraśmibhiḥ pītaṃ jalamabhreṣu tiṣṭhati । punaḥ patati tad bhūmau pūryante tena cārṇavāḥ ।। tataḥ samudrāḥ svāṃ velāmatikrāntāstu kṛtsnaśaḥ ।
parvatāśca vilīyante mahī cāpsu nimajjati ।। tasminnekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame । yoganindrāṃ samāsthāya śete devaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। caturyugasahasrāntaṃ kalpamāhurmaharṣayaḥ ।
vārāho vartate kalpo yasya vistāra īritaḥ ।। asaṃkhyātāstathā kalpā brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakāḥ । kathitā hi purāṇeṣu munibhiḥ kālacintakaiḥ ।। sāttvikeṣvatha kalpeṣu māhātmyamadhikaṃ hareḥ ।
tāmaseṣu harasyoktaṃ rājaseṣu prajāpateḥ ।। yo ayaṃ pravartate kalpo vārāhaḥ sāttviko mataḥ । anye ca sāttvikāḥ kalpā mama teṣu parigrahaḥ ।। dhyānaṃ tapastathā jñānaṃ labdhvā teṣveva yoginaḥ ।
ārādhya giriśaṃ māṃ ca yānti tat paramaṃ padam ।। so ahaṃ sattvaṃ samāsthāya māyī māyāmayīṃ svayam । ekārṇave jagatyasmin yoganidrāṃ vrajāmi tu ।। māṃ paśyanti mahātmānaḥ suptaṃ kālaṃ maharṣayaḥ ।
janaloke vartamānāstapasā yogacakṣuṣā ।। ahaṃ purāṇapuruṣo bhūrbhuvaḥ prabhavo vibhuḥ । sahasracaraṇaḥ śrīmān sahasrāṃśuḥ sahasradṛk ।। mantro agnirbrāhmiṇā gāvaḥ kuśāśca samidho hyaham ।
prokṣaṇī ca śruvaścaiva somo ghṛtamathāsmyaham ।। saṃvartako mahānātmā pavitraṃ paramaṃ yaśaḥ । vedo vedyaṃ prabhurgoptā gopatirbrahmaṇo mukham ।। anantastārako yogī gatirgatimatāṃ varaḥ ।
haṃsaḥ prāṇo atha kapilo viśvamūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ ।। kṣetrajñaḥ prakṛtiḥ kālo jagadbījamathāmṛtam । mātā pitā mahādevo matto hyanyanna vidyate ।। nārāyaṇaḥ puruṣo yogamūrtiḥ ।
jñātvātmānamamṛtatvaṃ vrajanti ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi pratisargamanuttamam । prākṛtaṃ hi samāsena śṛṇudhvaṃ gadato mama ।। gate parārdhadvitaye kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।
kālāgnirbhasmasāt kartuṃ karoti nikilaṃ matim ।। svātmanyātmānamāveśya bhūtvā devo maheśvaraḥ । dahedaśeṣaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। tamāviśya mahādevo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ ।
karoti lokasaṃhāraṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ rūpamāśritaḥ ।। praviśya maṇḍalaṃ sauraṃ kṛtvāsau bahudhā punaḥ । nirdahatyakhilaṃ lokaṃ saptasaptisvarūpadhṛk ।। sa dagdhvā sakalaṃ sattvamastraṃ brahmaśiro mahat ।
devatānāṃ śarīreṣu kṣipatyakhiladāhakam ।। dagdheṣvaśeṣadeveṣu devī girivarātmajā । ekāsā sākṣiṇī śaṃbhostiṣṭhate vaidikī śrutiḥ ।। śiraḥ kapālairdevānāṃ kṛtastragvarabhūṣaṇaḥ ।
ādityacandrādigaṇaiḥ pūrayan vyomamaṇḍalam ।। sahasranayano devaḥ sahasrākṛtiriśvaraḥ । sahasrahastacaraṇaḥ sahasrārcirmahābhujaḥ ।। daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaḥ pradīptānalalocanaḥ ।
triśūlī kṛttivasano yogamaiśvaramāsthitaḥ ।। pītvā tatparamānandaṃ prabhūtamamṛtaṃ svayam । karoti tāṇḍavaṃ devīmālokya parameśvaraḥ ।। pītvā nṛttāmṛtaṃ devī bhartuḥ paramamaṅgalā ।
yogamāsthāya devasya dehamāyāti śūlinaḥ ।। saṃtyaktvā tāṇḍavarasaṃ svecchayaiva pinākadhṛk । jyotiḥ svabhāvaṃ bhagavān dagdhvā brahmāṇḍamaṇḍalam ।। saṃsthiteṣvatha deveṣu brahmaviṣṇupinākiṣu ।
guṇairaśeṣaiḥ pṛthivīvilayaṃ yāti vāriṣu ।। sa vāritattvaṃ saguṇaṃ grasate havyavāhanaḥ । tejastu guṇasaṃyuktaṃ vāyau saṃyāti saṃkṣayam ।। ākāśe saguṇo vāyuḥ pralayaṃ yāti viśvabhṛt ।
bhūtādau ca tathākāśaṃ līyate guṇasaṃyutam ।। indriyāṇi ca sarvāṇi taijase yānti saṃkṣayam । vaikārike devagaṇāḥ pralaṃya yānti sattamāḥ ।। vaikārikastaijasaśca bhūtādiśceti sattamāḥ ।
trividho ayamahaṅkāro mahati pralaṃya vrajet ।। mahāntamebhiḥ sahitaṃ brahmāṇamatitejasam । avyaktaṃ jagato yoniḥ saṃharedekamavyayam ।। evaṃ saṃhṛtya bhūtāni tattvāni ca maheśvaraḥ ।
viyojayati cānyonyaṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ param ।। pradhānapuṃsorajayoreṣa saṃhāra īritaḥ । maheśvarecchājanito na svayaṃ vidyate layaḥ ।। guṇasāmyaṃ tadavyaktaṃ prakṛtiḥ parigīyate ।
pradhānaṃ jagato yonirmāyātattvamacetanam ।। kūṭasthaścinmayo hyātmā kevalaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ । gīyate munibhiḥ sākṣī mahānekaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। evaṃ saṃhārakaraṇī śaktirmāheśvarī dhruvā ।
pradhānādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ dahed rudra iti śrutiḥ ।। yogināmatha sarveṣāṃ jñānavinyastacetasām । ātyantikaṃ caiva layaṃ vidadhātīha śaṅkaraḥ ।। ityeṣa bhagavān rudraḥ saṃhāraṃ kurute vaśī ।
sthāpikā mohanī śaktirnārāyaṇa iti śrutiḥ ।। hiraṇyagarbhā bhagavān jagat sadasadātmakam । sṛjedaśeṣaṃ prakṛtestanmayaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ ।। sarvajñāḥ sarvagāḥ śāntāḥ svātmanyevavyavasthitāḥ ।
śaktayo brahmaviṇvīśā bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ ।। sarveśvarāḥ sarvavandyāḥ śāśvatānantabhoginaḥ । ekamevākṣaraṃ tattvaṃ puṃpradhāneśvarātmakam ।। anyāśca śaktayo divyāḥ santi tatra sahasraśaḥ ।
ijyante vividhairyajñaiḥ śakrādityādayo amarāḥ ।। ekaikasya sahasrāṇi dehānāṃ vai śatāni ca । kathyante caiva māhātmyācchaktirekaiva nirguṇāḥ ।। tāṃ tāṃ śaktiṃ samādhāya svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ ।
karoti dehān vividhān grasate caiva līlayā ।। ijyate sarvayajñeṣu brāhmaṇairvedavādibhiḥ । sarvakāmaprado rudra ityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ ।। sarvāsāmeva śaktīnāṃ brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।
prādhānyena smṛtā devāḥ śaktayaḥ paramātmanaḥ ।। ādyaḥ parastād bhagavān paramātmā sanātanaḥ । gīyate sarvaśaktyātmā śūlapāṇirmaheśvaraḥ ।। enameke vadantyagniṃ nārāyaṇamathāpare ।
indrameke pare viśvān brahmāṇamapare jaguḥ ।। brahmaviṣṇavagnivaruṇāḥ sarve devāstatharṣayaḥ । ekasyaivātha rudrasya bhedāste parikīrtitāḥ ।। yaṃ yaṃ bhedaṃ samāśritya yajanti parameśvaram ।
tat tad rūpaṃ samāsthāya pradadāti phalaṃ śivaḥ ।। tasmādekataraṃ bhedaṃ samāśrityāpi śāśvatam । ārādhayanmahādevaṃ yāti tatparamaṃ padam ।। kintu devaṃ mahādevaṃ sarvaśaktiṃ sanātanam ।
ārādhayed vai giriśaṃ saguṇaṃ vātha nirguṇam ।। mayā prokto hi bhavatāṃ yogaḥ prāgeva nirguṇaḥ । ārurukṣustu saguṇaṃ pūjayet parameśvaram ।। pinākinaṃ trinayanaṃ jaṭilaṃ kṛttivāsasam ।
padmāsanasthaṃ rukmābhaṃ cintayed vaidikī śrutiḥ ।। eṣa yogaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sabījo munisattamāḥ । tasmāt sarvān parityajya devān brahmapurogamān । ārādhayed virūpākṣamādimadhyāntasaṃsthitam ।।
bhaktiyogasamāyuktaḥ svadharmanirataḥ śuciḥ । tādṛśaṃ rūpamāsthāya samāyātyantikaṃ śivam ।। eṣa yogaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sabījo atyantabhāvane । yathāvidhi prakurvāṇaḥ prāpnuyādaiśvaraṃ padam ।।
atrāpyaśakto atha haraṃ viṣṇuṃ bahmāṇamarcayet । atha cedasamarthaḥ syāt tatrāpi munipuṅgavāḥ । tato vāyvagniśakrādīn pūjayed bhaktisaṃyutaḥ ।। ye cānye bhāvane śuddhe prāgukte bhavatāmiha ।
athāpi kathito yogo nirbojaśca sabījakaḥ ।। jñānaṃ taduktaṃ nirbojaṃ pūrvaṃ hi bhavatāṃ mayā । viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ virañciṃ ca sabījaṃ bhāvayed budhaḥ । sathavāgnyādikān devāṃstatparaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ ।।
pūjayet puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ caturmūrtidharaṃ harim । anādinidhanaṃ devaṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam ।। nārāyaṇaṃ jagadyonimākāśaṃ paramaṃ padam । talliṅgadhārī niyataṃ tadbhaktastadapāśrayaḥ ।
eṣa eva vidhirbrāhme bhāvane cāntike mataḥ ।। ityetat kathitaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvanāsaṃśrayaṃ param । indradyumnāya munaye kathitaṃ yanmayā purā ।। avyaktātmakamevedaṃ cetanācetanaṃ jagat ।
tadīśvaraḥ paraṃ brahma tasmād brahmamayaṃ jagat ।। etāvaduktvā bhagavān virarāma janārdanaḥ । tuṣṭuvurmunayo viṣṇuṃ śakreṇa saha mādhavam ।। namaste kūrmarūpāya viṣṇave paramātmane ।
nārāyaṇāya viśvāya vāsudevāya te namaḥ ।। namo namaste kṛṣṇāya govindāya namo namaḥ । mādhavāya namastubhyaṃ namo yajñeśvarāya ca ।। sahasraśirase tubhyaṃ sahasrākṣāya te namaḥ ।
namaḥ sahasrahastāya sahasracaraṇāya ca ।। oṃ namo jñānarūpāya paramātmasvarūpiṇe । ānandāya namastubhyaṃ māyātītāya te namaḥ ।। namo gūḍhaśarīrāya nirguṇāya namo astu te ।
puruṣāya purāṇāya sattāmātrasvarūpiṇe ।। namaḥ sāṃkhyāya yogāya kevalāya namo astu te । dharmajñānādhigamyāya niṣkalāya namo namaḥ ।। namostu vyomatattvāya mahāyogeśvarāya ca ।
parāvarāṇāṃ prabhave vedavedyāya te namaḥ ।। namo buddhāya śuddhāya namo yuktāya hetave । namo namo namastubhyaṃ māyine vedhase namaḥ ।। namo astu te varāhāya nārasiṃhāya te namaḥ ।
vāmanāya namastubhyaṃ hṛṣīkeśāya te namaḥ ।। namo astu kālarudrāya kālarūpāya te namaḥ । svargāpavargadātre ca namo apratihatātmane ।। namo yogādhigamyāya yogine yogadāyine ।
devānāṃ pataye tubhyaṃ devārtiśamanāya te ।। bhagavaṃstvatprasādena sarvasaṃsāranāśanam । asmābhirviditaṃ jñānaṃ yajjñātvāmṛtamaśnute ।। śrutāstu vividhā dharmā vaṃśā manvantarāṇi ca ।
sargaśca pratisargaśca brahmāṇyasyāsya vistaraḥ ।। tvaṃ hi sarvajagatsākṣī viśvo nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ । trātumarhasyanantātmaṃstvameva śaraṇaṃ gatiḥ ।। etad vaḥ kathitaṃ viprā yogamokṣapradāyakam ।
kaurmaṃ purāṇamakhilaṃ yajjagāda gadādharaḥ ।। asmin purāṇe lakṣmyāstu saṃbhavaḥ kathitaḥ purā । mohāyāśeṣabhūtānāṃ vāsudevena yojanam ।। prajāpatīnāṃ sargastu varṇadharmāśca vṛttayaḥ ।
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ yathāvallakṣaṇaṃ śubham ।। pitāmahasya viṣṇośca maheśasya ca dhīmataḥ । ekatvaṃ ca pṛthaktvaṃ ca viśeṣaścopavarṇitaḥ ।। bhaktānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ samācāraśca śobhanaḥ ।
varṇāśramāṇāṃ kathitaṃ yathāvadiha lakṣaṇam ।। ādisargastataḥ paścādaṇḍāvaraṇasaptakam । hiraṇyagarbhasargaśca kīrtito munipuṅgavāḥ ।। kālasaṃkhyāprakathanaṃ māhātmyaṃ ceśvarasya ca ।
brahmaṇaḥ śayanaṃ cāpsu nāmanirvacanaṃ tathā ।। varāhavapuṣā bhūyo bhūmeruddharaṇaṃ punaḥ । mukhyādisargakathanaṃ munisargastathāparaḥ ।। vyākhyato rudrasargaśca ṛṣisargaśca tāpasaḥ ।
dharmasya ca prajāsargastāmasāt pūrvameva tu ।। brahmaviṣṇuvivādaḥ syādantardehapraveśanam । padmodbhavatvaṃ devasya mohastasya ca dhīmataḥ ।। darśanaṃ ca maheśasya māhātmyaṃ viṣṇuneritam ।
divyadṛṣṭipradānaṃ ca brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। saṃstavo devadevasya brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā । prasādo giriśasyātha varadānaṃ tathaiva ca ।। saṃvādo viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ ।
varadānaṃ tathāpūrvamantardhānaṃ pinākinaḥ ।। vadhaśca kathito viprā madhukaiṭabhayoḥ purā । avatāro atha devasya brahmaṇo nābhipaṅkajāt ।। ekībhāvaśca devasya viṣṇunā kathitastataḥ ।
vimoho brahmaṇaścātha saṃjñālābho harestataḥ ।। tapaścaraṇamākhyātaṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ । prādurbhāvo maheśasya lalāṭāt kathitastataḥ ।। rudrāṇāṃ kathitā sṛṣṭirbrahmaṇaḥ pratiṣedhanam ।
bhūtiśca devadevasya varadānopadeśakau ।। antardhānaṃ ca rudrasya tapaścaryāṇḍajasya ca । darśanaṃ devadevasya naranārīśarīratā ।। devyā vibhāgakathanaṃ devadevāt pinākinaḥ ।
devyāstu paścāt kathitaṃ dakṣaputrītvameva ca ।। himavadduhitṛtvaṃ ca devyā māhātmyameva ca । darśanaṃ divyarūpasya vaiśvarūpasya darśanam ।। nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ kathitaṃ pitrā himavatā svayam ।
upadeśo mahādevyā varadānaṃ tathaiva ca ।। bhṛgvādīnāṃ prajāsargo rājñāṃ vaṃśasya vistaraḥ । prācetasatvaṃ dakṣasya dakṣayajñavimardanam ।। dadhīcasya ca dakṣasya vivādaḥ kathitastadā ।
tataśca śāpaḥ kathito munīnāṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। rudrāgatiḥ prasādaśca antardhānaṃ pinākinaḥ । pitāmahasyopadeśaḥ kīrtyate rakṣaṇāya tu ।। dakṣasya ca prajāsargaḥ kaśyapasya mahātmanaḥ ।
hiraṇyakaśipornāśo hiraṇyākṣavadhastathā ।। tataśca śāpaḥ kathito devadāruvanaukasām । nigrahaścāndhakasyātha gāṇapatyamanuttamam ।। prahrādanigrahaścātha baleḥ saṃyamanaṃ tataḥ ।
bāṇasya nigrahaścātha prasādastasya śūlinaḥ ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ vaṃśavistāro rājñāṃ vaṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ । vasudevāt tato viṣṇorutpattiḥ svecchayā hareḥ ।। darśanaṃ copamanyorvai tapaścaraṇameva ca ।
varalābho mahādevaṃ dṛṣṭvā sāmbaṃ trilocanam ।। kailāsagamanaṃ cātha nivāsastatra śārṅgiṇaḥ । tataśca kathyate bhītirdvārivatyā nivāsinām ।। rakṣaṇaṃ garuḍenātha jitvā śatrūn mahābalān ।
nārādāgamanaṃ caiva yātrā caiva garutmataḥ ।। tataśca kṛṣṇāgamanaṃ munīnāmāgatistataḥ । naityakaṃ vāsudevasya śivaliṅgārcanaṃ tathā ।। mārkaṇḍeyasya ca muneḥ praśnaḥ proktastataḥ param ।
liṅgārcananimittaṃ ca liṅgasyāpi saliṅginaḥ ।। yathātmyakathanaṃ cātha liṅgāvirbhāva eva ca । brahmaviṣṇostathā madhye kīrtito munipuṅgavāḥ ।। mohastayostu kathito gamanaṃ cordhvato apyadhaḥ ।
saṃstavo devadevasya prasādaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।। antardhānaṃ ca liṅgasya sāmbotpattistataḥ param । kīrtitā cāniruddhasya samutpattirdvijottamāḥ ।। kṛṣṇasya gamane buddhirṛṣīṇāmāgatistathā ।
anuvaśāsitaṃ ca kṛṣṇena varadānaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। gamanaṃ caiva kṛṣṇasya pārthasyāpi ca darśanam । kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasyoktā yugadharmāḥ sanātanāḥ ।। anugraho atha pārthasya vārāṇasīgatistataḥ ।
pārāśaryasya ca munervyāsasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ ।। vāraṇasyāśca māhātmyaṃ tīrthānāṃ caiva varṇanam । tīrthayātrā ca vyāsasya devyāścaivātha darśanam । udvāsanaṃ ca kathitaṃ varadānaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
prayāgasya ca māhātmyaṃ kṣetrāṇāmatha kīrtinam । phalaṃ ca vipulaṃ viprā mārkaṇḍeyasya nirgamaḥ ।। bhuvanānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca jyotiṣāṃ ca niveśanam । kīrtyante caiva varṣāṇi nadīnāṃ caiva nirṇayaḥ ।।
parvatānāṃ ca kathanaṃ sthānāni ca divaukasām । dvīpānāṃ pravibhāgaśca śvetadvīpopavarṇanam ।। śayanaṃ keśavasyātha māhātmyaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ । manvantarāṇāṃ kathanaṃ viṣṇormāhātmyameva ca ।।
vedaśākhāpraṇayanaṃ vyāsānāṃ kathanaṃ tataḥ । avedasya ca vedānāṃ kathanaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।। yogeśvarāṇāṃ ca kathā śiṣyāṇāṃ cātha kīrtanam । gītāśca vividhāguhyā īśvarasyātha kīrtitāḥ ।।
varṇāśramāṇāmācārāḥ prāyaścittavidhistataḥ । kapālitvaṃ ca rudrasya bhikṣācaraṇameva ca ।। pativratāyāścākhyānaṃ tīrthānāṃ ca vinirṇayaḥ । tathā maṅkaṇakasyātha nigrahaḥ kīrtyate dvijāḥ ।।
vadhaśca kathito viprāḥ kālasya ca samāsataḥ । devadāruvane śaṃbhoḥ praveśo mādhavasya ca ।। darśanaṃ ṣaṭkulīyānāṃ devadevasya dhīmataḥ । varadānaṃ ca devasya nandine tu prakīrtitam ।।
naimittikastu kathitaḥ pratisargastataḥ param । prākṛtaḥ pralayaścordhvaṃ sabījo yoga eva ca ।। evaṃ jñātvā purāṇasya saṃkṣepaṃ kīrtayet tu yaḥ । sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
evamuktvā śriyaṃ devīmādāya puruṣottamaḥ । saṃtyajya kūrmasaṃsthānaṃ svasthānaṃ ca jagāma ha ।। devāśca sarve munayaḥ svāni sthānāni bhejire । praṇamya puruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ gṛhītvā hyamṛtaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
etat purāṇaṃ paramaṃ bhāṣitaṃ kūrmarūpiṇā । sākṣād devādidenena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā ।। yaḥ paṭhet satataṃ martyo niyamena samāhitaḥ । sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
likhitvā caiva yo dadyād vaiśākhe māsi suvrataḥ । viprāya vedaviduṣe tasya puṇyaṃ nibodhata ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvaiśvaryasamanvitaḥ । bhuktvā ca vipulānsvarge bhogāndivyānsuśobhanān ।।
tataḥ svargāt paribhraṣṭo viprāṇāṃ jāyate kule । pūrvasaṃskāramāhātmyād brahmavidyāmavāpnuyāt ।। paṭhitvādhyāyamevaikaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate । yor'thaṃ vicārayet samyak sa prāpnoti paraṃ padam ।।
adhyetavyamidaṃ nityaṃ vipraiḥ parvaṇi parvaṇi । śrotavyaṃ ca dvijaśreṣṭhā mahāpātakanāśanam ।। ekatastu purāṇāni setihāsāni kṛtsnaśaḥ । ekatra cedaṃ paramametadevātiricyate ।।
dharmanaipuṇyakāmānāṃ jñānanaipuṇyakāminām । idaṃ purāṇaṃ muktvaikaṃ nāstyanyat sādhanaṃ param ।। yathāvadatra bhagavān devo nārāyaṇo hariḥ । kathyate hi yathā viṣṇurna tathānyeṣu suvratāḥ ।।
brāhmī paurāṇikī ceyaṃ saṃhitā pāpanāśanī । atra tat paramaṃ brahma kīrtyate hi yathārthataḥ ।। tīrthānāṃ paramaṃ tīrthaṃ tapasāṃ ca paraṃ tapaḥ । jñānānāṃ paramaṃ jñānaṃ vratānāṃ paramaṃ vratam ।।
nādhyetavyamidaṃ śāstraṃ vṛṣalasya ca sannidhau । yo adhīte sa tu mohātmā sa yāti narakān bahūn ।। śrāddhe vā daivike kārye śrāvaṇīyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ । yajñānte tu viśeṣeṇa sarvadoṣaviśodhanam ।।
mumukṣūṇāmidaṃ śāstramadhyetavyaṃ viśeṣataḥ । śrotavyaṃ cātha mantavyaṃ vedārthaparibṛṃhaṇam ।। jñātvā yathāvad viprendrān śrāvayed bhaktisaṃyutān । sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmasāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।
yo aśraddadhāne puruṣe dadyāccādhārmike tathā । sa pretya gatvā nirayān śunāṃ yoniṃ vrajatyadhaḥ ।। namaskṛtvā hariṃ viṣṇuṃ jagadyoniṃ sanātanam । adhyetavyamidaṃ śāstraṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ tathā ।।
ityājñā devadevasya viṣṇoramitatejasaḥ । pārāśaryasya viprarṣervyāsasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।। śrutvā nārāyaṇād divyāṃ nārado bhagavānṛṣiḥ । gautamāya dadau pūrvaṃ tasmāccaiva parāśaraḥ ।।
parāśaro api bhagavāna gaṅgādvāre munīśvarāḥ । munibhyaḥ kathayāmāsa dharmakāmārthamokṣadam ।। brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ sanakāya ca dhīmate । sanatkumārāya tathā sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ।।
sanakād bhagavān sākṣād devalo yogavittamaḥ । avāptavān pañcaśikho devalādidamuttamam ।। sanatkumārād bhagavān muniḥ satyavatīsutaḥ । lebhe purāṇaṃ paramaṃ vyāsaḥ sarvārthasaṃcayam ।।
tasmād vyāsādahaṃ śrutvā bhavatāṃ pāpanāśanam । ūcivān vai bhavadbhiśca dātavyaṃ dhārmike jane ।। tasmai vyāsāya gurave sarvajñāya maharṣaye । pārāśaryāya śāntāya namo nārāyaṇātmane ।।
yasmāt saṃjāyate kṛtsanaṃ yatra caiva pralīyate । namastasmai sureśāya viṣṇave kūrmarūpiṇe ।।
